40001001	Me a bol ma nywolirok pa Yesu Kristo, nyakwar Daudi, nyakwar Ibrayimu:
40001002	Ibrayimu onywolo Isaka, Isaka to nywolo Yakobo, Yakobo to nywolo Yuda gi wutumin go;
40001003	Yuda to nywolo Perez gi Zera i yoki jo Tamar, Perez to nywolo Heziron, Heziron to nywolo Ram;
40001004	Ram to nywolo Aminadab, Aminadab to nywolo Nason, Nason to nywolo Salmon;
40001005	Salmon gi chiege Rahab to jonywolo Bowaz, Bowaz gi chiege Ruth to jonywolo Obed, Obed to nywolo Yese;
40001006	Yese to nywolo Daudi Kere. Daudi to nywolo Solomon ma min oido chipa Uriya;
40001007	Solomon to nywolo Rehobowam, Rehobowam to nywolo Abiya, Abiya to nywolo Asa;
40001008	Asa to nywolo Yehosafat, Yehosafat to nywolo Yoram; Yoram to nywolo Uziya;
40001009	Uziya to nywolo Yotham, Yotham to nywolo Ahaz, Ahaz to nywolo Hezekiya;
40001010	Hezekiya to nywolo Manase; Manase to nywolo Amos, Amos to nywolo Yosiya;
40001011	Yosiya to nywolo Yekoniya gi wutumin go, gikenyo to itero jo paka ŋechin yu Babilon;
40001012	Munyo otyek tero jo yu Babilon, Yokoniya onywolo Salutyel, Salutyel to nywolo Zerubabel;
40001013	Zerubabel to nywolo Abiwud, Abiwud to nywolo Elyakim, Elyakim to nywolo Azor;
40001014	Azor to nywolo Zadok; Zadok to nywolo Akim, Akim to nywolo Eliyudi,
40001015	Eliyudi to nywolo Elyazar; Elyazar to nywolo Mathan, Mathan to nywolo Yakobo;
40001016	Yakobo to nywolo Yozefu, mobedo chwor Marya, monywolo Yesu milwoŋo ni Kristo.
40001017	Ri ameno, wok kwoŋ Ibrayimu tundo kwoŋi Daudi, obedo luse ji apar g'aŋwen; odoko wok kwoŋ Daudi, tundo munyo oter jo yu Babilon, obedo luse ji apar gaŋwen; kendo wok munyo oter jo yu Babilon tundo kwoŋ Kristo, bende obedo luse ji apar g'aŋwen.
40001018	Me apaka nywolirok pa Yesu Kristo obedo: Munyo Yozefu fuodi oido nyaka jochikere nywomirok kodi Marya min Yesu, ma fuodi korwako go i ot, to nenere ni go oido otyeko gamo iye i men pa Chuny Maleŋ.
40001019	Gikenyo Yozefu chwore, rupiri oido obedo dhano motire aka komito miyo go wichkwot, oido paro weyo go nyaliŋliŋ.
40001020	Neni, munyo fuodi go paro ameno, malaika pa Ruoth to bino ri go i lek, to wacho ri go ni, “Yozefu wuodi pa Daudi, ikiri ilwor rwako Marya bedo dhako perin, rupiri go yach gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ.
40001021	Go bino nywolo nyathi ma jayach, aka ibino chwoko nyinge ni Yesu; rupiri go ama bino botho ji pere kwoŋ recho pajo.”
40001022	Gino jye otimere, ŋey gima jatuchi wach Were oluwo wotundi i kare ni,
40001023	“Nyako ma fuodi kuya jachwo bino gamo iye, to nywolo nyathi ma jayach, ma ibino chwoko nyinge ni Emanwel,” dwoŋ mere ni, “Were ni gi wan.”
40001024	Yozefu munyo ochiew, to timo paka malaika pa Were owacho ri go, to tero Marya bedo chiege;
40001025	aka koŋeyere gine tundo munyo ochowo nywolo nyathi no to chwoko nyinge ni Yesu.
40002001	Munyo otyek nywolo Yesu i tindi ma Bethlehem, i Yudeya i ndir ma Herode oido kere, joryeko mogo ma jofuonjere kwoŋ michalin jowok yu Wokchieŋ to jobino Yerusalem;
40002002	aka jopenjo ni, “Nikune nyathi monywol bedo kere pa Joyudaya? Waneno michala pere munyo owok yu Wokchieŋ amomiyo onyo wabino lamo go.”
40002003	Munyo Kere Herode owinjo gime, obwok, aka kir gi ji man jye i Yerusalem.
40002004	Go olwoŋo jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar jye kodi jofuonji ma Chik kanyachiel to penjo jo ni, “Ibino nywolo Kristo kune?”
40002005	Jodwoko ni, “I tindi ma Bethlehem, i Yudeya.” Me a gima jatuchi wach Were ondiko ni,
40002006	“In Bethlehem, i piny pa Yuda, iŋati ikiasa thin i dyer jodhum ma Yuda; kole kwoŋin ama jatel bino wok'iye, ma bino bedo jakwath pa Joisrael.”
40002007	Gikenyo Herode olwoŋo wendo ma jowok yu Wokchieŋ no i romo ma nyaliŋliŋ, aka oŋeyo kwoŋ jo ndir won ma michala no omenyer'iye ri jo.
40002008	Gikenyo ooro jo Bethlehem gi wach me: “Kidhi win wirangi kama di nyathi no maber aka ka winwaŋo go wimiyan ŋeyo, ŋey abende abin alam go.”
40002009	Gi wach me joeye kenyo, aka munyo oido jowotho i royo, joneno michala ma ndir cha joneno yu Wokchieŋ, motelo jo chuka otundo to chungo kama nyathi no oido ni iye.
40002010	Josangala swa, kendo jowinjo maber moasere munyo joneno michala no!
40002011	Jodonjo i ot to joneno nyathi bongi Marya yokimere. Joguro chongi gin piny jolamo go, to joyawo migowe pajo, to jochwayo mich: zawabu, buban, kodi mo maŋwe kur.
40002012	Were onyutho jo i lek nike jokiri jogiki kendo pa Herode, ri ameno jodok yu piny pajo gi royo man.
40002013	Munyo jotyeko kadho, malaika pa Ruoth omenyere ri Yozefu i lek munyo wacho ni, “Ayi malo ikwanyi nyathi gi yokimere wiringi i piny Misir, aka wibedi koro nyuka anowachi ri win ndir ma dwoko. Herode lerango nyathi no munyo mito neko.”
40002014	Amomiyo Yozefu oay malo okwanyo nyathi gi yokimere, to joay wor kidho yu Misir;
40002015	kama go obed'iye chuka Herode otho. Meno omiyo gima jatuchi wach Were owacho chon otundo i kare ni, “Alwoŋo wuodan wok Misir.”
40002016	Munyo Herode oneno ni joryeko ma jowok yu Wokchieŋ jothumo ri go ryeko, keme omako go to wodho or nike woneki woko nyithindho mayach jye ma joromo oro aryo gik chien, i Bethlehem kodi loka mothenere gine. Otimo gino jye chungo kwom gima go oido otyeko ŋeyo kwoŋ ndir ma go openj'iye joryeko cha kwoŋ menyirok pa michala.
40002017	Ameno gima Yeremiya jatuchi wach Were owacho otundo i kare ni,
40002018	“Derino winjere yu Rama, derino ma ywak malith gi ndur. Rakel ywako nyithindho pere. Kiyey wokwey chunye, rupiri ongoye modoŋ.”
40002019	Munyo Herode otyeko tho, malaika pa Ruoth omenyere ri Yozefu i lek yu Misir;
40002020	aka owacho ni, “Ayi malo ikwanyi nyathi gi yokimere widoki i piny Israel rupiri joma oido jorango neko go jotyeko tho.”
40002021	Amomiyo Jozefu oay malo, okwanyo nyathi gi yokimere to jodok yu piny Israel.
40002022	Munyo Yozefu owinjo ni Akelayus ama olunjo kom pa bamere Herode paka kere ma Yudeya, lworo omako go dok kendo kenyo. Were omedo menyo rigo i lek, amomiyo go okidho i adech ma Galileya,
40002023	to gero pecho pere i tindi ma Nazareth. Go otimo ameno ma miyo gima jatuchi wach Were owacho wotundi ni, “Ibino lwoŋo go ni Janazareth.”
40003001	I hongo no Yohana Jakibatisa obino to chako tito wach Were i thim ma Yudeya munyo wacho ni:
40003002	“Ŋuti win, rupiri Ker ma polo ni chiegin!”
40003003	Yohana oido a ŋata Isaya jatuchi wach Were chango oluwo kwoŋe chon munyo wacho ni: “Nyatoro koko i thim ni: Yiki win royo pa Ruoth, Tiri win rigo royo pere.”
40003004	Ruuk pa Yohana oido otim ma yer ŋamira, aka go oido tweyo pyere gi del ma pyen, aka chiemo pere oido obedo bonyo kodi mo kich.
40003005	Ji jobino bonge wok Yerusalem, wok i adech ma Yudeya, kodi wok i adeche jye mothoko jwom Yordan.
40003006	Jotucho gimarecho pajo aka omiy jo batisimo i Yordan.
40003007	Munyo Yohana oneno kweth Jofarisayo kodi Josadukayo jobino bonge limo batisimo, owacho ri jo ni, “Win nyithindhi thwole, ŋata onyutho win ryeko ma both kwoŋ keme pa Were ma chiegin bino?
40003008	Timi win gima nyutho nike wityeko ŋuto gimarecho mewin kichutho.
40003009	Aka wikiri wipar ni winyalo nwaŋo kagoŋirok munyo wiwacho ni, ‘Ibrayimu obedo kwari wan.’ Awacho ri win ni Were nyalo kwanyo kada telin me to loko nyikway Ibrayimu!
40003010	Kada pama le otyek yiko ma toŋo yen gi i tyendi gin! Yath jye ma kinyak gimaber ibino toŋo woko tibolo i mach!
40003011	Amiyo win batisimo kodi pi ma nyutho nike wityeko ŋuto; to ŋata bino luwan chien bino miyo win batisimo gi Chuny Maleŋ kodi mach. Go loyan gi dwoŋ tektek ma akiripi kada tiŋo war pere.
40003012	Go nitye g'odher pere ma yeko nyingi kal jye; go bino choko kal pere malilo to konjo i dero pere, to waŋo woko chuŋ i mach makitho.”
40003013	I hongo no Yesu owok Galileya to kidho Yordan to bino bongi Yohana ni womiy go batisimo.
40003014	To Yohana otemo juko go ka wacho ri go ni, “Aŋata oido aripo limo batisimo bongin, odoko ibino bongan ayino!”
40003015	To Yesu odwoko go ni, “Weyi watim ameno pama. Kole i tim me wabino tiro gimoro jye ma Were yenyo.” To Yohana yeyo.
40003016	Tekin Yesu chowo limo batisimo, owok i pi. Gikenyo polo oyawere ri go aka oneno Chuny Maleŋ loro piny i chal pa akuru to pye kwoŋe.
40003017	Gikenyo dwondi nyatoro oluwo wok i polo ni, “Me a Wuodan won mamaro, aka asangala gine.”
40004001	Gikenyo Chuny Maleŋ otero Yesu i thim ŋey jwogi wotem go.
40004002	Munyo go ochowo odyechieŋ gi wor pyero aŋwen munyo riyo, Yesu owinjo kech.
40004003	Jwogi obino bonge to wacho ni, “K'inen ibedo Wuodi Were adyeri, ere apawiri telin me wolokere chiemo.”
40004004	Yesu odwoko ni, “Ondik ni, ‘Dhano kinyal kwo gi chiemo kende, to gi wach jye mawok i dhoki Were.’ ”
40004005	Gikenyo jwogi otero Yesu i tindi maleŋ to ketho go wi kisul ma Ot pa Were,
40004006	to wacho ri go ni, “K'inen ibedo Wuodi Were ere paporiye piny, kole ondik ni, ‘Were bino oro rin jomalaika pere, ma jobino byelin i chingi gin, aka ikibino chadho tyendin kwoŋ tele.’ ”
40004007	Yesu odwoko ni, “Kole ondik bende ni, ‘Ikiri item Ruoth Were perin.’ ”
40004008	Gikenyo jwogi otero Yesu wi got mabor swa, to nyutho go ker ma piny jye, gi dwoŋ mani iye jye.
40004009	Jwogi owacho ni, “Abino miyin gigo jye, ka iryewere ruwaŋan t'ilaman.”
40004010	Gikenyo Yesu odwoko ni, “Eye bongan Sitan! Ondik ni, ‘Lami Ruoth Were perin aka itiy ri go won kende.’ ”
40004011	Gikenyo jwogi oweyo go; aka jomalaika jobino jomiyo go kony.
40004012	Munyo Yesu owinjo ni otwey Yohana, go oay to kidho Galileya.
40004013	Go oeye Nazareth, to kidho Kapernaum, tindi ma dho jwom Galileya, i adech mapa Zebulun kodi Naftal.
40004014	Gime otimere ma miyo gima Isaya jatuchi wach Were owacho wotundi i kare ni,
40004015	“Piny pa Zebulun, piny pa Naftal, thenge ma yu wakawaka, i thengi Yordan, Galileya, pa Jopath!
40004016	Ji moido jonitye i mudho joneno lero madwoŋ; Aka ri joma oido jonitye i piny ma mudho ma tho, lero otyeko menyere.”
40004017	Wok i hongo no kadho yuwaŋe Yesu ochako fuonjo ka wacho ni, “Ŋuti win recho rupiri Ker ma polo ni chiegin.”
40004018	Munyo Yesu oido wotho dho Wakawaka Galileya, go oneno wutimere aryo ma jokitoga, Simon (milwoŋo ni Petro) kodi Andereya omin go, munyo oido jochiko rech i wakawaka gi bwoo rupiri oido jobedo jokitoga.
40004019	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Biye luwan win aloki win jokitoga ji.”
40004020	Piyo piyo jono joweyo bwoo pajo, to joluwo go.
40004021	Yesu omedere woth aka oneno wutimere aryo man, Yakobo kodi Yohana, yach pa Zebedayo. Onwaŋo jonitye i yee pajo gi baa gin Zebedayo joyiko bwoo pajo, to lwoŋo jo.
40004022	Piyo piyo jono joweyo yee pajo gi baa gin, to joluwo Yesu.
40004023	Yesu owotho i Galileya parom, munyo fuonjo Wach Maber kwoŋ Ker pa Were i kalamo pa Joyudaya, gi botho two kodi ramirok ma nger jye.
40004024	Wach ma mako kwoge onyay i piny Sirya gipi, momiyo ji jokelo ri go ji jye monwaŋo jotwo kiti two mopokere jye, kodi ramirok ma nger jye moido chando jo: ji ma jwogi ni kwoŋ gin, joma tho fum, kodi jonyaŋinya; to Yesu botho jo jye.
40004025	Kweth ji moasere joluwo go wok Galileya kodi Dekapoli (tindi mochokere apar) wok Yerusalem, Yudeya, kodi piny ma loka Yordan.
40005001	Yesu oneno kitipa ji, to idho wi got, aka munyo otyeko bedo piny, jofuonjirok pere jobino bothe;
40005002	aka ochako fuonjo jo ni:
40005003	“Josilwany a joma chandere i chuny gin, rupiri Ker ma polo obedo apa jo.
40005004	“Josilwany a joma ywak, rupiri ibino kweyo chuny jo.
40005005	“Josilwany a joma mwol, rupiri jobino lunjo piny.
40005006	“Josilwany a joma nitye g'awanya madwoŋ ma timo gima Were yenyo, rupiri ibino yeŋo jo.
40005007	“Josilwany a joma nyutho jowoti gin wor, rupiri Were bino nyutho jo bende wor.
40005008	“Josilwany a joma chuny gin olony, rupiri jobino neno Were.
40005009	“Josilwany joma kweyo piny, rupiri ibino lwoŋo jo ni nyithindho pa Were.
40005010	“Josilwany a joma ilwenyo gi jo ru timo gima Were yenyo, rupiri Ker ma polo obedo apa jo!
40005011	“Win wi josilwany ka ji joyeto win aka jolwenyo gi win, ka jowacho wach jye kwoŋ win rupiri wibedo joma luwan.
40005012	Yodere win aka wisangala, rupiri kemba mewin obedo moasere i polo. Me apaka chango jotimo kir ri jotuchi wach Were machon.
40005013	“Wibedo kado chumbi ma piny. To ka kado chumbi orwenyo woko chwe mere, aŋo ma nyalo miyo go bedo mamit kendo? Lokere gima ongoye kony; amomiyo ikonjo woko to ji nyono gi tyendi gin.
40005014	“Win wiŋati wibedo lero ma piny. Tindi moger wi tendere madwoŋ kipanere.
40005015	Ongoye ŋata chwinyo tala to ryewo i agono; kuchiel go ripo ŋawo tala no malo kuma nyalo miyo lero ri ji jye ma ot.
40005016	Ri ameno lero mewin bende ripo menyo iye jye ŋey ji jowoneni gima beyo ma witimo to jopako Baa win mani polo.
40005017	“Wikiri wipar nike abino ka kwanyo woko Chik pa Musa kodi fuonji pa jotuchi wach Were, to abino nyutho dwoŋ mere maradyeri ayin.
40005018	Adyeri awacho ri win, ka polo gi piny fuodi nitye, ongoye kada gimathin kosa adech mondhilo kwoŋ Chik mibino kwanyo woko, to bino bedo ama tundo kama gimoro jye otyeko timer'iye.
40005019	Amomiyo nyatoro jye mokweri winjo kada gimoro nyaka mathin kwoŋ Chik aka ofuonji joman bende timo ameno, bino bedo ŋata loyo thino i Ker ma polo. Kuchiel nyatoro jye mowinji Chik aka ofuonji joman bende timo ameno, bino bedo ŋata dwoŋ swa i Ker ma polo.
40005020	Amomiyo, awacho ri win ni wikibino nyalo donjo i Ker ma polo kwanyo woko ka wibedo gi leŋo ma kalo apa jofuonji ma Chik kodi Jofarisayo i timo gima Were yenyo.
40005021	“Wityeko winjo ni chango owach ri ji machon ni, ‘Ikiri ineki, aka nyatoro jye ma janek ibino tero go ruwaŋ jathum banja.’
40005022	To pama onyo awacho ri win ama: ŋata omaki nge g'omin bino bedo gi banja kapido. Ŋata otim rooro kwoŋ omin ibino tero go ruwaŋ jothumi banja, aka ŋata oyeti omin ni, ‘Mamiŋ ma bu kony,’ ibino bolo go i mach makitho.
40005023	Amomiyo ka onwaŋo itero mich perin ri Were wi alitar to gikenyo ipoyo nike omerin nitye gi dhaw kodin,
40005024	weyi mich perin i nyim alitar kenyo, kutho ikidhi iyiki wach g'omerin aka nyaka idwoki imiyi Were mich perin.
40005025	“Ka dhano ni gi wach moro kodin aka mito terin kapido, yiki gine wach no ma fuodi hongo nitye, ka fuodi wikitundo kapido. Ka winotundi kenyo, go bino bolin i chingi jathumi banja, ma bino kethin i chingi joserikale ma katwech titweyin.
40005026	Ibino bedo kenyo, awacho rin, nyuka inochul kir pesa machowe mothumi rin.
40005027	“Wityeko winjo paka chango owach ni, ‘Ikiri itim chot.’
40005028	To pama awacho ri win ama: ŋata ŋiyo dhako moro aka chunye wanya go, meno otyeko timo gine chot gi i chunye.
40005029	Amomiyo k'inen waŋin marachuch miyin timo gimarach, goli woko iboli woko! Kole ber ikeŋi adech moro ma delkwoŋin loyo nwaŋo delkwoŋin gipi tibolo i mach makitho.
40005030	K'inen chingin marachuch miyin timo gimarach, ŋondi ibol woko! Rupiri ber iremi chingin achiel loyo delkwoŋin gipi kidho i mach makitho.
40005031	“Chango chon owach ni, ‘Nyatoro ma ryemo woko chiege ripo miyo go balwa ma ryemo go i ndiiko.’
40005032	To pama awacho ri win ni: nyatoro jye moryemi chiege ri wach moro jye ma kobedo wach ma kidakana, meno go miyo chiege donjo i chot. Aka ŋata nywomo dhako ma pameno, meno bende timo gine chot.
40005033	“Wityeko winjo paka chango chon owach ni, ‘Ikiri ikwoŋere ma twodo, to timi gima ikwoŋere timo i nyim Ruoth.’
40005034	To pama awacho ri win ni: ikiri ikwoŋere kada mathin ka itimo chikirok, ikiri ikwoŋere gi polo, rupiri meno kom pa Were,
40005035	kosa gi piny, rupiri meno kaywomo tyende, kosa gi Yerusalem, rupiri meno obedo tindi pa Kere madwoŋ;
40005036	Odoko ikiri ikwoŋere gi wiyin, rupiri ikinyal loko kada yer achiel matar wobedi machol kosa machol wobedi matar;
40005037	Wachi nyaka ni, ‘Ey’ kosa ‘Be’; gima kalo kenyo man m'inowachi meno wok bongi Ŋatarach.
40005038	“Wityeko winjo chango chon paka owach ni, ‘Waŋ chulo kwor gi waŋ, lak bende gi lak.’
40005039	To onyo pama awacho ri win ni: ikiri ichul kwor kwoŋ ŋata timo rin marach. Ka nyatoro ogoyo lembin marachuch g'adhoŋ, weyi wogoyi lembin maracham bende.
40005040	Aka ka nyatoro oterin i kapido ru yenyo sat perin, weyi go woteri kir kot perin bende.
40005041	Aka ka nyatoro oromin wothi mairo achiel, wothi gine mairo aryo.
40005042	Ka dhano okwayin gimoro, miyi go, aka ka nyatoro mito gimoro mochiko chulo, miyi go.
40005043	“Wityeko winjo chango chon paka owach ni, ‘Mari mere perin, aka dakere kodi jakwor perin.’
40005044	To onyo pama awacho ri win ni, mari win jokwor mewin, odoko kwayi win ri joma timo ri win marach,
40005045	aka nyaka wibino bedo nyithindho pa Baa win mani polo; kole go miyo chieŋ pere lyel ri ji marecho kodi mabeyo ma rom, aka go miyo joma beyo gi joma recho jye koth.
40005046	Raŋo ma di wigen ni womiy win kemba ka wimaro ji ma bende jomaro win won kende? Jochoki misolo bende jokitim ameno?
40005047	To ka wimothere wiwegi gi wegi, meno witimoye aŋo mopokere kodi gima ji man jotimo? Jopath bende jokitim ameno?
40005048	Bedi win maleŋ paka Baa win mani polo leŋ.
40006001	“Gwokere win wikiri winyuthi tim mewin mabeyo i waŋi ji ni aka ji jowoneni to jofuoyo win. Ka witimo ameno i dyer ji wikolim kemba bongi Baa win mani polo.
40006002	“Amomiyo ka wimiyo jachandi gimoro, wikiri wiasa nyutho kamaler, paka joma rendere jotimo i kalamo pa Joyudaya kodi i royo mokare i tindi. Jotimo ameno nike ji jowopaki jo. Adyeri awacho ri win, otyek miyo jo kemba pajo mopoŋ.
40006003	To ka ichwayo ri jachandi gimoro, konyi go ma kada mere perin ma kachunyin koŋeyo,
40006004	ŋey wobedi gima nyaliŋliŋ, aka Benin, ma neno gima itimo nyaliŋliŋ, ama bino miyin kemba.
40006005	“Ka ikwayo, ikiri ichale kodi joma jorendere! Jomaro chungo ka jokwayo i kalamo pa Joyudaya kodi i thengi royo mokare ma tindi ŋey dhano jye wonen jo. Adyeri awacho ri win, ameno jotyeko limo kemba pajo kichutho.
40006006	To ka ikwayo, donji i ot perin ichiegi thigo, aka ikway Benin, ma kinenere kamaler. Aka Benin, ma neno gima itimo nyaliŋliŋ bino miyin kemba.
40006007	“I kwayo perin, ikiri ior wach kweth mongoye kony paka jokafiri jotimo; ato joparo ni Were bino winjo jo ru kwayo pajo maboyo.
40006008	Amomiyo wikiri wichale gi jo; kole Baa win mani polo oŋeyo gima wichando kada ma fuodi wikikwayo go.
40006009	Me apaka wiripo kwayo, ‘Bawan mani polo, Nyingin wolwor
40006010	Ker perin wobin, Gima iyenyo wotimere i piny paka timere i polo.
40006011	Miyi waye konon chiemo mawan ma noknok;
40006012	Chwaki ri wan gimarecho mawan; Paka wachwako ri joma timo ri wan marach.
40006013	Ikiri iter wan ka ratem, to bothi wan ayino kwoŋ Ŋatarach, [rupiri ker obedo aperin, kodi men, kodi dwoŋ, chil gi chil.] Ameno.’
40006014	“Kole ka wichwako ri ji recho ma jotimo ri win, Baa win mani polo bende bino chwako win.
40006015	To ka wikichwaki recho pa joman, ameno Baa win mani polo bende kibino chwako ri win recho ma wityeko timo.
40006016	“Aka ka wiriyo kech, wikiri winenere pa wigut paka joma rendere. Ato jonyieko waŋ gin ŋey ji jye jowoŋey nike joriyo kech. Adyeri awacho ri win, ameno jotyeko limo kemba pajo mopoŋ.
40006017	To ka iriyo kech, lwoki waŋin kendo iyiki wiyin,
40006018	aka joman jokiri jowoneni nike iriyo kech; Benin kende ma kinenere kamaler ama bino ŋeyo. Aka Benin, ma neno gima itimo nyaliŋliŋ, ama bino miyin kemba.
40006019	“Wikiri wikan ŋaŋo mewin i piny ka, kama masirigi kodi nyal jobino nyiek'iye, aka jokwo jobino donj'iye to jokwalo woko;
40006020	to kuchiel, kani win ŋaŋo mewin i polo, kama masirigi kodi nyal jokibino nyiek'iye, aka jokwo jokibino donj'iye kwalo.
40006021	Kole kama di ŋaŋo perin ama chunyin bed'iye ndir jye.
40006022	“Waŋ meno tala ma del; ka waŋin olama, delkwoŋin gipi lero bino poŋ'iye;
40006023	to ka waŋin kolama, delkwoŋin bino bedo i mudho. Amomiyo ka lero ma kwoŋin olokere mudho, mudho bino asere marom nedi?
40006024	“Ongoye ŋata nyalo tiyo ri ruodhe aryo; go bino maro achiel to dak man, kosa nyalo tiyo ri achiel to chayo man. Ikinyal tiyo ri Were kodi ri lim bende.
40006025	“Amomiyo awacho ri win gime: wikiri wirembi kwoŋ girachama kodi giramadha ma wiyenyo ma kwo, kosa ruk ri delkwoŋ win. Adyer kwo pa dhano kiloy chiemo, odoko delkwoŋe kiloy ruk?
40006026	Neni win winyin ma joucho malo, jokipidhi kodhi, jokichoki chiemo jokethi i dere, to kole Baa win mani polo kuro jo! To kere win wikiloy winyin no bori?
40006027	Ŋa kwoŋ win ma nyalo medo kiyindira i kwo pere ru rembo ri gikipiny no?
40006028	“To raŋo ma wirembo ri ruk? Neni win thiwi dudi paka jodongo; jokichwer kwok i tich odoko wegi jokitim ruk pajo.
40006029	To awacho ri win kada Solomon, ma chango oŋaŋ moasere, kobedo gi ruk mabeyo paka nyaka achiel kwoŋ thiwi dudi me.
40006030	To k'inen meno apaka Were ruko lum, ma konon nitye to yawere mere thwo tiwaŋo i kendo, go koruki win maloyo kenyo, a ji ma yeyo pajo nok me!
40006031	Amomiyo wikiri wichaki rembo, ka wiwacho ni, ‘Wanocham aŋo?’ kosa ni ‘Wanomadhi aŋo?’ kosa ni ‘Wanoruki aŋo?’
40006032	Kole me a gikipiny ma jokafiri joyenyo hongo jye; aka Baa win mani polo oŋeyo nike wiyenyo gigo jye.
40006033	To kutho rangi win Ker pa Were kodi tiro ma go yenyo, aka go bino miyo win gikipiny me jye.
40006034	Amomiyo wikiri wirembi ri gima dikin; kole kis ndelo won yawere gi wach mere. Kiyenyere medo teko man wi teko ma piny moyawere kelo.
40007001	“Wikiri withum banja ri jowoti win, aka bende Were kothum ri win banja.
40007002	Kwoŋbedo ibino thumo ri win banja i yo achiel ma withumo gine banja ri jowoti win, aka ibino tiyo kwoŋ win gi chik ma witiyo gine kwoŋ jowoti win.
40007003	Amomiyo, raŋo m'iŋiyo nyaka yath mondhilo mani manitye i waŋ omerin, t'ikidew kwoŋ thwon kasik manitye i waŋin won?
40007004	Iere nedi wacho ri omerin ni, ‘Mondo, weyi akwany woko nyaka yath mondhilo no i waŋin,’ mato iwon bende initye gi thwon kasik i waŋin?
40007005	In, jarendirok! Kutho kwanyi woko thwon kongolo kasik i waŋin, aka nyaka ibino neno maber ŋey inokwany woko yath mondhilo i waŋ omerin.
40007006	“Ikiri imiy gwokere gikipiny maleŋ, jobino wire rin to jokayin ayino; kendo ikiri ibol gee mawelo ri mbiji, jobino nyono anyona ayino.
40007007	“Kwayi, aka inolim; rangi, aka inonwaŋ; gudi thigo aka ibino yawo rin.
40007008	Kole dhano jye ma kwayo, limo; aka ŋata rango, nwaŋo, aka ŋata gudo thigo, iyawo ri go.
40007009	Ŋa kwoŋ win bachere ji ka ma di miy wuode tele, ka okwayo mugat?
40007010	Kosa di miy go thwol, ka okwayo rech?
40007011	Kole kada wirecho ameno, wiŋeyo miyo nyithindho mewin gikipiny mabeyo. Aka Baa win mani polo oloy win didi i miyo joma kwayo go, gikipiny mabeyo!
40007012	“Timi win ri jowoti win gima wimito jowotim ri win: me a dwoŋ Chik pa Musa kodi fuonji pa jotuchi wach Were.
40007013	“Donji gi i waŋkach madiny, rupiri waŋkach malach ni gi royo mayot luwo, to tero jo i reyirok, aka joma thoth joluwo royo no.
40007014	Waŋkach madiny ni gi royo matek luwo, to tero jo i kwo, aka ji manok ama jonwaŋo royo no.
40007015	“Gwokere win kwoŋ jotuchi wach matwodo, ma jobino bongi win i chal pa rombo gi woko, to iyadyeri mere jobedo arara i chuny gin.
40007016	Ri ameno wibino ŋeyo jo kwoŋ gimanyak wok i tim pajo. Kudho oryaŋ bende chiene nyak vini? Odoko kudho alwi bende chiene nyak nyandere?
40007017	Kole yath maber nyak gimaber, aka yath marach bende nyak gimarach.
40007018	Yath maber kinyal nyak gimarach, aka yath marach kinyal nyak gimaber.
40007019	Yath jye ma kinyak gimaber itoŋo woko tibolo i mach.
40007020	Amomiyo wibino ŋeyo jotuchi wach matwodo chungo kwoŋ gimanyak ma nenere i tim pajo.
40007021	“Ki dhano jye ma lwoŋan ni, ‘Ruoth, Ruoth,’ ma bino donjo i Ker ma polo, kende ŋata timo gima Baba mani polo yenyo.
40007022	I ndelo no, joma thoth jobino wacho ni, ‘Ruoth, Ruoth, kole watucho mikwenda pa Were i nyingin, waryemo woko jwogi i nyingin aka watimo giraura madongo momore i nyingin!’
40007023	Gikenyo abino wacho ri jo ni, ‘Akuya win, kendo eye win bongan win wijotimi recho me.’
40007024	“Amomiyo dhano jye ma winjo wach paran me aka tiyo gine bino chale gi dhano maryek mogeto ot pere wi tele.
40007025	Koth ochwe, mikula omol, aka asur okudho ot no matek. To ot no kopodho, kwoŋbedo oger wi tele.
40007026	To ŋata winjo wach paran me aka kitiy gine, chalo dhano mamiŋ mogero ot pere i kwoyo.
40007027	Koth ochwe, mikula omol, asur okudho ot no matek, to podho. Podho no oasere marom kune!”
40007028	Munyo Yesu ochowo wacho gime, kweth ji jouro swa kite ma go ofuonjo gine.
40007029	Go onwaŋo kichale kodi jofuonji ma Chik, rupiri go ofuonjo pa ŋata oido ni gi men.
40008001	Munyo Yesu oloro wi got, kweth ji joluwo go.
40008002	Gikenyo jadhowo moro obino bonge, oryewere piny runyime, to wacho ni, “Jadwoŋ ka iyenyo inyalo bothan.”
40008003	Yesu ochwayo chinge to geyo go munyo wacho ni, “Ayenyo, bothi!” Gikenyo dhowo pere ochango i hongo no won.
40008004	To Yesu wacho ri go ni, “Neni! Ikiri iwachi ri nyatoro, to kidhi titir bongi jachwayi ri Were wi alitar, go wokaŋasa in, aka imiy mich ma chowirok ma nyutho dhano jye nike iboth, paka mitere i Or ma Musa ondiko.”
40008005	Munyo Yesu odonjo Kapernaum, jaserikale madwoŋ ma Jaroma oromo gine to kwayo kony ni,
40008006	“Jadwoŋ, jatich paran ni pecho two nyaŋinya i kanindo, kinyal ay, aka nitye i litho madwoŋ swa.”
40008007	Yesu owacho ni, “Abino kidho botho go.”
40008008	Jaserikale odwoko ni, “Be Jadwoŋ, kiripi ran in donjo i ot paran, wachi nyaka wach achiel to jatich paran both.
40008009	Kole abende anitye gi jodongo ma jotelan, aka nitye joserikale ma bende joluwan; ka awacho ri me ni kadhi, to kadho; ri man ni biye, to bino; aka ka aoro jago paran ni, timi gimanyo, to go timo.”
40008010	Yesu ouro munyo owinjo gime, omiyo owacho ri ji monwaŋo joluwo go ni, “Awacho ri win, fuodi akineno kiti yeyo me i nyatoro jye i Israel.
40008011	Poyi win gime! Joma thoth jobino wok yu Wokchieŋ kodi yu Podhochieŋ to jobedo dhower i Ker ma polo kodi Ibrayimu, Isaka, kodi Yakobo.
40008012	To joma oido joripere bedo i Ker ibino bolo jo woko i mudho kama jobino ywak'iye to jomwodo laki gin.”
40008013	Aka Yesu owacho ri jaserikale ni, “Doki pecho, paka iyeyo, gima iyenyo wotimere rin.” Aka jatich pa jaserikale oboth sawa no won.
40008014	Yesu okidho pecho pa Petro, aka kenyo or Petro mobedo min chiege oido ni kanindo kwoŋe oowere.
40008015	Gikenyo go ogeyo chingi dheno, to two weyo go; aka oay malo to chako rweyo go.
40008016	Munyo piny oyutho, ji jokelo bongi Yesu ji ma jwogi ni kwoŋ jo. Yesu oryemo woko jwogi gi wach pere to botho jotwo jye.
40008017	Go otimo ama ma miyo gima jatuchi wach Were Isaya owacho ni, “Go won okwanyo woko nyapo mawan, to tiŋo two mawan,” wotundi i kare.
40008018	Munyo Yesu oneno kweth ji jothoko go, owodho or ni jowopori loka man ma wakawaka.
40008019	Jafuonji ma Chik moro obino bonge to wacho ni, “Jafuonji ayikere kidho kodin kama inochom'iye jye.”
40008020	Yesu odwoko go ni, “Kibwe jonitye gi kero pajo, aka winyin bende jonitye gi odi gin, to Wuodi Dhano ongoye kodi kama go othen'iye wiye.”
40008021	Achiel kwoŋ jafuonjirok pere owacho ni, “Jadwoŋ, weyi kutho akidhi ayiki baba.”
40008022	Yesu odwoko go ni, “Luwan. Weyi jomotho wegi jowoyiki jomotho pajo.”
40008023	Munyo Yesu odonjo i yee, jofuonjirok pere jokadho gi go.
40008024	Piyo piyo no asur madwoŋ obino i wakawaka momiyo pi matula oido umo woko yee aka Yesu oido nindo.
40008025	Jofuonjirok jokidho bonge to jochiewo go ka jowacho ni, “Bothi wan, Ruoth! Wachiegin tho!”
40008026	Yesu odwoko ni, “Wibwok ameno raŋo! Apaka yeyo mewin nok ama!” Gikenyo go oay malo to oro asur kodi wakawaka moido tula kwe; aka gimoro jye okwe maber.
40008027	Dhano jye odhyer. Jowacho ni, “Me kiti dhano manedi? Kir asur kodi kitula pa pi jye winjo go!”
40008028	Munyo Yesu obino i adech ma Gadara, yu loka man ma wakawaka, ji aryo moido jo ni gi jwogi aka jowok i ŋungu miyik'iye ji, joromo gine. Jono oido joger swa, amomiyo ji bin jolworo luwo royo no.
40008029	Piyo piyo no jokoko malo ni, “Iyenyo timo aŋo gi wan, Wuodi Were? Ibino chando wan ma fuodi ndir motire kotundo?
40008030	Chiegin kenyo, oido nitye sidwol mbiji ma chiemo.”
40008031	Gikenyo to jwogi jokwayo Yesu ni, “Ka imito ryemo wan woko, ere dhiri wan i sidwol mbiji no.”
40008032	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Kidhi win.” Gikenyo jowok to jodonjo i sidwol mbiji. Sidwol gi bee oloro piny wok wi tendere to jomunyere i pi.
40008033	Ji monwaŋo jokwayo mbiji joringo to jokidho i tindi, to jowacho ri ji ma kenyo gimoro jye motimere ri joma onwaŋo jwogi ni kwoŋ jo.
40008034	Gino omiyo dhano jye ma tindi owok kidho romo gi Yesu; aka munyo joneno go, jokwayo go ni woeye i adech pajo.
40009001	Yesu odonjo i yee to chiewere gik yu loka man ma wakawaka, to bino i tindi ma thugin won.
40009002	Kenyo, jomogo jokelo ri go dhano moido two nyaŋinya ma jotiŋo wi kitanda. Munyo Yesu oneno kiti yeyo pa jono, owacho ri ŋata two nyaŋinya ni, “Ikiri irembi, wuodan; gimarecho perin ochwak rin.”
40009003	Gikenyo jofuonji ma Chik wegi jowacho kendigin ni, “Ŋat me kole luwo marach kwoŋ Were!”
40009004	Yesu oŋeyo gima oido joparo to wacho ni, “Raŋo ma wiparo gikipiny marecho ameno?
40009005	Mene mayot, wacho ni, ‘Gimarecho perin ochwak rin,’ kosa wacho ni, ‘Ayi malo iwothi?’

40009007	Jalo oay malo to doki pecho.

40009009	Yesu oeye kenyo, aka munyo wotho, oneno jachoki misolo ma nyinge Mathayo obedo piny kama go oido tiyo iye. Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Luwan.” Mathayo oay malo to luwo go.
40009010	Munyo Yesu oido chiemo modyechieŋ i ot pa Mathayo, jochoki misolo mathoth kodi joma recho jobino to jobedo gi Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere dhower.
40009011	Munyo Jofarisayo mogo joneno gime, jowacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Raŋo ma jafuonji mewin chiemo gi jochoki misolo kodi joma recho?”
40009012	Yesu owinjo jo to wacho ni, “Jomolama ama jokiyeny jamilerwa, to joma two ayino ama joyenyo.
40009013	Kidhi win winiaŋ atoŋa momiyo ondik ni, ‘Ayenyo wor ayino, ma kiweno rachow ma lee.’ Kole akibino lwoŋo ji motire, to joma recho ayino.”
40009014	Gikenyo joma luwo Yohana Jakibatisa jobino bongi Yesu gi penji ni, “Raŋo wan kodi Jofarisayo wariyo kech noknok, to jofuonjirok perin jokiriy kada dichiel?”
40009015	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Chiene wendo ma kalima ma nywomirok bende jobedo gi rem ma fuodi jamweha nitye gi jo? Kinyalere! To ndir bino tundo ma ibino kwany'iye woko jamweha bongi jo nyaka to joriyo kech.
40009016	“Ongoye nyatoro ma kwoyo kot moti gi kiremo manyien, rupiri kiremo no leywayo kot to kamoyech medere bedo madwoŋ ayino.
40009017	Odoko ongoye nyatoro ma konjo medho vini manyien i migowa pyendere machon. Ka otimo ameno, pyendere lemwoch woko, to vini oy woko, to pyendere bende nyiekere. Kuchiel, ripere vini manyien wokonji i migowa pyendere manyien, ŋey nyaka gigo jaryo no jye bino kurere maber.”
40009018	Munyo Yesu oido fuodi wacho ri jo gime, jaserikale madwoŋ ma Jayudaya obino bonge, to ryewo chonge piny runyime ka wacho ni, “Nyaran nyaka owok tho won; to biye kethi chingin kwoŋe, aka go bino kwo.”
40009019	Gikenyo Yesu oay malo oluwo go, kanyachiel gi jofuonjirok pere.
40009020	Dhako moro, moido remo madit oy kwoŋe oro apar g'aryo gipi obino yu ŋey Yesu to geyo dhoki nanga pere.
40009021	Dheno owacho gi i chunye ni, “Bedi ayanja agey kada nyaka nanga pere won, d'abedo maber.”
40009022	Yesu owire to neno go to wacho ni, “Ikiri irembi, nyaran! Yeyo perin otyeko bothin.” I hongo no won to dheno bedo maber.
40009023	Gikenyo Yesu okidho i ot pa jaserikale madwoŋ. Aka munyo oneno jokudhi madundo, kodi kweth ji moido joucho, owacho ni,
40009024	“Ngoye win ka wijojye; nyathi ma nyako no kotho, go nindo ayino!” To jono jonyiero go.

40009026	Wach no olak i adech ma piny no gipi.

40009029	Gikenyo go ogeyo waŋ jo aka owacho ni, “Ere, wobedi ameno chungo kwoŋ yeyo mewin!”
40009030	Waŋ jono ochako neno. To Yesu chiko jo teltel ni, “Wikiri wiwachi ri nyatoro.”
40009031	To joeye kenyo munyo jonyayo wach kwoŋ Yesu i adech jye ma piny no.
40009032	Munyo ji oido jokadho, jomogo jokelo ri Yesu obadha ma jwogi oido ni kwoŋe.

40009035	Gikenyo Yesu okidho i tindi jye kodi loka jye. Go ofuonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya munyo tito Wach Maber ma Ker, aka obotho ji kwoŋ kiti two kodi ramirok jye.

40010001	Yesu olwoŋo jofuonjirok pere apar g'aryo kanyachiel to miyo jo men ma ryemo woko chuny mochido kodi ma botho kiti ramirok jye kodi two jye.
40010002	Me a nyingi jomoor apar g'aryo: Marapena Simon (milwoŋo ni Petro) kodi Andereya omin go; Yakobo kodi Yohana omin go, woti Zebedayo;
40010003	Filipo kodi Batholomayo; Thoma kodi Mathayo, jachoki misolo; Yakobo wuodi pa Alfayo kodi Thadeyo;
40010004	Simon ma wok Kana ma jalwenyi ri piny pere; kodi Yuda Iskaryot mochamo sereko ri Yesu.
40010005	Yesu ooro japar g'aryo no gi fuonji me: “Wikiri wikidhi i piny pa Jopath kosa i tindi moro jye ma Samarya,
40010006	kwanyo woko, kidhi win bongi roombo morwenyo ma ot pa Joisrael.
40010007	Kidhi wifuonji ni, ‘Ker ma polo ni chiegin.’
40010008	Bothi win jotwo, chierino win jomotho, lonyi win jodhowo, ryemi win jwogi. Wilimo ma bu chul, amomiyo bende miyi win ji ma bu chul.
40010009	Wikiri witiŋ zawabu kada feza, kosa dome moro i migowa mewin.
40010010	Wikiri witiŋ migowa ma kwach i woth mewin, kosa sat man, kosa war, kosa luth. Jatich ripo limo gima go tiyo rigo.
40010011	“Ka witundo i tindi kosa loka moro, donji win aka wirangi ŋata yeyo jolo win, aka wibedi gi go chuka winoeye kenyo.
40010012	Ka widonjo i ot, mothi win jo ni, ‘Syem wobedi kodi win.’
40010013	Ka ji ma kenyo jojolo win, weyi syem mewin wodoŋi kenyo; to ka jokojolo win, syem mewin wodwoki ri win.
40010014	Aka ka nyatoro kojolo win, kosa okwero chiko ithe ri win, ka wiwok pecho no kosa i tindi no, witeŋ woko fukefuke ma tyendi win.
40010015	Adyeri awacho ri win, ndelo ma thumo banja bino bedo marach ri tindi no loyo Sodom kodi Gomora.
40010016	“Neni win! Onyo adhiro win paka roombo i dyer arara. Wiripo bedo maryek pa thwol odoko mamwol pa akuru.
40010017	Kure win, rupiri ji jobino mako win to jotero win i kapido, aka jobino chwado win i kalamo pa Joyudaya.
40010018	Ibino tero win bongi jodhum madongo kodi kerin kwoŋ bedo an, ŋey wititi Wach Maber ri jo kodi ri Jopath bende.
40010019	Ka oter win kapido, wikiri wirembi gima wibino wacho kosa paka winoluw. Ato ibino miyo win gima winowachi.
40010020	Kole wach ma winowachi kobedi mewin; to bino wok bongi Chuny pa Baa win ma bino luwo i win.
40010021	“Omin dhano won ama bino tero omin go woneki, aka bachere bende jobino timo ameno ri nyithindho pajo; nyithindho bende jobino wire ri jonywol pajo to jomiyo ineko jo.
40010022	Dhano jye bino mon gi win, kwoŋbedo an. To ŋata ochir chuka gike bino both.
40010023	Aka ka ilwenyo gi win i tindi achiel, ringi win i man. Awacho ri win, wikochow tich mewin i tindi jye ma Israel ma fuodi Wuodi Dhano kobino.
40010024	“Ongoye jafuonjirok ma loyo jafuonji pere gi dwoŋ, aka ŋecha bende kiloy ruoth pere gi dwoŋ.
40010025	Ripo ka jafuonjirok odongo to chale kodi jafuonji pere, kendo ŋecha bende wochale gi ruoth pere. Aka kotyek lwoŋo won pecho ni Belzebul, kosa to joma ni pecho pere olwoŋ jo gi nyingijo marecho manedi!
40010026	“Amomiyo, wikiri wilwor ji. Ongoye gimoro jye moum ma koyaw, kosa nyaliŋliŋ moro jye ma kothangi kamaler.
40010027	Gima onyo awacho ri win i mudho wiripo medo wacho odyechieŋ. Aka gima wiwinjo omwoŋ liŋliŋ wiripo wacho gi i tipin wiy ot.
40010028	Wikiri wilwor joma neko del to jokinyal neko chuny; to lwori win Ŋat ma nyalo nyieko woko kwo madel kodi chuny jye i mach makitho.
40010029	Obicho aryo kinyew nyaka siringi achiel be? To kada achiel kwoŋ jo kinyal podho piny ma Baa win koŋeyo.
40010030	Aka kole kir yewiy win jye otyek kwano.
40010031	Amomiyo wikiri wibedi malwor; welo mewin loyo apa obicho kweth.
40010032	“Ŋata otuchan i dyer ji nike go ŋata luwan, abende abino tucho nyinge ameno i nyim Baba mani polo.
40010033	To ŋata okwedere kwoŋan i dyer ji nike go kobedo aparan, abende abino kwedere kwoŋe i nyim Baba mani polo.
40010034	“Wikiri wipar nike abino kelo syem i piny; be, akibino kelo syem, to abor ayino.
40010035	Abino thuyo woti ji gi bachere pajo, nyigi ji gi megi jo, mondiwoti ji kodi adhachere pajo;
40010036	jakwor pa dhano bino bedo joma ot pere won.
40010037	“Ŋata omari bamere kosa yokimere loyan koripi bedo aparan, odoko bende ŋata omari wuode kosa nyare loyan koripi bedo aparan.
40010038	Moro jye ma kotiŋ musalaba pere to luwan koripi bedo aparan.
40010039	Ŋata won otemi gwoko kwo pere bino rwenyo woko, to ŋata oboli woko kwo pere kwoŋbedo an, bino limo.
40010040	“Ŋata jolo win, meno jolan, aka ŋata jolan meno jolo ŋata ooran.
40010041	Ŋata jolo jamikwenda pa Were rupiri go jamikwenda bino limo kemba machale g'apa jamikwenda. Ŋata jolo dhano maleŋ rupiri go leŋ, bino limo kemba pa ŋataleŋ.
40010042	Aka adyeri awacho ri win, ŋata omiyi achiel kwoŋ nyithindho ma joluwan me kada nyaka pi maŋich rupiri go obedo ŋata luwan, ŋato kibino keŋ kemba pere.”
40011001	Munyo Yesu ochowo fuonjo jofuonjirok pere apar g'aryo, oeye kenyo to kidho fuonji gi tito Wach Maber i tindin ma chiegin gi kenyo.
40011002	Aka munyo Yohana Jakibatisa owinjo gi i twech kwoŋ tich pa Kristo, ooro jofuonjirok pere megi bonge.
40011003	Jopenjo Yesu ni, “Wachi ri wan, in a ŋata owach nike lebino kosa wakur ŋat man?”
40011004	Yesu odwoko ni, “Giki wiwachi ri Yohana gima pama wiwinjo kodi ma wineno.
40011005	Joma waŋ gin otho joneno, jomoŋol jowotho, jodhowo jolony, joma ithi gin otho jowinjo, aka jomotho ichierino jo, aka ifuonjo jochandi Wach Maber.
40011006	Jasilwany a ŋata kibedi gi kiganagana kwoŋan!”
40011007	Munyo jofuonjirok pa Yohana joay jodok, Yesu oluwo ri kweth ji kwoŋ Yohana ni, “Munyo wikidho both Yohana i thim, onwaŋo wigeno neno aŋo? Midole ma koyo yengo?
40011008	To aŋo won ma wikidho yu koro neno? Neno dhano morukere i nengin mabeyo mayomi? Kole joma ruko nengin mayom no jonwaŋere i udi pa kerin ayino.
40011009	To yagi, aŋo won motero win korago? Neno jatuchi wach Were? Adyeri awacho ri win, go loyo kir jatuchi wach Were.
40011010	Me a ŋata ondik kwoŋe ni, ‘Eno adhiro jamikwenda paran yu wiyin, ma bino yiko rin royo.’
40011011	Adyeri awacho ri win, kwoŋ woti mon jye, ongoye motyeko yudhere malo i dwoŋ loyo Yohana Jakibatisa. Kuchiel, kada ŋata oasa thin i Ker ma polo jye loyo go gi dwoŋ.
40011012	Wok i ndir pa Yohana Jakibatisa chuka tundo konon, otyek mwonjo Ker ma polo gi maker, aka ji ma jomaker jodonj'iye gi mbaka.
40011013	Ato jotuchi wach Were jye kodi Chik pa Musa, joluwo kwoŋ Ker pa Were tundo ndir pa Yohana;
40011014	aka ka wiyeyo gima awacho, go ama obino paka Eliya monwaŋo ripo bino.
40011015	Ŋata ni gi ithe wowinji!
40011016	“To onyo anopima luse ji ma pama g'aŋo? Jochalo nyithindho ma jo ni dyer kisya. Bwora achiel koko ri nyawote ni,
40011017	‘Wakudho ri win madundo mamit, to wikwero myel! Wawero ri win wer tho, to wikwero ywak!’
40011018	Neni Yohana obino ma riyo kech aka kimedhi, to jowacho ni, ‘Nigi jwogi kwoŋe.’
40011019	Onyo wuodi Dhano obino ma chiemo aka oro giramadha, to jowacho ni, ‘Panen jaworo ma jamadhi vini, jawodhi jochoki misolo kodi joma recho!’ Kuchiel ryeko pa Were ineno adyeri mere chungo kwoŋ tim ma wok'iye.”
40011020	Gikenyo Yesu ochako kwoŋo tindin ma go oasa tim'iye giraura rupiri ji jokoŋuto gimarecho pajo.
40011021	“Kidamba otundi ri win, Korazin! Kodi Bethsaida! Kole bedi giraura motim i win tim i Tire kodi Sidon, di ji ma kenyo joruko kutya, to jobukere gi buru ma nyutho ni joŋuto gimarecho pajo.
40011022	To awacho ri win, ndelo ma thumo banja bino bedo ma dhey ye ri Tire kodi Sidon loyo ri win.
40011023	Aka in, Kapernaum, oido imito wotiŋin malo kir i polo? Ilebolin i piny pa jomotho ayino. Ato bedi giraura motyek timo rin tim i Sodom ayin, kole di Sodom fuodi nitye kir konon.
40011024	To awacho rin, i ndelo ma thumo banja Sodom bino limo girachula ma dhey ye loyin.”
40011025	I hongo no Yesu owacho kamaler ni, “Afuoyin Baba, Ruoth ma polo gi piny, rupiri ipano gikipiny me ri joma ryek kodi jomofuonjere tiwodho kamaler ri nyithindho ayino.
40011026	Ey, Baba, kole ama apaka chunyin osangala ni wotimere.
40011027	Baba otyeko miyan gimoro jye, aka onyo ongoye ŋatoŋeyo Wuode kwanyo woko Bamere, kendo ongoye ŋat'oŋeyo Bamere kwanyo woko Wuode kodi joma Wuode odyero nyutho jo kamaler.
40011028	Biye win bongan wijojye ma wiol aka wilachere i tiŋo byeto mapek, lebino miyo win ywomirok.
40011029	Byeli win okol paran i ŋuti win aka wifuonjere kwoŋan; kole abedo moth aka abwonere iyi adundo paran; aka wibino nwaŋo ywomirok i chuny win.
40011030	Kole okol paran yot aka byeto paran sew.”
40012001	Munyo hongo moro okadho, Yesu oluwo gi i ndelin ma ŋano; jofuonjirok pere oido jowinjo kech, to jochako fuono withi ŋano gi chamo.
40012002	To munyo Jofarisayo joneno, jowacho ri go ni, “Panen, kole jofuonjirok perin jotimo gima koyey timo i Sabato.”
40012003	Go owacho ri jo ni, “Fuodi wikisoma gima Daudi otimo, kodi joma oido nigi go;
40012004	paka go odonjo i ot pa Were to jochamo mugat momiy Were moido kiripi ni go kosa joma oido ni gine jowochami, kwanyo woko jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kende?
40012005	Kosa fuodi wikisoma i Chik pa Musa, paka kis ndelo ma Sabato jochwayi ri Were wi alitar ma Ot pa Were joturo chik ma Sabato, to kikwan ri jo recho?
40012006	Awacho ri win, kole gimadwoŋ ma kalo Ot pa Were ni ka.
40012007	Aka bedi wityeko ŋeyo dwoŋ wach me ni, ‘Ayenyo wor ayino ma kiweno rachow ma lee’, d'onyo wikithum banja ri jomongoye gi recho moro.
40012008	Kole Wuodi Dhano obedo Ruoth ma Sabato.”
40012009	Yesu oeye kenyo to kidho donjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya moro,
40012010	kama onwaŋ'iye dhano ma chinge otho. To jopenjo go ni, “Chik yeyo botho dhano i Sabato?” Jopenjo ameno ni aka ŋey jowokethi kwoŋe recho.
40012011	To go owacho ri jo ni, “Ŋa kwoŋ win ma ka rombo pere achiel opodho i bur i ndelo ma Sabato weyo kenyo ma kofudho woko?
40012012	Onyo welo dhano kalo apa rombo kadidi? Ri ameno kitur Chik timo gimaber i Sabato.”
40012013	Gikenyo owacho ri jal ma chinge otho no ni, “Ryeyi chingin!” To jalo ryeyo chinge no to bende lokere maber paka nyawote ma kuchiel.
40012014	Gikenyo Jofarisayo joay jokadho to jotimo chan ma neko Yesu.
40012015	Munyo Yesu oŋeyo gino, oeye kenyo. Ji mathoth joluwo go, to botho jotwo jye,
40012016	aka omiyo jo or ni kiri jowowachi ri joman kwoŋ go.
40012017	Owach ameno ŋey gima jatuchi wach Were Isaya owacho wotundi ni:
40012018	“Panen jatich paran ma atyeko yero ma amaro aka chunyan sangala gine. Abino ketho Chuny Maleŋ paran i go, aka go bino tucho tiro ri nonin jye.
40012019	Go kibino pyemo kosa koko, kosa luwo malo i royo mokakere ma tindi.
40012020	Go kibino turo midole mokom, kosa neko tala maliel ma nimnim. Go bino riwin chuka omiyi tiro oloyi lweny.
40012021	Nonin jye jobino ketho geno pajo i nyinge.”
40012022	Gikenyo jomogo jokelo ri Yesu obadha ma waŋe otho aka oido kinyal luwo ru jwogi moido ni kwoŋe. Yesu obotho ŋato to nyalo luwo kir gi neno.
40012023	Kweth ji jodhyer swa, to jowacho ni, “Kosa me nyalo bedo Nyakwar Daudi?”
40012024	To munyo Jofarisayo jowinjo gime jodwoko ni, “Go ryemo woko jwogi gi men pa Belzebul, ruoth pa jwogi.”
40012025	Yesu oŋeyo gima oido joparo to wacho ri jo ni, “Piny moro jye ma tyakere bwora gi bwora aka wegi jolwenyo, bino podho.
40012026	Amomiyo ka Sitan oere ryemo woko Sitan i ker pa jwogi dwoŋ mere ni won otyeko kelo tyakirok, onyo ker pere ochungi nedi?
40012027	K'inen aryemo woko jwogi gi men pa Belzebul, kere onyo men pa ŋa ma joma luwo win joryemo gine jo? Amomiyo joma luwo win won ama jobino thumo banja woloyi win!
40012028	To k'inen aryemo woko jwogi gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ, nyutho ni kere onyo Ker pa Were otyeko tundo bongi win.
40012029	“Ongoye ŋata nyalo turo ot pa jameni to nyaga lim pere, kwanyo woko ka okutho otweyo jameni no aka ŋey wonyali kinyaga gima ni ot pere.
40012030	“Ŋata kitiyere kodan meno lwenyo kodan, aka adyeri ŋata kikonyan gi choko gikipiny, meno kedho woko ayino.
40012031	Amomiyo awacho ri win, ibino chwako ri ji recho kodi gima kotire ma joluwi kwoŋ Were; to ŋata oluwi gima kotire kwoŋ Chuny Maleŋ, kibin chwako go i hongo ma pama kir gi i mabino yuwaŋe jye.
40012032	Moro jye ma luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Wuodi Dhano ibino chwako go, to ŋata oluwi gima kotire kwoŋ Chuny Maleŋ kibin chwako go, pama kendo gi i kare mabino jye.
40012033	“Ka iyenyo olemo maber, iripo bedo gi tyendi yath olemo bende maber; to ka ini gi tyendi yath marach, bende ibino nwaŋo olemo marach. Kole bero pa yath iŋeyo kwoŋ gimanyak kwoŋe.
40012034	Win nyithindhi thwole! Di winyal luwo nedi wach maber mato wirecho? Kole wach ma dhano luwo meno gima opoŋ i chunye.
40012035	Dhano maber wodho gikipiny mabeyo wok kwoŋ gikipiny mabeyo mopoŋ i chunye; aka dhano marach bende wodho gikipiny marecho wok kwoŋ recho mopoŋ i chunye.
40012036	“Aka awacho ri win, i ndelo ma thumo banja, dhano jye bino tito wach jye masisiri ma go otyeko luwo.
40012037	Kole wach perin ama nyalo miyo ikwanyo woko kwoŋin banja, kosa iketho kwoŋin banja.”
40012038	Gikenyo jofuonji ma Chik mogo kodi Jafarisayo joluwo malo ni, “Jafuonji wayenyo neno ranyuth m'itimo.”
40012039	Yesu odwoko ni, “Luse ji marecho ma kigenere i waŋ Were ama kwayo ranyuth. Ongoye ranyuth m'ilemiyo win kwanyo woko apa Yona jatuchi wach Were.
40012040	Paka Yona ochowo odyechieŋ adek kodi wor adek i iyi rech, apaka bende Wuodi Dhano bino chowo odyechieŋ adek gi wor adek i iyi lowo.
40012041	I ndelo ma thumo banja, ji ma Nineve jobino chungo gi luse ji ma pama to jothumo banja loyo jo, rupiri joŋuto gimarecho pajo munyo jowinjo Yona fuonjo; to kole ŋat ma loyo Yona gi dwoŋ ee ni ka!
40012042	I ndelo ma thumo banja kere ma dhako ma wok Sheba i thenge ma yu Tyendi piny bino chungo to thumo banja woloyi win, rupiri go owotho othoko piny wok kama bor bino winjo ryeko pa Solomon; aka kole ŋat ma loyo Solomon gi dwoŋ ee ni ka!
40012043	“Ka chuny mochido owok kwoŋ dhano, wotho i piny mothwo ka rango kabedo maywomirok to kinwaŋ.
40012044	Ri ameno ka konyalo nwaŋo, won wacho ni, ‘Abino gik i ot paran ma awok'iye.’ Ka odwoko to nwaŋo ot no ni nono kendo olony aka oyik maber,
40012045	gikenyo go lewok to kidho kelo chuny mochido wadi man abiryo marecho loyo go, to jobino donjo gi bedo kenyo. Kwo pa ŋato bino lokere marach loyo paka onwaŋo nitye chon. Meno apaka bino timere ri ji marecho ma pama.”
40012046	Munyo Yesu fuodi oido luwo gi ji, min kodi wutimin jotundo. Jochungo woko, aka jokwayo luwo gi go.
40012047	Ri ameno ŋatachiel moido ni kenyo owacho ri go ni, “Panen, yokin kodi wutimerin jochungo woko, aka jomito luwo kodin.”
40012048	Yesu odwoko ni, “Ŋa ma yokan? Jokune ma wutimera?”
40012049	Gikenyo go ochimo jofuonjirok pere to wacho ni, “Panen! Jome a mama gi wutimera!
40012050	Kole ŋata timo gima Baba mani polo yenyo wotimi, meno ama obedo omera, nyamera, gi yokan.”
40013001	I ndelo no won, Yesu owok i ot to kidho i thengi wakawaka kama go obed'iye piny wofuonji ji.
40013002	Paka muma ji mothoko go onwaŋo oasa dwoŋ, go odonjo i yee to bed'iye, kareno ji jye jochungo i thengi pi.
40013003	Go ooro agechin munyo luwo ri jo kwoŋ gikipiny madit ama: “Onwaŋo nitye dhano mokidho chwoyo.
40013004	Munyo go bayo kodhi i ndelo, megi opodho i thengi yo to winyin jobino to jochamo woko.
40013005	Megi opodho i lowo ma wi tele, kama lowo oido rep'iye. Kodhi no okwako twi, rupiri lowo oido rep.
40013006	Aka munyo chieŋ olyel, gimotwi no oner woko; odoko paka tyendi gimotwi no onwaŋo fuodi kodonjo bor i lowo, gino jye othwo woko mayot.
40013007	Kodhi megi opodho i kudhin, to kudhin no dongo to diyo woko gimotwi no.
40013008	To kodhi megi podho i lowo ma diwa, to nyak: megi nyinge miya achiel, megi pyero auchiel, megi pyero adek.”
40013009	Gikenyo to Yesu wacho ni, “Ŋata ni gi ithe wowinji!”

40013011	Yesu odwoko ni, “Ryeko ma nyaliŋliŋ ma Ker ma polo omiy win, to komiy jo.
40013012	Kole dhano ma nitye gi gimoro ibino medo go man to bedo kodi gima kalo ma go yenyo, to ŋata ongoye gi gimoro ibino kwanyo woko kwoŋe kada nyaka mathin ma go oido ni gine.
40013013	Me ama omiyo aoro agechin ka aluwo gi jo, rupiri joŋiiyo to jokineen, jochiko ithi gin to jokiwinji, odoko jokiniaŋ dwoŋ mere.
40013014	Amomiyo wach pa Isaya jatuchi wach Were otundo i kare ni, ‘Adyeri wibino chiko ithi win, to wikoniaŋ; odoko wibino ŋiiyo, to wikoniaŋ dwoŋ gima wineno.
40013015	Rupiri chuny jome olokere manwaŋ, ithi gin onyo kiwinji, aka waŋ gin jomiyo woko Kole waŋ gin d'onyalo neno odoko ithi gin d'onyalo winjo, kendo paro pajo d'onyalo niaŋ dwoŋ wach to jogik bongan, aka ameno d'abotho jo.’
40013016	To win wijosilwany swa! Waŋ win neno aka ithi win winjo.
40013017	Adyeri awacho ri win! Jotuchi wach Were mathoth kodi ji pa Were mathoth chango joyenyo swa neno gima wineno, to jokonyalo neno, kodi winjo gima wiwinjo, to jokonyalo winjo.
40013018	“Onyo chiki win ithi win aka wifuonjere dwoŋ agecha pa jachwoyo.
40013019	Ka nyatoro winjo mikwenda kwoŋ Ker to kiniaŋ dwoŋ mere, jwogi bino to mayo go woko gima onwaŋo ochwoy i adundo pere; me a kodhi mopodho i thengi royo.
40013020	Kodhi mopodho i lowo ma wi tele nyutho joma jolo mikwenda gi kisangala tekin jowinjo.
40013021	To wach no kirochi i chuny jo. Amomiyo ka teko kosa chandirok moro obino ru wach no, jonyochere piyo.
40013022	Kodhi mopodho i kudhin nyutho joma winjo mikwenda, to rembo ri kwo ma piny kodi maro ŋaŋo, diyo wach no piny to lokere gima kinyak.
40013023	Aka kodhi mochwoy i lowo ma diwa nyutho joma winjo mikwenda to joniaŋ dwoŋ mere; jonyak gimabeyo, megi miya achiel, megi pyero auchiel, megi pyero adek.”
40013024	Yesu oluwo ri jo i agecha man ama: “Ker ma polo chalo dhano mochwoyo kodhi maber i ndelo pere.
40013025	Obedo wor achiel, munyo dhano jye oido nindo, jakwor obino to chwoyo weeyo i dyer ŋano no, to kadho.
40013026	Munyo gima ochwoy odongo to chako ŋok, weeyo bende to nenere.
40013027	Jotich pere jobino bonge to jowacho ni, ‘Jadwoŋ, kole ichwoyo kodhi maber i ndelo perin; to weeyo odoko owok yu kune?’
40013028	Go odwoko ni, ‘Jakwor moro am'otimo ameno.’ To jopenjo go ni, ‘Iyenyo wakidhi wafudhi woko weeyo no?’
40013029	Go odwoko ni, ‘Be, rupiri ka wiero choko weeyo no winyalo fudho gi ŋano bende.
40013030	To weyi kutho jojye jowodongi kanyachiel chuka ndelo ma kecho otundi, aka anowachi ri joma kecho ni: kutho fudhi win woko weeyo witwey kanyachiel i wich ma bolere i mach, ŋey gikenyo nyaka wichoki ŋano to wiketho i dero paran.’ ”
40013031	Yesu oluwo ri jo i agecha man ama: “Ker ma polo chalo kodhi kalantus, moasa thin kwoŋ kodhi man jye;
40013032	dhano kwanyo to pidho i ndelo pere, aka ka otyeko dongo loyo gimatwi jye gi dwoŋ. Go lokere yath ma winyin jobino to jogero odi gin i jange.”
40013033	Yesu odoko oluwo ri jo i agecha man ama: “Ker ma polo chalo thow ma dhako nyalo kwanyo to ruwo gi moko i nywero chuka moko gipi yenyo.”
40013034	Yesu oluwo ri muma ji i agechin i gikipiny mowach me jye; go kowacho gimoro ri ji ma kooro agecha.
40013035	Go otimo ameno ma miyo gima jatuchi wach Were owacho wotundi i kare ni, “Abino oro agechin ka aluwo gi jo, abino wacho ri jo gima oido opanere wok i chwech pa piny.”
40013036	Gikenyo Yesu oeye bongi muma ji to donjo i ot. Jofuonjirok pere jobino bonge to jowacho ni, “Tuchi ri wan dwoŋ agecha ma weeyo mani i ndelo.”
40013037	Yesu odwoko ni, “Ŋata ochwoyo kodhi maber, meno Wuodi Dhano;
40013038	ndelo, meno piny me; kodhi maber meno nyithidho ma Ker pa Were; weeyo meno nyithidho pa jwogi;
40013039	aka jakwor mochwoyo weeyo meno jwogi won. Ndelo ma kecho meno giki ndir, aka jokecho meno jomalaika.
40013040	Aka paka weeyo ichoko aka iwaŋo i mach, apaka bende bino bedo i hongo ma giki ndir:
40013041	Wuodi Dhano bino oro jomalaika bino choko wok i ker pere gimoro jye ma miyo ji timo gimarach, kodi joma recho jye,
40013042	to jobolo jo i kendo madwoŋ ma mach, kama jobino ywak'iye kareno jokayo laki gin.
40013043	Aka joma jotire jobino lyel pa mach i Ker pa Baa jo. Amomiyo winji win ka winitye gi ithi win!
40013044	“Ker ma polo chalo ŋaŋo mopan i ndelo. Dhano moro ochombo kwoŋe, gikenyo to umo kendo. Go odok gi kisangala momiyo go okidho to tana woko gikipiny man jye ma go oido ni gine, to gik nyiewo ndelo no.
40013045	“Ker ma polo bende chalo janyiew ma rango gee mawelo.
40013046	Ka go onwaŋo mawelo tektek, go kidho to tana woko gikipiny man jye ma go oido ni gine, to gik nyiewo gee no.
40013047	“Ker ma polo bende chalo bwoo ma jokitoga jobolo i wakawaka, to jomako rech ma nger jye.
40013048	Ka otyeko poŋ, jokitoga joywayo wi geŋin i thengi pi to jobedo piny poko rech: mabeyo mere iketho i kibumbulu, aka mongoye kony mere ibolo woko.
40013049	Meno apaka bende bino bedo i ndelo ma rumachien: jomalaika jolebino to jokwanyo woko joma recho bongi jomotire,
40013050	to jobolo jo i kendo madwoŋ ma mach. Kenyo jobino ywak'iye kareno jokayo laki gin.”
40013051	Yesu openjo jo ni, “Winiaŋ dwoŋ gikipiny me?” Jodwoko ni, “Ey.”
40013052	Gikenyo go odwoko ni, “Amomiyo, jafuonji jye ma Chik motyek fuonjo go kwoŋ Ker ma polo, chale gi won pecho ma wodho gikipiny machon kodi manyien jye wok i dero pere.”
40013053	Munyo Yesu ochowo wacho agechin me, oeye kenyo,
40013054	to gik i tindi pajo. Go ofuonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya, aka joma jowinjo fuonji pere jodhyer swa. Jopenjo ni, “Go onwaŋo kune ryeko me kodi men ma timo giraura?
40013055	Me won kobedo wuodi pa japachi? Yokimere ki Marya, aka Yakobo, Yozefu, Simon, kodi Yuda meno ki wutimin go?
40013056	Nyimin go jye jokinitye ka gi wani? Go onwaŋo gime jye kune?”
40013057	Gikenyo jokwero go. Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Jatuchi wach Were imiyo dwoŋ iye jye kwanyo woko i tindi pajo won kodi i pecho pajo won.”
40013058	Go kotimo giraura madit kenyo kwoŋbedo onwaŋo jongoye gi yeyo.
40014001	I ndir ma Herode oido obedo ruoth ma Galileya, owinjo kwoŋ Yesu.
40014002	Go wacho ri joserikale pere ni, “Me Yohana Jakibatisa won ama ochierino, amomiyo men ma timo giraura me nitye i go.”
40014003	Ato Herode ama ndir cha owodho or ni womaki Yohana wotwey, tiketho go i ka twech. Go otimo ameno ru wach pa Herodya, chipa omin go milwoŋo ni Filipo,
40014004	rupiri Yohana omena wacho ri Herode ni, “Kobedo gimotire bedo gi dhako no!”
40014005	Herode oyenyo neko go to oido lworo Joyudaya, rupiri oido jotero Yohana paka jatuchi wach Were.
40014006	I ndelo ma poyo nywolirok pa Herode, nyapa Herodya omyelo i nyim wendo gi bee. Herode osangala gine swa,
40014007	momiyo ochiko nyano ni, “Akwoŋere nike abino miyin gimoro jye m'inokwayan!”
40014008	Paka yokimere omiyo go ryeko, go okwayo ni, “Miyan wich Yohana Jakibatisa i sen ka!”
40014009	Kere ogut, to ru kwoŋirok pere ma go oido otyeko timo i nyim wendo pere gi bee, go owodho or nike gima nyano oyenyo womiy go.
40014010	Ameno go ooro ji kidho ŋondo wich Yohana i katwech.
40014011	Wich no okel i ot i sen timiyo nyano to tero bothi yokimere.
40014012	Jofuonjirok pa Yohana jobino, jokwanyo delkwoŋe, to joyiko aka jokidho to jowacho ri Yesu.
40014013	Munyo Yesu owinjo wach no, oeye kenyo gi yee to kidho kakende. Munyo ji jowinjo gino, joluwo go wok i tindin pajo.
40014014	Yesu owok i yee, aka munyo oneno kweth ji, omako wor i chunye gi jo, to botho jotwo pajo.
40014015	Othyeno no, jofuonjirok pere jokidho bonge to jowacho ni, “Kole piny otyeko yutho, aka ka dyer thim. Sewila ji jowokidhi loka jowonyiew chiemo.”
40014016	Yesu odwoko ni, “Jokiripi eye ka. Wiwegi miyi win jo chiemo moro jowochami.”
40014017	Jodwoko ni, “Gima wanitye gine ka obedo nyaka mugat abich kodi rech aryo kende.”
40014018	Yesu owacho ni, “Keli gino jye bongan ka.”
40014019	Gikenyo ooro ji bedo piny i lum, aka okwanyo mugat abich gi rech aryo no, oŋiyo malo i polo, to fuoyo Were. Go oturo mugat no to miyo jofuonjirok, aka jofuonjirok jokwanyo to jopoko ji.
40014020	Dhano jye ochiemo to yeŋ. Rumachien jofuonjirok jochoko ŋinjeŋinje modoŋ to poŋo aditin apar g'aryo.
40014021	Welo chwo ma jochiemo onwaŋo romo chiegin gana abich, ma kokwan mon gi nyithidho.
40014022	Gikenyo Yesu omiyo jofuonjirok pere donjo i yee jowoteli kidho ri go yu loka ma kocha ma wakawaka, ka fuodi go won oido sewila ji.
40014023	Munyo otyeko kisewila ji, go okutho oidho wi got kende kwayo. Munyo piny otundo othyeno, Yesu oido ni kenyo kende,
40014024	kareno yee otundo bor i wakawaka lwenyo gi pi ma tula, aka asur oido kudho wok yu wiye.
40014025	I dyer sawa abuŋwen kodi apar g'aryo modikini, Yesu obino bongi jo munyo wotho wi pi.
40014026	Munyo jofuonjirok joneno go wotho wi pi, lworo omako jo. Jowacho ni, “Manago yamo!” To jokoko gi lworo.
40014027	Piyo piyo no to Yesu luwo gi jo munyo wacho ni, “Wikiri wirembi, me an. Wikiri wilwor.”
40014028	Gikenyo Petro oluwo malo ni, “Ruoth, ka meno in adyeri, oran awoki abin bongin wi pi.”
40014029	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Biye”, to Petro wok i yee to wotho wi pi munyo kidho bongi Yesu.
40014030	To tekin go neno asur, lworo omako go to chako munyirok i pi. Gikenyo go okoko ni, “Ruoth! Bothan!”
40014031	Yesu ochwayo chinge mayot to mako go munyo wacho ni, “Ijayeyo mathin. Raŋo ma iganagana?”
40014032	Aka munyo jotyeko donjo i yee to asur kwe.
40014033	Joma onwaŋo ni yee jolamo go ka jowacho ni, “Adyeri, in i Wuodi Were.”
40014034	Jochiewere aka jotundo loka ma Genesaret.

40014036	Jokwayo go nike woyeyi jotwo jowogeyi kada nyaka dhoki nanga pere won; aka joma jogeyo go jye jobedo maber.
40015001	To Jofarisayo megi gi jofuonji ma Chik jobino bongi Yesu wok Yerusalem to jo penjo go ni,
40015002	“Iraŋo jofuonjirok perin jochayo kula pa kwarere mawan? Jokilogi chingi gin paka mitere ka jokidho chiemo!”
40015003	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “To iraŋo ma wichayo Or pa Were to wiluwo kula mewin wiwegi?
40015004	Kole Were owacho ni, ‘Wori benin gi yokin’, aka, ‘Ŋata yeto bamere kosa yokimere ibino neko.’
40015005	To win wifuonjo ni ka nyatoro owacho ri bamere kosa yokimere ni, ‘Kony moro jye ma d'amiyin onyo obedo mich moyik ri Were ayin’, gikenyo go onyo kiripi woro bamere kosa yokimere.
40015006	Me apaka wilwogo woko Or pa Were, kareno wiluwo fuonji mewin wiwegi.
40015007	Win wijorendirok! Isaya otucho wach ma mako kwoŋ win me motire ni,
40015008	‘Ji me jomiyan dwoŋ gi dhoki gin kende, to chuny gin ni bor kodan!
40015009	Ongoye kony ri jo laman, kwoŋbedo jofuonjo or mobedo apa dhanadhana.’ ”
40015010	Gikenyo Yesu olwoŋo kweth ji bonge to wacho ri jo ni, “Chiki win ithi win, aka winiaŋi!
40015011	Gima donjo i dhoki dhano ama kiloki go makoch: to gima wok i dhoke ama loko go makoch.”
40015012	Gikenyo jofuonjirok pere jobino bonge to jowacho ni, “Iŋeyo paka Jofarisayo chuny gin oramo jo i gima iwacho no?”
40015013	Yesu odwoko ni, “Gimoro jye ma twi ma Baba mani polo ama kopidho ibino fudho woko.
40015014	Weyi ri win jo! Jobedo jotel ma waŋ gin otho; aka ka jathowaŋ achiel ama kodo jathowaŋ man, jaryo jye jopodho i bur.”
40015015	Petro oluwo malo ni, “Titi ri wan dwoŋ agecha me.”
40015016	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Kere wibende fuodi wikiniaŋ gimoro?
40015017	Wikiniaŋ ni gimoro jye ma donjo i dhoki dhano donjo i iye, aka kadho akadha to wok woko?
40015018	To gikipiny ma wok i dhoki dhano wok i chunye; gikipiny ma chalo ameno ama loko dhano makoch.
40015019	Ato i adundo ama wok'iye paro marecho ma rwako go i nek, timo chot, kodi kidakana, kwo, rooro, gi nyieko nyingi joman.
40015020	Me a gikipiny ma loko dhano makoch. To chiemo ma kologi chingi jo paka jowacho ni iripo timo no ama kiloki dhano makoch.”
40015021	Yesu oeye kenyo to kadho i adech ma chiegin gi tindi ma Tire kodi Sidon.
40015022	Dhako Jakanan moro ma wok i adech no obino bonge to ywakere ni, “Nyakwar Daudi, timi reye wor! Nyaran jwogi ni kwoŋe aka nitye marach tektek.”
40015023	Yesu kodwoko go gimoro. To jofuonjirok pere jobino bonge to jokwayo go ni, “Sewila go wokadhi, rupiri go eno luwo wan aka koko kichar!”
40015024	Gikenyo Yesu odwoko ni, “Ooran nyaka bothi roombo morwenyo ma ot pa Israel kende.”
40015025	Munyo dheno owinjo ameno, obino to guro chonge katyendi Yesu munyo wacho ni, “Ruoth, konyan!”

40015027	Dheno odwoko ni, “Meno adyeri, jadwoŋ, to kole kada gwokere bende jochamoye ŋinjeŋinje modoŋ ma podho wok i meza pa jodongo pajo.”
40015028	Gikenyo Yesu odwoko go ni, “Dhakodwoŋ, ini gi yeyo madwoŋ! Gima iyenyo wotimere rin.” Aka i hongo no won ama nyare obed'iye maber.
40015029	Yesu oeye kenyo to luwo gi i thengi wakawaka ma Galileya munyo kadho. Kenyo go oidho tendere moro to bedo piny.
40015030	Kweth ji jobino bonge munyo jokelo jomoŋol, joma waŋ gin otho, joma tyendi gin owiyere, obadhin kodi joma two mathoth, kareno joketho jo katyendi Yesu, to go botho jojye.
40015031	Ji jodhyer swa munyo joneno obadhin joluwo, joma tyendi gin owiyere jolama, jomoŋol jowotho, aka joma waŋ gin otho joneno; aka jopako Were pa Israel.

40015033	Jofuonjirok jopenjo ni, “Wanonwaŋ chiemo kune i thim ka ma nyalo pidho kweth ji me?”

40015035	Gikenyo Yesu ooro kweth ji no bedo piny.

40015037	Jojye jochiemo to joyeŋ. Rumachien jofuonjirok jochoko ŋinjeŋinje modoŋ to poŋo aditin abiryo.

40015039	Gikenyo Yesu osewila ji to donjo i yee to kidho i adech ma Magadan.
40016001	Jofarisayo kodi Josadukayo mogo jobino bongi Yesu munyo joyenyo chiiko go, to jokwayo go ni wotim giraura ri jo mowok i polo.
40016002	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Ka waŋchieŋ kidho podho wiwacho ni, ‘Piny kidho kwe, rupiri pondeponde obokere.’
40016003	Aka odikini maŋich wiwacho ni, ‘Koth lechwe, rupiri pondeponde obokere aka piny odisa.’ Wiŋeyo tito chal pa piny i ŋiyo pondeponde; to wikinyal tito ranyuth ma mako kwoŋ ndir ma pama!
40016004	Kole luse ji marecho ma jokidew kwoŋ Were kada mathin ama rango ranyuth ma giraura. Ongoye giraura mibino miyo win kwanyo woko giraura pa Yona kende.” Gikenyo go oweyo jo to kadho.
40016005	Munyo jofuonjirok jochiewere to jokidho loka ma wakawaka man, wiyi gin owil gi tiŋo mugat moro.

40016007	Jochako luwirok wegi kendigin ni, “Go wacho ama kwoŋ bedo wakitiŋo mugat moro.”
40016008	Yesu oŋeyo gima onwaŋo jowacho, to penjo jo ni, “Raŋo ma wiluwere kendiwin ni wingoye kodi mugat moro? Apaka yeyo mewin nok ama?
40016009	Fuodi wikiniaŋi? Wikipoy ndir ma atur'iye mugat abich ri chwo gana abich, kodi aditin adi ma wichoko?
40016010	Aka mugat abiryo ri chwo gana aŋwen? Wipoŋo aditin adi?
40016011	Wibedo nedi ma wikiniaŋ ni oido akiluw kwoŋ mugat? Gwokere win kwoŋ thow pa Jofarisayo kodi Josadukayo.”
40016012	Gikenyo nyaka jofuonjirok joniaŋ ni go onwaŋo kiwachi ri jo kurok kwoŋ thow mioro i mugat, to kwoŋ fuonji pa Jofarisayo kodi Josadukayo ayino.
40016013	Yesu okidho i adech ma chiegin kodi Keserya Filipya kama go openj'iye jofuonjirok pere ni, “Ji jowacho ni Wuodi Dhano obedo ŋa?”

40016015	Aka go openjo jo ni, “To win wiwacho ni an ŋa?”

40016017	Yesu odwoko ni, “Simon wuodi pa Yona, i jasilwany swa! Adyeri me kobino rin wok bongi dhano moro, to Baba ma ni polo ama onyuthin.
40016018	Amomiyo awacho rin, in i Petro, aka wi tele me abino ger'iye kitipa pa jomoyeyo paran, ma kada tho kibino nyalo loyo kitipa no.
40016019	Abino miyin rayaw ma yawo Ker ma polo; gima inotwey i piny ka, ibino tweyo i polo; odoko gima inogony i piny ka, ibino gonyo i polo.”
40016020	Gikenyo Yesu ochiko jofuonjirok pere ni kiri jowotuchi ri moro nike go obedo Kristo.
40016021	Wok i hongo no kadho malo, Yesu ochako wacho kamaler ri jofuonjirok pere ni go ripo kidho Yerusalem wochandere tektek i chingi jotel pa ji kodi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, kodi jofuonji ma Chik. Jola neko go, aka i ndelo maradek ibino chierino go kendo.
40016022	Petro otero go gichien to chako ayi kwoŋe ni, “Were wogeŋi gino, Ruoth! Gime wokiri wotimere rin!”
40016023	Yesu owire to wacho ri Petro ni, “Eye bongan, Sitan! Iriwere ran i royo, rupiri paro perin me kiwoki bongi Were, to wok bongi dhano ayin.”
40016024	Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Ka moro mito luwan, go won kutho ripo kwerere kende, wotiŋi musalaba pere, aka woluwan.
40016025	Aka ŋata omiti botho kwo pere won bino rwenyo kwo; to ŋata orweny kwo pere kwoŋbedo an bino nwaŋo kwo.
40016026	Bero aŋo ma dhano olim ka oloki piny gipi apere to rwenyo kwo pere won? Kosa aŋo ma dhano owili gi kwo pere?
40016027	“Kole Wuodi Dhano lebino gi dwoŋ pa Bamere gi jomalaika pere, aka bino chulo dhano jye kemba pere chungo kwoŋ tim pere.
40016028	“Adyeri awacho ri win, nitye joma jochungo ka ma jokibino tho ma fuodi jokoneno Wuodi Dhano ka bino i Ker pere.”
40017001	Rumachien ma ndelo auchiel, Yesu okwanyo Petro kodi wutimere Yakobo gi Yohana, to tero jo wi got mabor kakendigin.
40017002	To go lokere ruwaŋ jo kenyo: waŋe olokere malyel pa waŋchieŋ, aka nengin pere olokere matar pa lero.

40017005	Munyo go oido fuodi luwo, pondeponde matar obino to thoko jo aka dwondijo mowok i pondeponde owacho ni, “Me Wuodan ma amaro kendo asangala gine; winji win go!”

40017010	Gikenyo jofuonjirok jopenjo Yesu ni, “Raŋo ma jofuonji ma Chik jowacho ni Eliya kutho ripo pen bino?”

40017012	To awacho ri win, Eliya otyeko kir bino to ji jokoŋeyo go, aka jotimo ri go paka joyenyo. I royo achiel Wuodi Dhano bende bino chandere i chingi jo.”
40017013	Gikenyo jofuonjirok joniaŋ nike go luwo ri jo kwoŋ Yohana Jakibatisa.

40017018	Yesu ooro jwogi no wok to wok, to jayach no both gi i hongo no won.
