40017026	Petro odwoko ni, “Kwoŋ jowiloka.” Ana Yesu, “Amomiyo, dwoŋ mere ni ji ma piny no jonitye i syem, jokichul.
40017027	To wakimiti ramo chuny jome, amomiyo kidhi i wakawaka ibol'iye siraget; kwanyi rech minoyway marapena, aka i dhoke ibino nwaŋ'iye pesa ma feza ma roman kodi win chulo misolo ma Ot pa Were; kwanyi ichuli jo misolo mawan.”
40018001	I hongo no jofuonjirok jobino bongi Yesu, to jopenjo go ni, “Ŋata dwoŋ loyo wadi jye i Ker ma polo?”
40018002	Yesu olwoŋo nyaka nyathi, to ketho go chungo i nyim jo,
40018003	aka owacho ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win ni, wikodonji i Ker ma polo, kwanyo woko ka wiwire aka wilokere paka nyithindho.
40018004	Ŋata dwoŋ loyo wadi jye i Ker ma polo obedo ŋata bwonere paka nyathi me.
40018005	Aka ŋata jolo nyaka nyathi ma nger me i nyingan, meno jolan.”
40018006	“Aka ŋata omiyi joma thindho ma joyeyan me timo recho d'ober ri go ka otwey kidi madwoŋ i ŋute tibolo go i wakawaka maluth.
40018007	Rach adyeri ri piny nike nitye gikipiny ma miyo ji timo recho! Gikipiny ma chalo ameno bino timere ndir jye, to bino racho loyo ri ŋata miyo kiti gikipiny no timirok!
40018008	“Ka chingin achiel kosa tyendin miyin timo gimarach, toŋi woko ibol woko! Ber rin donjo i kwo ma bu chingin kosa tyendin loyo bedo gi chingin jye kodi tyendin jye tibolin i mach makitho.
40018009	Aka ka waŋin miyin itimo gimarach, goli iboli woko! Ber rin swa donjo i kwo gi nyaka waŋin achiel loyo bedo gi waŋin aryo jye tibolin i mach makitho.
40018010	“Neni ni wikichay nyaka joma thindho me; kole awacho ri win, i polo koro jomalaika pajo jonitye ruwaŋ Baba mani polo hongo jye.
40018011	[Kole Wuodi Dhano obino botho jomorwenyo.]
40018012	“Wiparo nedi? Aŋo ma dhano di tim ka go nitye gi roombo miya achiel to achiel kwoŋ jo rwenyo? Go kiwey pyero abuŋwen g'abuŋwen jochiemo wi tendere kenyo to kidho rango nyaka rombo achiel morwenyo no?
40018013	Aka k'onwaŋo rombo no, awacho ri win, go kole bedo gi kisangala madwoŋ ri rombo no loyo pyero abuŋwen g'abuŋwen ma jokorwenyo cha.
40018014	I royo achiel, Baa win mani polo bende kiyeny achiel kwoŋ joma thindho me rwenyo.
40018015	“Ka omerin timo rin marach, kidhi bonge inyuthi go recho pere. To timi ameno nyaliŋliŋ, nyaka i dyer wijaryo. Ka go owinjin, meno ityeko dwoko omerin bongin.
40018016	To ka go okwer winjin, kwanyi ŋatachiel kosa ji man aryo ikidhi gi jo, aka ŋey wach moro jye woridho munyo ji aryo kosa adek jothyelo paka ondik.
40018017	To ka kowinjo jo bende, ere tuchi gimoro jye ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo. Aka ka go okwer winjo kir kitipa pa jomoyeyo bende, onyo teri go paka jakichar kosa jachoki misolo.
40018018	“Adyeri awacho ri win, gima winotwey i piny ka ibino tweyo i polo, gima winogony i piny ka ibino gonyo i polo.
40018019	“Aka awacho ri win kendo, ka ji aryo kwoŋ win i piny ka joyeyere i gimoro ma jokwayi, Baba mani polo bino timo ri jo gino.
40018020	Ato kama ji aryo kosa adek jochoker'iye i nyingan, meno anitye i dyer jo kenyo.”
40018021	Gikenyo Petro obino bongi Yesu to penjo go ni, “Ruoth, ka omera timo ran marach, anochwaki go didi? Dibiryo?”
40018022	Yesu odwoko ni, “Be, ki dibiryo, to di pyero abiryo di biryo.
40018023	Ato Ker ma polo chalo kere mochano kidho penjo jotich pere jowotiti ri go kwoŋ lim pere ma jotich pere no jo ni gine.
40018024	Go onwaŋo nyaka chako timo amanago tikelo achiel kwoŋ jomoido joni gi banja pere ma muma pesa gana apar.
40018025	To paka ŋato oido ongoye gi nger ma chulo banja no, ruoth pere owodho or nike wotana go, kodi chiege kodi nyithindho pere kodi lim pere jye, wochuli banja no.
40018026	Jatich no ogoyo chonge piny i nyim kere, to kwayo go ni, ‘Diyi chunyin kodan, abino chulin gimoro jye.’
40018027	Ruoth pere chunye oramo ri go, amomiyo ochwako go banja no to weyo go kadho.
40018028	“To munyo jatich no oido kadho, oromo gi jatich nyawote monwaŋo ni gi banja pere ma muma pesa miya achiel, go omako ŋato to chako deyo. Owacho ni, ‘Chulan pesa paran m'ikopa!’
40018029	Jatich nyawote ogore piny to kwayo go ni, ‘Diyi chunyin kodan, abino chulin!’
40018030	To go koyeyo; kuchiel omiyo obol ŋato i twech chuka wochuli banja no.
40018031	Munyo jotich man joneno gime paka otimere, chuny gin oramo jo swa, to jokidho bongi ruoth pajo to jowacho ri go gimoro jye motimere.
40018032	Gikenyo ruoth olwoŋo jatich no to wacho ni, ‘In i dhano marach! Achwakin banja monwaŋo initye gine bongan gipi rupiri iywakere ran;
40018033	onyo in di ikimakoye wor gi jatich nyawotin, paka atimo rin?’
40018034	Nge omako ruoth swa to bolo jatich no i katwech chuka bende ochuli penzi kir machowe.”
40018035	Yesu ochowo wach ni, “Meno apaka Baba mani polo bino timo ri win ka wikichwaki omin win, gi chuny win jye.”
40019001	Munyo Yesu ochowo wacho gikipiny me, oweyo Galileya to kidho i adech ma Yudeya, loka man ma jwom Yordan.
40019002	Kweth ji joluwo go kenyo, to botho jo.
40019003	Jofarisayo megi jobino bonge to jotemo chiiko go munyo jopenjo go ni, “Chik mawan yeyo dhano ryemo chiege ru wach moro jye?”
40019004	Yesu odwoko ni, “Fuodi wikisoma ndiiko ma wacho ni ŋata ochweyo jo wok i chakirok ochweyo jachwo gi dhako,
40019005	to wacho ni, ‘Ru atoŋa me jachwo bino weyo bamere gi yokimere to chwire kwoŋ chiege, aka jaryo jobino lokere del achiel.
40019006	Amomiyo onyo jokibedi ji aryo, to del achiel.’ Ri ameno gima Were otyeko riwo kanyachiel, moro wokiri wopoki.”
40019007	Jofarisayo jopenjo go ni, “Raŋo to ma Musa omiyo or ni jachwo womiyi chiege balwa ma ridho ni jopokere ka ryemo go?”
40019008	Yesu odwoko ni, “Musa oyeyo win ryemo mon mewin rupiri chuny win nwaŋ. To oido kobedo ameno wok i ndelo ma chwech.
40019009	Awacho ri win, ŋata ryemo chiege ma kobedo rupiri otimo chot, to nywomo dhako man, meno otimo chot. [Kendo ŋata onywomo dhako moryemi bende meno otimo chot.”]
40019010	Jofuonjirok pere jowacho ni, “Ka meno a gima nitye i dyer jachwo gi dhako, kere ber loyo ka dhano konywomo.”
40019011	Yesu odwoko ni, “Ongoye ŋata nyalo yeyo fuonji me, kwanyo woko joma Were omiyo jo kende.
40019012	Kole nitye wach mopekere ma miyo ji weyo ma jokunywomo: jomegi rupiri onywol jo ameno, joman kwoŋbedo ji jokolo toloko jo ameno; aka joman jokinywom ro miyo kwo pajo ri tich ma Ker ma polo. Ŋata nyalo niaŋ wojoli fuonji me.”
40019013	Jomogo jokelo nyithindho bongi Yesu nike go wikethi chinge i wiy jo wokwayi ri jo, to jofuonjirok joay kwoŋ ji.
40019014	Yesu owacho ni, “Weyi win nyithindho jowobin bongan, aka wikiri wijuki jo, rupiri Ker ma polo obedo ri joma pameno.”
40019015	Gikenyo go oketho chinge kwoŋ jo to kadho.
40019016	Ndelo moro jayach moro obino bongi Yesu to penjo go ni, “Jafuonji, bero aŋo ma aripo timo aka alim kwo makirumi?”
40019017	Yesu odwoko ni, “Raŋo m'ipenjan kwoŋ gimaber. Nitye ŋatachiel kende maber. Maki or ka imito donjo i kwo.”
40019018	Go openjo ni, “Or mene?” Yesu odwoko ni, “Ikiri ineki, ikiri itim chot, ikiri ikwali, ikiri ichwayi misegey ma twodo,
40019019	lwori benin gi yokonin; odoko mari nyawotin paka iwon imarere.”
40019020	Jayach no odwoko ni, “Atyeko mako or no jye. Aŋo modoko odoŋ ran atima?”
40019021	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Ka iyenyo bedo ŋataber kichutho, kidhi itana gimoro jye mini gine aka pesa mere imiy jochandi, aka ibino bedo gi ŋaŋo i polo; ŋey nyaka ibin iluwan.”
40019022	Munyo jayach no owinjo wach no, okadho mogut kwoŋ bedo go oido ni gi ŋaŋo madit swa.
40019023	Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, bino bedo matek swa ri jaŋaŋo donjo i ker ma polo.
40019024	Odoko awacho ri win, yot ri ŋamira donjo i yore piso loyo ri jaŋaŋo donjo i Ker pa Were.”
40019025	Munyo jofuonjirok jowinjo gime, jodhyer tektek. Jopenjo ni, “Ka ameno onyo ŋa won ma nyalo both?”
40019026	Yesu oŋiyo jo tirtir aka odwoko ni, “Gime kinyalere ri ji; to ri Were gimoro jye nyalere.”
40019027	Gikenyo Petro oluwo malo ka wacho ni, “Panen, watyeko weyo gimoro jye to waluwin. Wanolimi aŋo?”
40019028	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, i ndir manyien, ma Wuodi Dhano bino bed'iye wi kom pere madhum ma di dwoŋ, gikenyo wijapar g'aryo ma wiluwan bende wibino bedo wi kombere madhum apar g'aryo, kareno withumo banjin ri nonin apar g'aryo ma Israel.
40019029	Aka nyatoro jye moweyo udi, kosa wutimin, kosa nyimin go, kosa bamere, kosa min, kosa nyithindho, kosa ndelin kwoŋbedo an, bino limo kendo di miya achiel, kanyachiel gi kwo makirum.
40019030	Aka ji mathoth ma pama jobedo marapena jobino bedo machowe, aka ma jobedo machowe ama jobino bedo marapena.”
40020001	“Ker ma polo chalo won ndelo vini moay odikini worwor ketho ji mogo tich i ndelo pere ma vini.
40020002	Go ochikere kodi jo ni bino chulo jo kemba ma ndir jye, siringi achiel ndelo achiel, to dhiro jo i ndelo pere.
40020003	Go odoko oay to kidho i katale sawa adek to neno jomogo jochungo kenyo ma bu tich.
40020004	Omiyo go owacho ri jo ni, ‘Wibende kidhi win witiy i ndelo paran ma vini, aka abino miyo win gima ripere jye.’
40020005	To jono jokidho. Aka sawa auchiel kodi sawa abuŋwen go odoko otimo ameno.
40020006	Dho kapa sawa apar g'achiel go okidho i katale kendo to neno ji mogo ma fuodi oido jochungo kenyo. Go openjo jo ni, ‘Raŋo ma winyieko ndelo gipi ma wikitim gimoro?’
40020007	Jodwoko ni, ‘Fuodi ongoye ŋat'omiyo wan tich.’ Gikenyo go owacho ri jono ni, ‘Ere wibende kidhi win witiy i ndelo vini paran.’
40020008	“Aka munyo piny otundo othyeno, won ndelo owacho ri jakuri jotich pere ni, ‘Lwoŋi jotich imiy jo kemba pajo, ichaki kodi jom'oketh i tich ma chowe, aka ichowi kodi joma open ketho jo i tich.’
40020009	Joma nende jochako sawa apar g'achiel, omiy jo siringi achielechiele.
40020010	Meno omiyo munyo joma jopen i tich jobino limo kemba pajo, joparo ni di jonwaŋo madwoŋ loyo, to jo bende omiy jo siringi achielechiele won.
40020011	Jojolo pesa pajo to jochako kiŋunyaŋunya gi won tich.
40020012	Jowacho ni, ‘Jome, moketh jo i tich ma chowe me, kole jotiyo nyaka sawa achiel won kende, to neni wan wathyele gi tich mapek ndelo gipi i min chieŋ, ama odoko ichulo jo marom gi wani!’
40020013	Won ndelo odwoko ŋatachiel kwoŋ jo ni, ‘Nyawotan akibuyin pesa. Kole nende wayeyere kodin timo tich odyechieŋ gipi kwoŋ siringi achiel.
40020014	In maki kemba perin idoki pecho; an awon ayero miyo ŋata aketho i tich ma chowe me kemba marom kodi mamiyin.
40020015	Iparo ni angoye kodi thwolo timo paka ayenyo gi pesa paran woni? Kosa nyieko makin nyaka ni rupiri atimo bero ri ŋat man?’ ”
40020016	Aka Yesu omedo ni, “Amomiyo joma chowe ama jobino bedo marapena, aka joma rapena jobino bedo ma chowe.”
40020017	Munyo Yesu onwaŋo kidho Yerusalem, otero jofuonjirok japar g'aryo gichien to luwo gi jo nyaliŋliŋ.
40020018	Owacho ri jo ni, “Ato onyo wakidho Yerusalem kama ibino bol'iye Wuodi Dhano i chingi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jofuonji ma Chik to jothumo rigo banja ma tho.
40020019	Aka jobino ketho go i chingi Jopath wonyieri go, wochwadi go, tiguro go kwoŋ musalaba, aka i ndelo maradek ibino chierino go.”
40020020	Gikenyo min woti Zebedayo obino bongi Yesu gi wote aryo to goyo chonge ruwaŋe munyo kwayo go gimoro.
40020021	Yesu openjo go ni, “Aŋo m'iyenyo?” Go odwoko ni, “Timi chikirok ni wotan me jobedi yu rachuch kodi yu racham perin k'ilokere Kere.”
40020022	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Wikuya gima wikwayo. Winyalo madho agwata ma akidho madho?” To jodwoko ni, “Wanyalo”.
40020023	Yesu owacho ni, “Adyeri winyalo ri win madho agwata paran, to angoye kodi men ma yero joma jobedi yu rachuch kodi yu racham paran. Kabedo me obedo apa joma Baba oyiko ri jo.”
40020024	Munyo jofuonjirok wadi gin apar jowinjo kwoŋ gino, nge omako jo gi wutimere aryo no.
40020025	To Yesu olwoŋo jojye kanyachiel bonge, to wacho ni, “Wiŋeyo nike joma dhumo Jopath jodhumo gi maker, aka jotel pajo jodhumo gi mbaka.
40020026	To kobedi i dyer win ameno. Kuchiel ka moro kwoŋ win mito bedo madwoŋ, go ripo bedo ŋecha mewin;
40020027	aka ŋata yenyo bedo marapena i dyer win, ripo bedo ŋecha mewin,
40020028	paka Wuodi Dhano ma kobino ka ni wotiy ri go, to ni wotiyi ri ji gi miyo kwo pere paka chul ri ji mathoth.”
40020029	Munyo Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere joeye Yeriko, kweth ji joluwo go.
40020030	Ji aryo ma waŋ gin otho oido jobedo i thengi royo; munyo jowinjo ni Yesu oido kadho, jochako koko ni, “Wuodi pa Daudi! Makiye kodi wan wor!”
40020031	Kweth ji no joay kwoŋ jo ka jowacho ni jowoliŋi! To jome jomedo koko malo loyo ni, “Nyakwar Daudi, makiye kodi wan wor!”
40020032	Gikenyo Yesu ochungo to lwoŋo jo to penjo jo ni, “Wimito atim ri win aŋo?”
40020033	Jodwoko ni, “Ruoth, wayenyo waŋ wan woneen.”
40020034	Yesu omako gi jo wor, aka tekin ogeyo waŋ jo to jochako neno to joluwo go.
40021001	Munyo joriko Yerusalem, jobino Bethfage, wi got Olivet, to Yesu oro jofuonjirok pere aryo yu wiye gi wach me:
40021002	“Kidhi win loka ma yu wiy win kama wibino nwaŋ'iye mapiyo, punda motwey i loch gi nyathi mere. Gonyi win jo wikel ran.
40021003	Aka ka ŋat moro owacho ri win gimoro, wachi win ri go ni, ‘Jadwoŋ ama yenyo jo,’ aka go bino weyo jowokadhi mayot.”
40021004	Gime otimere ma miyo gima jatuchi wach Were owacho wotundi i kare ni,
40021005	“Wachi ri tindi ma Zayun ni, Neni kere perin bino bongin. Go mwol aka obedo wi punda, wi nyathi punda, wi punda mathin.”
40021006	Gikenyo jofuonjirok jokadho yu wiye to jotimo paka Yesu ooro jo;
40021007	jokelo punda gi nyathi mere, joketho kwoŋ jo nangin pajo, to jomiyo Yesu bedo wiye.
40021008	Muma ji madwoŋ jopedho nangin pajo i royo, kareno joman jotoŋo jangi yen aka jopedho i royo.
40021009	Muma ji moido wotho yu wiy Yesu kodi moido luwo go chien jochako koko ni, “Ozana! Pak wobedi ri Nyakwar Daudi! Were womiyi ŋata bino i nyingi Ruoth silwany! Ozana! Pak wobedi malo swa i polo!”
40021010	Munyo Yesu odonjo Yerusalem, ji ma tindi gi bee jochako woy, kareno jopenjo ni, “Me ŋa?”
40021011	Muma ji odwoko ni, “Me Yesu jatuchi wach Were, mawok Nazareth ma Galileya.”
40021012	Yesu odonjo i Ot pa Were aka oryemo woko joma oido jonyewere kosa jotana gikipiny i Ot pa Were; oŋilo woko mezin pa joma wilo pesa kodi kombere pa joma oido jotana akurin.
40021013	To wacho ri jo ni, “Ondik i Ndiiko Maleŋ ni Were owacho ni, ‘Ot paran ibino lwoŋo ni ot ma kwayo,’ ama onyo wiloko ŋungu pa jokwo ayino!”
40021014	Joma waŋ jo otho kodi jomoŋol jobino bonge i Ot pa Were to botho jo.
40021015	Jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jofuonji ma Chik nge omako jo munyo joneno giraura ma go otimo, kareno nyithindho jokoko i Ot pa Were ni, “Wopak Nyakwar Daudi!”
40021016	Gikenyo jopenjo Yesu ni, “Iwinjo gima jowacho?” Yesu odwoko ni, “Awinjo maber. Fuodi wikisoma ndiiko ma wacho ni, ‘I dhoki nyithindho kodi nyithindho maŋich ama owok'iye pak maber ma kichutho?’ ”
40021017	Yesu oweyo jo to wok i tindi no kareno chomo yu Bethaniya, to nindo korago.
40021018	Munyo Yesu ogik i tindi odikini yawere mere, go oido winjo kech.
40021019	Go oneno kiti makuyu moro michamo i thengi royo to kidho i tyende, to konwaŋo kwoŋe gimonyak kwanyo woko bokee kende. Gikenyo go owacho ri makuyu ni, “Ikodoko inyak gimoro!” Piyo piyo to makuyu no thwo.
40021020	Jofuonjirok joneno gime to jodhyer. Jopenjo ni, “Othwo mayot nedi ama?”
40021021	Yesu odwoko ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, ka wibedo gi yeyo, aka wikiganagana, wibino nyalo timo gima atimo ri makuyu me; ki meno kende, wibino nyalo wacho ri got me ni, ‘Ayi ka ibolere i nam,’ to timo ameno.
40021022	Ka wini gi yeyo, wibino limo gimoro jye ma wikwayo Were.”
40021023	Yesu odonjo i Ot pa Were aka munyo go fuonjo, jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jotel pa Joyudaya jobino bonge to jopenjo go ni, “Men aŋo m'ini gine ma timo gikipiny me? Ŋa m'omiyin men no?”
40021024	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Abende abino penjo win gimoro, ka widwokan aka abende anowachi ri win kama anwaŋ'iye men ma atimo gine gikipiny me.
40021025	Men pa Yohana mamiyo ji batisimo owok kune; owok bongi Were kosa bongi dhano?” Wegi jochako pyem kendigin ni, “Wawachi aŋo? Ka wadwoko ni, ‘Owok bongi Were,’ go bino penjo wan ni, ‘To raŋo ma wikiyeyo Yohana?’
40021026	To ka wadwoko ni, ‘Owok bongi dhano,’ walworo gima ji jonyalo timo, kwoŋbedo ji jye joridho ni Yohana oido obedo jatuchi wach Were.”
40021027	Ri ameno jodwoko Yesu ni, “Wakuya.” Gikenyo go bende owacho ri jo ni, “Abende akowachi ri win kama anwaŋ'iye men ma atimo gine gikipiny me.”
40021028	“Onyo wiparo nedi? Jal moro oido ni gi wote aryo. Go okidho bongi wuode madwoŋ to wacho ni, ‘Wuodan, kidhi itiyi reye i ndelo konon.’
40021029	Go odwoko ni, ‘Akotim ameno,’ to rumachien odoko owiro paro to kidho tich i ndelo vini.
40021030	Gikenyo baa jo okidho bongi wuode man, to kwayo go bende ameno. Wuode no odwoko ni, ‘Alekidho, jadwoŋ,’ to go kokidho.
40021031	Mene kwoŋ jaryo no motimo gima bamere oyenyo?” To jodwoko ni, “Wuode madwoŋ”. Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, jochoki misolo kodi mon ma jotana delkwoŋ jo i timo gi wichkwot ama jolekidho i Ker pa Were to widoŋ.
40021032	Kole Yohana obino i dyer win kareno nyutho win royo motire ma wiluw, to wikwero yeyo go; to jochoki misolo kodi mon ma jotana delkwoŋ jo i timo gi wichkwot ama joyeyo go. Odoko kada munyo wichowo neno ameno jye fuodi wikiwiro paro mewin wiyey go.”
40021033	Yesu owacho ni, “Winji win agecha man: obedo won lowo moro mopidho vini pere i ndelo, ogoyo chiel othoko gine, okunyo bur ma biyo medho ma vini, to gero ot achurchur makur. Gikenyo go oketho ndelo vini no i chingi jotich to eye pecho kidho woth.
40021034	Munyo ndir otundo ma fuono vini, go ooro ŋechin pere bongi jotich nike jowomiyi go vini pere.
40021035	Jotich jomako ŋechin pere no, jogoyo achiel, joneko man, to jogoyo man gi telin.
40021036	Go odoko ooro ŋechin man mathoth loyo joma rapena, to jotich jotimo jo ameno bende.
40021037	Machowe, go ooro ri jo wuode won ka wacho ni, ‘Waŋin jobino woro wuodan.’
40021038	To munyo jotich joneno wuode, jowacho i dyer gin wegi ni, ‘Me won a wuode ma bino lunjo gikipiny pere. Waneki go win eno, aka wakwanyi lim pere!’
40021039	Ri ameno jomako go, jobolo go woko ma ndelo vini, to joneko go.
40021040	“Onyo ka won ndelo vini obin, otim aŋo ri jotich no?”
40021041	Jodwoko Yesu ni, “Go adyeri bino neko ji marecho no to ketho ndelo vini i chingi jotich man ma jobino miyo go vini pere mofuon i ndir motire.”
40021042	Yesu openjo jo ni, “Fuodi wikisoma i Ndiiko Maleŋ ni, ‘Kole tele won ma jogeto jochayo ni bu kony ama olokere tele ma thyelo kindi ot. Me obedo tich pa Ruoth; aka neno maber swa ri wan!’
40021043	“Amomiyo awacho ri win, Ker pa Were ibino kwanyo woko kwoŋ win timiyo ji ma jobino nyak gimotire.
40021044	[Ŋata opodhi wi tele me bino ŋadere wolokere mathindhothindho; aka ŋata tele me opodhi kwoŋe tele me opodhi kwoŋe, tele bino ŋinyo go loko go pa fukefuke.”]

40022001	Yesu odoko ooro agechin munyo luwo gi jo ka wacho ni,
40022002	“Ker ma polo chalo kere moyiko kalima ma nywomirok ri wuode.
40022003	Ooro jotich pere wacho ri wendo molwoŋ ni jowobin i kalima; to jokomito bino.
40022004	Ri ameno go odoko ooro jotich man gi mikwenda me: ‘Wachi win ri jomolwoŋ ni atyeko yiko kis gimoro i kalima paran; megikwe paran kodi dhok machwe otyek neko, aka gimoro jye onyo oyikere. Biye win i kalima ma nywomirok.’
40022005	To jomolwoŋ jo jokodewo, jokadho i tich pajo ayino; achiel okadho i ndelo pere, ŋat man i mitan pere;
40022006	aka joman jomako jotich no, jogoyo jo, to joneko jo.

40022009	ere onyo kidhi win i royo mokakere i tindi, wilwoŋ ji mathoth ma winonwaŋ jye jowobin i kalima paran.’
40022010	Gikenyo jotich no jokidho i royo mokakere i tindi to jochoko ji jye ma jonyalo nwaŋo, mabeyo gi marecho parom; aka ot ma kalima opoŋ ji.
40022011	“To munyo kere odonjo kikaŋasa wendo, oneno kenyo nyatoro ma koruko nanga ma kalima.

40022017	Onyo wachi ri wan paro perin. Bedo gimotire i Chik mawan chulo misolo pa Kaisar, kosa be?”
40022018	Yesu oŋeyo chan pajo marach no to wacho ni, “Jorendirok! Raŋo ma witemo chiiko an?
40022019	Nyuthan win pesa ma wichulo gine misolo!” Jokelo ri go pesa mothedhi,
40022020	to penjo jo ni, “Chal pa ŋa kodi nyingi ŋa mani kwoŋe me?”
40022021	Jodwoko ni, “Apa Kaisar.” Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Amomiyo, miyi win Kaisar gipa Kaisar, aka Were bende miyi win go gipa Were.”
40022022	Munyo jowinjo gime, jouro swa; to joweyo go to jokadho.
40022023	Ndelo no won Josadukayo ma jowacho ni ji jokichierino kwoŋ jomotho jobino bothi Yesu,
40022024	to jopenjo go ni, “Jafuonji, Musa ofuonjo ni ka dhano mongoye gi nyithindho otho, omin ripo lunjo chi tho no wonywoli gine nyithindho ri ŋatotho no.
40022025	Onwaŋo nitye wutimere abiryo ma yado jobedo i dyer wan ka: Marapena onywomo, to tho ma kolimo nyithindho, ameno go oweyo chiege ri omin.
40022026	Gino odoko otimere ri omin mararyo, gi maradek, tundo kwoŋ wutimere abiryo jye.
40022027	Rumachien, to dhako no won tho.
40022028	Onyo, i ndelo ma rumachien munyo jomotho jochierino, dheno obedi chipa ŋa kwoŋ ji abiryo no, rupiri jojye chango jobedo gine.”
40022029	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Wipodho swa, rupiri wikuya Ndiiko Maleŋ kosa men pa Were,
40022030	rupiri i chierino pa ji kobed'iye nywomirok kosa nywom, to jobino chalo jomalaika pa Were i polo.
40022031	Onyo ma mako kwoŋ chierino: fuodi wikisoma gima Were owacho ri win munyo wacho ni,
40022032	‘Abedo Were pa Ibrayimu, Were pa Isaka, kodi Were pa Yakobo.’ Dwoŋ mere ni go obedo Were pa joma kwo ma kiweno apa jomotho.”
40022033	Munyo kweth ji jowinjo gime jodhyer swa.
40022034	Munyo Jofarisayo jowinjo ni Yesu omiyo Josadukayo jorumo kodi girawacha, jochokere kanyachiel.
40022035	Aka achiel kwoŋ jo, mobedo jafuonji ma Chik, openjo go ma chiiko go ni,
40022036	“Jafuonji, or mene maloyo dwoŋ i Chik?”
40022037	Yesu odwoko ni, “ ‘Mari Ruoth Were perin g'adundo perin jye, gi chunyin jye, gi paro perin jye.’
40022038	Me a Or maloyo jye gi dwoŋ kendo ama telo.

40026020	Munyo hongo mothyeno otundo, Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere apar g'aryo jobedo piny chiemo.
40026021	Aka munyo jochiemo Yesu owacho ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, achiel kwoŋ win bino chamo ran sereko.”

41001015	Go owacho ni, “Ndir otundo, aka Ker pa Were ochore chiegin. Ŋuti win gimarecho mewin, aka wiyeyi Wach Maber.”
41001016	Munyo Yesu wotho dho thengi wakawaka ma Galileya, oneno jokitoga, Simon kodi Andereya omin go, munyo oido jochiiko bwoo pajo i wakawaka.
41001017	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Luwan win abino loko win jokitoga ji.”
41001018	Piyo piyo no joweyo bwoo pajo, to jochako luwo go.

41001020	Piyo no to lwoŋo jo, to joweyo baa gin Zebedayo kodi jotich pere i yee to joluwo go.
41001021	Gikenyo Yesu gi jofuonjirok pere jokidho Kapernaum; aka i ndelo ma Sabato, Yesu odonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya to fuonjo.
41001022	Ji jouro swa, rupiri go ofuonjo pa ŋata ni gi men, ma kiweno paka jofuonji ma Chik.
41001023	Piyo piyo no dhano ma chuny mochido oido ni kwoŋe odonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya ni pil, to chako koko ni,
41001024	“Imito timo wan nedi, Yesu Janazareth? Ibino ka reyo wan woko? Aŋeyin, i ŋataleŋ pa Were.”
41001025	Yesu oay kwoŋe munyo wacho ni, “Liŋi kendo woki woko i eye kwoŋe.”
41001026	Gikenyo chuny mochido no oyengo ŋato gi men to wok kwoŋe munyo koko gi derino madwoŋ.
41001027	Gino omiyo ji jye dhyer tektek to wegi jopenjere kendigin ni, “To me aŋo? Kole me fuonji manyien! Go oro kir chuny mochido wok aka jowinjo go!”
41001028	Gikenyo nyinge olak i adech ma Galileya jye parom.
41001029	Tekin jowok i kalamo pa Joyudaya, Yesu kodi Yakobo jokidho kodi Andereya pecho pa Simon.
41001030	Or Simon ma dhako onwaŋo nitye i kanindo kwoŋe oowere, to jowacho ri Yesu mayot paka dhako dwoŋ no two.
41001031	Yesu okidho bonge, omako chinge, to dheno ay malo. Ameno two no oweyo go, to go chako rweyo jo.
41001032	Othyeno no, munyo waŋchieŋ otyeko podho, ji jokelo ri Yesu jotwo jye, kodi joma onwaŋo jwogi ni kwoŋ jo.
41001033	Ji ma tindi gipi to jowura ri go dhoot.
41001034	Yesu obotho ji madit monwaŋo joramere gi two mopekere opokere: aka oryemo woko jwogi bende, ma koyeyo jo luwo, rupiri oido joŋeyo go.
41001035	Yawere mere odikini, ma piny fuodi kochot, Yesu ochiew to wok i ot no, to kidho gichien kwayo.
41001036	To Simon gi wadi jowok rango go,
41001037	aka munyo jonwaŋo go, jowacho ri go ni, “Dhano jye dwarin.”
41001038	Yesu odwoko ni, “Ere wakidhi win i tindi man, afuonji korago bende; kole gino ama okelan.”
41001039	Owotho Galileya munyo fuonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya, kendo munyo ryemo woko jwogi kwoŋ ji.
41001040	Gikenyo jadhowo moro obino bothi Yesu, to guro chonge piny, to kwayo go ni, “Ka iyeyo, inyalo bothan.”
41001041	Yesu omako gine wor, aka ochwayo chinge ogeyo go, to wacho ni, “Ayeyo; bothi.”
41001042	Gikenyo won, dhowo no oeye kwoŋ ŋato, to kwoŋe chango molony.
41001043	Yesu ochiko go teltel munyo sewila go ni,
41001044	“Ikiri iwachi ri nyatoro gime; kidhi inyuthere i waŋ jachwayi ri Were wi alitar, aka imiy go mich paka Musa oketho i chik, aka dhano jye woŋeyi ni ityeko both adyeri.”
41001045	To jalo ochako nyayo wach no iye jye, momiyo Yesu odoko konyalo donjo i tindi kamaler, to obedo gichien kuma ongoye iye ji, aka kenyo ama ji jobino iye bonge wok kaman man jye.
41002001	Munyo ndelo okadho manok, Yesu ogik Kapernaum, aka wach olak ni go odwoko yu pecho.
41002002	Gikenyo ji jochokere kir i dhoot mongoye ka leŋo, to go fuonjo jo.
41002003	Munyo fuodi go fuonjo, ji aŋwen jokelo nyatoro ma two nyaŋinya.
41002004	To paka muma ji koyeyo jo baro royo ma rwako go bongi Yesu, jomwomo wiy ot kama otitere gi Yesu, aka munyo joyawo hola ma romo, jochwayo kitanda ma janyaŋinya no oido onind'iye nyuka otundo piny.
41002005	Munyo Yesu oneno yeyo pajo, owacho ri janyaŋinya no ni, “Nyathi paran, gimarecho perin ochwaki rin.”
41002006	Kenyo onwaŋo nitye jofuonji ma Chik mogo, to wegi joparo kendigin ni,
41002007	“Raŋo ma ŋatin luwo ama? Kole go luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Were? Ŋata bende nyalo chwako gimarecho ma kiweno Were won?”
41002008	Yesu oŋeyo ni meno a paro moido jo ni gine, to wacho ri jo ni, “Raŋo ma wibedo gi paro no i chuny win?
41002009	Aŋo mayot wacho? Wacho ri janyaŋinya ni, ‘Gimarecho perin ochwaki rin,’ kosa ni, ‘Ayi malo, itiŋ kitanda perin iwothi?’
41002010	Ere wey anyuthi win ni Wuodi Dhano ni gi men i piny ka ma chwako gimarecho.” Gikenyo owacho ri janyaŋinya no ni,
41002011	“Awacho rin, ayi malo, tiŋi kitanda perin idoki pecho.”
41002012	Jalo oay malo, otiŋo kitanda pere, to wotho i waŋ ji jye, aka jojye jodhyer to jopako Were munyo jowacho ni, “Fuodi oido wakineno gima chalo ama.”
41002013	Yesu odoko okidho dho thengi wakawaka ma Galileya, aka kweth ji jochokere bonge, to fuonjo jo.
41002014	Aka munyo wotho, oneno Levi jachoki misolo, wuodi pa Alfayo, obedo piny i ot ma misolo, to wacho ri go ni, “Luwan.” Jalo oay malo to luwo Yesu.
41002015	Rumachien, Yesu okidho pecho pa Levi gi jofuonjirok pere, to bedo dhower. Jochoki misolo kweth kodi jomarecho bende joluwo go yu koro. Jojye bende jochiemo kanyachiel gi Yesu.
41002016	Munyo jofuonji ma Chik ma dyer Jofarisayo joneno Yesu chiemo kodi jomarecho gi jochoki misolo, jopenjo jofuonjirok pere ni, “Raŋo ma go chiemo gi jochoki misolo Kodi jomarecho?”
41002017	Munyo Yesu owinjo gino, odwoko jo ni, “Jomolama ama jokiyeny jamilerwa, to jomatwo ayino ama joyenyo: kole akibino lwoŋo jomabeyo, to abino lwoŋo jomarecho ayino.”
41002018	Ndelo moro munyo jofuonjirok pa Yohana Jakibatisa kodi apa Jofarisayo onwaŋo joriyo kech, jomogo jobino to jopenjo Yesu ni, “Raŋo ma jofuonjirok pa Yohana Jakibatisa kodi apa Jofarisayo joriyo kech aka aperin jokiriy?”
41002019	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “To, wendo ma jonitye i kalima ma nywomirok jonyalo nedi riyo kech mato jamweha fuodi nitye gi jo? I hongo ma go fuodi ni gi jo jokiriy kech be.
41002020	To ndir bino tundo ma jamweha bino ey'iye bongi jo, meno aka nyaka jochaki riyo kech.
41002021	“Ongoye ŋata kwoyo kiremo nanga ma fuodi nyien wi nanga moti. Ka otimo ameno, kiremo manyien bino ywayo woko kasegere nanga no to medo yech malach loyo waŋe machon.
41002022	Ongoye ŋata konjo vini manyien i mugowa pyen mere moti; ka otimo ameno, mugowa pyen bino yech to vini oy, to go keŋ vini kir gi mugowa no jye. To, vini manyien bende ikonjo i migowa pyen manyien!”
41002023	Ndelo ma Sabato moro, Yesu onwaŋo wotho i ndelo ŋano, to jofuonjirok pere jochodo withi ŋano malomalo.

41002026	paka go odonjo i Ot pa Were i ndir pa Abiyathar, jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar aka ochamo mugat ma jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kende ama oyey jo chamo, to miyo ji pere bende?”
41002027	Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Sabato oketh ma bero pa dhano, to dhano kochwey ri Sabato;

41003001	Gikenyo Yesu odoko odonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya, aka dhano ma chinge otho onwaŋo nitye kenyo.
41003002	Kenyo bende oido nitye jomogo ma jokiyo neno ni kono Yesu obothi ŋato i ndelo ma Sabato, ŋey jowokethi kwoŋe banja.
41003003	Yesu owacho ri ŋata chinge otho no ni, “Biye ka. Chungi, ji jye jowonenin.”
41003004	To Yesu penjo jo ni, “Chik yeyo wan timo bero i ndelo ma Sabato, kosa racho ayin? Botho kwo, kosa neko ayin?” To joliŋ aliŋa.
41003005	Yesu ogawo jo gi keme, rupiri chuny jo oido nwaŋ, aka owacho ri ŋato ni, “Ryeyi chingin.” Ŋato oryeyo chinge, to chinge bedo maber kichutho.
41003006	Gikenyo Jofarisayo jowok woko, aka piyo piyo no jo kodi jopa Herode jochako thumo ryeko ma neko Yesu.
41003007	Yesu gi jofuonjirok pere jokidho dho wakawaka. Aka kweth ji joluwo go ji ma jowok Galileya kodi Yudeya,
41003008	i tindi ma Yerusalem kodi i adech ma Idumeya, gi ma loka Yordan, gi ma yu tindi Tire kodi Sidon. Kweth ji me jobino munyo jowinjo gima Yesu oido timo.
41003009	Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere dwaro ri go yee wobed'iye, munyo oneno ni kweth ji no jonyalo diyo go;
41003010	ato go oido otyeko botho ji mathoth, amomiyo dhano jye monwaŋo ni gi two orire bonge ni wonyali geyo go.
41003011	Aka bin chuny mochido mani kwoŋ ji ka joneno Yesu, jogore piny dhowaŋe to jokoko ni, “In i Wuodi Were”.
41003012	Yesu ochiero chuny mochido kichutho miyo ji ŋeyo go.
41003013	Yesu okidho wi got, to lwoŋo bonge joma go won omito, to jobino bothe.
41003014	Go oyero ji apar g'aryo bedo bonge, g'atoŋa ma oro jo fuonji rumachien,
41003015	gi nwaŋo men ma ryemo woko jwogi.
41003016	Me a japar g'aryo ma go oyero: Simon m'omiyo nyinge ni Petro;
41003017	Yakobo gi Yohana woti Zebedayo m'omiyo jo nyingi gin ni “Bonages”, dwoŋ mere ni joma mwoch pa lithkoth,
41003018	Andereya, Filipo, Batholomayo, Mathayo, Thoma, Yakobo wuodi pa Alfayo, Thadeyo, Simon Jalweny ri nono pere,
41003019	kodi Yuda Iskaryot mochamo ri go sereko.
41003020	Yesu odok pecho, aka kweth ji odoko jochokere bothe ma jokonyalo yeyo jo kada chiemo.
41003021	Munyo wade pere jowinjo wach no, jobino ni jowomaki go, rupiri ji oido jowacho ni wiye onyiekere.
41003022	Jofuonji ma Chik ma jowok Yerusalem joero wacho ni, “Belzebul ni kwoŋe, aka ryemo jwogi gi men pa Belzebul.”
41003023	Gikenyo Yesu olwoŋo jo bonge to chako bolo ri jo agechin mogo ni, “Sitan nyalo ryemo woko Sitan nyawote nedi?”
41003024	Ka ker moro won otyakere munyo ji mere wegi jolwenyo kendigin, kole ker no kinyal chungo.
41003025	Ka pecho moro otyakere munyo ji ma kenyo wegi jolwenyo kendigin, pecho no bende kinyal chungo.
41003026	Aka ka Sitan onyo won owire lwenyo gi wadi, kole meno ker pere otyakere kinyal chungo, aka chiegin tur.
41003027	Ongoye nyatoro ma nyalo donjo i ot pa dhano ma jameni, to nyaga gikipiny pere, ma kokutho otweyo ŋato aka nyaka onyali kinyaga gikipiny pere.
41003028	“Adyeri awacho ri win, gimarecho pa ji jye ibino chwako ri jo, kada luwo gima kotire kwoŋ gimaleŋ;
41003029	To moro ma luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Chuny Maleŋ, kocwaki go; meno otimo gimarach ma chil gi chil.”
41003030	Yesu oluwo ameno rupiri jomogo oido jotyeko wacho ni chuny mochido ni kwoŋe.
41003031	Yoki Yesu gi wutimin go bende jotundo to jochungo woko aka jodhiro wach ni jomito neno go.
41003032	Muma ji onwaŋo obedo piny othoko go; to jowacho ri go ni: “Yokin kodi wutimerin ichade jochungo woko jomito nenin.”

41003034	Aka obolo waŋe oŋiyo jomobedo piny thoko go, to wacho ni, “Kole jome a mama gi wutimera.
41003035	Dhano jye ma timo gima Were mito, ŋato ama obedo omera, kodi nyamera kodi mama.”
41004001	Yesu odoko ochako fuonjo ji i thengi wakawaka ma Galileya. Kweth ji moasere jochokere bothe, amomiyo go odonjo i wakawaka to bedo i yee. Aka ji jye jobedo dho thengi wakawaka.
41004002	Yesu ofuonjo gikipiny madit munyo luwo i agechin, aka i fuonji pere owacho ni,
41004003	“Winji win! Dhano moro okidho chwoyo.
41004004	Aka munyo bayo kodhi, megi opodho i thengi royo, to winyin jobino jodimo woko.
41004005	Kodhi megi opodho wi tele kuma lowo rep'iye; jokwako twi, rupiri lowo oido rep.
41004006	To munyo chieŋ olyel, orewo jo, to paka tyendi gin oido orawere, joner to jothwo woko.
41004007	Kodhi megi opodho kuma di kudhin, aka kudhin odongo gi jo to mwonyo jo woko ma jokonyalo nyak gimoro.
41004008	Aka kodhi megi opodho i lowo maber ma diwa, to jonyak withi gin, ma megi nyingi gin pyero adek, megi pyero auchiel, megi miya achiel.”
41004009	Aka Yesu owacho ni, “Ŋata ni gi ithe ma winjo wowinji.”
41004010	Gikenyo munyo Yesu oido ni kende, joma onwaŋo jo ni bonge, kanyachiel gi jofuonjirok pere apar g'aryo, jopenjo go tyendi agecha me.
41004011	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Otyek miyo win ŋeyo nyaliŋliŋ ma Ker pa Were,
41004012	to jonicha ma jo ni woko iwacho ri jo gikipiny g'agechin, ŋey nyaka, ‘Kada jotem ŋiyo jokonyal neno, kada jotem winjo jokonyal niaŋ, Ipoyo di jonyalo gik bongi Were to chwako jo.’ ”
41004013	Gikenyo Yesu openjo jo ni, “Kere wikuya dwoŋ agecha me? Onyo winoŋey nedi dwoŋ agechin man?
41004014	Jachwoyo chwoyo wach pa Were.
41004015	Dichieŋ wach megi podho thengi royo; meno ji ma jowinjo wach no, to tekin jotyeko winjo, to Sitan bino to kwalo woko wach monwaŋo ochwoy i chuny gin.
41004016	Ji man jochale kodi kodhi mopodho wi tele ma lowo rep'iye. Me a joma tekin jowinjo wach to jojolo gi kisangala.
41004017	To wach no kimoki i chuny jo, aka bedo ye i chuny jo nyaka hongo machiek. To ka teko kosa achanda mogo obino, ro wach no, jono jopodho mayot.
41004018	Ji man jochalo kodhi mochwoy kama di kudhin. Me a joma jowinjo wach,
41004019	to rembo ri kwo ma piny me, kodi awanya ma ŋaŋo ma piny kodi giman mathoth jomwonyo wach to kinyak gimoro.
41004020	To ji megi jochalo kodhi mochwoy i lowo maber ma diwa. Jowinjo wach, jojolo, aka wach nyak: megi pyero adek, megi pyero auchiel, megi miya achiel.”
41004021	Gikenyo Yesu omedo wacho ni, “Tala bende odoko iryewo iyagono nedi? Kosa iketho nedi i tyendi kitanda, ma kolyer malo wi akare mere?
41004022	Kole gima opan jye ibino wodho kamaler, aka gima oum ibino yawo kamaler.
41004023	Ŋata ni gi ithe ma winjo gima afuonjo wowinji.”
41004024	To wacho ri jo ni, “Kethi win i tim gima wiwinjo; paka ipima gima imiyo ji, apaka bende ibino kipima rin gima ibino miyin, aka ibino medin kir man.
41004025	Aka ŋata nitye gi gikipiny mathoth ibino medo go man, ŋata ongoye gine ibino mayo go kada nyaka mathin monwaŋo go ni gine.”
41004026	Yesu owacho ni, “Ker pa Were chalo dhano mochwoyo kodhi i ndelo pere.
41004027	Go nindo wor, to chiew odikini to yindin odyechieŋ gipi, kareno kodhi twi to dongo. Go kiŋey kada paka gino dongo.
41004028	Lowo won miyo gimopidhi dongo to nyak.
41004029	Gino kutho turo thyaŋ to ŋok, rumachien withe gi nyinge tegino. Ka kal ochiek i ndelo, won ndelo kwanyo athero, rupiri kecho otundo.”
41004030	Yesu odoko owacho ama: “Di wawachi ni Ker pa Were chalo aŋo? Kosa agecha aŋo ma wanoori ma tito?
41004031	Gime chalo nyaka kodhi mondhilo ma i ndir ma pidho thin swa loyo kodhi man jye ma piny.
41004032	To ka otyek pidho, twi to dongo madwoŋ loyo yen wadi jye; ryeyo jange madongo, aka winyin jonyalo geto odi gin i jange.”
41004033	Yesu bin fuonjo ji munyo bolo agechin mathoth thoth paka meno.
41004034	Oluwo gi jo i royo mamiyo jowoniaŋi wach. Go koluwo gi jo mongoye agechin; to ka nitye gi jofuonjirok pere wegi kakendigin, tito ri jo gimoro jye gi thenethene mere.
41004035	Munyo piny oumere, Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Wapori win loka makocha ma wakawaka.”
41004036	Joweyo kweth ji, to jodonjo i yee kendigin, to jochako chiewirok. Yee megi oido bende nitye kenyo.
41004037	Gikenyo koyo madwoŋ obino gi men to yengo wakawaka, to miyo pi tula to chako donjo i yee pa kidho poŋo.
41004038	Yesu oido nitye chien i yee, otheno wiye nindo. Jochiewo go to jowacho ri go ni, “Jafuonji, ikidew ni wachiegin tho?”
41004039	Yesu ochiew, oay kwoŋ koyo no, to wacho ri wakawaka ni, “Kudere! Kwe!” Aka koyo okwe to wakawaka jye pye.

41004041	Jodhyer swa to wegi jowacho kendigin ni, “Me ŋa ma kir koyo gi wakawaka jye winjo wach pere!”
41005001	Yesu gi jofuonjirok pere jopor loka man ma wakawaka ma Galileya, to jodonjo i piny ma Gerasa.

41005003	Ŋato oido nitye gi chuny mochido, aka oido bedo i kalyele. Ongoye moro monwaŋo nyalo tweyo go kada gi lijegere aka bedi liŋ.
41005004	Ndir mathoth onwaŋo itweyo chinge gi tyende, to hongo jye chodo woko lijegere, to ŋinyo woko okol ma tyende.
41005005	Odyechieŋ gi wor jye go oido helahela i kalyele kodi wi tendere munyo hola aka yaŋere gi telin.

41005013	Yesu oyeyo jo. Chuny mochido jowok kwoŋ jalo to jodonjo i mbiji. Sidwol mbiji gi bee, ma romo chiegin gana aryo gipi jomwomere gi ŋwech wok dho thengi tendere to jomunyere i wakawaka.
41005014	Jokwath mbiji jokedhere gi ŋwech to jonyayo wach no i tindi kodi i ndelin kama ji onwaŋo jotiy'iye. Aka ji jokidho neno gimotimere.

41005020	Gikenyo ŋato omako royo to wotho i tindin apar (milwoŋo ni Dekapoli), munyo wacho ri ji gima Yesu otimo ri go; aka ji jye ma jowinjo jouro tektek.
41005021	Munyo Yesu odoko opor loka man gi yee, aka oido obedo thengi wakawaka, kweth ji jothoko go kenyo.
41005022	Yayiro, ruoth ma kalamo pa Joyudaya, bende obino.
41005023	Aka munyo oneno Yesu, oryewere piny dho tyende to kwayo go gi geregere ni, “Nyaran two swa, mondo bowe ikidhi ikethi chingin kwoŋe wobedi maber.”
41005024	Yesu omako royo gi go. Aka muma ji madwoŋ oluwo go to thoko go ni rap.
41005025	Kenyo onwaŋo nitye dhako moro moido otyeko chandere gi remo ma oy chowo hongo ma oro apar g'aryo gipi;
41005026	aka go onwaŋo otyeko temo woth kwoŋ jomilerwa momore ma go fuodi chandere achanda. Dheno oido otyeko nyieko lim ma go oido ni gine jye, to kabedo ma chango, two omedere ayino.
41005027	Go oido otyekoye winjo kwoŋ Yesu, ri ameno orire i dyer ji yu ŋeye to geyo nanga pere.
41005028	Ato owacho g'ichunye ni, “Ka anogey kada nyaka nanga pere won, abino bedo maber.”
41005029	Go ogeyo kanzo pa Yesu, to remo chok gi kenyo won, aka won bende owinjo ni two pere otyeko chango.
41005030	Munyo Yesu owinjo meni owok kwoŋe, owire piyo i dyer ji to penjo ni, “Ŋata ogeyo nengin paran?”
41005031	Jofuonjirok pere jodwoko ni, “Ineno kweth ji jodire kwoŋin ama aka odoko fuodi ipenjo ni, ‘ŋat'ogeyan?’ ”
41005032	To Yesu medo rango gi waŋe thenge gi thenge munyo mito neno ŋata ogeyo go.
41005033	Gikenyo dhako no owok kamaler gi lworo kodi kirin, rupiri oŋeyo gima go otimo; aka opodho katyendi Yesu to tito ri go gimoro jye.
41005034	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Nyaran, yeyo perin obothin; doki pecho i syem, aka two perin no woweyin kichutho.”
41005035	Munyo Yesu fuodi luwo, jomogo jokonjere ma jowok pa yayiro, ruoth ma kalamo pa Joyudaya, to jowacho ni, “Nyarin otyeko tho, odoko ichando jafuonji raŋo?”
41005036	To Yesu kere onwaŋo winjo, amomiyo owacho ri ruoth ma kalamo pa Joyudaya ni, “Ikiri ilwori, bedi gi yeyo ayin.”
41005037	Yesu koyeyo moro oluwo go, kwanyo woko Petro gi Yakobo kodi Yohana omin go.
41005038	Munyo jotundo pecho pa ruoth no, Yesu oneno paka jokalyel joywak gi geregere, jogoyo ndur, aka jowoy.
41005039	Aka munyo go odonjo i ot, owacho ri jo ni, “Woy gi ywak me jye maraŋo? Nyathi me kotho, go nindo ayin.”
41005040	Gikenyo jonyiero Yesu ayino, amomiyo go oryemo jojye woko, to kwanyo baa nyathi gi yokimere kodi jofuonjirok pere, to donjo gi jo kuma opyel'iye nyathi no.
41005041	Go omako chingi nyathi no to wacho ri go ni, “Talitha, kumi!” Dwoŋ mere ni, “Nyathi manyako, awacho rin, ay malo.”
41005042	Piyo piyo no nyako no oay malo ni sew to chako woth; aka nyako nago no onwaŋo romo oro apar g'aryo. Ji jobedo gi dhyer swa munyo gime otimere.
41005043	Yesu ochiko jo teltel ni kiri jowowachi ri nyatoro; to oro jo miyo nyano girachama.
41006001	Yesu okidho i tindi ma thugin kodi jofuonjirok pere.
41006002	I ndelo ma Sabato, go ochako fuonji i kalamo pa Joyudaya aka munyo kweth ji monwaŋo ni kenyo jowinjo go, jouro swa. Jowacho ni, “Go onwaŋo kune fuonji me jye? Ryeko aŋo ni momiy go? Go nyalo nedi timo giraura?
41006003	Me won ki japach, wuodi pa Marya, omin Yakobo kodi Yose kodi Yuda kodi Simon? Aka nyimin go jongoye bongi wan won ka?” Ameno to jokwero yeyo go.
41006004	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Jatuchi wach Were kichay kaman, kwanyo woko i piny pere won, kodi bongi wade pere won kodi bongi jothugin wegi.”
41006005	Yesu konyalo timo kenyo giraura madwoŋ, kada nende obotho nyaka jotwo mogo manok munyo ketho chinge kwoŋ jo.
41006006	Yesu ouro swa paka jono jongoye gi yeyo.
41006007	Yesu okidho loka moro ma chiegin to fuonjo ji kenyo. Go olwoŋo jofuonjirok pere apar g'aryo, to miyo jo men ma ryemo woko chuny mochido;
41006008	aka omiyo jo or ni, “Wikiri witiŋ gimoro jye kwanyo woko luth, kendo wikiri witiŋ mugat kada mugowa moro kosa pesa.
41006009	Ruki win war, to wikiri wiruki nengin aryo.”
41006010	Aka owacho ri jo ni, “Ka widonjo pecho moro, bedi win kenyo chuka winowoki i adech no.
41006011	Ka witundo kamoro to jokwero jolo win, kosa winjo fuonji mewin, ka wikadho teŋi win woko fukefuke ma tyendi win, paka ranyuth ma theko win gi jo.”
41006012	Gikenyo jochako woth pajo munyo jofuonjo ji ni jowoŋuti gimarecho pajo.
41006013	Joryemo woko jwogi mathoth, aka jowiro jotwo mathoth gi mo to jobotho jo.
41006014	Kere Herode owinjo kwoŋ gino, rupiri nyingi Yesu oido otyeko ŋeyere kamoro jye. Ji megi oido jowacho ni, “Yohana Jakibatisa osukina kendo amomiyo go nitye gi men ma timo giraura.”
41006015	To joman jowacho ni, “Go Eliya.” Joman jowacho ni, “Go achiel kwoŋ jotuchi wach Were machon.”
41006016	Munyo Herode owinjo gino, owacho ni, “Yohana, ma ndir cha aŋondo woko ŋute, ama odoko osukina kendo!”
41006017	Herode won gipi ama ooro ji mako Yohana ni wobol katwech. Go otimo ameno ru wach pa Herodya, ma go onywomo, mato meno oido chipa Filipo, omin go.
41006018	Yohana onwaŋo omena wacho ri Herode ni, “Kobedo gimotire in nywomo chipa omerin!”
41006019	Gikenyo Herodya omako nge gi Yohana aka oido yenyo neko go, to konyalo timo ameno.
41006020	Herode onwaŋo lworo Yohana, rupiri oŋeyo ni Yohana obedo dhano maber kendo maleŋ. Amomiyo oido kuro go ma racho moro di konyalo podho kwoŋe. Herode onwaŋo omaro winjo luwo pa Yohana kada nende hongo jye chunye onwaŋo waŋo go swa ka owinjo gima go wacho.
41006021	Rumachien Herodya olimo hongo maber. Ndelo ma poyo nywolirok pa Herode otundo, aka Herode otimo kalima madwoŋ ri ruodhe madongo, kodi jotel pa lwak jolweny, kodi ji ma joŋeyere ma Galileya.
41006022	Nyar Herodya odonjo kuma wendo oido jo ni iye to myelo, to sangala Herode kodi wendo jye tektek. Gikenyo Herode owacho ri nyano ni, “Imito amiyin aŋo? Abino miyin gimoro jye minokway.”
41006023	Owacho ri nyano gi kwoŋirok ni, “Achikere miyin gimoro jye minokway, kada adech ma ker paran!”
41006024	Gikenyo nyano owok woko to penjo min ni, “Akway aŋo?” Min odwoko ni, “Wich Yohana jakibatisa.”
41006025	Nyano ogik mayot bongi kere to wacho ni, “Amito imiyan wich Yohana jakibatisa i sen pama won me!”
41006026	Wach no omiyo kere kwoŋe okwe tektek, to konyalo thwono go, rupiri oido otyeko kwoŋirok i waŋ wendo pere jye.
41006027	Amomiyo kere ooro jago pere kelo wich Yohana Jakibatisa.
41006028	Jago okelo wich Yohana i sen to miyo nyako no, aka nyano omiyo yokimere.
41006029	Munyo jofuonjirok pa Yohana jowinjo gime, jobino to jokwanyo delkwoŋ Yohana to joyiko.
41006030	Jomoor jodwoko bongi Yesu to jowacho ri go gimoro jye ma jotimo gi ma jofuonjo.
41006031	Aka owacho ri jo ni, “Biye wakidhi win kamoro kakendiwan wiywomereye mathin,” rupiri ji kweth oido jobino aka joman jokadho moido jomono kir jomoor chiemo.
41006032	Gikenyo jodonjo i yee, to jokidho kama bu ji, kama di jonyalo bed'iye kendigin.
41006033	To ji mathoth joneno munyo jokadho, aka joŋeyo jo, ri ameno joredo korago gi ŋwech wok i tindi jye, aka jotelo kir tundo kenyo ri Yesu gini.
41006034	Munyo Yesu otundo loka, oneno kweth ji to mako wor gi jo, kwoŋbedo oido jochalo roombo ma bu jakwath, amomiyo ochako fuonjo jo gikipiny momore.
41006035	Munyo piny onwaŋo chiegin yutho, jofuonjirok pere jobino bonge to jowacho ri go ni, “Kole ka dyer thim, aka piny chiegin yutho;
41006036	sewila ji jowokidhi loka kodi i tindi ma chiegin jowonyiew chiemo achama.”
41006037	Yesu odwoko ni, “Win ama wimiy jo chiemo achama.” Jopenjo go ni, “Imito wakidhi wanyiew mugat ma siringi gana pyero aŋwen wamiy jo jowochami?”
41006038	Gikenyo Yesu openjo jo ni, “Winitye gi mugat adi? Kidhi win winen.” Munyo jonwaŋo mugat jowacho ri go ni, “Mugat abich gi rech aryo.”
41006039	Gikenyo Yesu ooro ji bedo piny i lum, i kitipin.
41006040	Ji jobedo piny, i kitipin ma ji miya achielechiele kodi ma pyero abichabich.
41006041	Gikenyo Yesu okwanyo mugat abich gi rech aryo no, oŋiyo polo, to ketho Were walwa, aka oturo mugat to miyo jofuonjirok pere poko ji. Opok ji jye, rech aryo no bende.
41006042	Dhano jye ochiemo oyeŋ.
41006043	Gikenyo jofuonjirok jochoko ŋinjeŋinje mugat gi rech modoŋ poŋ aditin apar g'aryo.
41006044	Chwo ma jochiemo jobedo gana abich.
41006045	Ma piyo, Yesu ooro jofuonjirok pere donjo i yee jowoteli kadho yu loka Bethsaida, kareno go fuodi sewila kweth ji.
41006046	Munyo otyeko kisewila jofuonjirok pere, okidho wi tendere kwayo.
41006047	Munyo piny oyutho, yee onwaŋo nitye i dyer wakawaka, kareno Yesu ni kende kamothwo.
41006048	Go oneno jofuonjirok pere jofamba gi chiewo yee, rupiri koyo oido owok yu wiy jo dwoko jo chien. Munyo piny otundo keko, i dyer sawa abuŋwen kodi apar g'aryo, Yesu obino bongi jo munyo wotho wi pi. Onwaŋo go kadho kwoŋ jo,
41006049	to joneno go wotho wi pi. Joparo ni go yamo to jokoko,
41006050	rupiri munyo joneno go, lworo omako jo swa. Yesu oluwo gi jo mayot, ka wacho ni, “Wikiri wirembi, me an. Wikiri wilwori!”
41006051	Gikenyo go odonjo i yee bongi jo, to koyo kwe. Jofuonjirok jodhyer swa,
41006052	rupiri fuodi oido jokoniaŋ odocho kwoŋ giraura ma mugat; oido tek ri jo niaŋ gino.
41006053	Yesu gi jofuonjirok pere jokalo wakawaka to jotundo loka Genesaret, kuma jotwey'iye yee pajo kwoŋ loch.
41006054	Munyo jowok i yee, ji joŋeyo Yesu mayot.
41006055	Ji joringo, jothoko piny i adech no parom, to jokelo ri go jotwo ma jotiŋo i par, kama jowinjo ni go ni iye.
41006056	Aka kama Yesu okidh'iye jye, i adech moro, i tindi, kosa loka moro, ji jokelo ri go jotwo i katale, to jokwayo go ni woyeyi jotwo jowogeyi kada nyaka dhoki nanga pere won; aka joma jogeyo dhoki nanga pere jye jobedo maber.
41007001	Jofarisayo kodi jofuonji ma Chik megi ma jowok Yerusalem jochokere bongi Yesu,
41007002	aka joneno jofuonjirok pere megi jochiemo gi chingi gin ma di chilo, dwoŋ mere ni jokologo maber andha, aka chik pa Joyudaya kiyeyi gino.
41007003	(Ato Jofarisayo kodi Joyudaya joluwo kite pa kwarerejo machon, ma oido kichiem ma fuodi kologi paka chik mere wacho.
41007004	Ka jowok i katale jokichiem ma fuodi jokolwoko kor chingi jo gipi paka chik wacho. Odoko nitye kite man ma thoththoth ma jomako paka lwoko kikopere, degi, kodi atewe.)
41007005	Amomiyo Jofarisayo me kodi jofuonji ma Chik jopenjo go ni, “Raŋo ma jofuonjirok perin jokiluw kite pa kwarerewan machon, kabedo ma chiemo gi chingi gin ma di chilo?”
41007006	To go wacho ni, “Kere Isaya chango oluwo giradyeri kwoŋ wijorendirok i Ndiiko Maleŋ ni, ‘Ji me jomiyan dwoŋ gi dhoki gin kende, to chuny gin nitye bor kodan.
41007007	Jokilaman g'adyeri aka gima jofuonjo obedo nyaka kula ma ji wegi ama joketho.’
41007008	“Wibolo gichien or pa Were to wichwire kwoŋ kula paji ayino.”
41007009	Yesu omedere gi wacho ni, “Wiryek swa ri nwaŋo royo ma bolo gichien chik pa Were, ŋey witiy gi kula mewin wegi!
41007010	Kole Musa chango owodho chik ni, ‘Lwori benin gi yokin,’ gi man ni,
41007011	‘Ŋata luwo marach kwoŋ bamere kasa yokimere wonek woko.’ To win wifuonjo ni ka moro nitye gi gimoro ma go oido nyalo konyo gine bamere kosa yokimere, to wacho ni, ‘Me Korban,’ (dwoŋ mere ni gipa Were)
41007012	meno go onyo otyeko limo ka goŋirok ma kwero konyo bamere kosa yokimere.
41007013	Ameno wichayo wach pa Were gi kula ma wiwegi wifuonjo ji, aka winitye gi gikipiny man mathoth ma chale gi me ma wikethere timo.”
41007014	Yesu odoko olwoŋo ji bonge to wacho ri jo ni, “Chiki win ithi win wijojye aka winiaŋ gima akidho wacho.
41007015	Gima woko ma donjo i dhano ama kiloki go makoch, to gima wok i chunye ama loko go makoch.
41007016	[Ŋata ni gi ithe ma winjo wowinji. ”]
41007017	Munyo go oeye bothi kweth ji to donjo i ot, jofuonjirok pere jopenjo go dwoŋ agecha no.
41007018	Yesu owacho ni, “Kere wibende wikuya? Fuodi wikiniaŋ kwoŋ gime? Wikiniaŋi ni gima woko ma donjo i dhano ama kiloki go makoch,
41007019	rupiri kidonji i chunye, to donjo i iye ayino aka rumachien wok woko?” (Gi wach no, Yesu onyutho ni chiemo jye ber achama.)
41007020	Aka omedo wacho ni, “Kole gima wok i dhano ama loko go makoch,
41007021	rupiri i chuny dhano ama recho chakere iye: chot, kwo, nek, turo chik ma nywomirok,
41007022	woro, recho, twodo, kidakana, nyieko, kedho recho pa joman, pakirok kodi timo gimiŋo.
41007023	Recho me jye wok i dhano aka loko go makoch.”
41007024	Yesu oeye kenyo to kidho i adech ma chiegin gi tindi ma Tire kodi Sidon. Go odonjo i ot, aka komito ni nyatoro woŋeyi ni go nitye kenyo, to konyalo muŋere.
41007025	Gikenyo dhako moro, ma chuny mochido oido ni kwoŋ nyare, owinjo kwoŋ Yesu to bino bonge mayot, to podho katyende.
41007026	Dheno onwaŋo obedo Japath, anywola ma Fonisya ma wok Sirya. Go okwayo Yesu nike woryemi woko jwogi no kwoŋ nyare.
41007027	To Yesu dwoko ni, “Weyi kutho watel pidho nyithindho; kobedo gimotire kwanyo chiemo pa nyithindho gi bolo ri gwokere.”
41007028	Ana dheno, “Ey, Jadwoŋ, to kole kada gwokere ma tyendi meza bende jochamoye kada nyaka ŋinjeŋinje chiemo ma nyithindho jochamo odoŋ!”
41007029	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Ro luwo perin me, ere doki pecho, jwogi otyeko wok kwoŋ nyarin!”
41007030	Dhako no odok pecho to nwaŋo nyare i kanindo kareno jwogi adyeri otyeko wok kwoŋe kichutho.
41007031	Yesu owok i adech ma Tire to luwo royo ma Sidon, i adech ma Dekapoli, munyo kidho dho wakawaka ma Galileya.
41007032	Jomogo jokelo ri go obadha ma ithe otho aka lewe odole, to jokwayo Yesu ni wokethi chinge kwoŋe.
41007033	Yesu okwanyo ŋato otero gichien, aka oketho lwet chinge i ithe aryo jye, to ŋulo law i chinge to geyo gine lew ŋato.
41007034	Gikenyo Yesu oŋiyo malo i polo, to omo chunye tektek, aka owacho ri ŋato ni, “Efufata,” nyaka ni “Yawere.”
41007035	Piyo piyo no ithi ŋato oyawere, tyendi lewe ogonyere, to chako luwo maber.
41007036	Yesu ochiko jo teltel ni kiri jowowachi ri nyatoro. To paka omedo chiko jo, apaka bende jomedo nyayo wach no iye jye.
41007037	Ji jye ma jowinjo wach no jouro swa. Jowacho ni, “Go otimo gimoro jye maber; go miyo kir joma ithi gin otho winjo wach, kodi obadhin luwo.”
41008001	Rumachien ma ndelo manok, muma ji man madwoŋ odoko ochokere kanyachiel. Munyo chiemo orumo kwoŋ jo, Yesu olwoŋo jofuonjirok pere to wacho ri jo ni,
41008002	“Chunyan raman ri ji me, rupiri jotyeko bedo kodan ndelo adek gipi, aka onyo pama jongoye gi girachama.
41008003	Ka anowachi ri jo dok pecho ma akikutho amiyo jo chiemo, jobino loch i royo to jopodho, aka megi kwoŋ jo jowok kama bor tektek.”
41008004	Jofuonjirok pere jopenjo go ni, “Kune i thim ka ma dhano nyalo nwaŋ'iye chiemo ma yeŋo ji me jye?”
41008005	Yesu openjo jo ni, “Winitye gi mugat adi?” Jodwoko ni, “Mugat abiryo.”
41008006	Gikenyo go ooro muma ji bedo piny. Aka okwanyo mugat abiryo no, oketho Were walwa, oturo, to miyo jofuonjirok pere poko ji, to jofuonjirok jotimo ameno.
41008007	Jo onwaŋo jo ni gi nyaka ongwek mathindho thindho manok bende. Munyo Yesu otyeko ketho Were walwa, oturo rech no bende, aka owacho ri jofuonjirok poko ji.
41008008	Dhano jye ochiemo oyeŋ; aka jochoko ŋinjeŋinje modoŋ,
41008009	to poŋo aditin abiryo.
41008010	Piyo piyo no Yesu odonjo i yee gi jofuonjirok pere, to jokidho i adech ma Dalmanutha.
41008011	Jofarisayo mogo jobino bongi Yesu to jochako pyem gine, to jokwayo go ni wotimi giraura ma nyutho ni men pere wok bongi Were. Oido chiko go.
41008012	Yesu oywe ywe mabor aka owacho ni, “Raŋo ma luse ji me jokwayo ranyuth? Adyeri awacho ri win, ongoye ranyuth mibino miyo ji me.”
41008013	Gikenyo oweyo jo, ogik i yee, to chiewere loka man.
41008014	Jofuonjirok wiy jo owil gi kwanyo mugat mogo, aka oido jonitye gi mugat achiel kende i yee.
41008015	Yesu ofuonjo jo ni, “Gwokere win, aka kure win kwoŋ thow pa Jofarisayo kodi thow pa Herode.”
41008016	Jofuonjirok jochako luwo kendigin ni, “Go wacho ama rupiri wakitiŋo mugat mogo!”
41008017	Yesu oŋeyo gima onwaŋo jowacho, ri ameno openjo jo ni, “Raŋo ma wiluwo kendiwin kwoŋ mugat ma wikitiŋo? Fuodi wikiniaŋ kwoŋ gimotimere ndir cha; chuny win olokere manwaŋi?
41008018	Winitye gi waŋ win to raŋo wikinyal neno? Winitye gi ithi win to raŋo wikinyal winjo?
41008019	Kere i ndelo ma atur'iye mugat abich ri ji gana abich, aditin adi mopoŋ'iye ŋinjeŋinje ma wichoko?” Jodwoko ni, “Apar g'aryo.”
41008020	Yesu odoko openjo jo ni, “Aka munyo aturo mugat abiryo ri ji gana aŋwen, aditin adi mopoŋ'iye ŋinjeŋinje modoŋ ma wichoko?” Jodwoko ni, “Abiryo.”
41008021	To penjo jo ni, “Onyo fuodi wikiniaŋ kwoŋ gime?”
41008022	Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere jotundo Bethsaida kama jomogo jokel'iye ri go ŋata waŋe otho, to jokwayo Yesu ni wogey go.
41008023	Yesu omako chingi ŋato to tero go gi bor wok i adech no. Munyo otyeko ŋulo law i waŋ ŋato, oketho chinge kwoŋe to penjo go ni, “Inyalo neno gimoro?”
41008024	Ŋato otemo neno to wacho ni, “Ey, anyalo neno ji, to jochalo yen ma wotho.”
41008025	Aka Yesu odoko oketho chinge i waŋ ŋato. Ru me ŋato oyaro waŋe kendo waŋe obedo maber, to chako neno gimoro jye maber.
41008026	Yesu ooro go wodoki pecho gi wach me ni, “Ikiri i donji i adech ma Bethsaida.”
41008027	Rumachien Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere jomako royo ma kidho i adech ma Keserya mapa Filipo. Munyo jowotho, openjo jo ni, “Wachi ran win: Ji jowacho ni an aŋa?”
41008028	Jodwoko ni, “Jomegi jowacho ni in Yohana Jakibatisa, joman ni in Eliya, aka joman ni in achiel kwoŋ jotuchi wach Were.”
41008029	Aka go openjo jo ni, “To win, wiwacho ni an aŋa?” Petro odwoko ni, “In Kristo!”
41008030	Yesu ochiko jo ni, “Wikiri wiwachi ri nyatoro gima wiŋeyo kwoŋan.”
41008031	Gikenyo Yesu ochako fuonjo jofuonjirok pere ni Wuodi Dhano bino chandere tektek, kendo jotel pa ji kodi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jofuonji ma Chik jobino kwero go. Ibino neko go to i ndelo maradek go bino chierino.
41008032	Otito ri jo gino maber swa. Gikenyo Petro otero go gichien to chako kipusa go.
41008033	To Yesu wire ŋiyo jofuonjirok pere, to bwoko Petro ni, “Eye bongan, Sitan. Paro perin obedo paro pa ji ma kiweno apa Were.”
41008034	Rumachien Yesu olwoŋo muma ji kodi jofuonjirok pere bonge, to wacho ri jo ni, “Ŋata mito bino bongan, won mito wokwerere kende kendo wotiŋi musalaba pere woluwan.
41008035	Rupiri ŋata mito botho kwo pere bino rwenyo woko, to ŋata rwenyo woko kwo pere kwoŋbedo an kodi ru Wach Maber, bino botho kwo pere.
41008036	Aŋo ma dhano olim ka oloki piny gipi apere, to rwenyo woko kwo pere won?
41008037	Aŋo ma dhano nyalo miyo ma wilo gine kwo pere?
41008038	Amomiyo ka dhano wiye okwoti kodan gi fuonji paran, i ndir ma ji kuy'iye Were, ndir ma ji odakan iye, Wuodi Dhano bende wiye bino kwot gi ŋato ka go dwoko i dwoŋ pa Bamere kanyachiel gi jomalaika maleŋ.”
41009001	Aka omedo wacho ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, nitye jomegi kwoŋ win ka ma jokotho ma fuodi jokoneno Ker pa Were ka bino gi men.”
41009002	Munyo ndelo auchiel okadho, Yesu okwanyo Petro gi Yakobo gi Yohana, to tero jo wi got mabor kakendigin. Gikenyo chal pere owire ruwaŋ jo,
41009003	aka nengin pere olokere matar, ma minyin ma ongoye ŋata nyalo lwoko nengin to lony matar amanago.
41009004	Gikenyo joneno Eliya gi Musa munyo joluwo gi Yesu.
41009005	Petro oluwo malo ka wacho ri Yesu ni, “Jafuonji, ber ri wan bedo ka, weyi wageti kayindin adek, achiel rin, achiel ri Musa, achiel ri Eliya.”
41009006	Ato oido go kuya girawacha, rupiri lworo oido omako jo tektek.
41009007	Pondeponde obino to umo jo gi tipo mere, aka derino owok i pondeponde ma wacho ni, “Me Wuodan ma amaro, winji win, go.”
41009008	Gikenyo jopoyo munyo joneno korin gi korin, to jokoneno nyatoro man kwanyo woko Yesu won kende gi jo.
41009009	Munyo joloro wi got, Yesu ochiko jo ni, “Wikiri wiwachi ri nyatoro gima wiwok neno, chuka Wuodi Dhano otyeki chierino kwoŋ jomotho.”
41009010	Jofuonjirok joliŋ gi wach no, to wegi jopenjere kendigin ni dwoŋ chierino kwoŋ jomotho no obedo aŋo.
41009011	Aka jopenjo Yesu ni, “Raŋo ma jofuonji ma Chik jowacho ni Eliya ama ripo telo bino?”
41009012	Yesu odwoko ni,
41009013	“Adyeri Eliya ama kutho ripo telo bino ŋey woyiki gimoro jye. To raŋo ma Ndiiko Maleŋ bende wacho ni Wuodi Dhano bino limo chandirok madwoŋ tikwero go? Awacho ri win, kole Eliya otyeko bino to ji jotimo ri go gima joyenyo jye, paka Ndiiko Maleŋ luwo kwoŋe.”
41009014	Munyo Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere adek no jogik bongi jofuonjirok pere man, jonwaŋo ji kweth jothoko jono kareno jofuonji ma Chik jopyemo kodi jo.
41009015	Tekin ji joneno Yesu, jobwok swa to joringo bothe to jomotho go.
41009016	Yesu openjo ni, “Oido wipyemo aŋo gi jo?”
41009017	Ŋatachiel i dyer ji odwoko ni, “Jafuonji, akelo wuodan bongin, rupiri chuny mochido ni kwoŋe aka kinyal kada luwo.
41009018	Hongo jye ka jwogi no omwonjo go, rwato go piny, aka bwoyo wok i dhoke, aka mwodo lake, to thwo matek. Akwayo jofuonjirok perin ni joworyemi woko jwogi no, to jokonyalo.”
41009019	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “A luse ji mongoye gi yeyo! Anobedi gi win kir keraŋo? Anodiy chunyan gi win kir keraŋo? Keli win go bongan ka.”
41009020	Jokelo jayach no bongi Yesu, to tekin jwogi mani kwoŋe neno Yesu, go opodho piny, to ŋindere i lowo kareno bwoyo wok i dhoke.
41009021	Yesu openjo bamere ni, “Ochowo hongo aŋo nyuka jwogi maki go?” Go odwoko ni,
41009022	“Wok i thino pere. Ndir madit otemo neko go munyo bolo go i mach kodi i pi. Maki gi wan wor, k'inyalo i kony wan!”
41009023	Yesu odwoko ni, “K'inyalo kendo ayin! Gimoro jye nyalere ri dhano mani gi yeyo.”
41009024	Piyo no baa jayach oluwo malo ni, “Anitye gi yeyo, to won kiromi, konyan!”
41009025	Munyo Yesu oneno muma ji rikere kwoŋe, owodho or ri chuny mochido ni, “Jwogi no ma ithe otho, mobadha, aryemin eye kwoŋ jayach me aka ikiri i giki kwoŋe kendo.”
41009026	Jwogi okoko malo, omiyo jayach no otho fum, to eye kwoŋe. Jayach no ochalo p'otho, momiyo dhano jye owacho ni, “Otyeko tho.”
41009027	To Yesu omako chinge to tiŋo go malo, to won tekere chungo.
41009028	Munyo Yesu otyeko donjo i ot, jofuonjirok pere jopenjo go nyaliŋliŋ ni, “Raŋo ma wakinyalo ryemo woko jwogi no?”
41009029	Yesu odwoko ni, “Kiti jwogi me ryemo mere tek ka ongoye kwayo gi riyo.”
41009030	Yesu gi jofuonjirok pere munyo jowok kenyo, joluwo Galileya. Go komito ji jowoŋeyi kama go ni iye,
41009031	rupiri oido go fuodi fuonjo jofuonjirok pere, ka wacho ri jo ama: “Ibino mako Wuodi Dhano tiketho i chingi joma jobino neko go; to chieŋ maradek go bino chierino.”
41009032	To jokoniaŋ dwoŋ wach no, to jolworo penjo go.
41009033	Yesu gi jofuonjirok pere jobino Kapernaum, aka munyo jo ni ot, openjo jo ni, “Onwaŋo wipyemo aŋo i royo?”
41009034	Jokodwoko go, kwoŋbedo oido nyaka jowok pyem wegi kendigin ni ŋa kwoŋ jo malayo wadi gi dwoŋ.
41009035	Yesu obedo piny, olwoŋo japar ga'ryo no to wacho ri jo ni, “Ŋata mito bedo marapena, ripo bedo machowe kwoŋ ji jye, kendo jatich ri wadi jye.”
41009036	Gikenyo go okwanyo nyathi moro, to wacho ri go chungo i dyer jo, to ketho chinge umo gine go, to wacho ri jo ni,
41009037	“Dhano jye ma jolo nyaka nyathi me i nyingan, meno jolan; aka ŋata jolan meno kijolan kendan, to jolo kir ŋata ooran bende.”
41009038	Gikenyo Yohana owacho ri Yesu ni, “Jafuonji, wanwaŋo ŋat moro ryemo woko jwogi i nyingin; to paka go kobedo achiel kwoŋ wan, wachiero go timo ameno.”
41009039	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Wikiri wichieri go; ongoye ŋata timo giraura i nyingan ma nyalo luwo kwoŋan marach.
41009040	Ŋata kimon gi wan, meno tiyere gi wan.
41009041	Adyeri awacho ri win, nyatoro jye momiyi win agwata pi amadha kwoŋbedo wi ji pa Kristo, go kibino keŋ kemba pere.
41009042	“Moro jye momiyi nyithindho me timo recho, d'ober ka otwey kidi madwoŋ i ŋute tibolo go i pendi wakawaka.
41009043	Aka ka chingin achiel rwakin i gimarach, ŋondi woko; kole ber rin donjo i kwo makirum gi chingin achiel loyo kidho gi chingin aryo jye i mach makitho,
41009044	[kuma kudin ma iye kitho, aka mach mere kitho.]
41009045	Aka ka tyendin achiel rwakin i gimarach, ŋondi woko; kole ber rin donjo i kwo makirum, miŋol loyo bolin i mach makitho gi tyendin aryo jye,
41009046	[kuma kudin ma iye kitho, aka mach mere kitho.]
41009047	Aka ka waŋin achiel rwakin i gimarach, goli woko; kole ber rin donjo i Ker pa Were gi waŋin achiel, loyo bedo gi waŋin aryo jye tibolin i mach makitho,
41009048	kuma kudin ma iye kitho, aka mach mere kitho.
41009049	“Kole dhano jye ibino loko maber pa gima othol i mach gi chumbi.
41009050	Kado chumbi ber, to ka olokere maboth, winyalo nedi dwoko ri go mito mere? Bedi win pa chumbi mamit i kite mewin, aka nyaka winobedi gi syem i dyer win.”
41010001	Yesu oeye kenyo to kidho i adech ma Yudeya kodi loka man ma Jwom Yordan. Kweth ji jobino bonge to go fuonjo jo, paka ndir jye oido omaro timo.
41010002	Jofarisayo mogo jobino bongi Yesu to jopenjo go ma temo go ni, “Chik yeyo dhano ryemo chiege?”
41010003	Yesu odwoko ni, “Musa chango ooro win timo nedi?”
41010004	Jowacho ni, “Musa oyeyo jachwo ndiko balwa maryemo chiege ka pokere gine.”
41010005	To Yesu wacho ri jo ni, “Musa ondiko ri win chik no, rupiri chuny win tek.
41010006	To wok i chakirok pa chwech, ‘Were ochweyo jachwo gi dhako.’
41010007	‘Amomiyo jachwo bino weyo bamere gi min, to chwire kwoŋ chiege,
41010008	to jaryo jolokere del achiel.’ Ri ameno jo onyo kidel aryo to del achiel.
41010009	Amomiyo gima Were otyeko riwo kanyachiel, wongoye nyatoro ma wopoki.”
41010010	Munyo jogik i ot, jofuonjirok pere jopenjo go kendo dwoŋ wach no.
41010011	Aka owacho ri jo ni, “Ŋata pokere gi chiege to nywomo dhako man, meno timo chot,
41010012	aka ameno bende, dhako ma pokere gi chwore to nywomere gi jachwo man, meno timo chot.”
41010013	Ji mogo jokelo nyithindho bongi Yesu ni wogeyi jo, to jofuonjirok pere joay kwoŋ jo.
41010014	Munyo Yesu oneno ameno, nge omako go gi jofuonjirok pere, to wacho ri jo ni, “Weyi nyithindho jowobin bongan; wikiri wichieri jo, kole Ker pa Were obedo apa joma pameno.
41010015	Adyeri awacho ri win, ŋata kojolo Ker pa Were paka nyathi mathin, kibino donj'iye.”
41010016	Gikenyo Yesu otwodo nyithindho gi chinge, oketho chinge kwoŋ jo, to miyo jo silwany.
41010017	Munyo Yesu ochako woth pere kendo, jal moro obino gi ŋwech to ryewere piny ruwaŋe to penjo go ni, “Jafuonji maber, atim aŋo ŋey alim kwo makirum?”
41010018	Yesu odwoko go ni, “Raŋo ilwoŋan ni maber? Ongoye ŋataber kwanyo woko Were kende.
41010019	Iŋeyo Or pa Were ma wacho ni, ‘Ikiri ineki, ikiri itim chot; ikiri ikwali; ikiri isegeya dhano nono; ikiri iwondi ji; ikiri icham gimahembi; lwori benin gi yokin.’ ”
41010020	Jalo odwoko ni, “Jafuonji, atyeko mako or no jye wok i thino paran.”
41010021	Gikenyo Yesu oŋiyo go gi mar to wacho ri go ni, “Gimoro achiel ama fuodi odoŋ rin timo: kidhi itana woko gima ini gine jye, pesa mere ipoki jochandi, aka ibino limo ŋaŋo i polo; aka ŋey ibin iluwan.”
41010022	Wach me okweyo kwoŋ jalo swa, to miyo go gut, rupiri go oido oŋaŋ tektek.
41010023	Yesu obolo waŋe oŋiyo korin gi korin, to wacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Bino bedo matek adyeri ri jaŋaŋo donjo i Ker pa Were!”
41010024	Jofuonjirok jodhyer swa kwoŋ wach me, to Yesu medo wacho ri jo ni, “Nyithindho paran, tek swa ri joma geno ŋaŋo donjo i Ker pa Were!
41010025	Yot ri ŋamira donjo i yore piso loyo ri jaŋaŋo donjo i Ker pa Were!”
41010026	Jofuonjirok jomedo dhyer, to wegi jowacho kendigin ni, “Ka ameno onyo ŋa won ma nyalo both?”
41010027	Yesu oŋiyo jo to wacho ni, “Ri dhano gime kinyalere, to ki ri Were, rupiri Were nyalo gimoro jye.”
41010028	Petro to ero wacho ni, “Aka wan to? Kole watyeko weyo gimoro jye to waluwin.”
41010029	Yesu odwoko ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, ongoye ŋata oweyi ot, wutimin, nyimin, yokimere, bamere, nyithindho, kosa lowo kwoŋbedo an kodi Wach Maber,
41010030	ma kibino limo gikipiny di miya achiel: udi, wutimin, nyimin, bachere mere, mege, nyithindho kodi lowo, kodi chandirok i ndir ma pama, to limo kwo makirum rumachien.
41010031	Aka ji madit ma pama jobedo marapena ama jobino bedo machowe; aka joma oido machowe ama jobino bedo marapena.”
41010032	Yesu kodi joma oido ni gi go onwaŋo jo ni royo jochomo yu Yerusalem kareno go otelo jo. Jofuonjirok pere jouro wach pere; aka ji moido joluwo jo bende lworo omako jo. Yesu odoko otero jofuonjirok apar g'aryo gichien to luwo kwoŋ gima onwaŋo kidho timirok kwoŋe.
41010033	Owacho ri jo ni, “Winji win, onyo wakidho Yerusalem kuma ibino keth'iye Wuodi Dhano i chingi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jofuonji ma Chik. Jobino thumo ri go banja ma tho, to joketho go i chingi Jopath.
41010034	Jono jobino nyiero go, ŋulo kwoŋe law, chwado go, gi neko go. To i ndelo maradek, go bino chierino.”
41010035	Yakobo gi Yohana, woti Zebedayo, jobino bongi Yesu to jowacho ri go ni, “Jafuonji, nitye gima wayenyo itim ri wan.”
41010036	Yesu openjo jo ni, “Aŋo ma wiyenyo atim ri win?”
41010037	Jodwoko ni, “Yeyi wabedi ŋatachiel yu chingin marachuch, ŋat man yu racham, i dwoŋ perin.”
41010038	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Wikuya gima wikwayo. Winyalo madho agwata ma anomadhi, gi limo batisimo ma anolim?”
41010039	Jodwoko ni, “Wanyalo.” Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Agwata ma anomadhi wibende wibino madho, odoko batisimo ma anolim wibende wibino limo,
41010040	to kabedo ma yu chingan marachuch kosa maracham kobedo tich paran poko. Me kabedo pa joma otyek yiko ri jo.”
41010041	Munyo jomoor wadi gin japar jowinjo wach no, nge omako jo gi Yakobo kodi Yohana,
41010042	omiyo Yesu olwoŋo jo bonge to wacho ri jo ni, “Wiŋeyo ni jodhum ma piny jodhumo ji gi maker; aka jotel pajo jodhumo gi mbaka.
41010043	To me k'apaka ripo bedo gi win. Ka nyatoro kwoŋ win mito bedo jadwoŋ, go ripo bedo jatich ri wadi;
41010044	aka ŋata mito bedo jatel i dyer win, ripo bedo ŋecha pa wadi jye.
41010045	Kole kada Wuodi Dhano bende kobino ni wotiy ri go; to obino ni wotiyi ri ji ayin kodi miyo kwo pere paka gichul ma gonyo ji mathoth.”
41010046	Yesu gi jofuonjirok pere jotundo Yeriko. Aka munyo joay kenyo, gi kweth ji, jakwach ma waŋe otho, milwoŋo ni Batimayo, ma dwoŋ mere ni wuodi pa Timayo onwaŋo obedo piny i thengi royo.
41010047	Tekin Batimayo winjo ni manago Yesu Janazareth ama kadho, to chako koko ka wacho ni, “Yesu, Wuodi pa Daudi, timi reye wor!”
41010048	Ji mathoth jobwoko go aka jooro go liŋ, to go omedo ameda koko malo ayino ni, “Wuodi pa Daudi, timi reye wor!”
41010049	Yesu ochungo to wacho ni, “Lwoŋi win go ka.” To jolwoŋo jal ma waŋe otho no, ka jowacho ri go ni, “Ikiri irembi, ayi malo, kole go dicha lwoŋin.”
41010050	Gikenyo go obolo nanga pere gichien, opor malo, to kidho bongi Yesu.
41010051	Yesu openjo go ni, “Imito atim rin aŋo?” Jal ma waŋe otho no owacho ni, “Jafuonji, yawi ran waŋan.”
41010052	To Yesu wacho ri go ni, “Kadhi, yeyo perin obothin.” Piyo piyo no, waŋe oyawere, to bende luwo Yesu.
41011001	Munyo joriko Yerusalem, i tindi ma Bethfage kodi Bethaniya, chiegin gi got Olivet, Yesu ooro jofuonjirok pere aryo kadho yu wiye,
41011002	gi wach me ni, “Kidhi win loka ma yu wiy win, aka tekin widonj'iye wibino nwaŋo nyathi punda motwey, ma fuodi dhano kobedo i wiye; gonyi to wikelo ka.
41011003	Ka moro openji win ni, ‘Witimo aŋo?’ Wachi win ni, ‘Ruoth ama yenyo punda me aka bino dwoko go ka mayot.’ ”
41011004	Jokidho to jonwaŋo nyathi punda moro otwey dhoot i thengi royo, to jogonyo.
41011005	To jomogo monwaŋo jochungo kenyo jopenjo jo ni, “Witimo aŋo no? Raŋo ma wigonyo nyathi punda no?”
41011006	Jodwoko paka Yesu owacho ri jo, to jono joweyo jo, to jokadho gi nyathi punda no.
41011007	Jokelo nyathi punda no ri Yesu, to jopedho nengin i dyeŋeye, to Yesu bedo i wiye.
41011008	Ji mathoth jopedho nengin i royo, aka joman jopedho jangi yen ma joturo i dudi.
41011009	Aka joma jotelo yu wiye kodi joma joluwo go yu chien jowero ni, “Ozana! Jasilwany a ŋata bino i nyingi Ruoth!
41011010	Silwany wobedi ri Ker mabino mapa bawan Daudi! Ozana malo i polo!”
41011011	Yesu otundo Yerusalem, to donjo i Ot pa Were; aka munyo otyeko ŋiyo korin gi korin oneno gimoro jye, owok to kadho Bethaniya gi jofuonjirok apar g'aryo, paka piny oido kidho yutho.
41011012	Yawere mere munyo jo ni royo jodwoko wok Bethaniya, Yesu onwaŋo winjo kech.
41011013	Munyo go oneno giborbor kiti makuyu moro michamo, ma boke otweyere kwoŋe, okidho neno ni kono nyalo nwaŋo kwoŋe nyandere, to munyo otundo dho tyende, konwaŋo gimoro kwanyo woko bokee; rupiri meno oido ki ndir ma nyandere nyak'iye.
41011014	Yesu owacho ri makuyu no ni, “Ongoye moro modoko ocham nyandere kwoŋin.” To jofuonjirok pere jowinjo gima go owacho no.
41011015	Munyo jotundo Yerusalem, Yesu odonjo i Ot pa Were, to chako ryemo woko joma nyiewere kodi jomiten i Ot pa Were. Oryewo mezin pa jowili pesa, kodi kombere pa joma onwaŋo jotana akurin;
41011016	aka koyeyo kada moro wotho gi gimoro i Ot pa Were.
41011017	Ofuonjo jo ka wacho ni, “Kondik i Ndiiko Maleŋ ni Ot paran ibino lwoŋo ni Ot ma kwayo mapa nonin jye? Ama win wiloko kapondo pa jokwo ayino!”
41011018	Jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jofuonji ma Chik jowinjo gime to jochako rango royo ma neko Yesu. To jolworo go, rupiri muma ji gi bee oido odhyer kwoŋ fuonji pere.
41011019	Munyo piny oyutho Yesu gi jofuonjirok pere joeye i tindi no.
41011020	Yawere mere odikini, munyo jowotho i royo, jonwaŋo makuyu no othwo wok malo kir i tyende.
41011021	Petro opoyo gima nyoro otimere to wacho ri Yesu ni, “Jafuonji, panen! Makuyu ma nyoro ikwoŋo cha otyeko thwo!”
41011022	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Bedi win gi yeyo i Were. Adyeri awacho ri win,
41011023	ŋata owachi ri got me ni, ‘Mukere woko, ikidhi imunyere i wakawaka,’ aka ongoye gi kiganagana i chunye, to yeyo ni gima go owacho bino timere, ibino timo ri go gino.
41011024	Amomiyo awacho ri win, ka wikwayo gimoro, yeyi win ni wityeko limo aka ibino miyo win gimoro jye ma wikwayo.
41011025	Aka ka wichungo wikwayo, chwaki win recho jye ma nyatoro otimo ri win, aka nyaka Baa win mani polo bende bino chwako recho mewin.
41011026	[Ka wikichwaki jowoti win, kada Baa win mani polo bende kibino chwako recho mewin.”]
41011027	Odoko jogik Yerusalem, aka munyo Yesu oido wotho i Ot pa Were to jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jofuonji ma Chik kanyachiel kodi jotel pa ji jobino bonge to jopenjo go ni,
41011028	“Inwaŋo men kune ma timo gikipiny me? Kosa ŋa momiyin men ma timo gikipiny me?”
41011029	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Alepenjo win gimoro achiel kende; dwokan win aka abino wacho ri win kama anwaŋ'iye men ma timo gikipiny me.
41011030	Men pa Yohana ma miyo ji batisimo owok kune: bongi Were kosa bongi ji? Dwokan win.”
41011031	Wegi jochako pyem kendigin ni, “Wadwoki nedi? Ka wadwoko ni, ‘Owok i polo,’ go bino wacho ni, ‘To raŋo ma wikwero yeyo go?’
41011032	Kosa di wadwoki ni, ‘Owok bongi dhano?’ ” (Ato onwaŋo jolworo ji, rupiri dhano jye onwaŋo otero Yohana paka jatuchi wach Were.)
41011033	Gikenyo jodwoko Yesu ni, “Wakuya.” To Yesu wacho ri jo ni, “Abende akowachi ri win kama men ma atimo gine gime wok'iye.”
41012001	Gikenyo Yesu ochako luwo ri jo g'agechin ni: “Dhano moro opidho yen vini i ndelo, othoko ndelo no gi chiel, okunyo bur ma biyo vini to gero ot achurchur ma kur. Go oketho ndelo vini i chingi jofur mogo to kadho wiloka.
41012002	Munyo ndir otundo ma fuono vini, go ooro jago pere bongi jofur pere no ni jowolimi rigo gimonyak moro wok i vini.
41012003	Jofur no jomako jago no jogoyo, to joryemo go ma bu gimoro.
41012004	Gikenyo won ndelo ooro jago man; ma bende jofur jogoyo lero to jofuta go swa.
41012005	Won ndelo ooro jago man, to joneko meno; jotimo jegin man mathoth ameno, munyo jogoyo jomegi aka joneko joman.
41012006	Ŋata onwaŋo odoŋ aora bongi jofur oido obedo wuode won ma migos. Amomiyo rumachien ooro wuode won gipi bongi jofur ka wacho ni, ‘Adyer jobino woro wuodan.’
41012007	To jofur no jowacho wegi kendigin ni, ‘Me won a musika pa won ndelo, weyi waneki go aka waŋati walunji lim pere!’
41012008	Gikenyo jomako go to joneko, to jobolo delkwoŋe woko ma ndelo.”
41012009	Yesu openjo ni, “Onyo won ndelo no otimi aŋo? Kole go bino neko woko jofur marecho no to ketho ndelo i chingi jofur man.
41012010	Fuodi wikisoma i ndiko ma wacho ni, ‘Kole tele ma jogeto jochayo ni bu kony ama olokere tele ma thyelo kindi ot;
41012011	me obedo tich pa Ruoth aka neno maber swa ri wan!’ ”
41012012	Jotel pa Joyudaya jotemo mako Yesu, rupiri joŋeyo ni go oido obolo agecha me kwoŋ jo. To jolworo muma ji, amomiyo joweyo go to jokadho.
41012013	Jooro Jofarisayo mogo kodi jopa Herode bongi Yesu chiiko go i luwo pere.
41012014	Jobino bonge to jowacho ni, “Jafuonji, waŋeyo ni ibedo ŋatotire, aka ikilwori nyatoro; ikidew kwoŋ dwoŋ pa nyatoro, to ifuonjo giradyeri kwoŋ gima Were yenyo ri dhano ayino. Ere wachi ri wan; yeyere i Chik mawan goyo misolo ri Kaisar, kosa be?”
41012015	Yesu oneno apondi pajo to dwoko ni, “Raŋo ma witemo chiiko an? Keli win pesa moro anen.”

41015001	Odikini worwor, jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, kodi jotel pa ji, kodi jofuonji ma Chik, kodi jopido gi bee, joyiko paro kanyachiel. Jotweyo Yesu gi lijegere to jotero go i nyim Pilato.

41015004	To Pilato penjo go kendo ni, “Ingoye gi radwoki? Winji kweth wach ma ji jokelo kwoŋin.”

41015015	Pilato omito kisangala kweth ji, amomiyo ogonyo ri jo Baraba. To oro jo chwado Yesu, to yeyo jo guro go kwoŋ musalaba.
41015016	Joserikale jorwako Yesu i dyedipo pa Pilato to jolwoŋo wadi gin.
41015017	Joruko ri go nanga aywoya ma rangi ariŋo, to jodolo thach okudho to jorwako i wiye pa sangarya maradhum.
41015018	Aka jomotho go ni, “Yoga Kere pa Joyudaya!”
41015019	Jogoyo wiye gi luth, joŋulo kwoŋe law, joguro chongi gin, aka joryewere ri go piny pa jomiyo go dwoŋ.
41015020	Munyo jotyeko nyiero go ameno, jolunyo woko nanga ma rangi ariŋo no to joruko ri go nengin pere won. To jotero go wogur wi musalaba.
41015021	Joromo kodi Simon i royo munyo oido bino i tindi, to jochuko go gi tiŋo musalaba pa Yesu. (Ŋato oido Simon ma Sireno, baa Alekizanda kodi Rufus).
41015022	Jokelo Yesu kuma ilwoŋo ni Golgotha, dwoŋ mere ni Kabedo pa Kahanga wich.
41015023	Jotemo miyo go vini moruw gi pigi yath moro maŋwe kur makweyo litho, to Yesu komadho.
41015024	Joguro go kwoŋ musalaba, aka jopoko nengin pere gi kwir maŋeyo adech ma kis dhano d'otero.
41015025	Sawa oido obedo odikini kapa sawa adek mogur'iye go wi musalaba.
41015026	Me a wach mondik yu wiye: “Kere pa Joyudaya.”
41015027	Joguro jokwo aryo bende wi musalaba gi Yesu, ŋatachiel yu chinge marachuch ŋat man yu chinge maracham.
41015028	[Ameno randik otundo i kare, ma wacho ni, “Okwan go kwoŋ jomarecho.”]
41015029	Jomokadho i royo joyengo wiy gin aka joyeto Yesu ni, “Ha! In ama onwaŋo ikidho kedho Ot pa Were t'igero man i ndelo adek!
41015030	Ere palor'iye wi musalaba ibothere wanen!”
41015031	Jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jotel pa ji kodi jofuonji ma Chik bende jonyiero Yesu munyo joŋalo go ni, “Obotho joman, to won kinyal bothere.

41015034	I hongo ma sawa abuŋwen, Yesu okoko gi derino madwoŋ ni, “Eloi, Eloi, lama sabach thani!” nyaka ni, “Were paran, Were paran raŋo iweyan!”
41015035	Ji megi moido jonitye kenyo munyo jowinjo wach me jowacho ni, “Winji win, go dicha lwoŋo Eliya.”
41015036	Ŋatachiel kwoŋ jo oringo gi changwe, obilo i vini mawach, to ketho i dhoke gi yath mabor. Oketho i dhoki Yesu gino munyo wacho ni, “Weyi wanen paka Eliya obin ogony go kwoŋ musalaba.”
41015037	Yesu okoko gi derino madwoŋ to tho.
41015038	Aka nanga moido olyer i Ot pa Were oyech wok malo kir piny.
41015039	Jaserikale madwoŋ moido ochungo chiegin gi musalaba, oneno paka Yesu okoko gi derino aka otho to wacho ni, “Adyeri, me oido Wuodi Were!”
41015040	Mon mogo oido jo ni kenyo jochungo giborbor. Idyer jo oido nitye Salome, Marya ma wok Magdala kodi Marya min Yakobo mathin kodi Yose.
41015041	Mon me yado joluwo Yesu gi miyo go kony munyo go nitye Galileya; aka onwaŋo nitye mon man bende mathoth ma jobino gine kir i Yerusalem.
41015042	Munyo piny kidho yutho, Yozefu ma wok Arimatheya otundo. Go oido obedo ŋata ni gi dwoŋ swa i kweth pa jopido, aka onwaŋo kuro bino pa Ker pa Were. Ndelo no onwaŋo obedo ndelo ma yikirok (dwoŋ mere ni, ndelo ma telo Sabato).
41015043	ri ameno Yozefu otimo miseni to kidho bongi Pilato to kwayo go delkwoŋ Yesu.
41015044	Pilato ouro swa ni Yesu otyeko tho. Olwoŋo jaserikale madwoŋ to penjo go ka Yesu otyeko tho adyeri.
41015045	Munyo otyeko winjo bongi jaserikale madwoŋ ni apaka obedo, Pilato oyeyo Yozefu kwanyo delkwoŋ Yesu.
41015046	Yozefu ogamo delkwoŋ Yesu wi musalaba, otweyo gi suka, to ketho i kalyel mogwor i tele. Oŋilo kidi madwoŋ to chulo gine dhok kalyel.
41015047	Marya ma wok Magdala kodi Marya min Yose onwaŋo jo ni kenyo joneno kuma oyik'iye Yesu.
41016001	Munyo ndelo ma Sabato orumo, Marya ma wok Magdala, kodi Marya min Yakobo, kodi Salome jonyiewo mo maŋwe kur mawiro gine delkwoŋ Yesu.
41016002	Odikini worwor i ndelo marapena ma tich, munyo chieŋ nyaka gulo, jokidho i kalyel.

41016004	Gikenyo joŋiyo yu malo to joneno ni kidi otyek ŋilo woko; kidi no oido ombo swa.
41016005	Gikenyo jodonjo i kalyel, to joneno jayach moro obedo piny yu rachuch, oruko nanga matar, to lworo mako jo tektek.
41016006	Jayach no owacho ni, “Wikiri wibedi gi lworo. Aŋeyo ni wirango Yesu Janazareth ma chieŋino ogur kwoŋ musalaba. Go ongoye ka; otyeko chierino! Ere panen win kama chieŋino oketh'iye go.
41016007	Onyo kidhi witer wach me ri jofuonjirok pere, kir ri Petro bende ni kole go otyeko telo kidho ri win Galileya; yu koro ama wibino neni'iye go paka ndir cha owacho ri win.”
41016008	Gikenyo jowok i kalyel gi ŋwech, rupiri lworo gi bwok oido opoŋ kwoŋ jo. Aka jokowacho kada ri nyatoro, rupiri oido jothoth gi lworo.
41016009	[Munyo Yesu otyeko chierino kwoŋ jomotho, odikini worwor, i ndelo marapena ma tich, omenyere ri Marya ma wok Magdala, ma ndir no oryemo kwoŋe jwogi abiryo.

41016013	Jome bende jogik to jowacho ri jofuonjirok wadi gin, to jye jokonyalo yeyo wach pajo.
41016014	Machowe, Yesu omenyere ri jofuonjirok apar g'achiel wegi munyo jochiemo. Go opusa jo paka jokobedo gi yeyo, aka odoko jobedo gi adundo manwaŋ, rupiri jokwero yeyo joma onwaŋo jotyeko neno go munyo ochierino.
41016015	Aka owacho ri jo ni, “Kidhi win i piny jye, wifuonji nono jye Wach Maber.

42002044	Paka oido joparo nike go nitye i kitipa ji ma jowotho gi jo, jowotho awotha ndelo gipi, to nyaka jochako rango go bongi wade pajo gi merin pajo.

42003001	I oro marapar g'abich ma dhum pa Kaisar Tiberyo, munyo Pontyo Pilato dhumo paka gavana ma Yudeya, kareno Herode ruoth ma Galileya, aka omin go Filipo ruoth ma Itureya gi Trakoniti, aka Lisania ruoth ma Abilene,

42003006	Aka dhano jye bino neno both pa Were!’ ”

42003008	Timi win gikipiny ma nyutho nike wiŋuto gimarecho mewin. To wikiri wichaki wacho wiwegi kendiwin ni, ‘Ibrayimu meno kwari wan!’ Kendo awacho ri win, kole Were nyalo kwanyo telin me to loko nyikway Ibrayimu.
42003009	Aka otyek kir ketho le ma toŋo woko yen gi i tyende; yath jye ma kinyak maber ibino toŋo woko tibolo i mach.”
42003010	Ji jye jopenjo Yohana ni, “Onyo waripo timo aŋo?”

42003014	Joserikale megi bende jopenjo go ni, “To wan waripo timo aŋo?” Owacho ri jo ni, “Ongoye mayo ji gikipiny g'akaka! Yeŋi win gi kemba mewin! Odoko, wikiri wichwoki dhok dhano!”
42003015	Geno pa ji ochako medirok; aka jochako paro ni ipoyo Yohana a Kristo.

42004001	Munyo Yesu otyeko poŋ gi Chuny Maleŋ, oeye Yordan to Chuny Maleŋ telo go i thim chowo ndelo pyero aŋwen,

42004019	Odoko ooran tito ni me a oro pa Ruoth manyutho ji ŋono pere.”
42004020	Gikenyo oumo kitawo no to dwoko ri ŋata kuro, to bedo piny, aka waŋ ji jye ma kalamo ochomere kwoŋ go.
