42004028	Munyo jowinjo gime, dhano jye keme omako i kalamo pa Joyudaya.
42004029	Joay jowodho go i tindi, to jotero go dho thengi tendere moger'iye tindi pajo munyo joyenyo dhiro go wofuodere piny.
42004030	To go oluwo gi dyer jo to kadho rigo.

42004032	aka jouro fuonji pere, rupiri wach pere oido ni gi men.

42004036	Ji jye jouro swa aka wegi jochako luwo kendigin ni, “Me wach aŋo? Go ryemo woko chuny mochido gi maker gi men to jowok awoka!”

42004039	Yesu ochungo kabuti dhako no to kwero two no bedo kwoŋe, to two weyo go. Piyo piyo no won to dhako no ay malo to chako rweyo jo.
42004040	I hongo no munyo waŋchieŋ kidho podho, ji jye moido jo ni gi jomatwo kiti two mopokere opokere, jokelo jo bothe to Yesu ketho chinge kwoŋ jo to joboth.

42005037	Aka ongoye ŋata kako medho ma vini manyien i mugowa pyendere moti rupiri medho no bino yecho woko pyendere no to oy, gikenyo to pyendere nyiekere woko.

42006020	Gikenyo Yesu otiŋo waŋe oŋiyo jofuonjirok pere, aka owacho ni, “Josilwany a win ma wichandere i chuny win: rupiri Ker pa Were mewin.
42006021	“Josilwany a win ma pama kech neko win: rupiri ibino yeŋo win. “Josilwany a win ma pama wiywak: rupiri wibino nyiero.
42006022	“Wi josilwany ka ji jodak win, joryemo win woko, joyeto win, aka jonyieko nyingi win ni wi jomarecho kwoŋbedo Wuodi Dhano.
42006023	“Sangala win ru ndelo ma bino tundo, aka uchi win gi myel. Kole kemba mewin bino bedo madwoŋ i polo. Me a kite ma bachere pajo jotimo ri jotuchi wach Were bende.
42006024	“To kidamba otundi ri win wijoŋaŋo: rupiri wityeko limo syem mewin.
42006025	“Kidamba otundi ri win ma pama widenya wiyeŋ: rupiri wibino pal gi kech. “Kidamba otundi ri win ma pama winyiero: rupiri wibino winjo malith to wiywak.
42006026	“Kidamba otundi ri win ma pama piny pako win: rupiri meno apaka chango kwarere mewin bende jopako jotuchi wach ma twodo.
42006027	“To awacho ri win ma wiwinjan, mari win jokwor mewin, kendo timi win maber ri joma mon kodi win.
42006028	Miyi win joma kwoŋo win silwany aka kwayi win ri joma yeto win.
42006029	Ka moro ogoyo lembin achiel adhoŋ, wiri ri go man bende; aka ka moro omayin kot perin, ikiri ichier go sat bende.
42006030	Nyatoro jye ma kwayin gimoro miyi go, aka ikiri ikway dhano ni wodwoki rin giperin motyeko mayin.
42006031	Timi ri jowotin paka imito bende jowotim rin.
42006032	Ka wimaro jomomaro win kende, fuoy aŋo ma wigeno limo? Kole kir jomarecho bende jomaro jomomaro jo.
42006033	Ka witimo maber ri joma timo ri win maber kende, fuoy aŋo ma wigeno limo? Kole kir jomarecho bende jotimo ameno.
42006034	Aka ka wimiyo joma wigeno ni jolechulo win gimoro kende, fuoy aŋo ma wigeno limo? Kole kir jomarecho bende jomiyo jomarecho wadi gin gikipiny ka jogeno ni ibino dwoko ri jo gima rom kodi ma jopoko.
42006035	Kuchiel, mari win jokwor mewin, aka witimi ri jo maber. Odoko miyi win ji gikipiny, ma wikigeno ni jobino chulo win. Wibino limo kemba madwoŋ, aka wibino bedo nyithindho pa Ŋatadwoŋ Maloyo; kole go won chunye ber gi joma jokifuoy go kodi jomarecho.
42006036	Bedi win gi wor paka Bawin jawor.
42006037	“Wikiri withum banja ri jowoti win, ŋey Were bende kibino thumo ri win banja. Wikiri wirodhi jowoti win aka bende korodhi win. Chwaki win recho pa jowoti win aka bende ibino chwako mewin;
42006038	Pok jowot win gikipiny, ŋey Were bino poko win bende: rapor mopoŋ, modile, moyengi to poŋ chuka oy; ama ibino ketho i chingi win. Kole rapor m'ioro ri jowotin ama Were bende bino oro ma kipima rin gine gima go dwoko rin.”
42006039	Yesu oluwo i agecha bende ni, “Ŋata waŋe otho bende nyalo kodo nyawote ma waŋe otho ma jojye jokopodho i bur?
42006040	Kole ŋata ifuonjo kiloy jafuonji pere gi dwoŋ, to ŋata ofuonji maber nyalo bedo marom kodi jafuonji pere.
42006041	Raŋo ineno nyaka yath mochile mondhilo mopodho i waŋ omerin aka ikinen kongolo kasik ma nitye i waŋin won?
42006042	Kosa inyalo nedi wacho ri omerin ni, ‘Omera, weyi akwany rin woko nyaka yath m'ochile mondhilo ma nitye i waŋin’, mato ikinyal neno kongolo kasik ma nitye i waŋin won? Jarendirok me, ber kutho ikwanyi woko kongolo kasik mani waŋin no, aka inonen odocho nyaka yath mochile mondhilo ma nitye i waŋ omerin, t'ikwanyo woko ri go.”
42006043	“Kole ongoye yath maber ma nyak gimarach, kosa yath marach ma nyak gimaber.
42006044	Aka kis yath iŋeyo ru gimanyak kwoŋe: Nyandere kifuon wi kudhin, odoko vini kifuon kwoŋ kudho oryaŋ.
42006045	Amomiyo dhano maber wodho tim mabeyo wok i kakano bero ma nitye i adundo pere; aka ŋatarach bende wodho tim marecho wok i kakano recho ma nitye i adundo pere. Kole wach ma dhano luwo jye wok i gimopoŋ iy adundo pere.
42006046	“Raŋo ma wilwoŋan ni, ‘Ruoth, Ruoth’, aka wikitim gima awacho ri win?
42006047	Dhano jye ma bino bongan aka winjo wach paran to tiyo gine, abino nyutho win paka go chalo:
42006048	Go chalo dhano ma munyo geto ot pere, okunyo tyendi ot maluth tundo i gee; aka munyo mikula opoŋ to mol kwoŋ ot no, konyalo yengo, rupiri ot onwaŋo oget matek.
42006049	To ŋata winjo wach me aka kitiy gine, chalo dhano ma munyo geto ot pere, kokunyo tyende maluth moromo; mikula omol kwoŋ ot no, to podho piyo piyo, to nyiekere kichutho.”

42007013	Munyo Ruoth oneno dheno, wor omako go gine, to wacho ni, “Ikiri iywaki.”

42007016	Dhano jye obwok to pako Were munyo jowacho ni, “Jatuchi wach Were madwoŋ omenyere i dyer wan: Were olyewo ji pere.”

42007020	Aka munyo jono jobino bonge jowacho ni, “Yohana odhiro wan bongin ka penjin nike, in a ŋata ripo bino, kosa wakuri ŋat mani?”
42007021	I hongo no Yesu obotho jotwo mathoth, to ryemo woko chuny mochido, aka ji mathoth monwaŋo waŋ gin otho joneno.
42007022	Ri ameno odwoko jo ni, “Kidhi wiwachi ri Yohana gima wityeko neno gi winjo: joma waŋ gin otho joneno, jomoŋol jowotho, jodhowo kwoŋ gin lony, joma ithi gin otho jowinjo, jomotho jochierino, jochandi ifuonjo jo Wach Maber.
42007023	Aka jasilwany a ŋata kiteran marach.”

42007025	Neni win, kole joma rukere ma noro aka jochiemo maber jonwaŋere i dyedipo pa kere ayin.
42007026	To onwaŋo wikidho neno aŋo won? Jatuchi wach Were? Adyeri awacho ri win, go loyo kir jatuchi wach Were!
42007027	Me a ŋata ondik kwoŋe ni, ‘Neni, adhiro rin jamikwenda paran yu wiyin, ma bino kutho yiko rin royo.’
42007028	Awacho ri win, kwoŋ joma mon onywolo jye ongoye maloyo Yohana gi dwoŋ; to kuchiel kir ŋata thin loyo i Ker pa Were, jye loyo go gi dwoŋ.”
42007029	(Munyo ji jye kodi jochoki misolo jowinjo go, joyeyere gi wach pa Were rupiri jonwaŋo batisimo pa Yohana.

42008001	Rumachien Yesu owotho i tindin kodi loka momore munyo tito aka fuonjo Wach Maber kwoŋ Ker pa Were. Japar g'aryo onwaŋo jo ni bonge,

42008007	Kodhi megi opodho i kudhin; aka kudhin odongo gi jo to diyo jo woko.

42008011	“Me a dwoŋ agecha no: Kodhi meno wach pa Were.

42008013	Kodhi mopodho wi tele kuma lowo rep iye, meno a joma jowinjo wach gi kisangala, to wach kirwaki tyende i chuny jo; joyeyo nyaka ma hongo manok, to jopodho ka ratem obino.
42008014	Aka kodhi mopodho i kudhin, meno a joma jowinjo, to rumachien rembo kodi ŋaŋo ma piny kodi kisangala ma kwo diyo jo piny, aka gima jonyak kitegino.
42008015	To kodhi mopodho i lowo ma diwa, meno a joma, munyo jotyeko winjo wach, jomako maber i chuny jo, aka jonyak maber ru diyo chuny jo.

42008019	Gikenyo min Yesu gi wutimin jobino bonge, to jokonyalo tundo bothe ru thotho pa ji.

42008023	Munyo jochiewere, Yesu opodho gi nindo, aka koyo madwoŋ obino to kudho wakawaka, to pi chako poŋ i yee, ma yee onwaŋo chiegin munyirok i pi.

42009008	Joman ni Eliya ama omenyere, aka joman jowacho ni achiel kwoŋ jotuchi wach Were machon am'osukina kendo.
42009009	Herode owacho ni, “Chango aŋundo woko wich Yohana; to me ŋa ma awinjo kwoŋe gikipiny me?” To chako rango neno Yesu.
42009010	Jomoor jodwoko to jowacho ri Yesu gimoro jye ma jotimo. Go okwanyo jo to jokodere gi chien i tindi milwoŋo ni Bethsaida.
42009011	Munyo lwak ji jowinjo ameno, joluwo jo. Yesu ojolo jo to luwo gi jo kwoŋ Ker pa Were, aka obotho jomatwo.
42009012	Munyo piny kidho yutho, jofuonjirok japar g'aryo jobino bongi Yesu to jowacho ni, “Sewila ji jowokidhi i adech ma chiegin kodi loka man jye koro jowonwaŋi kanindo kodi girachama. Kole ka obedo dyer thim.”
42009013	To Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Wiwegi miyi win jo girachama.” Jodwoko ni, “Gima wani gine a nyaka mugat abich gi rech aryo won kende. Kono bedi wanyalo kidho nyiewo chiemo ri kweth ji me jye di watimo amanago.”
42009014	(Jono onwaŋo joromo chiegin chwo gana abich.) Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Wachi win jowobedi piny i kitipa ma pyero abich abich.”
42009015	Jotimo ameno to jooro ji jye bedo piny.
42009016	Gikenyo Yesu okwanyo mugat abich kodi rech aryo no, otiŋo waŋe malo oŋiyo polo, to miyo silwany: aka oturo to chwayo ri jofuonjirok pere jowopoki lwak ji.
42009017	Ji jye jochiemo paka joyenyo aka ochoki ŋinjeŋinje modoŋ to poŋo aditin apar g'aryo.
42009018	Ndelo moro munyo Yesu oido kwayo kakende aka jofuonjirok pere oido jo ni bonge, openjo jo ni, “Ji jowacho ni an a ŋa?”
42009019	Aka jodwoko ni, “Yohana Jakibatisa; to joman ni Eliya; aka joman ni achiel kwoŋ jotuchi wach Were machon am'osukina kendo.”
42009020	Yesu owacho ni, “To win wiwacho ni, an a ŋa?” Petro oluwo malo, to wacho ni, “Kristo pa Were.”
42009021	Ru wach no Yesu ochiko jo teltel ni kiri jowowachi ri nyatoro gime;
42009022	owacho ni, “Wuodi Dhano ripo chandirok i royo kweth, aka jotel pa ji kodi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jofuonji ma Chik jobino kwero go to joneko go, to ichierino go i ndelo maradek.”
42009023	Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Ka moro mito luwan, go won kutho ripo kwerere kende, wotiŋi musalaba pere kis ndelo, aka woluwan.
42009024	Ato ŋata won omiti botho kwo pere bino rwenyo woko; to ŋata orwenyi kwo pere ran bino botho kwo no.
42009025	Kony aŋo ma dhano onwaŋ ka oloki piny gipi apere to rwenyo kosa bolo woko kwo pere won?
42009026	Ŋata wiye kwot kodan gi wach paran, Wuodi Dhano bende wiye bino kwot kodi go ka odwoko i dwoŋ pere kodi i dwoŋ pa Bamere kodi apa jomalaika maleŋ.
42009027	To awacho ri win adyeri, kwoŋ win nitye joma jochungo ka ma jokiletho ma fuodi jokoneno Ker pa Were.”
42009028	Munyo ndelo aboro okadho nyuka Yesu wachi gikipiny me, go okwanyo Petro gi Yohana gi Yakobo to joidho wi got kwayo.
42009029	Aka munyo kwayo to chal pere wire, omiyo ruk pere olokere matar chilili.
42009030	Gikenyo chwo aryo, Musa kodi Eliya, joluwo gine.
42009031	Jomenyere i dwoŋ ma polo aka joluwo gi Yesu paka go chiegin chowo atoŋa pa Were mobedo tho pere i Yerusalem.
42009032	Petro gi wadi oido nindo okwalo jo, to munyo jochiew, joneno dwoŋ pa Yesu kodi chwo aryo ma jochungo bothe.
42009033	Munyo ji aryo no oido joeye bongi Yesu, Petro owacho ri go ni, “Jadwoŋ, apaka bedo ka ber ama! Weyi wageti kayindin adek: achiel rin, achiel ri Musa, achiel ri Eliya;” to go oido kuya kir gima go wacho.
42009034	Munyo fuodi go luwo ameno, pondeponde obino to umo jo, to lworo omako jofuonjirok munyo jodonjo i pondeponde no.
42009035	Gikenyo dwondi jo moro owacho gi i pondeponde ni, “Me Wuodan, mayero, winji win go!”
42009036	Munyo dwondi jo no otyeko luwo, onenere ni Yesu won ama oido odoŋ kende. Jofuonjirok joliŋ gi gikipiny no ma jokowacho ri nyatoro i hongo no kada gimoro kwoŋ gima joneno.
42009037	Yawere mere, munyo joloro wi got, kweth ji joromo gi Yesu.
42009038	Gikenyo, dhano moro okoko i dyer ji ni, “Jafuonji, akwayin ikonyiye wuodan, rupiri go a nyathi achiel won ma ani gine.
42009039	Aka jwogi moro mwonjo go noknok, miyo go koko malo, to fum redho go piny, to gwecho chuka bwoyo wok i dhoke, to futa go aka kimiti kada weyo go.
42009040	Akwayo jofuonjirok perin ni joworyemi woko jwogi no kwoŋe, to jokonyalo.”
42009041	Yesu odwoko ni, “A luse ji ma bu yeyo kendo momyenere, anobedi gi win kir keraŋo ma fuodi anere gi win? Keli wuodin ka”
42009042	Munyo jayach no kidho, jwogi owito go aka ofuodo go piny to gwecho. To Yesu oay kwoŋ chuny mochido no, to botho jayach no, to dwoko go ri bamere.
42009043	Aka dhano jye ouro men pa Were. To munyo ji jye fuodi jouro gima Yesu otimo, owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni,
42009044	“Weyi wach me wodonji i ithi win; rupiri ibino ketho Wuodi Dhano i chingi ji.”
42009045	To jokoniaŋ dwoŋ wach no, aka opan ni kiri jowoniaŋi; kendo lworo omako kir jo penjo go wach me.
42009046	Pyem ochakere i dyer jo ni kwoŋ jo ŋa maloyo wadi gi dwoŋ.
42009047	To munyo Yesu oniaŋ paro ma chuny jo, okwanyo nyathi moro to ketho go chungo kabothe.
42009048	Aka owacho ri jo ni, “Ŋata jolo nyathi me i nyingan meno jolan; aka ŋata jolan, meno jolo ŋata ooran; kole ŋata oasa thin i dyer win meno a ŋata dwoŋ loyo.”
42009049	Yohana odwoko ni, “Jadwoŋ, wanwaŋo nyatoro ryemo jwogi i nyingin, to wachiero go, rupiri go kiwothi gi wan.”
42009050	To Yesu odwoko go ni, “Wikiri wichieri go; kole ŋata kimon gi win meno nitye yu thenge mewin.”
42009051	Munyo ndir pere orikere ma dok i polo, Yesu oridho paro ma kidho Yerusalem.
42009052	Aka odhiro jomikwenda pere yu wiye, to jokidho loka ma Samarya yiko ri go kabedo.
42009053	To jono jokoyeyo jolo go paka go oido omako yo ma kidho Yerusalem.
42009054	Munyo jofuonjirok pere joneno ama, Yakobo gi Yohana jowach ni, “Ruoth, imito walwoŋ mach wok i polo wowaŋi woko jo?”
42009055	To Yesu owire oŋiyo jo to bwoko jo.
42009056	Aka jomedere kadho yu loka man.
42009057	Munyo jowotho, joromo gi dhano i royo mowacho ri Yesu ni, “Abino luwin kama inokidh'iye jye.”
42009058	Yesu odwoko ni, “Kibwe jo ni gi kero pajo, aka winyin ma malo bende jo ni gi odi gin, to Wuodi Dhano ongoye kodi katheno wiye.”
42009059	To ri ŋat man Yesu owacho ni, “Luwan.” To ŋato dwoko ni, “Jadwoŋ, weyi kutho akidhi ayiki baba, otho.”
42009060	To Yesu dwoko go ni, “Weyi jomotho jowoyiki jomotho pajo, tich perin kidho nyayo wach kwoŋ Ker pa Were ayin.”
42009061	Ŋat man owacho ni, “Aleluwin Jadwoŋ, to weyi kutho akidhi asewila jopecho.”
42009062	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Dhano jye ma furo gi kwer dhok aka kethere ŋiyo chien meno kiripi gi Ker pa Were.”
42010001	Rumachien Ruoth oyero ji pyero abiryo g'aryo man aka ooro jo yu wiye jaryo jaryo, i kis tindi kodi kamoro jye ma go onwaŋo yiko tund'iye.
42010002	Owacho ri jo ni, “Kecho opikere, to jotich ama nok, amomiyo kwayi win Ruoth ma won kecho wodhiri jotich jowokechi ri go.
42010003	Onyo kadhi win pama won. Eno, adhiro win pa roombo i dyer arara.
42010004	Wikiri witiŋ mugowa pesa, kosa mugowa chiemo, kendo kada war.
42010005	I ot moro jye ma widonj'iye, kutho mothi win jo ni, ‘Syem wobedi i ot me.’
42010006	Aka k'inen onwaŋere ŋata jolo syem kenyo, syem mewin bino doŋ ri go; to ka kameno, bino giki ri win.
42010007	Bedi win i ot achiel munyo wijolo chiemo kodi giramadha ma jomiy win, rupiri jatich chamo gikwok pere. Wikiri wikowere i udi man.
42010008	Ka widonjo i tindi moro tijolo win, chami win gima okethi ruwaŋ win.
42010009	Bothi win jotwo mani kenyo aka wiwachi ri jo ni, ‘Ker pa Were ochore chiegin gi win.’
42010010	To ka widonjo i tindi moro aka kojol win, kidhi win i royo ma tindi no to wiwacho ni,
42010011	‘Onyo wateŋo woko kir fukefuke ma tindi mewin moido odoŋ i par tyendi wan wodoŋi i wiy win; to kada ameno ŋeyi win ni Ker pa Were orikere chiegin.’
42010012	Awacho ri win, i ndelo ma thumo banja, Sodom bino limo girachula madhey ye loyo tindi no.
42010013	“Kidamba otundi rin, Korazin! Kidamba otundi rin, Bethsaida! Kole bedi giraura motim i win tim i Ture kodi Sidon, di chango joŋuto chon, aka di jobedo piny to joruko gunia, to jobukere gi buru ma nyutho ni joŋuto recho.
42010014	Were bino nyutho wor madwoŋ i ndelo ma thumo banja ri Tire kodi Sidon loyo ri win.
42010015	Aka in Kapernaum, onwaŋo iyenyo tiŋirok malo tundo i polo? Ibino bolin i piny pa jomotho ayino!”
42010016	Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Ŋata winjo win, meno winjan; ŋata kwero win meno kweran; aka ŋata kweran, meno kwero Ŋatooran.”
42010017	Jofuonjirok pyero abiryo g'aryo cha jodwoko munyo josangala, ka jowacho ni, “Ruoth, kiri jwogi jye jowinjo wan ka waoro nyingin.”
42010018	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Aneno Sitan munyo podho pa lithkoth mowok i polo.
42010019	Onyo atyeko miyo win men ma nyono gi tyendi win thwole kodi thwolgwok, gi nyalo woko men pa jakwor jye; kendo ongoye gima bio timo win marach.
42010020	To wikiri wisangala ni chuny mochido jowinjo win; kuchiel sangala win ni nyingi win ondik i polo ayino.”
42010021	I hongo no won Yesu osangala i Chuny Maleŋ aka owacho ni, “Afuoyin Baba, Ruoth ma polo kodi piny, paka ipano gikipiny me ri jomaryek kodi jomofuonjere tinyutho nyithidho ayin. Ey Baba, gime otimere paka i yero.
42010022	“Baba otyeko miyan gimoro jye; aka ongoye ŋata oŋeyo Wuode kwanyo woko Bamere, kendo ongoye ŋata oŋeyo Baba kwanyo woko Wuode kodi joma Wuode oyero nyutho jo Bamere.”
42010023	Gikenyo Yesu owire ri jofuonjirok pere to wacho ri jo nyaliŋliŋ ni, “Josilwany a joma waŋ gin neno gima wineno!
42010024	Aka awacho ri win, jotuchi wach Were kodi kerin mathoth, chango joyenyo neno gima wineno to jokoneno, gi winjo gima wiwinjo to jokowinjo.”
42010025	Gikenyo jafuonji ma Chik moro omito temo Yesu; oay to penjo ni, “Jafuonji, mitere atim aŋo ŋey adonji i kwo makirum?”
42010026	Yesu bende openjo go ni, “Chik wacho nedi? Somere nedi?”
42010027	Odwoko ni, “Mari Ruoth Were perin g'adundo perin jye, gi chunyin jye, gi men perin jye, gi paro perin jye, kendo mari nyawotin paka iwon imarere.”
42010028	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Idwoko motire; ere timi ameno aka ibino kwo.”
42010029	To paka ŋato onwaŋo yenyo nyutho tiro pere, openjo Yesu ni, “Nyawotan a ŋa?”
42010030	Yesu odwoko ni, “Jal moro oido wotho i royo kareno owok Yerusalem kidho Yeriko, to podho i chingi jokwo, ma jolunyo kwoŋe nengin jye, jogoyo go, to joweyo go kenyo ma chunye kende ama gudere.
42010031	Gikenyo jachwayi ri Were wi alitar moro oido luwo royo no, to munyo oneno ŋato, oluwo i thengi royo to kadho akadha.
42010032	Ameno bende Jalevi mobino kenyo oneno go, to kadho kwoŋe gi i thengi royo.
42010033	To munyo Jasamarya moro otundo bonge, ama omako gi go wor munyo oneno go;
42010034	okidho bonge to chako tweyo adholin pere, to konj'iye mo gi vini. Rumachien otiŋo go to ketho go wi kayina pere won, aka otero go i ot wendo, to miyo go kony kenyo.
42010035	Yawere mere okwanyo siringi aryo to chulo jakuri ot wendo ka wacho ni, ‘Kuri ran go maber, aka ka adwoko abino chulin gimoro jye m'inomedi oro ma konyo go.’
42010036	Onyo kwoŋ ji adek me, iparo ni ŋa mobedo nyawoti jal mopodho i chingi jokwo no?”
42010037	Go odwoko ni, “Ŋata onyutho go wor.” Yesu odwoko ni, “Ibende kidhi itim ameno.”
42010038	Munyo Yesu gi jofuonjirok pere jomedo woth, jotundo loka moro, to dhako moro ma nyinge Maritha jolo go i ot pere.
42010039	Dheno oido ni gi nyamin milwoŋo ni Marya, mobino to bedo piny dho katyendi Yesu to winjo fuonji pere.
42010040	To Maritha won oido ni gi mindin madit mogeŋo go winjo fuonji momiyo owacho ni, “Ruoth, ikipar paka nyamera oweyan gi tich kendan? Mondo wachi ri go wokonyan.”
42010041	To Ruoth odwoko ni, “Maritha, Maritha, chunyin ramin kendo rembo kwoŋ gimathoth,
42010042	mato nyaka gimoro achiel won ama mitere. Marya ayino am'oyero gimaber mere, ma kokwany kwoŋe.”
42011001	Ndelo moro Yesu onwaŋo nitye kamoro kwayo, aka munyo ochowo, achiel kwoŋ jofuonjirok pere owacho ni, “Ruoth, fuonji wan kwayo, paka Yohana ofuonjo jofuonjirok pere.”
42011002	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Wachi win ama ka wikwayo: ‘Bawan mani polo, Nyingin wolwor paka leŋ. Ker perin wobin.
42011003	Miyi wan ndelo jye chiemo mawan ma noknok.
42011004	Chwaki ri wan gimarecho mawan, paka wabende wachwako dhano jye ma timo ri wan marach. Aka ikiri iter wan karatem. To bothi wan ayino kwoŋ gimarach.’ ”
42011005	Aka Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Ŋa kwoŋ win mani gi mere pere, ma ka okidho bothe dyer wor to kwayo go ni, ‘Mere paran, kopa ye an mugat adek, anochulin;
42011006	nyawotan moro mowok bor ee nyaka tundo ran pama won me, aka angoye gi gimoro ma anomiy go!’
42011007	Jalo to dwoko gi i ot ni, ‘Ikir iolan, atyeko kir diyo thigo, aka nyithindho paran gi an won wanitye i kanindo; akinyal ay malo bino miyin.’
42011008	Awacho ri win, kada di ŋato koay miyo go gimoro paka mere, to ru amen pere, jalo bino ay malo to miyo go gimoro jye ma go yenyo.
42011009	“Amomiyo awacho ri win, kwayi win, aka omiy win; rangi win, aka winonwaŋ; gudi win thigo, aka oyaw ri win.
42011010	Kole ŋata kwayo ndir jye limo, ŋata rango, ndir jye nwaŋo; aka ŋata gudo thigo, bende ndir jye iyawo ri go.
42011011	Ŋa kwoŋ win ma baa nyithindho, ma ka wuode okwayo go rech to miyo thwol ayino?
42011012	Kosa ka okwayo go tongi gweno to miyo go thwolgwok?
42011013	K'inen win ma wirecho, wiŋeyo miyo nyithindho mewin gimaber, onyo Bawin mani polo oloy win ma rom nedi i miyo joma kwayo go Chuny Maleŋ!”
42011014	Gikenyo Yesu oido ryemo woko jwogi mobadha; munyo jwogi no owok, obadha oluwo, aka ji jouro swa.
42011015	To joman jowacho ni, “Go ryemo jwogi gi men pa Belzebul, jadwoŋ pa jwogi jye.”
42011016	Aka joman, ma temo go, jokwayo go ranen mawok i polo.
42011017	To Yesu paka oido oŋeyo paro pajo, owacho ri jo ni, “Ker jye ma won tyakere dyere bino tur, odoko pecho ma won tyakere dyere podho.
42011018	Onyo ka Sitan won owire to tyakere dyere, ker pere ochungi nedi? Ato wiwacho ni aryemo jwogi gi men pa Belzebul.
42011019	Medo kwoŋ meno, ka kere aryemo jwogi gi men pa Belzebul, nyithindho mewin joryemo jo gi men pa ŋa? Meno amomiyo jobino thumo banja loyo win.
42011020	To k'inen aryemo jwogi gi lwet Were, kole meno Ker pa Were otyeko tundo ri win.
42011021	Ka dhano ma jameni, manitye gi gilweny, kuro pecho pere, meno gikipiny pere otyek gwoko;
42011022	to ka ŋata loyo go gi men omwonji go to kengila go, bino mayo go gilweny monwaŋo go geno to poko jowote gikipiny m'onyaga no.
42011023	Ŋata ongoye i thenge paran meno jakwor paran, aka ŋata kikonyan gi choko roombo kanyachiel meno kedho woko ayino.
42011024	“Ka chuny mochido owok kwoŋ dhano, kidho i kabedo mothwo mongoy'iye pi munyo rango kaywomirok; to ka konwaŋo kamoro wacho ni, ‘Abino gik i ot paran kama awok'iye.’
42011025	Aka ka odwoko to nwaŋo ni ot oywey aka oyik maber,
42011026	kidho to omo jwogi wadi man abiryo marecho loyo go, to jodonjo to jobedo kenyo; aka kiti ŋato lokere marach loyo ma yado chon.”
42011027	Munyo Yesu owacho ameno, dhako moro okoko i dyer ji ka wacho ri Yesu ni, “Jasilwany a dhako motiŋin i iye, to miyin dhoth.”
42011028	Yesu odwoko ni, “Kuchiel josilwany meno a joma jowinjo wach pa Were to joketho i tim!”
42011029	Munyo lwak ji oido medere, Yesu owacho ni, “Luse ji ma pama obedo luse marach; kwayo ranyuth, to ongoye m'ibino miyo jo kwanyo woko ranyuth pa Yona.
42011030	Kole paka Yona obedo ranyuth ri ji ma Nineve, apaka Wuodi Dhano bende bino bedo ranyuth ri luse ji ma pama.
42011031	Kere ma dhako ma wok i thenge ma yu Tyendi piny bino ay gi luse ji me to kelo kwoŋ jo wach i ndelo ma thumo banja, rupiri go owotho wok i piny mabor bino winjo ryeko pa Solomon; aka awacho ri win, kole ŋatadwoŋ ma loyo Solomon ee ni ka.
42011032	I ndelo ma thumo banja, ji ma Nineve jobino chungo to jokelo kwoŋ win wach, rupiri joŋuto gimarecho pajo munyo jowinjo wach ma Yona otito; aka awacho ri win, kole ŋatadwoŋ ma loyo kir Yona ee ni ka!
42011033	“Ongoye ŋata chwinyo tala pere to pano kosa umo g'agono; kuchiel go ketho tala no wi meza, aka joma donjo i ot jowonyali neno lero.
42011034	Waŋin meno a tala ma delkwoŋin; ka waŋin olama, delkwoŋin gipi bedo maler; to ka kolama, delkwoŋin gipi bende bedo i mudho.
42011035	Amomiyo kure aka ŋey lero ma kwoŋin kolokere mudho.
42011036	K'inen delkwoŋin ni gi lero mathoth aka ongoye kama di mudho, meno bino bedo maler kichutho, paka tala malyel miyo lero.”
42011037	Munyo Yesu fuodi luwo, Jafarisayo moro okwayo go ni wokidhi wochiemiye gine; ri ameno Yesu odonjo i ot pere to bedo dhower.
42011038	Jafarisayo no ouro swa munyo oneno nike Yesu kokutho ologo paka chik pajo yenyo aka ochiemo.
42011039	To Ruoth owacho ri go ni, “Win Jofarisayo wilwoko ŋey kikopo kodi atewe to woro kodi recho madit ama opoŋ i chuny win.
42011040	Ji ma paro pajo chiek! Wiparo ni Were ma chango ochweyo ŋey gimoro ama kochweyo iye bende?
42011041	To miyi jochandi gima ni iyi kikopo kodi atewe aka gikipiny no jye bino bedo molony ri win.
42011042	“Kidamba otundi ri win, Jofarisayo! Rupiri wimiyo Were achiel kwoŋ apar ma gikipiny machielirok maŋwe kur paka: katungulu, binzari, kodi yen maŋwe kur man, to wijala tiro kodi maro Were; gikipiny me oido wiripo timo ma wikijala man.
42011043	“Kidamba otundi ri win, Jofarisayo! Ato wimaro kabedo mamalo i kalamo pa Joyudaya, kodi jolo moth i katale.
42011044	Kidamba otundi ri win! Wichalo kalyele ma koketh kwoŋ jo ranyuth aka ji wotho i wiy jo ma jokiŋey.”
42011045	Achiel kwoŋ jofuonji ma Chik owacho ri go ni, “Jafuonji, k'iwacho ameno kole onyo iyeto wan bende!”
42011046	Yesu odwoko ni, “Kidamba otundi ri win bende, wi jofuonji ma Chik! Wiketho migugu idyeŋey ji ma kiyot tiŋo, to wiwegi wikigey migugu no kada gi lwet chingi win achiel.
42011047	Kidamba otundi ri win, kole wigero kalyele pa jotuchi wach Were ma chango bachere mewin joneko.
42011048	Ameno wiwegi wibedo joridhi wach no aka wifuoyo gima bachere mewin jotimo; ato jo joneko jo, aka win wigero kalyele pajo.
42011049	Amomiyo Ryeko pa Were wacho ni, ‘Abino dhiro ri jo jotuchi wach Were kodi jomikwenda; aka jobino neko megi, joman to jochando.’
42011050	Amomiyo ji ma pama ibino ketho kwoŋ jo banja ma oyo remo pa jotuchi wach Were jye wok i chwech ma piny,
42011051	chako kwoŋ remo pa Abel tundo i remo pa Zekariya ma joneko i dyer alitar kodi kabedo maleŋ. Ey, awacho ri win, ji ma pama ibino ketho ri jo banja kwoŋ recho no jye!
42011052	“Kidamba otundi ri win, jofuonji ma Chik! Wikwanyo rayaw ma thigo ma ot ryeko; to wiwegi wikwero donjo i ot no, odoko wigeŋo joman ma joyenyo donj'iye!”
42011053	Munyo Yesu eye kenyo, jofuonji ma Chik kodi Jofarisayo jochako diyo go tektek, gi temo omo iye gi penji kwoŋ gikipiny mathoth,
42011054	kareno jobuto ri go ŋey jowomaki go i wach pere moro.
42012001	I hongo no, munyo kweth ji gana gi gana oido jonyonere dho bothe, Yesu okutho ochako wacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Kure win kwoŋ gipa Jofarisayo matiyo pa thow, mobedo rendirok.
42012002	Ongoye gima oum ma koyaw i lero, kosa gimopan ma koŋeyere.
42012003	Amomiyo gimoro jye ma wimwoŋo i cholo bino winjere i lero, aka gimoro jye ma wimwoŋo i udi nyaliŋliŋ ibino kedho kamaler wi udi malo.
42012004	“Awacho ri win, jowotan, wikiri wilwori joma neko del, mato kwoŋ meno ongoye giman ma jonyalo medo timo.
42012005	Weyi anyuthi win Ŋata wiripo lworo: lwori win ŋata k'otyeko neko dhano, ni gi men ma bolo i mach makitho; adyeri awacho ri win, lwori wi Go.
42012006	“Obicho abich kitana siringi aryo be? To ongoye kada achiel ma Were wiye wil gine.
42012007	Medo kwoŋ meno, kir yewiy win jye Were otyeko kwano. Amomiyo wikiri wilwori; kole wiloyo obicho gi welo!
42012008	“Aka awacho ri win: dhano jye matucho i dyer ji nike go oyeyan, Wuodi Dhano bende bino tucho go ruwaŋ jomalaika pa Were.
42012009	To ŋata okwedere kwaŋan i dyer ji, Wuodi Dhano bende bino kwedirok kwoŋe ruwaŋ jomalaika pa Were.
42012010	Nyatoro jye ma luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Wuodi Dhano ibino chwako go; to ŋata oluw gima kotire kwoŋ Chuny Maleŋ kibino nwaŋo chwak.
42012011	“Ka joteri win i kalamo pa Joyudaya kodi i waŋ jodhum kodi ruodhe, wikiri wirembi kwoŋ gima winowachi kosa gima winodwoki.
42012012	Kole Chuny Maleŋ bino fuonjo win i hongo no won gima wiripo wacho.”
42012013	Ŋatachiel i dyer muma ji owacho ri Yesu ni, “Jafuonji, wachi ri omera wopoki kodan gikipiny ma walunjo.”
42012014	Yesu odwoko ni, “Jawodhan, ŋa mokethan jathumi banja mewin, kosa jathek kwoŋ gikipiny mewin?”
42012015	To medere wacho ri jono ni, “Kure win, odoko gwokere win kwoŋ woro ma nger jye, rupiri kwo pa dhano kichungi i thotho pa lim ma go ni gine, kada bedi ni go nigi makalo ma go yenyo.”
42012016	Gikenyo Yesu oluwo i agecha ama: “Jaŋaŋo moro chango obedo gi ndelo chiemo monyak ri go mathoth swa.
42012017	Ameno go oparo g'ichunye ni, ‘Anotimi aŋo, kole angoye gi kaketho kweth chiemo paran me?’
42012018	To wacho ni, me a gima onyo aletimo: abino kedho woko dere paran jye t'achweyo madongo loyo, t'akonjo kal paran kodi gikipiny man jye i iye.
42012019	Gikenyo abino wacho ri chunyan ni, chunyan, ini gi kweth gikipiny mabeyo modhure rin ma nyalo chowo oro kweth; ikiri ipar gimoro, onyo chiemi, medhi, iyodere!
42012020	To Were owacho ri go ni, ‘Mamiŋ me! Kole wor ma konon won me ibino omo chunyin: onyo kweth gikipiny modhure me jye obedi apaŋa?’ ”
42012021	Yesu ochowo wachi nike, “Me apaka bedo ri joma jodhuro lim kweth ri syem pa jowegi to jongoye gi ŋaŋo i waŋ Were.”
42012022	Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Amomiyo awacho ri win ni wikiri wirembi kwoŋ kwo mewin, gima winochami, kosa kwoŋ delkwoŋ win, gima winoruki.
42012023	Kole kwo loyo chiemo, aka delkwoŋ dhano loyo ruk.
42012024	Pari win kwoŋ winyin milwoŋo ni agak, jokichwoyi kosa jokechi; jongoye gi dero kosa kachoko chiemo; Were won ama pidho jo! Onyo wiloyo winyin no gi bero didi?
42012025	Aka ŋa kwoŋ win ma i rembo pere nyalo medoye hongo ma kwo pere kada masisiri?
42012026	To k'inen wikinyal timo gima thin paka meno, raŋo ma wirembo kwoŋ gikipiny man?
42012027	Pari win kwoŋ dudi ma thiwe ŋon paka jodongo; jokitiy kosa jotimi ruk pajo. To kada Solomon, gi ŋaŋo pere no jye, oido ongoye gi ruk mabeyo paka achiel kwoŋ dudi me.
42012028	To k'inen Were ruko dudi ma konon nitye to dikin iwaŋo i kidhur yuk, onyo Were koruki win loyo dudi no? Apaka yeyo mewin nok ameno!
42012029	Amomiyo wikiri wirembi kwoŋ gima winochami kodi gima winomadhi, odoko wikiri wiasa paro.
42012030	Kole jokafiri ma piny gipi ama jorango gikipiny no; aka Bawin oŋeyo ni wiyenyo gikipiny me.
42012031	Kuchiel, kutho rangi win Ker ma polo, aka go bino miyo win gikipiny no.
42012032	“Wikiri wibedi malwor, nyaka roombo paran! Kole Bawin sangala gi miyo win Ker.
42012033	Tana win lim mewin jye aka pesa mere wipoki jochandi. Bedi win gi migowe ma kiyechi, aka wikan ŋaŋo mewin i polo kama komojere iye, kendo ongoye jakwo ma nyalo gey'iye, kosa masirigi moro nyiek'iye.
42012034	Kole kama ŋaŋo perin ni iye ama chunyin bende bed'iye.
42012035	“Rukere win ma tich aka wimoki talin mewin.
42012036	Bedi win paka jotich ma jokuro ruoth pajo wodwoki wok i kalima ma nywomirok, ma joyikere yawo thigo tekin go gudo.
42012037	Jotich no josilwany ma ruoth pajo onwaŋi jo ni waŋ gin ka go bino. Awacho ri win adyeri, go bino tweyo nanga moro i kore, to bedo piny dhower to poko jo chiemo. Miti go odwoki munyo piny keko kosa munyo ochot;
42012038	aka jotich no josilwany ka onwaŋ joyikere.
42012039	Ŋeyi win gime, ni bedi won pecho ŋey hongo ma jokwo jobin'iye turo ot pere, di koyeyo kada ŋatachiel turo thigo pere.
42012040	Wibende wiripo chungo ma wiyikere, kole Wuodi Dhano ledwoko i hongo ma wikipar ni dwok'iye.”
42012041	Petro openjo ni, “Ruoth, iluwo i agecha me kwoŋ wani kosa kwoŋ joman jye?”
42012042	Ruoth odwoko ni, “Jatich ma kuro pecho mene maryek? Meno a ŋata ruoth pere oketho go kuro pecho gi poko ji chiemo ka hongo otundo.
42012043	Jatich no jasilwany ma ka ruoth pere odwoko bino nwaŋo go i tich.
42012044	Adyeri awacho ri win ni go bino ketho ŋato kuro lim pere jye.
42012045	To jatich ma won wacho ni, ‘Kole ruoth paran fuodi ogalo gi dwoko,’ to chako goyo wadi machwo gi mamon, to chiemo to medho, to mer,
42012046	ruoth pere bino dwoko i ndelo ma go kipar kodi i hongo ma go kuya, aka ruoth pere bino miyo go girachula to loko go achiel kwoŋ joma kigenere.
42012047	“Jatich moŋeyo gima ruoth pere yenyo, to fuodi kochako kada timo gino, ibino chwado go matek,
42012048	to jatich moido koŋeyo rigo, to bende ripo achwada kiboko ru gim'otimo, ibino chwado go manok. Dhano jye moyim rigo gimoro, ibino mito kwoŋe gimathoth; ato ka oyim ri dhano gimombo gi genirok, bende ibino mito kwoŋe gima loyo meno.
42012049	“Abino kelo mach i piny, aka mach ago wany swa ma agomba ni bedi oido otyeko kir chako lyel!
42012050	Nitye batisimo ma aripo limo, aka rembo paran dwoŋ swa ka fuodi kotimere!
42012051	Wiparo nike akelo syem i piny? Be, awacho ri win, akelo tyakirok ayino.
42012052	Kole wok pama, i ot ma di ji abich bino bedo tyakirok: jadek jobino pokirok kwoŋ jaryo.
42012053	Baa nyathi bino dak wuode, aka wuodi nyatoro bende bino dak bamere; min nyathi bino dak nyare, nyar nyatoro bende bino dak yokimere; adha nyako manywolo chwore bino dak chi wuode no, chi wuodi nyatoro bende bino dak adhamere.”
42012054	Yesu owacho ri ji ni, “Ka wineno pondeponde chokere yu Podhochieŋ, piyo piyo wiwacho ni, ‘Koth kidho chwe,’ to bende timere ameno.
42012055	Aka ka wineno koyo ma wok yu Tyendi piny, wiwacho ni, ‘Lyetho leasirok,’ aka bende timere ameno.
42012056	Wi jorendirok! Wiŋeyo tito chal pa piny kodi apa pondeponde; to raŋo ma wikinyal tito hongo ma pama?
42012057	“To raŋo ma wiwegi wikinyal neno gima otire ma ripere atima?
42012058	Ka wimako yo kodi ŋata osa in pa jathumi banja, temi paka inyalo yiko gine wach gi i royo, ka k'ameno go bino terin bongi jathum banja, to jathumi banja dhirin i chingi jaserikale, to jaserikale bolin i twech.
42012059	Awacho rin, ikowoki kenyo chuka inochuli pesa kir machowe.”
42013001	I hongo no jomogo oido jo ni kenyo ma jowacho ri Yesu kwoŋ Jogalileya ma Pilato oruwo remo pajo kodi mich ma chowirok pajo.
42013002	Aka Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Wiparo ni Jogalileya no amoido ji marecho loyo Jogalileya man, rupiri jochandere ameno?
42013003	Awacho ri win, ni k'ameno; to ka wikiŋuto gimarecho mewin wibende wibino reyere woko paka jo.
42013004	Kosa wiparo ni japar g'aboro ma ot achurchur ma Silowam oryewere kwoŋ jo to neko jo, wiparo nike oido jobedo jomarecho loyo ji jye monwaŋo jonitye Yerusalem?
42013005	Awacho ri win, k'ameno, to ka wikiŋuto wibende wibino reyere woko paka jo.”
42013006	Yesu oluwo i agecha ni, “Dhano moro oido nitye gi kiti makuyu michamo m'opidho i ndelo vini pere, aka obino rango nyandere mere to konwaŋo.
42013007	Ameno owacho ri jadoyi ndelo vini ni, ‘Neni pama onyo oro adek gipi ma ariwin ka rango nyandere wi makuyu me, to akinwaŋi. Onyo toŋi go woko; raŋo ma go nyieko lowo ka?’
42013008	Jatich odwoko ni, ‘Jadwoŋ, okutho weyi go kenyo oro me, nyuka anofuri tyende to aketh'iye lowo motop.
42013009	Aka ka onyak nyandere oro mabino, meno ber, to ka konyak, aka inotoŋi go woko.’ ”
42013010	I ndelo ma Sabato moro, Yesu onwaŋo fuonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya.
42013011	Aka dhako moro onwaŋo nitye kenyo moido chuny mochido ma two oido nitye kwoŋe aka oido otyeko two oro apar g'aboro; go oido ogwomere ma kinyal ryerok ayi malo.
42013012	Munyo Yesu oneno go, olwoŋo go to wacho ri go ni, “Dhako me, pama onyo iboth i two perin.”
42013013	Gikenyo munyo Yesu oketho chinge kwoŋe, piyo piyo no to dheno chungo moryere, to pako Were.
42013014	To ruoth ma kalamo pa Joyudaya chunye owaŋ rupiri Yesu obotho dheno i Sabato, omiyo owacho ri ji ni, “Ndelo nitye auchiel ma waripo tiy'iye; amomiyo biye win i ndelo no kwayo both, ma kiweno ndelo ma Sabato.”
42013015	Ruoth odwoko go ni, “Win, jorendirok! Nitye nyatoro kwoŋ win ma kigony thwon pere kosa punda pere wi loch i ndelo ma Sabato to tero i pi?
42013016	To yagi, dhako me ma nyar Ibrayimu, aka Sitan onwaŋo otweyo go kweth oro apar g'aboro gipi, ama d'ikonyal gonyo go i twech me kada nende i ndelo ma Sabato?”
42013017	Munyo owacho ameno, jokwor pere jye wichkwot omako jo, kareno ji jye oido josangala ru giraura ma Yesu otimo.
42013018	Yesu odoko owacho ni, “Ker pa Were chale kodi aŋo? Anopima g'aŋo won?
42013019	Go chalo nyingi kodhi mondhilo ma nyatoro okwanyo to pidho i ndelo pere; aka odongo to lokere yath mombo, to winyin ma malo bino to jogero odi gin i jange.”
42013020	Aka odoko owacho ni, “Anopima Ker pa Were g'aŋo kendo?
42013021	Go chalo thow ma dhako moro okwanyo to rwako i masiyo adek ma moko m'obak nyuka moko gipi oyenyo.”
42013022	Yesu owotho ka fuonjo ji malomalo i tindin kodi i thenge jye munyo chomo yu Yerusalem.
42013023	Ŋat moro openjo go ni, “Ruoth, kosa ji manok ama jolebothi?” Yesu odwoko jo ni,
42013024	“Temi win paka winyalo donjo gi i dhoot madiny, rupiri awacho ri win ni, ji madit jobino temo donjo to jokonyal.
42013025	“Ka won pecho otyeko ay malo to diyo thigo, kada winotemi chungo woko kenyo to wigudo thigo munyo wiwacho ni, ‘Ruoth, yawi ri wan,’ go bino dwoko ni, ‘Akuya ran win kama wiwok'iye.’
42013026	Odoko wibino temo wacho ni, ‘Kole chango wachiemo to wamedho kodin kanyachiel; aka ifuonjo kir i tindi mawan.’ To go bino dwoko ni,
42013027	‘Akuya ran win kama wiwok'iye. Eye win bongan, wijotimi gimarecho!’
42013028	“Gikenyo ywak gi kayo lak bino bedo, kareno wineno Ibrayimu kodi Isaka kodi Yakobo gi jotuchi wach Were i Ker pa Were aka win am'obol win woko.
42013029	Aka ji mawok yu Wokchieŋ kodi yu Podhochieŋ yu Wich piny kodi yu Tyendi piny, jobino mako kabedo pajo i kalima i Ker pa Were.
42013030	Gikenyo joma pama jobedo machowe ama jobino bedo marapena, aka joma oido marapena ama jobino bedo machowe.”
42013031	I hongo no won, Jofarisayo mogo jobino, to jowacho ri Yesu ni, “Eye ka, rupiri Herode mito nekin.”
42013032	To Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Kidhi wiwachi ri kibwe no ni, ‘Kole aryemo woko jwogi aka alechango two konon gi dikin aka ndelo maradek abino chowo tich paran.’
42013033	Kada ameno aripo medirok gi woth paran konon gi dikin gi yawere, rupiri kinyalere neko jatuchi wach Were kaman ma kiweno i Yerusalem.
42013034	“A ji ma Yerusalem, ma joneko jotuchi wach Were modhir ri jo, aka megi jogoyo jo gi telin! Didi ma atyeko temo choko win bongan aumi win pa min gweno ma umo nyithindhe i bwombe, to wikwero!
42013035	Kole Ot pa Were mani kenyo ibino jwango, aka awacho ri win, wikonenan kendo nyuka winowachi ni, ‘Jasilwany a ŋata bino i nyingi Ruoth!’ ”
42014001	I ndelo ma Sabato moro, Yesu okidho chiemo i ot pa achiel kwoŋ Jofarisayo madongo; aka ji joryeko waŋ gin kwoŋe tektek.
42014002	Gikenyo dhano moro ma tyende gi chinge oido obumbere obino bongi Yesu,
42014003	to Yesu luwo malo munyo penjo jofuonji ma Chik kodi Jofarisayo ni, “Chik mawan yeyo botho dhano i ndelo ma Sabato, kosa be?”
42014004	To joliŋ aliŋa. Yesu okwanyo ŋato, obotho go to sewila go.
42014005	Aka Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Ŋa kwoŋ win ma ka punda pere kosa thwon pere opodho i dago maluth i ndelo ma Sabato, di kinyal ywayo to wodho woko mayot?”
42014006	To jokonyalo dwoko go wach no.
42014007	Munyo Yesu oneno paka wendo joyero kabedo mamalo, oluwo ri jo i agecha ni,
42014008	“Ka olwoŋin i kalima ma nywomirok, ikiri iyer kabedo mamalo, ipoyo ŋat man ma loyin gi dwoŋ bende olwoŋ;
42014009	ameno ŋata olwoŋo win nyalo bino to wacho rin ni, ‘Weyi kabedo no ri ŋat me.’ Gikenyo, ibino ay gi wichkwot madwoŋ, t'ikowere i kabedo ma piny loyo.
42014010	Kuchiel, k'ibedo wendo, chomi yu kabedo ma piny t'ibedo kenyo, aka ka ŋata olwoŋo win obino, ama wowachi rin ni, ‘Jawodhan, choreye yu malo kacha.’ Ameno dhano jye mani kodin dhower kenyo bino miyin dwoŋ.
42014011	Ato ŋata won miyere dwoŋ ibino dwoko piny, aka ŋata won bwonere ama ibino miyo dwoŋ.”
42014012	Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri jadwoŋ molwoŋo go ni, “Ka iyiko kalima ri ji, ikiri ilwoŋ merin perin kosa wutimerin kosa wade perin kosa joger perin ma joŋaŋ kende, rupiri jono jonyalo chulin kemba munyo bende jolwoŋin.
42014013	To ka iyiko kalima madwoŋ, lwoŋi jochandi, joma giyagiya, jomoŋol kodi joma waŋ gin otho bende,
42014014	aka inolimi silwany, rupiri jono mere jokonyal chulin kemba moro, to Were won ama bino chulin i ndelo ma jomaleŋ jobino chierin'iye.”
42014015	Munyo achiel kwoŋ jomobedo dhower gi Yesu owinjo gime, owacho ri Yesu ni, “Jasilwany a ŋata ocham mugat i Ker pa Were.”
42014016	To Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Dhano moro chango otimo kalima madwoŋ, to lwoŋo ji mathoth.
42014017	Aka i hongo ma chiemo, go odhiro jotich pere wacho ri joma go olwoŋo ni, ‘Biye win, kole gimoro jye otyeko yikere.’
42014018	To jojye jochako kwayo chwak ayino. Ŋat marapena owacho ni, ‘Atyeko nyiewo lowo, aka aripo kidho neno; akwayin ichwaki ran.’
42014019	Ŋat man owacho ni, ‘Atyeko nyiewo megikwe abich, aka onyo akidho temo jo; akwayin ichwaki ran.’
42014020	Ŋat man owacho ni, ‘Kole nyaka anywomo manyien, ri ameno akinyali bino.’
42014021	Gikenyo jatich no ogik to dwoko wach ri ruoth pere. Won pecho owacho ri jatich pere no gi nge ni, ‘Kidhi i royo madwoŋ kodi i royo jye mokakere i tindi, idwoki kodi jochandi gi jomomyenere gi joma waŋ gin otho kodi jomoŋol.’
42014022	To jatich no owacho ni, ‘Jadwoŋ gima iwacho no jye otyeko timere, to fuodi kabedo nitye modoŋ.’
42014023	Aka won pecho odoko owacho ri jatich no ni, ‘Kidhi i royo man woko ma tindi kodi i thengi royo mogo jye, ilwoŋi ji jowobin i ot paran, ot wopoŋi.
42014024	Awacho ri win ni ongoye moro kwoŋ joma onwaŋo otel lwoŋo jo mobil chiemo paran.’ ”
42014025	Gikenyo kweth ji moasere oido jokwaŋo Yesu; aka Yesu owire oŋiyo yu chien to wacho ri jo ni,
42014026	“Moro jye ma bino bongan kinyal bedo jafuonjirok paran ma k'okutho okwero bamere gi yokimere, kodi chiege, kodi nyithindho pere gi wutimin gi nyimin, kir gi kwo pere won.
42014027	Ŋata won kitiŋi musalaba pere aka luwan, kinyal bedo jafuonjirok paran.
42014028	Ere ŋa kwoŋ win ma ka mito gero ot achurchur, kikuthi bedi piny to kwano welo pesa ma mitere, to neno ka nyalo chowo tich no kosa be?
42014029	Ka kameno, ka go otyeko gero tyendi ot, to chowo mere dhyero go, ji jye ma joneno geto no jobino chako nyiero go,
42014030	ka jowacho ni, ‘Neni win, ŋatin orikin chako geto gima go konyalo chowo.’
42014031	Kosa, kere mene ma ka kidho romo gi kere man i lweny, kikuthi bedi piny to rango ryeko paka go nyalo kwanyo jolweny gana apar kidho romo gi ŋat cha mani gi jolweny gana pyero aryo?
42014032	Aka k'oneno ni kinyali, ka kere man cha fuodi ni boriye, to dhiro ri go jamikwenda wokwayi winjirok ma syem i dyer jo ayin.
42014033	Amomiyo, i dyer win ŋata kimaran loyo gimoro jye ma go ni gine, meno kinyal bedo jafuonjirok paran.
42014034	“Chumbi ber, to ka chwe mere orumo woko, bero no odoko ogiki nedi?
42014035	Chumbi no ngoye kony ri lowo kosa ri kidhur yuk matopo lowo; ikonjo woko ayin. Ŋata ni gi ithe ma winjo wowinji.”
42015001	Ndelo moro jochoki misolo kodi jomarecho mogo jobino bongi Yesu winjo go.
42015002	Gikenyo Jofarisayo kodi jofuonji ma Chik jochako kigesa ni, “Ŋat me jolo jomarecho aka chiemo kir gi jo!”
42015003	Amomiyo, Yesu oluwo ri jo i agecha ama:
42015004	“Ŋa kwoŋ win ma ka nitye gi roombo miya achiel, aka achiel rwenyi, kiwey pyero abuŋwen g'abuŋwen i saa to kidho rango morwenyo cha chuka onwaŋi?
42015005	Aka ka otyeko nwaŋo rombo no, tiŋo i goke gi kisangala.
42015006	Gikenyo ka otundo pecho lwoŋo merin gi joger pere munyo wacho ni, ‘Biye sangala win kodan, rupiri atyeko nwaŋo rombo paran moido orwenyo.’
42015007	Ameno bende awacho ri win, kisangala bino asirok i polo maloyo ru ŋatachiel ma ŋuto recho pere loyo ji motire pyero abuŋwen g'abuŋwen ma kiyenyere ri jo ŋuto kendo.
42015008	“Kosa dhako mene ma ka nitye gi jegejege pesa ma siringi apar to rwenyo achiel, kichwiny tala, to yweyo ot, to rango maber swa iye jye chuka nwaŋo?
42015009	Aka ka onwaŋo pesa no, lwoŋo merin gi joger pere kanyachiel munyo wacho ri jo ni, ‘Biye sangala win kodan, rupiri anwaŋo pesa paran moido orwenyo.’
42015010	Ameno bende awacho ri win, kisangala nitye ri jomalaika pa Were ka jagimarach achiel oŋuto recho pere.”
42015011	Yesu omedo wacho ni, “Jal moro oido nitye gi wote aryo;
42015012	wuode mathin owacho ri bamere ni, ‘Baba, miyan pama lim jye ma aripo lunjo.’ Gikenyo baa jo opoko go lim pere.
42015013	Ndelo okadho manok, to wuode mathin no choko lim pere jye monwaŋo go ni gine, to kadho wiloka mabor, to nyieko woko lim pere no i kwo marach.
42015014	Aka munyo ochowo nyieko woko gimoro jye, kech madwoŋ odonjo i piny no to go bedo ma bu gimoro.
42015015	Gikenyo go okidho bedo paka misemel pa nyatoro i piny no to miyo go tich kwayo mbiji.
42015016	Aka go d'osangala chamo amola majanjal ma mbiji chamo, to moro ongoye momiyo go gimoro.
42015017	To munyo oparo i chunye, owacho ni, ‘Kole jotich pa baba jye jo ni gi chiemo ma jochamo denge to doŋ; to raŋo ma akidho tho kech ama!
42015018	Aleay mayot t'adok bongi baba t'awacho ri go ni, baba, atyeko nyieko i waŋ Were kodi i waŋin.
42015019	Pama akiripi kada alwoŋa ni wuodin kendo; teran paka achiel kwoŋ jotich perin.’
42015020	Gikenyo go oay mayot to chako woth ma dok bongi bamere. “To munyo fuodi go nitye bor ye gi pecho, bamere oneno go; wor opoŋ i chunye to ringo, to podho i kor wuode to chwiyo lembe.
42015021	Gikenyo wuode owacho ni, ‘Baba, atyeko timo gimarach i nyim Were kodi i nyimin. Pama akiripi kada alwoŋa ni wuodin.’
42015022	To bamere olwoŋo jotich pere munyo wacho ni, ‘Redi win! Keli win ruk mabeyo jye wirwaki ri go. Rwaki win ri go peta i lwet chinge gi war i tyende;
42015023	aka kidhi wikel rwath dhyaŋ machwe no wineki, aka weyi konon wachami kalima.
42015024	Kole wuodan me oido otyeko tho to pama onyo kwo; onwaŋo otyeko rwenyo to pama onyo onwaŋere.’ Gikenyo to kalima chakere.
42015025	“I hongo no wuode madwoŋ oido nitye i ndelo. To munyo dwoko aka oido chiegin riko pecho, owinjo wer gi myel.
42015026	Gikenyo olwoŋo jatich achiel to penjo go ni, ‘Aŋo matimere?’
42015027	Jatich odwoko ni, ‘Omerin ama odwoko pecho, aka benin oneko rwath machwe cha, rupiri wuode odwoko maber, kendo molama.’
42015028	Omin madwoŋ nge omako to kwero kir donjo i ot; gikenyo bamere owok woko to temo naŋo go ni wodonji.
42015029	To go odwoko bamere ni, ‘Wowe! Atyeko tich rin kweth oro me jye, ma akichayin kada dichiel, to kole ongoye kada nyathi dyel m'imiyan nike bende atimiye gine kalima ri merin paran.
42015030	Aka wuodin monyieko lim perin gi mon ma jotana delkwoŋ jo i timo gi wichkwot me, ama onyo odwoko pecho to ineko ri go rwath dhyaŋ machwe!’
42015031	Bamere odwoko go ni, ‘Wuodan, kole ndelo jye ini kodan pecho ka, aka gimoro jye mani gine meno aperin.
42015032	Aka oido ripere ni watim kalima wasangala ye; kole omin in me onwaŋo otyeko tho, to pama onyo kwo; onwaŋo otyeko rwenyo, to pama onyo onwaŋere.’ ”
42016001	Yesu odoko owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Obedo jaŋaŋo moro monwaŋo nitye gi jakur mowachi ri go ni nyieko anyieka lim pere.
42016002	Go olwoŋo ŋato to penjo go ni, ‘Awinjo aŋo me kwoŋin? Titi ran kwan kwoŋ tich perin ma kur, rupiri ikile bedo jakur kendo.’
42016003	Gikenyo jakur no won owacho kende ni, ‘Paka ruoth paran onyo kwanyo woko kwoŋan tich ma kur, anotim aŋo? Angoye gi men ma fur, aka wiyan kwot kir kidho kwayirok. Bedo ran wichkwot madwoŋ.
42016004	Ka ameno, awon aŋeyo gima aletimo ma kada oryeman i tich jomogo jobino jolan i pechin pajo.’
42016005	Gikenyo go othumo ryeko to lwoŋo joma jo ni gi banjin pa ruoth pere achielechiele. Ri marapena, owacho ni, ‘Ruoth paran banja in aŋo?’
42016006	Ana ŋato ni, ‘Jerikan miya achiel ma mo wuto.’ Jakur no owacho ni, ‘Ere kwanyi papila perin ma chikirok, ibedi piny mayot aka indiki pyero abich ayino.’
42016007	Ri ŋat man, owacho ni, ‘To in ini gi banja aŋo?’ Ana ŋato ni, ‘Gunia miya achiel ma kal.’ Jakur no owacho ni, ‘Ere kwanyi papila perin machikirok indiki pyero aboro ayino.’
42016008	Ruoth opako jakur ma kigenere no mato go othumo ryeko; ato nyithindho ma piny me joryek i tim pajo wegi loyo nyithindho ma lero.”
42016009	Yesu omedo wacho ni, “Awacho ri win, maki win mere ka wioro ŋaŋo ma kotire ma piny, aka k'orumo aka ibino jolo win i kabedo ma chil gi chil.
42016010	Dhano ma genere i gikipiny mathindho ibino geno go i gimadwoŋ; ŋata kigenere i gikipiny mathindho kogen go i gimadongo.
42016011	Amomiyo ka wikinyalo genirok i ŋaŋo ma kotire ma piny ka, ŋa ma di gen win gi ŋaŋo maradyeri?
42016012	Aka ka ikinyalo genirok i gikipiny pa ŋat man, ŋa m'omiyin gim'obedi aperin won?
42016013	“Ongoye jatich ma nyalo bedo ŋecha pa ruodhe aryo; go bino dak achiel to maro man: bino woro achiel to chayo man. Ikinyal tiyo ri Were kodi ri pesa bende.”
42016014	Jofarisayo jowinjo gikipiny me jye, aka jonyiero Yesu rupiri oido jomaro pesa.
42016015	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Winyuthere ri ji ni wibeyo, to Were oŋeyo chuny win. Kole gima ji paro ni ber moasere, ama bedo gima ongoye kir gi kony i waŋ Were.
42016016	“Chik pa Musa kodi ndiiko pa jotuchi wach Were obedo gi men tundo i ndir pa Yohana Jakibatisa; wok i ndir no Wach Maber ma Ker pa Were ochak tito, aka dhano jye rire donj'iye gi maker.
42016017	To yot ri polo gi piny reyirok, ma kiweno nyieko woko kada nyaka adech mondhilo kwoŋ Chik.
42016018	“Dhano jye ma ryemo chiege to nywomo dhako man meno timo chot; aka ŋata nywomo dhako ma chwore oryemo bende timo chot.
42016019	“Chango obedo jaŋaŋo moro ma ruko nangin mawelo mamalo swa aka chamo chiemo mawelo tektek ndir jye.
42016020	Aka jachandi moro ma nyinge Lazaro bin ryewere piny dho waŋkach pere, kareno adhola odheth kwoŋe gipi.
42016021	Go oido kuro chamo nyaka ŋinjeŋinje chiemo mapodho piny wok i dhower pa jaŋaŋo no; aka ameno gwokere bende jobino to jonaŋo adholin pere.
42016022	Ndelo otundo ma jachandi no otho to jomalaika jotiŋo go, to jotero go bothi Ibrayimu, i polo; jaŋaŋo bende otho tiyiko.
42016023	Munyo go oido nitye i litho madwoŋ swa i piny pa jomotho, otiŋo waŋe malo to neno Ibrayimu gi bor koro, kodi Lazaro kabute.
42016024	Gikenyo olwoŋo go ni, ‘Baba Ibrayimu! Makiye kodan wor idhir ran Lazaro wobili lwet chinge i pi wokweyi ran gine lewan, rupiri ani litho madwoŋ i mach me!’

42016026	To ki meno kende, okethi bur mwombe maluth swa i dyer wan kodi win mageŋo ŋat moro jye ma d'omiti ŋondo wok i thenge mawan bino yu bongi win, kosa wok i thenge mewin bino yu bongi wan korin’

42017001	Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Gikipiny ma miyo ji podho i gimarach ripo bino; to kidamba bino bedo ri ŋata omiy gikipiny no timirok!
42017002	D'ober ri go bedi twey kidi mombo i ŋute tibolo go i wakawaka, loyo go kidho miyo achiel kwoŋ nyaka jomathindho me timo gimarach.
42017003	Kure wini! Ka omerin timo gimarach, kweri rigo, aka ka oŋuti, chwaki go.
42017004	Ka otimo rin marach dibiryo ndelo achiel, aka hongo jye go bino bongin ka wacho ni aŋuto, chwaki go.”
42017005	Jomoor jowacho ri Ruoth ni, “Medi ri wan yeyo mawan.”

42017007	“Bedi moro kwoŋ win nitye gi jatich ma furo, kosa ma kwayo roombo, iparo ni ka jatich no odwoko wok i ndelo, d'owacho ri go ni, ‘Redi mayot i bedi piny ikutho ichiemi?’

42017009	Odoko, i paro ni di go ofuoyo jatich no ka otimo gimoor go?’

42017011	Munyo Yesu oido kidho Yerusalem, oluwo gi i kew ma poko Samarya kodi Galileya.

42017016	to podho piny dho katyendi Yesu to fuoyo go. Jalo oido obedo Jasamarya.

42017019	Aka owacho ri jalo ni, “Ayi malo imaki royo perin; yeyo perin otyeko bothin.”
42017020	Jofarisayo megi jopenjo Yesu ndir ma Ker pa Were obin'iye. Go odwoko ni, “Ker pa Were kilebino i royo ma nenere.
42017021	Ongoye ŋata bino wacho ni, ‘Neni, ee ni ka, kosa ni kacha,’ rupiri Ker pa Were nitye i dyer win won ka.”
42017022	Aka owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Hongo bino tundo ma wibino kiwany'iye neno kada nyaka ndelo achiel kwoŋ ndir pa Wuodi Dhano, to wikibino neno.
42017023	Nitye joma jobino wacho ri win ni, ‘Neni, go dicha!’ kosa ni ‘Neni, go ee ka!’ To wikiri wiay ni wikidho rango go.
42017024	Kole paka lithkoth pilin i pondeponde aka menyo thenge gi thenge, apaka Wuodi Dhano bende obedi i ndelo pere.
42017025	To go ripo kutho chandirok tektek, ji ma ndir me jowokweri go.

42017027	Dhano jye onwaŋo chiemo, medho, aka chwo gi mon jonywomere chuka ndelo otundo ma Nowa odonj'iye i yee, aka mikula obino to neko woko ji jye ma piny.
42017028	Odoko bino bedo paka i ndir pa Lot bende. Dhano jye oido chiemo, medho, nyiewere kendo tana, furo chiemo aka geto.

42017031	“I ndelo no, ŋata nitye malo wi ot wokiri wolori ni donjo i ot kwanyo gikipiny pere mani kenyo; ameno bende, ŋata nitye i ndelo wokiri wodwoki pecho.
42017032	Poyi win chipa Lot!
42017033	Ŋata temo botho kwo pere bino rwenyo woko; ŋata rwenyo woko kwo pere ama bino botho.
42017034	Wor no, awacho ri win, ji aryo jobino nindo i kanindo achiel; ŋatachiel ibino kwanyo tiweyo ŋat man kenyo.
42017035	Mon aryo jobino rego kanyachiel; achiel ibino kwanyo tiweyo nyawote kenyo.

42019020	Gikenyo jatich machowe obino to wacho ni, ‘Jadwoŋ, siringi gana achiel perin ee; akano mopanere i kitambala.
42019021	Ato onwaŋo alworin, rupiri in idhano ma jamahembi. Ikwanyo gima iŋati ikiketho, aka ikecho gima iŋati ikichwoyo.’
42019022	Jalo owacho ri ŋato ni, ‘Ijatich marach, abino thumo rin banja chungo kwoŋ wach perin won! Kere iŋeyo nike abedo jamahembi; ni akwanyo gima akiketho, aka akecho gima akichwoyo;
42019023	to raŋo ma ikiketho pesa paran i kakan, di ka adwoko d'anwaŋo omedere?’

42022058	Hongo machiek okadho to ŋat man neno Petro to wacho ni, “In achiel kwoŋ jonago!” To Petro odwoko ni, “Ojame, ki an!”
42022059	Aka munyo sawa achiel okadho, jal moro omedo wacho g'amen ni, “Ongoye kiganagana ni ŋat me bende oido nitye bothe, rupiri go bende Jagalileya!”
42022060	To Petro odwoko ni, “Ojame, akuya gima iluwo kwoŋe!” Gikenyo won, munyo fuodi go luwo, wuodi gweno okoko.
42022061	Ruoth owire oŋiyo Petro, aka Petro opoyo wach pa Ruoth, paka owacho ni, “Ma fuodi wuodi gweno kukoko konon, ibino kwedere kwoŋan didek.”
42022062	Gikenyo Petro owok to ywak malith.
42022063	Ji monwaŋo jokuro Yesu joyeto go to jochwado go.
42022064	Joboyo waŋe gi nanga aka jopenjo go ni, “Ŋat'ogoyin ŋa? Tuchi ri wan!”
42022065	Aka jowacho gikipiny man madit mayeto go.
42022066	Munyo piny oyawere, kitipa pa jotel pa Joyudaya kodi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jofuonji ma Chik joromo kanyachiel, titero Yesu i kapido pajo.
42022067	Ana jo ni, “Wachi ri wan, in a Kristo?” Go odwoko jo ni, “Ka awacho ri win, wikoyeyi;
42022068	aka ka apenjo win penji, wikodwokan.
42022069	To wok pama kadho yu waŋe, Wuodi Dhano bino bedo yu rachuch pa Were Majameni jye.”
42022070	Jojye jopenjo ni, “Kere in i Wuodi Were?” Go odwoko jo ni, “Kole eno wiwacho.”
42022071	Jowacho ni, “Odoko wayenyo wach mene kendo maridho gime! Kole ee wawegi watyeko winjo wach mowok i dhoke won!”
42023001	Kweth ji gi bee joay to jotero Yesu ruwaŋ Pilato
42023002	kama jochako kel'iye kwoŋe wach ni, “Wanwaŋo jalin komo ji, munyo wacho ri ji ni kiri jowogoyi misolo ri Kaisar aka ŋoyo ni go Kristo mobedo kere.”
42023003	Pilato openjo go ni, “In Kere pa Joyudaya?” Yesu odwoko ni, “Eno iwacho.”
42023004	Gikenyo Pilato owacho ri jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi muma ji no ni, “Akinwaŋi gima miyan athumi banja loyo ŋatin.”
42023005	To nyaka jomedo wacho gi men ni, “Go gi fuonji pere kelo ri ji gwenyirok kwoŋ adhum! Go ochako i Galileya, okidho Yudeya gi bee, aka pama onyo obino ka.”
42023006	Munyo Pilato owinjo gino, openjo ni, “Yesu obedo Jagalileya?”
42023007	Aka munyo go owinjo ni Yesu wok iyadech ma Herode dhum'iye, odhiro go bongi Herode won, ma i hongo no oido bende nitye Yerusalem.
42023008	Herode osangala swa munyo oneno Yesu, rupiri oido otyeko winjo kwoŋe, aka oido otyeko kiwanya neno go hongo malach; oido geno neno Yesu ka timo giraura mogo.
42023009	Amomiyo Herode openjo Yesu kweth penji, to Yesu kodwoko kada wach achiel.
42023010	Jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jofuonji ma Chik jochungo kenyo munyo jokelo wach madongo swa kwoŋ Yesu.
42023011	Herode kodi joserikale pere jokelo ginyiero kwoŋ Yesu to jotimo ri go gichay. Rumachien joruko ri go nanga maŋon to jodwoko go bongi Pilato.
42023012	I ndelo no won ama Herode kodi Pilato jomak'iye mere; rupiri yado onwaŋo jodakere.
42023013	Pilato olwoŋo jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jodhum pa ji kodi ji jye kanyachiel,
42023014	to wacho ri jo ni, “Wikelo ŋatin bongan ka wiwacho ni go komo ji. Onyo atyeko kikaŋasa wach mokel kwoŋe jye ruwaŋ win, to akinwaŋi ni banja loyo go i gikipiny marecho ma wikelo kwoŋe no jye.
42023015	Kada Herode bende konwaŋo kwoŋe banja moro, amomiyo odwoko go bongi wan. Ongoye gima ŋatin otimo ma miyi neki go.
42023016	Amomiyo amito nike wochwadi go, to aweyo go kadho.”
42023017	[I kis hongo ma kalima ma Kadho Pilato yado omaro gonyo ri jo jatwech achiel.]
42023018	Gikenyo ji jye jokoko ni, “Neki go! Gonyi ri wan Baraba ayin!”
42023019	(Baraba me onwaŋo otwey ru gwenyirok kwoŋ adhum mobedo i tindi, kodi ru neko ji).
42023020	Pilato oido mito gonyo Yesu, amomiyo odoko oluwo gi jo;
42023021	to jodwoko gi koko ni, “Guri go, guri go kwoŋ musalaba!”
42023022	Pilato owacho ri jo madidek ni, “To racho aŋo won ma go otimo? Kole akinen racho mogo ma go otimo ma di miyi neki go. Amomiyo alechwado go t'agonyo go.”
42023023	To ji oido jo ni g'arom kodi koko moasere ni woguri go kwoŋ musalaba. Kenyo to dwondi jo umo woko paro man jye.
42023024	Ri ameno Pilato otimo ri jo paka oido joyenyo.
42023025	Ogonyo ri jo ŋata jomito, ŋata onwaŋo otwey ru gwenyirok kodi neko ji, to miyo jo Yesu ni jowotimi gine gima jomito.
42023026	Jokadho gi Yesu, aka munyo fuodi jowotho, joromo gi dhano ma nyinge Simon ma wok Sireno monwaŋo bino i tindi. Jomako go, to jochuko go gi tiŋo musalaba yu ŋey Yesu.
42023027	Kweth ji moasere joluwo Yesu; kwoŋ jo oido nitye mon mogo monwaŋo joywako go, aka jowinjo malith swa.
42023028	Yesu owire oniyo jo to wacho ni, “Mon ma Yerusalem! Wikiri wiywakan, to wiwegi ywakere win kodi nyithindho mewin.
42023029	Kole ndelo odyedere bino ma ji jobino wach'iye ni, ‘Josilwany a mon ma jokonywol, ma jokolimo nyithindho, ma jokomiyo nyithindho dhoth!’
42023030	Meno a hongo ma ji bino wach'iye ri gote ni, ‘Podhi win kwoŋ wan,’ gi ri tendere ni, ‘Ryewere win kwoŋ wan’.
42023031	Rupiri ka gikipiny ma kite no itimo munyo yen fuodi numu, aŋo mobedi ka yen othwo?”
42023032	Jotero jomogo jaryo moido jobedo jokwo ni woneki jo kanyachiel gi Yesu.
42023033	Munyo jotundo kuma ilwoŋo ni, “Kahanga wich”, joguro Yesu kwoŋ musalaba, kodi jokwo aryo no, achiel yu rachuch man yu racham pere.
42023034	Yesu owacho ni, “Baba, chwaki jo rupiri jokuya gima jotimo.” To jogoyo kwir ma poko ruk pere.
42023035	Ji oido jochungo kenyo joŋiyo jo, kareno jodhum pa Joyudaya jonyiero aka joŋalo go ni, “Obotho joman; ere weyi won wobothere, ka go a Kristo ma Were oyero adyeri!”
42023036	Joserikale bende jonyiero go; jobino bonge to jochwayo ri go pigi gimoro ma kech ni womadhi,
42023037	to joŋalo go ni, “Ere iwon bothere, k'inen ibedo Kere pa Joyudaya adyeri.”
42023038	Wach me bende ondik yu wiye: “Me Kere pa Joyudaya.”
42023039	Achiel kwoŋ jokwo molyero kenyo oŋalo go ni, “Kosa in iki Kristo? Ere iwon bothere aka ibothi wan bende!”
42023040	To nyawote obwoko go munyo wacho ni, “Ikilwori Were? Kole ibende ilimo girachula paka apere.
42023041	Aka girachula mawan obedo ru ndir, rupiri walimo gima ripo gi recho ma watimo; to go kotimo recho moro kada achiel.”
42023042	To wacho ri Yesu ni, “Yesu, poyan chieŋ midwok'iye gi men ma Ker perin!”
42023043	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Adyeri awacho rin, konon ibino bedo kodan i kabedo ma yu polo.”
42023044	Dho kapa sawa auchiel, waŋchieŋ oumere to mudho chulo piny gipi kir i sawa abuŋwen;
42023045	aka nanga molyer i Ot pa Were oyech to pokere aryo.
42023046	Yesu okoko gi derino madwoŋ ni, “Baba! Aketho chunyan i chingin!” Munyo otyeko wacho ameno to nyaka tho.
42023047	Jadwoŋ pa joserikale monwaŋo ni kenyo oneno gimotimere, opako Were, munyo wacho ni, “Adyeri jal me oido dhano maber!”
42023048	Munyo ji moido jochokere kenyo neno gima obedi joneno gimotimere, jojye jodok pecho munyo jogoyo pal chuny jo gi rem.
42023049	Ji jye moido joŋeyo Yesu, kanyachiel gi mon ma joluwo go wok Galileya, jochungo gi bor neno gikipiny me.
42023050	Onwaŋo nitye dhano ma nyinge Yozefu, ma wok i tindi pa Joyudaya ma Arimatheya. Go oido achiel kwoŋ jopido kendo dhano maber
42023051	moido koyeyere gi tim kodi atoŋa pa jonicha marach, aka oido go kuro bino ma Ker pa Were. Kada go oido jakweth pa jonek no, go koyeyere gi paro kodi tim pajo.
42023052	Go okidho bongi Pilato to kwayo delkwoŋ Yesu.
42023053	Gikenyo ogamo del no to boyo gi suka matar, to ketho i kalyel mogwor i tele, ma fuodi oido koyik'iye dhano moro jye.

42023056	Gikenyo jodok pecho to joyiko gikipiny kodi mo maŋwe kur ri delkwoŋe. I Sabato joywomere paka Chik wacho.
42024001	Odikini maŋich i ndelo ma chako tich, mon no jokidho i kalyel munyo jotiŋo gikipiny maŋwe kur ma joyiko no.

42024003	to jodonj'iye; to jokonwaŋo delkwoŋ Yesu.

42024005	Mon no joryewere piny, munyo lworo omako jo, aka chwo no jowacho ri jo ni, “Raŋo ma wirango ŋata kwo kwoŋ jomotho?
42024006	Go ongoye ka; otyeko chierino. Poyi win gima go owacho ri win munyo fuodi nitye gi win i Galileya ni
42024007	ibino ketho Wuodi Dhano i chingi ji marecho, jowoguri go kwoŋ musalaba to ichierino go i ndelo maradek.”

42024010	Mon no oido obedo Marya ma wok Magdala, Yoana kodi Marya min Yakobo; jono, kodi mon man ma jobedo bothi jo, jotero wach me ri jomoor.

42024012	Petro oay oringo yu kalyel; oluŋere to neno nengin ma kalyel kende mongoye gimoro man. Gikenyo go odok pecho munyo dhyer kwoŋ gimotimere.
42024013	I ndelo no won, jaryo kwoŋ jo oido jokidho yu loka milwoŋo ni Emaus, chiegin mairo abiryo wok Yerusalem,
42024014	aka onwaŋo joluwo kwoŋ gikipiny jye motimere.

42024020	To jotel mawan mapa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi ruodhe, jotero go ni wothumi ri go banja ma tho, to joguro go kwoŋ musalaba.
42024021	Aka onwaŋo wageno nike go ama bino botho Israel! Medo kwoŋ meno jye, konon ndelo maradek chuka gino timere.

42024023	to jokonwaŋo delkwoŋe. Jodwoko munyo jowacho ni jomalaika moro jomenyere ri jo ma jowacho nike go kwo.
42024024	Jowoti wan megi bende jokidho i kalyel aka jonwaŋo ni obedo adyeri paka mon no jowacho ri jo won, to jokoneno ri gin go won.”

42024027	Yesu otito ri jo gima Ndiiko Maleŋ oluwo kwoŋe chako kwoŋ kitawin pa Musa tundo i ndiiko pa jotuchi wach Were jye.

42024029	to jojuko go munyo jowacho ni, “Rwayi gi wan; kole piny oyutho aka onyo lokere machol.” Ri ameno Yesu odonjo to bedo gi jo.
42024030	Munyo obedo dhower gi jo, okwanyo mugat to miyo silwany; gikenyo to turo mugat no to miyo jo.
42024031	Gikenyo waŋ jo oyawere to nyaka joŋeyo go; to go leny woko i waŋ jo ni many.

42024034	aka onwaŋo jowacho ni, “Ruoth bende ochierino won, aka Simon otyeko neno go!”

42024040	Owacho gime to nyutho jo chinge gi tyende.

42024043	ma go ojolo to chamo ruwaŋ jo.

42024048	Wibedo jokony i gikipiny me.

43001001	I chakirok, wach oido nitye; go oido nitye gi Were, aka wach no oido obedo Were won.
43001002	Wok i chakirok go oido nitye gi Were.
43001003	Gi go Were ochweyo gimoro jye ma nitye, ongoye gima nitye ma go ama kochweyo.
43001004	Gimoro jye ma nitye olimo kwo i go aka kwo no oido a lero pa ji.
43001005	Lero no lyel i mudho aka mudho kinyal niaŋ kwoŋe.
43001006	Dhano moro obino, ma Were ooro, nyinge Yohana.
43001007	Go obino paka jamikwenda ma luwo ri lero no, ŋey dhano jye woyeyi ru wach pere.
43001008	Go ama oido ki lero no, to jamikwenda ma luwo ri lero ayin.
43001009	Lero maradyeri ma miyo ji jye lero, won ama onwaŋo lebino i piny.
43001010	Go obedo i piny, ma chakirok mere owok bonge, to piny koŋeyo go.
43001011	Go obino i piny pere won, to ji pere jokojolo go.
43001012	To ji jye ma jojolo go ma joyeyo i nyinge, omiyo jo men ma lokirok nyithindho pa Were.
43001013	Nywolirok pa jono kobedo ma remo pa dhano, kosa ru mito pa ji, to ru mito pa Were won.
43001014	Wach olokere Dhano, aka obedo gi wan, to waneno dwoŋ pere paka Wuodi Were achiel kende, mowok bongi Were Bawan, mopoŋ gi ŋono kodi adyeri.
43001015	Yohana obedo paka jamikwenda pere mokoko ka wacho ni, “Me a ŋata atyeko luwo kwoŋe ni, ‘Ŋata luwan chien loyan swa gi dwoŋ, rupiri go otelo bedo ran.’ ”
43001016	Adyeri, wajojye watyeko nwaŋo ŋono wi ŋono kwoŋ ŋaŋo pere.
43001017	Kole Chik obino gi i chingi Musa, to ŋono kodi adyeri obino ri wan ka luwo bongi Yesu Kristo.
43001018	Ongoye moro motyeko neno Were, kwanyo woko Wuode won morikere ruŋeti Bamere ama onyutho wan go.
43001019	Me a gima Yohana owacho munyo Joyudaya ma Yerusalem jooro jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kanyachiel gi Jolevi penjo go ni, “To in iŋa?”
43001020	Yohana kokwero dwoko, to owacho kamaler ni, “Aŋata akibedo Kristo.”
43001021	To jopenjo go ni, “To in iŋa won? In Eliya?” Go odwoko ni, “A ki go.” Jopenjo go kendo ni, “Ibedo jatuchi wach Were?” Ana go ni, “Be!”
43001022	Gikenyo jowacho ni, “Ere wachi ri wan ŋat'ibedo to. Waripo dwoko wach ri joma jooro wan. Iwacho aŋo ma mako kwoŋin iwon.”
43001023	Ana Yohana ni, “Abedo, ‘Dwondi ŋata koko i thim ni, Tiri win royo pa Ruoth wowoth'iye!’ ” (Me a gima jatuchi wach Were, Isaya owacho.)
43001024	Jofarisayo ama jodhiro jomikwenda no.
43001025	Jopenjo Yohana ni, “Ka in iki Kristo kosa Eliya kosa jatuchi wach Were, to raŋo m'imiyo batisimo?”
43001026	Yohana odwoko ni, “An amiyo batisimo kodi pi; to idyer win ka ochungo ŋata wikuya.
43001027	Go luwan chien, aka akiripi kada gonyo thol war pere.”
43001028	Gikipiny me jye otimere i Bethaniya loka ma jwom Yordan kama go oido miy'iye ji batisimo.
43001029	Yawere mere Yohana oneno Yesu munyo bino bonge to wacho ni, “Neni Nyathi rombo pa Were ma kwanyo woko gimarach ma piny!
43001030	Me a ŋata oido aluwo kwoŋe munyo awacho ni, ‘Moro luwan chien, aka loyan gi dwoŋ rupiri go ama otelo bedo ran.’
43001031	An won oido akiŋeyo go, to abino timo tich ma miyo ji batisimo gi pi ŋey go wonenere kamaler ri Joisrael.”
43001032	Me a mikwenda ma Yohana omiyo, “Aneno Chuny Maleŋ oloro wok i polo to pye kwoŋe.
43001033	An oido akiŋeyo go, to Were mooran miyo ji batisimo gi pi ama owacho ran ni, ‘Ŋat'inonen Chuny Maleŋ loro piny to pye kwoŋe, meno a ŋata ripo miyo ji batisimo gi Chuny Maleŋ.’
43001034	Aka atyeko neno gi tito ri ji nike ŋat me won a Wuodi Were.”
43001035	Yawere mere Yohana onwaŋo ochungo kenyo kodi jofuonjirok pere aryo;
43001036	aka munyo oneno Yesu wotho, owacho ni, “Neni Nyathi rombo pa Were!”
43001037	Jofuonjirok aryo no jowinjo munyo go wacho ameno to joluwo Yesu.
43001038	Yesu owire to neno jono munyo joluwo go, to penjo jo ni, “Wiyenyo aŋo?” Jodwoko ni, “Rabi, ibedo kune?” (Rabi, nyaka ni jafuonji).
43001039	Go odwoko ni, “Biye neni win.” Gikenyo jokidho gine to joneno kama go bed'iye, to jochowo ndelo no bonge (ato onwaŋo obedo kapa sawa apar mothyeno).
43001040	Achiel kwoŋ ji aryo ma jowinjo gima Yohana owacho, to joluwo Yesu, obedo Andereya, omin Simon Petro.
43001041	Gikenyo Andereya onwaŋo Simon, omin go, to wacho ri go ni, “Wanwaŋo Mesiya.” (Wach me dwoŋ mere ni Kristo).

43001043	Yawere mere Yesu oyiko paro ma kidho Galileya, to nwaŋo Filipo to wacho ri go ni, “Luwan!”
43001044	(Filipo onwaŋo wok Bethsaida, tindi ma Andereya kodi Petro bende onwaŋo jowok'iye.)
43001045	Gikenyo Filipo onwaŋo Nathanayel to wacho ri go ni, “Watyeko nwaŋo ŋata Musa ondiko kwoŋe i kitawo ma Chik, kodi ŋata jotuchi wach Were jondiko kwoŋe. Go obedo Yesu, wuodi Yozefu ma Nazareth.”

43001048	Nathanayel openjo go ni, “Iŋeyan nedi?” Ana Yesu, “Anenin munyo ibedo i tyendi makuyu, ma fuodi Filipo kobino lwoŋin.”
43001049	Nathanayel odwoko ni, “Jafuonji, ibedo Wuodi Were! In a Kere pa Joisrael!”
43001050	Yesu owacho ni, “Iyeyo nyaka rupiri awacho rin nike anenin munyo ibedo i tyendi makuyu? Ibino neno gikipiny madongo maloyo me!”
43001051	Aka Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Adyeri awacho rin, ibino neno munyo polo oyawere kareno jomalaika pa Were joidho malo aka joloro piny wi Wuodi Dhano.”
43002001	I ndelo maradek kalima ma nywomirok obedo i tindi ma Kana i Galileya. Min Yesu oido ni kenyo
43002002	aka Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere bende oido olwoŋ jo i kalima no.
43002003	Munyo vini jye orumo, min Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Kole vini orumo ri jo.”
43002004	Yesu odwoko ni, “Dhakodwoŋ, iraŋo ithuyan gi wach me? Kole ndir paran fuodi kotundo.”
43002005	Gikenyo min Yesu owacho ri joma poko chiemo gi giramadha ni, “Timi win gimoro jye ma go owachi ri win.”
43002006	Joyudaya jonitye gi kite ma logo, ri ameno kenyo oido nitye degi auchiel ma telin, aka kis achiel onwaŋo dwoŋ ma romo ayigin aŋwen kosa auchiel.
43002007	Yesu owacho ri jotich ni, “Ere poŋi win pi i degi no.” Jopoŋo degi no gi pi kir malo ni sit,
43002008	to wacho ri jo ni, “Onyo twomi win pi moro witer ri jadwoŋ ma telo kalima.” Jono jotero ri go pi no,
43002009	to go bilo, aka onwaŋo oido otyeko lokere vini. Go koŋeyo kama vini no owok'iye to jotich ma jotwomo pi ama joŋeyo. Gikenyo go olwoŋo won kalima,
43002010	to wacho ri go ni, “Kole dhano jye kutho pen poko vini maber tektek mere, aka ka wendo jotyeko medho moromo aka nyaka poko vini ma ndir jye. To in ikano vini maber tektek mere tundo pama!”
43002011	Yesu otimo giraura marapena me i Kana i Galileya; kenyo go onyuth'iye dwoŋ pere, aka jofuonjirok pere joyeyo go.
43002012	Munyo gino orumo, Yesu kodi yokimere, gi wutimin kodi jofuonjirok pere jokidho Kapernaum, to jobedo kenyo ndelo manok.
43002013	Munyo ndir oido orikere ma poyo ndelo ma Kadho, Yesu okidho Yerusalem.
43002014	Go onwaŋo ji jotana gikipiny i Ot pa Were paka: dhok, roombo, kodi akurin; aka joma wilo pesa oido jobedo dho meza pajo.
43002015	Gikenyo go omino adasa to ryemo woko lee jye i Ot pa Were, gi roombo kanyachiel gi dhok; aka oywoyo woko pesa to ŋilo woko mezin pa jowili pesa;
43002016	Ooro joma tana akurin ni, “Kwanyi wi woko akurin no ka! Wikiri wiloki Ot pa Baba katale!”
43002017	Gikenyo jofuonjirok pere jopoyo gima ondik ni, “Maro Ot perin, a Were, waŋo chunyan pa mach.”
43002018	Rumachien Joyudaya jodwoko bonge gi penji ni, “Giraura aŋo m'inyalo timo ma nyutho wan nike initye gi men matimo gime?”
