43002020	Jopenjo go ni, “Ot pa Were me motero wan oro pyero aŋwen g'achiel gipi gero, ama iwacho ni ibino gero i ndelo adek won kende?”
43002021	To Ot pa Were ma Yesu oluwo kwoŋe oido obedo delkwoŋe ayino.
43002022	Amomiyo munyo go ochierino kwoŋ jomotho, jofuonjirok pere jopoyo nike go oido wacho gino ayin; gikenyo to joyeyo gima ondik kodi wach ma Yesu owacho.
43002023	Munyo go fuodi ni Yerusalem i kalima ma Kadho, ji madit joyeyo nyingi go munyo joneno ranyuth m'otimo.
43002024	To Yesu konyuthere kamaler ri jo kwoŋbedo go oido oŋeyo dhano jye.
43002025	Oido ongoye kony nyatoro wacho ri go gimoro kwoŋ jo rupiri go won oido oŋeyo gima ni chuny jo.
43003001	Nitye nyatoro ma nyinge Nikodemo, jatel pa Joyudaya, mobedo Jafarisayo.
43003002	Ŋato obino bongi Yesu Wor achiel to wacho ri go ni, “Jafuonji, waŋeyo paka ibedo jafuonji ma Were ama ooro. Ongoye ŋata nyalo timo giraura m'itimo kwanyo woko ka Were ni gine.”
43003003	Yesu odwoko ni, “Adyeri awacho rin, ongoye ŋata nyalo neno Ker pa Were kwanyo woko ka onywole madiryo.”
43003004	Nikodemo openjo ni, “Nyalere nedi ŋata otyeko dwoŋ nywolirok kendo? Kole go kinyal donjo i iyi min kendo ŋey wonywol go madiryo!”
43003005	Ana Yesu, “Adyeri awacho rin, ongoye ŋata nyalo donjo i Ker pa Were kwanyo woko ka olimo nywolirok ma pi kodi ma Chuny.
43003006	Gima del onywolo bedo madel, aka gima Chuny onywolo bende bedo machuny.
43003007	Ikiri ibedi gi dhyer ni awacho rin ni, ‘Iripo nywolirok madiryo!’
43003008	Kole koyo kudho yu thenge m'omito jye; wiwinjo derino mere, to wikiŋey kama owok'iye kosa kama chom'iye.” Meno bende apaka ŋata onywolere machuny chalo.
43003009	To Nikodemo omedo openjo ni, “Gime nyalere nedi?”
43003010	Yesu odwoko ni, “In i jafuonji madwoŋ ma Israel gipi, ama ikuya gime?
43003011	Adyeri awacho rin, waluwo gima waŋeyo, aka wawacho gima watyeko neno to ongoye moro kwoŋ win ma yeyo jolo mikwenda mawan.
43003012	K'inen wikiyey ka awacho ri win gikipiny ma piny ka; onyo winonyal nedi yeyo ka awacho ri win gikipiny ma polo?
43003013	Aka ongoye moro motyeko kidho i polo kwanyo woko Wuodi Dhano mobino i piny wok i polo.
43003014	“Aka paka Musa oŋawo thwol ma nyweny wi yath moro i thim, apaka bende ibino ŋawo Wuodi Dhano malo.
43003015	Ameno nyaka dhano jye ma yeyo go bino bedo gi kwo makirum.
43003016	Kole Were omaro piny tektek to miyo Wuode achiel g'achiel, ni nyatoro jye ma yeyo go wokiri wotho to wobedi gi kwo makirum.
43003017	Ato Were kooro Wuode i piny ka nike wothumi ri piny banja, to ni piny wonyali limo both kwoŋ go ayino.
43003018	Ongoye moro jye ma yeyo Wuodi Were m'ibino thumo ri go banja, to moro jye ma kiyey ama otyek thumo ri go banja ni oloyo go chon kwoŋ bedo koketho yeyo i nyingi Wuodi Were achiel kende.
43003019	Me apaka thumo banja bedo: lero obino i piny to ji jomaro mudho ayino kapa lero, rupiri jotimo gikipiny marecho.
43003020	Aka moro jye ma timo gikipiny marecho meno odak lero aka kibin kama di lero, rupiri kimiti ni tim pere marecho wonyuthere kamaler.
43003021	To ŋata timo gimotire bino kama di lero, ŋey lero wonyuthi nike go otimo tich pere munyo winjo Were.”
43003022	Rumachien Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere jokidho i adech ma Yudeya to chowo kenyo hongo moro gi jo munyo miyo ji batisimo.
43003023	Yohana oido bende miyo ji batisimo i Ayenon, chiegin gi Salim, rupiri pi oido nitye kenyo kweth. Ji oido jokidho bonge hongo jye womiyi jo batisimo.
43003024	(Gime otimere ma Yohana oido fuodi kotwey.)
43003025	Jofuonjirok pa Yohana megi jochako pyem kodi Jayudaya moro kwoŋ lonyirok ma nyadin.
43003026	Gikenyo jobino bongi Yohana to jowacho ri go ni, “Jafuonji, dhano moido nitye kodin loka mecha ma Yordan miluwo kwoŋe, pama miyo ji batisimo aka dhano jye onyo kidho bonge!”
43003027	Yohana odwoko ni, “Ongoye dhano ma nyalo bedo gi gimoro kwanyo woko ka Were amomiyo go.
43003028	Wiwegi wibedo jokony paran ni awacho ni aŋata akibedo Kristo, to ooran telo ri go ayin.
43003029	“Jamweha ama migole manyako bedo apere; jakony pa jamweha chungo ruŋete to chiko ithe wowinji gima timere, aka go sangala swa ka owinjo dwondi jamweha. Meno bende apaka kisangala paran onyo oromo.
43003030	Go ripo medo ŋeyirok kareno ŋeyirok paran mojere woko.”
43003031	Ŋata wok malo i polo ama loyo ji jye; ŋata wok i piny ka meno dhano ma piny ka, aka luwo kwoŋ gikipiny ma piny ka. To Ŋata wok i polo loyo ji jye.
43003032	Go luwo kwoŋ gima go otyeko neno gi winjo, to ongoye ŋata jolo mikwenda pere.
43003033	To ŋata otyeko jolo mikwenda pere otyeko niaŋo ji gi ranen nike Were obedo jaradyeri.
43003034	Ŋata Were ooro, luwo wach pa Were, rupiri Were miyo go Chuny Maleŋ mopoŋ ma kobuyo.
43003035	Were Baba omaro Wuode aka oketho gimoro jye i chingi go.
43003036	Ŋata yeyo Wuode nitye gi kwo makirum; ŋata kiwinji Wuode kolimi kwo, to keme pa Were ama bino tundo ri go.
43004001	Munyo Yesu oniaŋ nike Jofarisayo jotyeko winjo ni go onyo ywayo ji bonge aka miyo ji madit batisimo loyo Yohana,
43004002	(Iyadyeri, Yesu komiyo nyatoro batisimo, to jofuonjirok pere ama oido jotimo ameno.)
43004003	Go oeye Yudeya to gik yu Galileya;
43004004	Aka go onwaŋo ripo luwo gi Samarya.
43004005	Go obino i tindi ma Samarya milwoŋo ni Sika, moido chiegin gi ndelo ma Yakobo chango omiyo Yozefu, wuode.
43004006	Waŋ pi pa Yakobo oido ni kenyo, aka Yesu munyo ool gi woth, obedo piny dho waŋ pi no oido obedo odyechieŋ kapa sawa auchiel.
43004007	Dhasamarya moro obino kulo, to Yesu wacho ri go ni, “Miyan ye pi amadhi.”
43004008	(Jofuonjirok pere onwaŋo fuodi jokidho i tindi nyiewo chiemo.)
43004009	Dhasamarya no odwoko ni, “Kole in i Jayudaya aka an a Jasamarya; inyalo nedi kwayan pi amadha?” (Ato Joyudaya oido jokitiyere gi Josamarya kosa jokiori atewe pa Josamarya kendo jokimadhi pi gi agwetin ma Josamarya jomadhiye pi.)
43004010	Yesu odwoko ni, “Bedi iŋey mich pa Were kodi ŋata kwayin pi amadha, d'ikwayo go aka d'omiyin pi makwo.”
43004011	Dhako no owacho ni, “Jadwoŋ kole ingoye kodi gitwomo pi aka waŋ pi luth. Inonwaŋ kune pi makwo m'iwacho no?
43004012	Iparo ni idwoŋ loyo kwari wan Yakobo momiyo wan waŋ pi me; aka go kodi wote, kodi mwendi pere jomadho pi me?”
43004013	Ana Yesu ni, “Moro jye ma madho pi me bino winjo riyo kendo;
43004014	to ŋata omadhi pi ma abino miyo go odoko kibino winjo riyo kendo. Aka pi ma anomiy go bino lokere i go waŋ pi mamol to miyo go kwo makirum.”
43004015	Ana dheno ni, “Jadwoŋ, miyan pi no aka ŋeyi akir adoko awinji riyo kosa adwoki ka kendo kulo.”
43004016	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Kidhi ilwoŋ chworin idwoki gine ka”
43004017	Dheno odwoko ni, “Angoye gi chworan.” Ana Yesu ni, “Itire wacho ni ingoye gi chworin,
43004018	rupiri ityeko nywomirok gi chwo abich, aka ŋata pama ibedo gine no bende kobedo chworin. Iwacho giradyeri.”
43004019	Dhako no owacho ni, “Jadwoŋ, onyo aniaŋ ni kere i jatuchi wach Were.
43004020	Kole kwarere mawan yado jolamo Were wi got me, to win wi Joyudaya wiwacho ni Yerusalem a kuma waripo lam'iye Were.”
43004021	Yesu odwoko go ni, “Dhako me, yeyi gima awacho rin; hongo bino tundo ma ji jokolam Baba wi got me kosa kada i Yerusalem.
43004022	Win Josamarya wilamo gima wikuya; to wan Joyudaya waŋeyo gima walamo, kwoŋbedo both wok bongi Joyudaya.
43004023	To hongo bino, aka ee otyeko kir tundo, ma joma lamo Baba i yo motire, jobino lamo go i Chuny kodi iyadyeri, rupiri Baba yenyo joma lamo go ameno.
43004024	Were obedo Chuny aka joma lama go joripo lamo go i chuny kodi iyadyeri.”
43004025	Dhako no owacho ri go ni, “Aŋeyo ni Mesiya (milwoŋo ni Kristo), lebino, aka ka obino lewacho ri wan kis gimoro.”
43004026	Yesu odwoko go ni, “An won a go, an maluwo kodin me.”
43004027	I hongo no won to jofuonjirok pa Yesu jodwoko, to jodhyer swa munyo jonwaŋo go luwo kodi dhako. To ongoye kwoŋ jo ŋata openjo go kada ni, “Imito aŋo?” kosa ni, “Raŋo m'iluwo gi dheno?”
43004028	Gikenyo dhako no oweyo dakipi pere, ogik i tindi, to wacho ri ji ma kenyo ni,
43004029	“Biye neni win dhano mowacho ran gimoro jye matyeko timo, kosa go a Kristo?”
43004030	Gikenyo ji joay i tindi to jokidho bongi Yesu.
43004031	I hongo no jofuonjirok oido jokwayo Yesu nike, “Jafuonji, chiemiye!”
43004032	To odwoko jo ni, “Anitye gi chiemo achama ma wikuya.”
43004033	Gikenyo jofuonjirok pere wegi jochako penjirok kendigin ni, “Yagi, kosa moro nende okelo ri go chiemo?”
43004034	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Chiemo paran obedo timo gima ŋata ooran yenyo gi chowo tich pere.
43004035	“Wingoye gi agecha ma wimaro luwo ni, ‘Odoŋ dwe aŋwen to kecho tundo?’ Awacho ri win, kaŋasa win ndelin maber: gim'ochwoy pama otyeko chiek aka otundo akecha.
43004036	Ŋata kecho limo kemba, aka ameno go choko gimonyak ri kwo makirum, ŋey jachwoyo kodi jakecho jye jowosangala kanyachiel.
43004037	Kole agecha me ripo ni, ‘Ŋatachiel chwoyo aka ŋat man kecho.’
43004038	Adhiro win kecho gima wikichwoyo; joman ama jonekere gi tich mere, aka onyo widonjo limo bero ma wok i kwok pajo.”
43004039	Josamarya mathoth ma tindi no joyeyo Yesu rupiri dhako no owacho ri jo ni, “Go owacho ran gimoro jye matyeko timo.”
43004040	Gikenyo Josamarya jobino bonge to jokwayo go nike wobedi gi jo, to Yesu bedo kenyo ndelo aryo.
43004041	Ji mathoth man joyeyo go ru fuonji pere,
43004042	aka jowacho ri dhako no ni, “Pama onyo wayeyo go, ki ru kwoŋbedo gima iwacho, to rupiri wawegi watyeko winjo go, aka onyo waŋeyo adyeri ni go a Jaboth pa piny.”
43004043	Munyo ndelo aryo no orumo, Yesu oeye kenyo to kidho Galileya,
43004044	kada nende go won onwaŋo otyeko wacho ni, “Jatuchi wach Were kimiy go dwoŋ i piny pere won.”
43004045	To munyo go otundo Galileya, ji jojolo go, rupiri jo wegi ndir cha jokidho Yerusalem i ndelo madwoŋ ma kalima ma Kadho to joneno gimoro jye ma go otimo i kalima no.
43004046	Gikenyo Yesu ogik i Kana ma Galileya, kama go ndir cha olok'iye pi vini. Kenyo onwaŋo nitye jadwoŋ moro ma wuode oido two yu Kapernaum.
43004047	Munyo jalo owinjo ni Yesu obino Galileya wok Yudeya, okidho bonge to kwayo go nike wokidhi Kapernaum wobothi ri go wuode monwaŋo chiegin tho.
43004048	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Ato ka wikineno ranyuth madongo wikoyey!”
43004049	Jadwoŋ ma Jaroma no odwoko ni, “Jadwoŋ, bowe wakadhi ka fuodi nyathi paran kotho.”
43004050	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Kadhi, wuodin bino kwo!” Jalo oyeyo gima Yesu owacho ri go to kadho.
43004051	Munyo fuodi ni royo kadho, jotich pere joromo gine to jowacho ri go ni wuode kwo.
43004052	Go openjo jo ni two oweyo go keraŋo, to jowacho ni, “Nyoro odyechieŋ kapa sawa abiryo ama two no owey'iye go.”
43004053	Gikenyo bamere opoyo ni i hongo no won ama Yesu owach'iye ri go ni, “Wuodin bino kwo.” Ri ameno go kodi pecho pere gipi joyeyo.
43004054	Me obedo giraura mararyo ma Yesu otimo munyo otyeko wok Yudeya okidho Galileya.
43005001	Rumachien, kalima pa Joyudaya ma nyadin obedo to Yesu kidho Yerusalem.
43005002	I Yerusalem, dho waŋkach milwoŋo ni Ma Rombo, ma i Dhoyudaya ilwoŋo ni Bethzatha, nitye dago moro mani gi kadonjo abich.
43005003	Aka kidhur ji matwo oido jonitye dho kadonjo no jye. Joma waŋ gin otho, jomoŋol, kodi jomatwo nyaŋinya. [Jono onwaŋo jokuro pi woichere;
43005004	rupiri dichiel dichiel malaika pa Ruoth oido bin loro piny i dago no to icho pi. Aka jatwo m'open donjo i dago no ka otyek icho pi, ama two pere ma nger jye both woko.]
43005005	Kenyo onwaŋo nitye nyatoro monwaŋo otyeko two oro pyeradek g'aboro.
43005006	Munyo Yesu oneno go opyele piny kenyo, to ŋeyo nike ŋato oido otyeko two hongo malach; ameno openjo go ni, “Imito bedo maber?”
43005007	Jatwo no odwoko ni, “Jadwoŋ, angoye gi moro ma nyalo kethan i dago ka pi oichere; ka nyaka ni atem donjo i pi, ŋat man ama telo donjo ran.”
43005008	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Ayi malo, kwanyi par perin, iwothi.”
43005009	Piyo piyo no, ŋato obedo maber, okwanyo par pere, to wotho kadho. Ndelo no oido obedo Sabato pa Joyudaya,
43005010	amomiyo jowacho ri ŋata owok both no ni, “Kole konon Sabato, aka Chik kiyeyin tiŋo par perin.”
43005011	Go odwoko ni, “Ŋata obothan owacho ni, Tiŋi par perin iwothi.”
43005012	Aka jopenjo go ni, “Manago ŋa no m'owacho rin ni itiŋ par perin iwothi?”
43005013	To jalo koŋeyo ŋatago, rupiri Yesu oido otyeko rwenyo i dyer ji mathoth moido jonitye kenyo.
43005014	Rumachien, Yesu onwaŋo go i Ot pa Were to wacho ri go ni, “Neni, pama onyo ityeko bedo maber! Onyo ikiri idoko igiki i timo recho, ka kameno giman nyalo timin marach maloyo meno.”
43005015	Gikenyo ŋato okadho to wacho ri Joyudaya ni Yesu ama obotho go.
43005016	Ru wach me, Joyudaya jochako lweny gi Yesu, rupiri omaro timo gima pameno i Sabato.
43005017	To Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Kole Baba tiyo noknok, aka abende onyo atiyo.”
43005018	Wach me omiyo Joyudaya jomedo ridho paro ma neko go; rupiri go oido koturo nyaka chik ma Sabato kende, to oido wacho bende ni Were meno Bamere won, aka ameno go won kethere i kabedo marom g'apa Were.
43005019	Gikenyo Yesu odwoko ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, Wuodi Were kitim gimoro gi men pere won; to go timo gima oneno Bamere timo. Gima Bamere timo ama Wuode bende timo.
43005020	Kole Were Baba omaro Wuode aka nyutho go gimoro jye ma go won timo. Go bino nyutho Wuode kir gikipiny maloyo me, aka wibino uro
43005021	rupiri paka Bamere chierino jomotho aka miyo jo kwo, apaka Wuode bende miyo joma go oyenyo kwo.
43005022	Baba won kithumi banja ri nyatoro, to omiyo Wuode men jye ma thumo banja
43005023	aka ŋey dhano jye wowori Wuodi Were paka joworo Bamere. Ŋata kiwor Wuodi Were meno bende kiwor Bamere mooro go.
43005024	“Adyeri awacho ri win, nyatoro jye ma winjo wach paran, to yeyo ŋata ooran, nitye gi kwo makirum. Aka kothumi ri go banja rupiri go otyeko wok i tho odonjo i kwo.
43005025	Adyeri awacho ri win, ndir bino tundo aka otyeko kir tundo ma jomotho jobino winj'iye dwondi Wuodi Were, aka dhano jye ma winjo dwonde bino kwo.
43005026	Ato paka Baba ni gi kwo kwoŋe, apaka otyeko miyo Wuode bende bedo gi kwo kwoŋe.
43005027	Aka go otyeko miyo Wuode men ma thumo banja, rupiri go obedo Wuodi Dhano.
43005028	Wikiri widhyeri kwoŋ gime; kole ndir bino ma jomotho jye ma jonitye i kalyel jobino winj'iye dwonde,
43005029	aka jobino wok kenyo: joma timo gimabeyo jobino chierino to jokwo, aka joma timo recho ibino chierino jo to ithumo banja loyo jo.
43005030	“Akinyal timo gimoro awon kendan; athumo banja paka Were wacho ran, amomiyo thumo banja paran otire, rupiri akitem timo gima awon amito, to gima ŋata ooran ama mito.
43005031	Bedi awon aluwo gima mako kwoŋan, d'onyo wach paran kibedi motire;
43005032	to nitye ŋat man ma chungo aka luwo kaparan, aka aŋeyo nike gima go wacho kwoŋan otire.
43005033	“Wioro jomikwenda bongi Yohana aka kole go otyeko luwo ma ridho adyeri no.
43005034	Kobedo nike athenere kwoŋ wach pa dhano, to awacho ama aka ŋey wilimi both ayin.
43005035	Yohana oido obedo paka tala malyel ka miyo lero, aka wiyeyo kir kisangala i lero pere nyaka hongo machiek.
43005036	To wach ma an awodh'iye kony dwoŋ maloyo kir ma Yohana omiyo: ato tich ma an atimo obedo ma Baba ama omiyan timo, aka tich no nyutho kamaler ni Baba ama ooran.
43005037	Aka Baba mooran, bende otyeko luwo kwoŋan. Fuodi wikiwinjo dwonde, odoko fuodi wikineno chal pere,
43005038	aka wingoye gi wach pere i win; rupiri wikiyeyo ŋata go ooro.
43005039	Wifuonjere Ndiiko Maleŋ rupiri wiparo ni wibino nwaŋ'iye kwo makirum; aka kole Ndiiko no ama luwo kwoŋan!
43005040	To jye fuodi wikiyey bino bongan limo kwo.
43005041	“Akiyeny pak pa ji,
43005042	to aŋeyo win maber, nike wingoye kodi mar pa Were i chuny win.
43005043	Ee abino i men pa Baba to wikijolan; to ka moro obin gi men pere won, ama wibino jolo.
43005044	Onyo winyalo yeyo nedi ka wimito pak mawok bongi wiwegi, aka wikitem limo pak mawok bongi Were won.
43005045	Wikiri wipar nike abino kiosa win bongi Baba. Musa ma wigeno kwoŋe no won ama bino kelo kwoŋ win wach.
43005046	Bedi wiyeyo Musa, d'onyo wiyeyan bende, rupiri go ondiko gima mako kwoŋan.
43005047	To ka wikiyey gima go ondiko, winonyal nedi yeyo gima awacho?”
43006001	Rumachien, Yesu ogik to chiewere i wakawaka ma Galileya (kosa ma Tiberya).
43006002	Lwak ji madwoŋ oluwo go, rupiri oido joneno ranyuth m'otimo kwoŋ botho jotwo.
43006003	Yesu oidho tendere, to bedo piny gi jofuonjirok pere.
43006004	Ndelo pa Joyudaya madwoŋ ma kalima ma Kadho, onwaŋo orikere.
43006005	Munyo Yesu oŋiyo kor gi korin to neno ni muma ji madwoŋ onwaŋo bino bonge, openjo Filipo ni, “Wanyalo nyiewo kune chiemo ma nyalo pidho ji me jye?”
43006006	(Openjo ama nyaka ma temo Filipo, rupiri go won oido otyeko ŋeyo gima go kidho timo.)
43006007	Filipo odwoko ni, “Kada pesa ma romo misara ma dwe auchiel jye kinyal nyiewo mugat ma romo dhano jye biloye kada abila won.”
43006008	Jafuonjirok pere man, Andereya, omin Simon Petro owacho ni,
43006009	“Jayach moro ee ka mani gi mugat abich ma bel kodi rech aryo. To me bende di kony aŋo ri kweth ji me jye?”
43006010	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Wachi ri ji jowobedi piny.” (Lum oido omore kenyo.) Ameno ji jye jobedo piny. Oido chwo romo chiegin gana abich.
43006011	Gikenyo Yesu okwanyo mugat, oketho Were walwa, to poko ji monwaŋo jobedo piny. Apaka bende otimo gi rech, aka ji jye jolimo paka joyenyo.
43006012	Munyo ji jye joyeŋ, go owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Choki win ŋinjeŋinje modoŋ; wakiri wawey gimoro wonyiekere kada mathin.”
43006013	Gikenyo jochoko gimoro jye, to jopoŋo aditin apar g'aryo ma mugat ma bel ma jomochiemo joweyo odoŋ.
43006014	Munyo ji joneno giraura ma Yesu otimo, jowacho ni, “Adyeri me obedo jatuchi wach Were moido ripere bino i piny!”
43006015	Munyo Yesu oŋeyo nike oido jomito bino loko go kere gi mbaka, go oeye kenyo to kidho pondo wi got kakende.
43006016	Munyo piny oyutho, jofuonjirok pere joloro yu wakawaka to
43006017	jodonjo i yee, to jochiewere jogik yu Kapernaum. Piny oyutho kir ma fuodi Yesu kodwoko bongi jo.
43006018	I hongo no asur madwoŋ oido kudho aka miyo pi ule marach.
43006019	Jofuonjirok oido jotyeko chiewirok ma romo mairo adek kosa aŋwen to joneno Yesu munyo wotho wi pi kareno bino chiegin gi yee; to lworo mako jo.
43006020	To Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Wikiri wilwori, kole me an.”
43006021	Gikenyo to jorwako go i yee gi kisangala, to piyo piyo no jotundo kamothwo kama onwaŋo jokidh'iye.
43006022	Yawere mere muma ji monwaŋo odoŋ loka wakawaka ma kocha joniaŋ nike yee achiel kende amonwaŋo odoŋ kenyo. Aka oido bende joŋeyo nike Yesu kodonjo i ye kodi jofuonjirok pere, to jokadho kendigin.
43006023	Onyo yee mogo mowok Tiberya, jotundo thengi pi chiegin kodi kuma muma ji chieŋino jocham'iye mugat, munyo Ruoth otyeko miyo silwany.
43006024	Munyo muma ji no joneno ni Yesu ongoye kenyo kodi jofuonjirok pere, jodonjo i yee no to jokidho yu Kapernaum rango go.
43006025	Munyo ji jonwaŋo Yesu yu loka, jowacho ri go ni, “Jafuonji, ibino ka i hongo mene?”
43006026	Yesu odwoko ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, wirangan rupiri chieŋino wichamo mugat wiyeŋ wijojye, to ma kiweno ni wineno ranyuth ma giraura.
43006027	Wikiri witiy ri chiemo ma nyiekere piyo; to tiyi win ri chiemo ma yindira to kelo kwo makirum. Me a chiemo ma Wuodi Dhano bino miyo win, rupiri Were Baba won otyeko ketho kwoŋ go ranyuth ma ridho wach no.”
43006028	Gikenyo jopenjo go ni, “Watimi aŋo ŋey watim tich pa Were?”
43006029	Yesu odwoko ni, “Me a tich ma Were mito ni witim: Yeyi win ŋata go ooro.”
43006030	Jodwoko ni, “Ranyuth aŋo ma giraura ma inotimi aka nyaka wanyal neno to wayeyin? Aŋo m'ilatimo ye won?
43006031	Kwarere mawan chango jochamo mana i thim paka ndiiko wacho ni, ‘Omiyo jo mugat mawok i polo achama.’ ”
43006032	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, Musa ama komiyo win mugat mawok i polo. To Baba won ama miyo win mugat maradyeri mawok i polo.
43006033	Rupiri mugat ma Were miyo obedo ŋata loro piny wok i polo aka miyo piny kwo.”
43006034	Gikenyo jokwayo go ni, “Jadwoŋ, onyo miyi wan mugat no wok konon.”
43006035	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Abedo mugat ma kelo kwo. Ŋata bino bongan kibino winjo kech, aka ŋata yeyan kibino winjo riyo.
43006036	“Aka atyeko kir wacho ri win ni wityeko nenan, to jye fuodi wikiyeyan.
43006037	Moro jye ma Baba miyan bino bino bongan. Akoryem woko nyatoro jye m'obin bongan.
43006038	Kole abino i piny wok i polo timo gima ŋata ooran yenyo, ma kiweno gima awon ayenyo.
43006039	Me a gima ŋata ooran yenyo ni atim: nike ji jye ma go omiyan kiri joworwenyi kada achiel, to nike achierino jo i kwo i ndelo ma rumachien.
43006040	Ato me obedo mito pa Baba, nike nyatoro jye moneni Wuode to yeyo go wobedi gi kwo makirum; aka abino chierino go i ndelo ma rumachien.”
43006041	Joyudaya jochako kiŋunyaŋunya kwoŋ go rupiri owacho ni, “Abedo mugat ma wok i polo.”
43006042	Gikenyo jowacho ni, “Me won ki Yesu wuodi pa Yozefu, aka waŋeyo kir bamere gi min? To raŋo ma go pama kethere wacho ni oloro piny wok i polo?”
43006043	Yesu odwoko ni, “Weyi win kiŋunyaŋunya wiwegi kendiwin.
43006044	Ongoye ŋata nyalo bino bongan kwanyo woko ka Baba mooran oywayo go bongan; aka abino chierino go i ndelo ma rumachien.
43006045	Kole ondik i kitawo pa jotuchi wach Were ni, ‘Were bino fuonjo ji jye.’ Moro jye ma winjo Baba aka fuonjere bonge bino bongan.
43006046	Me kinyuthi ni nitye moro motyeko neno Baba, kwanyo woko ŋata owok bongi Were kende ama otyeko neno go.
43006047	“Adyeri awacho ri win, ŋata yeyo jye nitye gi kwo makirum.
43006048	Abedo mugat ma kelo kwo.
43006049	Kole kwarere mewin jochamo mana i thim, to jotho.
43006050	To ee mugat ma wok i polo ma ka nyatoro ochamo kibino tho.
43006051	Abedo mugat ma kelo kwo mobino i piny wok i polo. Ŋata ochamo mugat me bino kwo chil gi chil. Aka mugat ma abino miyo win meno a delkwoŋan, ma abino miyo aka nyaka piny wolimi kwo.”
43006052	Gime oero pyem ri Joyudaya wegi kendigin. Jopenjo ni, “Ŋatin nyalo nedi miyo wan delkwoŋe ni wacham?”
43006053	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win ni ka wikichamo delkwoŋ Wuodi Dhano to wimadho remo pere wikobedi gi kwo i win.
43006054	Ŋata chamo delkwoŋan aka madho remo paran nitye gi kwo makirum, aka abino chierino go i ndelo ma rumachien.
43006055	Kole delkwoŋan meno chiemo adyeri aka remo paran bende giramadha adyer.
43006056	Ŋata chamo delkwoŋan aka madho remo paran bedo i an aka abedo i go.
43006057	Baba makwo ooran, aka akwo kwoŋbedo go. Meno bende apaka ŋata chaman bino limo kwo wok kwoŋan.
43006058	Amomiyo me obedo mugat mobino wok i polo; kichale kodi mugat ma kwarere win jochamo to jotho. Ŋata chamo mugat me bino kwo chil gi chil.”
43006059	Yesu owacho gime munyo fuonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya ma Kapernaum.

43006062	To kosa bedi winen Wuodi Dhano munyo gik malo kama yado go nity'iye chon!
43006063	Chuny pa Were ama miyo go kwo; delkwoŋe won bu kony. Wach ma atyeko wacho obedo chuny kodi kwo.
43006064	Ama jye nyaka joman kwoŋ win jokiyey.” (Ato Yesu oido oŋeyo wok i chakirok joma jokoyeyo kwoŋ go kodi ŋata d'ochamo ri go sereko.)
43006065	Aka omedo wacho ni, “Me amomiyo awacho ri win nike ongoye ŋata nyalo bino bongan kwanyo woko ka Baba ama omiyo go onyalo timo ameno.”
43006066	Wok i hongo me, jomathoth moido joluwo go jowire to joweyo ameno luwo go.
43006067	Ameno Yesu openjo japar g'aryo ni, “To win, wibende wimito weyani?”

43006069	Aka onyo wayeyo odoko waŋeyo nike in iŋati Maleŋ mowok bongi Were.”

43006071	Go oido luwo kwoŋ Yuda, wuodi pa Simon Iskaryot. Rupiri Yuda, kada onwaŋo obedo achiel kwoŋ japar g'aryo, go ama oido kidho chamo ri Yesu sereko.
43007001	Rumachien, Yesu owotho yu Galileya; ato komito kidho Yudeya, rupiri Joyudaya oido jomito neko go.

43007004	Ongoye ŋata pano tich ma go timo ka mito nike woŋeyere maber. Paka itimo gikipiny me, onyo weyi piny gipi woŋeyi.”
43007005	(Kada wutimin go bende oido jokoyeyo go).
43007006	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Ndir paran motire fuodi kotundo. To ri win hongo jye ripo.
43007007	Ji ma piny kinyal dak win, to jodakan, rupiri amena wacho ri jo nike tim pajo recho.
43007008	Wiwegi kidhi win i kalima no, akibino kidh'iye, rupiri hongo paran motire fuodi kotundo.”
43007009	Owacho ri jo ameno to bedo i Galileya.
43007010	Munyo wutimin jotyeko kadho i kalima, Yesu bende okidho nyaliŋliŋ.
43007011	Joyudaya onwaŋo jorango go i kalima no. Jopenjo ni, “Nikune jalago?”

43007017	Ŋata yeyo timo gima Were yenyo bino ŋeyo ka gima afuonjo wok bongi Were kosa ka aluwo gi men paran won.
43007018	Kole ŋata luwo gi men pere won temo miyirok dwoŋ. To ŋata mito dwoŋ ri ŋatooro go meno otire, aka ongoye gi twodo i go.
43007019	Musa omiyo win Chik, Kameno? To kole ongoye kada ŋatachiel kwoŋ win ma mako Chik no. Raŋo ma wiyenyo nekan?”
43007020	To ji jodwoko ni, “Ini gi jwogi kwoŋin! Ŋata yenyo nekin ŋa?”
43007021	Yesu odwoko ni, “Atimo gimoro nyaka achiel won to wijojye widhyer.
43007022	Musa ooro win thumirok (kobedo Musa to kwarere pajo ama jochako), to kole withumo dhano kir i Sabato.
43007023	Onyo ka nyathi ma jayach ithumo i Sabato ma kitur Chik pa Musa, raŋo ma wimako nge kodan ni rupiri abotho dhano to bedo maber i Sabato?
43007024	Wikiri witer wach moro chungo kwoŋ nyaka gima nenere gi woko, to kutho wiripo niaŋ tyendi wach motire.”
43007025	Wok i hongo no ji mogo ma Yerusalem jowacho ni, “Me k'aŋata joradhum joyenyo neko?
43007026	Neni! Kole go ee luwo i dyer ji, aka ongoye kir ŋata luwo kwoŋe. Kosa jotel joŋeyo nike go a Kristo?
43007027	Kole waŋeyo kama jame wok'iye, mato ka Kristo obin, ongoye ŋata leŋeyo kama go wok'iye.”

43007029	to an aŋeyo go, rupiri awok bonge aka go ama ooran.”
43007030	Gikenyo jotemo mako go, to ongoye ŋata oketho chinge kwoŋe, rupiri ndir pere oido fuodi kotundo.
43007031	To kada ameno ji mathoth i dyer kitipa no joyeyo go, aka jopenjere ni, “Ka Kristo obin, otim tich madongo loyo ma jalin otyeko timo?”
43007032	Munyo Jofarisayo jowinjo ji madit jomwoŋo gikipiny me kwoŋe, jo kodi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar jooro joserikale ma Ot pa Were mako Yesu.
43007033	Yesu owacho ni, “Abino bedo gi win hongo machiek, to agik bongi ŋata ooran.
43007034	Wibino rangan to wikonwaŋan; aka kama akidh'iye wikinyal tundo.”
43007035	Joyudaya jopenjere wegi kendigin ni, “Jame chiegin kidho kune kama wakinyal nwaŋ'iye go? Kosa go lekidho yu tindin ma Yunani kama ji mawan man jonityeye?
43007036	Go wacho ni wibino rangan to wikibino nwaŋan, kendo ni, ‘Wikinyal tundo kama akidh'iye.’ Gime dwoŋ mere aŋo?”
43007037	Ndelo machowe ma kalima ama obedo ndelo moloyo dwoŋ. I ndelo no, Yesu ochungo to luwo gi dwonde ma malo ni, “Ka nitye moro jye ma riyo neko wobin bongan womadhi pi,
43007038	paka ondik ni, ‘Moro jye ma yeyan, pi mamol ma kelo kwo makirum bino mol wok i chunye.’ ” (
43007039	Yesu owacho ama kwoŋ Chuny Maleŋ ma joma joyeyo go oido jolelimo rumachien. I hongo no Chuny Maleŋ oido fuodi komiy ji, rupiri Yesu oido fuodi kotiŋ malo i dwoŋ.)
43007040	Ji megi kwoŋ jono jowinjo go munyo wacho gime aka jowacho ni, “Ŋat me obedo jatuchi wach Were adyeri!”

43007042	Kondik ni Kristo bino bedo nyakwar Daudi, aka ibino nywolo go i Bethlehem, tindi pa Daudi?”

43007049	To lwak ji me, paka jokuya Chik pa Musa onyo kole Were okwoŋo jo!”

43008020	Yesu owacho gime jye munyo fuonjo i Ot pa Were, dho tyelo kama ikan'iye lim. Aka ongoye ŋata omako go rupiri ndir pere oido fuodi kotundo.

43008022	To Joyudaya jowacho ni, “Ka go wacho ni wakinyal kidho kama go kidh'iye, dwoŋ mere nike go ledere wotho?”
43008023	Yesu odwoko ni, “Win wichakere i piny, to an awok malo. Win ji ma piny ka, to an a ki dhano ma piny ka.
43008024	Amomiyo awacho ri win nike wibino tho i gimarecho mewin. Aka wibino tho i gimarecho mewin rupiri wikiyey nike, ‘An a Go ma atucho ri win.’ ”

43008029	Aka ŋata ooran ni kodan, koweyan kendan, rupiri ndir jye atimo gima sangala go.”

43008033	Jodwoko ni, “Kole wabedo nyikway Ibrayimu, kendo fuodi wakibedo ŋechin pa nyatoro, odoko iwacho nedi ni ibino loko wan joma ni syem?”
43008034	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, moro jye ma timo gimarach meno ŋecha pa gimarach.
43008035	Ndir jye ŋecha kibedi japecho; to nyathi anywola ama ndir jye bedo japecho.

43008038	Aluwo kwoŋ gima Baba onyuthan, to win witimo gima bawin owacho ri win.”
43008039	Gikenyo jodwoko go ni, “Bawan obedo Ibrayimu.” Yesu odwoko ni, “Bedi adyeri winyithindho pa Ibrayimu, di witimo gima chango go otimo.
43008040	To an ma awacho ri win adyeri ma awinjo bongi Were, ama jye fuodi wimito nekan. Kole Ibrayimu kotimo gima chal ameno!
43008041	Adyeri witimo gima bawin otimo.” Jodwoko ni, “Wakibedo nyithindho ma dudi. Wanitye gi Bawan achiel kende, Were won gipi.”
43008042	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Bedi Were a Bawin adyeri, di wimaran, rupiri awok bongi Were aka onyo ani ka. Akibino gi wi tungan, to go ama ooran.
43008043	To raŋo ma wikiniaŋ gima awacho? Obedo rupiri wikimiti winjo fuonji paran.
43008044	Wibedo nyithindho pa bawin, jwogi, aka wimito timo gima bawin no yenyo. Wok chon go oido janek. Fuodi go kobedo yu thenge maradyer, rupiri adyeri ongoye i go. Ka go twodo meno go timo gikula pere won, rupiri go jatwodo aka go a baa jotwodo jye.
43008045	To rupiri awacho ri win giradyeri amomiyo wikiyeyan.
43008046	Ŋa kwoŋ win ma nyalo nyutho ni atimo gimarach? To k'inen awacho giradyeri raŋo ma wikiyeyan?
43008047	Ŋata wok bongi Were winjo wach pa Were. Gima omiyo wikiyey winjo wach paran, obedo rupiri wikibedo apa Were.”
43008048	Joyudaya jopenjo Yesu ni, “Kere wakinuŋo munyo wawacho nike in i Jasamarya aka jwogi ni kwoŋin?”
43008049	Yesu odwoko ni, “Angoye gi jwogi moro jye, aworo Baba, to win wikiworan.
43008050	Akirangi dwoŋ paran awon, to nitye Ŋata rango aka ama bino bedo jathumi banja.
43008051	Adyeri awacho ri win, ni ŋata winjo fuonji paran kibino tho.”
43008052	Joyudaya jowacho ri go ni, “Pama onyo nyaka waŋeyo odocho nike initye gi jwogi. Ibrayimu kodi jotuchi wach Were jotho, aka odoko iwacho ni, ŋata winjo fuonji perin kibino tho.
43008053	Onyo iwacho nike idwoŋ loyo Ibrayimu Bawan motyeko tho. Aka jotuchi wach Were bende jotho. Iparo nike in i ŋa?”
43008054	Yesu odwoko ni, “Bedi awon amiyere dwoŋ, dwoŋ paran donyo ongoye gimoro. Ŋata miyan dwoŋ manago Baba -- aka a ŋata wilwoŋo ni Were mewin.
43008055	Fuodi wikiŋeyo kir go, to an aŋeyo go aka awinjo wach pere. Bedi awachi ni akuya go, d'abedo jatwodo paka win. To aŋeyo go aka awinjo wach pere.
43008056	Bawin Ibrayimu osangala nike oido leneno ndelo paran; oneno aka osangala.”
43008057	Joyudaya jowacho ri go ni. “K'inen fuodi ikirom kada oro pyero abich, ama iwacho ni ityeko neno Ibrayimu?”
43008058	Yesu odwoko ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, ma fuodi konywol Ibrayimu oido anitye.”
43008059	Ru meno jodimo telin ma goyo gine go to go opondo to eye i Ot pa Were.
43009001	Munyo Yesu wotho, oneno ŋat moro ma chango onywol ma waŋe otho.
43009002	Jofuonjirok pere jopenjo go ni, “Jafuonji, ŋata otimo gimarach momiyo ŋat me onywol ma waŋe otho? Gimarach pere woni, kosa apa jonywol pere?”
43009003	Yesu odwoko ni, “Tho waŋ pere kimaki kwoŋ gimarach pere kosa apa jonywol pere. Go waŋe otho nike nyaka tich pa Were wonenere ka tiyo i go.
43009004	Ka fuodi piny ler waripo timo tich pa ŋata ooran, mudho bino, ma ongoye dhano monyal tich.
43009005	Ka fuodi anitye i piny aŋata abedo lero ma piny.”
43009006	Munyo otyeko wacho ameno, Yesu oŋulo law piny to dwanyo lowo mathin gi law no to mwono waŋ ŋato gi chwodho no,
43009007	aka owacho ri go ni, “Kidhi ilwoki waŋin i Jwom Silowam.” Gikenyo ŋato okidho lwoko waŋe, to dwoko ma waŋe neno.
43009008	Joger pere kodi ji moido jotyeko neno go munyo kwayere, jopenjo ni, “Me won k'aŋata yado bedo piny aka kwayere?”
43009009	Jomegi jowacho ni, “Me go won,” to joman jowacho ni, “Be, ki go, chale gine ayino.” Gikenyo ŋato won owacho ni, “An won a ŋatago.”
43009010	Jopenjo go ni, “To waŋin oyawere nedi won?”
43009011	Go odwoko ni, “Jal milwoŋo ni Yesu odwanyo chwodho moro, omwono gine waŋan, to wacho ran ni, ‘Kidhi i jwom Silowam ilwoki waŋin.’ Gikenyo akidho, to tekin atyeko lwoko waŋan to anyalo neno.”
43009012	Jopenjo go ni, “Go ni kune?” Go odwoko ni, “Akuya ran.”
43009013	Gikenyo jotero ŋata yado waŋe oido otho me bongi Jofarisayo.
43009014	Ndelo ma Yesu odwany'iye chwodho aka oyawo waŋ ŋato oido obedo Sabato.
43009015	Amomiyo Jofarisayo odoko jopenjo ŋata waŋe yado otho no paka ochako neno. Go owacho ri jo ni, “Go oketho chwodho moro i waŋan, to alwoko waŋan aka onyo aneno.”
43009016	Jofarisayo mogo jowacho ni, “Ŋata otimo gino kinyal wok bongi Were, rupiri go kikur chik ma Sabato.” To joman jowacho ni, “Ŋata jarecho d'onyalo nedi timo tich madwoŋ ameno?” To tyakirok bedo i dyer jo.
43009017	Gikenyo Jofarisayo odoko jopenjo ŋato ni, “Iwacho nike go oyawo waŋin, to iwon iwacho aŋo kwoŋ go?”
43009018	Ana go ni, “Go jatuchi wach Were.” Gikenyo Joyudaya jokomito yeyo nike go oido waŋe otho aka onyo pama neno, chuka jolwoŋo jonywol pere
43009019	to jopenjo jo ni, “Me wuodi win? Wiwacho nike go onywol ma waŋe otho? Ka ameno, raŋo ma go pama neno?”
43009020	Jonywol pere jodwoko ni, “Waŋeyo nike go wuodi wan, aka go onywolere ma waŋe otho.
43009021	To wakuya paka go ochako neno, kosa ŋata oyawo waŋe. Penji win go won; kole go otegino, aka won nyalo luwo kwoŋe.”
43009022	Jonywol pere jowacho ama kwoŋe rupiri oido jolworo Joyudaya; ato Joyudaya oido jotyeko ridho ni moro jye m'otucho ni Yesu obedo Kristo ibino ryemo go woko i kalamo pa Joyudaya.
43009023	Amomiyo jonywol pere jowacho ni, “Kole go otegino; penji win go won!”
43009024	Gikenyo jodoko jolwoŋo ŋat monywol ma waŋe otho no mararyo to jowacho ri go ni, “Miyi Were dwoŋ. Waŋeyo nike jalo jagimarach.”
43009025	Ŋato odwoko ni, “Akuya kosa go jagimarach kosa be, to gima aŋeyo kende a ni oido waŋan otho to pama onyo aneno.”
43009026	Jomedo penjo go ni, “Go otimo rin aŋo won? Oyawo waŋin nedi?”
43009027	Go odwoko ni, “Atyeko wacho ri win, to wikwero winjo. Aŋo man ma wimito winjo kendo? Kono miti wibende wimito bedo jofuonjirok pere!”
43009028	Gikenyo jokwoŋo go to jowacho ni, “Ibedo jafuonjirok pa jalo; wan wabedo ri wan jofuonjirok pa Musa.
43009029	Waŋeyo ni Were oluwo gi Musa; to jalo, wakuya kiri kama go wok'iye!”
43009030	Ŋato odwoko ni, “Iraŋo? Meno obedo gidhyer swa! Wikuya kama go wok'iye, mato go oyawo kir waŋan!
43009031	Waŋeyo nike Were kiwinji jomarecho; go winjo joma jomiyo go dwoŋ aka jotimo gima go mito.
43009032	Wok i chakirok pa piny fuodi kowinji ni nyatoro oyawo waŋ dhano monywol ma waŋe otho.
43009033	Kole bedi ŋat me kowok bongi Were, di konyalo timo gimoro.”
43009034	Jodwoko go ni, “In m'idongo gi recho wok i nywolirok perin bende onyo ifuonjo wan aŋo?” To joryemo go woko i kalamo pa Joyudaya.
43009035	Yesu owinjo ni joryemo go woko, to munyo onwaŋo go, openjo go ni, “Iyeyo Wuodi Dhano?”
43009036	Ŋato odwoko ni, “A ŋa no jadwoŋ, ŋey ayey go?”
43009037	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Ityeko neno go, aka go won ama luwo kodin pama me.”
43009038	Ŋato owacho ni, “Ruoth, ayeyo,” to lamo Yesu.
43009039	Yesu owacho ni, “Abino i piny ka thumo banja, ŋey joma waŋ gin otho jowoneen, aka jomaneno jowolokere joma waŋ gin otho.”
43009040	Jofarisayo megi, monwaŋo jonitye bonge kenyo, jowinjo go wacho ameno to jopenjo go ni, “Onyo nyutho ni wabende waŋ wan otho?”
43009041	Yesu odwoko ni, “Bedi waŋ win otho d'onyo wingoye gi recho; to paka wiwacho ni winyalo neno, dwoŋ mere kere fuodi winitye i recho.”
43010001	“Adyeri awacho ri win, ŋata kidonji i dyer sidwol roombo gi dhoot, to idho gi yu thenge man, meno go jakwo kendo jamahembi.
43010002	Ŋata donjo gi dhoot meno a jakwath roombo.
43010003	Jakuri dhoot yawo ri go, roombo jowinjo dwonde aka go lwoŋo roombo pere gi nyingi gin aka wodho jo woko.
43010004	Ka otyeko wodho jo woko, telo jo, to joluwo go, rupiri joŋeyo dwonde.
43010005	Jokibino luwo ŋat man, jobino ŋwech jowoeye bongi ŋato ayino, rupiri jokuya dwonde.”
43010006	Yesu owacho ri jo agecha me, to jokoniaŋ gima go owacho no.
43010007	Yesu odoko owacho ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, Aŋata abedo dhoot pa roombo.
43010008	Joman jye ma jotelo yu wiyan jobedo jokwo kendo jomahembi; to roombo kowinjo jo.
43010009	Aŋata abedo dhoot. Moro jye madonjo gi bongan bino both; go bino donjo to wok, to nwaŋo lum moloth.
43010010	Jakwo bino nyaka kwalo, neko kodi nyieko woko. An abino nike jowolimi kwo, aka kwo ma gi bee.
43010011	“Aŋata abedo jakwath maber. Jakwath maber yeyo tho ri roombo pere.
43010012	Jatich achula kibedi won roombo, ka oneno arara bino, weyo jo to ringo, to arara kwanyo roombo to kedho jo woko.
43010013	Go ringo rupiri go jatich achula, aka kidew kwoŋ roombo.
43010014	An a jakwath maber. Aŋeyo roombo paran,
43010015	aka bende joŋeyan paka Baba oŋeyan, aka abende aŋeyo go, aka ayeyo tho ri roombo.
43010016	Ani gi roombo man ma jongoye i sidwol me. Aripo kelo jo bende; jobino winjo dwondan, aka jobino lokere sidwol achiel kodi jakwath achiel.
43010017	“Baba omaran rupiri ayeyo bolo woko kwo paran, rumachien to adoko anwaŋo kendo.
43010018	Ongoye ŋata kwanyo kwoŋan kwo me. Awon arwenyo woko gi mito paran. Anitye gi men ma rwenyo go woko, kendo anitye gi men ma dwoko go. Me gima Baba ooran timo.”
43010019	Tyakirok odoko obedo i dyer Joyudaya ru wach me.
43010020	Jomathoth kwoŋ jo jowacho ni, “Go nitye gi jwogi! Neko omako! Wiwinjo luwo pere raŋo?”
43010021	To joman jowacho ni, “Ŋata ni gi jwogi kinyal luwo ama! Jwogi bende di nyal botho joma waŋ gin otho?”
43010022	I hongo no ndir otundo ma kalima ma lonyirok i waŋ Were, mobedo i Ot pa Were i Yerusalem; i ndir no pe oido oŋicho piny.
43010023	Yesu oido wotho i kalikondi pa Solomon i Ot pa Were, to
43010024	Joyudaya jochokere jothoko go kenyo to jowacho ri go ni, “Ileweyo wan i kiganagana kir keraŋo? Wachi ri wan kamaler ka in a Kristo.”
43010025	Yesu odwoko ni, “Atyeko wacho ri win, to wikimiti yeyo. Tich ma atimo i nyingi Baba ama luwo ran;
43010026	to wikibino yeyo rupiri wingoye i roombo paran.
43010027	Roombo paran winjo dwondan; aŋeyo jo, aka joluwan.
43010028	Amiyo jo kwo makirum, aka jokibino tho; ongoye moro ma bino mayan jo.
43010029	Baba momiyan jo dwoŋ loyo ji jye, aka ongoye nyatoro ma nyalo kwanyo jo woko i chingi Baba.
43010030	Aka wan kodi Baba wabedo achiel.”
43010031	Gikenyo Joyudaya odoko jokwanyo telin ma goyo gine go.
43010032	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Atyeko timo tich mabeyo madit mowok bongi Baba; onyo mene kwoŋ jo ma wimito goyan'iye gi telin?”
43010033	Joyudaya jodwoko ni, “Wakimiti goyin ru tich mabeyo mitimo, to ru luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Were, rupiri in idhano aka ikethere lwoŋirok ni ibedo Were!”
43010034	Yesu odwoko ni, “Kere kondik i Chik mewin wegi nike Were owacho ni, ‘Wibedo werin?’
43010035	Ka Were olwoŋo jomokel rijo wach pere ni werin (aka gima ondik kiturere),
43010036	onyo winowachi ri ŋata Were ooro i piny ni go luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Were ni rupiri awacho ni abedo Wuodi Were?
43010037	Ere onyo wikiri wiyey k'inen akitim tich pa Baba.
43010038	To k'inen atimo gikipiny ago, kada nende wikiyeyan, yeyi win kada nyaka tich no aka winoŋey kichutho ni Baba nitye i an aka anitye i go.”
43010039	Gikenyo odoko jotemo mako Yesu to budho jo.
43010040	Yesu odoko ogik ochiewere i Yordan to por loka yu kama yado Yohana batis'iye ji to bedo kenyo.
43010041	Ji madit jobino bonge aka jowacho ni, “Yohana kotimo giraura moro, to gima go owacho kwoŋ jame jye obedo adyeri.”
43010042	Aka ji kweth joyeyo go kenyo.
43011001	Dhano milwoŋo ni Lazaro, ma Bethaniya oido two. Me obedo tindi ma Marya kodi Maritha, nyamin go, oido jobed'iye.
43011002	(Marya me ama ndir moro oolo mo maŋwe kur i tyendi Ruoth to yweyo gi yewiye; aka ama Lazaro, omin go, oido two.)
43011003	Nyimere no jodhiro wach ri Yesu ni, “Ruoth, mere perin m'imaro two.”
43011004	Munyo Yesu owinjo, owacho ni, “Two pa Lazaro kilechowere gi tho; gime otimere ma nyutho dwoŋ pa Were, aka nyaka Wuodi Were wolim'iye dwoŋ.”
43011005	Yesu oido omaro Maritha gi nyamin, kodi Lazaro.
43011006	To kada munyo go owinjo wach ni Lazaro two, omedo bedo kama oido ni iye ndelo aryo man.
43011007	Gikenyo nyaka go owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Weyi wagiki win Yudeya kendo.”
43011008	Jofuonjirok jodwoko ni, “Jafuonji kole nyaka okadho hongo machiek won chuka Joyudaya jomiti goyin gi telin, ama odoko onyo iyiko gik yu korago?”
43011009	Yesu owacho ni, “Ndelo nitye gi sawa apar g'aryo, kameno? Ka dhano wotho odyechieŋ, kichier, rupiri go neno lero.
43011010	To ka go owotho wor, chier, rupiri lero ongoye.”
43011011	Yesu omedo wacho ni, “Mere mawan Lazaro nindo, to abino kidho chiewo go.”
43011012	Jofuonjirok jowacho ni, “Ruoth, ka go nindo bino bedo maber.”
43011013	To wach pa Yesu dwoŋ mere oido ni Lazaro otyeko tho, to joparo nike go wacho nindo ma ndir jye.
43011014	Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri jo kamaler ni, “Lazaro otyeko tho;
43011015	to ri bero mewin asangala nike onwaŋo angoye yu koro aka ŋey wiyey. Ere weyi wakidhi win bothe.”
43011016	Thoma (milwoŋo ni Rut) owacho ri jofuonjirok wadi ni, “Weyi wajojye wakidhi watho kanyachiel gine!”
43011017	Munyo Yesu otundo, onwaŋo ni Lazaro oido otyeko bedo ndelo aŋwen i bur.
43011018	Bethaniya onwaŋo kitundi mairo aryo wok Yerusalem
43011019	aka Joyudaya mathoth onwaŋo jobino limo Maritha kodi Marya gi kweyo chuny jo i teko pajo ma tho pa omin jo.
43011020	Munyo Maritha owinjo ni Yesu bino, owok woko romo gine; to Marya odoŋ pecho.
43011021	Maritha owacho ri Yesu ni, “Ruoth bedi chieŋino ibedi ka, di omin an kotho.”
43011022	To aŋeyo ni kada pama Were bino miyin gimoro jye mikwayo go.
43011023	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Omin in lechierino.”
43011024	Go odwoko ni, “Aŋeyo ni go bino chierino i ndelo ma rumachien.”
43011025	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Anaŋata chierino kodi kwo; ŋata yeyan bino kwo, kada go otho;
43011026	aka ŋata kwo aka yeyan kibino tho. Iyeyo gime?”
43011027	Go odwoko ni, “Ey, Ruoth! Ayeyo nike in i Kristo, Wuodi Were, moido genere ni lebino i piny ka.”
43011028	Munyo Maritha otyeko wacho gime, ogik pecho lwoŋo Marya nyamin go nyaliŋliŋ. Owacho ri go ni, “Jafuonji obino aka lwoŋin.”
43011029	Munyo Marya owinjo gime, oay malo to redo kidho romo gine. (
43011030	Yesu oido fuodi kotundo loka no, to oido nitye kama Maritha orom'iye gine.)
43011031	Joyudaya monwaŋo jonitye i ot gi Marya moido jokweyo chuny go i teko pere munyo joneno go oay malo to rure woko, joluwo go. Joparo nike oido go kidho dho kalyel ywak.
43011032	Munyo Marya otundo kama Yesu ni iye to neno go, opodho piny dho tyende, to wacho ni, “Ruoth, bedi chieŋino ini ka di omin an kotho!”
43011033	Munyo Yesu oneno go ywak, aka Joyudaya ma jobino gine bende joywak, geregere omako go, aka owinjo malith swa i chunye.
43011034	Openjo jo ni, “Wiyiko go kune?” Jodwoko ni, “Ruoth biye neni.”
43011035	Yesu oywak.
43011036	Gikenyo Joyudaya jowacho ni, “Neni paka onwaŋo omaro go!”
43011037	To jomegi kwoŋ jo jowacho ni, “Ŋata obotho kir waŋ dhano moido otho iraŋo ma di go kogeŋo tho pa jame?”
43011038	Geregere odoko omako Yesu to kidho dho kalyel, monwaŋo obedo ŋungu mochul dhoke gi tele.
43011039	Yesu omiyo jo or ni, “Kwanyi win woko tele!” Maritha nyamin jatho, odwoko ni, “Ruoth, kole pama onyo go ŋwe marach; chuka yiki go onyo me ndelo maraŋwen!”
43011040	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Akiwacho rin nike ibino neno dwoŋ pa Were ka iyeyo?”
43011041	Gikenyo oŋilo woko tele. Yesu oŋiyo malo to wacho ni, “Baba, afuoyin ni i winjan.
43011042	Aŋeyo ni ndir jye iwinjan, to awacho ama ma bero pa ji mani ka, ŋey jowoyeyi ni iŋat'ioran.”
43011043	Munyo otyeko wacho gime, okoko gi dwonde ma malo ni, “Lazaro, woki!”
43011044	Ŋatotho no owok motwey chinge gi tyende gi nengin, kareno nanga man oboy gine waŋe. Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Gonyi win go, aka wiwey wowothi.”
43011045	Joyudaya mathoth ma oido jobino limo Marya joneno gima Yesu otimo, to joyeyo go.
43011046	To joman kwoŋ jo jogik bongi Jofarisayo to jowacho ri jo gima Yesu otimo.
43011047	Ameno Jofarisayo kodi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar joromo kodi jopido to jowacho ni, “Watim win aŋo? Neni paka jame onyo timo giraura madit!
43011048	Ka wayeyo go omedere gi tich me, ji jye jobino yeyo go, aka Ruodhe ma Roma jobino ay to joŋinyo woko Ot pa Were gi ryemo wako nono mawan gipi!”
43011049	Ŋatachiel kwoŋ jo ma nyinge Kaifas, moido a jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar i oro no owacho ni, “Wikuya gimoro kada achiel!
43011050	Wikiniaŋ ni ber ri win ka ŋatachiel otho ri ji jye, loyo nono gipi reyirok woko?”
43011051	Iyadyeri, go kowacho gime i paro pere won; kwanyo woko paka go oido jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar i oro no, go otucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were nike Yesu chiegin tho ri Joyudaya jye.
43011052	Aka ki ri Joyudaya kende, to ma choko kanyachiel nyithindho pa Were ma jokele iye jye.
43011053	Amomiyo wok i ndelo no kadho malo jotimo chan ma neko Yesu.
43011054	Ri ameno Yesu kowotho kamaler kendo i Yudeya, to oeye to kidho kamoro machiegin gi thim, i tindi milwoŋo ni Efuraim. Kenyo ama go obed'iye gi jofuonjirok pere.
43011055	Kalima pa Joyudaya ma Kadho, oido ni chiegin, aka ji mathoth jowok thenge gi thenge jokidho Yerusalem, timo kula ma lonyo delkwoŋ gin ma fuodi kalima no kotundo.
43011056	Jo oido jorango Yesu, aka munyo jochokere i Ot pa Were, wegi jopenjere ni, “Wiparo nedi? Kosa go kobin i kalima?”
43011057	Jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi Jofarisayo oido jotyeko wodho or ni ka moro nitye moneno kama Yesu ni iye ripo dhiro wach, ŋey jowomaki go.
43012001	Munyo fuodi odoŋ ndelo auchiel aka ndelo ma kalima ma Kadho wotundi, Yesu okidho Bethaniya, kama Lazaro, ma Yesu ochierino kwoŋ jomotho bed'iye.
43012002	Joyiko rigo kenyo chiemo mothyeno aka Maritha oido a japoki chiemo kareno Lazaro obedo gi Yesu dhower.
43012003	Gikenyo Marya okwanyo chupa mo maŋwe kur swa ma romo adech kilo gipi, ma nyingi yath moro aka mawelo, to olo i tyendi Yesu, to yweyo gi yewiye. Kur pa mo no mamit otweyo ot gipi.
43012004	Achiel kwoŋ jofuonjirok pa Yesu, Yuda Iskaryot, ŋata oido lechamo ri go sereko, okwero ni,
43012005	“Iraŋo kotana mo maŋwe kur me siringi miya adek to ipoko jochandi pesa no?”
43012006	Go owacho ama ki ru kwoŋbedo go paro kwoŋ jochandi, to rupiri go oido jakwo. Go oido a jamigowa pesa aka onwaŋo dichieŋ konyere gi pesa me.
43012007	To Yesu wacho ni, “Weyi dheno! Oyik ni go wokani mo me chuka ndelo ma yikirok paran.
43012008	Ndir jye wibino bedo gi jochandi, to an akibino bedo gi win ndir jye.”
43012009	Muma ji madwoŋ jowinjo ni Yesu oido nitye Bethaniya to jokidho kenyo; ki ru wach pa Yesu kende, to ru mito neno Lazaro bende, ma Yesu ochierino kwoŋ jomotho.
43012010	Ameno jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar jochano neko Lazaro bende;
43012011	rupiri ru gimotimere kwoŋe, Joyudaya mathoth joweyo jotel pajo to joyeyo Yesu.
43012012	Yawere mere muma ji madwoŋ monwaŋo obino i kalima ma Kadho, jowinjo ni Yesu oido bino Yerusalem.
43012013	Ri ameno jokwanyo jangi thith to jokidho romo gine munyo jokoko ni, “Ozana! Silwany pa Were wobedi ri ŋato ma bino i nyingi Ruoth! Silwany pa Were wobedi ri Kere ma Israel!”
43012014	Yesu onwaŋo nyathi punda to bedo wiye, paka Ndiiko Maleŋ wacho ni,
43012015	“Tindi ma Zayun, ikiri ibedi gi lworo, kole Kere perin bino bongin, mobedo wi nyathi punda.”
43012016	Jofuonjirok pere jokoniaŋ kwoŋ gime i hongo no, to munyo Yesu otyek tiŋo malo i dwoŋ nyaka jopoyo nike ndiko owacho gime, aka ni d'otim kwoŋe gime.
43012017	Muma ji ma ndelago jobedo bongi Yesu i hongo ma go olwoŋ'iye Lazaro wok i kalyel aka ochierino go kwoŋ jomotho, jomedo nyayo wach no.
43012018	Ji kweth jokidho romo gine rupiri jowinjo nike go otimo giraura no.
43012019	Gikenyo Jofarisayo wegi jowacho kendigin ni, “Wineno, wakinyal gimoro be! Neni win paka piny gipi onyo luwo go”
43012020	Joyunani mogo bende oido jobedo megi kwoŋ joma jokidho Yerusalem lamo Were i ndir ma kalima no.
43012021	Jobino bongi Filipo, moido wok Bethsaida i Galileya, to jokwayo ni, “Jadwoŋ, wamito neno Yesu.”
43012022	Filipo okidho to wacho ri Andereya, aka jaryo no jokidho to jowacho ri Yesu.
43012023	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Pama onyo hongo otundo ma miyo Wuodi Dhano dwoŋ.
43012024	Adyeri awacho ri win, ka nyingi kal moro k'opidhi i lowo to tho, go doŋ adoŋa achiel mangil. To k'otho, nyaka nywolo nyingi kal momore.
43012025	Ŋata won omaro kwo pere, bino rwenyo woko kwo; to ŋata kwero kwo pere i piny ka ama bino kuro ri kwo makirum.
43012026	Nyatoro jye ma tiyo ran ripo luwan, aka jatich paran bino bedo kama an'iye. Aka Baba bino miyo nyatoro jye ma tiyo ran dwoŋ.
43012027	“Pama chunyan raman; to anowachi nedi? Ni, ‘Baba, bothan kwoŋ hongo me?’ To be, me a gima omiyan atundo i hongo ma chandirok me.
43012028	Baba, miyi nyingin dwoŋ.” Gikenyo dwondi jo moro oluwo wok i polo ni, “Atyeko miyo nyingan dwoŋ, kendo abino medo timo ameno.”
43012029	Muma ji moido ochungo kenyo owinjo dwondi jo no to jowacho ni manago lithkoth, aka joman jowacho ni, “Chalo malaika oluwo gine!”
43012030	To Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Kobedo ri an amomiyo dwondi jo me oluwo, to ri win.
43012031	Ndir otundo ma thumo banja ri piny me; kendo jadhum ma piny me onyo ibino ryemo woko.
43012032	K'otyek tiŋan malo wok piny abino ywayo ji jye bongan.” (
43012033	Ameno, go onyutho kiti tho ma go oido kidho chandirok.)
43012034	Muma ji odwoko ni, “Kole Chik mawan wacho ni Kristo bino kwo chil gi chil. To idoko iwacho ni Wuodi Dhano iripo tiŋo malo nedi? Wuodi Dhano no a ŋa?”
43012035	Yesu odwoko ni, “Lero no fuodi nitye gi win hongo moro ye. Wothi win ka fuodi lero no nitye gi win, ka mudho fuodi koumo win; kole ŋata wotho i mudho kiŋey kuma go chom'iye.
43012036	Yeyi win lero no ka fuodi wini gine, ŋey wibedi nyithidho ma lero.” Rumachien munyo Yesu otyeko wacho gime okidho pondo ri jo.
43012037	Kada Yesu oido otyeko timo ranyuth madongo me i waŋ jo, jye fuodi jokoyeyo go.
43012038	Gime otimere ama ŋey gima jatuchi wach Were, Isaya, owacho wotundi i kare ni, “Ruoth, ŋa moyeyo mikwenda ma wakelo? Were onyutho ŋa men pere?”
43012039	Ri ameno jokonyalo yeyo paka Isaya odoko owacho kaman ni,
43012040	“Were ochulo waŋ jo to umo paro pajo, nike waŋ jo wokiri woneen, paro pajo wokiri woniaŋi gimoro, ŋey jowokiri jowonyali gik bongan, ni aboth jo.”
43012041	Isaya owacho ama rupiri oneno dwoŋ pa Ŋato, aka oluwo kwoŋe.
43012042	Kada ameno, jotel pa Joyudaya mathoth bende joyeyo Yesu; to paka onwaŋo jolworo Jofarisayo, jokowacho gino nyatirtir ni aka ŋey wokiri woryem jo woko i kalamo pa Joyudaya.
43012043	Ato oido jomaro fuoy pa ji loyo fuoy pa Were.
43012044	Gikenyo Yesu oluwo gi dwonde mamalo ni, “Nyatoro jye ma yeyan kiyeyan kende to yeyo ŋata ooran bende.
43012045	Ŋata nenan meno neno ŋata ooran bende.
43012046	Abino i piny ka paka lero ŋey nyatoro jye ma yeyan, wokiri wodoŋi i mudho.
43012047	To ka moro winjo mikwenda paran aka kimaki, akithum ri go banja, Ato akibino thumo banja ri piny, to botho piny ayino.
43012048	Nitye ŋata bino thumo banja ri nyatoro jye ma kweran aka kijol fuonji paran; wach m'atyeko luwo ama bino bedo jathumi ri go banja i ndelo ma rumachien,
43012049	rupiri akiluwo gi men paran won, to Baba am'ooran gima aripo wacho kodi luwo.
43012050	Aka aŋeyo nike or pere kelo kwo makirum. Amomiyo gima awacho jye, awacho paka Baba ooran wacho.”
43013001	Ma fuodi ndelo ma kalima ma Kadho, kotundo, Yesu oniaŋ nike hongo pere otundo ma eye i piny wokidhi bongi Bamere. Paka ndir jye go oido omaro jopere i piny ka, omaro jo kir i gike.
43013002	Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere oido jonitye dhower othyeno. Aka jwogi oido otyeko ketho paro machamo ri Yesu sereko i chuny Yuda wuodi pa Simon Iskaryot.
43013003	Yesu oŋeyo ni Bamere otyeko ketho gimoro jye i chinge; go oŋeyo nike owok bongi Were aka onyo go kidho gik bongi Were.
43013004	Ri ameno Yesu oay dhower, olunyo nanga pere ma woko, to tweyo taulo i pyere.
43013005	Gikenyo okonjo pi mogo i besen, to chako lwoko tyendi jofuonjirok pere, to yweyo gi taulo mapyere.
43013006	Munyo otundo bongi Simon Petro, Simon openjo go ni, “Ruoth, onyo ikidho lwoko tyendan?”
43013007	To Yesu odwoko ni, “Pama fuodi ikuya gima atimo, to ibino ŋeyo rumachien.”
43013008	Ana Petro, “Ikibino lwoko tyendan kada mathin.” Yesu odwoko ni, “Ka akilwoko tyendin meno kere ikinitye kanyachiel kodan.”
43013009	Simon Petro odwoko ni, “Ruoth onyo ikiri ilwoki nyaka tyendan kende, to lwoki ran kir chingan gi wiyan bende!”
43013010	Yesu owacho ni, “Moro jye motyeko lwok meno otyeko lony kwoŋe gipi aka kiyeny lwok kendo, mitere wolwoki tyende won kende. Wijojye wilony, kwanyo woko ŋatachiel.”
43013011	(Yesu onwaŋo otyeko ŋeyo ŋata kidho chamo ri go sereko, amomiyo owacho ni, “Wijojye wilony, kwanyo woko ŋatachiel.”)
43013012	Munyo go otyeko lwoko tyendi jo, oruko nanga pere mawoko to gik i kabedo pere dhower. Go openjo ni, “Wiŋeyo dwoŋ gima awok timo ri win?
43013013	Wilwoŋan ni Jafuonji kodi Ruoth, aka witire, rupiri meno an adyeri.
43013014	Onyo paka an mabedo Ruoth mewin odoko Jafuonji mewin, awok lwoko tyendi win, wibende wiripo lwoko tyendi jowoti win.
43013015	Amiyo win ranen, ŋey wibende witim gima awok timo ri win.
43013016	Adyeri awacho ri win, ongoye ŋecha maloyo ruoth pere gi dwoŋ, kendo ongoye jamikwenda madwoŋ loyo ŋata ooro go.
43013017	Paka pama onyo wiŋeyo gikipiny me, ka witimo ameno wibino limo silwany!
43013018	“Akiluw kwoŋ wijojye; aŋeyo joma ayero. To Ndiiko Maleŋ ripo timere mawacho ni, ‘Ŋata ochiemo kodan owire ran marach.’
43013019	Awacho ri win gime pama ma fuodi kotimere, aka ka otimere wibino yeyo ni, ‘An a go’.
43013020	Adyeri awacho ri win, moro jye ma jolo nyatoro ma aoro, meno bende jolan aka ŋata jolan, meno bende jolo ŋata ooran.”
43013021	Munyo Yesu otyeko wacho gime, ochako winjo rem i chunye to luwo kamaler ni, “Adyeri awacho ri win, ŋatachiel kwoŋ win kidho chamo ran sereko.”
43013022	Jofuonjirok joŋiyere waŋ, munyo jodhyer swa kwoŋ ŋata go oido wacho.
43013023	Achiel kwoŋ jofuonjirok ma Yesu omaro, onwaŋo bende obedo kabuti Yesu.
43013024	Simon Petro ogwelo ŋato aka owacho ni, “Penji go ŋata go luwo kwoŋe.”
43013025	Gikenyo jafuonjirok no ochore chiegin to thenere kwoŋ Yesu to penjo ni, “Manago ŋa, Ruoth?”
43013026	Yesu odwoko ni, “Ŋata abino pilo mugat i achiero t'amiyo go meno a ŋatago.” Gikenyo go okwanyo mugat, opilo, to miyo Yuda, wuodi pa Simon Iskaryot.
43013027	Tekin Yuda jolo mugat no, Sitan odonjo kwoŋe. Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Kwaki timo gima iyiko timo!”
43013028	Ongoye dhano kwoŋ joma oido jonitye dhower no moniaŋ gimomiyo Yesu owacho ri go ameno.
43013029	Paka Yuda ama oido jamigowa, jofuonjirok megi joparo ni Yesu owacho ri go ni wokidhi wonyiewi gima jomito ma kalima, kosa ni womiyi jochandi gimoro.
43013030	Tekin Yuda jolo mugat no, owok woko mayot; aka piny oido otyeko yutho.
43013031	Munyo Yuda otyeko kadho, Yesu owacho ni, “Pama Wuodi Dhano onyo otyeko limo dwoŋ, aka Were bende onyo otyeko limo dwoŋ i go.
43013032	K'inen Were onyo otyeko limo dwoŋ i go, meno Were won gipi ama bino miyo Wuode dwoŋ, aka bino timo ameno mayot.
43013033	Nyithindho paran, fuodi abino bedoye gi win hongo machiek. Wibino rangan, aka bende awacho ri win gima atyeko wacho ri Joyudaya ni, ‘Wikinyal tundo kama akidh'iye.’
43013034	Amiyo win or manyien ni, marere win. Paka atyeko maro win apaka bende wiripo marere.
43013035	Ka kis dhano omaro nyawote, meno aka ji jye jobino ŋeyo nike wijofuonjirok paran.”
43013036	Simon Petro openjo ni, “Ruoth, ikidho kune?” Ana Yesu, “Wikinyal luwan kama akidh'iye gi pama; to rumachien aka wibino luwan.”
43013037	Petro openjo ni, “Ruoth, raŋo ma akinyal luwin pama? An ayikere kir tho rin!”
43013038	Yesu odwoko ni, “Iyikere adyeri tho ran? Adyeri awacho rin, ka fuodi wuodi gweno kokoko, ibino kwedirok kwoŋan didek.”
43014001	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Wikiri wirembi kosa wiguti. Yeyi win Were, aka yeyan win bende.
43014002	Kisikin omore i ot pa Baba, aka akidho yiko ri win kabedo. D'akiwacho ri win ama bedi kobedo adyeri.
43014003	Aka ka atyeko kidho yiko ri win kabedo, abino dwoko t'aomo win, ŋey wibedi kodan kama ani iye.
43014004	Wiŋeyo kama akidh'iye kodi royo mere.”
43014005	Thoma owacho ri go ni, “Ruoth, wakuya kama ikidh'iye: wanyalo ŋeyo nedi royo ma tundo korago?”
43014006	Yesu odwoko ni, “An aŋata royo, aŋata adyeri, kodi kwo; ongoye ŋata bino bongi Baba, ka koluwo bongan.”
43014007	Owacho ri jo ni, “Ka wiŋeyan, meno bende wiŋeyo Baba; aka wok konon onyo wiŋeyo go, aka wityeko neno go.”
43014008	Filipo owacho ri go ni, “Ruoth, nyuthi wan Were Bawan, meno won kende leromo wan.”
43014009	Yesu odwoko ni, “Atyeko bedo gi win hongo malach ama jye, to fuodi ikuya an, Filipo? Moro jye motyeko nenan meno otyeko neno Baba. To raŋo ma wiwacho ni, ‘Nyuthi wan Were Bawan?’
43014010	Wikiyey, ni anitye i Baba aka Baba ni i An? Wach ma atyeko wacho ri win, kiwoki bongan an won. Baba ma bedo i an, ama timo tich pere.
43014011	Yeyi win nike anitye i Baba, aka Baba nitye i an. Ka kameno yeyi win kada ru tich pere won.
43014012	Adyeri awacho ri win, moro jye ma yeyan bino timo tich ma an atimo, ey, bino timo kir ma loyo me, rupiri akidho bongi Baba.
43014013	Aka abino timo gimoro jye ma winokway i nyingan; ameno aka ŋey dwoŋ pa Baba wonyuthere i Wuode.
43014014	Ka wikwayo gimoro jye i nyingan abino timo.
43014015	“Ka wimaran, wibino mako or paran.
43014016	Aka abino kwayo Baba to miyo win Jakony man ma wobedi gi win ndir jye,
43014017	meno Chuny maradyeri ma piny kinyal jolo, rupiri kinyal neno go kosa ŋeyo go. To wiŋeyo go, rupiri go nitye gi win aka bino bedo i win.
43014018	“Akibino weyo win paka nyithindho kiich; abino dwoko bongi win.
43014019	I hongo machiek piny kibino nenan kendo, to wibino nenan; aka paka akwo, wibende wibino kwo.
43014020	Ka ndelo no otundo, wibino ŋeyo nike anitye i Baba, aka winitye i an, paka anitye i win.
43014021	“Moro jye ma jolo or paran aka mako, meno a ŋata omaran. Baba bino maro ŋata omaran; aka abende abino maro go to anyuthere ri go.”
43014022	Yuda (ki Yuda Iskaryot) owacho ni, “Ruoth, onyal bedo nedi nike ibino nyuthere ri wan to ki ri piny?”
43014023	Yesu odwoko ni, “Nyatoro jye momaran bino winjo mikwenda paran. Baba bino maro go aka wabino bino bino bonge to wabedo bonge.
43014024	Nyatoro jye ma komaran kiwinji wach paran. Aka mikwenda ma wityeko winjo k'aparan, to wok bongi Baba m'ooran.
43014025	“Atyeko wacho ri win gime jye ma fuodi anitye gi win.
43014026	To Jamiy ryeko, Chuny Maleŋ ma Baba bino dhiro i nyingan, bino fuonjo win gimoro jye aka bino poyo win gimoro jye matyeko wacho ri win.
43014027	“Syem ama onyo aweyo ri win; amiyo win syem paran; aka akimiy win paka piny miyo. Wikiri wirembi i chuny win; odoko wikiri wibedi gi lworo.
43014028	Kole wiwinjo munyo awacho ri win ni, ‘Abino weyo win, to abino dwoko bongi win.’ Bedi wimaran, di wisangala ni akidho bongi Baba, rupiri go loyan gi dwoŋ.
43014029	Ato eno atyeko wacho ri win pama, ma fuodi kotimere, aka ka otimere wibino yeyo.
43014030	Onyo akibino medo luwo kodi win mathoth, rupiri jadhum ma piny me bino. Go ongoye gi men kwoŋan,
43014031	to piny jye ripo ŋeyo nike amaro Baba; amomiyo atimo gimoro jye ma go ooran. Ere ayi win waeye ka.”
43015001	“Aŋata abedo yath vini maradyeri, aka Baba a won ndelo mere.
43015002	Go turo woko jangi yath moro jye i an ma kinyak, aka sewila to yiko jangi yath jye ma nyak ŋey womedi nyak madit.
43015003	Pama onyo wityeko lony gi wach ma atyeko luwo ri win.
43015004	Doŋi win i an, aka abende abino doŋ i win; rupiri jangi yath kinyal nyak ka komakere gi yath mere. Wibende wikinyal nyak ka wikidoŋ i an.
43015005	“Aŋata abedo yath vini maradyeri, aka win wibedo jangi yath no. Ŋata doŋ i an, aka abende adoŋ i go, bino nyak madit; ato wikinyal timo gimoro jye ma bu an.
43015006	Nyatoro jye ma kidoŋi i an chalo jangi yath mibolo woko to thwo woko; jangi yen ma chalo ameno, ichoko kanyachiel to ibolo jo i mach, to jowaŋ woko.
43015007	Ka widoŋ i an, to wach paran doŋ i win, winyalo kwayo gimoro jye ma wiyenyo to ibino miyo win.
43015008	Me apaka Baba bino limo dwoŋ: Ka wiwodho gimanyak madit ma nyutho ni wibedo jofuonjirok paran.
43015009	Amaro win paka Baba omaran; bedi win i mar paran.
43015010	Ka wimako or paran, wibino doŋ i mar paran, paka abende amako or pa Baba aka anitye i mar pere.”
43015011	“Atyeko wacho ri win gime ŋey kisangala paran wobedi i win, aka kisangala mewin wobedi mopoŋ.
43015012	Me a gima aooro win timo: marere win, paka amaro win.
43015013	Ongoye mar ma dhano nyalo bedo gine loyo meno ma go nyalo miyo kwo pere ri merin pere.
43015014	Wibedo merin paran, ka witimo gima aoro win.
43015015	Akilwoŋ win ni jotich kendo rupiri jatich kiŋey gima ruoth pere timo. Kuchiel alwoŋo win ni merin, rupiri atyeko wacho ri win gimoro jye ma awinjo bongi Baba.
43015016	Wiŋati wikiyeran, to aŋata ayero win aka adimo win ni wikidhi winyak gima yindira. Meno aka nyaka Baba bino miyo win gimoro jye ma winokway go i nyingan.
43015017	Amomiyo, me a gima aoro win timo: marere win”.
43015018	“Ka piny dak win, poyi win nike otelo dakan.
43015019	Bedi wibedi ji pa piny, di piny omaro win paka ji pere. To ayero win wok i piny me, aka wikibedo apere; amomiyo piny dak win.
43015020	Poyi win gima atyeko wacho ri win, ‘Ŋecha ongoye ma loyo ruoth pere gi dwoŋ.’ Ka jolwenyo kodan, jobino lwenyo gi win bende.
43015021	To jobino timo ri win gime jye rupiri wibedo ji paran; aka jokuya ŋata ooran.
43015022	Bedi akibino to aluwo gi jo di jongoye gi racho; to pama onyo jongoye gi kagoŋirok kwoŋ gimarecho pajo.
43015023	Moro jye ma dakan meno dak Baba bende.
43015024	Bedi fuodi akitimo idyer jo tich moido fuodi ongoye ŋata otimo, di jongoye gi racho; to pama onyo jotyeko neno gima atimo aka jodak wan gi Baba.
43015025	Gime obedo ameno, aka ŋey gima ondik i Chik pajo wotundi i kare ni, ‘Jodakan nono.’
43015026	“Ka Jamiyi ryeko, mobedo Chuny maradyeri ma anodhir ri win, ma loro wok bongi Baba obin, go bino luwo kwoŋan.
43015027	Aka win bende, wibino pido ran, rupiri wityeko bedo kodan wok i chakirok.
43016001	“Awacho ri win gime aka wikiri wiyengere i yeyo mewin.
43016002	Jobino ryemo win woko i kalamo pa Joyudaya, aka ndir bino tundo ma moro jye maneko win bino paro nike ka timo ameno meno tiyo ri Were.
43016003	Jobino timo gikipiny me ri win rupiri jokuya Baba kosa an.
43016004	To awacho ri win gime, ni ka ndir mere otundi, wibino poyo nike atyeko luwo ri win kwoŋe.” “Akutho akiwacho ri win gime rupiri oido fuodi anitye gi win.
43016005	Pama onyo akidho bongi ŋata ooran, to ongoye kwoŋ win kada ŋata penjan ni, ‘Ikidho yu kune?’
43016006	Ato paka onyo atucho ri win gime, rembo onyo opoŋ i chuny win.
43016007	To adyeri awacho ri win: Bedo gimaber ri win ka akadho, rupiri ka akikadho, Jamiyi ryeko kilebino bongi win. To ka atyeko kadho, nyaka abino dhiro ri win go.
43016008	Aka ka go obino, go bino miyo piny ramirok kwoŋ gimarecho, kodi tiro, kodi thumo banja;
43016009	kwoŋ gimarecho, rupiri jokoyeyan;
43016010	kwoŋ tiro, rupiri akidho bongi Baba aka odoko wikonenan;
43016011	kwoŋ thumo banja, rupiri jadhum ma piny ka otyek thumo ri go banja.
43016012	“Anitye kodi gikipiny man awacha ri win, to gunyoni fuodi wikinyal chiro.
43016013	To ka Chuny maradyeri obin, go bino nyutho win adyeri jye. Ato go kibino luwo gi i wiye won, to bino wacho ri win gima go owinjo, odoko go bino nyutho win kwoŋ gima lebino rumachien.
43016014	Go bino miyan dwoŋ, rupiri go bino wacho ri win gimoro jye m'okwanyo bongan.
43016015	Gimoro jye ma Baba ni gine meno aparan; amomiyo atyeko wacho ri win nike go bino wacho ri win gimoro jye ma go okwanyo bongan.
43016016	“I hongo machiek wikibino nenan; to i hongo machiek wibino nenan kendo.”
43016017	Megi kwoŋ jofuonjirok pere jopenjere wegi kendigin ni, “Gime dwoŋ mere aŋo? Go wacho ri wan ni, ‘I hongo machiek wikibino nenan, to i hongo machiek wibino nenan kendo.’ Odoko ni, ‘Rupiri akidho bongi Baba.’ ”
43016018	Jomedere gi penjo ni, “Hongo machiek me, dwoŋ mere aŋo? Fuodi wakiniaŋ gima go luwo kwoŋe?”
43016019	Yesu oŋeyo nike jomito penjo go, ri ameno owacho ri jo ni, “Onyo wiwegi wipenjere kwoŋ gima awok wacho ni, ‘I hongo machiek wikibino nenan, to i hongo machiek wibino nenan kendo?’
43016020	Adyeri awacho ri win, wibino ywak to wirem, kareno piny sangala. Wibino winjo malith, to winjo malith mewin no bino lokere kisangala.
43016021	I hongo ma nywol, dhako winjo litho, rupiri hongo pere ma chandirok otundo, to ka otyeko nywolo nyathi pere go wiye wil gi litho cha, rupiri go onyo sangala nike nyathi otyeko nywolere i piny.
43016022	Meno apaka bende nitye gi win: pama onyo wiwinjo litho, to abino neno win kendo, aka chuny win bino poŋ gi kisangala, kiti kisangala ma moro kinyal mayo win.
43016023	“Ka ndelo no otundo wikibino kwayan gimoro. Adyeri awacho ri win, Baba bino miyo win gimoro jye ma winokway i nyingan.
43016024	Gunyoni fuodi wikikwayo gimoro i nyingan, kwayi win aka wibino limo, ŋey kisangala mewin wobedi mopoŋ.”
43016025	“Awacho ri win gikipiny me g'agechin, to ndir bino tundo ma akibino oro agechin kendo, to abino luwo ri win nyatirtir kwoŋ Baba.
43016026	Ka ndir no otundo, wibino kwayo go i nyingan; aka akiwachi ni abino kwayo go gimoro ri win,
43016027	rupiri Baba won omaro win rupiri wimaran aka wiyeyo nike awok bongi Were.
43016028	Awok bongi Baba to abino i piny, aka onyo aeye i piny agik kendo bongi Baba.”
43016029	Gikenyo jofuonjirok pere jowacho ri go ni, “Nyaka onyo iluwo nyatirtir, ma kiweno i agechin.
43016030	Nyaka onyo waŋeyo ni iŋeyo gimoro jye; ikiyeny moro wopenjin kendo. Me miyo wayeyo nike adyeri iwok bongi Were.”
43016031	Yesu odwoko jo ni, “Onyo nyaka wiyeyo?
43016032	Ndir bino tundo, aka otyeko kiri tundo ma wijojye wibino kedher'iye to dhano jye dok pecho pere, aka wibino weyan kendan. To akinitye kendan, rupiri Baba nitye kodan.
43016033	Atyeko wacho ri win gime ŋey wibedi i syem i riwirok kodan. Piny bino miyo wichandere. To bedi win miseni! Atyeko loyo chandirok ma piny!”
43017001	Munyo Yesu otyeko wacho gime, oŋiyo polo to wacho ni, “Baba, hongo otundo. Miyi Wuodin dwoŋ, aka ŋey Wuodin womiyin dwoŋ.
43017002	Kole imiyo go men kwoŋ ji jye, ŋey go womiyi joma imiyo go jye kwo makirum.
43017003	Aka me a kwo makirum: nike ji jowoŋeyin, Were achiel maradyeri, kendo jowoŋeyi Yesu Kristo m'ioro.
43017004	Atyeko nyutho dwoŋ perin i piny; achowo timo tich m'imiyan timo.
43017005	Onyo pama, Baba, miyan dwoŋ i waŋin, dwoŋ moido ani gine kodin ma fuodi kochwey piny.
43017006	“Atyeko miyo nyingin ŋeyirok i waŋ ji m'imiyan wok i piny. Jo oido jobedo ji perin, to imiyan jo aka jotyeko mako wach perin.
43017007	Pama onyo joŋeyo ni gimoro jye m'imiyan wok bongin,
43017008	rupiri amiyo jo mikwenda m'imiyan, aka jojolo; joŋeyo adyeri ni awok bongin, aka joyeyo nike iŋat'ioran.
43017009	“Akwayo ri jo. Akikwayi ri piny, to ri ji m'imiyan, rupiri jobedo aperin.
43017010	Gimoro jye ma ani gine meno aperin, odoko gimoro jye m'ini gine meno aparan, aka atyeko limo dwoŋ kwoŋ jo.
43017011	Akibino doŋ i piny ka, to jo fuodi jonitye i piny ka, to an onyo abino bongin. Baba Maleŋ, kuri jo maber gi men ma nyingin m'imiyan, ŋey nyaka jowobedi achiel paka wan kodin wabedo achiel.
43017012	I hongo monwaŋo ani gi jo, akuro jo maber gi men ma nyingin m'imiyan. Agwoko jo, aka kwoŋ jo ongoye ŋata orwenyo, kwanyo woko ŋat ma amien oido oripo podho rigo ŋey gima ndiiko wacho wotimere.
43017013	Onyo pama abino bongin, aka awacho gikipiny me i piny, ŋey jowolimi kisangala paran to poŋ i chuny jo.
43017014	Amiyo jo mikwenda perin aka piny odak jo, rupiri jokobedo ji pa piny paka an bende akibedo dhano pa piny.
43017015	Akikway ni ikwany jo woko i piny, to nike ikur jo maber kwoŋ men ŋatarach piny, jo bende jokobedo ji pa piny.
43017016	Paka akabedo dhano pa piny, jo bende jokobedo ji pa piny.
43017017	Lonyi chuny jo i adyeri, rupiri wach perin obedo adyeri.
43017018	Onyo aoro jo i piny paka chango ibende ioran i piny.
43017019	Aka ri bero pajo onyo amiyere rin ŋey jo bende jowonyali miyirok ri iyadyeri.
43017020	“Akikwayi ri jome kendijo, to ri joma bende joyeyan ru mikwenda pa jome.
43017021	Akwayo nike jojye jowonyali bedo achiel, Baba, paka initye i an aka anitye i in. Jo bende jowobedi i wan, ŋey piny woyeyi nike iŋati ioran.
43017022	Amiyo jo dwoŋ m'imiyan, ŋey jowobedi achiel paka wan kodin wabedo achiel;
43017023	abedi i jo aka ibedi i an, ŋey jowobedi achiel kichutho, aka nyaka piny woŋeyi nike ioran aka imaro jo paka imaran.
43017024	“Baba, ityeko miyan jo, aka ayenyo jowobedi kodan kama ani iye, jowonyali neno dwoŋ paran m'imiyan; kole imaran kir ma fuodi kochwey piny.
43017025	Baba Motire, piny kuya in, to aŋeyin aka jome joŋeyo nike iŋati ioran.
43017026	Atyeko miyo jo ŋeyin aka abino medo timo ameno, ŋey mar perin ma initye gine ran wobedi i jo, aka awon bende abedi i jo.”
43018001	Munyo Yesu ochowo kwayo me, oay kodi jofuonjirok pere to jokalo jwom Kiduron. Kenyo oido nitye ndelo moro, to Yesu kodi jofuonjirok pere jodonj'iye.
43018002	Yuda, jachami sereko, oido bende oŋeyo kenyo, rupiri ndir madit Yesu onwaŋo otyeko bedo kenyo kodi jofuonjirok pere.
43018003	Ameno Yuda okidho kenyo kodi kitipa pa joserikale kodi jokur mogo ma Ot pa Were ma jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi Jofarisayo jooro. Jotiŋo mach odingili, talin, gi gilweny.
43018004	Yesu oido oŋeyo gimoro jye monwaŋo kidho timirok kwoŋe. Ri ameno ochore bongi jo to penjo jo ni, “Wirango ŋa?”
43018005	Jodwoko ni, “Yesu Janazareth.” Go odwoko ni, “A an me.” Yuda jachami sereko, onwaŋo ochungo gi jo.
43018006	Munyo Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “A an me”, jogik gi yuŋey gin to jooy piny ngulungulu.
43018007	Yesu odoko openjo jo ni, “Wirango ŋa won.” Jowacho ni, “Yesu Janazareth.”
43018008	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Atyeko wacho ri win ni a an me. Ere ka wirangan, weyi win jome jowokadhi.”
43018009	Gime otimere ama ŋey gima ndir no go owacho wotundi i kare ni, “Ongoye kada achiel morwenyo kwoŋ jojye m'imiyan.”
43018010	Simon Petro oido nitye g'abor; oyuyo to toŋo ŋecha pa jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, to chodo woko ithe marachuch. Nyingi ŋecha no oido Malko.
43018011	Yesu owacho ri Petro ni, “Dwoki abor i ode! Onyo akiramadhi agwata ma chandirok ma Baba omiyani?”
43018012	Lwak joserikale kodi jotel pajo kodi Joyudaya ma jokur jomako Yesu, jotweyo go,
43018013	to jotero go pa Anas moido obedo baa chipa Kaifas, moido jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar i oro no.
43018014	Kaifas me ama ndir cha omiyo Joyudaya ryeko nike oido ber loyo ka ŋatachiel otho ri ji jye.
43018015	Petro kodi jafuonjirok man joluwo Yesu. Paka jafuonjirok man no oido oŋeyere maber gi jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar no, go bende odonjo gi Yesu i dyedipo pa jadwoŋ no.
43018016	Petro odoŋ woko to chungo chiegin gi dhoot. Jafuonjirok man, moido oŋeyere maber gi jadwoŋ no, ogik oluwo gi nyako moido kuro dhoot, to rwako Petro.
43018017	Nyako moido kuro dhoot owacho ri Petro ni, “In won me k'achiel kwoŋ jofuonjirok pa ŋato?” Petro odwoko ni, “Be, akibedo.”
43018018	Piny onwaŋo ŋich, ri ameno jotich kodi jokur jomoko mach aka onwaŋo jochungo jothoko mach no jooyo. Petro bende okidho to chungo gi jo ka oyo mach.
43018019	Jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar no openjo Yesu kwoŋ jofuonjirok pere kodi fuonji pere.
43018020	Yesu odwoko ni, “Ndir jye aluwo kamaler ri piny, aka afuonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya kodi i Ot pa Were, kama Joyudaya jye jochokere iye, aka ongoye gima fuodi awacho nyaliŋliŋ.
43018021	To raŋo ma wipenjan ameno? Penji win ji ma jotyeko winjan. Kole joŋeyo gima atyeko wacho ri jo.”
43018022	Munyo Yesu owacho ama, achiel kwoŋ jokur ogoyo lembe g'adhoŋ aka owacho ni, “Inyalo nedi luwo ameno gi jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar?”
43018023	Yesu odwoko ni, “Ka awacho gimoro marach, nyuthi ginago kamaler. To ka gima awacho otire, raŋo igoyan?”
43018024	Gikenyo Anas odhiro go, ma fuodi otwey chinge, pa Kaifas, jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar.
43018025	Petro oido fuodi ochungo kenyo oyo mach. Gikenyo jowote jopenjo go ni, “Ibende ikibedo achiel kwoŋ jofuonjirok pa ŋato?” To Petro kwedere ni, “Be, akibedo achiel kwoŋ jo.”
43018026	Achiel kwoŋ ŋecha pa jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, wat pa ŋata Petro oido ochodo woko ithe cha, oluwo malo ni, “Akinenin bonge i ndelo kacha?”
43018027	Petro odoko okwedere to wacho ni, “Be”, piyo piyo no to wuodi gweno koko.
43018028	Jokwanyo Yesu i ot pa Kaifas to jotero go i chiel pa gavana. Piny onwaŋo obedo odikini worwor. Joyudaya jokodonjo i chiel rupiri oido joyenyo jowokure ma jokobedo makoch i kite ma chik, ŋey jowochami kalima ma Kadho.
43018029	Amomiyo Pilato owok woko romo gi jo to wacho ni, “Banja aŋo ma wi osa jame?”
43018030	Jodwoko ni, “Di wakikelo go bongin bedi go kotimo racho moro.”
43018031	Pilato owacho ni, “Wiwegi kwanyi win go aka winen banja pere i kite ma chik mewin.” Joyudaya jodwoko ni, “Koyey wan neko dhano.”
43018032	(Me onyutho adyeri gima Yesu onwaŋo otyeko wacho munyo go nyutho kiti tho ma go le tho.)
43018033	Pilato ogik i chiel to lwoŋo Yesu to penjo go ni, “In i Kere pa Joyudaya?”
43018034	Yesu odwoko ni, “Penji me wok bongin i won, kosa joman ama jowacho rin kwoŋan?”
43018035	Pilato odwoko ni, “Iparo nike a Jayudaya? Kole ji perin wegi kodi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar ama jokelin bongan. Itimo aŋo?”
43018036	Yesu owacho ni, “Ker paran kobedo ma piny ka; bedi ker paran bedi ma piny ka, di jomaluwan jolwenyo ma geŋan ma d'akipodho i chingi Joyudaya. To, ker paran ki ma piny ka!”
43018037	Gikenyo Pilato openjo go ni, “Kere in i kere?” Yesu odwoko ni, “Eno iwacho ni an kere. Onywolan ri gino aka abino i piny ka luwo ri adyeri. Nyatoro jye ma tiyere g'adyeri winjo dwodan.”
43018038	Pilato openjo ni, “Aka adyeri meno aŋo?” Gikenyo Pilato ogik woko bongi Joyudaya to wacho ri jo ni, “Akinen banja moro kwoŋ go.
43018039	To paka winitye gi chik mewin, ndir jye agonyo ri win jatwech moro i hongo ma kalima ma Kadho, wimito agony ri win Kere pa Joyudaya?”
43018040	Jodwoko go gi koko ni, “Be, ki go! Wamito Baraba!” (Baraba oido jakwo mojokojo.)
43019001	Gikenyo Pilato otero Yesu to oro jo chwado go.
43019002	Joserikale jodolo thach okudho to joketho i wiye pa junga; joruko ri go kanzo ma rangi ariŋo.
43019003	Aka jobino bonge to jowacho ni, “Yindira Kere pa Joyudaya!” To jogoyo lembe adhoŋ.
43019004	Pilato odoko ogik to wacho ri muma ji no ni, “Neni win ee awodho go bongi win, ma miyo win ŋeyo nike akinyalo nwaŋo gima miyan thumo ri go banja.”
43019005	Gikenyo owodho Yesu woko munyo oruko junga ma thach okudho kodi kanzo ma rangi ariŋo. Pilato owacho ri jo ni, “Neni win! Me a jal ago!”
43019006	Munyo jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi ji pajo joneno go, jokoko ni, “Guri go kwoŋ musalaba! Guri go kwoŋ musalaba!” Pilato owacho ri jo ni, “Ere kwanyi wi go wiwegi wiguri go kwoŋ musalaba. Akinen gima d'imiyan athum ri go banja.”

43019013	Munyo Pilato owinjo wach me, otero Yesu woko to bedo piny i kom ma thumo banja kama ilwoŋo ni, “Kalikondi ma Tele.” (I Dhoyudaya bedo “Gabatha.”)

43019016	Gikenyo Pilato oketho Yesu i chingi jo ni woguri kwoŋ musalaba. Gikenyo Yesu obedo i chingi jokur.

43019018	Joguro go kenyo kwoŋ musalaba; joguro ji aryo man bende kwoŋ musalaba, ŋatachiel yu rachuch ŋat man yu racham pere kareno Yesu obedo dyere.
43019019	Pilato ondiko wach to oro jo ketho wi musalaba ni, “YESU MA NAZARETH, KERE PA JOYUDAYA.”
43019020	Joyudaya mathoth josoma gino, rupiri kama ogur'iye Yesu kwoŋ musalaba oido chiegin gi tindi. Wach no oido ondik i Dhoyudaya, Dholatin, kodi Dhoyunani.
43019021	Jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar pa Joyudaya jodaŋin ri Pilato ni, “Ikiri indiki ni, ‘Kere pa Joyudaya,’ to ndiki ni, ‘Jal me owacho nike, An a Kere pa Joyudaya.’ ”
43019022	Pilato odwoko ni, “Gima atyeko ndiko meno atyeko ndiko.”
43019023	Munyo joserikale jotyeko guro Yesu kwoŋ musalaba, jokwanyo nengin pere, to jopoko adech aŋwen, kis jaserikale otero adech achiel. Jokwanyo kanzo bende mokwoy ma nanga achiel, mongoye kama oriw gine.
43019024	To Joserikale jowacho ni, “Wakiri wayechi me; ere weyi wagoy kwir wanen ŋata oteri.” Gime otimere ma miyo gimondik wotundi i kare ni, “Wegi jopokere nengin paran Jogoyo kwir ri kanzo paran.” Aka joserikale jotimo ameno won.
43019025	Joma oido jochungo chiegin gi musalaba pa Yesu obedo yokimere, nyamin yokimere, Marya chipa Kulopa, kodi Marya ma wok Magdala.
43019026	Munyo Yesu oneno yokimere kodi jafuonjirok ma go omaro jochungo kenyo, owacho ri yokimere ni, “Dhakodwoŋ, wuodin eno.”

43019028	Yesu oŋeyo ni gimoro jye orumo, to ma miyo gimondik wotundi owacho ni, “Riyo nekan.”
43019029	Agwata oido ni kenyo mopoŋ vini mawach; jorwako changwe i vini no, joketho i jangi yath, to jochwayo ri go i dhoke.
43019030	Yesu obilo vini to wacho ni “Orumo!” Gikenyo okulo wiye to weyo chunye chot.
43019031	Gikenyo Joyudaya jokwayo Pilato nike wotur tyendi jom'oneki tikwanyo jo kwoŋ musalaba, rupiri meno oido ndelo ma yikirok ri Sabato, aka jokomito ni delkwoŋ jono wobedi kwoŋ musalaba i ndelo ma Sabato, rupiri Sabato obedo ndelo madwoŋ.
43019032	Amomiyo joserikale jokidho to joturo tyendi ŋat marapena kodi apa ŋat man monwaŋo onek jo kanyachiel gi Yesu.
43019033	To munyo jotundo bongi Yesu to joneno nike go otyeko tho, jokoturo tyende.
43019034	Achiel kwoŋ joserikale oroko ŋeti Yesu gi toŋ, to piyo piyo remo gi pi wok.
43019035	Ŋata oneno gime munyo timere oluwo kwoŋe. Wach pere otire, kendo go oŋeyo ni luwo giradyeri aka ŋey wibende wiyey.
43019036	Gime otim nike randik wotundi i kare ni, “Ongoye choko pere kada achiel ma bino tur.”
43019037	Aka randik man wacho ni, “Ji jobino ŋiyo ŋata jochwowo.”
43019038	Rumachien, Yozefu, ma Arimatheya, okwayo Pilato ni go wokwanyi delkwoŋ Yesu. (Yozefu oido jafuonjirok pa Yesu ma nyaliŋliŋ, rupiri go oido lworo Joyudaya.) Pilato owacho ri go ni go nyalo kwanyo delkwoŋ Yesu; gikenyo Yozefu okidho to kwanyo delkwoŋ Yesu.
43019039	Nikodemo bende, ma ndir moro okidho neno Yesu wor, obino, kareno otiŋo gima ŋwe kur chiegin kilo pyeradek, moruw kodi pigi yen man.
43019040	Jaryo me jokwanyo delkwoŋ Yesu to jotweyo i sukin matar gi mo maŋwe kur me i kite ma yikirok pa Joyudaya.
43019041	Kama ogur'iye Yesu kwoŋ musalaba oido nitye ndelo ma di kalyel moido fuodi koyik'iye nyatoro.
43019042	Paka ndelo oido obedo ma telo Sabato pa Joyudaya, aka kalyel onwaŋo ni chiegin, joyiko Yesu kenyo.
43020001	I Sabiti odikini worwor, ma fuodi piny riprip, Marya ma wok Magdala okidho kalyel to neno ni oŋil woko tele ma dhok kalyel.
43020002	Go oringo to kidho bongi Simon Petro kodi jafuonjirok man ma Yesu omaro, to wacho ri jo ni, “Jokwanyo woko Ruoth i kalyel aka wakuya kama oketh'iye go!”
43020003	Gikenyo Petro gi jafuonjirok man no joay to jokidho i kalyel.
43020004	Jaryo no oido joringo, to jafuonjirok man no odwire oyombo Petro to telo tundo i kalyel.
43020005	Go oluŋere to neno sukin ama odoŋ, to kodonjo iye.
