43020007	kodi nanga monwaŋo otwey gine wiy Yesu m'odole gichien kakende.
43020008	Gikenyo, jafuonjirok, motelo tundo i kalyel bende odonjo to neno to yeyo.
43020009	(Jono fuodi oido jokoniaŋ odocho kwoŋ randik ma wacho ni go ripo chierino).
43020010	Gikenyo jofuonjirok no jodok pecho pajo.
43020011	Marya ochungo munyo ywak dho thengi kalyel;
43020012	gikenyo go oneno jomalaika aryo kenyo, i nengin matar, ma jobedo piny kama onwaŋo oketh'iye delkwoŋ Yesu, achiel yu wiye man yu tyende.
43020013	Jopenjo go ni, “Dhakodwoŋ, iywak aŋo?” Go odwoko ni, “Jokwanyo Ruoth paran, aka akuya kama joketh'iye go!”
43020014	Munyo go otyeko wacho ameno, go owire to neno Yesu ochungo kenyo; to koŋeyo ni manago Yesu.
43020015	Yesu openjo go ni, “Dhakodwoŋ, raŋo iywak. Irango ŋa?” Paka dheno oparo ni meno won ndelo, owacho ri go ni, “K'iŋati ikwanyo go, jadwoŋ, wachi ran kama iketh'iye go akidhi aom go.”
43020016	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Marya!” Go owire yu bonge to wacho gi Dhoyudaya ni, “Raboni!” (Dwoŋ mere ni Jafuonji.)
43020017	Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Ikiri imakan rupiri fuodi akigik both Baba. To kidhi bongi wutimera iwachi ri jo ni akidho malo bongi Baba ma Bawin, Were paran ma Were mewin.”
43020018	Gikenyo Marya ma wok Magdala owacho ri jofuonjirok pere nike, “Atyeko neno Ruoth,” to lyesa ri jo gima Yesu owacho ri go jye.
43020019	Munyo piny oumere i ndelo ma Sabiti no, jofuonjirok oido jochokere kanyachiel kareno jochiego thigin, rupiri oido jolworo Joyudaya. Gikenyo Yesu obino to chungo i dyer jo to wacho ni, “Syem wobedi kodi win.”
43020020	Munyo go otyeko wacho ameno, onyutho jo chinge gi ŋete. Jofuonjirok kisangala opoŋ i chuny jo munyo joneno Ruoth.
43020021	Gikenyo Yesu odoko owacho ri jo ni, “Syem wobedi kodi win. Paka Baba ooran abende aoro win.”
43020022	Go owacho gime to kudho jo gi luya to wacho ni, “Limi win Chuny Maleŋ.
43020023	Gimarecho pa ji ma winochwaki ri jo, ibino chwako ri jo; to gimarecho pa ji ma wikochwaki ri jo bende kochwaki ri jo.”
43020024	Achiel kwoŋ jofuonjirok, Thoma (milwoŋo ni Rut) onwaŋo ongoye bongi jo munyo Yesu obino.
43020025	To jofuonjirok wadi jowach ri go ni, “Watyeko neno Ruoth!” Thoma owacho ri jo ni, “Ka akineno waŋpoyo ma musumal oweyo i chinge, t'arwako lwetan kama musumal odonj'iye i ŋete, akoyey.”
43020026	Munyo ndelo abiryo okadho, jofuonjirok oido jonitye kanyachiel kendo, aka Thoma oido ni gi jo. Thigin jye oido ochiegi, to Yesu obino to chungo i dyer jo to wacho ri jo ni, “Syem wobedi gi win.”

43020028	Thoma odwoko ni, “Ruoth paran kendo Were paran!”

43021001	Rumachien, Yesu onyuthere kendo ri jofuonjirok pere dho wakawaka ma Tiberya. Me apaka go otimo.
43021002	Simon Petro, Thoma (milwoŋo ni Rut), Nathanayel (ma wok Kana i Galileya) woti Zebedayo kodi jofuonjirok pa Yesu man jaryo jye oido jo ni kanyachiel.
43021003	Simon Petro owacho ri jo ni, “Akidho kitoga.” Jowacho ni, “Wabino kidho kodin.” Ameno jodonjo i yee, to wor no gipi jokomako gimoro.
43021004	Munyo chieŋ gulo, Yesu ochungo dho thengi pi, to jofuonjirok jokoŋeyo ni manago Yesu.
43021005	Gikenyo go owacho ri jo ni, “Yach me, wityeko makoye gimoro?” Jodwoko ni, “Ongoye gimoro.”
43021006	Go owacho ri jo ni, “Boli win bwoo mewin yu thengi yee marachuch aka wibino mako gimoro.” Gikenyo jobolo bwoo pajo, to jokonyalo wodho ru thotho pa rech.
43021007	Jafuonjirok ma Yesu omaro owacho ni, “manago Ruoth!” Munyo Simon Petro owinjo ni manago Ruoth, otweyere gi nanga pere mawoko (rupiri oido olunyo woko nengin pere), to por i pi.
43021008	Jofuonjirok modoŋ jobino dho geŋin gi yee to joywayo bwoo ma rech opoŋ'iye, rupiri onwaŋo jokini bor gi geŋin kamothwo, to oido romo chiegin mita miya achiel kende.
43021009	Munyo jotundo wi geŋin joneno chuk mach mokur kenyo gi rech i wiye kodi mugat.
43021010	Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri jofuonjirok pere ni, “Keli win rech mogo ma wityeko mako.”
43021011	Simon Petro odonjo i yee to kelo bwoo wi geŋin, mopoŋ'iye rech madongo miya adek gi pyero abich g'adek; to kada oido rech dit ameno, jye bwoo koyech.
43021012	Yesu owacho ri jo ni, “Biye chiemi win.” Ongoye kada ŋatachiel kwoŋ jofuonjirok mobedo gi miseni ma penjo go ni, “In i ŋa?” rupiri oido joŋeyo ni manago Ruoth.
43021013	Gikenyo Yesu okidho, okwanyo mugat no, to miyo jo, to timo ameno bende gi rech.
43021014	Me oido hongo maradek ma Yesu onyuther'iye ri jofuonjirok pere munyo otyeko chierino kwoŋ jomotho.
43021015	Munyo jotyeko chiemo, Yesu openjo Simon Petro ni, “Simon, wuodi Yohana, imaran loyo jome?” Go odwoko ni, “Ey Ruoth, iŋeyo nike amarin.” Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Pidhi nyithindhi roombo paran.”
43021016	Madiryo Yesu odoko openjo go ni, “Simon wuodi Yohana, imarani?” Go odwoko ni, “Ey Ruoth, iŋeyo paka amarin.” Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Kwayi roombo paran.”
43021017	Madidek Yesu odoko omedo penjo go ni, “Simon wuodi Yohana, imarani?” Gikenyo Petro chunye oramo, rupiri Yesu openjo go madidek ni, “Imarani?” Ameno odwoko go ni, “Ruoth, kole iŋeyo gimoro jye, iŋeyo paka amarin.” Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Pidhi roombo paran.
43021018	Adyeri awacho rin, munyo fuodi ithin onwaŋo iwon irukere t'ikidho kama iyenyo jye; to ka iti ibino ryeyo chingin ŋat man ama worukin to terin kama d'ikimito kidh'iye.”
43021019	(Ameno Yesu owacho ama ma nyutho paka Petro d'otho ma miyo Were dwoŋ.) Gikenyo Yesu owacho ri go ni, “Luwan.”
43021020	Petro owire to neno jafuonjirok man luwo jo ma Yesu omaro, ma ndir cha othenere bongi Yesu dhower to penjo ni, “Ruoth, ŋata kidho chamo rin sereko?”
43021021	Munyo Petro oneno go, owacho ri Yesu ni, “Ruoth, to ŋatin?”
43021022	Yesu odwoko go ni, “Ka amito ni ŋato wokwo chuka anodwoki, meno mako kwoŋini? Luwan ayino!”
43021023	Gikenyo wach onyay i dyer jofuonjirok pa Yesu nike jafuonjirok no k'otho. To Yesu kowacho nike go k'otho; go owacho nike, “Ka amito ni go wokwo chuka anodwoki, meno mako kwoŋini?”
43021024	Go a jafuonjirok ma luwo kwoŋ gikipiny me, aka ama ondiko gikipiny me; aka waŋeyo nike gima go ondiko obedo adyeri.
43021025	Onyo, nitye gikipiny man kweth ma Yesu otimo. Bedi ndik jye achielechiele, aparo nike piny gipi di konyalo tiŋo kitawin mere.

44004001	Munyo Petro gi Yohana oido fuodi joluwo ri ji, jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, jotel pa jokur ma Ot pa Were, kodi Josadukayo jobino to joay kwoŋ jo.

44004011	Yesu won a ŋata ndiiko luwo kwoŋe ni, ‘Kole tele won ma jogeto jochayo ni bu kony ama olokere tele ma thyelo kindi ot.’
44004012	“Aka both kinwaŋere bongi ŋat man, rupiri ongoye nyingi nyatoro man jye i piny gipi, ma Were omiyo ji, ma waripo nwaŋ'iye both.”
44004013	Jokweth ma pido jodhyer munyo joneno miseni pa Petro gi Yohana, gi ŋeyo nike me ji mogo ma jokofuonjere kada. Gikenyo joniaŋ nike jome yado jobedo bongi Yesu.
44004014	To onwaŋo ongoye gimoro ma di jonyal wacho, rupiri joneno jal moboth no ochungo kenyo gi Petro gi Yohana.
44004015	Amomiyo jowacho ri Petro gin ni jowoeye i kapido, to jochako kikaŋasa wach wegi kendigin.
44004016	Jopenjere ni, “Wanotimi aŋo gi jome? Dhano jye ma Yerusalem oŋeyo nike jome jotyeko timo giraura madwoŋ me, aka wakinyal kwero.
44004017	To ma geŋo wach me medo nyay i dyer ji, weyi wawachi ri jo nike kiri jowomedi luwo kendo ri nyatoro jye i nyingi ŋato.”
44004018	Gikenyo jolwoŋo jo dwoko aka jochiko jo teltel ni kiri jowofuonji i nyingi Yesu.
44004019	To Petro gi Yohana jodwoko ni, “Wiwegi thum win gimotire atima i waŋ Were, winjo win, kosa winjo Were;
44004020	rupiri wakinyal weyo luwo kwoŋ gima wawegi watyeko neno gi winjo.”
44004021	Jopido jomedo bwoko jo gi men swa, to joweyo jo jokadho. Jokoneno yo ma di jomiyo gine jaryo no girachula, rupiri ji jye oido jopako Were kwoŋ gimotimere.
44004022	Aka ŋata giraura ma both otimere kwoŋe no oido kalo oro pyero aŋwen.
44004023	Tekin ityeko weyo jo, Petro gi Yohana jogik i kweth pajo to jowacho ri jowot gin gima jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jotel pa ji jowacho.
44004024	Munyo jowinjo gime, jo jye joriwere kanyachiel i kwayo Were ni, “Ruoth ma Jachwech ma polo gi piny, kodi wakawaka kodi gima ni iye jye!
44004025	Chango iluwo i Chuny Maleŋ gi dhoki kwari wan Daudi, jatich perin, ni, ‘Raŋo ma Jopath jo ni gi keme?
44004026	Kerere ma piny joyikere aka jodhumbe joromo kanyachiel, kwinyo Ruoth kodi Kristo (mowir gi mo) pere!’
44004027	Kole adyeri Herode kodi Pontyo Pilato joromo kanyachiel i tindi me gi Jopath kodi ji ma Israel ma chano timo gimarecho ri Yesu, Jatich perin Maleŋ, m'iwiro gi mo.
44004028	Jochokere ma timo gimoro jye ma in, gi men perin kodi mito perin, oido ityeko yiko ni d'otimere.
44004029	Aka pama, Ruoth, neni paka jobwoko wan, amomiyo miyi jotich perin men ma tito mikwenda perin gi miseni.
44004030	Ryeyi chingin ma botho ji, itimi ranyuth ma giraura kodi gidhyer i nyingi jatich perin maleŋ, Yesu.”
44004031	Munyo jotyeko kwayo, kama onwaŋo jo ni iye oyengere. Chuny Maleŋ opoŋ kwoŋ jo to jochako luwo wach pa Were gi miseni.
44004032	Kitipa pa jomoyeyo obedo achiel i paro kodi i chuny gin. Ongoye ŋata owacho ni lim pere obedo maraora pere kende, to obedo apa ji jye.
44004033	Jomoor jothyelo wach ma chierino pa Ruoth Yesu gi men moasere, aka jojye jonwaŋo silwany madwoŋ.
44004034	Ongoye moro i kitipa pajo moido chando gimoro, rupiri jomonwaŋo jonitye gi lowo kosa udi jotana to jokelo pesa mere
44004035	to joketho i chingi jomoor. Meno ama bin ipoko dhano jye mani kitipa monwaŋo chando gimoro.
44004036	Gikenyo Yozefu, Jalevi m'onywol Sipuro, ma jomoor jolwoŋo ni Barunaba (dwoŋ mere ni, “Ŋata kweyo chuny ji”),
44004037	otana lowo pere, to kelo pesa mere to miyo jomoor.
44005001	To onwaŋo nitye nyatoro milwoŋo ni Ananiya, gi chiege ma nyinge Safira, ma jotana lowo pajo mogo.
44005002	To go okano pesa moro ma konyirok, aka chiege oŋeyo gime, to modoŋ ama go otero ri jomoor.
44005003	Petro owacho ri go ni, “Ananiya, raŋo miyeyo Sitan odonjo i chunyin to miyin itwodo ri Chuny Maleŋ to ikano adech ma pesa m'ilimo i lowo perin?
44005004	Ma fuodi ikitana lowo no, onwaŋo kobedo aperin? Aka munyo ityeko kitana, pesa mere oido kobedo aperin? To raŋo ma iridho i chunyin nike itim gima pameno? Ikiwondo ji to iwondo Were won!”
44005005	Tekin Ananiya winjo gime, ogore piny to tho, aka dhano jye mowinjo gime, lworo opoŋ kwoŋe.
44005006	Yach mogo jodonjo, jotweyo go gi suka to jotero go to joyiko go.
44005007	Munyo hongo okadho ma romo sawa adek, chiege bende odonjo ma koŋeyo gima oido nende otimere.
44005008	Petro openjo go ni, “Wachi ran, me oido a gima in gi chworin wilimo gipi i gimewin?” Go odwoko ni, “Ey, meno won a welo mere.”
44005009	Gikenyo Petro owacho ri go ni, “Raŋo ma in kodi chworin wiyiko paro ma temo Chuny Maleŋ? Neni! Joma jowok yiko chworin eno jokonjere dhoot, aka jobino tiŋin jowoterin woko bende!”
44005010	Gikenyo won to dheno podho piny dho katyendi Petro to tho. Yach cha jodwoko, aka munyo jonwaŋo go otho, jotiŋo go bende to jokidho yiko go kabuti chwore.
44005011	Kitipa pa jomoyeyo gi bee gi joman ma jowinjo gino lworo madwoŋ opoŋ kwoŋ jo.
44005012	Jomoor jotimo ranyuth ma giraura madit i dyer ji. Jomoyeyo bin joromo i kalikondi pa Solomon.
44005013	Ongoye ŋat moro man ma kobedo jakweth pajo motemo riwirok gi jo, kada ji oido jomiyo jo dwoŋ.
44005014	Kada ameno welo pa chwo kodi mon ma jomedo yeyo Ruoth oidho malo mayot.
44005015	Ranyuth momore kodi giraura otim i waŋ ji gi chingi Jomoor ma kiri jotwo bin itero jo i royo mokakere ma tindi to jobedo kenyo i kanindo kodi i par pajo munyo jogeno ni kada nyaka tipo pa Petro wogeyi jomegi kwoŋ jo ka go kadho kenyo.
44005016	Ji bende jowok i tindi mothoko Yerusalem to jochokere kenyo munyo jokelo jotwo kodi joma chuny mochido chando jo, aka joboth jojye.
44005017	Gikenyo jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi wadi jye, ma kweth pa Josadukayo, jobedo gi nyieko madwoŋ ri jomoor.
44005018	Jomako jomoor to joketho jo i od twech mani kenyo.
44005019	To i wor no, malaika pa Ruoth oyawo waŋkach ma od twech, to wodho woko jomoor, to wacho ri jo ni,
44005020	“Kidhi win wichungi i Ot pa Were, aka wiwachi ri ji jye kwoŋ kwo manyien me.”
44005021	Munyo ŋamba oyweyo, jomoor jodonjo i Ot pa Were to jochako fuonji paka owachi ri jo. Munyo jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi wadi jotundo, jolwoŋo jotel pa Joyudaya kanyachiel bedo i romo mopoŋ i kapido. Gikenyo odhiro wach i od twech nike wokel jomoor bongi jo.
44005022	To munyo joserikale jotundo, jokonwaŋo jomoor; gikenyo jogik to jodwoko wach ri jopido ni,
44005023	“Munyo watundo i od twech wanwaŋo ochiegi aka jokur jye oido jochungo kenyo; to munyo wayawo wakinwaŋo moro kada achiel iye.”
44005024	Munyo jaserikale ma telo jokur ma Ot pa Were kodi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar jowinjo gime, jodhyer swa, kareno joparo kwoŋ gima obedi ru wach no.
44005025	Gikenyo dhano moro odonjo to wacho ri jo ni, “Neni win ji ma wirwako i od twech ichade jochungo i Ot pa Were jofuonjo ji.”
44005026	Gikenyo jaserikale okadho gi ji pere to dwoko gi jomoor. Jokooro meni, rupiri jolworo ni ji jonyalo goyo jo gi telin.
44005027	Jorwako jomoor i ot to jomiyo jo chungo ruwaŋ kitipa pa jopido, to jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar osa jo ka wacho ni,
44005028	“Nyoro wachiko win ni wiŋuti ru meno, wikiri widoki wifuonji i nyingi ŋato, to kole onyo wipoŋo Yerusalem gi bee gi fuonji mewin, aka wimito ridho ni tho pa jame obedo gimarach mawan.”
44005029	Petro gi jomoor man jodwoko ni, “Waripo winjo or pa Were ma kiweno apa ji.
44005030	Were pa bachere wan ama ochierino Yesu ma wiguro kwoŋ yath to wineko.
44005031	Were ochierino go aka oketho go yu rachuch pere paka Jadhum kodi Jaboth, womiyi Israel hongo ma ŋuto gi limo chwak ma gimarecho pajo.
44005032	Kendo wan wabedo jokony i gikipiny me--wan wajukony kanyachiel kodi Chuny Maleŋ mich pa Were ri jomawinjo or pere.”
44005033	Munyo jokweth ma pido jowinjo gime jolimo nge mathoth to joridho nike woneki jomoor.
44005034	To ŋatachiel kwoŋ jo milwoŋo ni Gamaliel ma Jafarisayo, odoko jafuonji ma Chik ma jomiyo dwoŋ swa, ochungo i pido, to oro jo wodho woko jomoor, ma hongo ma thin,
44005035	to wacho ri jopido ni, “Joisrael, gwokere win kwoŋ gima wiyenyo timo ri jome.
44005036	I hongo mokadho Thyodas okethere munyo ŋoyo ni go ŋat moro madwoŋ; ji ma romo miya aŋwen joluwo go. To kole oneki go, to jomoido joluwo go jokedhere woko, to kitula pere reyere woko.
44005037	Rumachien, Yuda ma Jagalileya bende owok kamaler i hongo ma kwano ji; go oywayo ji megi bonge to kole oneki go bende, to jomoido joluwo go jokedhere woko.
44005038	Amomiyo i wach pa jome, wikiri witimi gimoro kwoŋ jo. Weyi win jo, rupiri ka atoŋa kodi tim pajo obedo yiko pa dhano, meno won bino rumo woko,
44005039	to ka wok bongi Were wikibino nyalo geŋo jome. Winyalo poyo ni wilwenyo gi Were won.” Jopido jowinjo ryeko ma Gamaliel omiyo jo.
44005040	Jolwoŋo jomoor no i ot, to jomiyo or ni wochwadi jo, aka jopiro jo ni kiri jowomedi luwo i nyingi Yesu, nyaka to jogonyo jo.
44005041	Jomoor joeye i kapido gi kisangala madwoŋ ni Were oparo kwoŋ jo ni joripo limo achanda ma kite no i nyingi Yesu.
44005042	Aka piny moyawere jye jomedere gi fuonjo ji Wach Maber ma Kwoŋ Yesu Kristo, i Ot pa Were kodi i pechin pa ji.
44006001	I hongo me munyo welo pa jofuonjirok medere dito, Joyudaya ma joluwo Dhoyunani joero kiŋunyaŋunya kodi Joyudaya ma jooro Dhoyudaya. Joyudaya ma joluwo Dhoyunani jowacho ni mon tho pajo kipar kwoŋ jo odocho i pok ma kis ndelo.
44006002	Amomiyo Jomoor apar g'aryo jolwoŋo kweth pa jofuonjirok gipi kanyachiel to jowacho ni, “Kiripi ka waweyo tich ma fuonjo Wach pa Were to wayindin gi tich ma poko chiemo ayin.
44006003	Amomiyo, wutimin wan, yeri win chwo abiryo i dyer win ma wiŋeyo ni jopoŋ gi Chuny Maleŋ kodi ryeko, aka wabino ketho jo i tich me.
44006004	Aka wawegi wabino liŋ i tich ma kwayo kodi fuonji.”
44006005	Kweth ji gi bee josangala gi wach pa jomoor, to joyero Stefano, jal mopoŋ gi yeyo kodi Chuny Maleŋ; kodi Filipo, kodi Purokoro, kodi Nikanor, kodi Timon, kodi Parmena kodi Nikolayo, Japath modonjo i dini pa Joyudaya wok Antyok.
44006006	Jokelo jono ruwaŋ jomoor, to jokwayo ri jo, to joketho chingi gin kwoŋ jo.
44006007	Gikenyo Wach pa Were omedere nyay. Welo pa jofuonjirok ma Yerusalem omedo idho malo mapiyo, aka jochwayi ri Were wi alitar mathoth jojolo to yeyo.
44006008	Stefano, dhano ma Were oŋaŋo gi silwany aka oasere gi men, otimo gikipiny madongo ma kelo dhyer kanyachiel gi giraura i dyer ji.
44006009	To ji megi, moido jobedo jokweth ma kalamo pa jomogony (paka onwaŋo ilwoŋo jo), kodi jokalamo ma Sireno kodi ma Alekizandurya, jopyemo gine. Jono gi Joyudaya man ma jowok Silisya kodi Asya jochako pyem gi Stefano.
44006010	To Chuny Maleŋ omiyo Stefano ryeko ma munyo luwo jokonyalo chiro go.
44006011	Amomiyo jonyiewo ji mogo ma jowacho ni, “Wawinjo go luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Musa kodi Were!”
44006012	Ameno jonyalo kisigila ji kodi jotel pa ji kodi jofuonji ma Chik. Jobino bongi Stefano, jomako go, to jotero go i kapido.
44006013	Gikenyo jokelo ji mogo ma jotwodo kwoŋ Stefano, ka jowacho ni, “Jame ndir jye luwo aluwa marach kwoŋ Ot maleŋ mapa Were mawan kodi kwoŋ Chik pa Musa.
44006014	Aka wawinjo munyo go wacho nike Yesu ma Nazareth me bino ŋinyo woko Ot pa Were to wiro woko kula jye ma wanwaŋo bongi Musa!”
44006015	Ji jye ma jobedo i kapido jochomo waŋ gin kwoŋ Stefano aka joneno ni waŋe ochale kodi waŋ malaika.
44007001	Jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar openjo Stefano ni, “Wach no obedo adyeri?”
44007002	Aka Stefano odwoko ni, “Wutimera gi bachere nan! Winjan win! Were mani gi dwoŋ omenyere ri kwari wan Ibrayimu munyo go fuodi nitye yu Mesopotamya, ma fuodi go kokidho bedo Haran,
44007003	aka Were owacho ri go ni, ‘Weyi jothuwin kodi piny mewin ikidhi i piny ma anonyuthin.’
44007004	Gikenyo go oeye i piny ma Kalideya to kidho bedo Haran. Aka rumachien munyo baa Ibrayimu otho, Were okwanyo go woko kenyo to kelo go i piny me, ma pama wibed'iye.
44007005	I hongo no Were k'omiyo Ibrayimu kada adech moro paka apere won, kada nyaka lowo ma romo par tyendi dhano; to Were ochiko ni bino miyo go piny no, aka rumachien d'obedo apere kodi apa nyikwaye, kada go onwaŋo fuodi ongoye gi nyathi.
44007006	Me a gima Were owacho ri go: ‘Nyikwayin jobin bedo i piny ma wiloka, kama jobino bed'iye ŋechin aka ibino kuro jo marach hongo ma romo oro miya aŋwen.’
44007007	Were owacho ni, ‘Abino thumo banja loyo nono ma jobino tich ri jo no, aka rumachien nyikwayin jobino wok i piny no to jodwoko laman ka.’
44007008	Gikenyo Were omiyo Ibrayimu chikirok ma thumirok paka ranyuth mere. Amomiyo Ibrayimu othumo Isaka munyo ndelo aboro otundo, aka Isaka obedo baa Yakobo, aka Yakobo obedo baa nono apar g'aryo.
44007009	“Kwarere ma nonin no jotimo nyieko gi omin gin Yozefu, to jotana go gi Jomisir paka ŋecha. To Were obedo gi Yozefu,
44007010	to wodho go maber i teko pere jye. Munyo Yozefu otundo ruwaŋ Farawo, kere pa Jomisir, Were omiyo go kite maber swa kodi ryeko momiyo go oywayo chuny Farawo. Farawo oloko Yozefu jadhum (gavana) ma piny kodi ma ot pere.
44007011	Gikenyo kech opodho i Misir gipi kodi i Kanan, mokelo chandirok madwoŋ. Kwarere mawan jokonyalo limo chiemo moro jye.
44007012	Amomiyo munyo Yakobo owinjo ni girachama nitye Misir, odhiro kwarere mawan koro kutho kidho lyewo marapena.
44007013	I wendo pajo mararyo, Yozefu onyuthere ri wutimin aka Farawo oniaŋ ni jono jobedo wutimin Yozefu.
44007014	Amomiyo Yozefu odhiro mikwenda ri Yakobo bamere, munyo wacho ri go kodi pecho gipi ni jowokidhi Misir. Welo pajo oido romo ji pyero abiryo g'abich.
44007015	Gikenyo Yakobo okidho Misir, kama go kodi kwarere mawan jotho iye.
44007016	Delkwoŋ jo oter Sekem, kama oyik'iye jo i kalyel ma Ibrayimu chango onyiewo kwoŋ nono pa Hamor gi pesa moro.
44007017	“Munyo ndir ochore chiegin ri Were ma ketho chikirok pere kodi Ibrayimu i tim, welo pa ji mawan i Misir oido oidho malo swa.
44007018	Rumachien kere man, ma koŋeyo wach pa Yozefu ochako dhum i Misir.
44007019	Go obuto ri ji mawan to lokere mager ri kwarere mawan, munyo romo jo jwango nyithindho pajo maŋich nike jowotho.
44007020	I ndir no ama onywol'iye Musa, nyathi maŋon swa ruwaŋ Were. Okur go pecho pa bamere hongo ma dwe adek.
44007021	Aka munyo owodhi go pecho pajo, nyar Farawo odimo go to pidho paka nyathi pere won.
44007022	Ofuonji go ryeko jye mapa Jomisir to lokere ŋata tek swa i wach kodi i tim.
44007023	“Munyo Musa oromo oro pyero aŋwen, oridho paro ma limo Joisrael wadi.
44007024	Oneno achiel kwoŋ jo munyo Jamisir moro timo ri go marach; gikenyo oredo konyo Joisrael no to chulo kwor kwoŋ Jamisir gi neko woko go.
44007025	(Go oparo nike ji pere wegi jobino ŋeyo ni Were oido oro go ma konyo jo, to kere jokoniaŋ).
44007026	Yawere mere Musa onwaŋo Joisrael aryo jogore, to temo theko jo ka wacho ni, ‘Jume, kole wibedo wutimere. Raŋo ma widhaw matek ama?’
44007027	To ŋata oido timo nyawote marach odhiro Musa gichien, to penjo ni, ‘Ŋata okethin ruoth ma thumo ri wan banja?
44007028	Imito nekan bende, paka nyoro ineko Jamisir?’
44007029	Munyo Musa owinjo gime oringo to eye Misir to chako bedo i piny Midyan kama olim'iye wote aryo.
44007030	“Munyo oro pyero aŋwen okadho, malaika omenyere ri Musa i mach mogaŋere monwaŋo lyel i kasugu dudi moro chiegin gi got Sinai.
44007031	Musa ouro swa gima go oneno, to dhire chiegin gi kasugu dudi no woneni maber. Gikenyo go owinjo dwondi Ruoth munyo wacho ni,
44007032	‘An Were pa kwarere nin, Were pa Ibrayimu kodi Isaka kodi Yakobo.’ Musa okirin gi lworo aka kotimo miseni ma ŋiyo.
44007033	To Ruoth wacho ri go ni, ‘Lunyi woko war ma tyendin, rupiri kama ichung'iye me kabedo maleŋ.
44007034	Adyeri atyeko neno chandirok pa ji paran i piny Misir, kendo atyeko winjo paka joywak malith, aka onyo aloro bino botho jo. Onyo biye, aleorin i Misir.’
44007035	“Me a Musa ma jono jokwero ka jopenjo go ni, ‘Ŋata okethin ruoth ma thumo ri wan banja?’ Kole go won a ŋata Were ooro paka ruoth kodi jaboth pajo gi men pa malaika momenyere ri go i kasugu dudi ma onwaŋo lyel mach.
44007036	Go ama otelo ji i royo wok Misir, munyo timo gikipiny ma miyo ji dhyer kanyachiel kodi giraura i Misir kodi i Wakawaka Mobokere, kodi i thim i hongo ma oro pyero aŋwen.
44007037	Me a Musa mowacho ri Joisrael ni, ‘Were bino kelo ri win jatuchi wach Were bende paka an, ma bino wok kwoŋ ji mewin won.’
44007038	Me a ŋata chango obedo i dyer Joisrael ma jochokere i thim kanyachiel kodi kwarere wan kodi malaika moluwo gine wi got Sinai; aka go olimo mikwenda ma kwo mapa Were m'okelo ri wan.
44007039	“To kwarere wan jokwero winjo go; jodhiro go gichien aka joparo kir kwoŋ gik yu Misir.
44007040	Amomiyo jowacho ri Aron ni, ‘Timi ri wan werin ma jobino telo wan. Wakuya gima otimo Musa no momiyo owodho wan i piny Misir.’
44007041	Gikenyo jochweyo gimoro ma chalo nyathi dhiaŋ to jochako lamo gino, to jotimo kalima ma miyo gino dwoŋ.
44007042	Gikenyo Were owiro ŋeye ri jo to miyo jochako lamo michalin ma polo, paka ondik i kitawo pa jotuchi wach Were ni, ‘Ji ma Israel! Manago i ndir cha wineko ran lee paka rachow i hongo ma oro pyero aŋwen i thim?
44007043	Kole wema pa were Molek ama witiŋo kodi chal ma michala pa were Refam, chal ma wichweyo ni wilam. Amomiyo abino ryemo win woko kalo kir Babilon.’
44007044	“Kwarere mawan oido jonitye gi wema pa Were i dyer thim. Oger paka Were ooro Musa timo, i chal ma Were onyutho Musa.
44007045	Rumachien, kwarere mawan ma jojolo wema wok bongi bachere pajo jotiŋo munyo jowotho kodi Yoswa to jotero i piny pa nonin ma Were oryemo woko ri jo. Aka wema no obedo kenyo kir i ndir pa Daudi
44007046	monwaŋo silwany pa Were, aka okwayo Were ni woyeyi go wogeri ot ri Were pa Yakobo.
44007047	To Solomon ama ogero ot no ri go.
44007048	“To Were Madwoŋ Maloyo kibedi ri gin i ot ma ji ama jogero; paka jatuchi wach oketho i Ndiiko ni,
44007049	‘Polo meno kom paran madhum, apaka Ruoth wacho, aka piny meno kom paran ma ajeng'iye tyendan. Kiti ot aŋo ma d'igero ran? Kosa ka ywomirok paran obedi aŋo?
44007050	Kosa chingan ama kochweyo gikipiny ni jye?’
44007051	“Wiyi win tek swa! Dwoŋ thumirok ongoye i chuny win kodi i ithi win. Wichale kodi kwarere mewin; wibende noknok wipyemo gi Chuny Maleŋ!
44007052	Nitye jatuchi wach Were kada achiel ma kwarere mewin jokolwenyo gine? Joneko kir jomikwenda pa Were, ma chango chon jotucho bino pa Ŋatotire, ma wityeko kir chamo ri go sereko to wineko go.
44007053	Win ma wijolo Chik pa Were ma malaikin jokelo ri win, ama wikwero winjo Chik no!”
44007054	Munyo jokweth ma pido jowinjo wach no, keme omako jo to chako mwodo laki gin.
44007055	To Sitefano, paka opoŋ gi Chuny Maleŋ, oŋiyo polo to neno dwoŋ pa Were kodi Yesu munyo ochungo yu rachuch pa Were.
44007056	Aka owacho ni: “Neni! Eno aneno polo oyawere aka Wuodi Dhano ochungo yu rachuch pa Were!”
44007057	Chungo kwoŋ wach me jomochokere kenyo jowoy aka jochulo ithi gin; gikenyo jojye jomwomere kwoŋe,
44007058	jowodho go woko ma tindi aka jogoyo go gi telin. Jomobedo i wach no joketho ruk pajo dho tyendi jayach milwoŋo ni Saulo.
44007059	Munyo jogoyo go, Sitefano owacho i kwayo ni, “Ruoth Yesu, joli chunyan.”
44007060	Gikenyo oguro chonge piny to koko malo ni, “Ruoth, ikiri ikethi kwoŋ jo gimarach me;” aka gi wach me opodho to kwe.
44008001	Aka Saulo oyeyere gi nek me. Gi i ndelo no won, kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Yerusalem ochako nwaŋo achanda malith. Jomoyeyo jye, kwanyo woko jomoor, jotyakere i adeche ma Yudeya kodi Samarya parom.
44008002	Chwo mogo ma jomiyere ri Were joyiko Sitefano munyo joywako go gi geregere madwoŋ.
44008003	To Saulo otemo reyo woko kitipa pa jomoyeyo munyo wotho i kis dhoot pa jomoyeyo ka choko jo, chwo gi mon, aka bolo jo i twech.
44008004	Jomoyeyo ma okedhi jo jokidho iye jye munyo jofuonjo Wach pa Were.
44008005	Filipo okidho i tindi ma Samarya to fuonjo ji kwoŋ Kristo.
44008006	Kweth ji jochiko ithi jo gi chuny jo achiel munyo jowinjo fuonji pa Filipo gi giraura ma go otimo.
44008007	Chuny mochido jowok kwoŋ ji madit gi derino madwoŋ; ji mathoth ma jotwo nyaŋinya, kodi jomoŋol bende jobedo maber.
44008008	Aka kisangala madwoŋ obedo Samarya gipi.
44008009	I tindi no oido nitye nyatoro milwoŋo ni Simon, ma yado miyo Josamarya dhyer gi thyeth pere. Go oido wacho nike go ŋatadwoŋ swa,
44008010	aka dhano jye i tindi, i kitipa ji ma nger jye ochiko ithe maber winjo go. Jowacho ni, “Jame a men pa Were milwoŋo ni, ‘Ma Siragama’ ”
44008011	Go oido otyeko miyo ji dhyer gi thyeth pere hongo malach swa momiyo bin jochiko ithi gin winjo go.
44008012	To munyo joyeyo fuonji pa Filipo kwoŋ Wach Maber ma Ker pa Were kodi nyingi Yesu Kristo, jolimo batisimo, chwo gi mon.
44008013	Simon jye bende oyeyo, aka munyo otyeko limo batisimo, obedo chiegin gi Filipo to dhyer swa munyo oneno ranyuth madongo kodi giraura monwaŋo itimo.
44008014	Munyo jomoor ma Yerusalem jowinjo nike ji ma Samarya jotyeko jolo wach pa Were, jodhiro Petro gi Yohana ri jo.
44008015	Munyo jotundo, jokwayo ri jomoyeyo nike jowolimi Chuny Maleŋ.
44008016	Ato Chuny Maleŋ onwaŋo fuodi koloro ri kada ŋatachiel kwoŋ jo; onwaŋo jotyeko limo batisimo kende i nyingi Ruoth Yesu.
44008017	Gikenyo Petro gi Yohana joketho chingi gin kwoŋ jo, to jolimo Chuny Maleŋ.
44008018	Munyo Simon oneno nike Chuny Maleŋ loro ri ji ka jomoor joketho chingi gin kwoŋ jo, ochwayo pesa ri Petro kodi Yohana
44008019	ka wacho ni, “Miyan win bende men me, aka wangi ka aketho chingan kwoŋ moro go bino limo Chuny Maleŋ.”
44008020	To Petro odwoko ni, “Kadhi itho koro gi pesa perin, rupiri oido iparo ni inyalo nyiewo mich pa Were gi pesa!
44008021	Ingoye gi kabedo i tich mawan me, rupiri chunyin kotire i waŋ Were.
44008022	Amomiyo ŋuti kwoŋ tim perin marach me, aka ikway Ruoth nike wochwakin kwoŋ paro marach me,
44008023	rupiri aneno ni duro opoŋ i chunyin, aka gimarach otweyin.”
44008024	Simon owacho ri Petro kodi Yohana ni, “Mondo kwayi win ran Ruoth, ŋey wongoye kada gimoro achiel ma wiluwo kwoŋe me ma wotiman.”
44008025	Munyo jotyeko niaŋo ji mikwenda pa Ruoth, Petro gi Yohana jogik Yerusalem. Jofuonjo Wach Maber malomalo i adeche momore i Samarya.
44008026	Malaika pa Ruoth oluwo gi Filipo ni, “Yikere ilekidho i royo ma yu Tyendi piny ma wok i Yerusalem aka laro yu Gaza.”
44008027	Me obedo royo ma thim. Gikenyo Filipo oyikere to kadho. I hongo no jatich ma Ethopya onwaŋo dok yu pecho. Ŋat me oido obedo jaserikale madwoŋ ma kuro dero ŋaŋo pa kere madhako ma Ethopya milwoŋo ni Kandase. Go oido owok Yerusalem lamo Were,
44008028	aka onwaŋo dok gi chawula pere munyo soma kitawo pa jatuchi wach Isaya malomalo.
44008029	Chuny Maleŋ owacho ri Filipo ni, “Kidhi iromi kodi chawula no.”
44008030	Filipo oringo bonge to winjo munyo go soma kitawo pa Isaya; gikenyo openjo go ni, “Iŋeyo dwoŋ gima isoma no?”
44008031	Ana Jaserikale, “Anyalo nedi ŋeyo dwoŋ mere ma nyatoro kotito ran?” Go olwoŋo Filipo ni woidhi chawula wobed'iye gine.
44008032	Adech ma randik moido go soma a me: “Paka rombo mitero thumo, kosa nyathi rombo milyelo yer mere, go koŋamo dhoke ni luwo.
44008033	I achanda pere odiy go piny i banja. Ŋa ma nyalo tito kwoŋ luse pere? Kole orey woko kwo pere i piny ka mapiyo.”
44008034	Jaserikale owacho ri Filipo ni, “Wachi ran, jatuchi wach me luwo kwoŋ ŋa me? Kwoŋ go won, kosa ŋat man?”
44008035	Gikenyo Filipo ochako tito ri go kwoŋ adech ma randik me; otito ri go Wach Maber mapa Yesu.
44008036	Munyo fuodi jowotho i royo, jotundo kama di pi, to jaserikale wacho ni, “Kole pi moro ee. Aŋo ma geŋan limo batisimo?”
44008037	[Filipo owacho ri go ni, “I nyalo limo batisimo ka iyeyo gi chunyin jye.” Ana go, “Ayeyo ni Yesu Kristo obedo Wuodi Were.”]
44008038	Jaserikale ooro jatich pere juko chawula; gikenyo jaryo no, Filipo kodi jaserikale jokidho i pi, to Filipo miyo go batisimo.
44008039	Munyo jowok i pi, Chuny Maleŋ pa Ruoth okwanyo Filipo. Joserikale odoko koneno go, to medere gi woth pere, munyo kisangala opoŋ i chunye.
44008040	Filipo opoyo munyo go nitye i Azoto; to wotho i tindi parom munyo fuonjo Wach Maber, chuka otundo Kaisareya.
44009001	Saulo oido fuodi medere i hongo no gi ywoyo wach ma bwoko gi neko jofuonjirok pa Ruoth. Okidho bongi jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar,
44009002	to kwayo balwa ma dhiro go i kalamo pa Joyudaya i Damasiko, ni ka onwaŋo joma luwo royo pa Ruoth kenyo, wonyali mako jo, chwo gi mon, to dwoko jo Yerusalem.
44009003	Munyo go fuodi oido ni royo kidho Damasiko, ma fuodi kotundo i tindi, lero owok i polo to umo go ni fungu.
44009004	Go ogore piny to winjo dwondi jo ma wacho ri go ni, “Saulo Saulo! Raŋo milwenyo kodan”?
44009005	Go openjo ni, “In i ŋa, Ruoth?” Dwondi jo no odwoko ni, “An Yesu m'ilwenyo gine.
44009006	To ayi malo ikidhi i tindi, kama ibino wacho rin iye gima inotimi”
44009007	I hongo no ji monwaŋo jowotho gi Saulo oido jochungo, mongoye wach ma jowacho; jowinjo dwondi jo no to jokoneno nyatoro.
44009008	Saulo oay malo kama onwaŋo opodh'iye to yawo waŋe, to konyalo neno gimoro. Gikenyo jomako chinge to jotero go Damasiko.
44009009	I hongo ma ndelo adek go konyalo neno gimoro, aka i hongo no go konyalo chiemo kosa madho gimoro.
44009010	Onwaŋo nitye i Damasiko jafuonjirok moro milwoŋo ni Ananiya. Ŋato olimo lek ma Ruoth owach'iye ri go ni, “Ananiya!” Odwoko ni, “Anika, Ruoth.”
44009011	Ruoth owacho ri go ni “Yikere ikidhi i Royo milwoŋo ni Nyatirtir, aka ipenji dhano ma wok Tarso milwoŋo ni Saulo i ot pa Yuda. Go nitye i kwayo pama won me.
44009012	Aka, i lek, go oneno dhano milwoŋo ni Ananiya munyo donjo to ketho chinge kwoŋe ŋey go wochaki neno kendo.”
44009013	Ananiya odwoko ni, “Ruoth, kole ji mathoth jotyeko luwo ran kwoŋ gikipiny marecho ma ŋato otyeko timo ri ji perin maleŋ ma Yerusalem.
44009014	Aka go obino Damasiko gi men ma jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar jomiyo go ma mako nyatoro jye ma yeyo i nyingin.”
44009015	Ruoth owacho ri go ni, “Kidhi, rupiri atyeko yero go wotiyi ran, ma miyo nyingan ŋeyirok bongi Jopath kodi kerin, kodi nyithindho pa Israel.
44009016	Aka abino nyutho go paka go ripo chandirok ran.”
44009017	Gikenyo Ananiya okidho, odonjo i ot to ketho chinge kwoŋ Saulo ka wacho ni, “Omera Saulo, Ruoth Yesu momenyere rin i royo munyo ibino ka, ooran nike inyali neno kendo ipoŋ gi Chuny Maleŋ.”
44009018	Piyo piyo gimoro ma chalo magambala ohale wok i waŋe to podho, to go chako neno kendo. Gikenyo go oay malo to imiyo go batisimo,
44009019	aka munyo otyeko chiemo, men pere odwoko. Saulo obedo ndelo manok gi jofuonjirok i Damasiko.
44009020	Go okidho nyatirtir i kalamo pa Joyudaya momore aka ochako fuonjo kwoŋ Yesu ka wacho ni, “Yesu obedo Wuodi Were.”
44009021	Ji jye ma jowinjo go jodhyer swa, aka wegi jopenjere ni, “Me k'aŋata oneko ji Yerusalem ma jotucho nyingi Yesu? Aka miti go onyo ameno kobino ka kodi atoŋa ma mako ji ma jotucho nyingi Yesu gi tweyo jo tero jo bongi jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar?”
44009022	To fuonji pa Saulo omedere bedo gi men loyo, aka tito pere ni Yesu obedo Kristo obedo mochwiny swa ma Joyudaya moido jonitye Damasiko jokonyalo dwoko go.
44009023	Munyo ndelo mathoth okadho, Joyudaya jochokere to joyiko paro ma neko Saulo;
44009024	to owachi ri go gima oido joyiko timo. Jonago jokuro go i waŋkach ma tindi Wor g'odyechieŋ ni jowoneki go.
44009025	To gi wor no, jomaluwo Saulo jokwanyo go to jowodho go gi i hoŋ ma kor ot i adita molyer gi thol.
44009026	Saulo okidho Yerusalem to temo makirok kodi jofuonjirok to jokonyalo yeyo nike go pama onyo bende olokere jafuonjirok, to jojye jolworo go ayino.
44009027	Gikenyo Barunaba obino okwanyo go to tero go bongi jomoor to tito ri jo paka Saulo ndir cha oneno Ruoth i royo to Ruoth luwo gine. Go bende owacho ri jo paka Saulo ofuonjo gi miseni i nyingi Yesu i tindi ma Damasiko.
44009028	Gikenyo Saulo obedo gi jo to wotho Yerusalem parom, munyo fuonjo gi miseni i nyingi Ruoth.
44009029	Go bende oluwo aka opyemo kodi Joyudaya ma joluwo Dhoyunani, to jotemo neko go.
44009030	Muny jomoyeyo joŋeyo gino, jotero Saulo yu Kaisareya to jodhiro go Tarso.
44009031	Gikenyo kitipa pa jomoyeyo i Yudeya gipi kodi Galileya kodi Samarya obedo gi hola ma syem. Jokonyere aka jodongo i welo ru kony pa Chuny Maleŋ, munyo jowotho i kwo ma lworo Were.
44009032	Paka Petro oido wotho i kabedo momore, ndelo moro go okidho lyewo ji ma jobedo Lida.
44009033	Kenyo go oromo gi dhano milwoŋo ni Ayineya, monwaŋo two nyaŋinya aka konyalo ay i kanindo oro aboro.
44009034	Petro owacho ri go ni, “Ayineya, Yesu Kristo bothin. Ayi malo iyiki kanindo perin.” Ayineya oay mayot.
44009035	Ji ma jobedo Lida kodi Saron joneno go, to jowire bongi Ruoth.
44009036	I Yopa onwaŋo nitye dhako moyeyo milwoŋo ni Tabisa, (Nyinge i Dhoyunani obedo Dokas, dwoŋ mere ni amudhe), moido oro hongo pere jye ma timo bero gi konyo jochandi.
44009037	I hongo no two omako go to tho. Olwok delkwoŋe to ipyelo i ot ma malo.
44009038	Paka Yopa oido kibor gi Lida, munyo jofuonjirok ma Yopa jowinjo ni Petro nitye Lida, jooro ji aryo bonge gi mikwenda me, “Mondo redi ibin.”
44009039	Gikenyo Petro oyikere to kidho bongi jo. Munyo go otundo, oter go i ot ma malo. Mon tho jye jothoko go munyo joywak aka jonyutho go satere gi kotere ma Dokas otimo munyo fodi kwo.
44009040	Petro oryemo jojye woko, aka oguro chonge to kwayo; aka owire kama di jatho to lwoŋo ni, “Tabisa, ayi malo!”
44009041	Petro otundo bonge to konyo go gi ay malo. Gikenyo Petro olwoŋo jomoyeyo kodi mon tho, to chwayo go makwo ri jo.
44009042	Wach me onyay i Yopa gipi, aka ji mathoth joyeyo Ruoth.
44009043	Petro obedo Yopa ndelo moromo kodi jajwayi pyendere milwoŋo ni Simon.
44010001	Onwaŋo nitye dhano i Kaisareya milwoŋo ni Kornelyo, jaserikale madwoŋ i lwak jolweny ma Roma milwoŋo ni kitipa pa Joitalya.
44010002	Go oido obedo jadin matek gi ot pere gi bee aka jolworo Were. Go oido miyo kony madit ri jochandi, aka onwaŋo kwayo Were noknok.
44010003	Dho kapa sawa abuŋwen odyechieŋ moro, go oneno chal momenyere ri go, monen'iye malaika pa Were munyo donjo to lwoŋo go ni, “Kornelyo!”
44010004	Go omoro waŋe kwoŋ malaika gi lworo aka owacho ni, “Aŋo jadwoŋ?” Ana malaika: “Were ojolo kwayo perin gi tich perin ma konyo ji, aka onyo opoyin.
44010005	Onyo ori jomogo i Yopa jowolwoŋi Simon ma nyinge man Petro.
44010006	Go obedo wendo pa Simon ma jajwayi pyendere ma bedo dho thengi wakawaka.”
44010007	Gikenyo malaika monwaŋo luwo gine okadho, aka Kornelyo olwoŋo jotich ma ot pere jaryo kodi jaserikale, ma bende jadin matek monwaŋo obedo achiel kwoŋ jokur pere.
44010008	Owacho ri jo gima otimere jye to oro jo Yopa.
44010009	Yawere mere kapa sawa auchiel modyechieŋ, munyo jonitye i woth pajo aka onwaŋo joriko Yopa, Petro oidho wi ot kwayo.
44010010	Gikenyo go ochako winjo kech to mito girachama; aka munyo fuodi itedo chiemo, ochako nur to neno chal momenyere ri go.
44010011	Oneno polo oyawere aka gimoro oloro mochalo suka malach m'ochar piny gi sonda mere aŋwen pa kidho umo piny.
44010012	I suka no onwaŋo nitye lee ma piny ma kite jye, gikipiny mamol gi kor gin piny kodi winyin ma malo.
44010013	Dwondi jo moro owacho ri go ni; “Ayi malo, Petro, ineki ichami!”
44010014	To Petro owacho ni, “Kameno, Ruoth! Fuodi yado akichamo gimoro jye mitero paka gima kichar, kosa ma kolony.”
44010015	Dwondi jo no odoko oluwo gine ni, “Gima Were otyeko lonyo, ikiri ilwoŋo ni gima kichar.”
44010016	Gime otimere didek to idwoko gino i polo.
44010017	Munyo Petro fuodi uro dwoŋ chal ma go oneno no, ji ma Kornelyo ooro rango kama ot pa Simon nitye iye jotundo kenyo to jochungo dho waŋkach.
44010018	Jolwoŋo gi dwondi jo ma malo to jopenjo ni, “Nitye wendo moro ka ma nyinge Simon Petro?”
44010019	Petro oido fuodi temo niaŋ i dwoŋ chal ma go oneno no to Chuny Maleŋ wacho ri go ni, “Kole nitye ji adek ka ma jorangin.
44010020	Amomiyo yikere ilor, aka ikiri imindaminda ma ikikadho gi jo, rupiri aŋata aoro jo.”
44010021	Gikenyo Petro oloro to wacho ri jo ni, “Ani a ŋata wirango. Wibino raŋo?”
44010022	Jowacho ni, “Jaserikale madwoŋ milwoŋo ni Kornelyo ama ooro wan. Go obedo ŋataber ma lamo Were aka Joyudaya joworo go swa. Achiel kwoŋ jomalaika pa Were owacho ri go nike wolwoŋin i ot pere, wonyali winjo gima inowachi.”
44010023	Petro orwako jono i ot to jonindo kenyo. Yawere mere go oyikere to kadho gi jo; aka jowote mogo ma jowok Yopa bende jokadho gine.
44010024	Yawere mere jotundo Kaisareya kama Kornelyo oido kur'iye go, kanyachiel gi wade pere gi merin pere ma go olwoŋo.
44010025	Munyo Petro nyaka donjo i ot, Kornelyo oromo gine, to podho dho tyende gi bwonirok.
44010026	Petro owacho ri go woay malo. Owacho ni, “Chungi, kole abende adhano adhana.”
44010027	Petro omedere gi luwo kodi Kornelyo munyo donjo i ot, kama onwaŋ'iye ji mathoth ma jochokere.
44010028	Owacho ri jo ni, “Wiwegi wiŋeyo maber nike din pa Jayudaya kiyey go riwirok kodi Jopath. To Were otyeko nyuthan ni akir ater dhano moro jye paka jakichar kosa ni kolony.
44010029	Amomiyo munyo ioro ji lwoŋan abino mongoye pyem. Onyo wach ran gima omiyo ilwoŋan.”
44010030	Kornelyo owacho ni, “Ndelo aŋwen mokadho onwaŋo akwayo i ot paran sawa abuŋwen modyechieŋ. Piyo piyo dhano morukere i ruk ma minyin ochungo ruwaŋan.
44010031	Owacho ni, ‘Kornelyo! Were owinjo kwayo perin, aka opoyo tich perin ma konyo ji.
44010032	Ori dhano moro Yopa wolwoŋi jal milwon ni Simon Petro ma obedo wendo pecho pa Simon jajwayi pyendere, ma bedo dho thengi wakawaka!’
44010033	Amomiyo aoro ji lwoŋin mayot, aka itimo maber bino. Pama onyo wajojye wani ka i nyim Were, wakuro winjo gimoro jye ma Ruoth oorin wacho.”
44010034	Petro ochako luwo ni, “Onyo pama aneno adyeri ni Were tero dhano jye marom.
44010035	Nyatoro jye ma lworo go aka timo gimotire, go jolo mongoye tito nono pere.
44010036	Wiŋeyo fuonji ma go odhiro ri ji ma Israel, ma tito Wach Maber ma kelo syem i Yesu Kristo, mobedo Ruoth pa ji jye.
44010037	Wiŋeyo gimadwoŋ motimere i Yudeya parom, chako Galileya, chako kwoŋ batisimo ma Yohana ofuonjo:
44010038	paka Were okonjo kwoŋ Yesu ma Nazareth Chuny Maleŋ kodi men; paka go okidho kamoro jye munyo timo bero gi botho jomatwo jye monwaŋo jonitye i achanda pa jwogi, rupiri Were oido ni gi go.
44010039	Wabedo jokony ma joŋeyo gimoro jye ma go otimo i piny Yudeya kodi i Yerusalem. Joneko go munyo joguro go kwoŋ musalaba.
44010040	To Were ochierino go kwoŋ jomotho i ndelo maradek, to miyo go menyere ri ji.
44010041	Ji jye jokoneno go, to wan ayino ma wabedo jokony ma Were otyeko yero. Wachiemo odoko waoro giramadha kanyachiel gine munyo Were otyeko chierino go kwoŋ jomotho.
44010042	Aka go ooro wan fuonjo ji Wach Maber, gi nyutho jo kamaler nike go a ŋata Were oketho thumo banja pa jomakwo gi jomotho.
44010043	Jotuchi wach Were jye joluwo kwoŋe, munyo jowacho ni nyatoro jye moyeyi go ibino chwako gimarecho pere gi men ma nyingi go.”
44010044	Munyo Petro fuodi luwo, Chuny Maleŋ oloro kwoŋ jojye monwaŋo jochiko ithi jo jowinjo fuonji.
44010045	Joyudaya ma joyeyo ma jobino wok Jopa gi Petro jodhyer ni Were okonjo mich pere ma Chuny Maleŋ kwoŋ Jopath bende.
44010046	Ato jowinjo munyo joluwo i dhudhok manyien ma nyakare ka jopako dwoŋ pa Were. Aka Petro owacho ni,
44010047	“Nitye ŋata nyalo geŋo jome limo batisimo ma pi mato bende jotyeko limo Chuny Maleŋ paka wan?”
44010048	Gikenyo go ooro jo ni jowolimi batisimo i nyingi Yesu Kristo. Rumachien jokwayo Petro gin ni jowobediye gi jo ndelo ma romo.
44011001	Jomoor kodi wadi jo ma Yudeya pa rom jowinjo ni Jopath bende jojolo wach pa Were.
44011002	Munyo Petro okidho Yerusalem, ji monwaŋo joyenyo ni Jopath bende jowothumere jogesa ni,
44011003	“Iraŋo wikidho bongi Jopath ma jokuthumere to wichiemo kir gi jo!”
44011004	Gikenyo Petro otito ri jo thenethene ma gima otimere woki i chakirok mere ama:
44011005	“An onwaŋo anitye ikwayo i tindi ma Yopa, to aneno gimoro munyo loro piny wok i polo mochalo suka mapando micharo piny kareno omaki thenge aŋwen jye to tundo bongan.
44011006	Akaŋasa iye maber to aneno lee ma nyatyende aŋwen, kodi ogwange, kodi gikipiny ma mol gi kor gin kodi winyin ma malo.
44011007	Aka awinjo dwondi jo moro mowacho ran ni, ‘Petro, ayi malo, neki jo ichami!’
44011008	To awacho ni, ‘Kameno Ruoth! Ongoye chiemo makichar kosa ma kolony motyeko donjo i dhokan.’
44011009	Dwondi jo mowok i polo no oluwo kendo ni, ‘Gima Were otyeko lonyo, ikiri ilwoŋo ni gimakichar.’
44011010	Gime otimere didek, aka rumachien oywayi to idwoko i polo.
44011011	I hongo no won ama ji mogo adek m'oor bongan wok Kaisareya jotundo i ot monwaŋo abed'iye.
44011012	Chuny Maleŋ owacho ran ni akidhi gi jono mongoye yero. Joma joyeyo auchiel me bende jowotho kodan kir i Kaisareya, to wajojye wadonjo i ot pa Kornelyo.
44011013	Go owacho ri wan paka oneno malaika moro ochungo i ot pere to wacho ri go ni, ‘Ori dhano Yopa wolwoŋi Simon ma nyinge Petro.
44011014	Go bino kelo ri win wach ma bino miyin kodi joodin jye limo both.’
44011015	Aka munyo achako luwo, Chuny Maleŋ oloro ri jo paka chango oloro ri wan i kachako.
44011016	Gikenyo apoyo gima Ruoth ndir cha owacho ni, ‘Yohana omiyo win batisimo gi pi to wibino limo batisimo gi Chuny Maleŋ.’
44011017	Onyo k'inen Were omiyo Jopath no bende mich achiel ma go omiyo wan munyo wayeyo Ruoth Yesu Kristo, onyo an aŋa, ma d'atem juko Were!”
44011018	Munyo jowinjo gime, joliŋ pyem, to jopako Were munyo jowacho ni, “Kere Were otyeko miyo Jopath bende hongo ma ŋuto gi bedo gi kwo.”
44011019	Jomoyeyo jokedhere ru lweny mobedo munyo oneki Sitefano. Jomegi jokidho kir yu Fonisya kodi Sipuro kodi Antyok munyo jotito mikwenda ri Joyudaya kende.
44011020	Aka jomoyeyo megi, ji ma jowok Sipuro kodi Sireno jokidho Antyok to jotito ri Joyunani mikwenda no bende, munyo jofuonjo jo Wach Maber kwoŋ Ruoth Yesu.
44011021	Chingi Ruoth onwaŋo ni gi jo, aka ji mathoth joyeyo to jowire bongi Ruoth.
44011022	Wach me otundo i kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Yerusalem to jooro Barunaba yu Antyok.
44011023	Munyo go otundo to neno ŋono pa Were moido ni kenyo, osangala to kwayo jojye ni jowobedi gi genirok kodi adyeri i waŋ Ruoth gi ridho madwoŋ;
44011024	ata Barunaba onwaŋo obedo dhano maber, mopoŋ gi Chuny Maleŋ kodi yeyo. Aka ji mathoth swa jomedere i kitipa ji pa Ruoth.
44011025	Gikenyo Barunaba okidho Tarso rango Saulo.
44011026	Munyo onwaŋo go, okelo go Antyok. I hongo ma romo oro gipi jaryo me joromo gi kitipa pa jomoyeyo, to jofuonjo ji madit swa. I Antyok me ama open lwoŋ'iye jofuonjirok ni Jokristo.
44011027	I kare no ama jotuchi wach Were megi jobin'iye Antyok wok Yerusalem.
44011028	Achiel kwoŋ jo, ma nyinge Agabo, ochungo malo gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ, to luwo kwoŋ kech madwoŋ ma bino bedo to swana piny gipi. (Kech no obino i adhum pa Klaudyo.)
44011029	Jofuonjirok joridho ni kis dhano kwoŋ jo ripo dhiro kony ri wadi jo ma Yudeya paka go nyalo.
44011030	Jotimo ameno, to jodhiro pesa ri jotel ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo munyo luwo gi i chingi Barunaba gi Saulo.
44012001	I hongo no Herode mobedo kere ochako lweny gi jomegi ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo.
44012002	Go owodho or to ineko Yakobo, omin Yohana, g'abor.
44012003	Munyo oneno ni gino osangala Joyudaya, go omedere oro ji mako Petro bende. (Gime otimere i ndir ma kalima ma Mugat ma Bu Thow.)
44012004	Munyo otyek mako ri go Petro, oketho go i od twech, to ketho go i chingi bwora aŋwen ma joserikale aŋwen aŋwen, kuro go. Herode oido oyiko wodho go kenyo wowinji banja pere ka kalima ma Kadho orumo.
44012005	Ameno Petro obedo i od twech; to ji ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo onwaŋo jokwayo Were ri go gi geregere madit.
44012006	Wor no won ma Herode onwaŋo kidho wodh'iye go ri ji, Petro onwaŋo nindo i dyer jokur aryo kareno otwey go g'atege aryo, aka jokur megi oido jonitye kir dho waŋkach ma od twech.
44012007	Piyo piyo malaika pa Ruoth omenyere, to lero meny i od twech. Malaika no ogwelo buti Petro, oyengo go to chiewo go aka owacho ni, “Kwakere! Ayi malo!” Gikenyo won to atege ma chinge budhere woko.
44012008	To malaika wacho ri go ni, “Rukere irwaki war perin.” Petro otimo ameno, to malaika wacho ni, “Ere ruki kabut perin iluwan.”
44012009	Petro oluwo go to jowok i od twech to go koŋeyo kada ni gima malaika no onwaŋo timo obedo adyeri; oparo nike kono manago menyirok moro ama go onyo neno.
44012010	Jokalo jokur marapena gi mararyo, to jotundo i waŋkach ma nyweny ma royo ma kidho yu tindi. Waŋkach no won oyawere kende ri jo, to jowok woko i royo. Piyo piyo to malaika no weyo Petro kenyo kende.
44012011	Gikenyo Petro nyaka oniaŋ kwoŋ gima owok timirok ri go, to wacho ni, “Nyaka onyo aŋeyo ni gime obedo adyeri! Ruoth ooro malaika pere wobothan kwoŋ men pa Herode kodi kwoŋ gikipiny jye ma Joyudaya oido jochano timo ran.”
44012012	Munyo otyeko niaŋ ameno, okidho pecho pa Marya min Yohana ma nyinge man Marko. Ji mathoth onwaŋo jochokere kenyo jokwayo.
44012013	Petro ogudo thigo ma woko to jatich ma nyako milwoŋo ni Roda bino.
44012014	To munyo go oniaŋ ni obedo dwondi Petro, ogik i ot gi ŋwech ma koyawo thigo ru kisangala madit, to wacho ri jo paka Petro ochungo woko i waŋkach.
44012015	Jowacho ri go ni, “Neko omakin!” Aka munyo go omedo wacho nike obedo adyeri, jodwoko ni, “Kono meno malaika pere ayin.”
44012016	I hongo no Petro omedo gudo thigo. Rumachien joyawo thigo aka munyo joneno go jodhyer swa.
44012017	Go onyutho jo gi chinge ni jowoliŋi, aka otito ri jo paka Ruoth owodho go i od twech. Owacho ni, “Wachi win ri Yakobo kodi jomoyeyo jye.” Gikenyo oweyo jo to kadho kaman.
44012018	Yawere mere odikini, ruwirok madwoŋ obedo i dyer jokur ma od twech ri gima otimo Petro.
44012019	Munyo Herode owodho or ma rango go, to jokonyalo nwaŋo go, oyenyo ni wopenji jokur to wodho or ni woneki jo. Rumachien Herode oay wok i Yudeya to kidho wochowi hongo moro yu Kaisareya.
44012020	Herode onwaŋo yado ni gi dhaw moro kodi ji ma Tire kodi Sidon; ameno jokidho bonge i muma neno go. Jono kutho jotelo mako mere gi Blasto, jal moido kuro chiel pa kere. Gikenyo nyaka jokidho bongi Herode to jokwayo go syem, rupiri piny pajo onwaŋo limo chiemo ma wok i piny pa kere no.
44012021	I ndelo moyik, Herode orwako ruk pere madhum, to bedo wi kom pere madhum, to chako luwo gi jo.
44012022	Gikenyo ji jokoko ni, “Me ki dwondi dhano ama luwo, to were moro ayin!”
44012023	Piyo piyo malaika pa Ruoth ogoyo Herode matek, rupiri go komiyo Were dwoŋ. Aka kudin ochamo go to tho.
44012024	To wach pa Were omedo nyay gi dongo.
44012025	Munyo Barunaba gi Saulo jochowo timo tich pajo, jogik yu Yerusalem kodi Yohana gi Marko.
44013001	I kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Antyok, oido nitye jotuchi wach Were mogo kodi jofuonji: Barunaba, Simeyo (milwoŋo ni Ma chol), Lusyo (ma wok Sireno), Manaen (modongo pa gavana Herode), kodi Saulo.
44013002	Ndelo moro munyo jolamo Ruoth aka joriyo kech, Chuny Maleŋ owacho ri jo ni, “Kethi ran win gichien Barunaba kodi Saulo, jowotimi tich ma alwoŋ'iye jo.”
44013003	Munyo jotyeko riyo kech kodi kwayo, joketho chingi gin kwoŋ jo to jodhiro jo kadho tich.
44013004	Munyo Chuny Maleŋ otyeko oro Barunaba gi Saulo, jokidho yu Selusya aka jochiewere wok kenyo to jokidho i kigoda ma Sipuro.
44013005	Munyo jotundo Salamis, jofuonjo wach pa Were I kalamo pa Joyudaya. Yohana Marko oido konyo jo i tich.
44013006	Jojye jochiewere yu loka i kigoda ma Pafo, kama jorom'iye gi jathyeth moro ma nyinge Bar Yesu, Jayudaya mobedo jatuchi wach matwodo.
44013007	Go oido tiyo ri gavana ma kigoda no, Serigio Paulo, monwaŋo obedo ŋataryek swa. Gavana no olwoŋo Barunaba kodi Saulo bonge rupiri oido mito winjo Wach pa Were.
44013008	To Elima jathyeth (meno a dwoŋ nyinge) opyemo gi jo ka temo ywayo woko gavana i yeyo.
44013009	Gikenyo Chuny Maleŋ opoŋ kwoŋ Saulo, ma bende oŋeyere ni Paulo, to ŋiyo waŋ jathyeth no tirtir
44013010	to wacho ni, “In wuodi pa jwogi, m'ibedo jakwor gi gimoro jye motire, aka imore kodi thenethene marecho ma twodo, kere ikileweyo wiro adyeri pa Ruoth i twodo?
44013011	Chingi Ruoth eno bino podho kwoŋin pama; waŋin bino tho, aka ikonen lero pa waŋchieŋ chowo hongo moro.” Piyo piyo no Elima owinjo munyo tor machol umo waŋe, to chako woth ariwa ariwa munyo temo nwaŋo dhano m'omaki chinge to telo go royo.
44013012	Gavana oyeyo munyo oneno gimotimere no; aka odhyer swa kwoŋ fuonji pa Ruoth.
44013013	Gikenyo Paulo kodi wadi jochiewere wok Pafo to jokidho yu Paga i adech ma Panfilya kama Yohana Marko owey'iye jo to gik yu Yerusalem.
44013014	Jomedere gi woth wok Paga to jokidho Antyok ma Pisidya; aka i ndelo ma Sabato jodonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya to jobedo piny.
44013015	Munyo kisoma mowok i Chik pa Musa kodi i ndiiko pa jotuchi wach Were orumo, jotel ma kalamo pa Joyudaya jodhiro ri jo mikwenda ni, “Wutimin wan, luwi win ye gi ji ka winitye gi wach ma medo gine jo men.”
44013016	Paulo ochungo, to miyo jo ranyuth gi chinge to chako luwo ni, “Joisrael jowotan, kodi Jopath jye ma jolamo Were, winji win!
44013017	Were pa ji ma Israel oyero kwarere mawan, to miyo nono pajo bedo madwoŋ i ndir ma jobed'iye i piny Misir. Were owodho jo wok Misir gi men pere moasere,
44013018	aka i hongo ma oro pyero aŋwen ofamba gi jo i dyer thim.
44013019	Go oreyo woko nonin abiryo i piny ma Kanan to loko ji pere wegi piny no chowo
44013020	hongo ma oro chiegin miya aŋwen gi pyero abich. Rumachien omiyo jo jothumi banjin, chuka tundo ndir pa Samwir jatuchi wach Were.
44013021	Aka munyo jokwayo kere, Were omiyo jo Saulo, wuodi pa Kis, janono pa Benjamin, bedo kere pajo ma oro pyero aŋwen.
44013022	Munyo Were otyeko kwanyo go woko, oloko Daudi kere pajo. Me a gima Were oluwo kwoŋe: ‘Anwaŋo ni Daudi wuodi pa Yese, obedo kiti dhano ma amito, ŋata bino timo gimoro jye ma ayenyo ni wotimi.’
44013023	Yesu, achiel kwoŋ nyikway Daudi, a ŋata Were oloko Jaboth pa ji ma Israel paka chango ochiko.
44013024	Ma fuodi Yesu kobino, Yohana ofuonjo ji jye ma Israel nike jowoŋuti gimarecho pajo womiy jo batisimo.
44013025	Aka munyo Yohana oido chiegin chowo tich pere, openjo ji ni, ‘Wiparo nike an a ŋa? Akibedo ŋata wikuro. To neni win, go luwan chien, aka akiripi kada lunyo war ma tyende.’
44013026	“Wutimera, nyikway Ibrayimu, kodi Jopath jye ma ka ma jolamo Were: fuonji ma mako kwoŋ both me otyek dhiro ri wan!
44013027	Kole ji ma Yerusalem kodi jotel pajo jokoŋeyo nike go a Jaboth, aka jokoniaŋ kada wach pa jotuchi wach Were misoma i kis Sabato. Kada ameno wach pa jotuchi wach Were otundo i kare munyo jothumo ri Yesu banja ma tho.
44013028	Aka kada jokonwaŋo atoŋa ma thumo ri go banja ma tho, jye fuodi jokwayo Pilato nike woneki go.
44013029	Aka munyo jotyeko timo gimoro jye ma Ndiiko Maleŋ luwo kwoŋe, jogamo go kwoŋ musalaba to joketho go i kalyel.
44013030	To Were ochierino go kwoŋ jomotho,
44013031	aka i ndelo madit onyuthere ri joma yado jowotho gine woki i Galileya tundo Yerusalem. Jono ama onyo pama jobedo jokony i wach pere i waŋ ji ma Israel.
44013032	Aka onyo bende wakelo ri win Wach Maber no.
44013033	Gima Were ochiko kwarere mawan nike d'otimo, pama go otyeko timo ri wan ma wabedo nyikway jo, munyo ochierino Yesu paka ondik i Zabul mararyo ni, ‘In Wuodan, konon alokere Benin.’
44013034	Aka me a gima Were owacho kwoŋ chierino pere kwoŋ jomotho ma odoko kogiki i topo: ‘Abino miyin silwany maleŋ ma bu kiganagana ma chango achiko Daudi.’
44013035	Aka adyeri go owacho kaman ni, ‘Ikoyey jatich perin wotopi.’
44013036	Kole Daudi oketho atoŋa pa Were i tim i ndir pere; rumachien go otho to iyiko chiegin gi kwarere pere, aka otho to top woko.
44013037	To ŋata Were ochierino kwoŋ jomotho konyalo top woko.
44013038	Ri ameno wutimere, wijojye wiripo ŋeyo adyeri nike fuonji kwoŋ chwako gimarecho ma ifuonjo win wok bongi Yesu;
44013039	Aka nyatoro jye ma yeyo i go igonyo go woko kwoŋ gimarach ma Chik pa Musa onwaŋo kinyal gonyo win kwoŋe.
44013040	Amomiyo gwokere win, ŋey gima jotuchi wach Were jowacho wokiri wotimere ri win ni:
44013041	‘Neni win, wijochay! Dhyeri win witho; rupiri aletimo tich mogo i ndir mewin won, to wikoyey tich no kada moro otem tito ri win!’ ”
44013042	Munyo Paulo kodi Barunaba oido jokidho wok i kalamo pa Joyudaya, okway jo ni jowogiki kendo i Sabato ma luwo aka jowomedi wacho ri jo kwoŋ gikipiny me.
44013043	Munyo ji jotyeko eye i romo, Joyudaya mathoth kodi Jopath ma jowire i din pa Joyudaya joluwo Paulo gi Barunaba. Jomoor joluwo gi jo aka jomedo jo miseni nike jowomedere i ŋono pa Were.
44013044	I Sabato ma luwo, chiegin kis dhano obino wok i tindi winjo wach pa Were.
44013045	Munyo Joyudaya joneno kweth ji, nyieko omako jo; jopyemo gi gima Paulo oido wacho aka joyeto kir go.
44013046	To Paulo kodi Barunaba jomedo luwo pajo gi miseni ni, “Oido yenyere ni wach pa Were wopen tito ri win ayino. To paka wikijol, aka wikiter i kwo mewin paka joma ripere limo kwo makirum, waleweyo win to wakidho bongi Jopath.
44013047	Kole meno a or ma Ruoth omiyo wan munyo owacho ni, ‘Aketho win paka lero pa Jopath, ni winyali kelo both ri piny gipi.’ ”
44013048	Munyo Jopath jowinjo gime josangala aka jopako fuonji pa Ruoth. Aka joma oido oyer ri kwo makirum jolokere jomoyeyo.
44013049	Wach pa Were onyay iye jye i adech no.
44013050	To Joyudaya josigila jotel pa ji i tindi kodi mon pa Jopath ma kitipa ma malo ma onwaŋo jolamo Were. Gikenyo jochako lweny gi Paulo kodi Barunaba to joryemo jo woko i adech no.
44013051	Jomoor joteŋo lowo ma par tyendi gin munyo jokwoŋo jo to jokadho yu Ikoniam.
44013052	Jofuonjirok ma Antyok jopoŋ gi kisangala i chuny jo kanyachiel gi Chuny Maleŋ.
44014001	Gima pameno bende otimere Ikoniam: Paulo kodi Barunaba jodonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya to joluwo wach momiyo Joyudaya kodi Joyunani mathoth joyeyo.
44014002	To Joyudaya ma jokonyalo yeyo josigila Jopath to joruwo paro pajo jowoeye kwoŋ jomoyeyo no.
44014003	Jomoor jobedo kenyo hongo malach. Joluwo gi miseni kwoŋ Ruoth, moridho ni fuonji pajo kwoŋ ŋono pere oido obedo adyeri munyo miyo jo men ma timo ranyuth kodi gidhyer.
44014004	To kitipa pa ji i tindi otyakere: jomegi jodok yu thenge pa Joyudaya, joman yu thenge pa jomoor.
44014005	Gikenyo Jopath kodi Joyudaya, kanyachiel gi jodhum pajo, joyiko lweny kodi jomoor gi goyo jo gi telin.
44014006	Munyo jomoor jolimo ŋeyo i wach no, joringo yu Listura kodi Derube, tindin ma Likonia, kodi i adech mothoko jo.
44014007	Kenyo ama jofuonjiye Wach Maber no.
44014008	Onwaŋo nitye nyatoro i Listura ma tyende jye oŋol; go oido oŋol wok i nywolirok pere aka konyalo woth.
44014009	Go onwaŋo obedo piny ochiko ithe winjo wach pa Paulo. Gikenyo Paulo oneno go tirtir aka munyo oneno nike ŋato ni gi yeyo aka nyalo limo both,
44014010	owacho ri go gi dwonde madwoŋ ni, “Ayi malo i chungi m'itire!” Ŋato oay malo arwat to chako thokirok gi woth.
44014011	Munyo muma ji oneno gima Paulo otimo, jochako koko i dhudhok Likonia pajo ni, “Werin jolokere ji aka joloro bongi wan!”
44014012	Jomiyo Barunaba nyinge ni Zeus, aka Paulo ni Hemes, rupiri go ama oluwo.
44014013	Gikenyo jachowirok i migam pa were Zeus, ma migam pere oido nitye dho tindi, okelo thwondhe mogo kodi thiwi ajwoka i waŋkach munyo go kanyachiel kodi ji ma tindi no onwaŋo jomito timo chowirok ri jomoor.
44014014	Munyo Paulo gi Barunaba jowinjo gima onwaŋo jokidho timo, joyecho nengin pajo to joringo i dyer muma ji munyo jokoko ni,
44014015	“Jume, raŋo ma witimo gime? Wabende wabedo ji paka win! Wanitye ka i atoŋa ma tito ri win Wach Maber, kwanyo win woko kwoŋ gikipiny me mongoye kony bongi Were Makwo, mochweyo polo gi piny, nam kodi gikipiny jye mani iye.
44014016	I ndir mokadho go oweyo nonin jye luwo yo pajo wegi;
44014017	to kada ameno go kodoŋ nono mongoye gima nyutho ni go nitye, rupiri go onyuthere ndir jye i gikipiny mabeyo ma go timo: go miyo win koth wok i polo kodi chiemo mipidho i hongo motire; go miyo win chiemo aka poŋo kisangala i chuny win.”
44014018	To kada joluwo kweth wach me, jye jomoor jokonyalo i yoto juko jono chowirok ri jo.
44014019	Joyudaya mogo jowok yu Antyok ma Pisidya kodi Yu Ikoniam; aka munyo jochowo ywayo ji yu thenge pajo, jogoyo Paulo gi telin, joywayo go, to jowodho go woko ma tindi munyo joparo nike go otyeko tho.
44014020	To munyo jomoyeyo jochokere jothoko go, oay malo to gik i tindi. Yawere mere go kodi Barunaba jokadho yu Derube.
44014021	Paulo kodi Barunaba jofuonjo Wach Maber i Derube to jolimo jofuonjirok mathoth. Gikenyo jogik Listura, kodi Ikoniam, kodi Antyok ma Pisidya.
44014022	Jomedo jomoyeyo meni to jomedo jo miseni nike jowochwire i yeyo. Jofuonjo ni, “Waripo donjo i Ker pa Were munyo waluwo i teko madit.”
44014023	Munyo jotyeko ketho jotel i kis kitipa pa jomayeyo gi kwayo kodi riyo kech, joketho jo i chingi Ruoth ma oido joketho geno pajo kwoŋe.
44014024	Munyo jochowo woth i adech ma Pisidya, jokidho yu Panfilya.
44014025	Jofuonjo i Paga to joloro Atalya.
44014026	Aka wok kenyo jochiewere to jogik Antyok, kama ndir cha oketh'iye jo gichien ri Were i kur ma ŋono pere kwoŋ tich ma oido jochowo me.
44014027	Munyo jotundo Antyok, jochoko ji ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo kanyachiel to jowacho ri jo gimoro jye ma Were otimo gi jo; kendo paka onyo oyawo royo ri Jopath ma yeyo.
44014028	Jotyeko kenyo hongo malach gi jomoyeyo.
44015001	Nitye jomogo ma jowok Yudeya to jobino Antyok to jochako fuonjo jomoyeyo ni, “Wikinyal limo both kwanyo woko ka withumere paka Chik pa Musa wacho.”
44015002	Paulo kodi Barunaba jobedo gi pyem mager tektek gi jo kwoŋ gime; gikenyo oridhi ni Paulo kodi Barunaba kodi joman ma Antyok jowokidhi Yerusalem jowoneni jomoor kodi jotel ma kitipin kwoŋ wach me.
44015003	Paka kitipa pa jomoyeyo ooro jo, joluwo yu Fonisya kodi Samarya to jowacho ri jo paka Jopath bende jowire bongi Were; wach me okelo kisangala madwoŋ ri jomoyeyo jye.
44015004	Munyo jotundo Yerusalem, kitipa pa jomoyeyo kodi jomoor kodi jotel ma kitipin jye jojolo jo maber, to jowacho ri jo gimoro jye ma Were otimo ri jo.
44015005	To jomoyeyo megi moido jonitye i kweth pa Jofarisayo jochungo to jowacho ni, “Mitere wothum Jopath aka wowachi ri jo mako Chik pa Musa.”
44015006	Gikenyo jomoor kodi jotel ma kitipin, joromo kanyachiel paro kwoŋ wach me.
44015007	Rumachien munyo pyem okadho kamabor, Petro ochungo to wacho ni, “Wutimera, wiŋeyo nike yu chien koro Were oyeran i dyer win fuonjo Jopath Wach Maber, nike jowonyali winjo jowoyeyi.
44015008	Aka Were, moŋeyo chuny ji, onyutho paka ojolo Jopath munyo bende omiyo jo Chuny Maleŋ, paka otimo gi wan.
44015009	Go kopoko wan gi jo; aka ochwako gimarecho pajo chungo kwoŋ yeyo pajo.
44015010	Amomiyo, raŋo ma wimito temo Were mawan munyo wiyimo ri jomoyeyo okol i goki jo ma kada kwarere wan kosa wawegi wakinyal tiŋo?
44015011	Be! Kole wayeyo ni wabino limo both kwoŋ ŋono pa Ruoth Yesu, paka jo bende.”
44015012	Gikenyo jomochokere jye joliŋ to jowinjo Barunaba kodi Paulo munyo jonuŋanuŋa ri ji giraura jye kodi gikipiny ma kelo dhyer ma Were otimo i dyer Jopath.
44015013	Munyo jochowo luwo, Yakobo oluwo malo ni, “Winjan win, wutimera!
44015014	Simon owok tito ri wan paka Were okutho onyutho paka dewo kwoŋ Jopath munyo kwanyo i dyer jo ji ma jowobedi apere won.
44015015	Kole wach pa jotuchi wach Were makere swa gi me. Paka ndiiko wacho ni,
44015016	‘Rumachien abino dwoko, apaka Ruoth wacho, aka abino gero kendo ot pa Daudi mopodho. Abino gero kamonyiekere jye kendo.
44015017	Aka ŋey ji man jye jobino rango Ruoth, jo kodi ji ma nonin jye milwoŋo gi nyingan.
44015018	Ruoth, momiyo gime oŋeyere wok chon ama owacho ameno.’
44015019	“Amomiyo aparo ni wakiripi chando Jopath ma jowire bongi Were;
44015020	kuchiel waripo ndiko balwa ma chiero jo lamo chal ma kichar kosa timo kidakana kosa chamo gimodey kosa remo moro jye kosa chiemo moro jye ma kolony ayin.
44015021	Kole Chik pa Musa otyek kisoma hongo malach i kalamo pa Joyudaya momore i Sabato jye, aka wach pere ifuonjo i tindi jye.”
44015022	Gikenyo jomoor kodi jotel ma kitipin pa jomoyeyo, kanyachiel gi kitipa pa jomoyeyo gipi joridho yero ji mogo i kitipa gi dhiro jo Antyok kodi Paulo gi Barunaba. Joyero Yuda milwoŋo ni Barsaba kodi Sila, ji aryo ma jomoyeyo jomiyo dwoŋ swa.
44015023	Jodhiro jono gi balwa me: “Wan jomoyeyo jowot win, ma joman jomoor aka joman jotel ma kitipin pa jomoyeyo, wadhiro moth ri jomoyeyo ma Jopath ma Antyok kodi Sirya kodi Silisya.
44015024	Watyeko winjo paka ji megi i kitipa mawan jobino koro to jokwinyo win gi luwo pajo mato wakifuonjo jo ni jowotimi ameno.
44015025	Amomiyo watyeko romo kanyachiel aka wajojye wayeyere yero jomikwenda mogo to wadhiro jo ri win. Jobino kanyachiel gi merin mawan Barunaba gi Paulo,
44015026	chwo ma jojala kwo pajo i tich ri Ruoth Yesu Kristo.
44015027	Amomiyo wadhiro ri win Yuda kodi Sila, ma wegi jobino wacho ri win gikipiny ma wandiko ri win.
44015028	Ato oneno ri Chuny Maleŋ kodi wan ni ber wakiri waturi win gi byeto kwanyo woko or me kende:
44015029	Wikiri wichami gima ochow gine jwogi; wikiri wichami remo; wikiri wichami lee modey; aka kure win kwoŋ kite ma kidakana. Wibino timo maber ka wikure kwoŋ gikipiny me. Kutho win.”
44015030	Jooro jomikwenda no to jokidho Antyok, kama jochok'iye kitipa pa jomoyeyo jye to jomiyo jo balwa no.
44015031	Munyo ji josoma balwa no, kisangala opoŋ i chuny jo ru mikwenda madwoko men.
44015032	Yuda kodi Sila, monwaŋo bende jotuchi wach Were, joluwo ma hongo malach kodi jomoyeyo no munyo jomedo jo men kendo jodwoko chuny jo.
44015033	Munyo jochowo hongo moro kenyo, jomoyeyo josewila jo gi syem, to jogik bongi jomoor.
44015034	[To Sila oridho paro ma doŋ kenyo.]
44015035	Paulo kodi Barunaba jochowo hongo moro i Antyok kanyachiel gi joman mathoth munyo jofuonjo wach pa Ruoth.
44015036	Rumachien Paulo owacho ri Barunaba ni, “Weyi wagiki walyewi wutimegi wan i tindi jye ma watyeko fuonj'iye Wach pa Were, aka wanen paka jonitye.”
44015037	Barunaba onwaŋo yenyo ni jowokadhi gi Yohana Marko bende,
44015038	to Paulo oparo ni jokiripi kadho gine, rupiri ndir cha go kobedo gi jo kir i giki tich pajo, to owire to weyo jo i Panfilya.
44015039	Jobedo gi pyem matek wegi kendigin, to jopokere. Gikenyo Barunaba okwanyo Marko to jochiewere jochomo yu Sipuro,
44015040	to Paulo oyero Sila to jokadho kareno jomoyeyo joketho go i kur ma ŋono pa Were.
44015041	Go oluwo yu Sirya kodi Sisilya, munyo jomedo kitipa pa jomoyeyo men.
44016001	Paulo ochomo yu Derube gi Listura. Jafuonjirok moro ma nyinge Timotheyo oido ni kenyo; go oido obedo wuodi pa dhakodwoŋ moro ma Jayudaya moyeyo, to bamere oido obedo Jayunani.
44016002	Jomoyeyo jye ma Listura kodi Ikoniam onwaŋo joluwo maber kwoŋ Timotheyo.
44016003	Paulo oyenyo kidho gi Timotheyo, ameno to kutho thumo go. Go otimo ameno rupiri Joyudaya makenyo jye oido joŋeyo ni baa Timotheyo obedo Jayunani.
44016004	Munyo jowotho i tindi momore, jomiyo jomoyeyo ma kamoro jye chik ma jomoor kodi jotel ma kitipin pa jomoyeyo ma Yerusalem joridho, aka jowacho ri jo mako chik me.
44016005	Ameno kitipa pa jomoyeyo omedi meni i yeyo aka odongo i welo ji kis piny moyawere jye.
44016006	Jono jowotho i adech ma Furigiya kodi Galasya: Chuny Maleŋ koyeyo jo fuonjo mikwenda i adech ma Asya.
44016007	Munyo jotundo yu loka mothenere gi Misya, jotemo kidho i adech ma Bithiniya, to Chuny Maleŋ pa Yesu koyeyo jo.
44016008	Ri ameno jowotho i Misya to joloro yu Trowa.
44016009	Paulo olimo menyirok wor no ma go onen'iye dhano ma Masedonia munyo ochungo aka kwayo go ni, “Biye yu Masedonia korin ikonyi wan!”
44016010	Tekin Paulo limo menyirok no, wayikere kidho Masedonia, rupiri oido waridho ni Were otyeko lwoŋo wan fuonjo Wach Maber ri ji kenyo.
44016011	Waweyo Trowa gi yee to wachiewere wakidho yu Samotura, aka yawere mere watundo Neyapoli.
44016012	Wok kenyo wadonjo Filipya, tindi ma i adech ma Masedonia; kenyo bende obedo kama Joroma jodhumo. Wachowo ndelo mogo i tindi no.
44016013	I ndelo ma Sabato wawok i tindi to wakidho i thengi jwom, kama waparo nike kakwayo pa joyudaya ni iye. Wabedo piny to waluwo gi mon moido jochokere kenyo.
44016014	Ŋatachiel kwoŋ jo mowinjo wan oido ilwoŋo ni Lidya, ma Thyatira, monwaŋo jamiten ma nengin ma rangi ariŋo. Go oido obedo dhako ma lamo Were, aka Ruoth oyawo paro pere ma winjo wach ma Paulo oido wacho.
44016015	Go kodi ji ma ot pere jolimo batisimo. Gikenyo go olwoŋo wan ni, “Biye win wibedi i ot paran, ka winiaŋ adyeri ni ayeyo Ruoth.” Aka go onyalo dwoŋo wan to wakidho.
44016016	Ndelo moro munyo oido wakidho i kakwayo, waromo kodi ŋecha moro manyako monwaŋo nitye gi chuny mochido moro ma miyo go thyedho ri ji gima bino i kwo pajo ma yuwaŋe. Go oido kelo pesa kweth ri jopere munyo tucho ri ji silwany pajo.
44016017	Go oluwo Paulo gi wan munyo koko ni, “Jome jotich pa Were Madwoŋ Maloyo! Jotito ri win royo ma both!”
44016018	Go otimo ameno ndelo mathoth, nyuka Paulo nge omako swa to wire to wacho ri jwok no ni, “I nyingi Yesu Kristo aorin, woki kwoŋ nyako me!” Jwok no owok kwoŋe i hongo no won.
44016019	Munyo wegi nyako no joneno ni yo pajo ma limo pesa onyo onyiekere woko, jomako Paulo gi Sila to joywayo jo to jotero jo bongi jodhum i katale.
44016020	Jokelo jo bongi joserikale ma Joroma to jowacho ni, “Jome joyudaya, aka jokelo ruwirok i tindi mawan ka.
44016021	Jofuonjo kite ma turo chik mawan; wan Wajoroma aka wakinyal mako kite no!”
44016022	Muma ji bende odonjo i kwinyo no, aka jothumi banjin joyecho nengin pa Paulo kodi Sila, to jowodho or ni wochwadi jo.
44016023	Munyo otyek chwado jo maloŋo, obol jo i twech, aka oor jakur chiego od twech matek.
44016024	Munyo jotyeko limo or me, jakuri od twech obolo jo i kisika ma iye to tweyo tyendi jo i kindi kasike madongo.
44016025	Dho kapa sawa auchiel ma wor, Paulo kodi Sila oido jokwayo aka jowero wer ma pako Were, aka jotwech oido jochiko ithi gin jowinjo jo.
44016026	Piyo piyo yengirok pa piny otimere, moyengo od twech kir i tyende. Gikenyo thigin jye joyawere arwat, to atege pa jotwech jye gonyere woko.
44016027	Jakuri jotwech ochiew, aka munyo oneno thigin ma od twech ni thwolo, oparo nike jomotwey jye onyo jokwale; gikenyo oyuyo abor pere aka oido won kidho nekirok.
44016028	To Paulo okoko gi derino ni, “Ikiri itim racho kwoŋin, wajojye fuodi wanitye ka.”
44016029	Jakur okwayo mach, omwomere i ot, to gore piny gi kirin dho katyendi Paulo gi Sila.
44016030	Gikenyo otero jo woko to penjo jo ni, “Jodongo, aripo timo aŋo ŋey alim both?”
44016031	Jowacho ni, “Yeyi Yesu Kristo, aka ibino limo both, in kodi ot perin gipi.”
44016032	Aka jofuonjo go wach pa Ruoth kodi joman jye ma ot pere.
44016033	I hongo ma wor no won, jakuri od twech otero jo lwoko adholin pajo; aka go kodi joot pere jye jolimo batisimo mayot.
44016034	Go otero Paulo kodi Sila i ot pere to miyo jo chiemo moro achama. Go kodi joot pere jye kisangala opoŋ i chuny jo ru yeyo Were.
44016035	Yawere mere odikini, jodhum ma Joroma jodhiro or ri joserikale ni, “Gonyi win jono jowokadhi.”
44016036	Gikenyo jakuri od twech owacho ri Paulo ni, “Jothumi banjin jodhiro or ni wogony win. Onyo winyalo kadho, kadhi win gi syem.”
44016037	To Paulo owacho ri joserikale ni, “Kole konwaŋ racho moro kwoŋ wan, aka otyek chwado wan i dyer ji mato wabedo Joroma! Odoko jobolo wan i twech; aka onyo pama jomito gonyo wan nyaliŋliŋ? Bee! Weyi wegi jowobin jowogony wan.”
44016038	Joserikale madongo jodhiro wach no ri jodhum ma Joroma; aka munyo jowinjo ni Paulo kodi Sila jobedo Joroma, lworo omako jo.
44016039	Ri ameno jokidho to jokwayo chwak bongi jo; gikenyo jowodho jo woko to jokwayo jo ni jowoeye i tindi.
44016040	Paulo gi Sila joweyo od twech to jokidho pecho pa Lidya. Kenyo jorom'iye kodi jomoyeyo, joluwo wach mamedo jo men, to jokadho.
44017001	Joluwo yu Anfipoli kodi Apolonia, to jobino Thesalonika, kama onwaŋo kalamo pa Joyudaya nitye iye.
44017002	Paka Paulo yado oido omaro timo, okidho i kalamo pa Joyudaya. Aka opyemo gi ji gi wach ma Ndiiko Maleŋ chowo hongo ma Sabato adek gipi,
44017003	munyo tito aka nyutho i wach ni Kristo oido ripo chandere aka ŋey wochierino go kwoŋ jomotho. Paulo owacho ni, “Yesu me obedo Kristo.”
44017004	Jomegi kwoŋ jo joniaŋ to joriwere gi Paulo kodi Sila; kitipa pa Joyunani mathoth ma jolamo Were, kodi mon mathoth ma joŋeyere bende jotimo ameno.
44017005	To Joyudaya nyieko omako jo to jochoko jomarecho mogo i ngudin mokakere ma tindi to jotimo bwora moro. Gikenyo jokelo woy madwoŋ i tindi gipi, to jomwonjo pecho pa Yason, munyo jorango Paulo kodi Sila wowodhi jo ri ji.
44017006	To munyo jokonwaŋo jo, joyware gi Yason kodi jomoyeyo mogo kir bongi judhum ma tindi kareno jokoko ni, “Jome jokelo ruwirok kis kamoro! Aka onyo bende jobino i tindi mawan ka, aka
44017007	Yason ama kano jo i ot pere. Jojye joturo chik pa Kaisar, ka jowacho ni odoko nitye kere man, ma nyinge Yesu.”
44017008	Gi wach me jokelo ri lwak ji kodi jodhum ma tindi woy madwoŋ.
44017009	Jodhum jomiyo Yason kodi joman tweyo pesa momit to iweyo jokadho.
44017010	Tekin piny lokere machol, jomoyeyo jodhiro Paulo gi Sila yu Bereya. Munyo jotundo koro, jokidho i kalamo pa Joyudaya.
44017011	Joyudaya ma kenyo oido joneno bor loyo ma Thesalonika. Jochiko ithi gin winjo fuonji gi maro madwoŋ, aka ndelo jye bin jofuonjere Ndiiko Maleŋ jowoneni ka gima Paulo ofuonjo jo oido obedo adyeri.
44017012	Mathoth kwoŋ jo joyeyo, aka mon kweth ma malo kodi chwo ma Joyunani bende joyeyo.
44017013	To munyo Joyudaya ma Thesalonika jowinjo ni Paulo fuonjo wach pa Were i Bereya bende, jobino kenyo to jochako nywowo j.
44017014	Piyo piyo jomoyeyo jodhiro Paulo i thengi jwom to Sila kodi Timotheyo jodoŋ Bereya.
44017015	Joma jokwaŋo Paulo jotero go kir yu Athen aka ŋey jogik Bereya gi wach pa Paulo ni Sila kodi Timotheyo jowokidhi bonge mayot.
44017016	Munyo Paulo oido kuro Sila kodi Timotheyo i Athen, chunye oramo swa munyo oneno ni tindi opoŋ gi gikipiny ma ji jochweyo ma jolamo.
44017017	Ri ameno go opyemo i kalamo pa Joyudaya kodi Joyudaya gi Jopath ma jolamo Were, kodi ji ma jobino ndelo jye i katale madwoŋ.
44017018	Joepikuryan kodi Jostoik mogo ma jopyem i wach bende jopyemo gine. Megi jowacho ni, “Jal mamiŋ me onyo bende kwot ni wacho aŋo?” Joman jowacho ni, “Chale pa go luwo kwoŋ werin mogo mawok loka man.” Jowacho ama rupiri Paulo onwaŋo luwo kwoŋ Yesu kodi chierino pere.
44017019	Ameno jokwanyo Paulo to jotero go i ot romo milwoŋo ni Arewopago, to jowacho ni, “Wamito ŋeyo fuonji manyien me ma iluwo kwoŋe.
44017020	Gikipiny me ma wawinjo iluwo kwoŋe wendo ri wan swa, aka wamito ŋeyo dwoŋ mere.”
44017021	(Ato ji ma Athen kodi jowiloka ma kenyo oido jomaro oro hongo pajo jye i luwo gi winjo gikipiny manyien motimere.)
44017022	Paulo ochungo i waŋ jomochokere i Arewopago no to wacho ni, “Ji ma Athen! Aneno ni i yo jye wimaro din tektek,
44017023	rupiri munyo awotho i tindi mewin t'aneno kama wilamer'iye taneno alitar mondik kwoŋe ni, ‘Ri Were ma koŋeyere.’ Onyo gima wilamo, kada wikuya no, ama ee atito ri win kwoŋe.
44017024	Were mochweyo piny kodi gima ni iye gi bee, obedo Ruoth ma polo kodi piny, aka kibedi i udi ma ji ama jogero.
44017025	Odoko go kiyeny kony moro bongi dhano igani go keŋ gimoro ma dhano ama nyalo miyo go, rupiri go won ama miyo ji jye kwo, luya kodi gimoro jye.
44017026	Wok kwoŋ dhano achiel go ochweyo nonin jye, to miyo jo bedo i piny gipi. Go won ama chango ochano ndir kodi kew ma kabedo ma ji di jobed'iye.
44017027	Otimo ameno ni jowonyali rango go, ni ipoyo di jonwaŋo go munyo jomudamuda jorango go. To iyadyeri won, Were kinitye bor gi nyatoro jye kwoŋ wan;
44017028	kole ‘I go wanwaŋo kwo aka wawotho kendo walama;’ paka jondiiko mewin mogo joluwo ni, ‘Adyeri wabedo nyithindho pere.’
44017029	Onyo paka wabedo nyithindho pa Were, wakiri wapar ni Were chale kodi zawabu, kosa feza, kosa tele ma dhano ama won othedho gi ryeko kodi ndijo pere.
44017030	I ndir ma fuodi ji oido jokuy'iye Were, go kokwano recho pajo, to pama go onyo oro ji jye i piny jye ŋuto gimarecho pajo,
44017031	rupiri go otyeko yiko ndelo ma go bino thum'iye banja ri piny gipi i tiro, aka ŋata go oyero ama bino thumo. Go otyeko ridho wach no ri dhano jye munyo chierino ŋato kwoŋ jomotho.”
44017032	Munyo jowinjo Paulo luwo kwoŋ chierino pa jomotho, megi kwoŋ jo jonyiero ayin, to joman jowacho ni, “Wamito iluwi kwoŋ gime kendo.”
44017033	Gikenyo Paulo oeye i kachokirok no.
44017034	Jomogo joluwo go to jolokere jomoyeyo; kwoŋ jo oido obedo Dyonisyo, achiel kwoŋ jokweth ma Arewopago, dhako milwoŋo ni Damari, kodi joman.
44018001	Rumachien, Paulo oeye Athen to kidho yu Korintho.
44018002	Kenyo go orom'iye kodi Jayudaya milwoŋo ni Akwila ma nywolere Ponto monwaŋo nyaka jowok Italya kodi chiege Prisila, rupiri Kaisar milwoŋo ni Klaudyo oido owodho chik ni Joyudaya jye jowoeye Roma. Paulo okidho neno jo
44018003	aka obedo gi jo to tiyo gi jo, rupiri bin go oido limo chiemo pere i timo wema, paka jono oido bende jotimo.

44018006	Munyo jopyemo gine to joluwo wach marecho kwoŋ go, Paulo oteŋo woko fukefuke ma nengin pere ka wacho ri jo ni, “Ka wirwenyo, remo mewin wodoŋi i wiy wiwegi! Kobedo wach paran. Wok pama kadho yuwaŋe abino kidho bongi Jopath ayino.”

44018019	Jotundo Efeso to Paulo weyo Prisila kodi Akwila kenyo. Go odonjo i kalamo pa Joyudaya to pyemo gi Joyudaya kenyo.
44018020	Kenyo jokwayo go ni wobedi gi jo hongo malach, to go koyeyo.

44019001	Munyo Apolo nitye Korintho, Paulo owotho i adech ma Yumalo to tundo Efeso. Kenyo go onwaŋ'iye jofuonjirok mogo
44019002	to penjo jo ni, “Wilimo Chuny Maleŋ munyo wiyeyo?” Jodwoko go ni, “Oido fuodi wakiwinjo kada ni Chuny Maleŋ bende nitye.”
44019003	Openjo jo bende ni, “K'inen ameno, wilimo batisimo mene?” Jodwoko ni, “Batisimo pa Yohana.”
44019004	Paulo owacho ni, “Batisimo ma Yohana omiyo ji obedo ma ŋuto gimarecho; to owacho ri ji ni joripo yeyo ŋata oido luwo go chien, aka meno a Yesu.”
44019005	Munyo jowinjo ameno, jolimo batisimo i nyingi Ruoth Yesu.
44019006	Paulo oketho chinge kwoŋ jo, to Chuny Maleŋ loro ri jo to joluwo dhudhok mopokere to jotucho mikwenda ma wok bongi Were.

44019009	To munyo jomegi kwoŋ jo jobedo gi wichtek to jokwero yeyo, aka joluwo gikipiny marecho kwoŋ Royo pa Ruoth ruwaŋ kitipa pa ji, Paulo oweyo jo to kadho gi jofuonjirok; aka ndelo jye jobedo gi pyem i ot romo ma Tirano.
44019010	Gime obedo ameno chowo hongo ma oro aryo, momiyo ji jye ma jobedo i adech ma Asya, Joyudaya kodi Joyunani, jowinjo Wach pa Ruoth.

44019012	ma kir kitambilin pere kodi nengin pere mawoko oido itero ri jotwo, aka two pajo ware woko aka chuny mochido wok kwoŋ ji.
44019013	Joyudaya mogo ma jothoko piny aka joryemo chuny mochido bende jotemo oro nyingi Yesu kwoŋ joma jo ni gi chuny mochido. Jowacho ri chuny marach moro ni, “Aorin i nyingi Yesu ma Paulo fuonjo.”
44019014	Wuoti jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar ma Jayudaya milwoŋo ni Sikeva jabiryo onwaŋo jotimo ameno.

44019016	Ŋata oido nitye gi chuny mochido no orodho jo to loyo jo gi men. Jojye jowok i ot pere gi ŋwech kinyoro g'adholin kwoŋ jo.
44019017	Joyudaya jye kodi Jopath ma jobedo Efeso jowinjo gime; lworo opoŋ kwoŋ jojye, aka omiy nyingi Yesu dwoŋ moasere.

44019019	Mathoth kwoŋ jomoido jothyedho jokelo kitawin pajo kanyachiel to jowaŋo ruwaŋ ji jye. Jokwano welo kitawin to jye bedo pesa ma romo jegejege feza gana piero abich.
44019020	Aka Wach pa Ruoth omedo nyay gi dongo i men tektek.
44019021	Munyo gikipiny me otyeko timire, Paulo oyiko paro ma luwo yu Masedonia gi Akaya aka wokidhi Yerusalem. Go owacho ni, “Ka atyeko kidho koro, aripo neno Roma bende.”
44019022	Gikenyo go ooro Timotheyo kodi Erasto, jokony pere aryo, yu Masedonia, to won chowo hongo moro i adech ma Asya.
44019023	Hongo no ama ruwirok madwoŋ obed'iye i Efeso ma mako kwoŋ Royo pa Ruoth.
44019024	Jatheth ma thedho feza moro milwoŋo ni Demeturyo, ma thedho chal ma udi mathindho gi feza ri were Artemi, oido konyo jomiten swa i nywolo ri jo ŋaŋo madit gi tich pere no.
44019025	Gikenyo go olwoŋo jojye kanyachiel, kodi joman ma tich pajo chale g'apere, to wacho ri jo ni, “Jume, kole wiŋeyo ni ŋaŋo mawan wok i tich me.
44019026	To wiwegi wityeko winjo gi neno gima jal milwoŋo ni Paulo me timo. Go otyeko wiro ji mathoth ka kodi i Efeso kodi chiegin i adech ma Asya gipi ka wacho ni werin mothedhi gi chingi jo kobedo were.
44019027	Aka ameno wach onyo rach rupiri tich mawan bino limo nyinge marach. Ki meno kende, racho bende nitye mogam pa were madhako Artemi bino ngoye kony, aka dwoŋ pere bino reyere woko mato were madhako me ilamo i Asya parom kodi i piny jye!”
44019028	Munyo jono jowinjo wach me, jolokere mager to jochako koko ni, “Artemi ma Efeso dwoŋ moasere!”
44019029	Woy no olak i tindi gipi. Jono jomwomere i ot minen'iye tuko to jomako Gayo kodi Aristaruko, Jomasedonia aryo monwaŋo jowotho gi Paulo.
44019030	Paulo won oido mito kidho luwo gi muma ji, to jomoyeyo jokoyeyo ri go.
44019031	Jodhum mogo moido merin pere, bende jodhiro ri go wach munyo jokwayo go ni wokiri wotemi kidho i ot minen'iye tuko no.
44019032	I hongo no i romo obedo woy kende kende; ji megi oido jokoko gimoro achiel, joman bende jokoko giman, aka jomegi jokoŋeyo kir gima okelo jo kanyachiel.
44019033	Joman joparo ni Alekizanda ama oero wach no, rupiri Joyudaya joketho go paka jatel. Gikenyo Alekizanda otimo ranyuth gi chinge to temo luwo ma yiko nyinge i dyer ji.
44019034	To munyo joniaŋ nike go Jayudaya, jojye jochako koko kiromo gimoro achiel chowo hongo ma sawa aryo gipi ni, “Artemi ma Efeso dwoŋ moasere!”
44019035	Rumachien jadwoŋ ma tindi onyalo miyo lwak ji kudirok munyo owacho ni, “Ji ma Efeso! Kole dhano jye oŋeyo ni tindi ma Efeso ama kuro migam pa were Artemi moasere no, kodi tele maleŋ mopodho wok i polo.
44019036	Ongoye ŋata nyalo kwero gime. Amomiyo, wiripo kudere ma kiweno timo gikipiny pa joneko.
44019037	Wikelo ji me ka kada onwaŋo jokikedhi ot pa were kosa jowachi gikipiny marecho kwoŋ were madhako.
44019038	Ka Demeturyo kodi jotich pere jonitye gi wach ma jokelo kwoŋ nyatoro, nitye ndelo mochan ma pido aka ruodhe bende jonitye; jonyalo kelo wach pajo to joosere wegi kenyo.
44019039	To ka nitye gimoro man ma wimito, ibino chowo wach no i romo paji paka chik wacho.
44019040	Aka giramen nyalo miyo iketho kwoŋ wan wach ma gwenyirok gi woy konon me. Kole ongoye gima di miyi win woy madwoŋ ama, aka di wakinyalo nyutho atoŋa mere.”
44019041	Munyo go otyeko wacho ameno, ochiego woko romo.
44020001	Munyo woy no orumo, Paulo olwoŋo jomoyeyo kanyachiel, aka munyo otyeko medo jo men to sewila jo. Gikenyo go oweyo jo to kidho yu Masedonia.
44020002	Munyo go otyeko woth i adech no gi medo jo men gi wach kweth, okidho Yunani
44020003	kama go obed'iye hongo ma dwe adek. Go oido yikere kidho Sirya to limo ŋeyo nike Joyudaya oido jochamo ri go sereko; gikenyo go oridho paro ma gik gi yu Masedonia.
44020004	Sopate, wuodi pa Piro ma Bereya, okidho gine; Aristaruko jokodi Sekundo ma Thesalonika, kodi Gayo ma Derube, kodi Timotheyo, kodi Tichiko gi Trofimo ma jowok Asya bende jowotho gine.
44020005	Jono jotelo aka jokuro wan i Trowa.
