44020006	Wachiewere wok Filipya rumachien munyo kalima ma Mugat ma Bu Thow orumo, aka i ndelo marabich aka wariwere gi jo i Trowa, kama wabed'iye sabiti achiel.
44020007	I ndelo marapena (i sabiti) odikini, munyo wabedo kanyachiel chiemo gi merin, Paulo oluwo gi ji luwo mabor kir i dyer wor, rupiri go oido yenyo kadho yawere mere.
44020008	Talin oido omore i ot mamalo kama oido warom'iye.
44020009	Jayach moro ma nyinge Yutiko onwaŋo obedo wi dirisa; to paka Paulo omedere luwo, Yutiko nindo onuro chuka nindo okadho gine to podho piny wok wi gorofa ma malo maradek. Jotiŋo go malo to jonwaŋo ni otyeko tho.
44020010	To Paulo oloro piny to luŋere kwoŋe to ketho kore kwoŋe to wacho ni, “Wikiri wilwor, go fuodi kwo!”
44020011	Gikenyo go ogik i ot mamalo, oturo mugat, to chamo. Munyo Paulo otyeko luwo gi jo hongo malach nyuka chieŋ ogulo, to okadho.
44020012	Jono jokadho gi jayach no ma kwo, to chuny jo dwoko maber.
44020013	Wamedere gi woth tundo i yee to wachiewere wachomo yu Aso, kama onwaŋo wakidho rwak'iye Paulo i yee. Go owacho ri wan timo ameno, rupiri oido kidho kenyo atyendi.
44020014	Munyo go oromo gi wan i Aso, warwako go i yee to wakidho yu Mitilene.
44020015	Wachiewere wok kenyo to watundo yu Kiyo yawere mere. Rumachien ma ndelo achiel, watundo Samo, aka yawere mere aka watundo Mileto.
44020016	Paulo oido oyenyo chiewirok kalo Efeso, ŋey nyaka wokiri wonyieki hongo i adech ma Asya. Go onwaŋo kwakere ka mito tundo Yerusalem i ndelo ma Pentekost ka nyalere.
44020017	Paulo odhiro wach Efeso wok Mileto munyo kwayo jotel ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo bino romo gine.
44020018	Munyo jobino, go owacho ri jo ni, “Wiwegi Wiŋeyo kite ma abed'iye gi win i hongo jye, wok i ndelo marapena ma tund'iye i adech ma Asya.
44020019	Gi bwonirok kodi pigi waŋan, atimo tich paran paka jatich pa Ruoth, i ndir ma teko obed'iye ran ru sereko pa Joyudaya.
44020020	Wiŋeyo nike akimuŋo win gimoro ma d'okonyo win munyo afuonjo win i dyer ji kamaler kodi i pechin mewin.
44020021	Afuonjo Joyudaya kodi Jopath parom nike jowoŋuti gimarecho pajo jowogiki bongi Were, to joyeyo Ruoth Yesu Kristo.
44020022	Aka gunyoni, gi wach pa Chuny Maleŋ akidho Yerusalem, ma akuya gima bino timan koro.
44020023	Kwanyo woko gima aŋeyo ame: i tindi jye Chuny Maleŋ otyeko nyuthan kichutho nike twech kodi teko ama kuran.
44020024	To akiter kwo paran pa gimadwoŋ, kosa pa gima di welo tekin achowo tich ma Ruoth Yesu ooran ma tito ri ji Wach Maber kwoŋ ŋono pa Were.
44020025	“Atyeko woth i dyer win jojye, munyo afuonjo Ker pa Were, to pama aŋeyo ni kwoŋ win ongoye ŋata odoko bino nenan kendo.
44020026	Amomiyo konon atucho ri win kamaler ni ka moro kwoŋ win orweny meno kiwach paran,
44020027	rupiri akimuŋo win atoŋa pa Were gipi.
44020028	Kure win wiwegi kodi sidwol roombo jye, ma Chuny Maleŋ oketho i chingi win, ni wibedi jotel mere, ma konyo kitipa pa jomoyeyo pa Were, ma go oloko apere gi remo pa Wuode won.
44020029	Kole aŋeyo ni ka atyeko eye, arara mager bino donjo bongi win, aka jokowori sidwol roombo.
44020030	Aka ndir bino tundo ma jomogo i dyer win won jobino ay gi twodo ma ywayo jomoyeyo bongi jo.
44020031	Amomiyo kure win, aka poyi win ni, odyechieŋ gi wor akikeŋ fuonjo dhano jye kwoŋ win gi geregere chowo hongo ma romo oro adek.
44020032	“To pama onyo aketho win i chingi Were kodi i wach ma ŋono pere ma nyalo dongo win to miyo win silwany ma go okano ri ji pere jye.
44020033	Fuodi akiwanya feza kosa zawabu pa nyatoro kosa ruk.
44020034	Wiwegi wiŋeyo ni atiyo gi chingan me aka alimo gimoro jye ma an kodi jowotan onwaŋo wayenyo aora.
44020035	Atyeko nyutho win i gikipiny jye nike timo tich gi men miyo wanyalo konyo jomanyap munyo wapoyo wach pa Ruoth Yesu m'owacho ni, ‘Silwany nitye madwoŋ ri ŋata poko gimoro loyo ŋata limo.’ ”
44020036	Munyo Paulo ochowo luwo, ogoyo chonge piny to kwayo gi jojye
44020037	Gikenyo jojye joywak gi geregere munyo jopodho i kore aka jochwiyo lembe.
44020038	Jorem swa ru wach pere ni odoko jokoneni go kendo. Rumachien to jokwaŋo go dho yee.
44021001	Munyo watyeko kisewila jo to wachiewere waeye, wabino nyatirtir i loka Kos, to yawere mere watundo Rod, aka wok kenyo wadonjo Patara.
44021002	Munyo wanwaŋo kenyo yee moido kidho Fonisya, waidho to wachiewere.
44021003	Munyo watundo kama wanyalo neni'iye Sipuro, wachiewere yu racham to wachomo yu Sirya. Waloro Tire kama ye oido kidho wodh'iye gikipiny m'otiŋo.
44021004	Wanwaŋo jomoyeyo mogo kenyo to wabedo gi jo sabiti achiel. Gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ jowacho ri Paulo nike wokiri wokidhi Yerusalem.
44021005	To munyo hongo mawan orumo, waweyo jo to wakadho i woth mawan. Jojye gi mon pajo gi nyithindho, jokwaŋo wan kalo tindi. Wajojye wagoyo chongi wan piny dho thengi pi to wakwayo.
44021006	Gikenyo kis dhano osewila nyawote, to waidho yee kareno jo jodok.
44021007	Munyo watyeko chiewirok mawan wok Tire, watundo Potolemayi, kama wamoth'iye jomoyeyo to wabed'iye gi jo ma ndelo achiel.
44021008	Yawere mere waeye to wakidho Kaisareya. Kenyo wakidho i ot pa Filipo jatiti Wach Maber, to wabedo bonge.
44021009	Go oido nitye gi nyithindho ma nyir aŋwen ma fuodi jokonywomere moido jotucho mikwenda ma wok bongi Were.
44021010	Munyo watyeko bedo kenyo ndelo mogo, jatuchi wach ma nyinge Agabo otundo kenyo wok Yudeya.
44021011	Go obino bongi wan to kwanyo del pa Paulo to won tweyo gine tyende gi chinge, to wacho ni, “Me a gima Chuny Maleŋ wacho, ‘Joyudaya jobino tweyo won del me ama i Yerusalem to jobolo go i chingi Jopath.’ ”
44021012	Munyo wawinjo ameno wan kodi ji ma kenyo wakwayo Paulo ni wokiri wokidhi Yerusalem.
44021013	To go odwoko ni, “Witimo aŋo, wiywak aka wikelo ran rembo i chunyan? Kole ayikere ki nyaka ri twech kende to kir ri tho jye i Yerusalem i nyingi Ruoth Yesu.”
44021014	Wakinyalo turo go i gime amomiyo chuny wan bende oeye to wawacho ni, “Weyi mito pa Ruoth wotimere.”
44021015	Munyo watyeko bedoye kenyo hongo moro, wayikere to waay to wakadho Yerusalem.
44021016	Jofuonjirok megi ma Kaisareya bende jowotho gi wan, to jotero wan i ot pa jal monwaŋo wakidho bedo pere milwoŋo ni Minason mawok Sipuro, moido obedo achiel kwon jofuonjirok ma jopen yeyo.
44021017	Munyo watundo Yerusalem jomoyeyo jojolo wan gi kisangala madit swa.
44021018	Yawere mere Paulo okidho gi wan neno Yakobo; aka jotel jye ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo oido jonitye kenyo.
44021019	Paulo omotho jo to miyo jo wach jye kwoŋ gimoro jye ma Were oido otyeko timo i dyer Jopath i tich pere.
44021020	Munyo jotyeko winjo go, jojye jopako Were. Gikenyo jowacho ri Paulo ni, “Omin wan neni, nitye Joyudaya kweth ma jotyeko lokere jomoyeyo, to jojye fuodi jochwire tektek kwoŋ Chik pa Musa.
44021021	Otyek wacho ri jo nike ifuonjo Joyudaya jye ma jo ni i dyer Jopath weyo Chik pa Musa, aka ni iwacho ri jo nike kiri jowothumi nyithindho pajo kosa luwo kula pa Joyudaya.
44021022	Onyo aŋo ma ripere atima? Adyer jobino winjo nike ityeko tundo ka.
44021023	Amomiyo timi gima wawacho rin. Wani gi ji mogo aŋwen ma jonitye i kwoŋirok ma nyadin.
44021024	Kidhi gi jome ibedi gi jo i tim ma lonyirok aka iwodhi ri jo chul kwoŋ gima joor jye, odoko jowolyel yewiy gin. I yo me dhano jye bino ŋeyo nike adyeri ingoye i gimoro jye ma joluwo kwoŋin, kuchiel in bende imako Chik pa Musa.
44021025	To ma mako kwoŋ Jopath ma jotyeko yeyo, watyeko dhiro ri jo balwa, munyo wawacho ri jo nike waridho paro ni kiri jowochami chiemo mochow gine werin motim gi chingi jo; kosa chamo remo, kosa lee moro jye modey, aka jowokure kwoŋ kite ma kidakana.”
44021026	Gikenyo Paulo otero jono aka yawere mere otimo gi jo tim ma lonyirok. Gikenyo go odonjo i Ot pa Were nyutho jo ndelo ma lonyirok no kidho rum'iye aka ŋey kis dhano kwoŋ jo wokeli mich pere ma chowirok.
44021027	Munyo ndelo abiryo oido chiegin rumo, Joyudaya mogo ma jowok i adech ma Asya joneno Paulo i Ot pa Were. Jono josigila lwak ji gi bee to jomako Paulo.
44021028	Jokoko ni, “Ji ma Israel! Konyi wan win! Me won a ŋata wotho kamoro jye aka fuonjo ji dakirok gi Joisrael, kwero Chik pa Musa kodi Ot pa Were me. Aka onyo okelo kir Jopath mogo i Ot pa Were to kocho kamaleŋ me!”
44021029	(Jowacho ama rupiri joneno Trofimo ma Efeso gi Paulo i tindi, aka joparo nike Paulo oido otero go i Ot pa Were).
44021030	Ruwirok olak i tindi gipi, aka ji jye joringo kanyachiel jomako Paulo, to jowodho go woko wok i Ot pa Were. Piyo piyo to ichiego woko dhoudi jye.
44021031	Muma ji onwaŋo temo neko Paulo to itero wach ri jatel ma lwak jolweny pa Joroma nike ruwirok nitye i Yerusalem gipi.
44021032	Piyo piyo jatel otero joserikale mogo madongo kodi joserikale man to jomwomere kwoŋ muma ji. Tekin ji neno go gi joserikale to joweyo goyo Paulo.
44021033	Jatel okidho bongi Paulo, omako go, to wodho or nike wotweyi Paulo gi lijegere aryo. Gikenyo go openjo ni, “Me ŋa; kendo otimo aŋo?”
44021034	Jomogo i muma ji jokoko gimoro achiel, joman giman. Ruwirok obedo mathoth momiyo jatel konyalo nwaŋo adyeri ma gima otimere; gikenyo ooro ji tero Paulo i chiel pa jolweny.
44021035	Jotundo gine i geŋin ma dhoot, to joserikale jotiŋo atiŋa go rupiri muma ji oido olokere mager swa.
44021036	Jojye oido joluwo go ka jokoko ni, “Neki wi go!”
44021037	Munyo jochiegin tero Paulo i chiel, go oluwo gi jatel ni, “Weyi awachi ye rin gimoro?” Jaserikale madwoŋ openjo ni, “Iŋeyo Dhoyunani?
44021038	In won me iki Jamisir ma ndir cha oruwo wiy ji to telo jogwenyirok gana aŋwen i thim?”
44021039	Paulo odwoko ni, “A Jayudaya to onywolan i Tarso ma Silisya, anywola ma tindi moŋeyere maber. Mondo yeyan aluwi gi ji.”
44021040	Jaserikale madwoŋ oyeyo go, to Paulo chungo i geŋin ma dhoot to miyo ji ranyuth gi chinge. Munyo jopye, Paulo oluwo gi jo gi Dhoyudaya ni,
44022001	“Wutimera gi bachere nan, winji win gima awacho ri win ma nyutho win paka angoye gi racho moro!”
44022002	Munyo jowinjo go luwo Dhoyudaya, jomedo kudirok; Paulo omedere gi luwo ni,
44022003	“A Jayudaya, monywol i Tarso ma Silisya, to adongo Yerusalem won ka paka jafuonjirok pa Gamaliel. Alimo fuonji matek kwoŋ Chik pa kwarere mawan, aka oido amiyere ri Were paka win bende ma wini ka konon me.
44022004	Alwenyo gi ji ma joluwo Royo pa Yesu no tundo kir i nek. Amako chwo gi mon aka abolo jo i od twech.
44022005	Jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi kitipa pa jotel pa ji gi bee jonyalo ridho ri win ni aluwo giradyeri. Alimo balwa wok bongi jo mondik ri Joyudaya jowoti wan ma Damasiko aka akidho koro mako ji kelo jo Yerusalem gi lijegere i chingi gin wochandi jo.
44022006	“Aka munyo oido atyeko woth ariko Damasiko, dho kapa sawa auchiel, lero madwoŋ owok malo abwap to thokan.
44022007	Gikenyo agore piny t'awinjo dwondi ŋata wacho ran ni, ‘Saulo, Saulo! Raŋo ilwenyo kodan?’
44022008	Apenjo ni, ‘In iŋa, Ruoth?’ Owacho ran ni, ‘An Yesu ma Nazareth m'ilwenyo gine.’
44022009	Ji monwaŋo ni kodan kenyo joneno lero no to jokowinjo dwondi ŋata onwaŋo luwo kodan no.
44022010	Apenjo go ni, ‘Atimi aŋo, Ruoth?’ Aka Ruoth owacho ran ni, ‘Ayi malo idonji Damasiko, aka kenyo ama ibino wacho rin gimoro jye ma Were ochano rin timo.’
44022011	Munyo waŋan onwaŋo otho ru lero moasere no, jowotan jomako chingan to joteran Damasiko.
44022012	“Kenyo onwaŋo nitye nyatoro milwoŋo ni Ananiya, jadin mowinjo Chik mawan aka Joyudaya jye ma Damasiko jomiyo go dwoŋ swa.
44022013	Go obino bongan to chungo kabutan to wacho ni, ‘Omera Saulo, chaki neno kendo!’ I hongo no won aneno kendo to aŋiyo go.
44022014	Gikenyo go owacho ran ni, ‘Were pa kwarere mawan oyerin ni iŋey gima go mito, ni inyal neno Ŋata otire pere gi winjo go munyo iwinjo dwonde won;
44022015	ameno ibino bedo jakony pere ma wacho ri ji gima ityeko neno gi winjo.
44022016	To onyo aŋo m'idoko ikuro? Ayi malo ilimi batisimo, aka recho perin wolwoki woko munyo ilwoŋo nyingi go.’
44022017	“Agik Yerusalem, aka munyo akwayo i Ot pa Were, aneno chal momenyere ran
44022018	m'aneno iye Ruoth munyo wacho ran ni, ‘Redi mayot ieye Yerusalem, rupiri ji maka jokojol gima iwacho kwoŋan.’
44022019	Adwoko ni, ‘Ruoth, kole joŋeyo maber paka yado akidho i kalamo pa Joyudaya momore, amako jomoyeyin, agoyo jo aka atero jo i twech.
44022020	Aka munyo ineko jatiti Wach perin Sitefano, oido ani kenyo, aka abende afuoyo odoko aŋata akuro kir ruk pa joma joneko go.’
44022021	Ruoth owacho ran ni, ‘Kadhi, rupiri abino dhirin bor swa i dyer Jopath.’ ”
44022022	Ji onwaŋo jowinjo luwo pa Paulo nyuka tundo i wach me, to jochako koko gi derino madwoŋ ni, “Kwanyi wi woko jalo i piny ka! Go kiripi wokwo kendo!”
44022023	Oido jokoko aka jokwadho nengin pajo i hongo aka jowito fukefuke malo.
44022024	Gikenyo jaserikale madwoŋ owodho or nike woter Paulo i chiel, to oro jo chwado go ma mito ŋeyo gima omiyo Joyudaya jokoko ri go ameno.
44022025	To munyo jochowo kikada go aka wochwadi, Paulo owacho ri jaserikale moro monwaŋo ochungo kenyo ni, “Kere chik yeyo win chwado ŋata obedo anywola ma Roma kada fuodi koosa go banja moro jye?”
44022026	Munyo jaserikale no owinjo ameno, okidho bongi jadwoŋ pa joserikale to penjo ni, “Wikidho timo aŋo? Kole jame obedo anywola ma Roma!”
44022027	Gikenyo jatel pa joserikale okidho bongi Paulo to penjo go ni, “Wachi ran, ibedo Jaroma?” Paulo odwoko ni, “Ey.”
44022028	Jatel pa joserikale no owacho ni, “An alokere Jaroma munyo atyeko chulo pesa malach swa.” Paulo odwoko ni, “To an onywolan paka Jaroma.”
44022029	Gikenyo piyo piyo, ji moido jokidho kelo penji ri Paulo joeye gichien kwoŋe; aka jatel pa joserikale lworo omako munyo oneno ni Paulo obedo anywola ma Roma, aka ama go oido otweyo gi lijegere.
44022030	Yawere mere jatel pa joserikale oyenyo ŋeyo adyeri ma wach ma Joyudaya jomito kelo kwoŋ Paulo; ri ameno ooro jo gonyo woko lijegere pa Paulo to oro jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jopido gi bee romo. Gikenyo go owodho Paulo, to kelo go ruwaŋ jo.
44023001	Paulo oŋiyo jopido nyatirtir to wacho ni, “Wutimera chunyan oŋeyo maber swa kwoŋ kwo paran gipi ni angoye gi racho ruwaŋ Were i hongo jye kir pama.”
44023002	Jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar ma nyinge Ananiya ooro joma onwaŋo jochungo kabuti Paulo goyo lembe.
44023003	Paulo owacho ri go ni, “Were bino goyin adyeri, in m'ichal kor ot mofuy matar gi woko! Wibedo kenyo ma thumo ran banja chungo kwoŋ Chik, aka win won ama odoko wituro Chik ago munyo wioro jo goyan!”
44023004	Ji monwaŋo jo ni chiegin gi Paulo jowacho ri go ni, “Inyalo nedi luwo marach kwoŋ jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar?”
44023005	Paulo odwoko ni, “Wutimera oido akiŋeyo nike go jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar rupiri ndiiko wacho ni, ‘Wikiri wiluwi marach kwoŋ jadhum pa ji mewin!’ ”
44023006	Munyo Paulo oneno nike jomegi kwoŋ jono oido jobedo Josadukayo aka joman Jofarisayo, okoko ri jopido ni, “Wutimera, a Jafarisayo aka Jofarisayo ama jonywolan. Anitye i kapido ka rupiri ageno ni jomotho jobino chierino!”
44023007	Tekin go otyeko wacho ameno, Jofarisayo kodi Josadukayo jochako dhawirok, to ji tyakere i bwora.
44023008	(Ato Josadukayo jowacho ni ji jokibino chierino kendo kwoŋ jomotho; aka nike ongoye jomalaika kosa gima obedo chuny, to Jofarisayo joyeyo gikipiny adek no jye).
44023009	Gikenyo woy omedo kidho malo; aka jofuonji ma Chik megi moido jo ni kweth pa Jofarisayo jochungo to jokwero matek ni, “Wakinyal nwaŋo racho moro kwoŋ jame! Miti kono malaika kosa chuny moro oluwo gine!”
44023010	Pyem olokere mager swa momiyo jaserikale madwoŋ lworo omako nike jobino yecho woko Paulo achielechiele. Ri ameno go ooro joserikale pere kidho i dyer muma ji piny jowokwanyi woko Paulo bongi jo gi mbaka jowoteri go i chiel.
44023011	Wor moluwo to Ruoth chungo kabuti Paulo to wacho ni, “Bedi miseni! Ityeko bedo jakony paran Yerusalem ka, aka iripo timo ameno Roma bende.”
44023012	Odikini yawere mere, Joyudaya joromo kanyachiel to joyiko paro. Jokwoŋere nike jokochiem kosa madho gimoro chuka joneki Paulo.
44023013	Onwaŋo jokalo ji pyero aŋwen ma joyiko paro me kanyachiel.
44023014	Gikenyo jokidho pa jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jotel pa ji to jowacho ni, “Watyeko timo kwoŋirok madwoŋ kanyachiel ni wakobil girachama moro jye ka fuodi wakaneko Paulo.
44023015	Onyo win kodi jopido dhiri win wach ri jaserikale madwoŋ ma Roma wokeli ri win Paulo munyo wirendere nike wimito medo niaŋ kwoŋ tyendi wach pere. Gikenyo waleneko go ma fuodi kotundo kir ka.”
44023016	To okewo pa Paulo owinjo sereko me to donjo i chiel to wacho ri Paulo gino.
44023017	Gikenyo Paulo olwoŋo jaserikale madwoŋ achiel to wacho ri go ni, “Teri jayach me bongi jatel pa joserikale; nitye gima go mito wacho ri jatel no.”
44023018	Jaserikale madwoŋ no okwanyo go otero go bongi jatel pa joserikale to wacho ni, “Jatwech milwoŋo ni Paulo olwoŋan aka okwayan ni akel jayach me bongin, nike nitye gima go lewacho rin.”
44023019	Jaserikale ma jatel omako chinge to won tero go gichien to penjo go ni, “Aŋo ma imito wacho ran?”
44023020	Ana go, “Joyudaya joriwo paro nike dikin jowokwayin iter Paulo ruwaŋ jopido, to jorendere ni jopido jomito medo niaŋ kwoŋ wach pere.
44023021	To ikiri iyey winjo wach pajo, rupiri nitye ji ma kalo pyero aŋwen ma jolepondo jowokuri go i royo. Jono jotyeko kwoŋere nike jokochiem kosa madho gimoro chuka joneki go. Pama won me jotyeko yikere ma timo ameno, aka jokuro ŋeyo paro perin won kende.”
44023022	Jaserikale ma jatel no owacho ni, “Ikiri iwachi ri nyatoro nike ityeko kelo wach me bongan.” To oro jayach no kadho.
44023023	Gikenyo jaserikale ma jatel no olwoŋo joserikale pere aryo madongo to wacho ri jo ni, “Kwanyi win joserikale miya aryo jowoyikere ma kidho Kaisareya, kanyachiel gi jokayina pyero abiryo kodi jotonge miya aryo, aka wiyikere ay keti sawa adek ma wor.
44023024	Neni kayina moro ri Paulo ma go owothi gine, aka witer go maber bongi gavana Felik.”
44023025	Gikenyo jaserikale ma jatel no ondiko balwa ama:
44023026	“An Klaudyo Lisya andiko ri jadwoŋ, gavana Felik, aka adhiro rin moth.
44023027	Joyudaya jomako ŋat me aka oido jokidho neko go. Alimo ŋeyo nike go obedo Jaroma, amomiyo akidho kodi joserikale paran botho go.
44023028	Paka onwaŋo amito ŋeyo wach ma jokelo kwoŋe, atero go i kapido pajo.
44023029	Anwaŋo nike go kotimo racho moro ma di miy neki go kosa twey go; wach mokel kwoŋe onwaŋo mako kwoŋ chik pajo wegi.
44023030	Aka munyo onyuthan nike Joyudaya jochamo ri go sereko, aridho paro ma dhiro go bongin. Awacho ri joma osa go jowokeli wach no gi bongin kenyo.”
44023031	Joserikale jotimo paka oor jo. Jokwanyo Paulo to jotero go wor no kir yu Antipaturi.
44023032	Yawere mere joserikale ma jotyendi gin jodwoko i chiel to joweyo jokayina jokadho gine.
44023033	Jotero go Kaisareya to jochwayo balwa ri gavana to jomiyo go Paulo.
44023034	Gavana osoma balwa no to penjo Paulo adech ma go wok'iye. Munyo onwaŋo ni go wok Silisya, owacho ni,
44023035	“Abino winjo wach perin ka joma osa in jotundo.” Gikenyo ooro jo kuro Paulo i chiel pa Herode.
44024001	Munyo ndelo abich okadho, jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, Ananiya, okidho Kaisareya gi jodongo mogo kodi ŋata oido luwo ri jo milwoŋo ni Tertulo. Jokidho ruwaŋ gavana Felik to joosa Paulo.
44024002	Olwoŋ Tertulo to jochako kelo wach pajo ama: “Jadwoŋ! Tel perin ma ryeko otyeko kelo ri wan syem chowo hongo malach, aka wirok mathoth motyeko bedo onyo pama okelo bero ri piny mawan.
44024003	Wajolo gime iye jye hongo jye, aka wakethin walwa swa.
44024004	Akimiti galin tektek, to akwayin itim ran ŋono iwinji wach mawan manok.
44024005	Ŋat me waneno paka jamijokere marach swa; go kelo ruwirok i dyer Joyudaya i piny gipi, aka go obedo jatel pa Jonazarin.
44024006	Go bende otemo kocho Ot pa Were to wamako go. [Onwaŋo waparo thumo ri go banja i nger ma Chik mawan,
44024007	to jaserikale madwoŋ Lisya donj'iye to kwanyo go bongi wan gi men.
44024008	Gikenyo Lisya ooro joma joosa go jowobin bongin.] Ka ikaŋasa wach pa jame maber, iwon ibino ŋeyo bonge gikipiny jye ma waos'iye go.”
44024009	Joyudaya bende jodonjo i wach no to jowacho nike gino jye otire.
44024010	Gavana ooro Paulo luwo, to Paulo wacho ni, “Aŋeyo nike ityeko bedo jathumi banja chowo hongo malach, amomiyo asangala gi limo silwany ma kwedirok kwoŋ wach pa jome ruwaŋin.
44024011	Paka iwon inyalo neno, fuodi kokalo ndelo apar g'aryo chuka akidhi Yerusalem kwayo.
44024012	Joyudaya jokonwaŋan apyemo gi nyatoro i Ot pa Were, kosa ni aruwo ji i kalamo pajo kamoro jye i tindi.
44024013	Aka jokinyal kada nyutho ni wach ma joos'iye an me obedo adyeri.
44024014	Me a gima ayeyo ruwaŋin: an alamo Were pa kwarere mawan munyo aluwo Royo ma jowacho ni kotire. Aka ayeyo gikipiny jye mondik i Chik pa Musa kodi i kitawin pa jotuchi wach Were.
44024015	Abende anitye gi geno kwoŋ Were paka jome, nike ji jye, mabeyo kodi marecho, jobino chierino kwoŋ jomotho.
44024016	Amomiyo atemo paka anyalo ndelo jye bedo gi paro motire ruwaŋ Were kodi ji.
44024017	“An oido angoye Yerusalem tyeko oro mogo, amomiyo oido akidho koro tero mich paran ri ji paran gi timo chowirok.
44024018	Aka i kare moido atim'iye ameno ama jome jonwaŋan'iye i Ot pa Were munyo atimo tim ma lonyirok. Muma ji oido ongoye bothan, aka ruwirok moro jye oido ongoye.
44024019	To Joyudaya mogo ma jowok i adech ma Asya onwaŋo jo ni kenyo; jo ama joripo bino bongin ka kelo wach pajo k'inen jo ni gi wach moro kwoŋan.
44024020	Ka kameno weyi jome wegi jowowachi recho ma jonwaŋan gine i ndir cha munyo achungo i waŋ pido,
44024021	ma kiweno gimoro achiel kende ama akoko gine munyo achungo i dyer jo ni, ‘Wimon kodan nyaka ni rupiri ayeyo ni jomotho jobino chierino aka amomiyo wiosa an konon.’ ”
44024022	Gikenyo Felik, monwaŋo otyek tito ri go maber kwoŋ Royo no, ochiego winjo banja. Owacho ri jo ni, “Abino thumo banja mewin ka jaserikale madwoŋ Lisya otundo.”
44024023	Ooro jaserikale monwaŋo ni gi Paulo kuro go, munyo miyoye go syem moro aka yeyo merin pere kelo ri go gima go yenyo.
44024024	Munyo ndelo mogo okadho Felik obino gi chiege Durosila, mobedo Nyajayudaya. Felik ooro jomogo lwoŋo Paulo bothe to winjo gima go wacho kwoŋ yeyo Kristo Yesu.
44024025	To munyo Paulo ochako gi luwo kwoŋ tiro, kurok, kodi bino pa ndelo ma thumo banja, lworo omako Felik to wacho ni, “Ere onyo eye, abino lwoŋin kendo ka alimo hongo.”
44024026	I hongo no go onwaŋo geno ni kono di Paulo omiyoye go pesa moro; ri ameno go oido lwoŋo Paulo adhik luwo gine.
44024027	Munyo oro aryo okadho, Porusyo Festo olunjo kapa Felik paka gavana. Felik onwaŋo mito mako mere kodi Joyudaya, amomiyo oweyo Paulo i jera.
44025001	Munyo ndelo adek okadho wok chuka Festo tundi i adech no, go owok Kaisareya to kidho Yerusalem.
44025002	Kenyo jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jotel pa Joyudaya jokelo ri go wach pajo kwoŋ Paulo. Jokwayo Festo
44025003	ni wotimi ri jo bero woyeyi wokel Paulo Yerusalem, rupiri oido joyiko neko go i royo.
44025004	Festo odwoko ni, “Paulo nitye i twech Kaisareya, aka awon abino gik koro mayot.
44025005	Weyi jotel mewin jowokidhi kodan Kaisareya to joosa go gi koro, k'inen go otimo racho moro.”
44025006	Festo odoko ochowo ndelo aboro kosa apar gi jo, aka nyaka okidho Kaisareya. Yawere mere go obedo piny i kapido, to oro jo kelo Paulo.
44025007	Munyo Paulo otundo, Joyudaya moido jowok Yerusalem jochungo jothoko go to jochako kiosa go wach madongo momore ma jokonyalo wodho adyeri mere.
44025008	To Paulo pyemo gi jo ni, “Fuodi akitimo racho moro kwoŋ Chik pa Joyudaya, kosa Ot pa Were, kosa kwoŋ Kaisar Kere pa Joroma.”
44025009	Festo oido mito limo fuoy bongi Joyudaya, ri ameno openjo Paulo ni, “Iyenyo kidho Yerusalem wawinji banja perin me gi koro?”
44025010	Paulo owacho ni, “Kole ama onyo ee achungo i kapido pa Kaisar won, kama ripere ni wowinj'iye banja paran. Akitimo racho moro ri Joyudaya paka iwon iŋeyo.
44025011	K'inen aturo Chik aka atimo gimoro ma miyan aripo gi tho, d'akikway ni abudhere. To ka adyeri angoye gi racho i wach ma joosa an iye, ongoye ŋata nyalo kethan i chingi jo. Onyo akodo wach paran bongi Kaisar.”
44025012	Gikenyo munyo Festo otyeko luwo kodi joma jomiyo go ryeko, odwoko ni, “Ikodo banja perin bongi kere, amomiyo ibino kidho bongi kere.”
44025013	Rumachien Kere Aguripa kodi Barunike jobino Kaisareya jolo Festo.
44025014	Munyo jochowo kenyo ndelo mogo, Festo otito ri kere wach pa Paulo ni, “Nitye dhano ka ma Felik oweyo i twech;
44025015	aka munyo akidho Yerusalem jotel pa jachwayi ri Were wi alitar kodi jotel pa Joyudaya joosa go bongan aka jokwayan ni athumi banja woloyi go.
44025016	To awacho ri jo ni, ‘Joroma jokibol dhano woko ka fuodi go konenere awaŋ g'awaŋ gi joma osa go to won kutho osere gi jo.’
44025017	Munyo jojye jobino ka, akigalo, to yawere mere abedo i kapido to aoro jo kelo go.
44025018	Joma osa go jochungo, to jokokelo kwoŋe recho mogo monwaŋo aparo ni di jokelo.
44025019	Gimobedo oido a nyaka pyem kwoŋ Chik pajo ma nyadin kodi kwoŋ nyatoro motho milwoŋo ni Yesu ma Paulo ŋoyo nike fuodi kwo.
44025020	Akinyalo ridho royo ma nwaŋo adyeri kwoŋ gikipiny me, amomiyo apenjo Paulo ka d'oyeyo kidho Yerusalem wowinji wach pere me gi koro.
44025021	To Paulo wodho ywak pere nike woweyi go i jera aka Kaisar ama wowinji banja pere. Amomiyo awodho or ni wokur go tundo ndir ma d'adhir'iye go bongi Kaisar.”
44025022	Aguripa owacho ri Festo ni, “Awon amito winjo wach pa jal me.” Festo odwoko ni, “Inowinji go dikin.”
44025023	Yawere mere Aguripa gi Barunike jobino gi noro gi dwoŋ moasere, aka jodonjo i kapido kodi ruodhe ma lweny kodi jomadongo ma tindi. Festo owodho or to ikelo Paulo i kapido.
44025024	Festo owacho ni, “Kere Aguripa, kodi ji jye ma wini ka gi wan, wineno ŋata Joyudaya jye, ma ka kodi ma Yerusalem joosa go bongan? Jokoko malo nike wokiri womedere gi kwo!
44025025	To akinyalo nwaŋo recho moro ma go otimo ma ripere gi wach ma tho. To paka go won okodo wach pere bongi Kere madwoŋ, aridho nike abino dhiro go bonge.
44025026	To angoye kodi gima nyatirtir manondiki kwoŋe ri kere madwoŋ, Kaisar. Amomiyo, akelo go ka ruwaŋ win, to tektek mere ruwaŋin, Kere Aguripa! Aka ka ityeko kikaŋasa wach pere, nyaka anobedi kodi gima anondiki.
44025027	Ato kineen motire dhiro jatwech ma konyuthi maber wach mios'iye go.”
44026001	Aguripa owacho ri Paulo ni, “Oyeyin luwo wach perin.” Paulo oryeyo chinge aka owodho wach pere ama:
44026002	“Kere Aguripa! Atero paka a jasilwany ni konon abino luwo wach ma kwanyan woko kwoŋ gikipiny jye ma Joyudaya joluwo kwoŋan.
44026003	Ato me obedo rundir, kwoŋbedo iŋeyo maber kula pa Joyudaya kodi dhawirok pajo. Amomiyo akwayin idiy chunyin iwinji wach paran.
44026004	“Joyudaya jye joŋeyo kwo paran wok i thino. Joŋeyo wok chon ni i kwo paran gipi abedo i piny paran won kodi i Yerusalem.
44026005	Ndir jye joŋeyo, ka joyeyo ridho ri win, ni yado onwaŋo abedo jakweth pa joma jomako swa din mawan, Jofarisayo.
44026006	Aka onyo achungo ka munyo iosa an ni rupiri ageno i chikirok ma Were otimo gi kwarere mawan;
44026007	chikirok ma nonin mawan apar g'aryo jye jogeno limo, paka jolamo Were wor g'odyechieŋ. Aka ru geno me, Jadwoŋ, amomiyo Joyudaya joosa an!
44026008	Raŋo tek ri win yeyo ni Were chierino jomotho?
44026009	“An won onwaŋo yado aparo ni aripo timo gimoro jye ma nyalere ma lwenyo gi nyingi Yesu ma Nazareth.
44026010	Aka meno a gima yado atimo i Yerusalem. Jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar oido jomiyan men aka atweyo kir ji pa Were mathoth i jera; aka kimeno kende, ka ithumo ri jo banja ma tho, abende agoyo kwir mere.
44026011	I ndir momore amiyo jo limo girachula i kalamo pa Joyudaya jye, aka atemo miyo jo kwedirok kwoŋ yeyo pajo. Keme omakan swa gi jo momiyo akidho kir i tindi ma wiloka lwenyo gi jo.”
44026012	“Gime amoido teran i Damasiko chungo kwoŋ men kodi or pa jotel pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar.
44026013	Munyo fuodi oido ani royo odyechieŋ, jadwoŋ, aneno lero ma loyo apa waŋchieŋ mowok malo to thoko wan kodi ji monwaŋo awotho gi jo.
44026014	Wajojye wagore piny, aka awinjo dwondi jo mowacho ran i Dhoyudaya ni, ‘Saulo, Saulo! Ilwenyo kodan raŋo? Iwon itimo gima kelo rin ayino litho, pa mirikwa ma temo gweyo kwer manyweny gi tyende.’
44026015	Apenjo ni, ‘In iŋa, Ruoth?’ Aka Ruoth odwoko ni, ‘An Yesu ma ilwenyo gine.
44026016	Onyo ayi ichungi gi tyendin. Amenyere rin ma lokin jatich paran iwachi ri joman gimomiyo konon inenan kodi giman jye ma anonyuthin yuwaŋe.
44026017	Abino bothin i chingi ji ma Israel kodi Jopath, ma adhirin bongi jo
44026018	ni iyaw waŋ jo jowonyali wirok wok i mudho donjo i lero kodi wok i men pa Sitan bino bongi Were, ŋey jowonyali limo chwak kwoŋ gimarecho pajo to jolimo kabedo i dyer joma Were oyero munyo joyeyan.’ ”
44026019	“Amomiyo, Kere Aguripa, akichayo menyirok mowok i polo ma aneno.
44026020	Atero wach me marapena i Damasiko, nyaka t'atero Yerusalem, kodi rumachien i Yudeya gipi, kodi i piny pa Jopath, ni joripo ŋuto gimarecho pajo jowowire bongi Were, gi timo gikipiny ma nyutho nike jotyeko ŋuto.
44026021	Wach no amomiyo Joyudaya jomakan munyo anitye i Ot pa Were to jotemo nekan.
44026022	To kir konon Were okonyan, amomiyo achungo ka munyo aridho wach me ri ji jye, ri jomathindho kodi jomadongo parom. Gima awacho obedo gimoro achiel ma jotuchi wach Were kodi Musa jowacho ni bino timere,
44026023	nike Kristo ripo chandere, aka ka otyeko bedo marapena i chierino kwoŋ jomotho, wokeli lero ma both ri Joyudaya kodi Jopath.”
44026024	Munyo Paulo fuodi osa ri kwo pere ameno, Festo okoko ri go ni, “Paulo, ijaneko! Fuonjirok perin madit no olokin janeko!”
44026025	Paulo odwoko ni, “Akijaneko Jadwoŋ! Wach m'aluwo obedo adyeri odoko aluwo wach me m'anitye milengela.
44026026	Kole Kere Aguripa oŋeyo gikipiny me, aka anyalo luwo kodi go gi misen jye. Aridho ni go otyeko kikaŋasa gikipiny me jye, rupiri gime kotimere nyaliŋliŋ yu tyelo.
44026027	Kere Aguripa, iyeyo wach pa jotuchi wach Were? Aŋeyo ni iyeyo.”
44026028	Gikenyo Aguripa owacho ri Paulo ni, “I hongo machiek won me iparo ni inyalo lokan Jakristo?”
44026029	Paulo odwoko ni, “Kada me hongo ma chiek kosa ma bor, kwayo paran bongi Were obedo ni in kodi wijojye ma wiwinjan konon ka winyali bedo paka an, to kareno ma kotwey win gi lijegere ayino.”
44026030	Gikenyo kere, gavana, Barunike kodi joman jye moido jobedo kenyo gi jo joay malo;
44026031	aka munyo jotyeko eye kenyo, wegi jowacho kendigin ni, “Ŋatin kotimo gimoro ma di miy woneki kosa tweyo go.”
44026032	Aka Aguripa owacho ri Festo ni, “Ŋat me d'onyo ogony bedi kokodo wach pere bongi Kaisar.”
44027001	Munyo oridhi nike wachiewere i nam wakidhi yu Italya, joketho Paulo kodi jomotwey mogo i chingi Julyo, jaserikale i lwak jolweny ma Roma milwoŋo ni, “Lwak jolweny pa Kaisar Agusto.”
44027002	Wadonjo i mel ma wok Aduramityo, monwaŋo chiegin ay wokidhi loka ma yu adech ma Asya, gikenyo to waay. Aristaruko, Jamasedonia ma Thesalonika, onwaŋo ni gi wan.
44027003	Yawere mere watundo Sidon. Julyo otimo wor gi Paulo to yeyo go kidho neno merin pere, jowomiyi go gim'oyenyo.
44027004	Wok kenyo wamedere gi chiewirok, to paka koyo onwaŋo kudho wok yu wiy wan, wachiewere yu thenge ma kigoda ma Sipuro kama koyo oido ongoy'iye.
44027005	Munyo watyeko chiewirok i nam kalo Silisya gi Panfilya, wabino Mira, i adech ma Lisya.
44027006	Kenyo jaserikale onwaŋo yee mowok Alekizandurya moido chiegin ay wokidhi yu Italya, to rwako wan iye.
44027007	Wachiewere mothmoth ndelo moromoye, aka rumachien i teko madwoŋ watundo dho tindi ma Kunido. To paka koyo koyeyo wan medirok yu thenge no, wachiewere yu thenge ma koyo ongoy'iye yu Salmon dho geŋin ma kigoda ma Kurete.
44027008	Warikere i thengi nam, aka i teko madwoŋ watundo kama ilwoŋo ni, “Thengi nam Maber”, ma kibor kodi tindi ma Laseya.
44027009	Paka hongo onwaŋo okadho malach, aka ndelo ma madwoŋ ma chwako recho oido otyeko kadho, odoko medirok gi chiewirok oido nyalo kelo teko, Paulo omiyo jo ryeko ni,
44027010	“Jowotan, aneno ni chiewirok mawan kidho kelo teko yu malo aka gikipiny madit bino nyiekere i mel, aka ki meno kende, to kir wan won bende wanyalo podho i teko.”
44027011	To jaserikale omedo tich gi wach pa jadwoŋ ma mel kodi won yee loyo gi ryeko ma Paulo oido okelo.
44027012	Paka kachungo pa mel i thengi nam no onwaŋo kiber bed'iye i ndir ma pe ŋich'iye piny, ji maloyo thotho jofuoyo dhirok i nam gi temo tundo yu Fenisya ka nyalere. Kanyago obedo kachungo pa mel i Kurete ma ŋiyo yu Wich piny i thenge ma yu rachuch kodi i Tyendi piny yu thenge ma yu rachuch bende, aka ka oido nyalere, di wabedo kenyo i hongo ma ŋicho no.
44027013	Koyo mawok yu Tyendi piny ochako kudho, aka ji joparo ni di jonyalo tiyo gi chan pajo; ameno joywayo gima juko ye to jochiewere gi dho geŋin ma thengi Kurete.
44027014	To piyo piyo koyo madwoŋ, milwoŋo ni Koyo ma wok yu rachuch ma Wich piny, okudho munyo loro wok i kigoda.
44027015	Koyo no ogoyo mel, aka paka oido kinyalere choro mel yu kama koyo wok'iye, chuny wan oeye to waweyo koyo kadho gi wan.
44027016	Walimo kagoŋirok moro munyo wachomo yu geŋin ma kigoda mathin milwoŋo ni Kauda. Kenyo watemo gi mbaka to wanyalo gwoko ye monwaŋo waywayo yu chien.
44027017	Munyo jotyeko ywayo yee gi tiŋo malo, jotemo kikoda mel matek gi thondhe kwoŋ geŋin. To paka oido jolworo nike jonyalo gurok i kwoyo dho thengi pi ma Libya, jolwogo nanga ma chiewirok to joweyo koyo won kadho gi mel.
44027018	Munyo koyo madwoŋ onwaŋo wito wan gi men, yawere mere jochako bolo woko gikipiny ma yee onwaŋo otiŋo,
44027019	aka yawere mere jobolo woko gikipiny michiewo gine mel gi chingi jo.
44027020	Ndelo okadho madit ma wakineno waŋchieŋ kosa michalin, aka koyo omedere gi kudho gi men. Rumachien chuny wan oeye kir kwoŋ kwo mawan.
44027021	Munyo ji onwaŋo jotyeko riyo kech ndelo madit, Paulo ochungo i dyer jo to wacho ni, “Jowotan, di chieŋino wiwinjo wach paran to wiweyo chiewirok wok Kurete; aka di wanyalo geŋo nyiekirok kodi rwenyo pa gikipiny me jye.
44027022	To onyo akwayo win, bedi win miseni! Ongoye ŋat moro kwoŋ win ma bino rwenyo kwo pere; to mel kende ama bino rwenyo,
44027023	rupiri nende wor malaika pa Were ma an alamo aka abedo apere obino bongan,
44027024	to wacho ni, ‘Paulo, ikiri ibedi gi lworo! Iripo chungo ruwaŋ Kaisar; aka Were, i bero pere, otyeko miyin kwo pa ji jye m'ichiewere gi jo me!’
44027025	Amomiyo, jowotan, bedi win miseni, rupiri ani gi geno i Were ni gime bino bedo paka awacho ri win won.
44027026	To waripo chombo kwoŋ kigoda moro.”
44027027	I wor marapar g'aŋwen, munyo koyo oido fuodi wito wan i nam ma Mediterania, dho dyer wor, jochiewi yee joŋicho nike oido wariko kamothwo.
44027028	Ri ameno jobolo piny tal motwey kwoŋe tele mapek to jonwaŋo ni lutho ma pendi pi oido obedo fut miya achiel gi pyero aryo. I kare moro kenyo jodoko jobolo tal to jonwaŋo ni pendi pi obedo fut pyero abuŋwen.
44027029	Munyo lworo omako jo ni mel mawan nyalo guro telin, jocharo piny gikipiny aŋwen ma juko yee gi yuchien wochungi to jokwayo ni piny woyawere.
44027030	Gikenyo jochiewi mel jotemo kwalok wok i mel; jobolo yee mathin i pi to jorendere nike oido jokidho wodho woko gikipiny ma juko yee ma yunyime.
44027031	To Paulo owacho ri jaserikale madwoŋ gi joserikale man ni, “Ka jochiewi mel jokodoŋ i mel ka wakinyal both.”
44027032	Gikenyo joserikale jothumo woko thondhe monwaŋo mako yee mathin no to joweyo kadho.
44027033	Munyo piny kidho yawirok, Paulo okwayo jojye ni jowochiemiye. “Wityeko riyo kech ndelo apar g'aŋwen pama, aka hongo no jye wikichamo gimoro.
44027034	Amomiyo akwayo win, chami wiye gimoro aka winwaŋi men rupiri ongoye kada yer achiel ma wiy win ma bino rwenyo.”
44027035	Munyo otyeko wacho ameno, Paulo okwanyo mugat, oketho Were walwa ruwaŋ jojye, to turo, to chako chamo.
44027036	Miseni omako jo, to dhano jye chamoye chiemo moro.
44027037	Wajojye oido waromo ji miya aryo gi pyero abiryo g'auchiel i mel no.
44027038	Munyo dhano jye otyeko chiemo, joloko mel masew munyo jobolo woko ŋano i wakawaka.
44027039	Munyo piny oyawere, jochiewi mel oido jokoniaŋ ni kamothwo ni chiegin, to joneno choŋino kodi kamonaŋere ma di kwoyo i thengi nam to joridho paro ni kanyalere di jotero mel kenyo.
44027040	Gikenyo jobolo gichien gikipiny ma juko mel to joweyo i pi, to bende jogonyo woko thondhe monwaŋo omako yath mitiro gine royo i mel. Gikenyo jotiŋo malo nanga machiewo yee to joyaro to koyo chako tero mel i choŋino.
44027041	To nyim mel oguro kwoyo ma piny to donj'iye, to moko ma kidhire kareno pi ma tula gi derino ŋinyo woko mbawin mogeti gine mel gi yuchien.
44027042	Joserikale joparo neko woko jotwech jye ŋey wongoye kwoŋ jo ŋata wokwale.
44027043	To jaserikale madwoŋ onwaŋo mito botho Paulo, amomiyo ochiero jo timo ameno. Kuchiel, ooro ji jye ma jonyalo buko pi jowopeni por iye jowobuki to jokadho.
44027044	Gikenyo nyaka jomodoŋ jowoluwi jo chien munyo jobedo wi mbawin mogo kosa adeche ma mel moturotur. Aka meno apaka wajojye wapor loka maber.
44028001	Munyo watundo loka maber, aka walimo ŋeyo nike kigoda piny no ilwoŋo ni Malta.
44028002	Ji ma kenyo josangala swa gi wan. Koth oido ochako chwe aka piny oido ŋich swa, amomiyo jomoko ri wan mach to jolwoŋo wan oyo.
44028003	Paulo onwaŋo otyeko dimo agwere mogo to ketho i mach, to thwol uu moro wok ru lyetho pa mach, to minere i chinge to moko gine.
44028004	Munyo ji ma kenyo joneno thwol no olyero i chingi Paulo, wegi jowacho kendigin ni, “Ŋat me ripo bedo ni go janek, rupiri kada oido oboth nam, jye fuodi tipo kiyey ni go wobothi.”
44028005	To Paulo owito woko thwol no i mach ma kotimo kwoŋe racho moro.
44028006	Onwaŋo jokuro neno go ka kwoŋe yenyo gi kwir kosa gore piny arwat gi tho. To munyo jotyeko kuro chowo hongo malach ma jokoneno gimoro jye ka timere kwoŋe, jowiro paro pajo to jowacho ni, “Go were moro!”
44028007	Chiegin kenyo oido nitye ndelo mogo mobedo apa Pubulyo, ruoth ma kigoda no. Go ojolo wan maber to wabedo wendo pere chowo hongo ma ndelo adek.
44028008	Baa Pabulyo oido ni kanindo kwoŋe oowere odoko iye ryemo. Paulo odonjo i ot pere, okwayo Were, to ketho chinge kwoŋe to botho go.
44028009	Munyo gime otimere, jotwo man jye i kigoda no jobino to jolimo both.
44028010	Jomiyo wan mich madit, aka munyo wachiewere joketho ri wan i yee no gimoro jye monwaŋo wayenyo i chiewirok mawan.
44028011	Munyo dwe adek okadho, wachiewere i mel wok Alekizandurya i mel milwoŋo ni, “Wutimere Marut” moywomere i kigoda no i ndir ma pe oido oŋich'iye piny.
44028012	Watundo i tindi ma Sirakuse to wabedo kenyo ndelo adek.
44028013	Wok kenyo wathokere gi chiewirok to watundo i tindi ma Rejum. Yawere mere koyo ochako kudho wok yu Tyendi piny, to kada ameno watundo i tindi ma Puteyoli i hongo ma ndelo aryo.
44028014	Wanwaŋo jomoyeyo jowoti wan mogo kenyo ma jokwayo nike wabedi gi jo ma sabiti achiel. Wok kenyo aka watundo Roma.
44028015	Jomoyeyo jowot wan ma Roma jowinjo kwoŋ wan to jobino romo gi wan i karomo milwoŋo ni Apiya kodi man ni Udi Machiemo Adek. Munyo Paulo oneno jo, ofuoyo Were to limo miseni.
44028016	Munyo watundo Roma, oyey Paulo bedo kakende gi jaserikale ma kuro go.
44028017	Munyo ndelo adek okadho, Paulo olwoŋo jotel pa Joyudaya ma kenyo i romo. Munyo jochokere owacho ri jo ni, “Wutimera! Kada oido akitimo racho moro ri ji mawan kosa kwoŋ kula ma wanwaŋo kwoŋ kwarere mawan, olokan jatwech i Yerusalem to ikethan i chingi Joroma.
44028018	Munyo jokaŋasa wach paran oido jomito gonyan, rupiri jonwaŋo ni akitimo racho moro ma di miyan atho.
44028019	To munyo joyudaya jopyemo gi paro me, aneno ni aripo kodo wach paran bongi Kaisar kada onwaŋo awon angoye ran gi wach m'aosa ji paran.
44028020	Ri ameno akwayo neno win gi luwo gi win, rupiri anitye gi lijegere me kwoŋan ru wach ma Joisrael jogeno kwoŋe.”
44028021	Jowacho ri go ni, “Fuodi wakilimo balwa mogo jye wok bongi Joyudaya ma mako kwoŋin, aka ongoye kada omin wan moro jye mowok koro gi wach moro, kosa moluwo gimoro marach kwoŋin.
44028022	To wamito winjo gima iwacho rupiri kamoro jye ji joluwo marach kwoŋ kweth me ma initye iye.”
44028023	Gikenyo joyiko ndelo gi Paulo, to ji kweth kwoŋ jo jobino i ndelo no kama Paulo oido bed'iye. Wok odikini tundo othyeno, Paulo otito ri jo mikwenda kwoŋ Ker pa Were. Otemo paka onyalo miyo jo ŋeyo maber kwoŋ Yesu munyo kwanyo wach i Chik pa Musa kodi i ndiiko pa jotuchi wach Were.
44028024	Jomegi kwoŋ jo joyeyo i chuny gin kwoŋ wach pere, to joman jokoyeyo.
44028025	Gikenyo joeye gi pyem i dyer jo wegi kendigin munyo Paulo otyeko wacho gimoro achiel me: “Chuny Maleŋ chango otire munyo luwo gi i dhok Isaya jatuchi wach Were ri kwarere mewin ni,
44028026	‘Kole Were owacho ni, Kidhi iwachi ri jome ni, Wibino winjo adyeri, to wikoniaŋ dwoŋ gima wiwinjo; Wibino ŋiyo adyeri, to waŋ win konen gimoro.
44028027	Kwoŋbedo paro pa jome olokere ma fuol. Jotyeko chulo ithi gin, to jomiyo waŋ gin. Bedi k'ameno, waŋ gin d'oneno gimoro, odoko ithi gin d'owinjo wach, aka chuny jo d'oniaŋ gimoro. Ameno di jonyalo wirok bongan to jolimo both.’ ”
44028028	Aka Paulo omedo ni, “Wiripo ŋeyo nike mikwenda pa Were kwoŋ both odhir ri Jopath; aka jobino winjo!”
44028029	[Munyo Paulo owacho ameno, Joyudaya joeye, munyo wegi jopyemo kendigin matek.]
44028030	Paulo obedo kenyo oro aryo munyo won chowo teko pere, aka ojolo ji jye ma jobino lyewo go,
44028031	to tito kwoŋ Ker pa Were to fuonjo kwoŋ Ruoth Yesu Kristo munyo luwo gi miseni jye kodi syem.
45001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, jatich pa Yesu Kristo kendo jamoor ma Were oyero to lwoŋo fuonjo Wach Maber pere,
45001002	ma Were chango ochiko munyo oro jotuchi wach pere, tiketho i Ndiiko Maleŋ.
45001003	Me obedo Wach Maber ma mako kwoŋ Wuode, Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo, monywole paka nyakwar Daudi;
45001004	to inyutho ji ni go obedo Wuodi Were gi men madwoŋ mapa Chuny ma kelo leŋo, munyo ochierino go kwoŋ jomotho.
45001005	I go Were omiyan silwany ma bedo jamoor ri Kristo, ŋey atel ji ma nonin jye jowoyeyi odoko jowowinji or.
45001006	Me bende mako win ma winitye Roma, ma Were olwoŋo bedo ji pa Yesu Kristo.
45001007	Amomiyo andiko ri wijojye mani Roma ma Were omaro to lwoŋo bedo ji pere won; Weyi Were Bawan kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo womiyi win ŋono gi syem.
45001008	Marapena afuoyo Were paran, i Yesu Kristo, ri wijojye; rupiri piny gipi winjo kwoŋ yeyo mewin.
45001009	Were nyalo ridho ni gima awacho obedo adyeri; Were no ama atiyo ri go gi chunyan jye munyo afuonjo Wach Maber kwoŋ Wuode. Were oŋeyo nike ndir jye apoyo win, i hongo jye ka akwayo.
45001010	Akwayo nike Were i mito pere, i hongo moro womiyaye thwolo ma limo win.
45001011	Kole ayenyo swa neno win ŋey anyal poko gi win silwany machuny, ma medo win men.
45001012	Dwoŋ mere ni win, kodan, wabino nwaŋo kony kiromo, win i yeyo paran aka an i yeyo mewin.
45001013	Poyi win gime wutimera: ndir mathoth ayiko bino limo win, to hongo jye gimoro geŋan bino. Atyeko yenyo swa ywayo jomegi i yeyo i dyer win bende, paka atyeko timo i dyer Jopath.
45001014	Kole or omakan matek kwoŋ ji jye, kwoŋ jokite mabeyo kodi jomarecho, kwoŋ jomofuonjere kodi joma kuya gimoro.
45001015	Amomiyo ayenyo swa fuonjo win bende ma winitye Roma Wach Maber.
45001016	Kole ageno swa Wach Maber, rupiri obedo men pa Were ma botho ji jye majoyeyo, marapena Joyudaya, aka nyaka Jopath bende.
45001017	Kole Wach Maber nyutho paka Were ketho ji i tiro gine ma bedo i yeyo, wok i chakirok tundo i gike. Ato randik wacho ni, “Ŋata oketh i tiro gi Were bino kwo gi yeyo.”
45001018	Were otyeko nyutho ni keme pere bino wok i polo to lwenyo gi recho jye kodi tim pa ji marecho ma royo pajo marecho geŋo adyeri ŋeyirok.
45001019	Were miyo jo girachula rupiri gima ji jonyalo ŋeyo kwoŋ Were nitye kamaler ri jo.
45001020	Chuka Were chwey piny, kada go won kinenere i men pere ma chil gi chil kodi i kite ma nyawerewere, gima nyutho ni go nitye nenere i gikipiny ma go ochweyo. Amomiyo dhano ongoye kodi gi goŋirok!
45001021	Ji joŋeyo Were, to jokimiy go dwoŋ pere, kendo kada temo fuoyo go ni walwa. Kuchiel, paro pajo olokere masisiri aka paro pajo ma kitiy modoŋ mudho otyeko poŋ'iye.
45001022	Jowacho ni joryek, to kere jomiŋ ayin;
45001023	kama di jolam Were makitho, jolamo ri gin gima othedhi i chal pa dhano matho, kosa apa winyin, kosa apa ogwange kosa apa thwole ayino.
45001024	Paka ji jomiŋ ameno, Were ojala jo jowotim gikipiny marecho ma chuny gin yenyo, aka jotimo gikipiny ma kelo wichkwot i del pajo, ŋat man gi nyawote.
45001025	Jowilo adyeri kwoŋ Were gi twodo; jolamo aka jotiyo ri gima Were ochweyo kapa lamo Jachwech won, miripo pako chil gi chil. Ameno.
45001026	Paka ji jotimo gime, Were ojala jo to weyo jo ri awanya makelo wichkwot. Kir mon bende jowiro or ma delkwoŋ gin munyo joweyo riwirok i del i yo motire to joriwere wegi kendigin, mobedo yo ma kotire.
45001027	Ameno, chwo bende joweyo riwirok gi mon paka ndir jye, to joowere g'awanya kwoŋ chwo wadi gin. Chwo jotimo wichkwot gi chwo wadi gin, amomiyo Were miyo jo girachula rundir ru tim pajo marecho no.
45001028	Paka ji jokwero ketho i paro pajo ryeko maradyeri ma mako kwoŋ Were, go onyo ojala jo ri paro motop, ma miyo jo timo gima oido jokiripi timo.
45001029	Joasere gi recho ma nger jye, racho, woro, kodi chamo tyendi ji gi piny; joasere gi nyieko, nek, gorok, twodo, paro marecho kwoŋ dhano. Jonyieko nyingi wadi gin,
45001030	aka joluwo kichar kwoŋ ji; jodak Were, joyetere, jobedo jopakirok, jokwoto; joparo yo momore ma timo recho; aka jokiwinji jonywol pajo;
45001031	jodakana, jokikur chikirok pajo, jokinyuthi wor odoko jokidew kwoŋ nyatoro.
45001032	Joŋeyo kir ni chik pa Were wacho ni ji ma kwo pajo chalo ameno joripere gi tho, to jye fuodi nyaka jomedere ameda gi timo gikipiny no won; aka maloyo racho: jofuoyo joman ma bende jotimo ameno.
45002001	Jowotan, withumo banja ri jowoti wini? Kere onyo wingoye gi kagoŋirok, kada wibedi jokune! Ato ka withumo banja ri jowoti win mato wibende witimo gikipiny marom gi ma jotimo, meno wiwegi withumere banja loyo win.
45002002	Waŋeyo ni Were otire ka thumo banja ri joma timo gikipiny ma pameno.
45002003	Nyawotan, iparo nike ka itimo gikipiny no won ma ithum'iye banja ri jowotin, inobothi kwoŋ thumo banja pa Were?
45002004	Kosa miti ichayo bero pere moasere, ka diyo chunye gi ji aka kudere. Adyeri wiŋeyo ni Were ber rupiri go temo tero win i ŋuto!
45002005	To initye gi wichtek aka chunyin di chay. Amomiyo iwon imiyo girachula perin lebedo madwoŋ swa i ndelo ma keme pa Were bino nyuther'iye ma thumo banja maradyeri.
45002006	Kole Were bino miyo dhano jye kemba chungo kwoŋ gima go otimo.
45002007	Ji megi hongo jye jotimo gimabeyo, aka jorango dwoŋ pa Were gi wor kodi kwo makirum; aka Were bino miyo jo kwo makirum.
45002008	Ji man joparo kwoŋ bero pajo wegi to jokwero gimotire, aka jotimo gima kotire. Jono Were bino konjo kwoŋ jo keme pere gi jok swa.
45002009	Chandirok gi litho bino bedo ri ji jye ma jotimo recho, kutho marapena ri Joyudaya, aka nyaka ri Jopath bende.
45002010	To Were bino miyo dwoŋ kodi wor gi syem ri nyatoro jye ma timo gimabeyo, marapena ri Joyudaya ŋey wotimi ri Jopath bende.
45002011	Kole Were tero ji jye marom.
45002012	Jopath, ma jongoye kodi Chik pa Musa, jotimo gimarecho aka jobino rwenyo bende mongoye Chik. Joyudaya ma jo ni gi Chik, jotimo gimarach aka ilethumo ri jo banja chungo kwoŋ Chik no.
45002013	Ato kobedo nyaka i winjo Chik gi ithi jo ama miyo iketho ji i tiro gi Were, to i timo gima Chik mito ayino.
45002014	Jopath jongoye gi Chik; to ka hongo jye gi yero pajo jotimo gima Chik mito, meno nyutho ni Chik tiyo i chuny jo, kada oido jongoye gi Chik.
45002015	Kite pajo nyutho ni gima Chik mito ondik i chuny jo. Paro pajo mani chuny jo bende nyutho ni gime otire, rupiri paro pajo dichieŋ miyo jo ŋeyo ni jonyieko wach kosa be.
45002016	Onyo, chungo kwoŋ Wach Maber m'afuonjo, me apaka bino bedo i ndelo no munyo Were, i Yesu Kristo, bino thumo banja ri paro ma nyaliŋliŋ jye ma chuny ji.
45002017	Aka in to? Ilwoŋere ni Jayudaya; ithenere kwoŋ Chik aka iyumere gi Were;
45002018	K'iŋeyo gima Were mito ni itim, aka ityeko fuonjere kwoŋ Chik yero gimotire;
45002019	aka k'iridho adyeri ni iripo nyutho joma waŋ gin otho royo paka lero pa joma nitye i mudho,
45002020	ibedo jatiri jomamiŋ g'adyeri, odoko ibedo jafuonji pa joma fuodi jokotegino. Iridho ni ini gi ryeko moromo, kodi adyeri ma wok i Chik.
45002021	Onyo in m'ifuonjo joman no, raŋo iwon ikifuonjere? K'ifuonjo nike, “Ikiri ikwal,” iwon odoko ikwalo nedi?
45002022	In miwacho ni, “Ikiri itim chot,” iwon idoko itimo chot nedi? In midak lamo chal ma kichar, idoko inyaga gikipiny wok i migam milam'iye werin mogo nedi?
45002023	In miyumere ni ini gi chik pa Were, raŋo midoko ikelo wichkwot ri Were kareno ituro chik pere?
45002024	Kole ondik ni, “Ru kiti win Joyudaya, amomiyo Jopath joluwo marach kwoŋ nyingi Were.”
45002025	Kole ka wiwinjo Chik, meno aka nyaka thumirok mewin di kony; to ka wituro Chik, meno kole thumirok mewin onyo chale pa kobedo thumirok.
45002026	Amomiyo ka Japath ma kothumere timo gima Chik mito, meno onyo Were kiter go paka ŋatothumere?
45002027	Aka Jopath jobino thumo banja woloyi win Joyudaya, rupiri kada wini gi Chik aka withumere jye fuodi wituro, kuchiel jo ama jowinjo Chik kada jokothumere.
45002028	Kere ŋa m'onyo obedo Jayudaya maradyer, m'othumere? Ŋata obedo Jayudaya nyaka gi thumirok mawoko meno ki Jayudaya maradyer, odoko thumirok maradyeri kobedo mitimo nyaka gi woko kende.
45002029	Kuchiel Jayudaya maradyeri meno mobedo Jayudaya i chunye, mothumere i chunye, aka meno tich pa Chuny Maleŋ pa Were, ma kiweno apa Chik mondik. Ŋato limo pak bongi Were, ma kiweno bongi dhano.
45003001	Onyo Joyudaya joloyo joman i yo mene? Kosa kony aŋo ma nitye i thumirok?
45003002	Nitye bero moromo ma bedo Jayudaya. Kutho marapena, Were ogeno Joyudaya to miyo jo mikwenda pere.
45003003	Aŋo to, ka jomegi kwoŋ jo jobedo joma kigenere? Onyo ru gino, nyutho ni Were kigenere?
45003004	Kameno be! Weyi Were wobedi jaradyeri kada dhano jye obedi jatwodo. Paka ondik ni, “Aka ŋey wonyuthere paka gima iluwo otire, aka iloy banja ka i pido kodin.”
45003005	Onyo wanowachi nedi ka tim mawan makotire konyo ma nyutho kamaler ni apa Were amotire? Wawachi ni Were timo marach ka miyo wan girachula? (Meno onyo aluwo paka dhano.)
45003006	Kameno be! Ka Were kotire nyalo nedi thumo banja ri piny?
45003007	To ka komo paran konyo ma nyutho tiro pa Were to kelo ri go dwoŋ, raŋo ma fuodi ithumo ran banja igani ajarecho?
45003008	To raŋo ma kiwachi ni, “Weyi watim recho ŋey bero wowok'iye?” Adyeri jomegi jotyeko kir yetan munyo jochwoko dhokan ni awacho ameno won! Ibino thumo banja loyo jo paka ripere.
45003009	Onyo wa Joyudaya wanitye maber i yo mene loyo Joman? Ongoye be! Atyeko nyutho ni Joyudaya kodi Jopath parom jojye jonitye i men pa gimarach,
45003010	paka ondik ni, “Ongoye dhano kada achiel motire, ongoye ma kada achiel,
45003011	ongoye moro ma niaŋ, kosa ma rango Were.
45003012	Ji jye joeye woko bongi Were, jojye jotyeko podho; Ongoye ŋata timo gimaber, ongoye kada achiel.
45003013	Dhoki jo chalo kalyel mothangere; Jooro lew jo ma twodo, aka wach ma chal kwir ama wok i dhok jo;
45003014	Dhok jo opoŋ'iye kwoŋ ma kech kodi duro.
45003015	Joyot gi kidho neko ji.
45003016	Joweyo gunda kodi rem kama jokidh'iye jye.
45003017	Fuodi jokoŋeyo yo ma syem,
45003018	odoko fuodi jokofuonjere lworo Were.”
45003019	Onyo pama watyeko ŋeyo ni gimoro jye ma Chik wacho, mako kwoŋ joma fuodi joluwo Chik, ŋey wogeŋ woko rendirok pa dhano, aka Were wonyal thumo banja ri piny gipi.
45003020	Kole ongoye dhano mibino kwano ri go tiro i waŋ Were ru nyaka timo gima Chik yenyo, rupiri Chik miyo dhano nyaka ŋeyo nike gimanyo obedo recho won kende.
45003021	To pama royo ma Were ketho gine ji i tiro gi go otyeko nyuthere, aka kimaki kwoŋ chik. Chik kodi ndiiko pa jotuchi wach Were jye joridho gima mako kwoŋ royo no.
45003022	Were ketho ji i tiro kwoŋ yeyo pajo i Yesu Kristo ayino. Were timo gime ri ji jye ma joyeyo Kristo, rupiri pokirok ongoye.
45003023	Paka ji jye jotyeko timo recho aka jo ni bor gi dwoŋ pa Were,
45003024	pama onyo ikwanyo woko banja kwoŋ ji jye ru mich ma ŋono pa Were kareno igonyo jo woko kwoŋ recho i Kristo Yesu
45003025	ma Were oketho paka rachow, ŋey gi tho pere go wolokere royo ma chwako recho pa ji chungo kwoŋ yeyo pa dhano. Were otimo ameno ma nyutho tiro pere, rupiri i ndir mokadho, go odiyo chunye to weyo ma kokwano recho pa ji;
45003026	to i ndir ma pama go kaŋasa recho pa ji, ma nyutho paka go won otire, aka go ama kwanyo woko banja kwoŋ ŋata ni gi yeyo i Yesu.
45003027	Onyo aŋo ma wanyalo yumirok gine? Kole ongoye! I royo mene? I royo ma kuro Chik? Be, i royo ma bedo gi yeyo ayino.
45003028	Ato onyo wachowo wach ni Were kwanyo woko banja kwoŋ dhano chungo kwoŋ yeyo, ma kiweno kwoŋ timo gima Chik mito.
45003029	Kosa Were obedo Were pa Joyudaya kende? Go kobedo Were pa Jopath bende? Kole go obedo Were pa Jopath bende.
45003030	Were nitye achiel, aka go bino kwanyo woko banja kwoŋ Joyudaya chungo kwoŋ yeyo pajo, aka bende bino kwanyo woko banja kwoŋ Jopath ru yeyo bende achiel no won.
45003031	Onyo nyutho ni waboli woko Chik ru yeyo me? Kameno be; kuchiel, waridhi Chik bende.
45004001	Onyo wanowachi aŋo kwoŋ Ibrayimu, kwari wan i del?
45004002	Bedi kwany woko banja kwoŋe chungo kwoŋ gikipiny ma go otimo, di go onyalo bedo kodi yumirok, to go kinyal yumere i waŋ Were.
45004003	To kere randik wacho aŋo? Ni, “Ibrayimu oyeyo Were, aka ru yeyo pere Were okwano go paka ŋatotire.”
45004004	Dhano ka tiyo ichulo go kemba ma kiter paka mich, to paka gima go otiyo ri go ayin.
45004005	To ka dhano kikethi geno kwoŋ tich pere, to ketho i yeyo Were ma kwanyo woko banja kwoŋ ji ayino, kiti yeyo no miyo ikwano ri go tiro.
45004006	Me a dwoŋ gima Daudi owacho munyo luwo kwoŋ kisangala pa ŋata Were jolo paka ŋatotire ma kokwano tich ma go otyeko timo:
45004007	“Josilwany a joma recho pajo Were otyeko chwako; joma go oumo recho pajo!
45004008	Jasilwany a ŋata Ruoth kibino kwano kwoŋe recho pere!”
45004009	Silwany ma Daudi oluwo kwoŋe me bedo apa jomothumere kende? Be. Bedo apa jomakothumere bende, rupiri watyeko nyutho wach wok i randik ni, “Ibrayimu oyeyo Were, aka ru yeyo pere Were okwano go paka ŋatotire.”
45004010	Gime otimere keraŋo? Otimere ma fuodi, kosa munyo Ibrayimu otyeko thumere? Ma fuodi, ma kiweno rumachien ma thumirok pere.
45004011	Othum go rumachien paka ranyuth ma ridho ni ru yeyo pere munyo fuodi go kothumere amomiyo Were okwano go paka ŋatotire. Meno amomiyo Ibrayimu obedo baa joma yeyo Were machuny, ma Were jolo jo paka jomotire, kada jokothumere.
45004012	Go obedo baa jomothumere bende, ki ni rupiri othum jo, to rupiri jonitye i kiti kwo ma yeyo ma Ibrayimu chango obedi'iye munyo fuodi kothum go.
45004013	Were ochiko Ibrayimu kodi nyikwaye ni piny me bino bedo apa jo. Chikirok me otim, ki ru kwoŋbedo Ibrayimu okuro Chik, to rupiri go oyeyo aka Were okwano go paka ŋatotire.
45004014	To k'inen joma kuro Chik ayino ama jobino lunjo gimochik, meno kere yeyo pa dhano ongoye kony, aka chikirok pa Were bende ongoye kony.
45004015	Chik kelo nge pa Were, to kama chik ongoy'iye, meno turo chik bende ongoye.
45004016	Ri ameno chikirok no chungo kwoŋ yeyo, ŋey wothenere kwoŋ ŋono pa Were aka womiyi nyikway Ibrayimu jye, aka ki nyaka joma jokuro Chik kende, to joma joyeyo paka chango Ibrayimu bende oyeyo. Ato Ibrayimu obedo baa wajojye ma chuny,
45004017	paka ndiiko wacho ni, “Alokin baa nonin mathoth.” Aka chikirok no otimere bongi Were won ma Ibrayimu oyeyo; Were ma chierino jomotho, ma or pere miyo gimoro ma oido ongoye chako bedo.
45004018	Ibrayimu oyeyo aka ogeno, munyo geno oido ongoye kir kony, amomiyo go olokere “Baa nonin mathoth,” paka ndiiko wacho ni, “Nyikwayin joletiŋo piny pa kweth michala.”
45004019	Oro pere oido chiegin romo miya achiel, to yeyo pere komojere munyo go oparo kwoŋ delkwoŋe monwaŋo chal p'otyeko tho, kosa munyo oneno ni Sara oido kinyal limo nyithindho.
45004020	Yeyo pere korumo, aka go koganagana kwoŋ chikirok pa Were; yeyo pere opoŋo kwoŋ go men, to fuoyo Were,
45004021	rupiri go oido oridho kichutho ni Were bino timo gima go otyeko chiko.
45004022	Meno amomiyo, ru yeyo pa Ibrayimu, Were okwano go paka ŋatotire.
45004023	Wach me ni, “Okwan go,” kondik ri Ibrayimu kende.
45004024	Ondik ri wan bende ma ibino kwano wan paka jomotire, wan ma wayeyo Ŋata ochierino Yesu Ruodhiwan kwoŋ jomotho.
45004025	Ojala Yesu ri tho ru gimarecho mawan, aka ochierino go i kwo ŋey wokwan ri wan tiro gi Were.
45005001	Paka onyo okethi wan i tiro gi Were chungo kwoŋ yeyo, onyo wanitye i syem gi Were kwoŋ Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo.
45005002	Go am'okelo wan i ŋono pa Were ma pama wachung'iye. Amomiyo wasangala i geno ma wani gine ma limo dwoŋ pa Were!
45005003	Maloyo meno, wasangala i chandirok mawan, rupiri waŋeyo ni chandirok kelo chiro,
45005004	chiro miyo Were fuoyo wan, aka fuoyo pere kelo ri wan geno.
45005005	Geno me kikwoti wiy wan, rupiri Were otyeko konjo mar pere i chuny wan, munyo omiyo wan Chuny Maleŋ, mobedo mich pa Were ri wan.
45005006	Munyo fuodi oido wanyap, Kristo otho ri jomarecho i hongo ma Were oyero. Raŋo ameno?
45005007	Kole tek swa moro tho ri ŋatotire. Kono moro nyalo miyere to tho ri ŋataber.
45005008	To Were otyeko nyutho wan paka omaro wan, rupiri munyo fuodi wabedo jomarecho, Kristo otho ri wan.
45005009	Paka tho pere onyo okelo wan i tiro gi Were, ma loyo kenyo, go bino botho wan kwoŋ keme pa Were.
45005010	Wan oido wabedo jokwor pa Were, to Were odwoko wan i tiyirok gine kwoŋ remo pa Wuode. Aka paka onyo watyeko dwoko i tiyirok gi Were, kwo pa Wuode onyo bino botho wan kichutho.
45005011	To kimeno kende; wasangala i Were kwoŋ Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo, ma pama odwoko wan i tiyirok gi Were.
45005012	Gimarach obino i piny ka luwo kwoŋ ŋatachiel, aka gimarach pere okelo tho. Gim'owok'iye, tho olak kwoŋ dhano jye, rupiri ji jye jo ni gi gimarach.
45005013	Gimarach oido nitye i piny ma fuodi kowodhi Chik; to kama Chik ongoy'iye kikwan'iye recho ri nyatoro.
45005014	To wok i ndir pa Adam tundo i ndir pa Musa, tho odhumo ji jye, kada joma oido jokotimo recho paka Adam munyo okwero mako chik pa Were. Adam obedo chal pa ŋata oido kidho bino rumachien.
45005015	To mich pa Were ma nono no, kichale gi gimarach ma Adam otimo. K'inen ji mathoth jotho ru gimarach pa Adam ŋatachiel no, ameno ŋono pa Were kodi mich ma nono mani ŋono pa ŋatachiel, Yesu Kristo, loyo meno bor swa.
45005016	Aka pokirok nitye i dyer mich pa Were kodi gimarach pa ŋatachiel. Munyo otyek timo gimarach achiel, gimoluwo a thumo banja ni, “Banja oloyo ŋato; ” to munyo gimarecho olokere madit, mich moido wakiripi gine obino ni, “Okwany woko banja pa ŋato!”
45005017	K'inen ru gimarach pa ŋatachiel ama omiyo tho ochako dhum kwoŋbedo ŋatachiel no, meno kere adyeri joma jonwaŋo ŋono mathoth kodi mich ma nono ma tiro bende jobino dhumo maloyo i kwo ru ŋatachiel, Yesu Kristo.
45005018	Amomiyo paka kibenga pa ŋatachiel omiyo banja oloyo ji jye, ameno bende ibino kwanyo woko banja kwoŋ ji mathoth ru winjo pa ŋatachiel.
45005019	Ato paka kibenga ma nyaturo chik pa ŋatachiel oloko ji kweth jogimarach, apaka bende winjo chik pa ŋatachiel miyo iloko ji kweth jomotire.
45005020	Munyo Chik obino, kibenga ma nyaturo Chik omedere; to kama recho meder'iye, ŋono pa Were bende medere loyo.
45005021	Amomiyo, paka gimarach odhumo i royo ma tho, ameno bende ŋono pa Were dhumo i royo ma kwanyo woko banja kwoŋ ji, munyo tero jo i kwo makirum kwoŋ Yesu Kristo Ruodhiwan.
45006001	Onyo wawachi nedi? Nike wamedere gi timo gimarach aka ŋey ŋono pa Were bende womedere?
45006002	Kameno be! K'inen watyeko tho ma nyutho kwero gimarach, wanyalo nedi doko medirok gi timo gimarach?
45006003	Kole adyeri wiŋeyo gime ni: munyo walimo batisimo i riwirok gi Kristo Yesu, walimo batisimo i riwirok gi tho pere bende.
45006004	Ri ameno, batisimo mawan nyutho ni oyik wan bende gi Yesu kendo wariwere gine i tho pere, ŋey paka Kristo ochierino kwoŋ jomotho ru men pa Bamere Moasere, ameno bende wanyalo bedo i kwo manyien.
45006005	Ato ka wariwere gi Yesu i tho paka go otho, meno bende apaka wabino riwere gine i chierino ma chalo apere.
45006006	Aka waŋeyo ni kwo mawan machon otyek neko gi Kristo wi musalaba, ŋey men ma miyo del timo gimarach wonyali reyere woko, aka ŋey wakiri wadoko wabedi ŋechin pa gimarach.
45006007	Kole ka dhano otho meno otyek gonyo go kwoŋ men pa gimarach.
45006008	Aka ka watyeko tho gi Kristo, wani gi yeyo nike bende wabino kwo gine.
45006009	Kole waŋeyo ni Kristo ochierino kwoŋ jomotho aka kibino tho kendo; tho ongoye gi men kwoŋe kende.
45006010	Tho ma go otho oido obedo tho ma kwero gimarach dichiel ma kichutho; aka kwo ma go onyo ni gine obedo ri Were.
45006011	I royo achiel wibende wiripo terere paka jomotyeko tho ma nyutho kwero gimarach aka onyo jokwo ri Were i Kristo Yesu.
45006012	Gimarach odoko wokiri wodhumi i delkwoŋ win ma tho me, kareno witimo gima awanya mere yenyo.
45006013	Odoko wikiri wimiy gimarach adech ma delkwoŋ win moro woori i timo kidakana, kuchiel miyi win Were kwo mewin, paka ji mokwany jo i tho to ikelo jo i kwo, aka miyi win go kwo mewin gipi woori i atoŋa motire.
45006014	Gimarach wokiri wodhumi win paka onyo wikibedi i men pa chik, to i ŋono pa Were ayino.
45006015	Kere onyo aŋo modoŋ? Watim gimarecho ni rupiri wakinitye i men pa chik to i ŋono pa Were ayino? Be!
45006016	Wikuya nike ka wimiyere paka ŋechin ma winjo nyatoro, meno adyeri wibedo ŋechin pa ruoth ma wiwinjo no, kosa apa gimarach ma kelo tho, kosa apa winjo Were ma kelo ri win tiro i waŋe?
45006017	To Were wofuoyi ni yado oido wibedo ŋechin pa gimarach, to pama wiwinjo adyeri mifuonjo win gi chuny win jye.
45006018	Aka paka otyek gonyo win woko kwoŋ gimarach, pama onyo wilokere ŋechin pa tiro.
45006019	Aoro wach ma nyadhanodhano ru nyapo ma wini gine ma niaŋ. Paka yado oido wimiyere i bedo ŋechin pa kidakana, kodi turo chik pa Were, onyo pama bende wiripo miyirok paka ŋechin pa tiro ri atoŋa ma lonyo.
45006020	Munyo oido wibedo ŋechin pa gimarach, oido wingoye i tiro.
45006021	Onyo bero aŋo ma wilimo i timo gikipiny ma kelo ri win wichkwot? Kole gima wok i gikipiny no obedo tho!
45006022	To paka onyo otyek theko win gi gimarach to wibedo ŋechin pa Were, bero ma wini gine onyo obedo lonyo, ma i gike bino miyo wilimo kwo makirum.
45006023	Kole kemba pa gimarach obedo tho; to mich ma Were miyo wan obedo kwo makirum i Kristo Yesu Ruoth mawan.
45007001	Wikuya, wutimere, ka aluwo gi joma joŋeyo chik, ni chik dhumo dhano ka go fuodi kwo?
45007002	Paka ranen, Chik tweyo dhako monywomere kwoŋ chwore ka chwore fuodi kwo; to tekin chwore tho, go gonyere woko kwoŋ chik ma mako kwoŋ chwore.
45007003	Amomiyo, ka go obedo gi jachwo man munyo fuodi chwore nitye, ibino tero go paka jatimi chot; to ka chwore otyeko otho, go nitye i syem i kite ma chik, aka go kitim chot ka go odoko obedo gi jachwo man.
45007004	Meno apaka nitye kodi win wutimera. Wibende wityeko tho kwoŋ gima mako kwoŋ Chik, rupiri wilokere adech ma delkwoŋ Kristo; aka onyo win apa go mochierino kwoŋ jomotho, ŋey wanyal kwo kareno wakonyo tich pa Were.
45007005	Munyo oido fuodi watimo gima del yenyo, awanya marecho ma Chik osigila oido tiyo i delkwoŋ wan, aka oido kelo ri wan tho.
45007006	To pama otyek gonyo wan woko kwoŋ Chik, rupiri watyeko tho ma nyutho ni wakwero gima chango oido otweyo wan. Pama onyo wakibedo jotich i chik machon mondik, to wabedo jotich i kwo manyien ma Chuny ayino.
45007007	Onyo wawachi nedi? Ni Chik meno won a racho. Kameno be! To ru Chik amomiyan aŋeyo gimarach. Kole d'akiŋeyo gimilwoŋo ni kikobo bedi Chik kowacho ni “Ikiri itim kikobo.”
45007008	Gimarach onwaŋo hola pere i or pa Were, ma kelo ran kikobo ma nger jye. Ka Chik ongoye, gimarach bende bedo gimotho.
45007009	An chon oido akwo munyo Chik fuodi ongoye; to munyo or pa Were obino, to gimarecho chako nenirok kamaler,
45007010	gikenyo t'atho; ameno or monwaŋo omiti ni wokeli kwo odoko olokere ran tho ayino.
45007011	Ato gimarach onwaŋo hola to wondan munyo luwo kwoŋ or; ameno to nekan.
45007012	Ri ameno Chik leŋ, aka or pa Were leŋ, otire, kendo ber.
45007013	Meno onyo nyutho ni gimaber okelo tho? Kameno be! Gimarach am'okelo ran tho munyo oro gimaber, ney kite pere maradyeri paka gimarach wonyuthere kamaler. Amomiyo, chungo kwoŋ or pa Were, gimarach olokere marach ma kichutho.
45007014	Waŋeyo ni Chik mako kwoŋ chuny, to an abedo dhano ma ni gi del, motana paka ŋecha ri gimarach.
45007015	Akiniaŋ odocho kwoŋ gikipiny m'atimo, rupiri akitim gima amito timo, kuchiel, atimo gima akimiti mere ayino.
45007016	Ka atimo gima akimiti timo, meno nyutho nike ayeyo ni Chik otire.
45007017	To iyadyeri awon, aŋata akitim gime; kuchiel gimarach ma nitye i an ama timo gino.
45007018	Aŋeyo ni bero ongoye i an, kosa awachi ni i delkwoŋan paka dhano. Anyalo yenyo timo gimaber, to akinyal.
45007019	Ato akitim gimaber ma amito timo; kuchiel atimo recho moido akimito timo ayino.
45007020	Ka atimo gima oido akimito timo, nyutho ni aŋata akitim ameno, to gimarach ma nitye i an ama timo ameno.
45007021	Ameno anwaŋo ni gime chale gi chik; ka amito timo gimaber, ayero gimarach ayino.
45007022	Kwo ma chunyan sangala i chik pa Were,
45007023	to anwaŋo ni chik man ama tiyo i delkwoŋan, chik ma lwenyo kodi gima paro paran yenyo. Gino lokan jatwech pa chik ma gimarach ma tiyo i delkwoŋan.
45007024	Adyer an adhano ma bu kisangala. Ŋata othekan gi del me ma teran i tho! Were wofuoy ma bino timo ameno kwoŋ Yesu Kristo Ruodhiwan!
45007025	Amomiyo, me apaka anitye: abedo ŋecha ri chik pa Were i paro paran, to i del abedo ŋecha ri chik pa gimarach.
45008001	Pama onyo kidoki kethi banja kwoŋ joma kwo pajo nitye i Kristo Yesu,
45008002	rupiri chik ma Chuny ma kelo ri wan kwo i Kristo Yesu, otyeko thekan gi chik mokelo gimarach kodi tho.
45008003	Gima Chik konyalo timo ru nyapo ma del pa dhano, Were onyalo timo. Othumo banja loyo gimarach ma del, munyo ooro Wuode won, mobino i chal ma del pa dhano ma jagimarach, aka wonyali reyo woko gimarach.
45008004	Meno aka ŋey gima Chik mito ama wotimere i wan, ma wakiter kwo mawan i timo gima del yenyo, to i timo gima Chuny ama yenyo.
45008005	Kole joma tero kwo pajo i timo gima del yenyo joketho paro pajo i gikipiny ma nyadel. Aka joma miyo kwo pajo i timo gima Chuny yenyo joketho paro pajo i Chuny.
45008006	Ketho paro i gikipiny ma nyadel meno tho, to ketho paro i gikipiny ma nyachuny meno limo kwo kodi syem.
45008007	Meno amomiyo paro mokethi kwoŋ gikipiny ma nyadel lokere jakwor pa Were, rupiri kiwinji chik pa Were, aka iyadyeri go kitim ameno.
45008008	Aka joma jotero kwo pajo i timo gima del yenyo jokinyal kisangala Were.
45008009	To kwo mewin kobedo ma nyadel, to obedo ma nyachuny, k'inen Chuny Maleŋ pa Were nitye i win. Ŋata ongoye gi Chuny pa Kristo i kwo pere, meno kobedo apa Kristo.
45008010	To ka Kristo nitye i in, meno delkwoŋin otyeko tho ma nyutho ni ikwero gimarach, aka chunyin onyo ni gi kwo ru tiro perin gi Were.
45008011	Ka Chuny Maleŋ pa Were mochierino Yesu kwoŋ jomotho nitye i win, meno ŋata ochierino Kristo kwoŋ jomotho bende bino miyo delkwoŋ win ma tho no kwo ru Chuny Maleŋ ma bedo i win.
45008012	Amomiyo, wutimera, wanitye gi banja, to ki ri del ni watim gima del yenyo.
45008013	Kole ka kwo mewin nitye paka del yenyo meno wikidho tho; to ka wineko woko tim marecho gi men pa Chuny, aka wibino kwo.
45008014	Ato joma Chuny Maleŋ pa Were ama telo jo ama jobedo nyithindho pa Were.
45008015	Kole wikilimo chuny ma lokirok ŋecha ma kelo ri win lworo; to wityeko limo Chuny ma loko win nyithindho pa Were, aka ka waywak ri Were ni “Baba! Baba!”
45008016	meno men pa Chuny no ama nyutho wan i chuny wan ni wabedo nyithindho pa Were.
45008017	Aka ka wabedo nyithindho pa Were, meno bende wabedo jolunji gikipiny pere paka jomisika kanyachiel gi Kristo, aka wabende wabino limo dwoŋ kanyachiel gi Kristo, ka bende wariwere gi go i chandirok pere.
45008018	Atero ni chandirok ma pama kirom gi dwoŋ ma ibino nyutho wan be.
45008019	Chwech gi pi kiyo neno gima Were bino nyutho nyithindho pere.
45008020	Kole omiy piny lokirok gima ongoye kony, ki ru mito pere, to Were won amomito ni wobedi ameno. Kada ameno, geno oido nitye ama:
45008021	nike ndelo moro ibino gonyo chwech wok kwoŋ topo ma fuodi dhumo go, to limo syem i dwoŋ ma nyithindho pa Were jobino limo.
45008022	Kole waŋeyo kir gunyo ni chwech gi bee chur gi litho ma chale gi litho ma nywol.
45008023	Aka kameno kende, to wan ma wanitye gi Chuny paka mich pa Were marapena, wabende wachur gi litho i iyi wan koro munyo wakuro Were woloki wan nyithindho pere aka wokethi wan i syem.
45008024	Kole geno amomiyo obothi wan; to geno motyeko nenere meno kidoki bedi geno. Ŋa ma geno gima go neno?
45008025	To ka wageno gima wakinen, meno aka wakuro ginago ma wadiyo chuny wan.
45008026	I royo achiel no bende, Chuny Maleŋ konyo wan i nyapo mawan; rupiri wakuya paka waripo kwayo; aka Chuny won ama pido ri wan bongi Were gi chur ma wach kinyal tucho.
45008027	Aka Were ma neno chuny ji, oŋeyo paro pa Chuny, rupiri Chuny pido bongi Were ri ji pere paka Were mito.
45008028	Kole waŋeyo ni gimoro jye timere kanyachiel ma bero ri joma jomaro Were, jono ma go olwoŋo ru atoŋa pere won.
45008029	Kole joma Were oŋeyo chon, bende oyiko ri jo kichutho bedo i chal pa Wuode, ŋey Wuode wobedi okayo i dyer wutimin go.
45008030	Amomiyo joma Were oyiko ri jo kabedo chon kichutho, bende olwoŋo jo; aka joma go olwoŋo, bende okwanyo woko banja kwoŋ jo; aka joma go okwanyo woko banja kwoŋ jo, bende opoko jo dwoŋ pere.
45008031	Onyo wanyalo wacho aŋo kwoŋ gikipiny me? Ka Were nitye yu thenge mawan, ŋata nyalo lwenyo gi wan?
45008032	K'inen Were kogwoko kir Wuode won, to omiyo go ri wajojye! Onyo go komiy wan gimoro jye nono kanyachiel gi Wuode?
45008033	Ŋa ma bino kelo banja kwoŋ ji pa Were moyer? Kole Were won ama kwanyo woko banja kwoŋ jo!
45008034	To ŋa modoko othumi ri jo banja? Ki Kristo Yesu motho, kendo ma Were ochierino go kwoŋ jomotho, aka onyo obedo yu chingi Were marachuch aka pido ri wan bongi Were!
45008035	Ŋa mopoki wan gi mar pa Kristo? Teko di tim ameno, kosa aŋedha chuny, kosa achanda, kosa kech, kosa bedo kinyoro, kosa tho, kosa abor?
45008036	Ato ndiiko wacho ni, “Ru wach perin imito neko wan ndelo jye, itero wan pa rombo mikidho thumo.”
45008037	I gikipiny me jye, watyeko loyo lweny i go momaro wan!
45008038	Kole aŋeyo maber ni kada tho, kosa kwo, kosa jomalaika, kosa jodhum ma polo, kosa gima pama, kosa gima bino rumachien, kosa men mogo,
45008039	kosa ŋawirok pa gimogo, kosa thutho pa gimogo, kosa gimogo jye i chwech, kinyal poko wan gi mar pa Were i Kristo Yesu Ruodhiwan.
45009001	Aluwo giradyeri i Kristo aka akitwodi; paro ma chunyan ridho gino gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ.
45009002	Ani gi rem kodi litho mathoth i chunyan.
45009003	Aparo ni di Were wokwoŋan ayin aka wopokan kodi Kristo ma bero pa ji paran, wade paran won ma del!
45009004	Jobedo Joisrael, ma Were oloko nyithindho pere to poko jo dwoŋ pere. Otimo chikirok pere kodi jo, to miyo jo Chik. Jonitye gi royo ma lamo Were maradyeri. Jotyeko jolo chikirok pa Were;
45009005	jowok kwoŋ kwarere wan machon, aka Kristo, paka dhano, onywolere wok i dyer jo. Weyi Were ma dhumo gimoro jye, wopak chil gi chil. Ameno.
45009006	Akiwachi ni chikirok pa Were othogaya ongoye kony; rupiri kobedo ni Joisrael jye ji pa Were;
45009007	odoko kobedo ni nyikway Ibrayimu jye nyithidho pa Were. Kole Were owacho ri Ibrayimu ni, “Nyikway Isaka kende ama ibino kwano paka aperin.”
45009008	Ma nyutho ni nyithindho monywol i yo ma kis ndelo ma nyadel jokobedo nyithindho pa Were; kuchiel, nyithindho monywol chungo kwoŋ chikirok pa Were ama ikwano paka nyikway go maradyeri.
45009009	Kole chikirok pa Were otim i wach me: “I hongo ma rom gi ma pama yu wa��e, abino dwoko aka Sara bino limo nyathi ma nyiyach.”
45009010	Aka ki meno kende; nger gino bende otimere ri Rebeka munyo ogamo iye to limo nyithindho ma rut, go kodi kwari wan Isaka.
45009011	Kada munyo fuodi konywol jo aka onwaŋo fuodi jokotimo kir gimoro maber kosa marach, (ma miyo yero pa Were wotimere,
45009012	kareno kichungi kwoŋ tim pa nyithindho no, to kwoŋ lwoŋo pa Were), Were owacho ri Rebeka ni, “Wuodin makayo bino tiyo ri mathin.”
45009013	Meno obedo paka ondik ni, “Amaro Yakobo, to adak Esau.”
45009014	Onyo wawachi nedi? Nike Were kotire? Kameno be.
45009015	Kole go owacho ri Musa ni, “Abino mako wor gi ŋata ayero timo ri go wor, abino ramere ri ŋata ayero ramirok ri go.”
45009016	Amomiyo, kichungi kwoŋ yero kosa men pa dhano, to chungo kwoŋ Were ma nyutho wor.
45009017	Kole ondik kwoŋ Farawo ni, “Alokin kere ri atoŋa ma aleorin iye ma nyutho men paran, gi miyo nyingan woŋeyere i piny gipi.”
45009018	Amomiyo Were mako wor gi ŋata go oyero, aka miyo dhano bedo jachay paka won oyero.
45009019	Moro kwoŋ win bino wacho ran ni. “K'inen obedo ameno, Were nyalo nedi ketho banja kwoŋ dhano? To ŋa, ma nyalo geŋo paro pa Were?”
45009020	To jawodhan in iŋa, dhano adhana, m'inyalo dwoko Were? Ayiga dak bende nyalo penjo ŋata ochweyo go ni, “Raŋo m'ichweyan ama?”
45009021	Kole jachwech ni gi syem ma oro lowo nyamasiga paka won oyero, gi chweyo degi aryo wok i lowo achiel modwany: dak achiel maraora i kabedo mawelo kodi man maraora i kabedo ma kis ndelo.
45009022	Iŋeyo nedi, kole ka Were otimo ameno ma mito nyutho keme pere gi miyo men pere woŋeyere! Amomiyo go odiyo chunye swa munyo chiro joma keme pere d'otiyo kwoŋ jo, moido ikidho reyo woko jo.
45009023	Aka iŋeyo nedi, kole ka Were otimo ameno ma mito nyutho dwoŋ pere moŋaŋ ri joma go kidho nyutho jo wor pere, ma go oyiko jolo i dwoŋ pere.
45009024	Kole meno mako kwoŋ wan ma go olwoŋo, ki nyaka wok kwoŋ Joyudaya kende, to kwoŋ Jopath bende.
45009025	Kole me a gima go wacho i kitawo pa Hoseya: “Ji me moido jokobedo aparan, abino lwoŋo jo ni, ‘Ji paran.’ Nono monwaŋo akimaro, abino lwoŋo ni, ‘Migos paran.’
45009026	Aka i kabedo monwaŋo owach'iye ri jo ni, ‘Wikibedo ji paran,’ kenyo ama ibino lwoŋ'iye jo ni nyithindho pa Were makwo.”
45009027	Aka Isaya luwo kwoŋ Israel ni, “Kada nyithindho pa Israel jothoth pa kwoyo ma nam, nyaka manok kwoŋ jo ama ibino botho.
45009028	Kole Ruoth bino chowo thumo banja pere i yoto ri piny.”
45009029	Aka gime nitye paka Isaya chango owacho ni, “Bedi Ruoth Majameni jye koweyo ri waye nyikway wan mogo, di wabedo paka Sodom, di walokere paka Gomora.”
45009030	To wanowachi nedi? Jopath monwaŋo jokitem bedo i tiro gi Were, onyo oketh jo i tiro gine ru yeyo pajo;
45009031	kareno Joisrael monwaŋo jorango tiro chungo kwoŋ Chik, jokonyalo kuro Chik nago.
45009032	To raŋo? Rupiri gima jotimo onwaŋo kochungo kwoŋ yeyo to kwoŋ tich mabeyo ayino. Jochier wi “tele ma redho jo,”
45009033	ma ndiiko luwo kwoŋe ni, “Neni, aketho i Zayun tele ma bino miyo ji chier, Tele ma bino miyo jo podho. To ŋata oyey go, kowey wiye wokwoti.”
45010001	Wutimera, ayenyo gi chunyan jye ni ji paran jye jowobothi! Neni paka akwayo Were ri jo!
45010002	Kole anyalo ridho ni chuny jo omaro Were, to maro pajo kichungi kwoŋ niaŋ motire.
45010003	Fuodi jokoniaŋ royo ma Were keth'iye gi go ji i tiro gine, aka wegi jotyeko temo chwogo royo pajo; amomiyo jokojolo royo ma Were keth'iye gine ji i tiro.
45010004	Kole Kristo amobedo kama Chik gik'iye, ŋey nyaka dhano jye mayeyo woketh i tiro gi Were.
45010005	Musa ondiko kwoŋ wach ma bedo i tiro gi Were i winjo Chik ni, “Ŋata timo gima Chik wacho, bino kwo gi Chik.”
45010006	To me a gima ndiiko wacho kwoŋ ketho dhano i tiro gi Were ru yeyo: “Ikiri iwachi i chunyin ni, ‘Ŋata oidhi i polo?’ ” (dwoŋ mere ni dwoko Kristo i piny ka).
45010007	“Kosa ni, ‘Ŋata olori piny i bur maluth?’ ” (dwoŋ mere ni kidho chierino Kristo kwoŋ jomotho.)
45010008	Me a gima Ndiiko wacho: “Kole wach nitye chiegin kodin, i dhokin kodi i chunyin” (dwoŋ mere ni wach ma yeyo ma wafuonjo);
45010009	rupiri ka itucho gi dhokin ni, “Yesu meno Ruoth,” aka iyeyo i chunyin nike Were ochierino go kwoŋ jomotho, ibino both.
45010010	Ato dhano yeyo gi i chunye to ikwanyo woko banja kwoŋe; aka tucho gi dhoke to limo both.
45010011	Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Moro jye ma yeyo go konwaŋ wichkwot.”
45010012	Me mako kwoŋ dhano jye, rupiri pokirok ongoye i dyer Joyudaya kodi Jopath; Were achiel ama obedo Ruoth pa ji jye, aka go miyo dhano jye ma lwoŋo go silwany.
45010013	Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Nyatoro jye m'olwoŋ nyingi Ruoth bino both”.
45010014	To jolwoŋ nedi ŋata fuodi jokoyeyo kwoŋe? Odoko joyey nedi ŋata fuodi jokowinjo wach ma mako kwoŋe? Odoko jowinji nedi mongoye ŋata otito ri jo mikwenda?
45010015	Aka jotiti nedi mikwenda, ka koor jo? Kole ondik ni, “Bino pa joma kelo Wach Maber obedo gimaber manedi!”
45010016	To ki Joisrael jye ma jojolo Wach Maber. Isaya won owacho ni, “Ruoth, ŋata oyeyo mikwenda mawan?”
45010017	Amomiyo yeyo wok i winjo mikwenda, aka mikwenda wok i fuonji kwoŋ Kristo.
45010018	To apenjo, obedo adyeri ni jokowinjo mikwenda? Kole jowinjo paka ndiiko wacho ni, “Derino ma dwondi jo olak i piny gipi, Wach pajo otundo i tum jye ma piny.”
45010019	Odoko apenjo, kosa Joisrael chango jokoniaŋ? Kole Musa won gipi a marapena dwoko ni, “Abino miyo witimi nyieko gi ji ma jokobedo nono motire. Abino miyo win nge gi ji mamiŋ.”
45010020	Aka Isaya ni gi miseni madwoŋ ka wacho ni, “Jomonwaŋo jokirangan ama jonwaŋan; Amenyere ri jomonwaŋo jokipenjan kada.”
45010021	To ma mako kwoŋ Israel go wacho ni, “Atiŋo chingan malo ndelo gipi ri ji ma jochay kendo ma jopyem.”
45011001	Onyo apenjo ni, Were otyeko bolo woko ji pere? Kameno be! An won bende abedo Jaisrael, nyakwar Ibrayimu, achiel kwoŋ jonono pa Benjamin.
45011002	Were kobolo woko ji pere ma go won oyero chako chon. Wikuya gima ndiiko wacho i adech ma Eliya pid'iye gi Were ka lwenyo gi Israel?
45011003	Owacho ni, “Ruoth, joneko jotuchi wach perin aka jonyieko woko alitar perin; aŋata adoŋ kendan, aka jorango kir nekan bende.”
45011004	Were omiyo go radwok aŋo? Odwoko go ni, “Atyeko ketho gichien ji gana abiryo ma fuodi jokolamo were Baal.”
45011005	Amomiyo bende kir gunyo fuodi nitye jomodoŋ, ma Were oyero ru ŋono pere.
45011006	Ka obedo ru ŋono pere, meno yero pa Were kichungi kwoŋ tim mabeyo ma dhano timo, rupiri d'onyo ŋono no kidoki bedi ŋono motire.
45011007	Onyo aŋo to? Gima Joisrael jorango tektek jokonwaŋo; jomoyer ama jonwaŋo, to jomodoŋ jobedo gi chuny jo matek.
45011008	Otimere paka ondik ni, “Were omiyo jo chuny ma miŋo, gi waŋ gin ma konyalo neno, kodi ithi gin ma konyalo winjo, kir konon.”
45011009	Aka Daudi wacho ni, “Mada kalima pajo wolokere ri jo bwo ma chiko jo, kodi gima redho jo; jowolimi girachula!
45011010	Mada waŋ gin chule woko ma jokinyal neno, miyi jowogwomere i chandirok pajo ndir jye.”
45011011	Amomiyo apenjo ni: Munyo Joyudaya jochier, jopodho to joreyere woko? Kameno be! Rupiri jotimo gimarach, both obino ri Jopath, ŋey womiyi Joyudaya jowotimi nyieko gi jo.
45011012	K'inen gimarach pa Joyudaya okelo silwany mathoth ri piny, aka podho pajo okelo ŋaŋo ri Jopath, onyo ka orwaki jo, silwany no bino thoth marom nedi?
45011013	Pama onyo aluwo gi win Jopath: ka fuodi abedo jamoor pa Jopath abino pakere gi tich paran.
45011014	Miti anyalo miyo ji ma nono paran won nyieko, ŋey anyal botho jomegi kwoŋ jo.
45011015	K'inen munyo obol jo woko, odwok piny gipi i tiyirok gi Were, onyo aŋo man m'obedi ka ojol jo, loyo nwaŋo kwo wok i tho!
45011016	Kole ka adech ma chiemo momiy Were paka gimanyak marapena leŋ, meno chiemo no gipi bende leŋ; aka k'inen tyendi yath leŋ, meno kir jange bende leŋ.
45011017	To k'inen otyek toŋo woko megi kwoŋ jangi yath vini mopidhi, aka win ma wibedo jangi vini mogo madudi onyo oriw win maber i kabedo pa motoŋ woko cha munyo ipoko win ye kwo moŋaŋ mani tyendi yath mopidhi no,
45011018	onyo wikiri wipakere ri jangi yen moŋwer woko cha, rupiri wibedo nyaka jangi yen, aka wiŋat wikithyel tyendi yath to tyendi yath ama thyelo win.
45011019	To wibino wacho ni, “Ey, kole oŋwer woko jangi yen cha ma leŋo ran hongo.”
45011020	Meno otire, oŋwer woko jo rupiri jokoyeyo, to wikiri wibedi gi paro ma pakirok kwoŋ gime; kuchiel, bedi win gi lworo ayino.
45011021	Ato k'inen Were koworo Joyudaya ma jobedo paka jangi yen motire mere, wiparo nike go bino woro win ayino?
45011022	Onyo neni win paka Were chunye ber aka odoko nyutho gero bende. Go ger kodi joma jopodho, to nyutho win bero tekin wichwire i bero pere; to ka wikitimo ameno, wibende ibino ŋwero win woko.
45011023	Aka ka Joyudaya joweyo bedo ma bu yeyo, ibino dwoko jo i kabedo pajo monwaŋo jo ni iye, rupiri Were nyalo dwoko jo kendo.
45011024	K'inen win Jopath oŋadi win paka jangi yath vini madudi to iriwo win kwoŋ vini mopidhi pecho, gima oido kinyalere, onyo Joyudaya ma jobedo jangi yath kwoŋ yath vini mopidhi, jobino bedo mayot nedi riwo jo kendo i kor yath mere won!
