45011025	Amito ni winiaŋ nyaliŋliŋ me, wutimera, ŋey wikiri wipar ni wiryek swa: wichtek pa ji ma Israel kobedo ma kiwire, to bino bedo chuka welo kwan pa Jopath mamitere jowobin bongi Were woromi.
45011026	Aka me apaka Israel gipi bino limo both, paka ondik ni, “Jaboth bino wok Zayun, Go bino kwanyo woko recho pa nyikway Yakobo jye.
45011027	Abino timo chikirok me gi jo, munyo akwanyo woko gimarecho pajo.”
45011028	Rupiri jokwero Wach Maber, Joyudaya jolokere jokwor pa Were ma bero mewin, win Jopath. To i yero pa Were, jobedo mere pere ma bero pa kwarere pajo.
45011029	Kole Were kiwir paro pere kwoŋ mich kodi lwoŋo pere ri nyatoro.
45011030	Gime rom kodi gima otimere ri win Jopath; chon oido wichayo Were, to kole pama onyo wilimo wor pa Were rupiri Joyudaya jotimo chay.
45011031	Ameno bende, Joyudaya pama jokiwinji Were, ŋey gi wor ma wilimo, jo bende jowolimi wor pa Were.
45011032	Kole Were otyeko loko ji jye jotwech pa chay, ŋey wonyuthi wor ri ji jye.
45011033	Thutho ma ŋaŋo pa Were kodi ryeko kodi niaŋ pere rom nedi! Ŋa ma nyalo tito paro ma go ochano? Ŋa ma nyalo niaŋ kwoŋ royo pere?
45011034	Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Ŋa moŋeyo paro pa Ruoth? Odoko ŋa ma nyalo miyo go ryeko?
45011035	Ŋa motyeko miyoye go gimoro ma ripo wonwaŋi chul?”
45011036	Kole go amochweyo gimoro jye, aka gimoro jye nitye kwoŋbedo go kodi ri go. Dwoŋ wobedi ri Were chil gi chil! Ameno.
45012001	Amomiyo, wutimera, ru wor pa Were moasere ri wan, agoyo ri win koko me: Miyi win delkwoŋ win ri Were paka rachow makwo, maleŋ ma sangala go. Meno a lamo machuny ma wiripo chwayo ri go.
45012002	Wikiri wiluw kula ma piny me, to bedi win ma wiwire i paro mewin, aka nyaka wibino ŋeyo mito pa Were: gimaber ma sangala go, odoko molony kichutho.
45012003	Aka gi mich ma Were omiyan awacho gime ri wijojye: Wikiri wipar ni wini malo loyo kama di wipar'iye. Kuchiel, bedi win milengela i paro mewin, kis dhano kwoŋ win, ma ripo gi yeyo ma Were omiyo go.
45012004	Wanitye g'adeche madit i del achiel, aka adeche me jye nitye gi tich mere.
45012005	Ameno kada wathoth, jye fuodi wabedo del achiel i Kristo, aka wamakere kanyachiel paka adeche mopokere opokere ma del achiel.
45012006	Amomiyo paka wanitye gi mich mopokere opokere chungo kwoŋ ŋono ma Were omiyo wan, weyi waor ama: K'obedo mich ma tucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were, timi ameno i chungo kwoŋ yeyo mini gine.
45012007	K'obedo mich ma chwayo, tiyi ri jowotin; k'obedo mich ma fuonji, fuonji wadin.
45012008	K'obedo mich ma medo wadin miseni, timi ameno; ŋata poko ri joman gima go nigine, wopoki gi chunye maber; jatel, wotiyi gi men; jawor, wonyuthi wadi wor gi kisangala.
45012009	Mar ripo bedo maradyeri. Kweri gimarach, chwire kwoŋ gimaber.
45012010	Marere win gi owirok ma chuny paka wutimere i Kristo, odoko bedi win mayil i miyo jowoti win dwoŋ.
45012011	Tiyi win matek, aka wikiri wibedi manyap. Chwayi win ri Ruoth gi chuny win jye.
45012012	Weyi geno mewin womiyi win kisangala, diyi win chuny win i teko mewin, aka kwayi win Were hongo jye.
45012013	Poki win ye lim mewin gi wutimin win ma jochando, odoko weyi win pechin mewin thwolo ri wendo.
45012014	Kwayi win Were womiyi jomalwenyo kodi win silwany; ey, kwayi wi go womiyi jo silwany ma kiweno kwoŋ.
45012015	Sangala win gi jomasangala, ywaki win gi jomaywak.
45012016	Nyuthi win dhano jye chuny maber marom. Wikiri wibedi jokwoto, to joli win tich kada mapiny. Wikiri wibedi gi paro ni wiryek.
45012017	Ka nyatoro otimo ri win marach, wikiri wichul kwor. Temi win timo gima ji jye tero ni ber.
45012018	Temi win paka nyalere neno ni wibedo i syem gi ji jye.
45012019	Wikiri wichul kwor wiwegi, jowotan; kuchiel weyi win keme pa Were ama wochuli. Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Ruoth wacho ni, ‘Chulo kwor obedo aparan; abino chulo.’ ”
45012020	Kuchiel ndiiko wacho ni, “Ka jakwor perin kech neko, pidhi go; ka riyo neko, miyi go giramadha; kole k'itimo ameno, meno chal pa onyo itoko chuk mach ma lyeth i wiye.”
45012021	Ikiri iyey recho wodhumin; kuchiel loyi recho gi bero.
45013001	Dhano jye ripo winjo or pa ruodhe ma piny; ato ongoye men maradhum ma Were ama koyeyo, aka jodhum ma jonitye Were ama oketho jo.
45013002	Nyatoro jye ma pyemo kodi men pa jodhum manitye, meno pyemo kodi gima Were ochano; aka moro jye ma timo ameno bino kelo wach kwoŋe won.
45013003	Kole joma timo gimaber jokilwor jodhum, to jomatimo recho ayino ama jolworo. Imito bedo ma bu lworo kwoŋ jadhum? Ere timi gimaber, aka go bino pakin.
45013004	Kole go jatich pa Were ma tiyo ri bero perin. To k'itimo recho, lwori go, rupiri jadhum kibedi gi gilweny nono. Go obedo jatich pa Were aka go nyutho joma timo recho keme pa Were.
45013005	Ru wach me dhano jye ripo winjo or pa ruodhe, ki nyaka ru keme pajo kende, to ru gima paro ma chunyin nyuthin bende.
45013006	Meno bende amomiyo wiripo goyo misolo, rupiri ruodhe jotiyo ri Were ka jotimo tich pajo no.
45013007	Amomiyo, chuli win gima wiripo chulo dhano; chuli misolo perin bongi ŋata iripo chulo, kodi lim perin bende ameno; aka wori win ŋata ripere awora, odoko miy dhano jye dwoŋ, ma ripere amiya dwoŋ.
45013008	Wikiri wibedi gi banja pa dhano moro jye. Nyaka banja ma wiripo bedo gine meno a marok i dyer win. Nyatoro jye momaro nyawote meno otyeko winjo Chik.
45013009	Or ma wacho ni, “Ikiri itim chot, ikiri ineki, ikiri ikwal, ikiri ibedi g'awanya,” jye kodi man oriw kanyachiel i or achiel ni, “Mari nyawotin paka iwon imarere.”
45013010	Nyatoro jye momaro nyawote kibino timo ri nyawote recho. Amomiyo, marok meno winjo Chik gi bee.
45013011	Medo kwoŋ meno, wiŋeyo ndir ma pama ni ndir otundo ri win ma chiew. Kole ndir ma both mawan onyo ochore chiegin loyo munyo nyaka wachako yeyo.
45013012	Wor chiegin rumo, aka piny chiegin yawirok. Ri ameno wawey win timo gikipiny mamudho to wakwanyo win gilweny ma lero.
45013013	Wabedi win i kwo motire paka ji ma jonitye i lero modyechieŋ, mongoye woro kosa mero, chot kosa kidakana, gorok kosa nyieko.
45013014	Kuchiel ruki win Ruoth Yesu Kristo, aka wikiri wiwey hola ri del, ma timo awanya mere.
45014001	Joli win i dyer win ŋatanyap i yeyo; to wikiri wipyem gine kwoŋ paro pere.
45014002	Yeyo pa ŋatachiel yeyo go chamo gimoro jye, to ŋatanyap i yeyo chamo fufa aŋweta kende.
45014003	Ŋata chamo gimoro jye wokiri wochay dhano ma kitim ameno; aka ŋata chamo fufa kende wokiri wothum banja ri ŋata chamo gimoro jye, kole Were otyeko jolo go.
45014004	In iŋa m'ithumo banja ri jatich pa ŋat man? Ruoth pere won ama nyalo ridho paka go tiyo maber kosa makiber odocho. Aka bino konyo go wochungi, rupiri Ruoth nyalo miyo go chungo matek.
45014005	Ŋatachiel paro ni ndelo achiel loyo ndelo man jye, kareno ŋat man paro ni ndelo jye rom. Dhano jye ripo bedo gi paro pere m'oridho matek.
45014006	Ŋata paro kwoŋ ndelo moro ni loyo nyawote timo ameno ka miyo Ruoth dwoŋ, ŋata chamo gimoro bende timo ameno ka miyo Ruoth dwoŋ, rupiri go fuoyo Were ru chiemo no. Onyo ŋata kwero chamo gikipiny mogo bende timo ameno ma miyo Ruoth dwoŋ, aka fuoyo Were.
45014007	Ongoye moro kwoŋ wan ma won kwo ri wach pere kende; odoko ongoye ma tho ri go won kende.
45014008	Ka wakwo, meno wakwo ri Ruoth odoko ka watho, meno bende watho ri Ruoth. Amomiyo, kada wakwo kosa watho, jye wabedo apa Ruoth.
45014009	Kole Kristo otho to chierino ŋey wobedi Ruoth pa jomakwo kodi jomotho jye.
45014010	Onyo raŋo m'ithumo banja ri omerin? Aka in! Raŋo m'ichayo omerin? Kole wajojye wabino chungo i nyim Were, go wothumi ri wan banja.
45014011	Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “ ‘Paka akwo,’ Ruoth wacho, ‘dhano jye bino guro chonge i nyiman, Aka dhano jye bino tucho ni abedo Were.’ ”
45014012	Amomiyo, dhano jye kwoŋ wan bino tito gima mako kwoŋ kwo pere ri Were.
45014013	Amomiyo wawey win thumo banja ri jowoti wan. Kuchiel, me a gima wiripo ridho: wikiri witim gimoro jye ma miyo nyawoti win chier, kosa podho i gimarach.
45014014	Riwirok paran kanyachiel gi Ruoth Yesu miyan aŋeyo adyeri ni ongoye gimakoch; kwanyo woko ka dhano oyeyo nike gimoro koch aka gino lokere makoch ri go.
45014015	K'imiyo nyawotin ramirok ru gima ichamo, meno kere ikitim gino gi mar. Ikiri imiy chiemo m'ichamo wokel ri nyawotin ma Kristo otho ri go podho.
45014016	Ikiri imiy gimitero paka ber wolim nyinge marach.
45014017	Kole Ker pa Were kobedo nyaka chiemo gi oro giramadha, to obedo tiro kodi syem kodi kisangala i Chuny Maleŋ.
45014018	Aka ŋata tiyo ri Kristo i royo me Were jolo, odoko ji bende fuoyo go.
45014019	Amomiyo, ndir jye wakidhi win ri gikipiny ma kelo syem aka konyo wawegi i miyirok men ayin.
45014020	Ikiri inyieki tich pa Were ru wach chiemo. Chiemo jye nyalo bedo ni olony achama, to kibedi gimotire chamo gimoro ma bino miyo dhano man podho i gimarach.
45014021	Gimotire a weyo chamo riŋo, madho vini, kosa timo gimoro man jye ma miyo omerin podho, kosa chunye ŋedhere, kosa lokere manyap i yeyo.
45014022	Ini gi yeyo? Ere maki yeyo perin no paka gima iwon iridho ruwaŋ Were. Jasilwany a ŋata kiwinji banja i chunye ka timo gima go ofuoyo!
45014023	To ka nyatoro ganagana kwoŋ gima go chamo, Were thumo banja loyo go ka ochamo gino, rupiri tim pere kochungo kwoŋ yeyo. Aka gimoro jye ma kochungo kwoŋ yeyo meno recho.
45015001	Wan ma wategino i yeyo waripo konyo jomanyap gi tiŋo byeto pajo. Kiripi ka wawegi wamiyere kisangala.
45015002	Kuchiel, ŋatachielechiele kwoŋ wan ripo miyo jager pere kisangala ma konyo go, ŋey wodongi ŋato i yeyo.
45015003	Kole Kristo won komiyere kisangala. Kuchiel, obedo paka ondik ni, “Yet ma jono joyetin gine omakan ayino.”
45015004	Kole gimoro jye mondik i kitawo maleŋ ondik ma fuonjo wan, ŋey walim geno i diyo chuny kodi i men ma Ndiiko Maleŋ miyo wan.
45015005	Weyi Were ma jadiy chuny ji kendo jadwoki men, womiyi winyal bedo kanyachiel i syem, munyo wiluwo ranen pa Yesu Kristo,
45015006	aka nyaka wijojye kanyachiel, gi dwondi win achiel, winyal pako Were kodi Baa Yesu Kristo Ruodhiwan.
45015007	Amomiyo jolere win paka Kristo ojolo wan, ma miyo Were dwoŋ.
45015008	Kole awacho ri win ni Kristo olokere jatich pa jomothumere (Joyudaya) ma nyutho nike Were genere, ma miyo chikirok pa Were m'otimo gi kwarere wan wotundi i kare,
45015009	bende gi miyo Jopath pako Were ru wor pere, paka ndiiko wacho ni, “Amomiyo abino kethin walwa i dyer Jopath, Abino wero munyo apako nyingin.”
45015010	Odoko wacho ni, “Sangala win, wi Jopath, kanyachiel gi ji pa Were moyer.”
45015011	Odoko wacho ni, “Paki win Ruoth, win Jopath jye!” aka weyi nonin jye jowopaki go.
45015012	Odoko Isaya wacho ni, “Nyakwar Yese lebino; Ibino tiŋo go malo wodhumi Jopath, Aka Jopath jobino ketho geno pajo i go.”
45015013	Were ma geno wok bonge wonyali poŋo win gi kisangala jye kodi syem chungo kwoŋ yeyo mewin, ŋey geno mewin womedere dongo gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ.
45015014	Wutimera, awon ani gi geno kwoŋ win, nike withoth gi bero, nike wipoŋ gi ryeko, aka wiwegi winyalo fuonjo jowoti win.
45015015	To kada ameno, i balwa ma atyeko ndiko ri win, abedo gi miseni kwoŋ gikipiny mogo ma apoyo win, ru ŋono ma Were opokan
45015016	ma bedo jatich pa Kristo Yesu ma tiyo ri Jopath. Atiyo paka jachwayi ri Were wi alitar kareno atito Wach Maber ma wok bongi Were, ŋeyi Jopath jowobedi mich ma Were jolo, ma Chuny Maleŋ olonyo ri go.
45015017	Amomiyo, i Kristo Yesu, anyalo bedo g'atoŋa ma yumirok gi tich paran ri Were.
45015018	Aka akibino yumirok gi giman ma kiweno gima Kristo otyeko timo munyo oran i miyo Jopath winjo Were, i yo ma wach kodi tim,
45015019	gi men ma wok'iye ranyuth kodi giraura, gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ pa Were. Gino omiyo kama awoth'iye jye, chako Yerusalem tundo Ilirikam, atyeko tito Wach Maber kwoŋ Kristo kichutho.
45015020	Amomiyo gima aasa yenyo timo obedo tito Wach Maber kama fuodi kowinj'iye kwoŋ Kristo, ŋey akir alwowere kwoŋ tich ma ŋat man otyeko chako.
45015021	Ato ndiiko wacho ni, “Joma fuodi kowachi ri jo kwoŋ go jobino neno, aka joma fuodi jokowinjo jobino niaŋ.”
45015022	Meno a gima onwaŋo omonan ndir madit bino bongi win.
45015023	To paka achowo tich paran i adech me, odoko paka atyeko yenyo bino neno win oro mathoth,
45015024	onyo ageno timo ameno pama. Amito neno win ka amako royo makidho yu Spain, winyal konyan i nger ma kidho koro, ka atyekoye kisangala i lyewo win hongo moromo.
45015025	Gunyoni, akidho Yerusalem tiyo ri ji pa Were koro.
45015026	Kole kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Masedonia kodi Yunani joridho paro ma miyo mich ma konyo jochandi i dyer ji pa Were ma Yerusalem.
45015027	Jo wegi joridho timo ameno; aka i adyeri joripo konyo jo; kole Joyudaya jopoko silwany pajo kodi Jopath, amomiyo Jopath bende joripo konyo Joyudaya gi silwany pajo ma gikipiny ma piny.
45015028	Ka achowo tich me, kareno atyeko tero ri jo pesa mochoki ri jo, nyaka abino mako yo ma kidho Spain, to alyewo win ka akidho yu korago.
45015029	Ka abino bongi win, aŋeyo ni alebino gi silwany pa Kristo mopoŋ.
45015030	Wutimera, agoyo ri win koko, i Ruoth Yesu Kristo kodi kwoŋ mar pa Chuny Maleŋ; riwere win kodan i kwayo mochwiny bongi Were,
45015031	nike go wokuran i bero kwoŋ jomakoyeyo i Yudeya, ŋey ji pa Were jowojoli tich paran i Yerusalem.
45015032	Amomiyo alebino bongi win gi kisangala mopoŋ, ka obedo mito pa Were, kareno awinjo syem i wendo paran bongi win.
45015033	Were ma kelo ri wan syem wobedi kodi wijojye. Ameno.
45016001	Afuoyo ri win nyamin wan Febe, ma tiyo paka jakony i kitipa pa jomoyeyo i Kenkereya.
45016002	Joli win go i nyingi Ruoth, paka ripere ri ji pa Were, aka miyi win go kony jye ma go omiti bongi win; kole go otyeko bedo jakony ri ji mathoth ma kir ran bende.
45016003	Mothi ran Prisila kodi Akwila, jotich jowotan i Kristo Yesu,
45016004	ma jojala kwo pajo ran. Aketho jo walwa, aka ki an kendan, to kitipa pa jomoyeyo pa Jopath jye bende.
45016005	Mothi ran kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma romo i ot pajo. Mothi ran mere paran ma kachunyan Epeneto, mobedo ŋat marapena i adech ma Asya i yeyo Kristo.
45016006	Mothi ran Marya, motyeko tich tektek ri win.
45016007	Mothi ran Androniko kodi Yuniya, Joyudaya jowotan ma jobedo i twech kodan; jojye joŋeyere maber i dyer jomoor, aka jolokere jokristo ma fuodi an.
45016008	Mothi ran Ampulyato, mere paran i Ruoth.
45016009	Mothi ran Urubano, jatich nyawotan i Kristo, kodi Sitako, mere paran swa.
45016010	Mothi ran Apele, ma chwirok pere kwoŋ Kristo oŋeyere maber. Mothi ran jopecho pa Aristobulo.
45016011	Mothi ran Herodyon, Jayudaya nyawotan kodi jokristo wutimin wan i pecho pa Narukiso.
45016012	Teri moth paran ri Turifena kodi Turifosa, mon ma jotiyo tektek i Ruoth. Mothi ran jawodhan swa, Pasis, motyeko timo kweth tich ri Ruoth.
45016013	Adhiro moth ri Rufo, jatich moŋeyere i tich pa Ruoth, kodi ri min, ma hongo jye oteran paka wuode.
45016014	Teri moth paran ri Asinkurito, Fulegon, Herume, Paturoba, Heruma, kodi wutimere i Kristo jye ma jo ni kanyachiel gi jo.
45016015	Mothi ran Filologo kodi Julya, Nereyo kodi nyamin, Olimpa kodi ji pa Were jye ma jonitye bongi jo.
45016016	Mothere win akor i leŋo. Kitipa pa jomoyeyo Kristo jye jodhiro ri win moth pajo.
45016017	Wutimera, agoyo ri win koko ni kure win kwoŋ joma kelo pokirok aka jogeŋo ri win royo gi gima opokere kodi fuonji ma wityeko jolo; eye win kwoŋ jo.
45016018	Kole joma timo gikipiny ma kite no jokitiy ri Kristo Ruodhiwan, to jotiyo ri iyi gin wegi gi wach pajo mamit kodi luwo ma dwoŋo paro pa joma onwaŋo jongoye gi racho.
45016019	Dhano jye otyeko winjo chwirok mewin kwoŋ Wach Maber, aka ru wach me josangala swa gi win. Amito wibedi maryek kwoŋ gimaber, aka ma wikitim recho.
45016020	Aka Were ma miyo wan syem, bino ŋinyo woko Sitan i par tyendi win i yoto. Ŋono pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo wobedi gi win.
45016021	Timotheyo, jatich nyawotan, bende dhiro ri win moth; kanyachiel gi Lusyo, Jason kodi Sosipate, Joyudaya jowotan.
45016022	An Terutiyo, jandiiko gi kalamu i balwa me, abende adhiro ri win moth paran ma nyakristo.
45016023	Gayo, won pecho ma an kodi jomoyeyo waromo i ot pere ka, dhiro ri win moth pere; Erasto, jatel ma tich ma tindi, kodi omin wan Kwaruto jye jodhiro ri win moth.
45016024	[Ŋono pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo wobedi kodi win. Ameno]
45016025	Weyi wamiy Were dwoŋ ma nyalo miyo wichungo matek i yeyo, i Wach Maber m'afuonjo win, mikwenda kwoŋ Yesu Kristo, kodi kwoŋ nyutho adyeri ma nyaliŋliŋ monwaŋo opan oro kweth mokadho.
45016026	To pama adyeri no otyek wodho kamaler i ndiiko pa jotuchi wach Were; kodi i or pa Were ma chil gi chil, ma onyo imiyo nonin jye ŋeyo, aka ji jye jowoŋeyi odoko jowowinji.
45016027	Ri Were ma nitye achiel kende maryek, dwoŋ wobedi kwoŋ Yesu Kristo Ruodhiwan chil gi chil. Ameno.
46001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, ma i mito pa Were olwoŋ bedo jamoor pa Kristo Yesu, jokodi omin wan Sostheno,
46001002	Ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo Were ma nitye Korinthya, ri ji jye molwoŋ bedo ji pa Were, ma jobedo apere i riwirok gi Kristo Yesu, kanyachiel gi ji jye ma kamoro jye ma jolwoŋo nyingi Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo, Ruoth mawan gi jo.
46001003	Were Baa wan kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo jowomiyi win ŋono gi syem.
46001004	Ndir jye aketho Were paran walwa ri win, ru ŋono momiyo win kwoŋ Yesu Kristo.
46001005	Kole i riwirok gi Kristo wilokere joŋaŋo i gimoro jye, tektek mere i luwo kodi i ryeko mewin
46001006	paka mikwenda ma mako kwoŋ Kristo otyeko ridhere i kwo mewin
46001007	to miyo wikichandi mich moro jye ka wikuro nike Ruoth Yesu Kristo womenyere kamaler.
46001008	Go bino miyo wichungo matek chuka gike, aka nyaka ibino nwaŋo win ma bu racho i Ndelo pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo.
46001009	Were molwoŋo win riwirok gi Wuode Yesu Kristo Ruodhiwan genere.
46001010	Agoyo koko ri win wutimera i nyingi Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo: Yeyere win wijojye, i gima wiwacho, aka nyaka tyakirok wokiri wobedi i dyer win; riwere win swa munyo winitye gi paro achiel kodi atoŋa achiel.
46001011	Ato ji megi ma jowok pecho pa Kilowe jodhiro ran wach nike dhawirok nitye i dyer win, wutimera.
46001012	Weyi awachi ama: kis dhano kwoŋ win wacho gipere, ni “An aluwo Apolo, ” ŋat man ni “An aluwo Petro” ŋat man ni “An aluwo Kristo.”
46001013	Nyutho nike Kristo opokere i dyere? Kere Paulo am'otho wi musalaba ri win? Kosa batisimo ma wilimo obedo i nyingi Paulo?
46001014	Afuoyo Were nike akimiyo win batisimo, kwanyo woko Kurispo kodi Gayo.
46001015	Amomiyo, ongoye ŋata nyalo wacho ni wilimo batisimo i nyingan paka jofuonjirok paran.
46001016	(Ey, abatisa Stefano kodi pecho pere bende; to akipoy ni abatisa ŋat man kendo.)
46001017	Kole Kristo kooran kibatisa ji, to tito Wach Maber ayin, ma ki gi ryeko ma nyadhanodhano, rupiri d'omiyo tho pa Kristo bedo ma bu men.
46001018	Kole mikwenda ma mako kwoŋ tho pa Kristo wi musalaba obedo gimiŋo ri jono ma jobino rwenyo; to ri wan ma wabino both, obedo men pa Were.
46001019	Ato ndiiko wacho ni, “Abino reyo woko ryeko pa jomaryek, to adhiro gi chien niaŋ pa jomofuonjere.”
46001020	Onyo nyaka ni kune ŋataryek? Nikune jondiiko? Nikune jopyem majoryek ma pama? Kole Were otyeko nyutho ni ryeko ma piny ka meno miŋo ayin!
46001021	Kole Were i ryeko pere omito ni ji kiri jowoŋeyi go gi ryeko pajo wegi. Kuchiel Were oridho botho jomayeyo, gi mikwenda ma wafuonjo ma wiŋoyo ni miŋo.
46001022	Joyudaya joyenyo giraura paka giranena, aka Joyunani jodwaro ryeko.
46001023	To wan, watito Kristo mogur kwoŋ musalaba, mikwenda mobedo yet ri Joyudaya kodi miŋo ri Jopath,
46001024	to ri jomolwoŋ i dyer Joyudaya gi Joyunani, obedo Kristo mobedo men pa Were gi ryeko pa Were.
46001025	Kole gima chale p'obedo miŋo pa Were fuodi ryek loyo ryeko pa ji. Aka gima chale p'obedo nyapo pa Were ni gi men loyo men pa ji.
46001026	Onyo poyi win paka oido winitye munyo Were olwoŋo win. Jomanok kwoŋ win ama di piny oneno paka jomaryek, kosa joma ni gi men, kosa joma ni gi dwoŋ i neno pa dhano.
46001027	To Were otimo atoŋa yero gima piny ŋisa ni gimiŋo ŋey wokwoti gine wiyi jomaryek, kodi gima piny tero paka nyap wokwoti gine wiyi jomen.
46001028	Were Oyero gima piny ŋisa aka chayo, aka paro ni meno ki gimoro, ŋey wonyieki woko gima piny paro nike gimadwoŋ.
46001029	Meno aka wongoye dhano ma nyalo pakirok i waŋ Were.
46001030	Were ama okelo win i riwirok gi Kristo Yesu, to loko Kristo bedo ryeko mawan, tiro mawan gi leŋo mawan, kodi chul ma gimarecho mawan to walimo syem.
46001031	Amomiyo, ndiiko wacho ni, “Ŋata mito pakirok wopakere i Ruoth.”
46002001	Wutimera, munyo abino bongi win fuonjo adyeri pa Were mopanere, akioro wach maboyo kodi ryeko mamalo.
46002002	Kendo akimito ŋeyo giman jye kwoŋ win munyo fuodi anitye gi win kwanyo woko Yesu Kristo, aka mogur wi musalaba.
46002003	Amomiyo munyo abino bongi win oido men oloyan kareno akirin ru lworo.
46002004	Aka luwo paran gi mikwenda paran kobedo i luwo ma ryeko pa ji, to i nyutho kamaler men pa Chuny Maleŋ,
46002005	ŋey yeyo mewin, wokiri wothenere kwoŋ ryeko pa dhano, to kwoŋ men pa Were ayin.
46002006	Kada ameno, waluwo gi ryeko ri joma jotegino i yeyo. To kobedo ryeko ma ndir me, kosa apa jodhum ma pama, ma jokidho reyirok woko.
46002007	Ryeko ma wafuonjo obedo ryeko pa Were mopanere, mopan ri ji, ma Were oido otyeko yiko miyo wan wok chon ma piny fuodi kochwey.
46002008	Ongoye kada achiel kwoŋ jodhum ma pama moido oŋeyo ryeko me. Bedi joŋeyi di jokoguro Ruoth mopoŋ gi dwoŋ kwoŋ musalaba.
46002009	To paka ndiiko wacho: “Gima dhano fuodi koneno kosa kowinjo wok chiene, gima dhano fuodi koparo kwoŋe ni d'otimere a gima Were oyiko ri jomomaro go.”
46002010	To Were onyutho wan nyaliŋliŋ me luwo i Chuny Maleŋ pere. Ato Chuny Maleŋ udo gimoro jye, kada gimoro mopanere kamadiny i Were.
46002011	To ŋa ma di ŋey paro pa dhano kwanyo woko chuny dhano won ma nitye i go? Meno bende apaka Chuny Maleŋ pa Were won amoŋeyo paro pa Were.
46002012	Wakilimo chuny ma nyapiny, to walimo Chuny mowok bongi Were, ma miyo waniaŋ kwoŋ gimoro jye ma Were omiyo wan ma nono.
46002013	Meno a wach ma waluwo; wakiluw wach ma ryeko ma dhano amofuojo wan, to waluwo gima Chuny Maleŋ ama fuonjo wan, aka watito adyeri ma Chuny ri joma bende jonitye gi Chuny Maleŋ.
46002014	To ŋata ongoye gi Chuny kinyal limo mich ma wok bongi Chuny Maleŋ pa Were, rupiri obedo ri go gimiŋo: aka go kinyal niaŋ kwoŋe, kwoŋbedo dwoŋ mere niaŋere ri ŋata bende ni gi Chuny Maleŋ pa Were.
46002015	Ŋata nitye gi Chuny nyalo niaŋ kwoŋ gimoro jye, aka ongoye ŋata niaŋ kwoŋ gima ni kwoŋ go.
46002016	Ato ndiiko wacho ni, “Ŋata di ŋey paro pa Ruoth aka womedi miyo go ryeko?” To wan, wanitye gi paro pa Kristo.
46003001	To wutimera, akinyalo luwo gi win paka joma nitye gi Chuny; to paka ji ma nyapiny, paka nyidhindho maŋich i yeyo manyakristo.
46003002	Apidho win gi chak ma kiweno chiemo matek, rupiri oido fuodi wikiyikere, aka kada pama jye fuodi wikiyikere,
46003003	kwoŋbedo fuodi kwo mewin obedo manyadel. Ka witimo nyieko wiwegi aka widhawere, meno kinyuthi paka fuodi wibedo ji ma kis ndelo munyo wioro kula mere?
46003004	Ka ŋatachiel kwoŋ win wacho ni, “An aluwo Paulo,” man ni, “An aluwo Apolo,” meno wikibedo ji ma kis ndelo?
46003005	Onyo, Apolo a ŋa? Aka Paulo a ŋa? Kole wabedo nyaka jotich pa Were ma jokelo ri win yeyo. Kis dhano kwoŋ wan otimo nyaka tich ma Ruoth omiyo go timo.
46003006	Apidho kodhi, Apolo oywoy'iye pi, to Were won amomiyo gimopidhi dongo.
46003007	Amomiyo gima mako kwoŋ ŋata opidho kosa ŋata oywoy'iye pi ama kobedo gima dwoŋ, kwanyo woko Were ma miyo gimoro dongo ama dwoŋ.
46003008	Japidho kodi jaywoyi pi jye jorom aroma; Were bino miyo jo kemba chungo kwoŋ tich ma jotimo.
46003009	Kole wariwere kanyachiel i tich ri Were, aka wibedo ndelo pa Were kodi geto pere.
46003010	Munyo aoro mich ma Were omiyan, atimo tich paka jandijo ma geto moketho tyendi ot, aka ŋat man ama onyo geto i kore. Aka dhano jye ripo gwoko paka go medo tich kwoŋ ot no.
46003011	Ato ongoye tyendi ot man ma nyatoro di chaki kendo, kwanyo woko motyeki chako no won, mobedo Yesu Kristo.
46003012	Joman jobino oro zawabu, feza, kosa telin mawelo wi tyendi ot no; aka joman mbawo, lum mothwo, kosa kanja.
46003013	Aka bero ma tich pa kis dhano bino nenere munyo Ndelo pa Kristo thango gino kamaler, rupiri mach ma Ndelo no bino kikaŋasa tich pa dhano jye; mach no bino kipima to nyutho bero kosa racho mere.
46003014	Ka nyatoro ogeti wi tyendi ot no to tich pere chiro mach, go bino limo kemba.
46003015	To ka tich pa moro owaŋi woko, go bino keŋ kemba mere kada nende go won bino both ri go, to kareno leboth igani obudhere owok i mach.
46003016	Wikuya nike wibedo Ot pa Were, aka Chuny Maleŋ pa Were bedo i win?
46003017	Ŋata nyieko Ot pa Were, Were bino reyo go Woko, rupiri Ot pa Were leŋ aka wiŋati wibedo Ot ago.
46003018	Moro wokiri wowondere. Ka moro kwoŋ win paro nike go ryek i hongo ma pama me, go ripo bedo pa ŋatamiŋ, ŋey wolokere ŋataryek.
46003019	Kole gima piny tero paka ryeko meno gimiŋo ri Were, rupiri ndiiko wacho ni, “Were chiiko jomaryek i ryeko pajo.”
46003020	Aka ndiiko man wacho ni, “Ruoth oŋeyo nike paro pa jomaryek ongoye kony.”
46003021	Amomiyo, ongoye pakirok moro jye kwoŋ gima dhano nyalo timo. Kole gimoro jye obedo mewin:
46003022	Paulo, kosa Apolo, kosa Petro, kosa piny me, kwo gi tho, kosa hongo ma pama kodi ma bino; me jye mewin.
46003023	Aka wibedo apa Kristo. Aka Kristo obedo apa Were.
46004001	Wiripo neno wan paka jotich pa Kristo, momiy jo adyeri pa Were mopanere.
46004002	Onyo gima yenyere kwoŋ dhano moketh i tich meno a genirok ri ruoth pere.
46004003	Aka, akidew kada onyo withum ran banja, kosa kapido ma piny me ama thum; kada awon akithum banja paran.
46004004	An awon akinen racho moro ma ani gine to meno kinyuthi nike angoye gi racho. Ruoth ama thumo ran banja.
46004005	Amomiyo wikiri withum ri nyatoro banja ma fuodi ndir kotundo. Kutho kur win bino pa Ruoth, ma bino wodho i lero gimoro jye mopondo i mudho kendo bino thango kamaler atoŋa ma chuny ji. I hongo no ama nyaka dhano jye bino lim'iye pak ma ripo gine wok bongi Were.
46004006	Wutimera, ma konyo win, aluwo kwoŋ Apolo kodan paka ranen, ŋey winiaŋ dwoŋ wach mondik ni, “Maki chik motire.” Meno aka bino ngoye kwoŋ win ŋata pakere gi dhano achiel to chayo ŋat man.
46004007	Aka ŋa ma neno gimopokere i in? Aŋo m'ini gine ma komiyin amiya? To inyalo kwot nedi, igani gima ini gine kobedo mich?
46004008	Kole kere wityeko ri win limo gimoro jye ma wiyenyo! Wityeko ŋaŋo! Wityeko lokirok kerin, kada wawegi wakibedo ameno! Bedi nyalere di wibedo kerin adyeri, aka di wabende wabedo kerin kanyachiel gi win.
46004009	Kole chali ran pa Were omiyo wan jomoor kabedo machowe swa, pa ji mothum ri jo banja matho, rupiri walokere giranena ri jomalaika kodi ji ma piny.
46004010	Wabedo jomamiŋ kwoŋbedo Kristo; to wiryeki ri win i Kristo! Wanyap, to witek ri win! Ochay wan, to win omiy win dwoŋ!
46004011	Kir gi pama fuodi wanitye gi kech kodi riiyo; waruko oselin; igoyo wan; wangoye gi pechin;
46004012	watiyo matek gi chingi wan aka walimo gikonyirok. Ka dhano okwoŋo wan, wamiyo go silwany ayin; ka ilwenyo gi wan, wachiro;
46004013	ka oyet wan, wadwoko wach i bero. Watyeko lokere yuk ma piny; aka kir pama won me wachal ri wan chwodho.
46004014	Andiko ri win ama ki ru mito kwoto wiy win; to atimo ama ma fuonjo win paka nyithindho paran ma kachunyan.
46004015	Kole kada wibedi gi jofuonji gana apar i kwo mewin, i Kristo winitye gi baa win achiel kende. Kole i kwo mewin i Kristo Yesu alokere baa win munyo akelo ri win Wach Maber.
46004016	Amomiyo, akwayo win ni luwi win kite paran paka ranen ma amiyo win.
46004017	Atoŋa me amomiyo adhiro ri win Timotheyo wuodan mamaro kendo mogenere i Ruoth. Go bino poyo win royo m'aluwo i Kristo Yesu, odoko m'afuonjo i kweth pa jokristo iye jye.
46004018	Jomegi kwoŋ win jopakere ka joparo ni kono akobin bongi win.
46004019	To ka Ruoth oyeyo, alebino bongi win mayot, aka abino neno men pa jopakirok no, ma kiweno nyaka luwo pajo kende!
46004020	Kole ker pa Were kobedo nyaka luwo kende, to obedo meni.
46004021	Mene ma wifuoyo? Abin bongi win g'adasa, kosa gi mar kodi mwolo?
46005001	Kole wawinjo ni chot nitye i dyer win moasare gima kitimere kada i dyer jokafiri; owachi ran nike nitye nyatoro mobedo gi chi bamere!
46005002	Meno a gima miyo win kwoto? Kole d'onyo wiwinjo gi rem ayin to wiryemo woko ŋata timo gino wok i kweth mewin.
46005003	Kada nende anitye bor gi win i del, to anitye gi win i chuny; aka atyeko kir thumo banja loyo ŋat'otimo gimarach no igani anitye gi win kenyo.
46005004	Ka wiromo kanyachiel, aka abende ani gi win i chunyan, gi men pa Ruodhiwan Yesu ma nitye gi wan,
46005005	wiripo chwayo ŋat me ri Sitan wonyieki delkwoŋe, g'awanya mere ŋey chunye wolimi both i ndelo pa Ruoth Yesu.
46005006	Kwoto mewin no kiripi! Wikuya ni, “Thow kada mathin nyalo miyo moko modwany gipi yenyo?”
46005007	Wiripo kwanyo woko thow machon ma gimarecho aka nyaka wibino bedo ma wilony. Aka ŋey wibino chale kodi moko modwany ma bu thow, paka aŋeyo nike wibedo ameno adyeri. Kole Kristo, nyathi rombo mawan ma kalima ma Kadho, otyek miyo ri wan.
46005008	Amomiyo onyo weyi watim kalima mawan, to ki gi mugat moketh'iye thow machon, marathuye kodi gimarecho, to kodi mugat ma bu thow, ma di tiro kodi adyeri.
46005009	I balwa m'andiko ri win awacho ni wikiri wimakere kodi jomodakana.
46005010	Akiluw kwoŋ jokafiri ma jodakana kosa joworo, kosa jokwo, kosa jolami chal makichar ma piny me. Kole bedi ameno d'onyo wiweyo piny ka kichutho!
46005011	Gima akidho ri go obedo nike wikiri wimakere gi dhano ma lwoŋere ni oyeyo to odakana, wor, kosa lamo chal makichar, kosa janyieki nyingi wadi, kosa jamero kosa jakwo. Wikiri wibedi kada piny chiemo gi dhano ma pameno.
46005012	Aŋo ma di miyan athum banja ri joma woko? Kole joma ni dyer jomoyeyo ama winyalo thumo ri jo banja!
46005013	Were won bino thumo banja ri joma ni woko paka ndiiko wacho ni, “Kwanyi win woko ŋatarach i dyer win.”
46006001	Ka ŋatachiel kwoŋ win nitye gi pyem g'omin, go nyalo nedi kidho bongi jothumi banjin ma jokafiri, kama di wey ji pa Were wegi jowochowi wach no?
46006002	Wikuya ni ji pa Were jobino thumo ri piny banja? To ka wiŋati wilethumo ri piny banja, thumo banjin mathindho nyalo dhyero win nedi?
46006003	Wikuya ni wabino thumo banjin ri jomalaika? K'inen ameno, banjin ma kwo me d'odhyer wan thumo nedi?
46006004	Amomiyo ka wach ma chalo ameno obino, iraŋo witero woko both ji ma jokristo jochayo ni ama jowochowi?
46006005	Meno awacho ma kwoto wiy win! Ongoye kada ŋatachiel i dyer win maryek ma nyalo chowo dhawirok ma nitye i dyer jomoyeyo!
46006006	Kuchiel dhano kidho i kapido g'omin to miyo jokafiri ama jothumo banja ri jo.
46006007	Iyadyeri, k'inen witero kiŋunyaŋya mewin i kawinjo banjin ma piny ka, nyutho nike wipodho swa. Thimba di wikidiyo chuny win ka moro otimo ri win marach? Iraŋo di wikidiyo chuny win ka nyatoro omayo win gimoro?
46006008	Kuchiel wiwegi witimo recho ri jowoti win: mayirok gikipiny, kir apa jomoyeyo jowot win won!
46006009	Wikuya ni jomarecho jokibino donjo i Ker pa Were? Moro wokiri wowondi win: Ongoye jokidakana, kosa jolami chal makichar, kosa mon ma jotana delkwoŋ jo i timo gi wichkwot, kosa jotimi chot, kosa joma timo kidakana chwo gi chwo wadi gin aka mon bende gi mon wadi gin,
46006010	kosa jokwo, kosa jomero, kosa jonyieki nyingi wadi gin, kosa jomiten ma jokwalo, ma bino donjo i Ker pa Were. Aka megi kwoŋ win oido wibedo ameno.
46006011	To onyo otyek lonyo win kwoŋ gimarach: oketh win i tiro gi Were i nyingi Ruoth Yesu Kristo gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ pa Were mawan.
46006012	Nyatoro nyalo wacho ni, “Kole oyeyan timo gimoro jye.” Ey, to bero kinyal bedo i kis gimoro. Abende anyalo wacho ni oyeyan timo gimoro jye, to akibino yeyo gimoro wolokan ŋecha pere.
46006013	Ŋat man bino wacho ni, “Kole chiemo obedo ri ich, aka ich bende ri chiemo.” Ey, to Were bino reyo woko gino jye. Delkwoŋ dhano kotim ri kidakana to ri Ruoth ayin; aka Ruoth bende bedo ri del.
46006014	Were ochierino Ruoth kwoŋ jomotho, aka go bende bino chierino wan i men pere.
46006015	Wikuya ni delkwoŋ win obedo adeche ma delkwoŋ Kristo? Onyo akwany adech ma delkwoŋ Kristo aloki delkwoŋ dhano ma tana delkwoŋe i timo gi wichkwot? Kinyalere!
46006016	Kosa miti wikuya ni ŋata riwo delkwoŋe kodi apa ŋatochale ameno lokere achiel gine? ndiiko wacho ni, “Jaryo jobino lokere del achiel.”
46006017	Aka ŋata bedo i achiel gi Ruoth lokere achiel i chunye kodi go.
46006018	Weyere win gi kidakana! Gimarach man ma dhano timo kimaki delkwoŋe to ŋata timo chot timo gimarach kwoŋ delkwoŋe won.
46006019	Ikuya ni delkwoŋin obedo Ot pa Chuny Maleŋ ma bedo i in, ma Were omiyini? Ikibedo aperin won, to apa Were.
46006020	Go onyiewo win gi welo mamalo. Amomiyo ori win delkwoŋ win ri dwoŋ pa Were.
46007001	Onyo wey wanen wach ma windiko ran kwoŋe: Dhano timo maber ka konywomo,
46007002	to paka timo gi wichkwot oasere, jachwo jye ripo bedo gi chiege; aka dhako jye ripo bedo gi chwore.
46007003	Jachwo ripo timo ri chiege gima dheno yenyo kwoŋ go, odoko dhako bende ripo timo ameno ri chwore.
46007004	Dhako monywomere won kidhum delkwoŋe, to chwore ama dhumo; i royo achiel jadhako won bende kidhum delkwoŋe, to chiege ama dhumo.
46007005	Wikiri wikwerere, kwanyo woko ka wiyeyere wijaryo timo ameno chowo hongo machiek, ŋey wilim hongo ma kwayo; to giki win mayot i kwo ma nywomirok, kakameno chiro mewin manok nyalo miyo widonjo i karatem pa Sitan.
46007006	Awacho ri win gime ki paka or, to paka ryeko m'amiyo win ayin.
46007007	D'ayeny ni ji jye jowobedi paka an; to kis dhano nitye gi mich ma Were omiyo go mopokere; ŋatachiel mich me, ŋat man mecha.
46007008	Onyo awacho gime ri joma konywomere kodi mon ma chwogi jo otho: d'obedo maber ri win bedo kendiwin paka an.
46007009	To ka wikinyal chiro awanya mewin, kidhi win winywomere; kole ber nywomirok loyo waŋ g'awanya.
46007010	Anitye gi or ri jomonywomere, aka kobedo aparan to apa Ruoth: dhako monywomere kiripi weyo chwore;
46007011	aka ka go otimo ameno, go ripo bedo kende kosa gik bongi chwore; odoko jachwo kiripi ryemo chiege.
46007012	Ri joman awacho (an won, ki Ruoth) ni: ka jachwo ma jakristo nitye gi chiege mongoye gi yeyo to dheno yeyo bedo gine, jalo kiripi woryemi go.
46007013	Odoko ka dhako ma jakristo nitye kodi chwore mongoye gi yeyo, to jalo yeyo bedo gine, go kiripi pokirok gi jalo.
46007014	Kole Were jolo jachwo mongoye gi yeyo ru riwirok gi chiege, aka dhako mongoye gi yeyo bende Were jolo ru riwirok gi chwore ma jakristo. Bedi kobedo ameno, di nyithindho pajo jobedo paka nyithindho ma nyakafiri; to paka nitye, Were jolo jo.
46007015	To ka ŋata bu yeyo mito pokirok kodi nyawote ma jakristo, weyi go wotimi ameno. I wach ma chalo ameno, jakristo mobedo jachwo kosa dhako, nitye gi syem ma yero; kole Were olwoŋin bedo i syem.
46007016	Iŋeyo nedi, in dhako ma jakristo, nike ikobothi chworin? Kosa iŋeyo nedi in jachwo ma jakristo, nike ikobothi chiegin?
46007017	Dhano jye ripo doŋ i kwo ma Ruoth olwoŋ'iye go. Me a chik ma afuonjo i kitipa pa jokristo jye.
46007018	Nitye ŋata onwaŋo otyeko thumirok i hongo ma Kristo olwoŋ'iye go? Kiripi ŋato wotemi kwanyo woko waŋ poyo ma thumirok. Kosa nitye ŋata onwaŋo fuodi kothumere i hongo ma Were olwoŋ'iye go? Kiripi ŋato woyenyi thumirok.
46007019	Kole thumirok kosa bedo ma dhano kothumere meno ama kobedo gima dwoŋ. Gimadwoŋ meno a winjo or pa Were.
46007020	Dhano jye ripo doŋ paka oido nitye munyo ojolo lwoŋo pa Were.
46007021	Oido ibedo ŋecha munyo Were olwoŋini? Ikiri idew; to k'inyalo nwaŋo syem perin, timi ameno.
46007022	Kole dhano ma Ruoth olwoŋo munyo ŋecha lokere dhano pa Were mani syem; aka rom aroma gi ŋata onwaŋo nitye i syem munyo olwoŋ go, ma lokere ŋecha pa Kristo.
46007023	Were onyiewo win i welo mamalo, amomiyo wikiri wilokere ŋechin pa ji.
46007024	Wutimera, dhano jye ripo doŋ i Were paka go oido nitye i hongo m'olwoŋ'iye go.
46007025	Onyo ma mako kwoŋ joma konywomere, akinwaŋo or bongi Ruoth, to akelo paro paran paka ŋata ru wor pa Ruoth ripere agena.
46007026	Chungo kwoŋ teko ma pama nitye, aparo ni ber ri dhano jye doŋ adoŋa paka go nitye.
46007027	Inywomo kosa inywomere? Ere ikiri item pokirok gi nyawotin. Ikinywomo kosa ikinywomere? Ere ikiri irangi dhako kosa jachwo.
46007028	To ka inywomo, ikitimo gimarach, odoko ka nyako onywomere, bende kotimo gimarach. To joma nywomo kosa nywomere jobino bedo gi teko madit i kwo me, aka oido ayenyo konyo jo kwoŋ gino.
46007029	Jowotan, me a dwoŋ gima awacho: hongo modoŋ nok, aka wok konon kadho malo jomonywomo jowobedi igani joma konywomo;
46007030	jomaywak, igani joma kiywaki; jomasangala, igani jomongoye gi kisangala; joma nyiewere, igani gikipiny ma jonyiewo k'apajo;
46007031	joma oro gikipiny ma piny, igani gikipiny no komayo jo hongo moro jye. Kole piny me, paka pama nitye, kibino odoko kiyindira.
46007032	Amito wingoye kodi rembo. Jachwo ma konywomo ketho chunye i tich pa Ruoth, rupiri go rango yo ma kisangala Ruoth;
46007033	to jachwo monywomo ketho chunye i gikipiny ma piny, rupiri go mito kisangala chiege,
46007034	aka chunye tero go korin gi korin. Dhako ma konywomere kosa nyako ketho chunye i tich pa Ruoth, rupiri go yenyo miyirok ri Ruoth i chunye kodi i del bende; to dhako monywomere ketho chunye i gikipiny ma piny, rupiri go rango yo ma kisangala chwore.
46007035	Awacho gime rupiri amito konyo win. Akitem ketho win i dinyo. Kuchiel amito witim gimotire m'oripo, kareno wimiyere i tich pa Ruoth mongoye ruwo paro.
46007036	K'inen jayach motyeko penjirok gi nyako onyo neno ni go timo gima kiripi ri nyawote no, aka nyako no oro pere kadho, aka go paro ni joripo nywomirok, ere jowotimi ameno paka go mito; ongoye kenyo gimarach.
46007037	To ka jachwo won otyeko ridho i chunye ni lenywom, mongoye ŋata romo go, to won thumo paro pere, timo maber.
46007038	Amomiyo, jachwo ma nywomo nyako pere no timo maber, to ŋata weyo ma konywomo, timo maber loyo.
46007039	Chik tweyo dhako monywomere kwoŋ chwore tekin chwore fuodi kwo; to ka chwore otho, go nitye gi syem ma nywomirok gi jachwo man ma go omiti; to wobedi i Ruoth.
46007040	To go d'obedo gi kisangala loyo, ka go odoŋ paka go nitye. Meno paro paran, aka aparo ni abende anitye gi Chuny Maleŋ pa Were.
46008001	Onyo, i wach ma mako kwoŋ chiemo mochow gine chal makichar: Ato adyeri, “Wajojye wani gi ŋeyo kwoŋ wach,” paka jowacho. Ŋeyo no adyeri, kelo ri dhano winjirok nono; to mar ama miyo dhano dongo i yeyo.
46008002	Dhano nyalo paro nike go oŋeyo gimoro, to kere fuodi ongoye gi ŋeyo motire ma go oido ripo bedo gine.
46008003	To ŋata omaro Were, Were ŋeyo go.
46008004	Amomiyo, i wach ma mako kwoŋ chamo chiemo mochow gine chal makichar: waŋeyo ni chal ma kichar kobedo gima ni gi kwo i piny ka; aka adyeri waŋeyo ni Were nitye achiel kende mongoye man.
46008005	Kada bedi ni gikipiny man milwoŋo ni, “werin”, oido nitye kuya i polo kosa i piny ka, (aka gikipiny milwoŋ ni, “werin” kodi “ruodhe” no, jothoth),
46008006	to ri wan Were nitye achiel kende, Were Bawan, mochweyo gikipiny jye, ma gimoro jye wok bonge; ma wakwo ri go; odoko Ruoth nitye achiel kende, Yesu Kristo, ma i go gikipiny jye ochwey, aka go ama miyo wakwo.
46008007	To ki ji jye ma jonitye gi ŋeyo i gime. Jomegi oido joasa ŋiiyo gi chal makichar ma kir konon ka jochamo nger chiemo no fuodi joparo nike meno chiemo mochow gine chal makichar; aka paka paro pajo fuodi nyap, joneno ni chiemo no onyo obedo gimakoch.
46008008	To chiemo k'ama kel wan chiegin gi Were; odoko wakikeŋ gimoro kada wakichiemo, kendo wakilim gimoro kada wachiemi.
46008009	To kure win, rupiri syem mewin nyalo lokere gima redho jomanyap i yeyo.
46008010	Ka dhano ma paro pere nyap i wach me nenin, in m'iŋoyo ni initye gi ŋeyo nago, munyo ichiemo i migam mapa chal makichar, gino komedi go men ma chamo chiemo mochow gine chal makichari?
46008011	Ameno ŋatanyap me, mobedo omerin ma Kristo otho ri go, bino rwenyo woko ru wach “ŋeyo” perin!
46008012	Aka k'itimo gimarach ameno ri jomoyeyo jowotin, t'imiyo paro ma chuny jo manyap no litho, meno itimo gimarach ri Kristo.
46008013	Amomiyo ka chiemo miyo omera timo gimarach, akodoko acham riŋo kendo, ŋey akir aredhi omera i yeyo pere.
46009001	Kere angoye gi syemi? Akibedo jamoori? Akityeko neno Yesu Ruodhiwani? Wikibedo jomowok i tich paran i Ruothi?
46009002	Kada nende akibedo jamoor ri joman, to aripo bedo ri win! Kole win a ranyuth nike abedo jamoor.
46009003	Me a wach ma athyelere gine kwoŋ joma dwaro wach kwoŋan.
46009004	Nyutho ni wangoye gi men ma limo chiemo gi giramadha i tich mawani?
46009005	Waŋati wakiripi woth gi mon mawan paka jomoor man jotimo, kodi wutimin Ruoth, kodi Petro?
46009006	Kosa wan kodi Barunaba kende ama waripo tiyo ri kwo mawan aka walim girachama?
46009007	Ŋa ma bedo jaserikale to won chulo gima go oro i lweny? Kosa ŋa ma jafur ma kicham gimanyak ma ndelo vini pere? Kosa jakwath mene ma kior chak ma wok kwoŋ mwendi pere won?
46009008	Wiparo ni gima awacho me wok i paro pa dhano? Chik bende kiwachi ameno woni?
46009009	Ondik i Chik pa Musa ni, “Ikiri ichul dhoki mirikwa ka ŋinyo rin withi ŋano nyinge wooyi.” Onyo, wiparo ni Were dewo kwoŋ megi kwe ayino kende?
46009010	Kosa go kowacho ameno ka luwo kwoŋ wan tektek mere? Kole gino ondik ri wan rupiri jafur furo, jaŋinyo ŋinyo kareno jojye jogeno migewo wok kwoŋ gim'okechi.
46009011	Kole watyeko chwoyo kodhi ma chuny i dyer win. Onyo meno waŋati wanyieko ka wanwaŋoye gimoro bongi win?
46009012	K'inen joman jo ni gi thwolo ma nwaŋo gimoro bongi win, onyo maraŋo ma wan ama wakigen kada ma loyo meno kwoŋ win? To wakioro thwolo no; kuchiel wachiro gimoro jye ni wakiri wakethi rageŋ i yo pa Wach Maber kwoŋ Kristo.
46009013	Kere wikuya nike joma tiyo i Ot pa Were jolimo chiemo pajo i Ot pa Were. Aka jomachwayo wi alitar jolimo pok i tich ma chwayo no.
46009014	Meno bende apaka joma tito Wach Maber mapa Ruoth joripo kwo gi wach no won.
46009015	To fuodi akioro thwolo no jye kada dichiel, kendo onyo akindiki gime ma kwayo win ni witimi ran ameno. Them onyo atho ma akiweyo nyatoro womayan gima apakere gine me to loko nyaka pa wach awacha.
46009016	To akinyal pakirok i tito Wach Maber, rupiri atimo gim'ooran aora. Aka d'obedo ran marach ka akitito Wach Maber me ri ji.
46009017	Bedi atimo tich paran paka awon ayero d'ageno limo kemba, to atimo tich ma aripo timo ma Were ama ogenan gine.
46009018	Onyo kemba paran aŋo? A me: tito Wach Maber ri ji mongoye chul, kendo ma akioro thwolo moido ani gine ma limo gimoro.
46009019	Oido akibedo ran ŋecha pa moro, to onyo awon alokere ŋecha pa dhano jye ŋey ayway ji mathoth paka nyalere.
46009020	I dyer Joyudaya abedo paka Jayudaya ŋey ayway jo; i dyer joma luwo Chik pa Musa, abedo paka ŋata luwo Chik (kada onwaŋo awon akibedo jaluwi Chik), ŋey ayway jo.
46009021	Ka anitye i dyer Jopath, abende abedo paka Japath woko ma Chik pa Joyudaya, ŋey ayway jo. Me kinyuthi ni akiwinji chik pa Were, rupiri anitye i chik pa Kristo.
46009022	Gi jomanyap i yeyo, abedo manyap paka jo, ŋey ayway jo. Amomiyo abedo gimoro jye ri ji jye aka anyal both jomegi kwoŋ jo.
46009023	Atimo gime ri bero pa Wach Maber, ŋey wopokan silwany mere.
46009024	Wikipoy ni i ŋwech ma pyem, joŋwech jye joringo, to ŋatachiel kende ama limo kemba. Amomiyo ringi chuka ibende ilim kemba.
46009025	Jatuko ma pyem moro jye ripo yikirok ka fuonjere chik ma tuko: go timo ameno ŋey wolim sangarya ma kiyindira, to wan walwenyo ri sangarya ma bino kiyindira chil gi chil.
46009026	Amomiyo akiringi aringa ameno nono, odoko akiwiti adol paran i hongo nono.
46009027	Amiyo del paran fuonji moromo aka wolokere mochwiny munyo adhumo go, ŋey ka atyeko tito ri joman Wach Maber, an awon akir akeŋ kemba mere.
46010001	Wutimera, amito wipoy gima otimere gi kwarere mawan ma joluwo Musa. Jojye jowotho i pendi pondeponde, aka jojye joluwo i dyer Wakawaka mobokere.
46010002	Jojye jolimo batisimo i pondeponde kodi i wakawaka paka jomaluwo Musa.
46010003	Jojye jochamo mugat nger achiel mowok bongi Were,
46010004	to jomadho giramadha nger achiel mowok bongi Were; ato jomadho pi mowok i tele mowotho gi jo aka meno oido obedo Kristo won.
46010005	To kada ameno Were kosangala kodi jomoloyo i thotho kwoŋ jo, amomiyo obol jo woko i thim to jotho.
46010006	Onyo gikipiny me jye obedo giranena ri wan, ma fuonjo wan nike wakiri wawanya gikipiny marecho paka jotimo.
46010007	Wikiri wilam chal makichar paka jomegi kwoŋ jo jotimo paka ndiiko wacho ni, “Jonicha jobedo piny chiemo gi medho, to joay myel.”
46010008	Wakiri watim chot paka jomegi kwoŋ jo jotimo, to gana pyero aryo g'adek kwoŋ jo tho i ndelo achiel.
46010009	Wakiri watem Ruoth, paka jomegi kwoŋ jo jotimo, to thwole neko jo.
46010010	Wakiri waŋunyaŋunya, paka jomegi kwoŋ jo jotimo to Malaika majanek reyo jo woko.
46010011	Gikipiny me jye otimere paka giranena ri joman, aka ondik ma fuonjo wan ma wanitye i hongo ma giki ndir chiegin tund'iye.
46010012	Ŋata paro ni ochungo motire wogwokere ŋey wokiri wopodhi.
46010013	Ongoye ratem mogo jye ma bino ri win ma kichale gi ma bino ri dhano jye. Kole Were genere, aka koyey ratem ma bino ri win wokadhi kor win, to ka ratem moro obino, go bino miyo win royo ma both aka ŋey winyal chiro.
46010014	Amomiyo, jowotan, gwokere win kwoŋ lamo chal makichar.
46010015	Aluwo gi win paka joma niaŋ; wiwegi kaŋasa win gima awacho.
46010016	Ka wafuoyo Were ri agwata ma di silwany ma wamadho, meno wakibedo i riwirok achiel gi remo pa Kristo? Aka mugat ma waturo aka wachamo; kobedo riwirok i achiel gi Kristo?
46010017	Kole paka mugat nitye achiel onyo wajojye bende, kada wathoth, wabedo del achiel, rupiri wajojye wachamo mugat achiel no.
46010018	Pari win kwoŋ Joisrael; joma chamo gima ochowere gine wiy alitar meno jokinitye kanyachiel i tich maralitar?
46010019	Gima awacho dwoŋ mere aŋo? Nike chal makichar kosa chiemo mochow gine chal no nitye iye gimoro?
46010020	Be, gima awacho obedo ni gima ochowere gine wi migam ma nyakafiri meno ochow gine jwogi, to ki Were. Aka akimiti ni wiriwere gi jwogi.
46010021	Wikinyal madho gim'owok i agwata pa Ruoth kodi apa jwogi bende. Wikinyal chiemo dhower pa Were to odoko wichiemo dhower pa jwogi bende.
46010022	Onyo wanomiy Ruoth wotimi nyieko? Wiparo nike watek loyo go?
46010023	Kada winopar ni, “Chik yeyo wan timo gimoro jye,” to kibedi ni kis gimoro jye di kony.
46010024	Wongoye moro ma rango bero pere won kende, to bero pa jowote bende.
46010025	Chami gimoro jye mitana i katale, mongoye kiganagana moro jye i paro ma chunyin.
46010026	Kole paka ndiiko wacho, “Lowo kodi gimoro jye man'iye obedo apa Ruoth.”
46010027	Ka ŋata ongoye gi yeyo olwoŋin chiemo aka iridho kidho, chami gima okethi ruwaŋin mongoye kiganagana moro jye i paro ma chunyin.
46010028	To ka moro owacho rin ni, “Me chiemo mochow gine chal makichar,” onyo ikiri icham chiemo no, ma kweyo chuny ŋata owacho rin ameno ma konyo paro ma chunye;
46010029	akiwachi ni ma konyo paro ma chunyin, to ma chuny ŋaticha ayin. Nyatoro nyalo penjo ni, “Onyo raŋo ma syem paran wochungi kwoŋ paro ma chuny ŋat man?
46010030	Ka atyeko ran fuoyo Were ri chiemo paran, raŋo ma ŋat man pusa an ru chiemo ma atyeko kir keth'iye silwany?”
46010031	Amomiyo, gima witimo jye, kosa wichiemo kosa wimadho gimoro, timi win ameno ma miyo Were dwoŋ.
46010032	Wikiri wiŋedhi chuny Joyudaya kosa Jopath, kosa kitipa pa jomoyeyo.
46010033	Wibende timi win paka atimo. Ato atemo kisangala dhano jye i gimoro jye m'atimo, mongoye paro kwoŋ bero paran won, to bero pa ji mathoth ayino, ŋeyi jowonyali limo both.
46011001	Timi win gima wineno kwoŋan paka abende atimo gima aneno kwoŋ Kristo.
46011002	Afuoyo win rupiri ndiri jye wipoyan aka wiluwo fuonji m'amiyo win.
46011003	To amito wiŋey ni Kristo obedo jatel pa jachwo jye, jachwo obedo jatel pa chiege, aka Were obedo jatel pa Kristo.
46011004	Amomiyo, jachwo ma lamo Were kosa tucho mikwenda pa Were moboyo wiye meno chayo jatel pere.
46011005	Aka dhako moro jye ma lamo Were kosa tucho mikwenda pa Were ma koboyo wiye meno bende chayo jatel pere: pokirok ongoye kwoŋ go kodi dhako molyel wiye.
46011006	Ka dhako kiboy wiye, ere wolyel woko. To paka obedo gi wichkwot dhako lyelo wiye kosa ŋado yey wiye, go ripo boyo wiye.
46011007	Jachwo kiripi boyo wiye, rupiri go nyutho chal kodi dwoŋ pa Were. Aka dhako nyutho dwoŋ pa jachwo.
46011008	Ato kochwey jachwo wok kwoŋ dhako, to dhako ama owok kwoŋ jachwo.
46011009	Aka jachwo kochwey ri dhako, to dhako ama ochwey ri jachwo.
46011010	Amomiyo ru jomalaika ma joneno, dhako ripo bedo gi giboyo wiye ma nyutho nike go nitye i men pa chwore.
46011011	To kada ameno, i kwo mawan i Ruoth, dhako kibedi ma kothenere kwoŋ jachwo, odoko jachwo bende kibedi ma kothenere kwoŋ dhako.
46011012	Ato paka dhako ochwey wok kwoŋ jachwo, apaka bende jachwo nywole wok kwoŋ dhako; aka gikipiny jye wok bongi Were.
46011013	Wiwegi neni win: otire ka dhako kwayo Were gi wiye ma koboyi?
46011014	Kwo ma kis ndelo won kifuonji win ye ni jachwo m'oweyo yey wiye ogaŋere meno won dwokere chien,
46011015	mato ri dhako meno a bero pere? Ato omiy go yewiye maboyo no paka giumirok.
46011016	To ka moro mito pyem kwoŋ gime, awacho nyaka ni wangoye gi kite man aluwa, kada i kitipa pa jomoyeyo Were jye.
46011017	I fuonji me, adyeri akifuoy win: rupiri chokirok mewin medo win racho ayin loyo bero.
46011018	Marapena, awinjo nike nitye pokirok mogo i chokirok mewin, to fuodi akiyey odocho ni timere ameno.
46011019	(Aka pokirok no ripo aripa bedo i dyer win ŋey joradyeri jowonenere kamaler.)
46011020	Ato ka wiromo kanyachiel kere wikibin ri win chamo chiemo pa Ruoth mothyeno ma gike,
46011021	rupiri ka wichiemo, dhano jye won chomere gi chiemo pere ma kikur wadi; ma miyo joman kech neko jo kareno joman jotyeko ri gin madho gimoro.
46011022	Wingoye gi pechin mewin ma chiemo gi or'iye giramadha? Kosa wimito chayo kitipa pa jomoyeyo Were ayino gi miyo jochandi kumo? Wiyenyo awachi ri win aŋo kwoŋ gime? Onyo afuoy wini? Be! Akotim ameno!
46011023	Kole alimo fuonji me wok bongi Ruoth aka abende akelo ri win: Nike Ruoth Yesu, wor mocham'iye ri go sereko, okwanyo mugat,
46011024	oketho Were walwa, oturo to wacho ni, “Me delkwoŋan, momiy win. Timi win ama ma poyan.”
46011025	I yo achiel, okwanyo agwata munyo chiemo mothyeno orumo to wacho ni, “Me agwata ma remo paran ma chikirok manyien. Onyo wangi kis ka wichamo mugat me aka wimadho gima ni i agwata me, meno witucho tho pa Ruoth chuka go odwoki.”
46011026	Kole chuka Ruoth obin, wibino tucho tho pere wangi ka wichamo mugat me aka wimadho gima ni i agwata me.
46011027	Amomiyo, ŋata ocham mugat pa Ruoth kosa omadhi gima ni i agwata pere i kite ma kiripi, meno timo gima kiripi kwoŋ del pa Ruoth kodi remo pere.
46011028	Dhano jye ripo kutho kikaŋasa kwo pere ma fuodi kochamo mugat me kosa madho gima ni i agwata me.
46011029	Ato ŋata chamo aka madho gikipiny me ma kinen dwoŋ mani i del pa Ruoth, meno won ketho banja kwoŋe.
46011030	Amomiyo jomathoth kwoŋ win jotwo aka jongoye gi men, aka joman jotyeko kir tho.
46011031	Bedi wakutho wakaŋasa kwo mawan di wakidonji i banja gi Were.
46011032	Ka Ruoth thumo ri wan banja meno miyo wan girachula ma tiro wan, ŋey wokiri wothumi ri wan banja kanyachiel gi ji ma piny.
46011033	Amomiyo, wutimera, ka wichokere kanyachiel i dhower pa Ruoth, kuri win jowoti win.
46011034	Ka nyatoro thoth gi kech, go ripo chiemo pecho aka ŋey ka wiromo kanyachiel kite mewin wokiri womiyi win donjo i banja gi Were. Kwoŋ wach man, abino chowo ka abino.
46012001	Onyo, wach ma mako kwoŋ mich mawok bongi Chuny Maleŋ, amito winiaŋ odocho kwoŋe, wutimera.
46012002	Wiŋeyo nike munyo oido fuodi wibedo jokafiri oido owondi win to itero win bongi chal makichar mobedo obadha.
46012003	Amomiyo amito wiŋey ni ongoye ŋata luwo gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ pa Were ma nyalo wacho ni, “Wokwoŋ Yesu!” Odoko ongoye ŋata nyalo wacho ni, “Yesu a Ruoth,” ka Chuny Maleŋ ama komiyo go men.
46012004	Mich ma chuny nitye mopokere opokere, to Chuny Maleŋ achiel ama poko jye.
46012005	Odoko tich nitye mopokere opokere, to Ruoth achiel ama itiyo ri go.
46012006	Mich ma timo tich bedo mopokere opokere, to Were achiel won ama poko dhano jye mich no.
46012007	Kis dhano jye imiyo ranyuth pa Chuny Maleŋ ri bero pa ji jye.
46012008	Chuny no miyo ŋatachiel mikwenda ma ryeko, ŋat man Chuny miyo mikwenda ma ŋeyo gimoro.
46012009	Chuny achiel no miyo ŋatachiel yeyo, aka ŋat man go miyo mich mopokere opokere ma botho two.
46012010	Chuny no miyo natachiel men ma timo giraura, ŋat man mich ma luwo mikwenda mawok bongi Were; aka ŋat man, men ma poko i dyer ranyuth mawok bongi Chuny Maleŋ kodi man ma kiwoki bonge. Ŋatachiel go miyo men ma luwo dhudhok mopokere opokere, ŋat man men ma tito dwoŋ dhudhok no.
46012011	To Chuny achiel ama timo gime jye; go miyo kis dhano mich mopokere paka go won yenyo.
46012012	Kole paka del obedo gimoro achiel ma nitye g'adeche mopokere, apaka bende Kristo chalo. Go obedo paka del achiel ma adeche omor'iye.
46012013	Kole wajojye, kada bedi Joyudaya kodi Jopath, kosa joma ni syem kodi ŋechin, jye Chuny achiel ama omiyo wan batisimo i del achiel, aka omiy wajojye limo Chuny Maleŋ achiel.
46012014	Kole del kotim g'adech achiel kende, to g'adeche momore.
46012015	Bedi tyendi jo wachi ni, “Paka akibedo chingi, onyo akibedo adech pa del,” meno di komono go bedo adech pa del.
46012016	Aka bedi ithi jo wachi ni, “Paka akibedo waŋ, onyo akibedo adech pa del,” meno bende di komono go bedo adech pa del.
46012017	Bedi del gipi bedi waŋ won kende, d'owinjo wach nedi? Aka bedi del gipi bedi ith won kende, d'oŋweyo gimoro nedi?
46012018	To paka nitye, Were oketho adeche mopokere ma del i kabedo pajo paka won oyenyo.
46012019	Bedi adeche jye lokere achiel kende, aŋo ma d'olwoŋ ni del?
46012020	To paka nitye, adeche omore ri gin, to jye fuodi jobedo del achiel.
46012021	Amomiyo, waŋ jo kinyal wacho ri chingi jo ni, “Akiyenyin!” Kosa wich bende wacho ri tyendi jo ni, “akiyenyin!”
46012022	Kuchiel, adeche ma del ma waparo ni nok gi kony, ama odoko yenyere loyo.
46012023	Aka adeche ma del ma waparo ni bu kony odocho ama wagwoko maber swa; odoko adeche ma del ma kineen maŋon odocho ama walith gine tektek,
46012024	Aka adeche moasa bero ama kiyeny. Were won am'oriwo wan to miyo adeche michayo no dwoŋ.
46012025	Ameno aka wongoye gi pokirok i del, kareno kis adech tiyere gi nyawote.
46012026	Ka adech achiel ma del olimo litho, adeche modoŋ jye jowinjo litho gine; ka adech achiel omiy dwoŋ, wadi jye josangala gine.
46012027	Onyo wijojye wibedo delkwoŋ Kristo, aka kis dhano obedo adech mere.
46012028	Aka i kitipa pa jomoyeyo, Were oketh'iye: marepena jomoor, mararyo jotuchi wach Were, maradek jofuonji, to luwo joma timo giraura, to luwo joma ni gi men ma botho two, kodi joma konyo jowoti gin, aka joman jodhum, kodi joma luwo dhudhok mopokere opokere.
46012029	Wiparo ni ji jye jobedo jomoor? Kosa jotuchi wach Were? Kosa jofuonji? Dhano jye ni gi men ma timo giraura?
46012030	Kosa botho two? Kosa luwo dhudhok mopokere? Kosa tito dwoŋ dhudhok no?
46012031	To kethi win chuny win kwoŋ mich ma loyo dwoŋ ayin. Aka alenyutho win royo maber ma loyo:
46013001	Kada aluw dhudhok pa ji kir g'apa malaika, to angoye gi mar, d'achal achala olaŋ ma koko wiy jo kosa dewe ma woy nono.
46013002	Kada abedi gi mich ma tucho mikwenda pa Were kodi ma niaŋ kwoŋ nyaliŋliŋ jye; odoko kada abedi gi yeyo ma nyalo ŋilo woko gote, to angoye gi mar, meno jye fuodi angoye kony.
46013003	Kada anyal poko gimoro jye mani gine; kada ayey delkwoŋan wowaŋ, ka angoye gi mar, meno kikonyan kada mathin.
46013004	Mar kudere odoko ni gi wor; mar ongoye gi nyieko, kwoto, kosa pakirok;
46013005	mar ongoye gi gero, kosa mima; kimaki nge piyo, aka kipar kwoŋ timo racho; mar kibedi gi duro;
46013006	mar kisangala gi recho, to sangala g'adyeri ayino.
46013007	Mar kijoki kichar; geno, aka kilachere.
46013008	Mar kirum chil gi chil. To mikwenda mitucho bino chok; dhudhok mopokere opokere bende bino rumo; aka mich ma ŋeyo gimoro bende jye bino ware woko.
46013009	Kole mich ma wani gine ma ŋeyo gimoro kodi ma tucho mikwenda pa Were jye jokobedo gim'ochowere.
46013010	To ka gim'ochowere obin, gikenyo gima kochowere bino leny woko.
46013011	Munyo fuodi anyathi, aluwo paka nyathi, odoko aparo paka nyathi; munyo alokere ŋata otegino, aweyo woko tim ma thino.
46013012	Kole pama fuodi waneno gikipiny maripirip pa ndewiro ma nimnim, to rumachien wabino neno gikipiny awaŋ g'awaŋ. Pama aŋeyo gikipiny adech kende; rumachien abino ŋeyo mochowere, aka mochowere paka Were oŋeyan.
46013013	Onyo gikipiny adek me: yeyo, geno kodi mar jye joyindira, to mar ama loyo jye.
46014001	Amomiyo wiripo bedo gi mar. Kethi win chuny win kwoŋ mich machuny, kodhi won mich ma tucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were!
46014002	Ŋata luwo dhudhok mopokere opokere kiluwi gi ji to gi Were ayin, rupiri ongoye ŋata niaŋ gima go wacho. Go luwo wach mopondo ma nyaliŋliŋ gi kony pa Chuny.
46014003	To ŋata tucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were meno luwo gi ji, miyo ji dongo aka medo jo men, odoko diyo chuny jo.
46014004	Ŋata luwo dhudhok mopokere opokere won konyere kende, to ŋata tucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were konyo kitipa pa jomoyeyo gipi.
46014005	Onyo ayenyo ri wijojye luwo dhudhok mopokere; to maloyo oido d'ayenyo ni winyal bedo gi mich ma tucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were. Kole ŋata tucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were ni gi kony loyo ŋata luwo dhudhok mopokere, kwanyo woko ka nitye ŋata tito dwoŋ gima go wacho i dhudhok ma ŋiaŋere; ney kitipa pa jomoyeyo gipi wolim kony.
46014006	Onyo, wutimera, ka abino bongi win, kony aŋo m'obedi ri win ka aluwo dhudhok mopokere ma wikiniaŋ? Ongoye kada masisiri, kwanyo woko ka akelo wach momenyere mogo mawok bongi Were, kosa amiyo win niaŋ kwong gimoro, kosa atucho mikwenda moro mawok bongi Were; kosa afuonjo win.
46014007	Kada ka waneno kwoŋ gikipiny mongoye gi kwo paka madundu kosa tongol, ŋa moŋey dwondi wer mituko ka dwonde kowok ma tito wer no?
46014008	Aka ka kokudhi dwondi gwara moŋeyere, ŋa moyikere ri lweny?
46014009	K'inen ameno, onyo ŋa moŋey gima iluwo kwoŋe ka mikwenda perin i dhudhok mopokere koŋey dwoŋ mere? Kole wach perin bino leny woko i koyo!
46014010	Adyer dhudhok omore i piny, to ongoye kada achiel kwoŋ jo ma dwoŋ mere ongoye.
46014011	To ka akiniaŋ dwoŋ gima nyatoro luwo, meno onyo alokere jakichar ri ŋata luwo, aka go bende lokere ran jakichar moro.
46014012	Paka wiwanya bedo gi mich pa Chuny, onyo maloyo jye, temi win swa oro mich ma konyo gero kitipa pa jomoyeyo gipi.
46014013	Amomiyo, ŋata luwo dhudhok mopokere opokere, mitere ri go kwayo mich ma tito dwoŋ mere.
46014014	Kole ka akwayo Were gi dhudhok mopokere opokere meno chunyan ama kwayo to paro paran kitim gimoro.
46014015	Onyo atim nedi? Abino kwayo gi chunyan, to abino kwayo gi paro paran bende; abino wero gi chunyan, to abino wero gi paro paran bende.
46014016	Ka wifuoyo Were gi chuny win, onyo dhano ma ndir jye m'obin i dyer joma kwayo owachi nedi ni, “Ameno” i kwayo mewin ma fuoyo Were mato go kuya gima wiwacho?
46014017	Nyalo bedo ni adyeri oido wifuoyo ri win Were maber i kwayo mewin, to ŋat cha kilim kony be.
46014018	Afuoyo Were ni aluwo gi dhudhok mopokere opokere loyo moro jye kwoŋ win.
46014019	To i kalamo pa jomoyeyo Kristo d'ayenyo ni aluwi kada nyaka wach abich gi paro paran ma ŋiaŋere, ma fuonjo joman, loyo luwo wach gana apar gi dhudhok mopokere.
46014020	Wikiri wibedi pa nyithindho i paro mewin, wutimera; bedi win nyithindho i gima mako kwoŋ recho, to wibedo jomotegino i paro mewin.
46014021	Ondik ama i chik: Ruoth wacho ni, “Abino luwo gi ji me, abino oro ji ma joluwo dhudhok mopokere, gi i dhok jowiloka. To kada ameno ji paran jokowinjan.”
46014022	Amomiyo, dhudhok mopokere opokere meno ranyuth ri joma koyeyo Were to ki ri jomoyeyo; aka mich ma tucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were obedo ranyuth ri jomoyeyo, ma kiweno ri joma koyeyo.
46014023	Onyo ka kitipa pa jomoyeyo gi bee jochokere kanyachiel aka dhano jye luwo dhudhok mopokere opokere, ka ji ma ndir jye kosa joma koyeyo jobin, jokowachi ni neko omako wini?
46014024	To ka wijojye witucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were, aka dhano ma koyeyo kosa ma kuya gimoro obin, bino ŋeyo recho pere chungo kwoŋ gima go winjo. Ibino thumo ri go banja chungo kwoŋ gima go winjo;
46014025	aka paro mopondo i chunye bino wodhere kamaler. Gikenyo go bino ryewere piny to lamo Were munyo tucho ni, “Adyeri, Were nitye gi win!”
46014026	Wutimere, gim'awacho dwoŋ mere aŋo? Ka wiromo kanyachiel i kwayo, ŋatachiel nitye gi wer, ŋat man gi fuonji, ŋat man gi menyirok ma wok i wach pa Were, ŋat man dhudhok mopokere, aka ŋat man jatiti dwoŋ dhudhok no. Gimoro jye wobedi ma konyo kitipa pa jomoyeyo.
46014027	Ka nyatoro oluw gi dhudhok mopokere, ji aryo kosa adek ma kikal kenyo ama joripo luwo, i weso, kareno ŋat man tito dwoŋ gimiluwo.
46014028	Ka ongoye moro ma nyalo tito dwoŋ mere, ere jaluwo wokiri womedere luwo i dhodhok no i romo, kwanyo woko won woluw i nyaliŋliŋ gi Were.
46014029	Ripere ji aryo kosa adek momiy jo mikwenda pa Were ama jowoluwi, kareno joman jokaŋasa wach m'oluw ka otire.
46014030	To ka ŋat man olimo menyirok ma wok i wach pa Were, ŋata onwaŋo luwo ripo liŋ.
46014031	Kole wijojye winyalo tucho mikwenda ma wok bongi Were ŋat achielechiele, ŋey dhano jye wonyali fuonjirok to ji jye limo men.
46014032	Aka chuny jotuchi mikwenda ma wok bongi Were kidhyer jo wegi dhumo;
46014033	ato Were kobedo jakeli nywowirok to obedo jakeli syem ayin.
46014034	Paka yenyere i kitipa pa jomaleŋ iye jye, mon mewin joripo liŋ i romo ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo. Koyey jo luwo, to joripo winjo or paka Chik bende wacho.
46014035	Ka jomito ŋeyo gimoro, joripo penjo chwogi jo yu pecho. Bedo gi wichkwot dhako luwo i romo ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo Kristo.
46014036	Kosa wach pa Were ochako bongi wini? Kosa wach no obino ri win kendiwini?
46014037	Ka moro ŋoyo nike go jatuchi mikwenda mawok bongi Were kosa nike go nitye kodi mich machuny, go ripo jolo gima andiko ri win paka obedo or pa Ruoth.
46014038	To ka kodewo kwoŋ wach me, meno ongoye ŋata odew kwoŋ go bende.
46014039	Amomiyo, wutimera, kethi win chuny win kwoŋ tucho mikwenda mawok bongi Were, aka wikiri wichieri ji luwo dhudhok mopokere opokere.
46014040	To gimoro jye ripere wotim i royo motire mochan maber.
46015001	Onyo wutimera, amito poyo win, Wach Maber ma atyeko fuonjo win, ma wijolo, ma yeyo mewin onyo ochung'iye matek.
46015002	Wach Maber ma afuonjo win no ama bino botho win ka wichwir'iye matek, ka kameno, meno wiyeyo gima ongoye.
46015003	Achwayo ri win gima abende ajolo, aka meno a gima dwoŋ swa: nike Kristo otho ri gimarecho mawan paka Ndiiko Maleŋ wacho;
46015004	nike oyik go tichierino go i kwo chieŋ maradek, paka Ndiiko Maleŋ wacho;
46015005	nike go omenyere ri Petro, aka rumachien bende ri jomoor apar g'aryo jye.
46015006	Rumachien go omenyere ri jofuonjirok pere ma kalo miya abich kiromo, aka mathoth kwoŋ jo fuodi jokwo, kada joman jotyeko nindo.
46015007	Gikenyo go omenyere ri Yakobo, gi rumachien ri jomoor pere jye.
46015008	Machowe, go omenyere ran bende, an ma achal pa ŋatonywol apoya.
46015009	Ato abedo jamoor moasa thin kwoŋ jomoor jye, ma kiripi kada alwoŋa ni jamoor, rupiri alwenyo gi kitipa pa jomoyeyo Were.
46015010	To ru ŋono pa Were, abedo ŋata abedo, aka ŋono ma go otimo ran kobedo ma bu kony. Kuchiel, atyeko tiyo matek loyo jomoor man jye, kada kobedo tich paran won, to ŋono pa Were mani kodan ama tiyo.
46015011	Amomiyo, kada obedo an kosa jo ama jotito ri win, to me a gima wijojye wiyeyo.
46015012	Onyo ka itito ni Kristo ochierino kwoŋ jomotho, jomegi kwoŋ win odoko jowacho nedi ni chierino pa jomotho ongoye?
46015013	K'inen chierino ongoye, nyutho ni kere Kristo kochierino be;
46015014	aka ka Kristo kochierino kwoŋ jomotho, meno kere fuonji mawan ongoye kony aka yeyo mewin bende ongoye kony.
46015015	Medo kwoŋ meno, nyutho ni wachwoko dhok Were, rupiri wawacho nike go ochierino Kristo kwoŋ jomotho mato kere kochierino go, k'inen obedo adyeri ni jomotho jokichierino.
46015016	Ato ka jomotho kichierino jo, meno nyutho ni kir Kristo bende kochierino.
46015017	Aka ka Kristo kochierino, meno nyutho ni kere yeyo mewin bu kony aka fuodi wirwenyo i gimarecho mewin.
46015018	Aka joma onwaŋo joyeyo ma jotyeko ywomere i Kristo kere bende jotyeko rwenyo woko ayin.
46015019	Ka wageno Kristo nyaka i kwo ma pama i piny ka kende meno kere waŋati wajolifol maloyo joman jye i piny gipi.
46015020	To iyadyeri otyek chierino Kristo kwoŋ jomotho, paka gimanyak monyak marapena kwoŋ jomotho ma bende jobino chierino.
46015021	Ato paka tho owok kwoŋ dhano achiel, i royo achiel chierino kwoŋ jomotho bende onyo wok kwoŋ ŋatachiel.
46015022	Paka ji jye jotho ru nywolirok kwoŋ Adam, ameno bende apaka ibino chierino ji jye i Kristo.
46015023	To kis dhano chierino gi hongo pere; Kristo marapena ri ji jye; nyaka joma jobedo apa Kristo bende jobino luwo i ndir ma bino pere.
46015024	Gikenyo, gike bino tundo; Kristo bino reyo woko adhum jye, gi dwoŋ, kodi men jye, to kodo ker ri Were Bawan.
46015025	Ato Kristo ripo dhumo chuka Were okethi jokwor jye i par tyende.
46015026	Jakwor ma ibino reyo ma chowe a tho.
46015027	Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Were oketho gimoro jye i par tyende.” Ato, ka owachi ni, “Gimoro jye okethi i par tyende”, meno kirwak Were bende iye, rupiri go amoketho gimoro jye i adhum pa Kristo.
46015028	Aka k'otyeki ketho gimoro jye i adhum pa Kristo, gikenyo go won, paka Wuodi Were, bende bino donjo i adhum pa Were, moketho gimoro jye i par tyende; ŋey Were wodhumi kis gimoro jye.
46015029	Ka kobedo ameno, to iraŋo jomegi jolimo batisimo kawaŋ jomotho? Ka obedo adyeri paka jowacho ni jomotho jokichierino, raŋo ma ji limo batisimo kawaŋ jomotho?
46015030	To wan, raŋo ma wayeyo chandirok hongo jye?
46015031	Wutimera, athenere gi tho ndelo jye, to pakirok mani gine ru win i kwo mawan i Kristo Yesu Ruodhiwan ama miyan atucho gime.
46015032	K'inen alwenyo g'ogwange mager ma Efeso, nyaka ru mbusa paka dhano, bero aŋo ma alim'iye? Ka jomotho kichierino paka jowacho, kere onyo, “Wey wachiemi wamedhi rupiri dikin waletho.”
46015033	Moro wokiri womiŋi win: kole, “Kitipa marach nyieko kite maber.”
46015034	Dwoki win i paro mewin motire wiwey timo recho. Awacho gime ma kwoto wiy win; ato jomegi kwoŋ win jokuya Were.
46015035	Nyatoro nyalo penjo ni, “Jomotho jobino chierino nedi? Jobino dwoko gi del ma chalo aŋo?”
46015036	In dhano mamiŋ! Kole kodhi m'ipidho i lowo kinyal twi gi kwo ka kokutho otho.
46015037	K'ipidho gimoro, ikipidhi gima twi gi kululu, to nyaka kodhi mere ayin paka nyigi ŋano, kosa kiti kodhi man,
46015038	Were miyo kodhi no kiti chal pere ma won oyenyo; go miyo kis kodhi achielechiele kiti chal pere ma ripo gine.
46015039	Aka gikipiny makwo kibedi nger achiel; ji jonitye gi del ma kite achiel, ogwange del ma kite man, winyin del ma kite man, rech bende del ma kite man.
46015040	Aka nitye chal ma nyapolo kodi ma nyapiny bende; onyo kiti ŋono pa gikipiny ma nyapolo obedo man, aka kiti ŋono pa gikipiny ma nyapiny bende obedo nger man.
46015041	Waŋchieŋ nitye gi lero mere, dwe gi lero man, aka michalin bende gi lero man: odoko kir i dyer michalin jye nitye lero mopekere.
46015042	Meno bende apaka bino bedo ka jomotho jochierino. Dhano miyiko obedo gima top; del ma go lechierino gine bino bedo gima kitopi.
46015043	Iyiko del manyap, to bino chierino mani gi men.
46015044	Iyiko paka del ma nyapiny, to bino chierino paka del ma nyachuny. K'inen del ma nyapiny nitye, meno del ma nyachuny bende ripo bedo.
46015045	Amomiyo ndiiko wacho ni, “Adam, dhano marapena olimo kwo;” to Adam machowe obedo Chuny ma miyo kwo.
46015046	Del ma nyachuny ama kitel, to ma nyapiny ama kutho telo, aka nyaka gima nyachuny luwo.
46015047	Adam marapena owok i piny, dhano ma fukefuke; Adam mararyo wok i polo.
46015048	Paka ŋat mochwey wok i fukefuke chalo, apaka ji jye ma piny ka bende jochalo; aka paka ŋata wok i polo chalo, bende apaka joma ni polo jochalo.
46015049	Aka paka waruko chal pa ŋatochwey gi fukefuke, ameno bende apaka wabino ruko chal pa ŋat mowok i polo.
46015050	Me a gima awacho, wutimera: del kodi remo kinyal donjo i Ker pa Were; aka gima tho bende kinyal donjo i kwo makitho ka kokutho owiro chal.
46015051	Weyi awachi ri win nyaliŋliŋ me: wajojye wakotho, to wabino wire ni wich,
46015052	mapiyo paka dyemo waŋ, k'ogoy gwara machowe. Ato gwara bino ywak, to jomotho jochierino gi del ma kibino tho kendo, aka wajojye wabino wire.
46015053	Ato del ma tho me ripo ruko del ma kitho aka ŋey kwo ma rumo piyo me wolokere ma kirum.
46015054	Amomiyo ka otyek rwako ri gima tho ruk ma kitho, aka gima kiyindira otyeki rwako ri go ruk ma yindira, nyaka ndiiko bino tundo i kare ma wacho ni, “Men pa tho otyeki loyo woko kichutho.”
46015055	“Tho, nikune paka idoko inoloy lweny? Tho, nikune kwir perin ma lunga?”
46015056	Ato kwir pa tho ma lunga wok i gimarach, aka gimarach nwaŋo men pere i Chik.
46015057	To Were wofuoy ma miyo wan loyo lweny i Yesu Kristo Ruodhiwan!
46015058	Amomiyo, wutimera, chungi win matek ma wichwiny, ma wikiyengere. Yindini win ndir jye i tich mewin ri Ruoth, rupiri wiŋeyo ni ongoye gima witimo i tich mewin ri Ruoth ma bu kemba.
46016001	Onyo wach ma mako kwoŋ pesa miripo choko ma konyo ji pa Were i Yudeya: Timi win gima awacho ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Galasya timo.
46016002	I ndelo marapena jye ma tich, i Sabiti, ŋatachielechele kwoŋ win ripo ketho gichen pesa moro, ma go nyalo ketho paka lim pere nitye, aka wokan kichutho, ŋey wongoye kendo choko pesa moro ka abino.
46016003	Ka abino, aledhiro ji mogo ma wifuoyo kiti jo, gi balwa manyutho jo, jowoteri mich mewin Yerusalem.
46016004	Ka yenyere ran kidho, bende jonyalo woth kodan.
46016005	Alebino bongi win ka atyeko wok yu Masedonia, rupiri ayiko luwo yu Masedonia.
46016006	Miti abino chowo hongo moro gi win, ma kono kada hongo ma chwir ma pe ŋich'iye piny no gipi, ŋey winyal konyan i medirok gi woth paran kamoro jye ma anokidh'iye kendo,
46016007	rupiri akimiti neno win nyaka i hongo machiek won akadha. Ageno chowo hongo moromoye gi win ka Ruoth oyeyo.
46016008	To abino bedo Efeso ka nyuka ndelo ma Pentekost.
46016009	Aka royo onyo oyawere ran malach ma tich, kada joma pyemo kodan jomore.
46016010	To ka Timotheyo obino bongi win, yikere win ma miyo go ŋeyo ni wijolo go maber, rupiri go bende tiyo ri Ruoth paka an.
46016011	Wongoye ŋata wochayi go, to wikonyi go womedere gi woth pere i syem, aka nyaka go bino dwoko bongan: kole wan kodi jomoyeyo jye wakuro neno go.
46016012	Onyo, i wach ma mako kwoŋ Apolo, atyeko temo dhiro go limo win kodi jomoyeyo man, to go won fuodi koneno ni ber wobin pama. To ka go olimo hongo, aka obin.
46016013	Bedi win waŋ win, chungi win matek i yeyo, bedi win miseni, bedi win gi men.
46016014	Gimoro jye ma witimo, timi win gi mar.
46016015	Aka wutimera, wiŋeyo kwoŋ Sitefano gi pecho pere paka jobedo jomotelo wirok i yeyo i Yunani, aka jomiyere tich ri ji maleŋ pa Were. Akwayo win wutimera,
46016016	yeyo tel pa ji machalo ameno, kodi apa joman jye ma jotiyo matek gi jo.
46016017	Asangala gi bino pa Sitefano, Fotinato, kodi Akaiko rupiri jobino kamewin,
46016018	aka joyomo chunyan kir gi chuny win bende. Joli win ji ma pameno.
46016019	Kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma i adech ma Asya jodhiro ri win moth; Akwila kodi Prisila, kodi kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma romo i ot pajo jodhiro ri win moth moasere i Ruoth.
46016020	Jomoyeyo ma ka jye jodhiro ri win moth. Mothere win akor i leŋo.
46016021	An Paulo, awon andiko moth me gi chingan.
46016022	Ŋata komaro Ruoth Yesu Kristo, wonwaŋi kwoŋ! Maranantha (Ruodhiwan biye!)
46016023	Ŋono pa Ruoth Yesu wobedi kodi win.
46016024	Mar paran wobedi kodi wijojye i Kristo Yesu.
47001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, jamoor pa Kristo Yesu i mito pa Were, jokodi omin wan Timotheyo, Ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo Kristo ma Korinthya, kodi ji pa Were jye ma Yunani.
47001002	Weyi ŋono gi syem mowok bongi Were Baa wan kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo wobedi gi win.
47001003	Wopaki Were ma Baa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo, Bawan ma jawor, Were ma jakweyi chuny ji!
47001004	Go kweyo chuny wan i teko ma waluw'iye jye, ŋey wanyal bende kweyo chuny ji ma jonitye i teko ma nger jye, munyo waoro kony ma wawegi bende watyeko limo bongi Were.
47001005	Paka wariwere gi Kristo i chandirok pere momore, ameno bende luwo kwoŋ Kristo wariwere gi go i kony pere moasere.
47001006	Ka wachandere, meno ma konyo win kodi ma both mewin; ka okony wan, meno okony win bende aka omiy win men ma chiro kiti chandirok ma wabende wachiro.
47001007	Amomiyo, geno mawan ma wani gine kwoŋ win kiyengere, rupiri waŋeyo ni paka wiriwere kodi wan i chandirok mawan, onyo wibende wiriwere gi wan i kony ma walimo.
47001008	Wakimiti wibedi ma wikuya, wutimin wan, teko ma walimo i adech ma Asya. Byeto moyim ri wan obedo madwoŋ aka mapek swa, momiyo oido wakigen kir kwo kendo.
47001009	Oido waparo nike otyek thumo ri wan banja ma tho. To gino obedo ameno ŋey wathenere, ki kwoŋ wawegi, to kwoŋ Were ayin, ma chierino jomotho.
47001010	Go obotho wan kwoŋ tho ma d'orach moasere, aka fuodi go bino botho wan. Waketho geno mawan kwoŋ go nike go bino medere gi botho wan kendo;
47001011	aka wiripo konyo wan gi kwayo. Meno aka ji mathoth jobino fuoyo Were ri wan, ru mich ma go omiy wan chungo kwoŋ kwayo pa ji mathoth.
47001012	Me a gima wapakere gine: Paro ma chuny wan miyo waridho ni i kwo mawan i piny ka, tektek mere i riwirok mawan gi win kanyachiel, wawotho i leŋo kodi i adyeri pa Were. Aka watimo ameno gi men ma ŋono pa Were, ma kiweno gi ryeko pa dhano.
47001013	Kole wakindiki ri win gima wikinyal kisoma gi niaŋ kwoŋe. Aka ageno nike paka fuodi wikiniaŋ kwoŋ wan odocho, wibino niaŋ kichutho,
47001014	(i gima pama winiaŋ wiyewiye), ŋey i Ndelo pa Ruoth Yesu winyal pakere gi wan paka bende wabino pakere gi win.
47001015	Paka onwaŋo atyeko ridho timo gime, oido ayiko bino lyewo win kutho, ŋey wilim silwany diryo.
47001016	Kole onwaŋo achano lyewo win ka akidho yu Masedonia, aka ka adwoko anwaŋiye kony bongi win i woth paran ma kidho Yudeya.
47001017	I chan paran me, oido achale pa jawiroki? Manago atimo chan ma nyapiny kareno awacho ni “Ey, ey,” kodi “Be, be” i hongo no won?
47001018	Paka Were obedo ŋata genere, chikirok mawan gi win kobedo “Ey” kodi “Be”.
47001019	Kole Yesu Kristo, Wuodi Were, ma wan kodi Sila gi Timotheyo wafuonjo win kwoŋe kobedo “Ey” kodi “Be”. Kuchiel i Kristo, fuonji no ndir jye bedo “Ey”.
47001020	Amomiyo chikirok pa Were jye, kada mathoth nedi, i Kristo bedo abeda “Ey”. Meno amomiyo i Yesu Kristo, wawacho “Ameno” mawan, ma miyo Were dwoŋ.
47001021	Kole Were won ama miyo wan, kanyachiel gi win, chungo matek i Kristo; aka go won ama owiro wan gi mo i tich pere,
47001022	to ketho ranyuth pere kwoŋ wan paka wabedo apere, to ketho Chuny Maleŋ i chuny wan ma ridho ni lemiyo wan gimoro jye ma go okano ri wan.
47001023	Alwoŋo Were wobedi jakony paran rupiri go oŋeyo chunyan! Kole aworo win amomiyo akidwoko yu Korinthya.
47001024	Onyo wakitem chuko win gi gima wiripo yeyo, rupiri wichungo matek i yeyo. Kuchiel, watiyo gi win ri kisangala mewin won.
47002001	Amomiyo, aridho paro nike akir adoko abin bongi win ramo chuny win kendo.
47002002	Aka ka aramo chuny win, ŋa man ma di miyan kisangala ma kiweno win won ma atyeko ramo chuny win?
47002003	Andiko ri win balwa aka ŋey ka abino bongi win, ji ma di miyan kisangala kiri jowomiyan gut ayino. Kole ageno kwoŋ wijojye nike kisangala paran bedo mewin bende.
47002004	Andiko ri win ma chunyan odwoyere kendo raman, gi pigi waŋan madit, ki ma ramo chuny win, to ma miyo win ŋeyo paka amaro win.
47002005	Onyo, ka moro obenga, kiram chunyan, to ramo chuny win ayino, ka akitero wach no bor tektek.
47002006	Girachula ma ji mathoth kwoŋ win jotyeko miyo go won romo.
47002007	Kuchiel, onyo pama wiripo chwako go gi miyo go miseni, woweyi bedo gi guto madwoŋ, to chunye ŋedhere woko.
47002008	Amomiyo, akwayo win ni winyuthi go mar mewin.
47002009	Kole me amomiyo andiko ri win balwa no: onwaŋo amito ŋeyo paka wichiro maber tem no, gi ŋeyo paka ndir jye wiyikere winjo fuonji paran.
47002010	Ka wichwako nyatoro i recho pere, abende achwako go. Kole ka achwako, k'inen adyeri ripere achwaki nyatoro, meno achwako go ma bero mewin i waŋ Kristo,
47002011	ŋey wageŋ Sitan kadho wan gi ryeko; ato waŋeyo chan pere.
47002012	Medo kwoŋ meno, munyo atundo Trowa kama akidho tit'iye Wach Maber mapa Kristo, anwaŋo ni Ruoth oido oyawo ran royo ma tich kenyo.
47002013	To fuodi oido ani gi rembo kwoŋbedo akinyalo nwaŋo omin wan Tito kenyo. Amomiyo asewila ji ma kenyo t'akidho yu Masedonia.
47002014	To Were wofuoy rupiri go noknok telo wan i loyo lweny i Kristo. Were oro wan paka jomikwenda pere ma miyo Kristo woŋeyere ri ji jye pa ŋweche kur ma tweyo piny.
47002015	Kole wachal ŋweche buban mamit ma Kristo waŋo ri Were ma kidho ri joma ibotho jo kodi joma rwenyo woko.
47002016	Ri joma jorwenyo woko, wachal ŋweche ma kelo tho; to ri joma ibotho, wachal ŋweche kur ma kelo kwo. Onyo ŋa ma di nyal tich me?
47002017	Wakichal jomathoth man, ma jooro mikwenda pa Were ma nwaŋ'iye lim; to rupiri Were ooro wan, waluwo g'adyeri ruwaŋ go, paka jotich pa Kristo.
47003001	Onyo chale pa wawegi odoko wayumere? Kosa nyalo bedo ni paka joman, onyo wabende wayenyo balwa ma fuoyo wan ri win kosa ma wok bongi win?
47003002	Kole wiwegi wibedo balwa mawan, mondik i chuny wan, ma dhano jye ŋeyo odoko soma.
47003003	Nenere kamaler ni wibedo balwa ma Kristo won ondiko ma mako kwoŋ tich mawan. Aka kondik gi bwino kwoŋ telin morudi, to ondik gi Chuny Maleŋ pa Were makwo kwoŋ telin ma chuny ji.
47003004	Wawacho gime gi miseni rupiri wanitye gi geno i Were kwoŋ Kristo.
47003005	To ki ni rupiri wawegi wani gi nyalo ma timo kis gimoro, to nyalo mawan wok bongi Were.
47003006	Go omiyo wanyalo tiyo ri chikirok manyien, ma kobedo apa Chik mondik, to apa Chuny Maleŋ, rupiri Chik mondik kelo tho, to Chuny miyo kwo.
47003007	To k'inen Chik ma kelo tho, mondik kwoŋ tele morudi obino gi dwoŋ moasere, ma Joisrael jokonyalo chomo waŋ gin kwoŋ Musa ru pilin ma waŋe, kada onwaŋo kidho rumo woko,
47003008	onyo dwoŋ ma wok i tich pa Chuny Maleŋ okadhi meno didi?
47003009	K'inen tich moido kelo kwoŋ ji banja obedo gi dwoŋ ameno, onyo tich ma kelo tiro ri ji obedi gi dwoŋ loyo meno didi?
47003010	Wanyalo wacho ni, rupiri dwoŋ ma pama onyo kalo machon, dwoŋ machon kere onyo orumo woko.
47003011	Ato ka gima rumo woko obino gi dwoŋ, meno gima yindira chil gi chil nitye gi dwoŋ ma loyo.
47003012	Amomiyo paka wanitye gi geno me, wabedo miseni swa.
47003013	Wakichal Musa, m'oboyo waŋe gi nanga, ni Joisrael kiri jowoneni pilin ma waŋe ka mojere to leny woko.
47003014	Paro pajo adyeri oido othore, rupiri kir konon ka josoma chikirok machon, nanga ma umo waŋ jo no fuodi doŋ adoŋa. Nanga no ware woko denge ka dhano ojolo Kristo.
47003015	Aka kir gi pama wo ena, ka josoma Chik pa Musa, nanga no fuodi umo auma paro pajo.
47003016	To ka dhano owire bongi Ruoth aka nyaka nanga no ware woko.
47003017	Onyo, “Ruoth”i luwo me, obedo Chuny; aka kama Chuny pa Ruoth ni iye, syem bedo kenyo.
47003018	Wajojye, onyo, wanyutho dwoŋ pa Ruoth gi waŋ wan ma koum; aka dwoŋ no, mawok bongi Ruoth mobedo Chuny, loko wan i chal pere, gi dwoŋ ma medere ameda.
47004001	Amomiyo, paka Were otyeko miyo wan tich me i wor pere, wakibino nyochere.
47004002	Waketho gichien tim ma nyaliŋliŋ ma kelo wichkwot; wakitiy gi twodo, odoko wakiwir wach pa Were. Kuchiel waluwo adyeri i lero, ma nyutho ji jye ni wanitye i tiro i waŋ Were.
47004003	Aka kada bedi ni Wach Maber ma wafuonjo opanere, kole opanere nyaka ri joma jokidho rwenyo won kende.
47004004	Were ma piny me oumo paro pa joma koyeyo gi mudho, ŋey womoni jo neno lero ma Wach Maber ma nyutho dwoŋ pa Kristo mobedo chal pa Were.
47004005	Ato wakifuonji kwoŋ wawegi: wafuonjo kwoŋ Kristo Yesu paka Ruoth, aka wabedo jotich ri win ri atoŋa pa Yesu.
47004006	Kole Were mowacho ni, “Lero wolyel wok i mudho,” ama omiyo lero pere lyel i chuny wan, ma kelo ri wan niaŋ kwoŋ dwoŋ pa Were, ma nenere i waŋ Kristo.
47004007	To wan ma wanitye gi ŋaŋo machuny me wachalo degi malowo, manyutho nike men moasere me wok bongi Were ayin ma kiweno bongi wan.
47004008	Teko diyo wan i thenge jye to kiŋiny wan woko; dichieŋ wadhyer, to chuny wan kiŋedhere woko;
47004009	I chando wan, to kojwangi wan; bende ogoy wan piny, to wakireyere woko.
47004010	Hongo jye watiŋo tho pa Yesu i delkwoŋ wan, aka ŋey kwo pere bende wonen i delkwoŋ wan.
47004011	I kwo mawan, ndir jye wathenere gi tho ri atoŋa pa Yesu, ŋey kwo pere wonenere i delkwoŋ wan ma kiruw tho me.
47004012	Me nyutho ni kere tho tiyo i wan; aka kwo ama tiyo rigo i win.
47004013	Ndiiko wacho ni, “Ayeyo, amomiyo aluwo.” Gi chuny ma yeyo achiel no, wabende onyo wayeyo amomiyo waluwo,
47004014	rupiri waŋeyo ni Were, mochierino Ruoth Yesu i kwo, bende bino chierino wan gi Yesu to kelo wan kanyachiel gi win ruwaŋe.
