47004015	Gino jye bedo ma bero mewin, ŋey ŋono pa Were ma tundo ri ji momore jowomedi fuoyo Were gi miyo go dwoŋ.
47004016	Meno ama omiyo wakilachere; kada men ma delkwoŋ wan mojere mathin mathin, to kwo ma chuny wan lokere manyien kis ndelo.
47004017	Aka teko mathin ma hongo machiek me bino kelo ri wan dwoŋ moasere ma chil gi chil, ma loyo teko no bor.
47004018	Amomiyo waketho paro mawan, ki kwoŋ gikipiny ma nenere, to kwoŋ gikipiny ma kinenere rupiri gima nenere chowo nyaka hongo machiek; to gima kinenere yindira chil gi chil.
47005001	Kole waŋeyo ni ka kayindi ma wabed'iye i piny, delkwoŋ wan me, okedhi woko, Were bino miyo wan ot ma chil gi chil i polo, ma dhano ama kogero.
47005002	Pama onyo wachukere gi awanya ma ruko ot mawan mani polo.
47005003	Ato k'oruki ri wan ot no, wakobedi kinyoro.
47005004	Ka fuodi wakwo i kayindi ma piny me, wachur aka wachukere gi paro ma diyo wan; ki rupiri wamito lunyo woko delkwoŋ wan, to rupiri wamito woruki ri wan del ma nyapolo ayino, aka ŋey kwo ma kirum womwonyi woko tho.
47005005	Were ama oyiko wan ri wirok me, aka omiyo wan Chuny Maleŋ ma ridho ni lemiyo wan gimoro jye ma go ochiko miyo wan.
47005006	Amomiyo hongo jye wanitye gi miseni. Waŋeyo nike ka tekin waripo i del me meno wanitye bor gi Ruoth.
47005007	Kole wakwo gi yeyo, ma kiweno gi gima waneno.
47005008	Awacho ni wapoŋ gi miseni, aka di wayenyi kir weyo delkwoŋ wan to wakadho bedo gi Ruoth.
47005009	To maloyo gimoro jye, wamito kisangala go, kada fuodi wanitye i del mawan me kosa be.
47005010	Kole wajojye waripo chungo ruwaŋ Kristo, go wothumi ri wan banja, ŋey kis dhano kwoŋ wan wolimi gima ripo gine chungo kwoŋ gima go otimo gi delkwoŋe, maber kosa marach.
47005011	Waŋeyo dwoŋ lworo Ruoth, amomiyo watemo naŋo ji. Were oŋeyo kwo mawan maber, aka ageno ni i chuny win wibende wiŋeyo wan.
47005012	Wakitem pakirok ri win kendo; kuchiel watemo miyo win thwolo ma yumirok gi wan ayin, aka nyaka wibino nyalo dwoko wach ma dhoki joma fuodi joyumere gi chal pa dhano ma woko, ma kiweno ma i adundo.
47005013	K'inen neko omako wan adyeri meno omako wan ri atoŋa pa Were; to ka wiy wan otire, meno otire ma bero mewin.
47005014	Ato mar pa Kristo ama dhumo wan, kareno waŋeyo ni dhano achiel otho ri ji jye, ma nyutho ni kere ji jye jotyeko tho.
47005015	Aka go otho ri ji jye, nike jomakwo kiri jowoteri kwo paka apa jo wegi to paka apa Kristo motho ri jo to ichierino go kwoŋ jomotho.
47005016	Amomiyo, wok pama wakithumi ri nyatoro banja chungo kwoŋ paro ma nyadhanodhano. Kada yado onwaŋo watero Kristo gi paro ma nyadhanodhano, pama wakitim ameno kendo.
47005017	Amomiyo ka moro nitye i Kristo, go obedo chwech manyien: gimachon okadho woko, manyien ama obino.
47005018	Gime jye wok bongi Were, ma i Kristo odwoko wan i tiyirok gine; aka omiyo wan tich ma dwoko joman bende i tiyirok gine.
47005019	Mikwenda mawan obedo ni: Were onyo dwoko ji ma piny i tiyirok gine i Kristo, aka kikwan gimarecho kwoŋ jo kendo. Were omiyo wan mikwenda paka go dwoko ji tiyirok gine kendo.
47005020	Amomiyo, wabedo jomikwenda ma joluwo ri Kristo, igani Were won gipi onyo goyo koko ri ji i wan. Kapa Kristo, wakwayo win ni dwoki win witiyere kodi Were!
47005021	Kristo oido ongoye gi gimarach, to Were omiyo go riwirok gi wan i gimarach mawan, ŋey i Kristo, wanyal bedo paka tiro pa Were.
47006001	Ri ameno, paka joma tiyo kanyachiel gi Were, wakwayo win ni paka wityeko jolo ŋono pa Were, onyo wikiri wiwey wonyiekere woko.
47006002	Kole Were wacho ni, “Awinjo dwondin i hongo paran ma nyutho wor, aka atyeko konyin i ndelo ma both.” Onyo me a hongo ma nwaŋo wor pa Were; me a ndelo ma limo both.
47006003	Wakimiti riwirok ri dhano moro jye i royo pere, rupiri meno nyalo miyo wochay tich mawan.
47006004	Kuchiel, i gimoro jye wanyutho ni wabedo jotich pa Were, munyo wachiro aŋedha chuny, teko, kodi peko gi diyo chuny madwoŋ.
47006005	Otyek goyo wan, tweyo wan, kodi woy gi wan; tich opikere ri wan, ruman nindo ngoye, to chiemo jye ngoye.
47006006	Watyeko nyutho ni wajotich pa Were gi lonyo, niaŋ, diyo chuny, kodi chuny maber, i Chuny Maleŋ, i mar mawan maradyeri,
47006007	i luwo adyeri, kodi i men pa Were. Wanitye gi tiro paka gilweny mawan, i chingi wan marachuch kodi maracham.
47006008	Imiyo wan dwoŋ, odoko ikwoto wiy wan; iyeto wan, aka odoko ipako wan. Itero wan paka jotwodo, mato waluwo adyeri;
47006009	paka joma koŋeyere, mato ji jye joŋeyo wan; itero wan pa jomotho, to kere wakwo. Kada chandi wan, kineki wan;
47006010	kada miyi wan gut, to ndir jye wasangala; wachale pa jochandi, to wamiyo jomathoth ŋaŋo; wachale pa joma jongoye gi gimoro, mato wanitye gi gimoro jye.
47006011	A Jokorinthya! Kole watyeko luwo kamaler ri win, wathango ri win chuny wan.
47006012	Wakipondo ri win; to wiŋat wipondo ri wan i chuny win.
47006013	Aluwo gi win igani winyithindho paran. Nyuthi wan win kiti paro ma wanitye gine ri win. Wibende yawi win chuny win malach paka watimo ri win.
47006014	Wikiri witiyere kanyachiel ma wirom kodi jomakoyeyo. Nyalere nedi tiro kodi komo bedo mere? Kosa nyalere nedi lero kodi mudho bedo kanyachiel?
47006015	Nyalere nedi Kristo kodi Jwogi tuyirok? Aŋo ma ŋata oyeyo Kristo riwo kodi ŋata koyeyo?
47006016	Tiyirok aŋo ma nitye i dyer Ot pa Were kodi chal makichar? Kole wabedo Ot pa Were makwo! Paka Were won owacho ni, “Abino bedo i jo to awotho gi jo. Abino bedo Were pajo, aka jobino bedo ji paran.”
47006017	Aka Ruoth wacho ni, “Amomiyo eye win bongi jo, aka wipokere gi jo. Wikiri wigeyi gima kolony, aka nyaka abino jolo win.
47006018	Abino bedo Baa win, aka wibino bedo wotan gi nyigan. Ruoth Majameni jye ama wacho.”
47007001	Paka wani gi chikirok me, jowotan mamaro, walonyi win kwoŋ gimoro jye ma kocho delkwoŋ wan, kosa chuny wan, aka warangi lokirok maleŋ ma kichutho, ka walworo Were i kwo mawan.
47007002	Nwaŋi win kabedo ri wan i chuny win. Wakitimo racho ri nyatoro, odoko wakinyieko kite pa moro, kosa temo timo gimahembi ri moro.
47007003	Akiwachi gime ma thumo ri win banja; rupiri paka atyeko wacho, winitye kachuny wan tektek momiyo wanitye kanyachiel, kada wakwo kosa watho.
47007004	Anitye gi geno madwoŋ i win; aka apakere gi win swa! Awinjo gi syem i win. Kada i teko mawan jye fuodi anitye atya gi kisangala.
47007005	Kir munyo watyeko tundo Masedonia jye wakiywomere kada, to wanwaŋo chandirok kis kamoro: kocha dhawirok okaro wan, korin lworo opoŋ i chuny wan.
47007006	To Were ma dwoko chuny jomobwok, odwoko chuny wan gi bino pa Tito.
47007007	Ki gi bino pere kende, to gi kony ma widwoko gine chunye bende. Go owacho ri wan paka wiyenyo swa nenan, paka wirem gi paka wiyikere konyan; gino omedan kisangala tektek.
47007008	Aka kada bedi ni balwa paran omiyo win rem, jye chunyan kiraman ni andiko. To kada ameno chunyan oramaye kwoŋ balwa no munyo aneno ni omiyo win rem nyaka hongo machiek won.
47007009	To pama asangala, ki rupiri amiyo win rem, to rupiri rem mewin omiyo wiŋuto recho mewin. Kole wibedo gi rem paka Were onwaŋo yenyo, amomiyo kere wakitimo ri win racho moro.
47007010	Kole rem ma wok bongi Were kelo ŋuto recho aka tero dhano i both; aka ongoye ramirok kenyo. To rem ma piny ka kelo tho ayin.
47007011	Ere neni win gima rem ma wok bongi Were no otyeko timo kwoŋ win; neni paka oloko win jomagenere, ma chuny win olony. Neni paka chuny win ramere, bwok, paro, maro Were, aka mito tiro ama wobedi. Kole wityeko nyutho ni wingoye gi racho i wach no jye.
47007012	Amomiyo, kada andiko balwa no, atimo ameno ki paka ŋata otimo marach, kosa ŋata otimi ri go marach. Kuchiel, andiko ma nyutho win kamaler, i waŋ Were, paka wimaro wan tektek.
47007013	Me amomiyo walimo miseni. Wakilimo miseni kende; to iyadyeri wamedo kisangala ru syem ma Tito onyutho kwoŋ kony ma wimiyo go ma dwoko chunye.
47007014	Kada bedi aŋata atel kiyuma win ri go, di wiyan kokwot be. Paka noknok waluwo ri win giradyeri, yumirok mawan ri Tito bende onyutho adyeri mawan.
47007015	Aka mar ma go ni gine ri win medere ameda ka go poyo paka wijojye wiwinjo or, gi paka wijolo go gi lworo gi kirin.
47007016	Asangala ni anyalo geno win kichutho!
47008001	Onyo wutimera, wamito wiŋey ŋono pa Were motyeko nyuthirok i dyer kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Masedonia.
47008002	I tem pajo maloŋo gi teko ma jolimo, kisangala pajo omedere chuka omiyo jobedo gi yomo ma chuny i wodho mich pajo, kada wegi oido jochandi.
47008003	Anyutho win ni adyeri jopoko gikipiny kweth paka jonyalo; aka ma kalo kir kenyo. Aka i yenyo pajo wegi,
47008004	jokwayo wan g'amen ni jowolimi silwany ma konyo ji pa Were i Yudeya.
47008005	Jokalo kir kama onwaŋo wanyalo geno! Marapena wegi jomiyere ri Ruoth; aka rumachien, gi mito pa Were, jomiyere ri wan bende.
47008006	Ri ameno wakwayo Tito, mochako tich me, ni womedere gine, aka wokonyi win wichow tich ma ŋono me.
47008007	Paka wimiyere i gimoro jye ma wini gine: i yeyo, i luwo, kodi niaŋ, i ketho kinen kodi i maro wan ameno bende neni win ni wimedere loyo i silwany ma poko bende.
47008008	Akikethi chik moro, to amito ŋeyo ka mar mewin obedo maradyeri; amomiyo anyutho win paka joman joketho kinen i miyo kony.
47008009	Kole wiŋeyo ŋono pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo ni kada go oido oŋaŋ, olokere jachandi ri bero mewin, ŋey go woloki win jomoŋaŋ kwoŋ chandi pere.
47008010	Me a paro m'amiyo win kwoŋ wach no: I oro morumo wiŋati witelo poko; aka ki meno kende to bende wiŋat witelo bedo gi maro ma timo ameno.
47008011	Amomiyo, medere win gine wichow tich no! Kethi win kinen i chowo tich no paka oido wiketho i timo chan mere, aka timi win ameno kodi gima wini gine.
47008012	Kole ka wini gi maro ma miyo mich, Were bino jolo mich mewin chungo kwoŋ gima winitye gine amiya, ma kiweno kwoŋ gima wingoye gine.
47008013	Wakimiti gonyo joman kareno wayimo kwoŋ win ayino byeto, to wamito thenge jye wobedi ma rom;
47008014	to paka pama onyo wimore gi lim, ber ka wikonyo joma jochando gimoro. Aka rumachien, ka wibende wichando gimoro aka jo jomore gi lim, bende jobino konyo win. Ameno aka thenge jye bino bedo ma rom.
47008015	Ato ndiiko wacho ni, “Ŋata ochoko lim madit kodoŋ gi moasa dito, aka ŋata ochoko lim manok kodoŋ gi moasa noko.”
47008016	Wafuoyo Were moketho i chuny Tito maro ma konyo win paka wakonyo win.
47008017	Go oyeyo munyo wakwayo go bino, to ki meno kende; go oido won bende oyikere amomiyo go oridho bino bongi win.
47008018	Aka wadhiro go kodi omin wan momiy dwoŋ swa i kitipa pa jomoyeyo Kristo jye ru tich pere ma fuonjo Wach Maber.
47008019	Medo kwoŋ meno, kitipa pa jomoyeyo oyero go woth gi wan ka wamedere gi tich ma ŋono me ri dwoŋ pa Kristo, gi nyutho paka wani gi maro ma miyo kony.
47008020	Wagwokere rupiri wakimiti kisigila kiŋunyaŋunya mogo bongi ji i tich mawan ma tero mich madwoŋ me.
47008021	Wamiyere timo gimotire, ki i waŋ Ruoth kende, to i waŋ ji bende.
47008022	Amomiyo, waoro omin wan no gi jo; obedo ŋata watyeko temo ndir mathoth, aka wanwaŋo ni go ni gi maro moromo ma konyo; aka go ogeno win tektek.
47008023	Ma mako kwoŋ Tito, meno jawodhan ma tiyo kodan i konyo win; aka wutimin wan man no jobedo jomikwenda ma jowok i kitipa pa jomoyeyo aka jokelo ri Kristo dwoŋ.
47008024	Amomiyo, nyuthi win jo mar mewin, kodi gima omiyo wayuma win ri jo, ŋey kitipa pa jomoyeyo jye jowoŋeyi gino.
47009001	Onwaŋo kiyenyere ni adoko andiki ri win kwoŋ dhiro kony ri ji pa Were i Yudeya.
47009002	Aŋeyo nike wiyeyo konyo, aka ayuma win ri ji ma Masedonia ka awacho ni, “Wutimere ma Yunani joyikere miyo kony wok denge i oro mecha.” Aka ketho kinen mewin oicho jomathoth kwoŋ jo bende konyo.
47009003	Onyo eno adhiro jomoyeyo me, ŋey yumirok mawan gi win i wach me wokiri wotho nono: to paka awacho, wibino yikere ma miyo kony.
47009004	Ka kameno, ka ji ma Masedonia jobin kodan to jonwaŋo ni wikiyekere, wiy wan bino kwot ma rom nedi; meno kareno wakiluw kwoŋ wichkwot mewin; rupiri waasa geno win!
47009005	Amomiyo, aparo nike ripere aori jomoyeyo me jowoteli bino ran bongi win, ŋey wiyikere kichutho nwaŋo mich ma wichiko miyo. Gikenyo bino nwaŋo ni mich no oyik chon ka atundo, aka meno bino nyutho ni wimiyo rupiri wiwegi wiyenyo, ma kiweno ni oromi aroma win timo.
47009006	Me a gima awacho: ŋata chwoyo kodhi manok bino kecho gimanyak manok; ŋata chwoyo kodhi mathoth bende bino kecho gimanyak mathoth.
47009007	Amomiyo, dhano jye ripo miyo gimoro paka won oridho timo, mongoye kiŋunyaŋunya kosa paro ni oromi aroma go timo; kole Were omaro ŋata miyo mich pere gi kisangala.
47009008	Aka Were nyalo miyo win i ŋono pere, gima kalo ma wiyenyo, ŋey ndir jye wibedi gi gimoro jye ma wiyenyo, kodi ma winyalo konyo gine tich jye mabeyo.
47009009	Ato ndiiko wacho ni, “Go ka miyo jochandi, miyo amiya jo gima bup; ato tiro pere yindira chil gi chil.”
47009010	Were ma miyo ji kodhi ma chwoyo, kodi chiemo achama, bino miyo win kodhi ma wiyenyo to miyo kodhi no dongo, ŋey gimawok i tim mewin mabeyo wonyak kweth.
47009011	Go bino miyo wiŋaŋ i kis gimoro ŋey winyal bedo jomiyo ndir jye, aka jomathoth jobino fuoyo Were ru mich mewin ma bino luwo gi bongi wan.
47009012	Kole tich ma witiyo me kikony chandi pa ji maleŋ pa Were kende, to bende miyo ji kweth jofuoyo Were.
47009013	Aka ru tich mewin motyeko nyuthere kamaler me, jomathoth jobino miyo Were dwoŋ ru chwirok mewin kwoŋ Wach Maber mapa Kristo ma witucho ni wiyeyo, kodi ru miyo kony mewin munyo wipoko lim mewin gi jo kodi joman bende.
47009014	Ameno, jobino kwayo ri win gi maro madwoŋ rupiri Were otyeko nyutho win ŋono madwoŋ.
47009015	Were wofuoy ru mich pere ma welo mere kiwachere!
47010001	An Paulo, agoyo koko ri win; an miwacho ni amwol ka anitye gi win, to abedo jamaker ri win ka ani bor gi win. Akwayo win gi mwolo kodi ŋono pa Kristo, ni
47010002	wikiri wimiyan abedi jamaker ri win ka abino; kole aŋeyo adyeri paka anyalo bedo jamaker mager gi joma joparo ni watiyo g'atoŋa ma piny.
47010003	Adyer wanitye i piny; to wakilweny paka piny lwenyo.
47010004	Ato gilweny ma waoro kobedo gilweny ma nyapiny, to obedo gilweny pa Were ma di men, ma ŋinyo woko chiel kada moger matek nedi,
47010005	gi kedho woko rageŋ jye ma pyem, kodi gimogo jye ma tiŋere malo aka temo juko ryeko pa Were, to tudo woko paro ma nyadhanodhano jye wogiki winjo Kristo.
47010006	Aka ka wityeko mwole kichutho, aka wabino yikere miyo tim jye ma chay girachula.
47010007	Onyo neni win paka gikipiny nitye. Ka moro kwanere paka dhano pa Kristo, meno ber, to go ripo ŋeyo ni wabende wabedo ji pa Kristo paka go.
47010008	Kole angoye gi wichkwot, kada atyeko yumirok ye gi men ma Ruoth omiyo wan ma geto yeyo mewin, aka ki ma reyo win woko.
47010009	Akimiti wochale pa amito bwoko win gi balwin paran.
47010010	Jomogo jowacho ni, “balwin pa Paulo ger aka di wach mapek, to ka go won nitye gi wan go nyap, aka luwo pere ongoye gimoro!”
47010011	Joma pameno ripo ŋeyo ni ongoye pokirok i gima wandiko i balwin mawan ka wangoye, kodi gima wabino timo ka wanitye kenyo gi win.
47010012	Ato wakitem kwanirok kosa pimirok kodi jomogo ma jokethere tiŋirok malo. Joma wegi jopimere aka joyumere kendigin meno joma jokiryek.
47010013	To wan, yumirok mawan kokali kew; bino bedo i kew ma tich ma Were oketho ri wan, ma rwako kir tich mawan ri win iye.
47010014	Aka wakikadhi bor gi kew mawan ka wayumere, rupiri win won ama wabino bongi win, munyo wakelo Wach Maber kwoŋ Kristo.
47010015	Amomiyo wakiyumere gi tich pa joman ayin. Kuchiel, wageno ni yeyo mewin bino dongo, aka wabino nyalo timo tich madwoŋ maloyo i dyer win.
47010016	Meno aka wanyalo tito Wach Maber i piny man ma kalo kamewin, ma wakiyumere gi tich ma joman ama jotyeko timo i ndelo pa dhano man.
47010017	Paka ndiiko wacho, “Ŋata mito yumirok, woyumere i Ruoth.”
47010018	Kole ŋata won pakere k'ama ji yeyere gine, to joma Ruoth won ama oyero ayino ama ji yeyere gi jo.
47011001	Ayenyo ni widiy chuny win kodan, kada chale pa abedo mamiŋ ye. Aka aŋeyo ni witimo ameno!
47011002	Atimo nyieko ri win paka Were timo; ato wichalo nyako maliw ma atyeko yiko ni wonywomere gi jachwo achiel kende, aka manago Kristo.
47011003	To alworo ni paro mewin bino nyiekere to wiweyo miyirok mewin maradyeri odoko ma kichutho ma winitye gine ri Kristo paka Eva otimo munyo jwogi owondo go gi twodo pere ma nyaryekoryeko.
47011004	Kole wirikin jolo dhano jye ma bino bongi win, kada ŋato fuonjo kwoŋ Yesu man, ma kiweno ma wafuonjo win kwoŋe; aka wijolo chuny kodi Wach Maber mopokere gi ma winwaŋo bongi wan.
47011005	Akipar nike ani chien kada masisiri kwoŋ jomoor mewin ma nyakare no!
47011006	Kono akifuonjere i luwo, to ki i ryeko be; aka watyeko nyutho win gime kamaler hongo jye kodi i gimoro jye.
47011007	Munyo atito ri win Wach Maber mapa Were akiyenyo kwoŋ win wodho chul moro; amwole ŋey atiŋ win malo. Meno onyo atimo marachi?
47011008	Kole onwaŋo akwalo lim pa jokristo man munyo ajolo kony pajo ma tich ri win ayino!
47011009	Aka munyo abedo gi win akijoko win ni wikonyan kada munyo onwaŋo ayenyo pesa; kole jomoyeyo ma Masedonia ama jokelo ran gimoro jye moido ayenyo. Fuodi akikelo ri win peko moro, kendo akibino timo ameno kir yu waŋe!
47011010	G'adyeri pa Kristo i an, achiko ni yumirok paran me ongoye ŋata bino juko kamoro jye i Yunani.
47011011	Raŋo ma awacho ama? Obedo rupiri akimaro wini? Kole Were oŋeyo ni amaro win.
47011012	Abino medere gi timo gima atimo, ŋey ageŋ “jomoor” man no bedo kodi atoŋa ma yumirok gi wacho ni bende jotiyo paka wan.
47011013	Jono jokobedo jomoor maradyeri; jobedo jomoor matwodo, ma jokethere ni jo bende jomoor pa Kristo.
47011014	Aka meno ki gidhyer, rupiri kir Sitan bende twodo to lokere paka malaika ma lero!
47011015	Amomiyo kobedo gidhyer ka jotich pere bende jotwodo ni jobedo jotich ma lero. Rumachien jobino limo gima ripo gi jo tirtir ru gikipiny ma jotimo.
47011016	Adoko amedo wacho: moro wokiri wopari nike amiŋ. To ka wiparo ameno, ere jolan win to kada paka ŋatamiŋ, aka ŋey ayumereye nyaka mathin.
47011017	Ato wach ma aluwo me kobedo wach ma wok bongi Ruoth; to me onyo aluwo paka ŋatamiŋ.
47011018	Paka nitye jomathoth ma joyumere gi nyaka gikipiny ma nyapiny, abende onyo aletimo ameno.
47011019	Ato wiryek ri win, amomiyo wiyeyere kir gi jomamiŋ!
47011020	Aka wiyeyere gi moro jye ma bino miyo win or ma nger jye, kosa loko win ŋechin, kosa chiemo kwoŋ win, kosa limo ŋaŋo i nyapo mewin, kosa chayo win, kosa goyo lembi win adhoŋ.
47011021	Kole wiyan kwot ka apoyo ni oido wanyap swa ma wakinyalo timo ameno. To ka moro timo miseni to yumere gi gimoro, ka aluwo paka ŋatamiŋ, abende onyo aletimo miseni ma yumirok amanago.
47011022	Jobedo Joyudaya? Kole an bende! Jobedo Joisrael? Kole an bende! Jobedo nyikway Ibrayimu? Kole an bende!
47011023	Jobedo jotich pa Kristo? Ka aluwo pa janeko, abedo jatich maber loyo jo! Atyeko tiyo matek loyo jo, atyeko bedo i twech ndir mathoth loyo jo, otyek chwadan ndir madit loyo jo, aka atyeko bedo chiegin gi tho ndir mathoth loyo.
47011024	Dibich Joyudaya jochwadan adasa pyero adek g'abuŋwen;
47011025	Joroma jogoyan gi ludhe didek, aka ogoyan gi telin dichiel; yee otyeko bare ran i pi didek, aka dichiel achowo sawa pyero aryo g'aŋwen i dyer wakawaka munyo lekaleka kodan.
47011026	I woth paran momore aboth ri mikula ma jwombe, kodi jomach; aboth kwoŋ ji ma piny paran won, kodi ri Jopath; aboth i tindi, kodi i thim; aboth kwoŋ nam madongo, kodi kwoŋ jomoyeyo matwodo.
47011027	Atyeko tich gi olo; ndir mathoth akibil nindo; abedo gi kech kodi riyo; ndir mathoth akichiem, odoko koyo goyan kinyoro.
47011028	Aka, m'akitucho gikipiny man, ndir jye abedo i rembo ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo jye.
47011029	Ka dhano nyap, abende abedo manyap gine; ka moro opodho i gimarach, kole awinjo gi rem.
47011030	Ka ripere ayumere, abino yumirok kodi gikipiny ma nyutho paka anyap.
47011031	Were kodi Baa Ruodhiwan Yesu, moripo g'apaka chil gi chil, oŋeyo nike akitwodi!
47011032	Munyo fuodi oido anitye Damasiko, gavana ma ndir pa Kere Areto oketho jokur i waŋkach ma tindi makan.
47011033	To owodhan munyo ichwayan piny i adita, gi i hoŋ moro i kor ot, ameno t'abudho go.
47012001	Aripo medo yumirok kada kikel bero moro. Onyo pama abino luwo kwoŋ chal ma menyere kodi menyirok ma Wach ma Ruoth omiyan.
47012002	Aŋeyo jakristo moro ma oro apar gaŋwen mokadho oyudhi go titero i polo maradek malo (akiŋeyo kuya gino otimere i del, kosa go oneno chal momenyere rigo; Were won amoŋeyo).
47012003	Weyi adok'amedi wacho: aŋeyo ni ŋato oyudhi titero i polo (to akuya ni gino otimere i del, kosa obedo chal momenyere ri go; Were won amoŋeyo).
47012004	Oter go i kabedo ma di syem i polo, aka kenyo go owinj'iye gikipiny makiwachere; gikipiny ma dhok dhano kinyal luwo.
47012005	Amomiyo, abino yumere kapa ŋato; to akibino yumirok kwoŋan an won, kwanyo woko gikipiny ma nyutho paka anyap.
47012006	Kada bedi amito yumirok, jye d'akibedo ŋatamiŋ rupiri d'aluwo giradyeri. To akoyumere, rupiri akimiti moro wobedi gi paro mamalo kwoŋan ma kalo gima go otyeko nenan atimo kosa owinjo munyo awacho.
47012007	To ma jukan ŋey akir akwoti gi pakirok ru menyirok ma urere m'aneno, okethi kwoŋan gima chalo okudho, ma tiyo paka jamikwenda pa Sitan ma wochandan aka wojukan akir abedi gi kwoto.
47012008	Didek akwayo Ruoth i wach me, ni wokwanyi woko gino.
47012009	To go odwokan ni, “Ŋono paran romin; kole men paran asere kama nyapo ni iye.” Amomiyo, asangala swa pakirok gi nyapo paran, ŋey men pa Kristo wobedi kwoŋan.
47012010	Aŋiyo ran gi nyapo, yet, chandirok, lweny pa ji kodi teko ru tich ri Kristo. Kole ka angoye gi men meno aka nyaka atek.
47012011	Onyo alokere paka ŋatamiŋ, aka wiŋati wimiyan abedo ameno. Kole wiŋati onwaŋo wiripo fuoyan, rupiri kada akibedo gimoro, to aki ni chien loyo “jomoor” mewin ma nyakare no.
47012012	Kole gikipiny ma nyutho ni dhano obedo jamoor maradyeri otim gi diyo chuny moasere i dyer win: ranyuth, giraura kodi tich madongo ma men.
47012013	Aŋo ma wikeŋ loyo kitipa pa jomoyeyo man, kwanyo woko nike akikwayo win kony. Mondo chwakan win kwoŋ kibenga no!
47012014	Me onyo maradek m'ayikere bino lyewo win, aka akibino mito gimoro kwoŋ win. Ayenyo win ayino, to ki gikipiny mewin. Kuchiel nyithindho mathindho k'ama jolimo gikipiny ri jonywol, to jonywol ama jolimo gikipiny ri nyithindho pajo mathindho.
47012015	Abino kisangala oro gimoro jye ma ani gine, ma kada an won gipi orirok ma konyo win. Ka amaro win tektek ameno, onyo wiŋati winomaran mathin ma kiromi?
47012016	Amomiyo, wibino yeyo ni, oido akibedo byeto ri win. To wiwacho ni abedo jaryeko aka achiiko win gi bwo ma twodo.
47012017	Nitye gima akwanyo kwoŋ win i jomikwenda m'adhiro ri wini?
47012018	Adhiro Tito ni wobin, aka adhiro go kir gi omin wan man ni wowothi gine. Kosa nitye gima Tito okwanyo kwoŋ wini? Nyutho ni wakitiyo g'atoŋa achieli? Kosa wakitimo chan achieli?
47012019	Oido wiparo ni hongo jye watemo gwoko thenge mawan i waŋ wini? Waluwo paka Kristo mito ni waluw i waŋ Were, aka gimoro jye ma watimo jowotan, kole watimo ma konyo win!
47012020	Alworo ni kono kani atundo kenyo anyalo nwaŋo ni wipokere kodi paka oido d'ayenyo wibedi, kosa kareno aŋata apokere kodi paka di wiyenyo abedi. Alworo ni abino nwaŋo widhaw, kosa witimo nyieko, wioro nge kosa witimo mima, winyieko nyingi jowoti win kodi luwirok kichar, pakirok kodi nywowirok.
47012021	Alworo nike ruman ka abino, Were paran bino miyan anwaŋo wichkwot t'aywak ru jomathoth ma jotimo recho i ndir mokadho aka fuodi jokoŋuto timo gikipiny makoch, chot kodi timo gi wichkwot.
47013001	Me onyo maradek ma abino lyewo win. “Jokony ripo bedo aryo kosa adek ma joridho kis banja mokel kwoŋ nyatoro.”
47013002	Ndir cha aniaŋo win kwoŋ jomotimo gimarecho munyo alyewo win mararyo; to adoko awacho kendo pama ma angoye bongi win ni: ka abino kendo, akibino weyo ŋatotimo recho chon kosa manyien ma kolimo girachula.
47013003	Ato wimito ŋeyo adyeri ka Kristo luwo i an. Go kinyap ka tiyere gi win; kuchiel go nyutho men pere i dyer win.
47013004	Kole ogur go wi musalaba i nyapo, to gi men pa Were go odoko kwo. Wabende wanyap i go; to gi men pa Were wabino kwo ka watiyere gi win.
47013005	Kaŋasa win kwo mewin winen ka fuodi wini gi yeyo. Wikuya ni Kristo Yesu nitye i wini? Kono kosa timo ameno odhyero win kichutho.
47013006	Ageno ni wibino ŋeyo ni kikaŋasa kwo mawan kodhyero wan.
47013007	Wakwayo Were ni di wikitim recho, ki ma nyutho ni kono wanyalo gimoro jye, to ni witim gimotire, kada wanochal jomopodho.
47013008	Ato wakinyal timo gima pyemo kodi adyeri pa Were, rupiri watiyo ri adyeri no.
47013009	Wasangala kada wabedo manyap tekin winitye gi men. Amomiyo, wakwayo nike wibende widongi i leŋo.
47013010	Andiko gime munyo angoye bongi win; atimo ameno ni ka atundo bongi win akir ater win gi mbaka, kareno aoro men ma Ruoth omiyan ma dongo win, ma kiweno ma reyo win woko.
47013011	Onyo jowotan, kutho win! Tiri win kwo mewin; winji win gima awacho; yeyere win wiwegi, bedi win i syem; aka Were ma jamar kodi syem bino bedo gi win.
47013012	Mothere win akor gi leŋo.
47013013	Ji pa Were jye jodhiro ri win moth.
47013014	Ŋono pa Ruoth Yesu Kristo, mar pa Were, kodi riwirok pa Chuny Maleŋ wobedi kodi wijojye.
48001001	An Paulo jamoor, ma lwoŋo pere kowok bongi dhano kosa kwoŋ dhano, to bongi Yesu Kristo kodi Were Baa wan, mochierino go kwoŋ jomotho.
48001002	Jomoyeyo jye ma jo ni ka joriwere kodan i dhiro moth ri kweth pa jokristo ma Galasya:
48001003	Weyi Were Baa wan kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo womiyi win ŋono gi syem.
48001004	Kristo omiyo kwo pere ru gimarecho mawan, ŋey wobothi wan kwoŋ ndir marach ma pama, i mito pa Were mawan ma Baa wan.
48001005	Dwoŋ wobedi ri Were chil gi chil! Ameno.
48001006	Adhyer kwoŋ win! I hongo machiek won onyo wijala ŋata olwoŋo win i ŋono pa Kristo, aka onyo wiluwo wach man ayino,
48001007	ma kobedo kir “Wach Maber!” Nenere paka nitye jomogo ma joruwo paro mewin aka jotemo wiro woko Wach Maber pa Kristo.
48001008	To kada obedi wan kosa malaika mowok i polo ama ofuonji win wach man mopokere kodi ma watyeko fuonjo win, weyi wothumi ri jo banja ma kidho i mach makitho!
48001009	Watyeko wacho gime chon, aka onyo odoko awacho kendo: ka nitye nyatoro ma fuonjo win wach man mopokere kodi ma wityeko jolo, weyi wothumi ri go banja ma kidho i mach makitho!
48001010	Onyo wiparo ni atemo dwaro fuoy pa ji, kosa apa Were ayin? Kosa wiparo ni atemo kisangala ji? Bedi fuodi atemo kisangala ji d'akibedo jatich pa Kristo be.
48001011	Amito ni wiŋey gime, wutimera: Wach Maber ma afuonjo dhano ama kochwogo.
48001012	Akinwaŋo wach me kwoŋ dhano, dhano ama kofuonjan; to, Yesu Kristo won ama onyuthan.
48001013	Kole wityeko winjo paka kwo paran oido nitye munyo oido amoko i din ma Nyayudaya, paka alwenyo gi kitipa pa jomoyeyo Were mongoye wor, aka atemo i royo jye reyo woko jo.
48001014	Onwaŋo atelo Joyudaya mathoth ma luse paran i mako din ma Nyayudaya. Aka onwaŋo aloyo jo gi ridho kula pa kwarere mawan.
48001015	To Were won, gi ŋono pere ama oyeran denge ma fuodi konywolan, to lwoŋan tich ri go.
48001016	Aka munyo oridho nyuthan Wuode, ŋey afuonji Jopath Wach Maber kwoŋ go, akikidho bongi nyatoro rango ryeko,
48001017	odoko akikidho Yerusalem neno joma jotelo bedo ran jomoor. To, akidho Arabya mayot, aka nyaka adwoko Damasiko.
48001018	Munyo oro okadho adek, aka nyaka akidho Yerusalem wendo ri Petro, to achowo bonge ndelo apar g'abich.
48001019	Akineno jomoor man kwanyo woko Yakobo, omin Ruoth.
48001020	Aridho ri win i waŋ Were ni gima andiko ri win me kobedo twodo.
48001021	Rumachien akidho i adech ma Sirya kodi Silisya.
48001022	I hongo no jye kitipa pa jomoyeyo i Yudeya oido fuodi jokuya an odocho.
48001023	Oido jotyeko winjo nyaka gima joman jowacho kende ni, “Jal ma yado lwenyo gi wan onyo pama fuonjo yeyo ma go oido otemo reyo woko!”
48001024	Gikenyo jopako Were ru wach ma jowinjo kwoŋan.
48002001	Munyo oro apar g'aŋwen okadho, agik Yerusalem kodi Barunaba, kareno akwanyo Tito bende awotho gine.
48002002	Akidho rupiri Were oido onyuthan nike akidhi; aka anyutho jotel Wach Maber moido atito ri Jopath. To atimo gino nyaliŋliŋ gi lworo munyo akimito nike tich paran i hongo mokadho kosa ma pama wotho nono.
48002003	Odoko nyawotan Tito, kada oido obedo Jayunani, koromi go thumirok.
48002004	Ato jomogo, ma jorendere nike jobedo jomoyeyo jowot wan, jodonjo i dyer wan, aka oido jomito ni wothumi go. Jome oido jolwi paka jopendo ka jomito ŋeyo ni syem aŋo ma wani gine i Kristo Yesu. Jono oido jomito loko wan ŋechin.
48002005	Wakiyeyo ri jo kada masisiri, ŋey adyeri ma Wach Maber wodoŋi ri win.
48002006	To joma oido itero jo paka jotel (awacho ama rupiri kikel ran pokirok moro gima onwaŋo jobedo; kole Were kinen dhano chungo kwoŋ chal mawoko), jokomedo wach moro jye manyien kwoŋ mikwenda paran.
48002007	Kuchiel, joneno ni Were oido omiyan tich ma fuonjo Jopath Wach Maber paka oido omiyo Petro tich ma fuonjo Joyudaya.
48002008	Ato Were moido tiyo i Petro paka jamoor pa Joyudaya, bende ama oido tiyo i an paka jamoor pa Jopath.
48002009	Yakobo, Petro, kodi Yohana, ma jobedo jotel, joyeyo riwo chingi jo gi wan kodi Barunaba munyo joniaŋ kwoŋ mich ma Were omiyan i ŋono pere. Wayeyere ni wan watiyi i dyer Jopath aka jo jowotiyi i dyer Joyudaya.
48002010	Joyenyo kwoŋ wan gimoro achiel kende ni wapoyi jochandi, aka meno a gima oido abende ayiko timo.
48002011	Munyo Petro obino Antyok, apyemo gine i dyer ji, rupiri banja oido loyo go kamaler.
48002012	Munyo fuodi jomogo ma Yakobo odhiro jokotundo kenyo, Petro onwaŋo chiemo kodi Jopath ma joyeyo. To munyo jome jotundo, to go dhire gichien munyo kwero chiemo gi jono rupiri go oido lworo joma joyenyo ni Jopath bende jowothumere.
48002013	Gino omiyo Joyudaya man ma joyeyo bende jochako rendirok paka Petro; ma kir Barunaba bende oido tim ago ywayo go.
48002014	Munyo aneno ni jokiwothi i yo ma ripo kodi adyeri ma Wach Maber, awacho ri Petro i waŋ jojye ni, “Ka in Jayudaya, itero kite pa Japath, ma kiweno apa Jayudaya, inyalo nedi temo romo Jopath nike jowoteri kite pa Joyudaya?”
48002015	Adyer wabedo Joyudaya i nywolirok mawan, ma kiweno Jopath ma jotimi recho.
48002016	To waŋeyo ni dhano iketho i tiro gi Were i yeyo kwoŋ Yesu Kristo, ma kiweno i timo gima Chik wacho. Kole ongoye ŋata iketho i tiro gi Were i timo gima Chik wacho.
48002017	Onyo ka watemo ni wokethi wan i tiro gi Were, to nwaŋere nike fuodi wabedo jorecho paka Jopath, meno nyutho ni kosa Kristo tiyo ma konyo recho? Kameno be!
48002018	Ka achako kendo gero gima atyeko kedho woko, meno nyutho ni aturo Chik.
48002019	Ato atyeko tho kwoŋ luwo Chik, aka Chik won ama onekan, ŋey akwo ri Were. Otyek guran wi musalaba gi Kristo;
48002020	pama onyo aŋata akikwo, to Kristo ama kwo i an. Aka kwo ma pama ani gine, nitye i yeyo Wuodi Were m'omaran to miyo kwo pere ran.
48002021	Akikwer ŋono pa Were, rupiri ka dhano okethi i tiro gi Were ru luwo Chik, nyutho ni Kristo kere otho nono.
48003001	Win Jogalasya mamiŋ! Ŋata omyeno win? Kole otiti i waŋ win won paka Yesu Kristo ogur wi musalaba!
48003002	Amito wiwachi ran nyaka gimoro achiel kende: wilimo Chuny Maleŋ pa Were i timo gima Chik wacho, kosa i winjo gi yeyo gima wiwinjo?
48003003	Winyalo nedi bedo mamiŋ ameno! Wityeko chako gi Chuny, to odoko wiyenyo chowo gi men ma nyadel ayin nedi?
48003004	Chandirok ma wityeko nwaŋo jye onyo otho nono? Adyer oido ongoye gima di winwaŋo ye?
48003005	Were miyo win Chuny Maleŋ pere aka timo giraura i dyer win rupiri witimo gima Chik wacho, kosa rupiri wiyeyo Wach Maber ma wiwinjo?
48003006	Kole ndiiko luwo kwoŋ Ibrayimu ni, “Go oyeyo Were, aka yeyo pere amomiyo Were ojolo go paka ŋatotire.”
48003007	Amomiyo, wiripo ŋeyo ni joma jonitye gi yeyo, meno a nyikway Ibrayimu maradyeri.
48003008	Aka ndiiko oneno chon ni Were d'oketho Jopath i tiro kodi go i yeyo. Amomiyo, ndiiko onyutho Ibrayimu Wach Maber chon kichutho ni, “Were bino miyo ji jye silwany kwoŋin;”
48003009	amomiyo ji jye ma joyeyo jolimo silwany paka chango Ibrayimu olimo.
48003010	Aka dhano jye ma chwire i winjo Chik meno ni gi kwoŋ ayino i kwo pere, rupiri ndiiko wacho ni, “Ŋata ndir jye kiwinji aka kitimi gimoro jye mondik i kitawo ma Chik meno ŋato okwoŋ!”
48003011	Obedo adyeri ni ongoye ŋata nwaŋo tiro i waŋ Were chungo kwoŋ Chik, rupiri ndiiko wacho ni, “Jomotire jobino kwo chungo kwoŋ yeyo.”
48003012	To Chik kichungi kwoŋ yeyo; kuchiel wacho ni, “Ŋata timo gimoro jye ma chik wacho bino kwo gine.”
48003013	Munyo Kristo olokere ŋata okwoŋ kawaŋ wan, ogonyo wan woko kwoŋ kwoŋ ma Chik kelo, rupiri ndiiko wacho ni, “Nyatoro jye molyer wi yath meno ŋata okwoŋ.”
48003014	Meno, aka ŋey womiy Jopath silwany ma Were ochiko Ibrayimu i Yesu Kristo, aka wanyal jolo Chuny ma Were ochiko chungo kwoŋ yeyo.
48003015	Wutimera, weyi akeli ranen kwoŋ gima kis ndelo: ka ji aryo joyeyere kwoŋ wach moro to jotimo chikirok i Ndiiko, ngoye ŋata nyalo turo chikirok no kosa medo kwoŋe gimoro.
48003016	I yo achiel, Were otimo chikirok pere kodi Ibrayimu gi nyakware. Ndiiko kiwachi ni gi “nyikwaye,” ma nyutho ni ji mathoth, to wacho ni, “gi nyakwarin,” dwoŋ mere ni ŋatachiel, mobedo Yesu Kristo.
48003017	Dwoŋ gima awacho ame: Chik, mobino rumachien ma oro miya aŋwen gi pyero adek, kinyal turo chikirok to reyo woko gima Were ochiko.
48003018	Kole ka lunjo lim bedo ru Chik motyek ketho meno nyutho ni gino kowok i chikirok moro. To Were i ŋono pere omiyo Ibrayimu gima go wolunji rupiri oido otimo gine chikirok.
48003019	To raŋo m'owodhi Chik? Owodhi Chik ru tim pa ji marecho, aka omiti ni wobedi chuka bino pa nyakwar Ibrayimu, m'otim gine chikirok. Jomalaika jokonyo i kelo Chik no kareno dhano ama obedo jathek ma chungo i dyer ji gi Were.
48003020	Aka jathek tiyo i dyer ji ma kalo achiel; Were obedo ŋatachiel ma nitye i thenge achiel.
48003021	Meno nyutho ni Chik pyemo gi chikirok pa Were? Be, kameno. Ato bedi wodhi chik ma d'okelo kwo ri ji, dwoŋ mere ni dhano d'onyal ketho i tiro gi Were chungo kwoŋ chik nago.
48003022	To ndiiko wacho ni gimoro jye ma piny nitye i men pa gimarach, to joma joyeyo jolenyalo limo mich m'ochik chungo kwoŋ yeyo Yesu Kristo.
48003023	Ma fuodi ndir ma yeyo kotundo, Chik onwaŋo oketho wajojye i twech, chuka wonyuthi yeyo kamaler.
48003024	Amomiyo Chik ama oido kuro wan paka jafuonji ma tiro wan nyuka Kristo wobin, ŋey wokethi wan i tiro gi Were i yeyo.
48003025	Paka ndir pa yeyo onyo otyeko tundo, jafuonji ma tiro ji no onyo ama kikur wan kendo.
48003026	Kole i Kristo Yesu wijojye onyo wibedo nyithindho pa Were chungo kwoŋ yeyo mewin.
48003027	Ato wijojye ma wilimo batisimo i Kristo, onyo wiruko kwoŋ win Kristo won gipi.
48003028	Amomiyo pokirok ongoye kwoŋ Joyudaya kodi Jopath, kwoŋ ŋechin kodi joma ni syem, kwoŋ chwo gi mon: wijojye wibedo achiel i Kristo Yesu.
48003029	Ka wibedo apa Kristo, kole meno wibedo nyikway Ibrayimu, aka wibedo musikin ma jobino lunjo lim ma Were ochiko.
48004001	Gima awacho ame: nyathi majachwo ma kidho lunjo lim pa bamere itero paka ŋecha ka fuodi go thin, kada go won oido a won gimoro jye.
48004002	I ketho rigo joma kuro go aka jotimo tich pere nyuka hongo ma bamere ochano tund'iye.
48004003	Meno apaka wabende munyo fuodi wathindho i gikipiny ma nyachuny onwaŋo wabedo ŋechin kareno chuny ma piny me amoido dhumo wan.
48004004	To munyo hongo motire otundo, Were ooro Wuode won, ma dhako bende ama onywolo, aka obedo i Chik pa Joyudaya,
48004005	ŋey wogonyi joma oido jonitye i men pa Chik, aka ŋey nyaka walokere nyithindho pa Were akela.
48004006	Paka wabedo wote, Were ooro Chuny Maleŋ pa Wuode i chuny wan, Chuny ma koko ni, “Aba, nyaka ni Baba.”
48004007	Amomiyo, onyo ikibedo ŋecha, to wuode, aka paka ibedo wuode, ibino lunjo lim moro jye ma Were okano ri wote paka musikin.
48004008	I ndir mokadho oido wikiŋeyo Were, amomiyo oido wibedo ŋechin pa gikipiny ma jokobedo were motire.
48004009	To paka pama onyo wityeko ŋeyo Were; kosa weyi awachi ni paka pama onyo Were oŋeyo win, winyalo nedi gik kendo bongi chuny manyap ma sisiri no? Raŋo ma wimito lokirok ŋechin pajo kendo?
48004010	Wimiyo gikipiny mogo dwoŋ paka: ndelo megi, dwe, ndir, kodi oro!
48004011	Kole chunyan raman, ipoyo ameno tich paran jye ri win onyo otho nono.
48004012	Akwayo win, wutimera, bedi win paka an, rupiri atyeko bedo paka win. Fuodi wikitimo ran racho moro.
48004013	Wipoyo ni gimomiyo afuonjo win Wach Maber kachako obedo two.
48004014	To wikichayan kosa kweran, kada two paran no oido obedo ri win tem. Kuchiel wijolan paka di wijolo malaika pa Were, kosa Kristo Yesu!
48004015	To aŋo m'onyo odoko otimere mato onwaŋo wisangala? Aka aridho ni onwaŋo winyalo kir golo woko waŋ win won, bedi nyalere, to wimiyan!
48004016	Onyo pama atyeko lokere jakwor mewin ru wacho ri win adyeri?
48004017	Jono jonyutho win mar g'atoŋa ma kiber. Gima jomito a nyaka pokan gi win, ŋey wibedi gi paro kwoŋ jo ayino, paka bende jo ni gi paro kwoŋ win.
48004018	Onyo, ber bedo gi paro kwoŋ dhano kodi atoŋa maber, aka meno apaka ripo bedo ndir jye, to ki nyaka ka anitye gi win kende.
48004019	Nyithindho paran ma amaro swa, kendo ma awinjo gi jo malith pa dhako ma nyathi ramo chuka kiti Kristo wowoki kwoŋ win!
48004020	Ani g'awanya adyeri ma bedo gi win kanyachiel, ni ipoyo d'awiroye paro m'ani gine kwoŋ win, rupiri arembo swa ri win!
48004021	Weyi apenji win ma fuodi witweyere wimito luwo Chik: kosa wikiwinji gima Chik wacho?
48004022	Kole ondik ni Ibrayimu oido nitye gi wote aryo, achiel m'olimo gi dhako mobedo ŋecha kodi man m'olimo gi dhako mani syem.
48004023	Wuodi pa dhako mobedo ŋecha onywol i yo ma kis ndelo, to wuodi pa dhako mani syem onywol i chikirok pa Were.
48004024	Weyi water gime paka agecha ri wan: mon aryo me jobedo paka chikirok aryo, achiel m'owok wi got Sinai, nyithindho pere jobedo ŋechin.
48004025	Haga chungo kapa got Sinai i Arabya; aka go obedo giranena kapa Yerusalem ma pama, mobedo ŋecha kanyachiel gi nyithindho pere.
48004026	To Yerusalem ma nyapolo nitye i syem, aka go a yoki wan.
48004027	Ato ndiiko wacho ni, “Sangala, in dhako ma migumba ma nyuka chiene oido fuodi kolimo nyithindho! Galagasa gi kisangala, in ma fuodi oido ikiwinjoye litho manywol! Kole dhako moido ojala onyo bino bedo gi nyithindho madit loyo dhako ma chwore koweyo.”
48004028	Onyo win, wutimera, wibedo nyithindho pa Were ma chikirok pere, paka chango Isaka.
48004029	Paka i hongo no nyathi m'onywol i yo ma kis ndelo olwenyo kodi nyathi m'onywol gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ; apaka bende nitye pama.
48004030	To ndiiko wacho nedi? Wacho ni, “Ryemi woko dhako mobedo ŋecha kir gi wuode, rupiri wuodi pa dhako mobedo ŋecha kolunji lim pa bamere kanyachiel gi wuodi pa dhako mani syem.”
48004031	Amomiyo, wutimera, wakibedo nyithindho pa dhako mobedo ŋecha, to apa dhako mani syem ayin.
48005001	Kristo otyeko gonyo wan i twech to miyo wan syem! Ri ameno chungi win, paka ji mani syem, aka wikiri wiyey lokirok ŋechin kendo.
48005002	Winji win! An Paulo awacho ri win gime: ka wiyeyo thumirok, meno nyutho ni Kristo ongoye gi kony moro ri win.
48005003	Amito medo wacho kendo ri dhano jye ma yenyo ni wothum ni go onyo ripo luwo Chik jye.
48005004	Win ma wiyenyo nike wokethi win i tiro gi Were chungo kwoŋ Chik kole wityeko pokirok kodi Kristo; aka wityeko kir podho gi eye kwoŋ ŋono pa Were.
48005005	To wani gi geno ni Were bino ketho wan i tiro gi go, gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ pa Were matiyo i yeyo mawan; aka meno a gima wakuro.
48005006	Kole i Kristo Yesu, thumirok kosa weyo ma kothumere kikel pokirok moro; gimadwoŋ obedo yeyo ayino ma nyuthere i mar.
48005007	Kole onwaŋo wiŋwecho maber, to ŋa m'odoko ochiero win winjo adyeri? Ŋato odwoŋo win nedi?
48005008	Kiti adwoŋa no kiwoki kwoŋ ŋata olwoŋo win be.
48005009	Kole “Nyaka thow manok won ama miyo moko gipi kwot” paka iwacho.
48005010	Aka fuodi aridho ni wikobedi gi paro man mopokere, to ŋato, kada bedi ŋa, ma ruwo wiy win no, bino wodho chul mere.
48005011	To an, wutimera, kere raŋo ma fuodi ilwenyo kodan k'inen adyeri fuodi afuonjo ni thumirok yenyere? Kole meno nyutho ni fuonji paran kwoŋ musalaba pa Kristo di kikwiny jomogo be.
48005012	Ayenyo ni joma jokwinyo win no jowomedere gine; weyi jowomedere gi thumirok.
48005013	To win, wutimera, olwoŋ win ni wibedi i syem. To syem me wokiri wolokere ri win gigoŋirok ma yeyo awanya ma del dhumo win. Kuchiel, konyere win chungo kwoŋ mar mewin.
48005014	Kole Chik gi bee olok machiek i or achiel ni, “Mari nyawotin paka iwon imarere.”
48005015	To ka chale pa wikayere aka wichamere p'ogwange meno kere kure win; ameno winyalo reyere woko kichutho.
48005016	Me a gima awacho: wothi win i Chuny aka wikotim gima awanya pa del mito.
48005017	Kole awanya pa del lwenyo gi Chuny aka Chuny bende lwenyo kodi awanya pa del; jaryo me jobedo jokwor, aka gino miyo ikinyal timo gima iyenyo ni itim.
48005018	Ka Chuny ama telin, meno nyutho ni ikitudere i luwo Chik.
48005019	Gima kula pa del timo neno kamaler: neno i kidakana, koch, kodi i tim ma kiripi;
48005020	i lamo chal makichar kodi yido, bedo i kwor gi dhano, laro dwoŋ, timo nyieko, mako ŋonge, gwondo, dhawirok, tyakirok,
48005021	kigomba gipa dhano, mero, timo woro, kodi timo gikipiny man ma chale gi me. Anyutho win kichutho paka atyeko timo chon, joma timo gikipiny me jokodonji i Ker pa Were.
48005022	To Chuny Maleŋ nyak gikipiny me: mar, kisangala, syem, diyo chuny, wor, bero, genirok,
48005023	mwolo, kodi kuro chuny. Ongoye chik ma pyemo gi gikipiny paka me!
48005024	Aka joma jobedo apa Kristo Yesu jotyeko neko woko kula pajo ma del, kodi ichirok mere kodi awanya mere.
48005025	Ka wakwo gi men pa Chuny, meno bende ber wawothi i kwo ma nyachuny.
48005026	Wakiri wabedi ma waparo ni wawegi wachowere, kosa watim kisinye kosa watim nyieko gi joman.
48006001	Wutimera, komaki moro munyo timo recho moro, win ma wimaro gima nyachuny witir go; to witimi ameno gi mwolo. Aka wiwegi gwokere win, ŋey wikiri widonji i karatem bende.
48006002	Konyere win gi tiŋo byeto ma jowoti win ni gine, rupiri ameno aka wibino mako chik pa Kristo.
48006003	Ka moro paro ni go gimoro, mato go ongoye gi dwoŋ moro meno won miŋere.
48006004	Dhano jye won ripo kikaŋasa kite. Ka ber, won nyalo yumirok gi i chunye, ma kopima kodi gima ŋat man otyeko timo.
48006005	Kole dhano jye won ripo tiŋo byeto ma go ni gine.
48006006	Ŋat'ifuonjo wach pa Were ripo pokoye gi jafuonji pere gikipiny mabeyo jye ma go ni gine.
48006007	Wikiri wiwondere, ongoye ŋata nyalo miŋo Were. Dhano jye kecho gima go ochwoyo.
48006008	Ka go ochwoyo i ndelo marawanya pa del pere, go bino kecho kenyo tho; ka go ochwoyo i ndelo ma Chuny, wok kwoŋ Chuny Maleŋ go bino kecho kwo makirum.
48006009	Amomiyo, wakiri waol gi timo bero; kole ka wakijok timo ameno, ndir bino tundo ma wabino kech'iye gimanyak.
48006010	Amomiyo, hongo jye ma wanitye gi thwolo waripo timo bero ri dhano jye, to tektek ri joma jobedo jowoti wan i yeyo.
48006011	Neni win nyikuta madongo m'andiko gine ri win gi chingan won!
48006012	Joma jotemo romo win nike withumere meno joma jomito kwoto gi pakirok kwoŋ gikipiny ma nyadel. Ato jotimo ameno nike aka wokiri wolwenyi gi jo ru yeyo musalaba pa Kristo.
48006013	Kole kada jomothumere wegi bende jokimaki Chik! Onyo jomito withumere aka ŋey jowoyumere nike wiyeyo tim ma nyadel no.
48006014	To an, abino yumirok gi musalaba pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo kende; kole gi musalaba pere aneno pa piny otho ran aka abende atho ri awanya ma piny.
48006015	Ki wach moro kosa dhano othumere kosa be. Kole gima dwoŋ a lokirok chwech manyien ayin.
48006016	Syem gi wor wobedi ri joma jobino mako tyendi wach me i kwo pajo, kodi ri ji pa Were jye!
48006017	Machowe: moro wokiri odoko wojokan; kole waŋpoyo ma anitye gine kwoŋan ka nyutho nike abedo ŋecha pa Yesu.
48006018	Weyi ŋono pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo wobedi kodi win, wutimera. Ameno.
49001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo jamoor pa Kristo Yesu gi mito pa Were, ri ji pa Were ma jonitye Efeso, jomoyeyo Kristo Yesu aka jogenere i kwo pajo,
49001002	Ŋono gi syem mowok bongi Were Bawan kodi Ruoth mawan Yesu Kristo wobedi gi win.
49001003	Were wofuoy, Baa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo, momiyo wan silwany gi mich jye ma chuny mawok i polo i Kristo.
49001004	Chon ma piny fuodi kochwey, go oyero wan bedo apere i Kristo, ni wabedi maleŋ, mongoye apuse ruwaŋ go.
49001005	Mar pa Were, omiyo go oridho chon ni walokere nyithindho pere i Yesu Kristo. Me obedo fuoyo pere kodi atoŋa pere.
49001006	Meno aka wopaki dwoŋ ma ŋono pere, mich pere ri wan, ma go omiyo wan ma nono i Wuode ma migos.
49001007	Kole remo pa Kristo okelo ri wan syem, kodi chwak ma gimarecho mawan, ru ŋono pa Were moasere
49001008	ma go okonjo ri wan. Gi ryeko jye kodi niaŋ,
49001009	Were otimo gima onwaŋo otyeko chano, to miyo wan ŋeyo chan pere ma nyaliŋliŋ ma go onwaŋo otyeko yiko timo i Kristo.
49001010	Chan pa Were ma go bino chowo timo ka ndir otundo, ma kelo chwech jye kanyachiel, gi gimoro jye mani polo kodi mani piny, kareno Kristo a jatel mere.
49001011	Kole gimoro jye timere gi chan pa Were kodi paro pere; aka Were oyero wan bende bedo ji pere i chan pere ma go oridho wok i chakirok.
49001012	Meno aka nyaka wan ma wapen geno Kristo, wanomiyi dwoŋ pa Were wopak.
49001013	Wibende munyo wiwinjo wach maradyeri, Wach Maber mokelo ri win both, wiyeyo Kristo aka Were oketho ranyuth pere kwoŋ win, munyo miyo win Chuny Maleŋ ma go won oido otyeko chiko win.
49001014	Chuny Maleŋ obedo ma ridho ni wabino limo gima Were otyeko chiko wan, chuka ji pere jolim both, ŋey dwoŋ pere wofuoy.
49001015	Amomiyo chuka awinji kwoŋ yeyo mewin i Ruoth Yesu kodi paka wimaro ji pa Were jye,
49001016	akikeŋ ketho Were walwa ri win gi poyo win i kwayo paran,
49001017	aka akwayo Were pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo, Bawan mani gi dwoŋ, ni womiyi win Chuny Maleŋ, ma bino loko win maryek to nyutho win Were, nike wiŋeyi go maber.
49001018	Odoko akwayo nike paro ma chuny win woyawere ma neno lero pa Were, to wiŋeyo geno ma go olwoŋ'iye win, kodi silwany madwoŋ ma go ochiko ji pere,
49001019	kendo paka men pere madwoŋ moasere tiyo ri wan ma wayeyo. Men no dwoŋ tektek,
49001020	aka ama go ooro ma chierino Kristo kwoŋ jomotho, to miyo go bedo yu chinge marachuch i polo.
49001021	Yesu Kristo dhumo jodhum jye, jodongo, jomeni, ruodhe; aka nyinge loyo nyingi jo jye minyalo miyo pama kodi i ndir mabino jye.
49001022	Were oketho gimoro jye i par tyendi go to miyo go bedo jatel ma gimoro jye i kitipa pa jomoyeyo,
49001023	mobedo delkwoŋ Kristo, aka a go won gi kululu ma poŋo kis gimoro iye jye.
49002001	I ndir mokadho oido witho i chuny win ru turo chik kodi timo gimarecho.
49002002	I ndir no oido wiluwo yo marecho ma nyapiny; oido wiluwo ruoth ma dhumo ker ma hongo malo, chuny ma pama dhumo ji ma jochayo Were.
49002003	Aka wajojye oido wachalo jo, munyo watimo gima chuny wan marecho oido tero wan iye, aka watimo gima delkwoŋ wan gi paro mawan oyenyo. Paka joman jye, di wabende walimo girachula pa Were.
49002004	To Were moŋaŋ gi ŋono, i mar pere madwoŋ m'omaro gine wan,
49002005	kada oido watho i chuny wan ru turo chik ma waturo, omiyo walimo kwo kanyachiel gi Kristo; aka wiboth chungo kwoŋ ŋono pa Were.
49002006	Aka Were ochierino wan gi Kristo, to ketho wan kanyachiel gine i kabedo mapolo i Kristo Yesu.
49002007	Otimo ama ma nyutho ŋono pere moŋaŋ moasere, munyo timo ri wan bero i Kristo Yesu.
49002008	Kole ru ŋono amomiyo wiboth chungo kwoŋ yeyo; aka me kobedo tim mewin wiwegi, to obedo mich pa Were.
49002009	Kobedo ru tim, ma moro d'opakere.
49002010	Wabedo chwech pa Were, aka ochweyo wan i Kristo Yesu, ni wabedi gi tim mabeyo, ma chango go oyiko chon ni wabedi gine.
49002011	Amomiyo win Jopath, ma Joyudaya jolwoŋo ni “joma kothumere,” aka wegi jolwoŋere ni “jomothumere” (gima mako kwoŋ gima wegi jotimo gine delkwoŋ gin) poyi win gima chango oido wibedo.
49002012	Poyi win ni i hongo no oido fuodi winitye bor gi Kristo. Onwaŋo wijokichar aka oido wikikwanere paka jokweth pa Israel. Oido wingoye i chikirok, kodi geno, kendo oido wingoye gi Were i piny.
49002013	To pama, i Kristo Yesu, win monwaŋo wini bor, onyo okel win chiegin, ru remo pa Kristo.
49002014	Kole Kristo won ama obedo syem mawan, moriwo Joyudaya gi Jopath kanyachiel. Go oturo woko chiel moido kelo pokirok aka miyo jo bedo jokwor.
49002015	Okwanyo woko Chik pa Joyudaya gi thenethene mere gi delkwoŋe, ŋey woloki nonin aryo me ji achiel i go, to kelo syem.
49002016	Tho pa Kristo wi musalaba oreyo woko dakirok; to riwo nonin aryo no gi Were i del achiel.
49002017	Ameno Kristo obino to tito Wach Maber ri win moido wini bor gi Were, gi kelo syem ri joma oido jo ni chiegin gi Were.
49002018	I Kristo wajojye wani gi thwolo i Chuny Maleŋ achiel ma kidho bongi Were Bawan.
49002019	Amomiyo, pama onyo wikibedo Jopath kosa jokichar kendo; to wibedo ji achiel gi ji pa Were; jopecho pa Were.
49002020	Wibende oger win i tyendi ot ma jomoor kodi jotuchi wach Were jokunyo aka tele ma mako tyelo ot meno Yesu Kristo won gipi.
49002021	Ot gipi chungo moriwere i go, to dongo paka ot maleŋ i Ruoth.
49002022	Wibende oger win i go, ŋey wibedi Ot ma Were bed'iye i Chuny Maleŋ pere.
49003001	Amomiyo an, Paulo jatwech pa Kristo Yesu, kamewin Jopath,
49003002	kono wityeko winjo paka Were gi ŋono pere omiyan timo tich ri win:
49003003	Were owodho nyaliŋliŋ pere, to nyuthan gima atyeko ndiko i chieko kwoŋe.
49003004	Ka wisoma gima andiko, wibino ŋeyo paka aniaŋ kwoŋ nyaliŋliŋ pa Kristo,
49003005	ma i hongo mokadho konyuthi ji, to pama Were onyo owodho gi Chuny Maleŋ ri jomoor kodi jotuchi wach pere.
49003006	Nyaliŋliŋ no a me: I Wach Maber, Jopath bende onyo jolunjo ŋaŋo pa Were kanyachiel gi Joisrael, paka adeche ma del achiel, aka bende onyo ofudi ri jo gima Were ochiko i Yesu Kristo.
49003007	Abedo jafuonji Wach Maber me ru ŋono pa Were momiyan kareno men pere tiyo i an.
49003008	Kada oido aŋata aasa thino kwoŋ jomaleŋ jye, Were odyeran ni ater ri Jopath Wach Maber kwoŋ ŋaŋo pa Kristo ma bu gike.
49003009	Kendo anyuthi ji paka chan pa Were ma nyaliŋliŋ moido opanere wok chon i paro pa Were mochweyo gimoro jye, ripere aketha i tim.
49003010	Nike i ndir ma pama, luwo kwoŋ kitipa pa jomoyeyo, Were wonyuthi jodhum, kodi jomeni machuny ma wi hongo malo ryeko pere gi thenethene mere momore.
49003011	Were otimo ama i chan pere ma bu gike, ma go oketho i tim kwoŋ gima Wuode Yesu Kristo Ruodhiwan otimo.
49003012	I go, kendo gi yeyo mawan i go, wanitye gi thwolo ma donjo bongi Were gi syem ma chuny wan odile.
49003013	Amomiyo, akwayo win ni wikiri wirembi, rupiri chandirok paran ri win bino kelo ri win dwoŋ.
49003014	Ri ameno, aguro chongan i nyim Baba,
49003015	ma pechin jye mani polo kodi i piny jonwaŋ nyingi jo kwoŋe.
49003016	Akwayo Were ni chungo kwoŋ dwoŋ pere moasere, womiyi win men i chuny win, gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ pere.
49003017	Odoko ni Kristo wolimi kabedo i chuny win ru yeyo mewin, aka kwo mewin wochungi moridhere i mar,
49003018	ŋey win kodi jomaleŋ jye winyali niaŋ kwoŋ lacho, gi boro, gi ŋawirok kodi thutho ma mar pa Kristo.
49003019	Aka wiŋey ni mar no loyo ryeko jye, aka Were wopoŋi mich pere gi bee i chuny win.
49003020	Onyo ŋata ni gi men ma tiyo i wan nyalo timo gimoasere ma kalo ma wakwayo kosa waparo.
49003021	Weyi dwoŋ wobedi ri go, i kitipa pa jomoyeyo go, kodi i Kristo Yesu, ndir jye chil gi chil. Ameno.
49004001	Amomiyo, an motweyan ru wach pa Yesu Kristo, akwayo win ni kwo mewin wobedi ma ripo gi lwoŋo mewin.
49004002	Bedi win mamwol, ma wimako gikipiny moth, gi diyo chuny, ma wikijoki gi jowoti win, kodi nyutho marok.
49004003	Temi win paka winyalo, kuro syem ma riwo win kanyachiel i Chuny Maleŋ.
49004004	Del nitye achiel, paka geno obedo achiel ma Were olwoŋ'iye wijojye.
49004005	Aka Ruoth nitye achiel, yeyo bende achiel, batisimo bende achiel;
49004006	Were nitye achiel, mobedo Baa ji jye, kodi Ruoth pa ji jye, aka tiyo i ji jye, odoko nitye i ji jye.
49004007	Dhano jye kwoŋ wan otyeko limo mich moro, ma ripo kodi ma Kristo d'onyalo miyo go,
49004008	paka owachi i ndiiko ni, “Munyo go oidho malo, okadho kodi ji mathoth monwaŋo otwey; aka opoko ji mich.”
49004009	Onyo, “Oidho malo,” dwoŋ mere aŋo? Dwoŋ mere ni go okutho oloro piny i pendi lowo.
49004010	Amomiyo, ŋata oloro piny a ŋata bende odoko oidho malo kalo pondeponde ŋey go woswana gimoro jye i piny.
49004011	Go amomiyo ji mich; go oloko jomegi jomoor, joman jotuchi wach Were, joman jotiti Wach Maber, joman oketho bedo jokwath kodi jofuonji.
49004012	Otimo ama ma yiko ji pa Were jye ri tich ma nyakristo, ma gero delkwoŋ Kristo.
49004013	Ameno aka wajojye wabino bedo i achiel i yeyo mawan kodi i ŋeyo Wuodi Were, to wategino i chuny, ma waripo gi kwo pa Kristo mopoŋ.
49004014	Wakiripi odoko bedo pa nyithindho, ma fuonji moro jye kwadho jo korin gi kocha pa koyo, kareno jomogo jowondo wan gi ryekoryeko moro kodi twodo.
49004015	Kuchiel ka waluwo g'adyeri munyo wanyutho mar, wabino dongo i royo jye i Kristo, mobedo wich kitipa pa jomoyeyo.
49004016	I chan pere, adeche mopokere ma del gipi joriwere kanyachiel gi fuch ma riwo jo. Amomiyo ka kis adech tiyo paka mitere aka del gipi dongo i mar.
49004017	Amomiyo, i nyingi Ruoth awacho ri win gime, odoko amedo ridho: kwo mewin odoko kiripi bedo paka apa jokafiri, ma paro pajo ongoye kony.
49004018	Chuny jo nitye i mudho, aka jonitye bor gi kwo pa Were ru miŋo pajo; ato wiy gin tek swa.
49004019	Paro ma chuny jo otyeko thore woko; kwo pajo nitye i kite marecho kende, aka jotimo gikoch g'awanya madit, mongoye wichkwot.
49004020	Meno k'agima wifuonjere kwoŋ Kristo!
49004021	Ipoyo kosa wikiwinjo adyeri ma nitye i Yesu maber odocho.
49004022	Kole ofuonji win ni wiboli woko kiti win machon, ma awanya marecho oido nyieko.
49004023	Paro mewin kodi chuny win ripo lokirok manyien,
49004024	aka nyaka wiruki kwo manyien, mochwey i chal pa Were, i tiro kodi leŋo.
49004025	Ri ameno, twodo onyo wongoye wok pama. Dhano jye ripo luwo ri nyawote giradyeri, rupiri wajojye wabedo adeche moriw kanyachiel.
49004026	Ka wimako nge, gino wokiri worwaki win i gimarach; aka wikiri wibedi gi nge ndelo gipi,
49004027	odoko wikiri wimiyi Jwogi thwolo.
49004028	Ŋata yado kwalo woweyi kwo, kuchiel wochaki tich, wotimi tich mabeyo gi chinge wonyal kir konyo jochandi.
49004029	Weyi win luwo wach ma ramo chuny jo, to luwi win wach mabeyo kendo kodi ma konyo joman, kende ma ripere i hongo moluwi iye no, ŋey wach mewin wonyali kelo ŋono ri joma winjo.
49004030	Wikiri wimiy Chuny Maleŋ gut, rupiri go obedo ranyuth ma Were oketho kwoŋ win ri ndelo ma both.
49004031	Kwanyi win woko duro, gi keme, kodi nge, gi dhaw kodi nyieko nyingi wadi win.
49004032	Bedi win mere ma wimako wor gi jowoti win aka wichwakere i yoto, paka Were ochwako win i Kristo.
49005001	Paka wibedo nyithindho pa Were ma kachunye, wiripo temo chalo go.
49005002	Wiripo bedo gi mar paka Kristo omaro wan to miyo kwo pere kamawan paka rachow ma ŋwe kur ri Were.
49005003	Paka ji maleŋ pa Were, kiripi ni wach ma kidakana, kosa koch, kosa woro wowachi kwoŋ win.
49005004	Kendo kiripi ni wach ma wiluwo wobedi ma kwoto wiy jo, mamiŋo, kosa kilyesa makoch. Kuchiel wiripo bedo munyo wifuoyo Were ayino.
49005005	Ŋeyi win gime ni: ongoye moro jye ma jachot, makoch, kosa mawor (kole woro chale pa lamo gima kobedo Were) m'olim gimoro i Ker pa Kristo kodi apa Were.
49005006	Wikiri wiyey moro wowondi win gi wach mongoye kony, rupiri gikipiny me jye ama bino miyo Were kigaga gi ji ma jokiwinji go.
49005007	Amomiyo wikiri wimakere gi kiti ji ma chalo ameno.
49005008	Kole chon oido wibedo jomudho, to pama onyo wilokere jolero i Ruoth. Ri ameno wothi win paka nyithidho ma lero.
49005009	Kole gima kelo lero obedo gikipiny mabeyo, motire kodi maradyeri.
49005010	Temi win fuonjirok gima sangala Ruoth.
49005011	Wikiri widonji i tim ma cholo ma kikony, kuchiel wodhi win gikipiny no kamaler.
49005012	(Temo luwo kwoŋ gikipiny ma jotimo nyaliŋliŋ kelo kir wichkwot).
49005013	Aka gima owodhi tithango kamaler nyaka bino nenere maber;
49005014	ato gimoro jye mothangi kamaler lokere lero. Amomiyo nitye wach ma wacho ni, “Chiewi, in janindo me, aka ayi ieye woko bongi jomotho, aka Kristo bino lyel i kwo perin.”
49005015	Amomiyo kure win i kwo mewin. Wikiri wibedi pa jomamiŋ, to bedi win pa jomaryek.
49005016	Wikiri winyieki hongo ma winitye gine, rupiri me ndir ma recho oaser'iye.
49005017	Wikiri wibedi mamiŋmiŋ, to niaŋi win gima Were mito.
49005018	Wikiri wimeri gi medho rupiri meno myenirok, to poŋi win gi Chuny Maleŋ ayin.
49005019	Weri win wer ma zabul kodi wer man jye machuny. Weri win gi dwondi win mamit ri Ruoth munyo wipako go i chuny win.
49005020	Aka fuoyi win Were noknok ri gimoro jye, i nyingi Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo.
49005021	Winjere win paka wiwinjo Kristo.
49005022	Mon jowowinji chwogi jo paka jowinjo Ruoth won.
49005023	Kole jachwo obedo jatel pa dhako paka Kristo obedo jatel pa kitipa pa jomoyeyo Were, ma jobedo delkwoŋe, aka go won a jaboth pajo.
49005024	To paka kitipa pa jomoyeyo winjo Kristo, ameno mon bende jowowinji chwogi jo i gimoro jye.
49005025	Chwo, mari win mon mewin paka Kristo omaro kitipa pa jomoyeyo to miyere ri go,
49005026	nike woloki go maleŋ kareno lonyo go gi pi kodi wach ma kwo,
49005027	ŋey wokeli kitipa no bonge motyeko lony ma bu chilo, kosa mongoye kama ojony kendo mongoye kwoŋe sandi mogo jye.
49005028	Ameno chwo bende joripo maro mon pajo paka delkwoŋ gin won. Ŋata omaro chiege meno won omarere.
49005029	(Ongoye moro ma ruman dak delkwoŋe won, kuchiel pidho aka kuro maber, paka Kristo timo ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo,
49005030	rupiri wabedo adeche ma delkwoŋe.)
49005031	Amomiyo jachwo weyo bamere gi yokimere to chwire kwoŋ chiege to jaryo no jolokere del achiel.
49005032	Me obedo wach mopondo madwoŋ swa, aka me onyo ageda ka akidho kwoŋ Kristo kodi kitipa pa jomoyeyo go.
49005033	Ri ameno jachwo jye ripo maro chiege paka won omarere, aka dhako bende ripo miyo chwore dwoŋ.
49006001	Nyithindho, winji win jonywol mewin i Ruoth, rupiri obedo gimotire timo ameno.
49006002	“Lwori benin gi yokin,” obedo or moteli medo gi chikirok iye ni,
49006003	“Aka nyaka gimoro jye bino bedo rin maber, t'iyindira i piny.”
49006004	Jonywol, wikiri wikuri nyithindho mewin i yo ma miyo jo nge. Kuchiel, fuonji win jo jowodongi i tim mabeyo kodi i fuonji pa Ruoth.
49006005	Ŋechin, winji win ruodhe mewin ma piny ka, gi lworo kodi kirin; aka witimi tich gi chuny win achiel, igani witimo ri Kristo won gipi.
49006006	Winji win jo, ki nyaka ni jowofuoyi win ka joneno win, to tiyi win paka jotich pa Kristo, ma jotimo gima Were yenyo.
49006007	Timi win tich mewin gi kisangala, igani witiyo ri Ruoth, ma kiweno ri ji.
49006008	Poyi win ni Ruoth bino miyo dhano jye kemba, kada bedi ŋecha kosa ŋata ni syem, ru tich pere maber ma go otimo.
49006009	Onyo ruodhe, wibende kuri win ŋechin mewin ameno. Weyi win bwoko jo paka wiŋeyo ni win kodi ŋechin mewin jye wibedo apa Ruoth achiel i polo, ma thumo banja ri dhano jye mongoye yero.
49006010	Machowe, bedi win ma wichwiny i Ruoth, kanyachiel gi i men pere moasere.
49006011	Ruki win gilweny jye ma Were poko, aka nyaka winonyali chungo matek gi chiro bwo pa jwogi.
49006012	Ato wakilwenyi gi ji wadi wan, to gi jodhum mogo, gi ruodhe mogo, kodi jomeni ma cholo ma piny me, kodi jodhum marecho machuny, ma wi hongo malo.
49006013	Amomiyo ruki win gilweny pa Were gipi, ŋey ka ndelo ma racho otundi, wibino nyalo chiro lweny pa jakwor, aka ka wityeko lwenyo kir i gike, bino nwaŋo ni fuodi witek.
49006014	Amomiyo chungi win matek, aka adyeri ama wobedi del mothoko pyer win, tiro ama wiruki paka kwot ma nyweny i dakoriwin,
49006015	aka yikirok ma tito Wach Maber ma kelo syem wobedi war ma tyendi win.
49006016	Medo kwoŋ gikipiny no jye, tiŋi win yeyo paka kwot mewin; meno ama wibino geŋo gi kweyo gine asere malyel mach ma Ŋatarach obay.
49006017	Kethi win both paka junga ma gwoko wiy win, aka wach pa Were paka abor ma Chuny Maleŋ miyo win.
49006018	Aka bedi win i kwayo, munyo wikwayo kony pa Were i royo momore hongo jye, paka Chuny nyutho win. Amomiyo bedi win milengela aka wikiri wilachere ndir jye, to kwayi win ri ji pa Were.
49006019	Kwayi win ran bende ni Were womiyan mikwenda ka ayikere luwo, ŋey aluwi gi miseni ka amiyo ji ŋeyo nyaliŋliŋ ma Wach Maber.
49006020	Kole abedo jamikwenda ma Wach Maber kada pama anitye i twech. Kwayi win ni abedi gi miseni ma luwo wach no paka ripere atimi.
49006021	Tichiko, omin wan ma jatich ma genere i tich pa Ruoth, bino kilyesa ri win kis gimoro, to wiŋeyo paka anitye, kodi gima atimo.
49006022	Amomiyo adhiro go bongi win, wiŋey paka wanitye, aka wokweyi chuny win.
49006023	Were Baba kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo, womiyi jomoyeyo jye syem gi mar, medo wi yeyo.
49006024	Ŋono wobedi gi ji jye ma jomaro Ruoth Yesu Kristo gi mar makirum.
50001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo kodi Timotheyo, jotich pa Kristo Yesu, Ri ji maleŋ pa Were jye ma jobedo Filipya ma joyeyo Kristo Yesu, kanyachiel kodi jotel ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo kodi jokony:
50001002	Weyi Were Bawan kodi Yesu Kristo womiyi win ŋono gi syem.
50001003	Afuoyo Were paran ri wijojye ndir jye ka aparo kwoŋ win;
50001004	aka noknok ka akwayo ri win, akwayo gi kisangala,
50001005	rupiri wikonyan gi tich ri Wach Maber wok ndelo marapena tundo konon.
50001006	Amomiyo aŋeyo gime nike: Were m'ochako tich maber i win, bino medere gine chuka orum i Ndelo pa Kristo Yesu.
50001007	Obedo gimaber ran paro ama kwoŋ win rupiri winitye i chunyan. Odoko, wiriwere kodan i ŋono ma Were omiyan me, ma bedo i twech kodi ma gwoko gi ridho Wach Maber.
50001008	Were oŋeyo nike aluwo adyeri ka awacho ni aparo kwoŋ win gi paro pa Yesu Kristo won.
50001009	Aka me a kwayo paran ri win: nike mar mewin womedere dongo noknok, i ŋeyo gimoro gi niaŋ maber i wach,
50001010	aka nyaka wibino nyalo yero gima oasa bero. Meno aka wibino bedo ma bu chilo moro jye kodi apuse i ndelo pa Kristo.
50001011	Kwo mewin bino nyak olemo ma kite mabeyo, ma Yesu Kristo won ama kelo, to miyo Were dwoŋ kodi pak.
50001012	Amito wiŋey, wutimera, nike gikipiny motimere ran otyeko konyo swa nyayo Wach Maber.
50001013	Gimowok iye, jokur jye ma chiel pa kere kodi joman jye jonyalo ŋeyo nike anitye i twech ka ru tich pa Kristo.
50001014	Aka bedo paran i twech otyeko miyo wutimere i Ruoth ma loyo thoth miseni ma medo tito wach pa Were gi derino mongoye lworo.
50001015	Iyadyeri jomogo kwoŋ jo jofuonjo wach pa Kristo gi nyieko kodi dhawirok, to joman jofuonjo gi paro maber.
50001016	Joman me jotimo ameno i mar, rupiri joŋeyo ni okethan ka ma wodho kony ri Wach Maber.
50001017	To jonicha jofuonjo kwoŋ Kristo gi woro ma kiweno g'adyeri, aka wegi jomito tiŋirok malo ayin; joparo nike jonyalo kisigila ran teko man ma fuodi anitye i twech.
50001018	To kiwach moro, asangala ayino, rupiri ji jofuonjo kwoŋ Kristo i royo jye ma nyalere, kada bedi g'atoŋa kuya mokom kosa motire. Aka abino medo kisangala,
50001019	rupiri aŋeyo ni ru kwayo mewin kodi kony mawok bongi Chuny Maleŋ pa Yesu Kristo, ibino gonyan wok i twech.
50001020	Kole ani g'awanya madwoŋ kodi geno nike wiyan kokwoti i tich paran, to ni hongo jye, ma kada pama won, abino bedo gi miseni madwoŋ ma kelo dwoŋ ri Kristo i del paran, kada akwo kosa atho.
50001021	Aka ri an, bedo gi kwo meno doŋ i Kristo, aka tho meno nwaŋo lim.
50001022	To ka amedere gi kwo i del, meno abino medo timo tich maber man; onyo akuya gima ripere ayer.
50001023	Atudere i dyer paro aryo: ayenyo swa weyo kwo me akidhi abedi gi Kristo, mobedo gimaber loyo;
50001024	to ma loyo, ri bero mewin, a an doŋ makwo.
50001025	Aŋeyo gime adyeri, amomiyo aridho ni abino doŋ. Abino bedo gi wijojye ma medo konyo win widongi kodi kisangala i yeyo.
50001026	Amomiyo ka anobedi gi win kendo, wibino bedo gi kisangala madwoŋ, i kwo mewin i Yesu Kristo.
50001027	Kada obedi nedi, bedi win gi kite ma ripo gi Wach Maber pa Kristo, ŋey kada ka anobin neno win, kosa ka awinjo awinja ayino kwoŋ win, obedi ni wichungo matek kodi atoŋa achiel, aka wilwenyo kanyachiel, gi paro achiel kende ri yeyo ma Wach Maber kelo.
50001028	Wikiri wibedi malwor ri jokwor mewin, to ndelo jye bedi win miseni, rupiri meno bino nyutho jo ni jorwenyo, to win wiboth, aka meno jye gima Were ama timo.
50001029	Kole go otyeko miyo win silwany, ki nyaka ma yeyo Kristo kende, to ma chandirok ri go bende.
50001030	Ato lweny m'onyo wini gine no a kiti lweny ma winenan munyo alwenyo i ndir mokadho aka wiwinjo ni fuodi ani gine.
50002001	Ka kwo mewin i Kristo nyalo medo win miseni, kosa mar pere nyalo dwoko chuny win, kosa winyalo riwirok i Chuny, kosa winitye gi wor kodi chwako jowoti win,
50002002	onyo sangala win an munyo wibedo gi paro achiel, gi mar achiel, kareno wibedo achiel i chuny win kodi i paro mewin.
50002003	Wikiri witim gimoro munyo wilaro dwoŋ, kosa wiyumere kichar; to bedi win gi bwonirok i waŋ jowoti win, munyo witero jo igani joloyo win gi dwoŋ.
50002004	Aka kis dhano kwoŋ win wopar kwoŋ gima jowote joyenyo, ma kiweno gima go ama yenyo.
50002005	Paro mewin ripo bedo paka ma Yesu Kristo oido ni gine:
50002006	Kada chal pere oido nitye i madala pa Were, go kotemo oro men no, kada nende go oido rom gi Were.
50002007	Kuchiel go oketho men no gichien, to kwanyo kabedo pa ŋecha, munyo onywol go i chal pa dhano. Aka munyo go onwaŋere i chal pa dhano,
50002008	obwonere aka owinjo Were chuka oyeyo kir tho: tho wi musalaba!
50002009	Amomiyo, Were otiŋo go malo i kabedo madwoŋ loyo, to miyo go nyinge madwoŋ loyo nyingi jo jye.
50002010	Chwech jye mani polo, kodi piny, kodi i pendi piny, jobino goyo chongi jo piny gi miyo nyingi Yesu dwoŋ.
50002011	Aka lew jo jye bino tucho ni Yesu Kristo obedo Ruoth, ma miyo Were Bamere dwoŋ.
50002012	Amomiyo, wutimera, paka noknok wiwinjo or, ki nyaka ruwaŋan kende, to tektek paka onyo angoye, tiyi win ri both mewin gi lworo kodi kirin.
50002013	Kole Were ama tiyo i win, ma miyo wiyeyi aka winyali timo atoŋa pere.
50002014	Timi win gimoro jye mongoye kiŋunyaŋunya kosa pyem,
50002015	ŋey wibedi ma wingoye g'apuse, ma witire paka nyithindho pa Were ma jongoye gi racho i dyer luse ji mokom kendo marecho, ma wiripo lyel i dyer jo paka michalin ma menyo piny.
50002016	Ka wichwire i mikwenda ma kwo, aka anobedi g'atoŋa ma yumirok gi win i Ndelo pa Kristo. Kole meno bino nyutho ni tekirok paran jye kodi tich kotho nono!
50002017	To kada onyo chale pa ikonjan woko pa vini mimedo wi rachow man kodi tich ma wok i yeyo mewin, jye fuodi asangala, aka apoko kisangala paran no gi wijojye.
50002018	Ri ameno, wibende sangala win aka wipoki kodan syem mewin.
50002019	Ageno i Ruoth nike abino dhiro ri win Timotheyo mayot, ŋey alimi miseni i wach ma kwoŋ win.
50002020	Angoye gi ŋat man kwanyo woko go, ma bende iyadyeri dewo kwoŋ win.
50002021	Ŋat man jye tho kwoŋ wach pere won, ma kiweno kwoŋ apa Kristo Yesu.
50002022	Aka wiwegi wiŋeyo paka Timotheyo otyeko nyutho nyalo pere, rupiri paka nyathi gi bamere, go otyeko tich kodan kanyachiel i fuonjo Wach Maber.
50002023	Ageno oro go bongi win, tekin aŋeyo paka gikipiny obedi ran.
50002024	Aka ageno i Ruoth ni awon abino tundo bongi win mayot.
50002025	Odoko aparo nike ripere adhiri ri win omin wan Epafurodito bende, motyeko tich gi lwenyo ruŋetan, aka otyeko kir tich paka jamikwenda mewin i konyan.
50002026	Go yenyo swa neno wijojye, aka chunye ramo swa rupiri wiwinjo ni go oido two.
50002027	Adyeri go oido two moido chiegin tho, to Were mako wor gine; aka ki gi go kende, to gi an bende, ŋey akir abedi gi litho mathoth i chunyan.
50002028	Amomiyo ayikere oro go bongi win, ŋey wisangala ka wineno go kendo, to litho ma chunyan mojere woko.
50002029	Amomiyo, joli win go gi kisangala jye, paka omin win i Ruoth, odoko wori win ji ma pameno,
50002030	rupiri go ojala kwo pere, aka oboth otho ru tich pa Kristo, kendo omiyan kony ma wiwegi di wikinyalo chowo.
50003001	Aka machowe, wutimera, bedi win gi kisangala i Ruoth. Gik i gima atyeko ndiko chon kijokan, aka meno medo gwoko win i yeyo.
50003002	Gwokere win kwoŋ jotimi recho, gwokere no, ma jochwire kwoŋ thumirok ma del.
50003003	Kole wan ayino ama watyeko limo thumirok maradyeri, wan ma walamo Were gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ, aka wayumere i Kristo Yesu. Odoko wakikethi geno moro kwoŋ thumirok ma del,
50003004	kada awon onwaŋo d'anyal bedo g'atoŋa ma ketho geno paran i gikipiny ma pameno. Ka moro ni g'atoŋa ma yumirok i del, ani gine ma loyo:
50003005	Alimo thumirok i ndelo maraboro wok nywolirok paran, abedo Jaisrael, anywola ma nono pa Benjamin, Jayudaya gikululu. Aka i wach ma kuro Chik ma nyayudaya, onwaŋo abedo Jafarisayo gipi;
50003006	aka i ketho kinen ma nyadin, alwenyo gi kweth pa jokristo. I bedo motire gi winjo Chik, onwaŋo angoye gi recho.
50003007	To gimogo jye ma d'akwan pa lim, onyo atero paka gimongoye kony ru yeyo Kristo.
50003008	Ki meno kende, akwano gimoro jye paka podho madwoŋ, rupiri gima di welo moasere a ŋeyo Kristo Yesu Ruoth paran. Ru wach pere atyeko bolo woko gimoro jye; atero jye paka woyo, ŋey alim Kristo,
50003009	ŋey abedi i go. Aka adoko akibedi gi tiro paran won, i royo ma kuro Chik, to pama anitye gi tiro ma wok bongi Were, aka ma chungo kwoŋ yeyo Kristo.
50003010	Gima ayenyo kende a ŋeyo Kristo, gi men ma chierino pere, kodi riwirok gi go i chandirok pere, gi bedo paka go i tho pere,
50003011	munyo ageno ni abende abino chierino kwoŋ jomotho.
50003012	Akiwachi nike atyeko nwaŋo gime, kosa ni atyeko lokirok maleŋ. Fuodi amedere gi tekirok nyuka anonwaŋi gima omiyo Kristo Yesu olokan apere.
50003013	Ato, wutimera, akipar nike adyeri oido atyeko tundo kanyago; gimoro achiel m'atimo, a weyo wiyan wowili gi gimotyeko kadho yu chien, gi temo paka anyalo tundo bothi gima ni yu wiyan.
50003014	Amomiyo aringo m'adiyo chunyan, kareno achomere kodi gike, ŋey alimi kemba ma Were olwoŋan ri go, i polo malo i Kristo Yesu.
50003015	Wajojye ma wategino i chuny waripo bedo gi paro achiel no. To ka ipoyo ruman wini gi paro mopokere, Were bino menyo ri win gino maber.
50003016	To kada ameno, weyi wakidhi yu malo gi kite ma watyeko luwo kir konon.
50003017	Wutimera, wijojye timi win paka atimo. Watyeko miyo win ranen maber. Amomiyo kaŋasa win joma luwo ranen no.
50003018	Ato paka atyeko wacho ri win gime chon dikweth, onyo ee adoko awacho gi pigi waŋan: nitye ji mathoth ma kwo pajo loko jo jokwor gi musalaba pa Kristo.
50003019	Jokidho reyirok i mach makitho, rupiri Were pajo obedo awanya ma delkwoŋ gin, aka jopakere kodi gima wiy jo di kwoti gine ayin. Joketho paro pajo kwoŋ gikipiny ma piny ka kende.
50003020	To wan, wabedo ji ma polo, aka wakuro dwoko pa Jaboth wok i polo, aka manago Ruoth Yesu Kristo.
50003021	Go bino wiro delkwoŋ wan manyap matho me, to loko ma chale gi delkwoŋe won ma didwoŋ, kareno oro men ma go nyalo kelo gine gikipiny jye i dhum pere.
50004001	Amomiyo, wutimera, amaro win swa, aka akeŋ win tektek. Ka wichungo ma wichwiny i Ruoth, merin paran, meno a kisangala paran.
50004002	Yudya kodi Sintika, mondo, akwayo win, temi win yeyirok paka nyimere i Ruoth.
50004003	Aka in bende, jatich nyawotan ma genere, amito ikonyi mon me; kole jotyeko tich matek kodan i nyayo Wach Maber, kanyachiel gi Kerementi kodi jotich jowotan jye, ma nyingi jo nitye i kitawo ma kwo.
50004004	Sangala win i Ruoth noknok; adoko awacho ni sangala win!
50004005	Nyuthi win mwolo ri ji jye. Ruoth bino mayot.
50004006	Wikiri wirembi ri gimoro jye, to i kis gimoro wachi win ri Were gima wiyenyo, munyo wikwayo aka wiywakere ri go gi fuoyo i chuny win.
50004007	Aka syem pa Were ma kalo kama dhano oŋey'iye jye, bino kuro paro mewin gi chuny win maber, i Kristo Yesu.
50004008	Machowe, wutimera, poŋi win i paro mewin gikipiny mabeyo mipako me: gikipiny maradyeri, ma didwoŋ, motire, molony, maber amara, kodi maŋon.
50004009	Kethi win i tim gima wifuonjere kosa winwaŋo bongan, ma wok i wach paran kodi i tim paran. Aka Were ma poko syem bino bedo gi win.
50004010	Ani gi kisangala madwoŋ moasere i Ruoth, ni wilimo hongo ma nyutho paka wiparo kwoŋan. Adyer oido wiparo kwoŋan, to oido fuodi wikilimo hongo ma nyutho ayino.
50004011	Aka akiwachi ama ni rupiri nitye gima ayenyo; kole atyeko fuonjere ŋiyo kodi gima ani gine.
50004012	Aŋeyo dwoŋ bedo m'achando gimoro, kodi dwoŋ bedo gi gikipiny m'ayenyo ma romo. Atyeko fuonjere nyaliŋliŋ ma diyo chunyan kamoro jye, hongo moro jye, kada ayeŋ kosa ani gi kech, kada amore gi gikipiny kosa anitye gi manok.
50004013	Anyalo timo gimoro jye i Kristo ma miyan men.
50004014	To obedo maber swa munyo wikonyan i teko paran.
50004015	Aka win Jofilipya wiwegi wiŋeyo maber ni munyo aweyo Masedonia, i ndir m'achako fuonjiye win Wach Maber, win kende oido a kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma joriwere kodan i poko kodi jolo gimogo.
50004016	Kir munyo oido anitye Thesalonika, widhiro ran kony ma kalo dichiel.
50004017	Kobedo nike arango limo mich; to amito ni womedi win magowa i migowin kan mewin.
50004018	Atyeko limo chul jye, kir gi kalo; ani gi gimoro jye mayenyo, paka Epafurodito otyeko kelo ran mich mewin jye. Gikipiny me chalo mich ma ŋwe kur, rachow ma jolere aka sangala Were.
50004019	Aka Were paran bino miyo win gimoro jye ma wiyenyo, wok kwoŋ ŋaŋo pere gi dwoŋ pere i Kristo Yesu,
50004020	Dwoŋ wobedi ri Were Baba chil gi chil. Ameno.
50004021	Mothi ran ji pa Were jye ma jonitye i Kristo Yesu. Wutimere ma jo ni ka kodan jomotho win.
50004022	Ji pa Were jye ma ka, kodhi jochiel pa Kaisar, jomotho win.
50004023	Ŋono pa Ruoth Yesu Kristo wobedi kodi win.
51001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, ma gi mito pa Were obedo jamoor pa Kristo Yesu, jokodi omin wan Timotheyo,
51001002	Ri ji maleŋ ma Kolosai, ma jobedo wutimin wan ma jogenere i Kristo: Were Bawan womiyi win ŋono gi syem.
51001003	Noknok wafuoyo Were, Baa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo, ka wakwayo ri win,
51001004	rupiri watyeko winjo yeyo mewin i Kristo Yesu, kodi mar mewin ri ji pa Were jye.
51001005	Yeyo kodi mar no owok i geno gima okan ri win i polo ma wityeko winjo kwoŋe i wach maradyeri, aka Wach Maber.
51001006	Wach Maber me otyeko bino ri win, aka nyay ka medere i piny jye, paka onyay i dyer win wok i ndelo ma wipen winj'iye kwoŋ ŋono pa Were to wiŋeyo adyeri mere jye.
51001007	Wifuonjere gime bongi Epafura, jatich kodi wan ma wamaro swa, aka obedo jatich ma genere ri Kristo kamawan.
51001008	Go bende owacho ri wan kwoŋ mar mewin mi Chuny omiyo win.
51001009	Ri ameno, fuodi wakikeŋ kwayo ri win, wok chuka wawinji kwoŋ win. Wakwayo Were wopoŋi win gi ryeko ma ŋeyo gima go yenyo, gi ryeko jye kodi niaŋ ma Chuny miyo.
51001010	Wakwayo ameno ŋey kwo mewin wobedi paka Ruoth mito, to witimo gima sangala go hongo jye. Kwo mewin bino nyak kiti tich mabeyo jye, aka wibino medere gi ŋeyo Were.
51001011	Weyi Were woloki win jomotegino gi men ma wok i dwoŋ pere moasere, ŋey winyali chiro gimoro jye gi diyo chuny kodi kisangala.
51001012	Aka fuoyi win Bawan, momiyo winyalo limoye gima Were okano ri ji pere i lero.
51001013	Kole go otyeko botho wan kwoŋ men ma mudho to kelo wan i Ker pa Wuode ma migos m'omaro,
51001014	ma walimo both i go, tichwako gimarecho mawan.
51001015	Kristo obedo chal pa Were ma kinenere. Go obedo Wuode ma kayo, aka loyo gimoro jye mochwey gi dwoŋ.
51001016	Kole luwo kwoŋ go Were ochweyo gimoro jye i polo kodi i piny gi gikipiny manenere kodi ma kinenere, kada kom madhum, kosa men, kosa jodhum, kosa ruodhe. Were ochweyo gimoro jye luwo kwoŋ go kendo ri go.
51001017	Go obedo ma fuodi gikipiny jye, aka chungo kwoŋ go gikipiny jye jonitye i kabedo pajo.
51001018	Go a jatel pa delkwoŋe, mobedo kitipa pa jomoyeyo jye, go a chakirok, okayo mopen chierino kwoŋ jomotho, ŋey go wolimi kabedo marapena i gikipiny jye.
51001019	Kole Were won ama omito ni go wobedi gi kwo pa Were gipi.
51001020	Amomiyo, kwoŋ Wuode, Were otyeko dwoko chwech jye bonge, ma nitye piny kodi i polo jye, munyo kelo syem gi remo pa Wuode mochwer wi musalaba.
51001021	Aka yado onwaŋo winitye bor gi Were, kareno wibedo jokwor pere i paro mewin kodi i gikipiny marecho moido witimo.
51001022	To pama, kwoŋ tho ma delkwoŋ Wuode, Were onyo odwoko win i tiyirok gine, ŋey go wokeli win ruwaŋe, ma wileŋ ma bu racho.
51001023	Ato wiripo medirok gi yeyo mewin, ma wiridhere aka wichwiny, ma wikiyengere i geno ma wilimo munyo wiwinjo Wach Maber. Me a wach ma wiwinjo aka otyek fuonjo dhano jye i piny, ma an Paulo, alokere jatich mere.
51001024	Pama onyo asangala gi chandirok paran ri win, aka chandirok paran i del konyan gi chowo gima fuodi odoŋ i chandirok pa Kristo ri delkwoŋe, mobedo kitipa pa jomoyeyo.
51001025	Olokan jatich ri kitipa no munyo Were omiyan tich ma kelo ri win Wach pere gi bee.
51001026	Me nyaliŋliŋ ma go onwaŋo fuodi opano ri dhano jye i hongo jye mokadho, to onyo pama owodho kamaler ri ji pere maleŋ.
51001027	Kole Were oyiko wodho nyaliŋliŋ pere ri Jopath, jowoŋeyi ŋaŋo madwoŋ man'iye, aka manago Kristo ma nitye i win, ma miyo wigeno limo dwoŋ pa Were.
51001028	Amomiyo wafuonjo ji jye kwoŋ Kristo, ka wanyutho jo royo ma gwokirok gi ryeko ma nger jye, ŋey wakel dhano jye ruwaŋ Were motyeko tegino i Kristo.
51001029	Amomiyo atiyo tektek munyo aoro men moasere ma Kristo poko, ma tiyo i an.
51002001	Amito wiŋey paka atiyo matek ri win, kodi ri ji ma Laudisya, kodi ri ji jye ma fuodi jokonenan.
51002002	Atimo ameno ŋey miseni wopoŋi i chuny jo aka ŋey jowobedi kanyachiel i mar to jolimo silwany ma niaŋ wach kichutho. Meno aka jobino ŋeyo nyaliŋliŋ pa Were, mobedo Kristo won gipi.
51002003	I go, okan'iye ryeko mathoth kodi niaŋ kwoŋ wach.
51002004	Awacho ri win ameno ŋey wikiri wiyey moro womiŋi win gi wach mothotho matwodo, kada chale pa ber.
51002005	Kole kada angoye i del, jye fuodi anitye gi win i chuny, aka asangala ka aneno miseni mewin kodi yeyo ma wiridho i Kristo
51002006	Paka wityeko jolo Kristo Yesu paka Ruoth, doŋi win i go i kwo mewin.
51002007	Weyi tyendi kwo mewin wopidhere to dongo i go, aka wimedi ridhirok i yeyo mewin paka ofuonji win, munyo hongo jye wifuoyo Were.
51002008	Amomiyo, neni win ni moro wokiri wokethi win i bwo pajo gi pyem kodi twodo masisiri, gi thenethene ma kula ma nyanono, gi wach kwoŋ chuny ma jodhumo i piny me, aka kiwoki bongi Kristo.
51002009	Kole kwo pa Were gipi nitye kwoŋ Kristo, i kwo ma nyadel;
51002010	aka wilimo kwo mopoŋ i riwirok gi go. Go a jadhum ma telo jodhum jye kodi men jye.
51002011	Kole bende withumere i riwirok gi Kristo, to thumirok me kobedo ma ji ama jotimo, to thumirok ma nyachuny, mobedo eye woko i men pa del ma gimarach, gi donjo i thumirok pa Kristo.
51002012	Kole munyo wilimo batisimo, meno kareno oyik win gi Kristo, aka bende wichierino gi go ru yeyo mewin i men pa Were ma tich, mochierino go kwoŋ jomotho.
51002013	Kada obedo ni chon oido witho i chuny win ru gimarecho mewin, odoko rupiri oido wibedo Jopath, ma jokithumere, to Were ochwako ri win gimarecho mewin jye, munyo omiyo wan kwo kanyachiel gi Kristo.
51002014	Were oreyo woko gimonwaŋo ondik kwoŋ wan marach, gi chik mere moido yenyo kwoŋ wan gikipiny kweth, to kwanyo woko kichutho munyo oguro gino kwoŋ musalaba.
51002015	Aka Kristo omayo woko jodhum gi ruodhe machuny men, to loko jo giranyera pa ji munyo tero jo paka jomomak i lweny.
51002016	Amomiyo, wikiri wiyeyi moro wokethi ri win chik kwoŋ gima wichamo, kosa wimadho, kosa gima mako kwoŋ kalima ma nyadin, kosa kalima ma dwe manyien, kosa ndelo ma Sabato.
51002017	Gikipiny no jye obedo nyaka tipo pa gikipiny moido lebino; to gimobedo maradyeri won nwaŋere i Kristo.
51002018	Wikiri wiyeyi moro womayi win kemba mewin munyo ŋoyo ni loyo win gi dwoŋ ru lek ma go nwaŋo, kareno nyutho bwonirok ma rendirok aka lamo jomalaika. Dhano ma pameno pakirok ama opoŋ kwoŋe, aka paro pere obedo ma nyadhano.
51002019	Go otyeko weyo chwirok kwoŋ Kristo, mobedo jatel mawan, ma kwoŋ go ama del pere gipi, ma fuche oriwo kanyachiel to makere, nwaŋi'ye men ma dongo paka Were mito ni wodongi.
51002020	K'inen onyo wityeko tho gi Kristo aka oketh win i syem munyo wieye woko kwoŋ chuny ma dhumo piny me, raŋo ma fuodi kwo mewin bedo paka apa ji ma piny me? Raŋo ma wikuro chik masisiri paka ni,
51002021	“Wikiri wimaki gime, wikiri wibili ginicha, wikiri wigeyi mecha?”
51002022	Kole gikipiny me jye bedo gimongoye kony tekin or jo. Jobedo nyaka chik ma dhano am'otimo aka ofuonjo.
51002023	Ato kiti chik no nenere pa giryeko i lamo jomalaika m'otyek chuko gine jo, kodi bwonirok ma rendirok, gi chando delkwoŋ gin; to iyadyeri jongoye kodi kony i dhumo awanya ma del.
51003001	Amomiyo paka otyek chierino win i kwo gi Kristo, onyo kethi win chuny win kwoŋ gikipiny ma polo, kama Kristo ni iye aka obedo yu rachuch pa Were.
51003002	Kethi win paro mewin kwoŋ gikipiny mani malo, ma kiweno kwoŋ ma piny ka.
51003003	Ato wityeko tho, aka kwo mewin onyo opan g'apa Kristo i Were.
51003004	Aka ka kwo mewin, mobedo Kristo onenere kamaler, aka nyaka wibende wibino nenere gine kanyachiel i dwoŋ pere.
