51003005	Amomiyo, wiripo neko woko awanya ma delkwoŋ win paka chot, kidakana, timo gi wichkwot, awanya marecho, gi woro (mobedo lamo chal makichar).
51003006	Kole ru gikipiny me keme pa Were bino podho kwoŋ joma jokiwinji go.
51003007	Onwaŋo yado wiwotho i kwo ma pameno, munyo awanya no ama oido dhumo kwo mewin.
51003008	To pama wiripo bolo woko kiti gikipiny ma chal meno: nge, keme, awacha nyingi, nyieko nyingi jo, yeti kodi luwo makoch.
51003009	Wikiri wiwondere i dyeri win, rupiri oido wityeko lunyo woko kwo machon gi kula mere,
51003010	aka onyo wiruko kwo manyien, ma Were, jachwech mere, hongo jye loko manyien i chal pere won, ŋey wokeli win i ŋeyo go maber odocho.
51003011	Gima wok'iye, ongoye Japath kosa Jayudaya, ŋatothumere kosa ŋata kothumere, ŋata kofuonjere, jonono mogo, joma ni chien, ŋechin, kosa ji mani syem; to Kristo a gima dwoŋ, aka nitye i ji jye!
51003012	Amomiyo paka wibedo ji pa Were moyer, maleŋ aka ma go omaro, onyo bedi win joma ramere ri wadi win, ma wini gi chuny maber, bwonirok, mwolo, kodi diyo chuny.
51003013	Diyi win chuny win gi wadi win, aka chwakere win ka moro kwoŋ win nitye gi kiŋunyaŋunya gi nyawote. Wiripo chwakere paka Ruoth bende otyeko chwako win.
51003014	[Aka ma loyo meno jye, kethi win mar, ma riwo gikipiny jye kanyachiel i riwirok mochowere.
51003015	Weyi syem pa Kristo, ma olwoŋ'iye win paka adeche ma del achiel wodhumi chuny win; Aka bedi win gi fuoyo Were.]
51003016	Weyi mikwenda pa Kristo gi ŋaŋo mere jye, wobedi i chuny win, munyo wifuonjo aka wimedo jowoti win men gi ryeko jye, kareno wiwero wer zabul, kodi wer machuny ka wifuoyo Were i chuny win.
51003017	Gimoro jye ma witimo kosa wiwacho, ripere witimi i nyingi Ruoth Yesu, munyo wifuoyo Were Baba kwoŋ go.
51003018	Mon, winji win chwogi win, paka ripere i Ruoth.
51003019	Chwo, mari win mon mewin, aka wikiri wiori liwugo ri jo.
51003020	Nyithindho, winji win jonywol mewin ndir jye, rupiri meno a gima sangala Ruoth.
51003021	Jonywol, wikiri wimiyi nyithindho mewin nge, rupiri chuny jo nyalo ŋedhere.
51003022	Ŋechin, winji win jodongo mewin i gimoro jye, aka witiyi, ki nyaka munyo joneno win, ma miyo jo kisangala, to tiyi win gi chuny win achiel, kareno wiworo Ruoth.
51003023	Gimoro jye ma witimo, timi win gi chuny win achiel, pa witiyo ri Ruoth, ma kiweno ri dhano.
51003024	Poyi win nike wibino limo kemba ma Ruoth okano ri win. Kole Kristo a Jadwoŋ ma witiyo ri go.
51003025	Aka jatimi recho jye ibino chulo go tim pere marecho no, rupiri Were tero dhano jye marom.
51004001	Ruodhe, bedi win ma witire i kite ma wikuro gine ŋechin mewin. Poyi win nike wibende wini gi Ruoth mewin i polo.
51004002	Bedi win jokinen i kwayo, munyo winitye milengela ka wikwayo gi fuoyo Were.
51004003	Aka kwayi win bende ri wan ni Were woyawi ri wan royo ma fuonjo mikwenda pere, ŋey watiti nyaliŋliŋ pa Kristo. Kole meno amomiyo pama anitye i twech.
51004004	Ri ameno kwayi win nike anyali luwo munyo aketho gikipiny i lero paka ripere atimi.
51004005	Bedi win maryek i kite ma witero gine joma fuodi jokoyeyo, munyo wioro hongo ma wini gine maber.
51004006	Kilyesa mewin ripo ndir jye bedo maŋon ma ywayo chuny jo pa kado chumbi, aka wiripo ŋeyo kite ma dwoko dhano jye maber.
51004007	Omin wan Tichiko ma wamaro mobedo jatich ma genere, aka jatich nyawotan i tich pa Ruoth, bino miyo win wach jye ma mako kwoŋan.
51004008	Aoro go bongi win wonyali wacho ri win paka wanitye, gi dwoko chuny win.
51004009	Go lebino kodi Onesimo, omin wan ma genere ma wamaro, mobedo achiel kwoŋ win. Jobino wacho ri win gimoro jye ma timere ka.
51004010	Aristaruko, ma nitye i twech kodan, dhiro ri win moth kodi Marko bende, omin Barunaba. (Wityeko winjo wach kwoŋe; joli win go ka obino bongi win).
51004011	Yesu milwoŋo ni Yusto, bende dhiro ri win moth. Jadek me kende a Joyudaya ma joyeyo kwoŋ Kristo, ma jotiyo kodan ri Ker pa Were, aka jotyeko konyan swa.
51004012	Epafura, ma bende obedo achiel kwoŋ win, kendo jatich pa Kristo Yesu bende motho win. Ndir jye go kwayo ri win gi maro madwoŋ, munyo kwayo Were womiyi wichungi matek, ma witegino kareno wiridho paro ma timo gima Were yenyo.
51004013	Awon anyalo ridho ri win ni go tiyo ri win matek kodi ri ji ma Lawodisya kodi Hirapoli.
51004014	Luka, jamilerwa ma wamaro, kodi Dimas jodhiro ri win moth pa jo.
51004015	Dhiri win moth mawan ri wutimin wan ma Lawodisya kodi ri dhakodwoŋ Ninfa gi kweth pa jokristo ma chokere i ot pere.
51004016	Ka otyek kisoma ri win balwa me, neni win nike osoma balwa no i kitipa pa jokristo ma Laodisya bende. Aka wibende soma win balwa ma jo Lawodisya jobino dhiro ri win.
51004017	Aka wachi win ri Arukipo ni, “Neni ni ichowo tich m'omiyin i tich pa Ruoth.”
51004018	An, Paulo, andiko ri win moth me gi chingan won; aka wiy win wokiri wowili gi lijegere motweyan me! Weyi ŋono pa Were wobedi kodi win.
52001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, Silvano kodi Timotheyo, Ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Thesalonika, ma jobedo apa Were Baba kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo: Ŋono gi syem wobedi ri win.
52001002	Noknok wafuoyo Were ri win, aka ndir jye watucho win i kwayo mawan.
52001003	Kole wapoyo i nyim Were mawan kodi Bawan paka wiketho yeyo mewin i tim, paka mar mewin omiyo witiyo matek, gi paka geno mewin i Ruoth mawan Yesu Kristo ochwiny.
52001004	Waŋeyo, wutimin wan, nike Were omaro win aka oyero win ni wibedi apere won.
52001005	Kole Wach Maber ma wakelo ri win, kobino nyaka i wach kende, to obino i men kodi i Chuny Maleŋ, gi ridho kichutho kwoŋ adyeri mere. Wiŋeyo paka kwo mawan obedo munyo oido wani gi win kenyo; aka obedo ri bero mewin won.
52001006	Wilokere joma luwo wan kodi Ruoth; aka kada wichandere tektek, wijolo mikwenda gi kisangala ma wok bongi Chuny Maleŋ.
52001007	Ri ameno wityeko lokirok ranen ri jomoyeyo jye i Masedonia kodi i Akaya.
52001008	Kole mikwenda ma mako kwoŋ Ruoth mowok bongi win kotundo ri Masedonia kodi Akaya kende, to wach kwoŋ yeyo mewin i Were olak iye jye. Amomiyo, ongoye gima di wawachi kendo.
52001009	Kole jokoro jye jowacho paka wijolo wan munyo walyewo win, gi paka wiweyo lamo chal makichar to wigik bongi Were, tiyo ri Were maradyeri odoko makwo,
52001010	gi kuro Wuode wobin wok i polo, mobedo Yesu, ma Were ochierino go kwoŋ jomotho, aka ama botho wan kwoŋ keme pa Were ma lebino.
52002001	Kole wiwegi wiŋeyo, wutimere, nike wendo mawan ri win kotho nono.
52002002	Wiŋeyo paka oido otyek timo wan marach gi yeto wan i Filipya ma fuodi wakibino Thesalonika. Kada ameno Were mawan omiyo wan miseni ma tito ri win Wach Maber ma wok bonge, kada pyem obedo madit.
52002003	Kole wach ma wakelo ma tiŋo win malo kochungo kwoŋ komo kosa atoŋa marach, odoko bende wakitemo wondo moro.
52002004	Kuchiel, ndir jye waluwo paka Were yenyo watim, kwoŋ bedo go ofuoyo wan aka oketho Wach Maber i chingi wan. Wakitemi kisangala ji, to wamito kisangala Were ayino, ma temo atoŋa ma chuny wan.
52002005	Kole wiŋeyo maber ni wakibino bongi win gi luwo ma dwoŋo win, kosa gi wach ma umo woro; aka Were obedo jakony mawan i gime!
52002006	Wakitemo rango pak bongi nyatoro, kada bongi win kosa bongi joman,
52002007	kada bedi ni nitye gima oido di wayenyo kwoŋ win g'arom paka jomoor pa Kristo. To wabedo moth munyo wanitye gi win, pa dhako ma kuro nyithindho pere maber swa.
52002008	Ru mar ma wamaro gine win amomiyo wabedo gi kisangala ma pokoye gi win, ki nyaka Wach Maber ma wok bongi Were kende, to kir kwo mawan won, rupiri onwaŋo wibedo ri wan ji mawelo swa!
52002009	Adyer jowoti wan, wipoyo paka watiyo aka wafamba! Watiyo wor g'odyechieŋ ŋey wakiri wabedi gimapek ri win munyo wafuonjo Wach Maber ma wok bongi Were.
52002010	Wibedo jokony mawan, paka Were bende, ni kite ma wanyutho win ma wiyeyo Kristo oido olony aka otire mongoye komo.
52002011	Wiŋeyo nike watero dhano jye kwoŋ win paka baa nyathi tero nyithindho pere.
52002012	Waruma win gi miyo win miseni, wadiyo chuny win, aka wakwayo win nike kwo mewin wobedi ma sangala Were, ma lwoŋo win donjo i Ker kodi i dwoŋ pere.
52002013	Aka ru wach me bende, ndelo jye waketho Were walwa. Munyo wakelo ri win mikwenda pa Were, wiwinjo aka wijolo, ki paka mikwenda pa dhano to mikwenda pa Were, mobedo ameno adyeri. Aka kole Were tiyo maber i dyer win jomoyeyo,
52002014	rupiri, jowotan, wibedo paka kitipin pa jomoyeyo i Kristo ma Yudeya jye, rupiri wibende wichandere i lweny mowok bongi ji mewin wegi, paka jo bende jochandere kwoŋ Joyudaya wadi jo,
52002015	ma joneko Ruoth Yesu kodi jotuchi wach pajo wegi, aka jolwenyo gi wan. Jokisangala Were be! Jolwenyo gi ji jye!
52002016	Jotemo kir juko wan fuonjo Jopath mikwenda ma d'okelo ri jo both. Me a gimarecho mopoŋ magike ma jotimo. Aka onyo pama keme pa Were ojok otundo ri jo.
52002017	To wan, jowotan, munyo olok wan pa nyithidho kiich, to ipoko wan gi win hongo machiek i del, to ki i chuny wan, wakeŋ win swa aka onwaŋo wayenyo gi maro mathoth neno win kendo!
52002018	Aka onwaŋo wayenyo dwoko bongi win. Iyadyeri an Paulo, atemo kir dwoko dikweth, to Sitan chiego ri wan royo.
52002019	Aka onyo geno mawan, kisangala mawan, kodi atoŋa mawan ma yumirok obedi aŋo ruwaŋ Ruodhiwan Yesu ka go odwoko?
52002020	Adyer wiŋati wikibedo pakirok mawan kodi kisangala mawani?
52003001	Machowe, wakinyalo medo chiro, amomiyo waridho bedo kendiwan i Athen,
52003002	kareno waoro Timotheyo, omin wan ma tiyo kodi wan ri Were i fuonjo Wach Maber kwoŋ Kristo. Waoro go bothi win womiyi win miseni gi konyo yeyo mewin,
52003003	aka moro kwoŋ win wokiri wogiki chien ru lweny me. Wiwegi wiŋeyo nike kiti lweny no obedo gima waripo luw'iye.
52003004	Kole munyo fuodi wanitye gi win wawacho ri win ma ndir fuodi kotundo nike ibino lwenyo gi wan, aka paka wiŋeyo maber, meno a gima otimere won.
52003005	Meno amomiyo, munyo akinyalo chiro kendo, adhiro Timotheyo bino ŋeyo gima tho kwoŋ yeyo mewin. Oido alworo ni ipoyo jakeli karatem otyeko temo win, aka tich mawan onyo otho nono!
52003006	To Timotheyo otyeko wok bongi win odwoko bongi wan, aka okelo ri wan wach maber kwoŋ yeyo mewin gi mar mewin. Owacho ri wan paka ndir jye wipoyo wan, aka wiyenyo swa neno wan, paka bende wayenyo neno win.
52003007	Amomiyo, jowotan, i teko mawan jye kodi i chandirok, walimo miseni kwoŋ win ru winjo kwoŋ yeyo mewin.
52003008	Kole pama kere onyo wakwo ka wichungo matek i Ruoth.
52003009	Kosa onyo wanyalo fuoyo Were ri win nedi ru kisangala ma wani gine i waŋ Were mawan ru win.
52003010	Wor godyechieŋ wakwayo go gi chuny wan jye ni woyeyi waneni win aka wanyal poŋo gima yenyere i yeyo mewin.
52003011	Onyo weyi Were mawan kendo Bawan won, kodi Ruodhiwan Yesu, jowoyiki ri wan royo ma bino bongi win!
52003012	Weyi Ruoth womiyi marok, i dyer wiwegi kodi ri ji jye, womedere gi dongo to lokere madwoŋ paka bende wamaro win.
52003013	Ameno go wonyali medo win men i chuny win i leŋo, ŋey wibedi ma bu racho i waŋ Were mawan kendo Bawan, chieŋ ma Ruodhiwan Yesu odwok'iye gi ji maleŋ pere jye.
52004001	Machowe, wutimera, paka wityeko fuonjere bongi wan kiti kwo ma wiripo bedo gine aka nyaka wisangala Were, onyo wakwayo win, kendo waruma win i nyingi Ruoth Yesu, medere ameda win gi timo ameno.
52004002	Kole wiŋeyo or ma wamiyo win, gi men pa Ruoth Yesu.
52004003	Me a gima Were mito ri win: ni wibedi maleŋ aka wingoye kichutho i kwo ma kidakana.
52004004	Kis jachwo jye kwoŋ win ripo ŋeyo royo ma nwaŋo chiege i leŋo gi dwoŋ,
52004005	ma kiweno g'awanya ma timo gi wichkwot pa jokafiri ma jokuya Were.
52004006	Aka i wach me, wongoye nyatoro ma wotimi ri nyawote racho, kosa ma woor kwo pere kichar. Kole watyeko wacho ri win gime chon, munyo wanyutho win gima wikure kwoŋe, nike Were bino chando joma timo recho ma kite no.
52004007	Were kolwoŋo wan bedo i kwo ma kidakana, to ma leŋo.
52004008	Amomiyo, ŋata kwero fuonji me kikwer wach pa dhano, to kwero Were won, ma miyo win Chuny Maleŋ pere.
52004009	Kiyenyere ndiko ri win kwoŋ marok ma wiripo bedo gine ri jowot win ma bende joyeyo. Kole wiwegi Were otyeko fuonjo win paka wiripo marok.
52004010	Aka adyeri wimaro jomoyeyo ma Masedonia gipi. To wakwayo win, wutimin wan, ni medi win ameda timo ameno.
52004011	Bedi win gi maro ma bedo ma wikudere, kareno wiparo kwoŋ tich mewin kende, aka witiyi ri gima nyalo kuro kwo mewin, paka watyeko wacho ri win wok chon.
52004012	Meno aka wibino bedo gi kwo motire i waŋ joma fuodi ni woko, ŋey wikiri wibedi ma wichando gimoro.
52004013	Wutimera, amito wiŋeyi odocho kwoŋ jomotho, aka nyaka wikokumi pa joma jongoye gi geno.
52004014	Ato paka wayeyo ni Yesu otho aka ochierino kendo, meno wayeyo ni Were bende bino dwoko joma jotyeko nindo i Yesu kanyachiel gine.
52004015	Kole wanyutho win gime wok i wach pa Were, nike wan ma fuodi wakwo, aka wadoŋ chuka hongo ma dwoko pa Yesu, wakoteli chierino ri joma onyo jonindo.
52004016	Derino ma wodho or bino bedo, to dwondi malaika madwoŋ winjere, kodi dwondi gwara pa Were, aka Ruoth won bino loro piny wok i polo! Jomotho munyo joyeyo Kristo jobino telo chierino;
52004017	aka ŋey ibino choko wan ma wakwo i hongo no, kanyachiel gi jo i pondeponde kidho romo gi Ruoth i hongo malo. Ameno wabino bedo gi Ruoth ndir jye.
52004018	Amomiyo, kweyi win chuny jowoti win gi wach me.
52005001	Kiyenyere ndiko ri win, wutimera, kwoŋ hongo kodi kare ma gikipiny me letimer'iye.
52005002	Kole wiwegi wiŋeyo maber nike Ndelo pa Ruoth bino bino paka jakwo ma bino wor.
52005003	Munyo ji jowacho ni, “Syem nitye aka gimoro jye oliŋ,” gikenyo arwat to reyirok tundo ri jo. Bino chale gi litho ma dhako winjo munyo chiegin nywol, aka jokobudhere be!
52005004	To win, wutimera, wikinitye i mudho, ma Ndelo no nyalo choro win pa jakwo.
52005005	Wijojye winyithindho pa lero, odoko winyithidho pa odyechieŋ; wakibedo ji pa wor kosa mudho.
52005006	Amomiyo, wakiripi bedo ma wanindo, paka joman; waripo bedo waŋ wan odoko milengela,
52005007	rupiri joma nindo jonindo wor, aka jomamer jomer wor.
52005008	To wabedo ji p'odyechieŋ, aka waripo bedo milengela. Weyi waruki i kor wan yeyo kodi mar paka gilweny, gi geno kwoŋ both paka junga ma lweny.
52005009	Were koyeyo ni keme pere wogeyi wan, to ni walimi both kwoŋ Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo,
52005010	motho ri wan ŋey kada wakwo kosa watho, jye fuodi wabino kwo gine.
52005011	Ru wach me, kweyi win chuny jowot win, aka konyere win paka eno witimo.
52005012	Wakwayo win, wutimera, ni wimiy joma jotiyo i dyeri win dwoŋ, joma Ruoth oyero ma telo win gi fuonjo win.
52005013	Teri win jo gi dwoŋ moasere kodi mar, ru tich ma jotimo ri win. Bedi win i syem gi jowoti win.
52005014	Jowoti wan ma wamaro, waruma win ni, wachi win ri joma bedo abeda m'ongoye tich jowogwokere; miyi win jomalworlwor miseni; konyi win jomanyap; aka diyi win chuny win gi jono jye.
52005015	Neni win ni nyatoro wokiri wochuli recho gi recho, to hongo jye atoŋa mewin wobedi ma timo bero ri jowoti win kodi ri ji man jye.
52005016	Bedi win gi kisangala ndelo jye,
52005017	kwayi win hongo jye ma wikikeŋ,
52005018	fuoyi win Were i gimoro jye ma timere; kole meno a mito pa Were ri win i Kristo Yesu.
52005019	Wikiri wigeŋi Chuny Maleŋ tich.
52005020	Wikiri wichay mikwenda ma Were ama oluwo luwo i dhok jotuchi wach pere,
52005021	to kaŋasa win gimoro jye wiŋey adyeri mere; chwire win kwoŋ gimaber,
52005022	aka weyi win timo kiti recho jye.
52005023	Weyi Were ma japoki syem wolonyi win kichutho; kendo wokuri chuny win, paro mewin, gi delkwoŋ win, ma bu racho moro jye, i ndir ma bino pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo.
52005024	Ŋata lwoŋo win ogenere, aka go bino timo ameno.
52005025	Jowoti wan ma wamaro, kwayi win ri wan bende.
52005026	Mothi win jomoyeyo jowot wan jye akor i leŋo.
52005027	Aoro win gi men pa Ruoth, kisoma balwa me ri jomoyeyo jye.
52005028	Ŋono pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo wobedi gi wijojye. Ameno.
53001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, Sila kodi Timotheyo, Ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Thesalonika ma jobedo apa Were Bawan kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo:
53001002	Weyi Were Bawan kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo jowomiyi win ŋono gi syem.
53001003	Waripo fuoyo Were ri win hongo jye, wutimin wan! Obedo ri wan gimotire timo ameno, rupiri yeyo mewin medo dongo swa aka mar ma kis dhano kwoŋ win nitye gine ri nyawote onyo medere.
53001004	Amomiyo, wawegi wayumere gi win i dyeri kitipa pa jomoyeyo Were. Wayumere gi kite ma wimedere gine chiro teko gi bedo kodi yeyo, i lweny jye kodi i chandirok ma win'iye.
53001005	Me a gima nyutho ni thumo banja pa Were otire, aka gima wok'iye, ibino kwano win paka joma ripo gi Ker pa Were, ma wichandere ri go.
53001006	Kole bedo gima otire ka Were okelo chandirok ri joma miyo wichandere,
53001007	aka bino kelo ywomirok ri win ma pama wichandere, kodi ri wan bende. Gino letimere ameno munyo Ruoth Yesu onenere wok i polo gi jomalaika pere ma jomen,
53001008	gi mach malyel, ma miyo joma kuya Were kodi joma kiwinji Wach Maber mapa Ruoth Yesu girachula.
53001009	Jobino limo girachula ma reyirok woko chil gi chil munyo okwany jo woko ruwaŋ Ruoth kodi men pere ma didwoŋ,
53001010	munyo go bino Ndelo no limo dwoŋ wok bongi ji pere maleŋ jye, kodi nwaŋo wor bongi jomoyeyo jye. Wibende wibino bedo i dyeri jo, rupiri wityeko yeyo mikwenda ma wakelo ri win.
53001011	Me amomiyo wakwayo ri win noknok, ni Were mawan wokonyi win winyali ripo gi kwo molwoŋ'iye win. Aka gi men pere, woyeŋi chuny win i atoŋa maber ma wini gine, kodi tich ma witimo wok kwoŋ yeyo.
53001012	Meno aka nyingi Ruodhiwan Yesu bino limo dwoŋ bothi win, aka win bende bonge, gi ŋono pa Were mawan kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo.
53002001	Gima mako kwoŋ dwoko pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo kodi choko wan kanyachiel bonge, wakwayo win jomoyeyo, ni
53002002	wikiri wikwaki bedo gi kiganagana i paro mewin, kosa limo bwok ru wach pa jomaŋoyo ni Ndelo pa Ruoth otyeko tundo. Ato moro nyalo bino pa jatuchi wach, kosa jafuonji, kosa ma wacho ni wandiko gino i balwa.
53002003	Wikiri wiyeyi nyatoro womiŋi win i royo moro jye, rupiri Ndelo no kotundi nyuka pyem kodi yeyo machowe obedi, to Jal ma kilwor chik m'oyik ri go kidho i mach makitho kutho nenere.
53002004	Go bino pyemo gi gimoro jye ma ji jolamo kosa jotero paka were, to won tiŋere malo to jengere i Ot pa Were munyo ŋoyo ni go a Were!
53002005	Wikipoyi ni atucho ri win gime jye munyo fuodi oido anitye gi win?
53002006	Aka wiŋeyo gima fuodi geŋo bino pa jalo, ŋey wonenere ka hongo pere motire otundo.
53002007	Kole men ma nyaliŋliŋ ma miyo ji kwero lworo chik otyeko chako tich; to ŋata geŋo gino bino timo ameno nyuka okwany woko go i royo.
53002008	Gikenyo nyaka Jal ma kilwor chik bino nenere, ma Ruoth Yesu bino neko woko gi luya ma dhoke, to reyo go woko gi menyirok ma dwoŋ pere munyo dwoko.
53002009	Jal ma kilwor chik no lebino gi men pa Sitan to timo ranyuth kodi gidhyer matwodo,
53002010	kodi gimarecho madit ma wondo joma jobino reyere woko, rupiri jokwero maro adyeri ma d'omiyo jo both.
53002011	Ru wach me Were ledhiro ri jo twodo madwoŋ ŋey jowoyeyi gima kotire,
53002012	aka wothum banja loyo ji ma jokoyeyo adyeri ma josangala kodi gimarach ayin.
53002013	Waripo fuoyo Were ri win hongo jye, jowot wan ma Ruoth omaro, rupiri Were oyero win wok i chakirok ni wilimi both gi men pa Chuny Maleŋ ma lonyo win, ru yeyo adyeri mewin.
53002014	Were olwoŋo win i yeyo me munyo oro Wach Maber ma wafuonjo win, ni wilim adech ma opok ri win kwoŋ dwoŋ pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo.
53002015	Amomiyo, jowotan, chungi win matek aka chwire win kwoŋ adyeri ma wafuonjo win adhok kodi i balwa mawan.
53002016	Weyi Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo won gipi, kodi Were Bawan, momaro wan aka i ŋono pere omiyo wan miseni makirum kodi geno maber,
53002017	wopoŋi chuny win miseni to miyo win men ma timo gi wacho gimoro jye maber.
53003001	Machowe, jowotan, kwayi win ri wan, ni mikwenda pa Ruoth womedere nyay mayot to limo dwoŋ, paka obedo i dyeri win.
53003002	Kwayi win bende ni Were wobothi wan kwoŋ jomarecho, rupiri kobedo ni dhano jye ni gi yeyo.
53003003	To Were genere, aka go bino miyo win men to kuro win maber kwoŋ Ŋatarach.
53003004	Wani gi geno kwoŋ win i Ruoth ni witimo gima waoro win, aka wibino medere gi timo ameno.
53003005	Weyi Ruoth womiyi wibedi gi mar pa Were i chuny win kodi chiro teko paka Kristo ochiro.
53003006	I nyingi Ruoth Yesu Kristo waoro win, jowotan mamaro; eye win kwoŋ jomoyeyo jye ma jotimo nyapo, ma jokimaki fuonji ma wamiyo win.
53003007	Kole wiwegi wiŋeyo maber ni wiripo luwo kwo ma wanyutho win. Wakibedo manyap munyo wanitye gi win,
53003008	aka wakichamo chiemo pa nyatoro ma wakichulo. Kuchiel, watiyo aka waol wor g'odyechieŋ ŋey wakiri wakeli peko ri nyatoro kwoŋ win.
53003009	Watimo ama ki rupiri wakiripi yenyo kwoŋ win kony; to watimo ameno ma miyo win ranen aluwa.
53003010	Ato munyo wanitye gi win wamiyo win chik ni, “Ŋata kimiti tich wokiri wochiemi.”
53003011	Wawacho ama rupiri wawinjo nike nitye jomogo i dyeri win ma jonyapnyap, ma jokitim gimoro jye kwanyo woko riyirok i tich pa wadi gin ayino.
53003012	I nyingi Ruoth Yesu Kristo waoro, odoko wakwayo ji ma pameno jowoyiki kiti gin, aka jowochaki tich, ŋey jowolimi gima konyo kwo pajo wegi.
53003013	Aka ri win, jowot wan, wikiri wioli gi timo gimotire.
53003014	Ka nyatoro ni kenyo ma kowinji mikwenda ma wadhiro ri win i balwa me, kaŋasa win go maber, aka wikiri witiyere gine, ŋeyi wiye wokwoti.
53003015	To wikiri witeri go paka jakwor, kuchiel fuonji win go paka omin win.
53003016	Weyi Ruoth won, ma poko syem, womiyi win syem hongo jye kodi i royo jye. Ruoth wobedi kodi dhano jye kwoŋ win.
53003017	An Paulo, andiko moth me gi chingan won, aka meno a ranyuth ma aketho i balwin paran jye. Me apaka andiko.
53003018	Weyi ŋono pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo wobedi gi wijojye.
54001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, jamoor pa Kristo Yesu ru or pa Were ma Jaboth mawan kodi Kristo Yesu mobedo geno mawan,
54001002	Ri Timotheyo, wuodan adyeri i yeyo: Weyi Were Bawan kodi Kristo Yesu Ruodhiwan womiyi win ŋono, wor gi syem.
54001003	Ayenyo ni ibedi Efeso paka aorin munyo oido anitye i woth paran achomo yu Masedonia. Juki joma kelo kenyo fuonji matwodo jowoweyi.
54001004	Wachi ri jo jowoweyi kigana ma kiniaŋere kodi bol moruwo ma nyingi kwarere jo, rupiri gino kelo pyem kendekende; jokikonyi chan pa Were, ma ŋeyere i yeyo.
54001005	Atoŋa ma or me obedo mar, aka wok i chuny molony, kodi i paro motire, kodi i yeyo maradyeri.
54001006	Jomogo joloko ŋey gin ri gikipiny me to jorwenyo royo pajo i pyem mamiŋo.
54001007	Joroda bedo jofuonji ma chik pa Were, to jokuya kir dwoŋ wach pajo wegi, kosa gikipiny ma joluwo kwoŋe gi miseni.
54001008	Waŋeyo ni Chik ber ka oor i royo motire.
54001009	Aka waŋeyo, nike chik kotim ri ji mabeyo, to ri joma turo chik kodi jowichtek, ri joma kilwor Were kodi jomarecho, ri joma kileŋ kodi joma kidewi kwoŋ Were; ri joma neko bachere pajo kodi megi jo, ri joma neko jowoti gin,
54001010	ri jomodakana, ri jomokom i timo gi wichkwot, ri joma tana ji, kodi jotwodo, gi joma wodho kony matwodo, kosa joma timo gimoro jye mopokere kodi fuonji motire
54001011	ma chungo kwoŋ Wach Maber ma di dwoŋ, ma Were moripo g'apaka oketho i chingan.
54001012	Afuoyo Kristo Yesu Ruodhiwan, momiyan men ma tich me, rupiri go oteran paka ŋata genere to kethan tiyo ri go,
54001013	kada chon oido aluwo kichar kwoŋe, kareno oido alwenyo gi ji pere munyo aluwo kichar kwoŋe. To Were otimo kodan wor, rupiri oido angoye gi yeyo aka oido akuya kir gima atimo.
54001014	Ruoth okonjo ran ŋono pere moasere to miyan yeyo gi mar ma nitye i Kristo Yesu.
54001015	Me obedo wach maradyeri, ma mitere ajola gi yeyo: ni Kristo Yesu obino i piny botho jomarecho. Aka aŋata aloyo i racho;
54001016	to ru wach me Were onyuthan wor, ŋey Kristo Yesu wonyuthi diyo ich pere i tiyo kwoŋan, ŋatarach maloyo jomarecho jye, paka ranen ri joma rumachien di joyeyo go to jolimo kwo makirum.
54001017	Ri Kere ma chil gi chil, ma kitho aka kinenere, mobedo Were kende, wor gi dwoŋ wobedi chil gi chil. Ameno.
54001018	Timotheyo, nyathi paran, amiyin or me ma ripo gi wach motuchi kwoŋin chon. Weyi wach no wobedi gilweny perin munyo ilwenyo lweny maber,
54001019	aka i chwire kwoŋ yeyo perin kareno paro ma chunyin otire. Jomegi jokowinjo paro ma chuny jo, to jonyieko woko yeyo pajo.
54001020	I dyeri jo nitye Himenayo kodi Alekizanda, m'atyeko bolo jo i men pa Sitan, ŋey wofuonji jo weyo luwo marach kwoŋ Were.
54002001	Amomiyo marapena, aoro win ywakirok ri Were, kwayo, poyo joman i kwayo, gi fuoyo Were ri ji jye;
54002002	kwayo ri kerin kodi joman jye ma jonitye i adhum, ŋey wabedi i kwo mokwe ma syem, munyo walworo Were aka wabedo gi kite ma ripere.
54002003	Gime ber aka sangala Were Jaboth mawan,
54002004	ma mito ni ji jye jowobothi to jolimo ŋeyo adyeri.
54002005	Kole Were nitye achiel, aka nitye ŋatachiel ma riwo Were gi ji, jal milwoŋo ni Kristo Yesu,
54002006	momiyere ma botho ji jye. Meno obedo giranena, i hongo motire, ni Were mito ji jye jowobothi.
54002007	Me amomiyo odiman bedo jamoor kendo jatiti wach ri Jopath, fuonjo mikwenda ma mako kwoŋ yeyo kodi adyeri. (Akitwodi, to awacho giradyeri!)
54002008	Amomiyo ayenyo ni kamoro jye ji jowokwayi, ma jomiyere ri Were aka jotiŋo chingi gin malo i kwayo, mongoye nge kosa kiŋunyaŋunya.
54002009	Kendo amito ni mon joworuki nengin mabeyo ma ripo, gi gwokirok; ma jokochowo paro pajo i kedo wich ma yodirok, kosa jaŋo kwoŋ gin thiwino ma zawabu kosa atege mawelo kosa ruk mawelo ma malo,
54002010	to jowobedi gi tim mabeyo paka ripere gi mon ma jowacho ni jolworo Were.
54002011	Mon joripo winjo fuonji munyo jokudere gi mwolo.
54002012	Akiyey mon fuonjo kosa bedo gi men kwoŋ chwo; joripo liŋ.
54002013	Kole otel chweyo Adam, aka nyaka ochwey Eva,
54002014	aka Adam k'amowondi; dhako ama owondi to turo chik pa Were.
54002015	To kada ameno, dhako bino limo both i nywolo nyithindho, ka go ochwire i yeyo kodi mar gi leŋo, kodi kurok maber.
54003001	Me wach motire: ka nyatoro wanya bedo jatel ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo, go wanya tich maber swa.
54003002	Jatel ripo bedo dhano mongoye gi komo; go ripo bedo jadhako achiel, moŋeyo kuro nge, ma niaŋ maber, ma timo gidwoŋ, moŋeyo jolo ji pecho pere; go ripo bedo ni nyalo fuonjo maber,
54003003	ma ki jamero kosa jagero, to wobedi ŋatamwol ma ki jadhaw; aka wokiri womari pesa.
54003004	Go ripo bedo ŋata nyalo tich ma pecho pere maber, to fuonjo nyithindho pere mwolo gi miyo ji dwoŋ.
54003005	Ato ka dhano kinyali tich ma pecho pere won, onyali nedi kuro kitipa pa jomoyeyo pa Were?
54003006	Go wokiri wobedi dhano ma nyaka owire manyien i yeyo; ameno go nyalo kwoto gi pakirok to ithumo ri go banja, paka othum ri Jwogi.
54003007	Go ripo bedo dhano ma ji ma woko jomiyo dwoŋ, aka nyaka kochay go to podho i bwo pa Jwogi.
54003008	Jokony ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo bende joripo bedo joma kiti jo otire, ma ki jotwodo; jokiri jowobedi jomero kosa jomawor i lim;
54003009	joripo chwire kwoŋ nyaliŋliŋ ma yeyo kodi paro motire.
54003010	Iripo temo jo kutho, aka ka jotire, nyaka jonyalo tich paka jokony.
54003011	Mon pajo bende joripo bedo ji ma kiti gin otire, ma jokiwerawera gi luwo kichar; joripo bedo jomoŋeyo kuro nge kendo joma genere i gimoro jye.
54003012	Jakony ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo ripo bedo jadhako achiel kende, aka jo kodi chiege joripo kuro nyithindho kodi pecho pajo maber.
54003013	Kole joma timo tich maber jolimo kachungo maber aka jonyalo luwo gi miseni kwoŋ yeyo ma nitye i Kristo Yesu.
54003014	Paka andiko balwa me rin, ageno bino nenin mayot,
54003015	to ka agalo, balwa me bino miyin iŋeyi kite ma waripo bedo gine i pecho pa Were, mobedo kitipa pa jomoyeyo pa Were makwo, siro kendo chakirok p'adyeri.
54003016	Mongoye kiganagana, nyaliŋliŋ mani yeyo mawan dwoŋ: Go onenere i chal pa dhano, Chuny Maleŋ onyutho paka go otire, aka jomalaika joneno go. Ofuonji kwoŋ go i piny jye, oyey go i piny gipi, aka oter go i polo.
54004001	Chuny wacho kamaler ni ji megi jobino weyo yeyo i ndir ma bino; jobino winjo chuny ma jotwodo to joluwo fuonji pa jwogi.
54004002	Fuonji no wok i twodo pa ji ma jorendere, ma paro ma chuny jo otho aka orere woko pa gima nyweny malyeth owaŋo.
54004003	Joma pameno jofuonjo ni nywom rach, aka jochiero ji chamo chiemo mogo. To Were ochweyo chiemo me achama, ma jomoyeyo aka joŋeyo adyeri jooro munyo jofuoyo Were.
54004004	Gimoro jye ma Were ochweyo ber; ongoye gima wochayi, to wojoli jye gi kwayo munyo ifuoyo Were.
54004005	Ato wach pa Were kodi kwayo miyo Were ketho silwany i gino.
54004006	K'ifuonjo jomoyeyo wach me, ibino bedo jatich maber mapa Kristo Yesu, modongo gi wach ma yeyo kodi fuonji ma go otyeko mako.
54004007	To weyi woko kigana ma Were ongoye iye, ma kiripere awacha. Bedi munyo ifuonjere kwo ma sangala Were.
54004008	Kada fuonjo del wobedi mochwiny nitye gi kony moro, to bedo gi kwo ma sangala Were ama nitye gi kony i royo jye, rupiri nitye iye chikirok ma kwo ma pama kodi ma bino.
54004009	Me wach motire ma ripo ajola kichutho.
54004010	Meno amomiyo watekere aka watiyo gi tekirok, rupiri waketho geno mawan i Were makwo mobedo Jaboth pa ji jye, to tektek mere apa jomoyeyo.
54004011	Wuodhi or aka fuonji gikipiny me.
54004012	Ikiri iyeyi moro wochayin ru thino perin, to bedi ranen ri jomoyeyo, i luwo, i kula, i mar, i yeyo kodi i lonyo ma chuny jo.
54004013	Ori hongo perin i kisoma ri ji Ndiiko Maleŋ, kodi fuonji nyuka anobin.
54004014	Ikiri ijala mich machuny ma ini gine, momiyin munyo jotuchi wach Were joluwo kwoŋe i ndir ma jodongo pa jomoyeyo joketh'iye chingi gin kwoŋin.
54004015	Kethi tich no jye i tim munyo imiyere ri jo, ŋey ji jye jowoneni paka tich perin kadho malo.
54004016	In won kaŋasa kwo perin, aka kaŋasa fuonji perin bende. Medere gi timo tich no, rupiri ka itimo ameno ibino bothere kir gi joma jowinjin bende.
54005001	Ikiri iay kwoŋ ŋata otegino gi gero, to nyuthi go wor paka d'itimo ri benin. Teri yach ma nyaka ay paka wutimerin,
54005002	mondongo paka megin, aka mon ma fuodi nyir paka nyimerin, gi leŋo jye.
54005003	Pari kwoŋ mon ma chwogi jo otho ma jonitye i chandirok.
54005004	Ka chi tho moro nitye gi nyithindho kodi nyikwaye, joripo kutho fuonjirok timo tich ma mako kwoŋ yeyo i pechin pajo, jowonyali konyo jonywol pajo, rupiri meno a gima sangala Were.
54005005	Dhako mobedo chi tho ma chandere, mongoye kodi jakur, wobedi dhako moketho geno pere i Were, aka ywakere ri Were noknok, ka kwayo go kony wor g'odyechieŋ.
54005006	To chi tho ma kethere yenyo girawanya meno otyeko tho, kada nende go kwo i del.
54005007	Miyi jo or me aka nyaka wongoye ŋata wopusa jo.
54005008	To ka nyatoro kipar kwoŋ wade pere, tektek mere joot pere won, meno otyeko kwedere kwoŋ yeyo aka rach loyo ŋata fuodi koyeyo.
54005009	Ikiri indiki nyingi chi tho moro ni wokwan go i kweth pa mon ma chwogi jo otho ka go fuodi kikal oro pyero auchiel. Kendo chi tho ma indiko ripo bedo ni oido konywomere ma kalo ka dichiel.
54005010	Kendo go ripo bedo ni oŋeyere ri tich mabeyo: dhako mokuro nyithindho pere maber, ojolo ji maber i ot pere, okonyo ji pa Were, okonyo joma ni teko, aka omiyere ri tich jye mabeyo.
54005011	To ikiri irwaki mon ma fuodi nyir i kweth pa mon ma chwogi jo otho; kole ka awanya pajo miy jo yenyo nywomirok, to jowiro ŋey gin ri Kristo,
54005012	gikenyo to joturo chikirok pajo marapena gine.
54005013	Medo kwoŋ meno, jonyalo fuonjere nyapo gi kula ma woth i dho udi pa ji; aka maloyo kenyo, jonyalo fuonjere kiwerawera gi luwirok kichar, gi bedo ma yilyil, gi luwo kwoŋ gima di kiripi jowoluwi kwoŋe.
54005014	Amomiyo, ayenyo ni mon ma chwogi jo otho kareno jo fuodi nyir jowonywomere, jowolimi nyithindho, aka jowokuri pechin pajo, ŋey jokiri jowomiyi jokwor mawan hongo ma luwo marach kwoŋ wan.
54005015	Kole mon megi ma chwogi jo otho jotyeko wirok aka onyo joluwo Sitan.
54005016	To ka dhako moro moyeyo nitye gi wade ma jobedo mon ma chwogi jo otho, weyi won wokonyi jo; wokiri wokeli peko ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo, aka ŋey kitipa wonyali konyo mon ma chwogi jo otho ma jochandere.
54005017	Jodongo ma jotiyo maber paka jotel, ripere miyo jo kemba ma romo, tektek mere joma asa timo tich ma tito wach gi fuonji.
54005018	Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Ikiri ichuli dhok mirikwa gi thach ka ywayo kwer furo,” odoko ni “Jatich jye ripo gi kemba pere.”
54005019	Ikiri iyey wach mokel kwoŋ jadwoŋ moro kwanyo woko ka ji aryo kosa adek joridho wach no.
54005020	Bwoki joma chwire i timo gimarach i dyer ji kamaler, ŋey joman lworo womaki jo.
54005021	I waŋ Were kodi Yesu Kristo, kodi jomalaika maleŋ, aorin ni winji fuonji me mongoye yero, aka ikiri itimi ri ji gimoro jye kareno idok yu thenge achiel.
54005022	Ikiri ikwakere ketho chingin i wiy nyatoro ri tich pa Were. Odoko ikiri iriwere gi moro i tim pere marecho; bedi m'ilony.
54005023	Onyo, ikiri imadhi pi kende, to bili ye vini manok ma konyo iyin gi toyo chiemo paka imaro two.
54005024	Gimarecho pa jomegi yot neno, aka bino miyo i thumo ri jo banja; to gimarecho pa joman nenere rumachien.
54005025	Meno bende apaka, tich mabeyo nenere kamaler; kendo kada jokothangere kamaler jokinyal panirok.
54006001	Ŋechin jye joripo tero ruodhe pajo paka joma ripere amiya dwoŋ, aka nyaka moro koluw marach kwoŋ nyingi Were kodi fuonji mawan.
54006002	Ŋechin ma ruodhe pajo joyeyo Kristo jokiripi chayo jo, rupiri jobedo jomoyeyo jowot jo. Kuchiel joripo tiyo ri jo maber loyo, rupiri joma limo kony kwoŋ tich pajo jobedo jomoyeyo momar. Iripo fuonjo gi tito gikipiny me.
54006003	Ŋata fuonjo fuonji mopokere aka kiyeyere gi wach motire mapa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo kodi fuonji kwoŋ lworo Were,
54006004	meno opoŋ gi pakirok kende, aka ongoye gim'oŋeyo. Go nitye g'awanya ma kiber ma pyem gi dhaw kwoŋ wach, aka me kelo nyieko, tyakirok, nyieko nyingi jo, kodi ŋicho kichar,
54006005	gi laro gikipiny i dyer ji ma paro pajo kitiy aka jongoye kodi adyeri. Joparo ni tich pa Were obedo royo ma limo ŋaŋo.
54006006	Kole nitye kemba madwoŋ ri dhano i lworo Were kodi i tero gima go ni gine paka romo go,
54006007	rupiri ongoye gima wakelo i piny, aka ongoye gima wabino kwanyo wok i piny ka.
54006008	Amomiyo, ka wanitye gi chiemo kodi ruk, meno won ripo romo wan.
54006009	To joma jomito ŋaŋo jopodho i karatem to jomoko i bwo pa awanya. Aka jodonjo i awanya mamiŋo ma kelo litho, ma tero ji i nyiekirok kodi i reyirok woko.
54006010	Kole maro pesa ama wok'iye recho ma nger jye. Jomegi jobedo g'awanya mathoth ri pesa amomiyo jopodho woko i yeyo aka jokelo gut madwoŋ i chuny gin.
54006011	To in, dhano pa Were, eye kwoŋ gikipiny no jye. Lwenyi ri tiro, lworo Were, yeyo, mar, chiro teko, kodi mwolo.
54006012	Temi paka inyalo lwenyo lweny maber mayeyo, aka inolimi kwo makirum; kole me a kwo ma Were olwoŋin iye munyo itucho maber yeyo perin i waŋ jomoneno mathoth.
54006013	I waŋ Were ma miyo gimoro jye kwo, kodi Kristo Yesu m'otucho maber yeyo no i waŋ Ponsyo Pilato, aorin
54006014	winjo gi kuro m'olony or pa Were ma bu racho, nyuka Ndelo ma Ruoth Yesu Kristo omenyer'iye.
54006015	Menyirok pere no Were won bino kelo i ndir pere, Were ma Jasilwany odoko won a Jadhum kende, Kere pa kerin, kendo Ruoth pa ruodhe.
54006016	Go kende ama kitho; go bedo i lero ma moro kinyal chore chiegin gine. Ongoye ŋata fuodi oneno go, odoko ongoye ŋata nyalo neno go. Ri go dwoŋ wobedi kodi men ma chil gi chil. Ameno.
54006017	Ori jomoŋaŋ i kwo ma piny me ni kiri jowokwoti, kosa ketho geno pajo kwoŋ gikipiny ma kigenere paka ŋaŋo, to kwoŋ Were ayino, ma poko wan gimoro jye ma kisangala mawan.
54006018	Ori jo timo gimabeyo, jowoŋaŋi i tich mabeyo, jowobedi jomiyo munyo jopoko gikipiny gi joman.
54006019	Ameno aka jobino choko ŋaŋo ma bino konyo jo i hongo ma bino, ŋey jowonyali limo kwo maradyeri.
54006020	Timotheyo, kuri maber gima okethi i chingin kuro. Eye i luwo ma kimakere gi Were kodi pyem kwoŋ “Ŋeyo wach,” mogo mamiŋo paka jomogo jolwoŋo ameno ma twodo,
54006021	rupiri jomegi joŋoyo ni jo ni gine, to gimowok'iye jorwenyo woko gi royo mayeyo. Ŋono wobedi kodi win.
55001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, jamoor pa Kristo Yesu i mito pa Were, moor tito kwo mochik ma wani gine i Kristo Yesu,
55001002	Ri Timotheyo wuodan mamaro: Weyi Were Bawan kodi Kristo Yesu Ruodhiwan womiyin ŋono, gi wor, kodi syem.
55001003	Afuoyo Were ma atiyo ri go gi paro ma chunyan molony, paka kwarere paran jotimo. Apoyin noknok i kwayo paran, wor g'odyechieŋ.
55001004	Ka apoyo pigi waŋin, amito nenin swa, ŋey kisangala wopoŋi i chunyan.
55001005	Apoyo yeyo perin mochwiny, kiti yeyo ma adhenin Loyi kodi yokin Yunisi oido jo ni gine, aka aridho nike i bende ini gine.
55001006	Ru wach no, apoyin inyali ketho i tim mich ma Were omiyin munyo aketho chingan kwoŋin.
55001007	Kole Were komiyo wan Chuny ma lworo, to omiyo wan Chuny ma bedo gi men, gi mar, kodi ma dhumo kwo mawan maber.
55001008	Amomiyo, ikiri ibedi gi wichkwot ma luwo kwoŋ Ruoth, kosa wichkwot kwoŋan, jatwech pere. Kuchiel bedi kodan i chandirok ri Wach Maber paka Were miyin men ma chiro,
55001009	go mobotho wan to lwoŋo wan bedo ji pere won, ki ru gima watyeko timo, to ru atoŋa pere won kodi ŋono. Go omiyo wan ŋono no i Kristo Yesu ma fuodi ndir kochakere,
55001010	aka pama onyo onyuth wan i menyirok pa Jaboth mawan, Kristo Yesu, motyeko reyo woko men pa tho, to kelo kwo gi kiyindira ma kirum i lero munyo oro Wach Maber.
55001011	Were ooran tito Wach Maber no paka jamoor kodi jafuonji;
55001012	meno amomiyo achandere ama. To kada ameno wiyan kikwoti, rupiri aŋeyo ŋata ayeyo kwoŋe, aka aridho ni go nyalo kuro gima atyeko miyo go nyuka Ndelo no tundo.
55001013	Chwire kwoŋ wach m'ityeko winjo bongan, paka fuonji motire aluwa, aka bedi i yeyo kodi i mar i Kristo Yesu.
55001014	Kuri gikipiny mabeyo mokethi i chingin gi kony pa Chuny Maleŋ ma nitye i wan.
55001015	Iŋeyo nike dhano jye i adech ma Asya ojwangan, kir Figelo kodi Hamogene.
55001016	Weyi Ruoth wonyuthi pecho pa Onesiforo ŋono, rupiri go omiyan kisangala ndir madit aka wiye kokwot nike anitye i twech.
55001017	Odoko tekin go tundo Roma, orangan tektek nyuka onwaŋan.
55001018	Weyi Ruoth womiyi go silwany ma limo ŋono bongi Ruoth i Ndelo no! Kole iŋeyo maber gima go otimo ran munyo anitye Efeso.
55002001	To in, wuodan, bedi gi men kwoŋ ŋono ma nitye i Kristo Yesu.
55002002	Teri wach m'iwinjan afuonjo ruwaŋ jokony mathoth ma jowinjo, aka ikethi i chingi ji ma genere, ma bende jobino nyalo fuonjo joman.
55002003	Chiri chandirok kodi wan, paka jaserikale pa Kristo Yesu ma genere.
55002004	Ongoye Jaserikale ma ruwere i wach pa ji ma kis ndelo, rupiri go mito kisangala jatel pere ma miyo go or.
55002005	Ameno bende, jaŋwech ma pyem kinyal limo kemba ka bende koluwo chik mere.
55002006	Jafur motyeko tiyo matek ripo limo pok marapena ma gima okech.
55002007	Pari kwoŋ gima awacho, aka Ruoth bino miyin ŋeyo dwoŋ gikipiny me jye.
55002008	Poyi Yesu Kristo, ma Were ochierino go kwoŋ jomotho, mobedo nyakwar Daudi. Me a Wach Maber ma afuonjo,
55002009	kendo ma achandere ri go aka onyo otweyan kir pa ŋata otimo kibenga madwoŋ. To wach pa Were kotwey i lijegere.
55002010	Amomiyo achiro gimoro jye ri bero pa ji pa Were moyer, ŋey jo bende jowonyali limo both ma nitye i Kristo Yesu, kanyachiel gi dwoŋ ma chil gi chil.
55002011	Me obedo wach motire: “Ka watyeko tho gine, wabende wabino kwo gine;
55002012	Ka wachiro chandirok, wabende wabino dhumo gine; Aka ka wakwedere kwoŋe, go bende bino kwedere kwoŋ wan;
55002013	ka wakibedo jomogenere, go doŋ ŋata ogenere, rupiri go kinyal won kwedirok kwoŋe.”
55002014	Bedi munyo ipoyo jo gikipiny me, aka wachi ri jo nyatirtir i waŋ Were ni kiri jowodhawere kwoŋ wach rupiri meno kikel bero moro, to nyieko ji ma jowinjo ayino.
55002015	Temi paka inyalo kisangala Were, paka jatich ma wiye kikwoti gi tich pere, aka fuonjo motire wach maradyeri mapa Were.
55002016	Eye i pyem ma Were ongoy'iye, rupiri meno bino miyo ji jomedere kwero lworo Were.
55002017	Gima jofuonjo bino bedo paka adhola modheth ma medo chamo del. Jofuonji aryo me a Himenayo kodi Fileto.
55002018	Jome jotyeko weyo adyeri aka onyo jomyeno yeyo pa joman munyo jowacho ni chierino pa ji otyeko bedo.
55002019	To tyendi geto mocwhiny ma Were otyeko ketho kiyengere, aka me a wach mondik kwoŋe: “Ruoth oŋeyo joma jobedo apere” kodi ni, “Nyatoro jye mobedo apa Ruoth ripo eye woko kwoŋ tim marecho.”
55002020	I ot malach nwaŋere achierin kodi atewe ma nger jye: megi obedo ma zawabu kodi feza, megi ma mbawo kodi lowo; megi aora i ndelo madwoŋ, to megi aora i ndelo ma kis ndir.
55002021	Ka moro olonyo kwo pere kwoŋ gikipiny marecho, go bino bedo achiero mioro i atoŋa madwoŋ, moketh gichien ri Ruoth aka ni gi kony ri go, rupiri oyikere woor go i tich mabeyo kendekende.
55002022	Amomiyo, weyi awanya ma thino, aka lweny ri tiro, yeyo, mar, kodi syem, kanyachiel gi joma kwayo Ruoth gi chuny gin molony.
55002023	To eye kwoŋ pyem mamiŋo kodi paro masisiri; ato iŋeyo nike gikipiny no kelo dhaw.
55002024	Jatich pa Ruoth kiripi bedo jadhawirok, to ripo bedo jawor ri ji jye. Ripo bende bedo ma nyalo fuonji kendo ma diyo chunye,
55002025	aka tiro joma pyemo gine gi mwolo. Kole nyalo bedo ni Were bino miyo jo hongo ma ŋuto to joŋeyo adyeri.
55002026	Gikenyo jobino bedo maryek to joboth kwoŋ bwo pa Jwogi, monwaŋo omako jo aka miyo jo timo gima go mito.
55003001	To ŋeyi gime: teko bino bedo madit i ndelo ma rumachien.
55003002	Ato ji jobino bedo jogwondo, jomawor i pesa, jokwoto, joyumirok, joyet, joma kiwinji jonywol pajo, joma kifuoy gimoro, joma kileŋ;
55003003	jobino bedo joma jongoye gi wor, joma jongoye gi chwak, jowachi nyingi wadi gin, jomawany kendo mager; jobino dak gimaber;
55003004	jobino bedo jokwedirok, joma kidew gimoro, joma kwot gi pakirok; jobino maro kisangala ma piny loyo Were;
55003005	jobino moko kwoŋ gima wiyewiye i yeyo Were, to jokwero men mere. Gwokere kwoŋ joma pameno.
55003006	Jomegi kwoŋ jo jodonjo i udi to jodiyo mon mamiŋmiŋ, ma jopoŋ gi recho aka awanya ma nger jye ywayo jo;
55003007	mon ma ndir jye jotemo fuonjirok to jokinyal ŋeyo adyeri.
55003008	Paka Janes kodi Jambure gin jopyemo gi Musa, ameno jono bende jopyemo kodi adyeri; jobedo ji ma paro pajo kitiy, aka yeyo odhyero jo.
55003009	To jokokadhi bor, rupiri dhano jye bino neno miŋo pajo, paka joneno apa chwo aryo no.
55003010	To ityeko kikaŋasa fuonji paran, kula paran, kodi atoŋa paran ma kwo; ityeko kikaŋasa yeyo paran, diyo chuny paran, mar paran, chiro paran,
55003011	lweny pa ji kodan kodi chandirok paran. Iŋeyo gikipiny me jye motimere ran Antyok, Ikoniam kodi Listura; Jye jobedo lweny mager ma achiro to Ruoth bothan kwoŋ jye no.
55003012	Iyadyeri dhano jye ma mito bedo gi kwo i Kristo Yesu, ji bino lwenyo gine.
55003013	Aka ji marecho kodi ma joraporapora jobino medirok gi recho, munyo jowondo jowoti gin kareno iwondo jo bende.
55003014	To in, medere i adyeri mofuonjin aka iyeyo m'ichwiny iye. Kole iŋeyo joma jofuonjin adyeri no,
55003015	gi paka wok i thino oido iŋeyo Ndiiko Maleŋ, ma nyalo miyin ryeko ma limo both kwoŋ yeyo Yesu Kristo.
55003016	Kole ndiiko jye Were ama omiyo men, aka konyo swa ma fuonjo adyeri, kipusa komo, tiro podho, gi fuonjo bedo gi kwo motire,
55003017	ŋey dhano ma tiyo ri Were wobedi ŋata ochowere maber, mani gi gikipiny ma timo tich mabeyo ma nger jye.
55004001	I waŋ Were kodi Yesu Kristo ma bino thumo banja ri ji jye, jomakwo kodi jomotho, odoko ru wach dwoko pere kodi bino pa Ker pere, aorin gi men moasere ni:
55004002	titi wach pa Were, kada ndir mere otundo kosa be, miyi ji niaŋ, pusa jo, medi jo miseni, aka fuonji munyo i diyo chunyin.
55004003	Kole ndir bino tundo ma ji jokowinj'iye fuonji maradyeri, to jobino tiyo g'awanya pajo wegi, odoko jobino choko jofuonji ma wegi joyenyo, jowofuonji jo gima ithi jo yilo jo winjo.
55004004	Jobino weyo winjo adyeri to joketho paro pajo kwoŋ kigana makichar.
55004005	To in, hongo jye iripo bedo milengela, chiro chandirok, timo tich pa jatiti Wach Maber ri joma fuodi jokoyeyo, aka timi tich perin jye paka jatich pa Were.
55004006	To an, onyo hongo otundo ran ma bedo rachow; hongo paran ma kadho otyeko tundo.
55004007	Atyeko lwenyo lweny maber, atyeko chowo ŋwech paran; atyeko kuro yeyo.
55004008	Aka pama onyo otyek yiko ran sangarya ma tiro, ma Ruoth, Jathumi banja motire, bino miyan i Ndelo no, aka ki an kendan, to go bino miyo ji jye ma jokuro go wonenere.
55004009	Temi paka inyalo bino bongan mayot.
55004010	Kole Dema omako mere gi piny ma pama aka onyo oweyan okadho yu Thesalonika. Kuresike okadho Galasya aka Tito okadho Dalmasya.
55004011	Luka kende ama ni kodan. Nwaŋi Marko ibin gine, rupiri go nyalo konyan maber.
55004012	Aoro Tichiko yu Efeso.
55004013	Ka ibino, keli ran kot paran ma aweyo Trowa gi Karupo; keli kitawin bende, tektek mere kitawo motim akwoya.
55004014	Alekizanda jathyeth otimo ran marach swa; Ruoth bino miyo go kemba ru gima go otimo.
55004015	Ibende gwokere kwoŋe, rupiri go opyemo swa kodi mikwenda mawan.
55004016	I kachako munyo alwenyo gi thyelo wach paran i kiosa, ongoye ŋata ochungo kabutan; ji jye joweyan. Akwayo ni Were wokiri wokwan kwoŋ jo recho no!
55004017	To Ruoth obedo kodan aka omiyan men, amomiyo anyalo tucho mikwenda jye ri Jopath jowowinji. Aka obothan i laki Simbwor.
55004018	Ruoth bino konyan i racho jye, to bothan ri Ker ma polo. Dwoŋ wobedi ri go chil gi chil. Ameno.
55004019	Adhiro moth ri Prisila kodi Akwila, kodi ri pecho pa Onesiforo.
55004020	Erasto odoŋ Korinthya; aka aweyo Trofimo i Mileto, rupiri go oido two.
55004021	Temi paka inyalo bino ma fuodi hongo ma piny ŋich'iye kotundo. Yubulo, Puden, Lino kodi Klaudya jodhiro rin moth pajo, odoko jomoyeyo jye bende jodhiro moth pajo.
55004022	Ruoth wobedi kodin. Ŋono pa Were wobedi kodi win.
56001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, jatich pa Were kendo jamoor pa Yesu Kristo. Oyeran aka ooran konyo yeyo pa ji pa Were moyer, gi telo jo jowoŋeyi adyeri ma kelo lworo Were,
56001002	mochungo kwoŋ geno kwo makirum. Were ma kitwodi, ochiko wan kwo me chon ma fuodi hongo kochakere,
56001003	aka munyo ndir mere otundo, go onyutho wach me. Okethi wach no i chingan, aka atito paka Were ma jaboth mawan ooran.
56001004	Andiko ri Tito, wuodan ma winjan i yeyo ma wariwo: Weyi Were Bawan kodi Kristo Jaboth mawan womiyin ŋono gi syem.
56001005	Aweyin Kurete ni itwenyi gikipiny ma fuodi oido okom, gi ketho jodongo ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo i tindi jye. Poyi ni:
56001006	jadwoŋ ma kitipa ripo bedo mongoye gi komo moro; go ripo bedo jadhako achiel, aka nyithindho pere joripo bedo jomoyeyo aka jokiri jowoŋeyere paka jomager kosa joma kiwinji or.
56001007	Ato paka go nitye i tich pa Were, jadwoŋ ma kitipa ripo bedo mongoye gi komo moro jye. Go wokiri wobedi jawinjirok, kosa jamaki nge kichar, kosa jamero, kosa ŋata ger, kosa jaworo.
56001008	Go ripo bedo jajoli wendo maber, ŋata omaro gimaber, ŋata dhumo kwo pere, motire, maleŋ, aka jakuri chik.
56001009	Go ripo chwire matek kwoŋ Wach Adyeri paka ofuonji go, ŋey bende wonyali fuonjo joman wach motire, gi juko woko pyem pa joma temo myeno wach no.
56001010	Kole jopyem mathoth bende jonitye, tektek mere Joyudaya ma jothumirok, ji ma luwo wach masisiri aka jowondo gine joman.
56001011	Yenyere juko fuonji pajo, rupiri joruwo pechin jye munyo jofuonjo gima onwaŋo jokiripi fuonjo, nyaka g'atoŋa ma limo pesa.
56001012	Achiel kwoŋ jo won, jatuchi wach pajo, owacho ni, “Ji ma Kurete jobedo jotwodo noknok, ogwange makichar, ma jowor aka jonyap.”
56001013	Aka gima ŋato owacho otire. Amomiyo, bwoki jo tektek, ŋey jowobedi gi yeyo molama,
56001014	aka odoko jokiri jowochwire kwoŋ kigana machon mapa Joyudaya kodi or pa ji ma jotyeko chayo adyeri.
56001015	Ri jomolony, gimoro jye olony; ri joma koch aka jokiyey, ongoye gima olony, rupiri paro pajo kodi niaŋ ma chuny jo oduwere.
56001016	Joŋoyo ni joŋeyo Were, to tim pajo nyutho ni jodak go. Jobedo jodakirok kendo joma kiwinji or, ma jokinyal timo gimaber.
56002001	To iripo fuonjo gima yeyere paka fuonji motire.
56002002	Wachi ri jodongo jowobedi joma dhumo chuny gin, joma ni gi kinen, jomaryek; jowobedi jomochwiny i yeyo pajo, i mar, kodi i chiro teko.
56002003	Aka bende wachi ri mon dongo jowobedi gi kite mabeyo i leŋo. Kiri jowobedi jowachi nyingi ji, kosa joma medho odhumo; joripo fuonjo gimabeyo
56002004	ŋey jowofuonji mon mathindho maro chwogi jo gi nyithindho pajo,
56002005	gi dhumo kwo pajo, kodi lonyo mongoye timo chot, to jobedo mon ma joŋeyo kuro udi, ma chuny jo beyo, ma jowinjo chwogi jo, ŋey moro wokiri woluwi marach kwoŋ Wach pa Were.
56002006	Odoko bende, fuonji yach ma nyaka ay manyien dhumo kwo pajo.
56002007	Aka in won, i gimoro jye, iripo bedo ranen ri jo i tich mabeyo, i fuonji perin, aka nyuthi jo m'iridho ni ifuonjo gimotire.
56002008	Ori wach motire ma moro kinyal kipusa, aka ŋey wichkwot womaki jokwor perin, rupiri jokonwaŋ gimarach awacha kwoŋ wan.
56002009	Fuonji ŋechin winjo ruodhe pajo gi temo kisangala jo i gimoro jye. Jokiripi pyem gi jo,
56002010	kosa kwalo jo. Kuchiel, joripo nyutho ni jobeyo aka jogenere, ŋey jowokeli bero ri fuonji kwoŋ Were ma Jaboth mawan, i gimoro jye ma jotimo.
56002011	Kole Were otyeko nyutho ji jye ŋono pere ma botho jo.
56002012	Ŋono no fuonjo wan weyo kwo ma kilwor Were kodi awanya ma piny, bedo gi dhumirok i kwo, bedo gi tiro, gi kwo molworo Were i piny ka,
56002013	munyo wakuro geno ma di silwany, gi menyirok madwoŋ mapa Were mawan madwoŋ moasere ma Jaboth,
56002014	Yesu Kristo, momiyere ri wan to botho wan kwoŋ recho jye, to loko wan ji molony ma jobedo apere won aka jochowere i timo gimabeyo.
56002015	Miyi ji ŋeyo gikipiny me, aka or men perin jye munyo imiyo joma winjin miseni aka bwoki jo ma tiro jo. Neni ni wongoye moro kwoŋ jo ma wochayin.
56003001	Poyi ji perin ni joripo mwolirok ri jodhum kodi ruodhe, winjo jo, gi yikirok timo gimoro jye maber.
56003002	Chieri jo luwo marach kwoŋ nyatoro, to jowobedi mongoye dhawirok, jomamwol, aka ndir jye jowonyuthi kite mabeyo ri ji jye.
56003003	Kole wan wegi onwaŋo yado wamiŋ, wajochay, aka oido orweny wan woko. Wan oido wabedo ŋechin pa awanya kodi kisangala ma piny; oido waoro kwo mawan ma timo ri ji racho kodi nyieko; oido wadakere gi ji.
56003004	To munyo bero kodi mar pa Were ma Jaboth mawan onenere,
56003005	go obotho wan; ki ru tich mabeyo mogo monwaŋo wawegi watyeko timo, to ru wor pere won. Go obotho wan gi lwok ma Chuny Maleŋ omiyo wan gine nywolirok manyien kodi kwo manyien.
56003006	Kole Were okonjo ri wan Chuny Maleŋ i thotho, luwo kwoŋ Kristo Jaboth mawan,
56003007	nike paka otyeko ketho wan i tiro gi ŋono pere, wanyali bedo nyithindho pere ma kayo kareno wageno lunjo kwo makirum.
56003008	Me wach maradyeri. Amito ni imedi ridho gikipiny me, ŋey nyaka jomoyeyo Were jowonyali miyirok i timo tich mabeyo. Gikipiny me beyo odoko di kony ri ji jye.
56003009	To weyi donjo i pyem mamiŋo, gi tito tyendi wat kwoŋ bol maboyo ma nyingi kwarere jo, tyakirok gi dhawirok kwoŋ Chik. Gikipiny me ongoy'iye chwee odoko ongoye kony.
56003010	Temi juko jakeli pokirok dichiel kosa diryo, aka rumachien ingoye kodi go gi tich.
56003011	Kole iŋeyo nike ŋata pameno okom, aka recho pere nyutho nike go won ochowo thumo banja pere.
56003012	Ka tekin adhiro Arutema kosa Tichiko bongin, itemi paka inyalo bino bongan i Nikopoli, rupiri atyeko yiko bedo kenyo i hongo ma pe ŋich'iye piny.
56003013	Temi paka inyalo konyo Zena japido ri chik kodi Apolo i woth pajo, aka ineni ni jonitye gi gimoro jye ma joyenyo.
56003014	Ji mawan joripo fuonjere timo tich mabeyo, ŋey jowolimi gikonyirok ma noknok aka nyaka jokiri jowobedi gi kwo mongoye kony.
56003015	Joma wani gi jo jye jodhiro ri win moth. Mothi ri wan ji jye ma jomaro wan i yeyo. Ŋono pa Were wobedi gi win.
57001001	Balwa mowok bongi Paulo, jatwech kwoŋbedo Kristo Yesu, kodi omin wan Timotheyo, Ri mere mawan kodi jatich nyawoti wan Filemon, kodi kitipa pa jomoyeyo Kristo ma romo i ot perin,
57001002	kodi nyamin wan Afiya, kodi jaserikale nyawoti wan Arukipo:
57001003	Weyi Were Bawan kodi Ruoth Yesu Kristo jowomiyi win ŋono gi syem.
57001004	Ndir jye ka apoyin i kwayo paran, omera Filemon, afuoyo Were
57001005	rupiri awinjo kwoŋ mar perin ri ji pa Were jye kodi yeyo m'ini gine i Ruoth Yesu.
57001006	Akwayo Were ni, riwirok mawan kodin paka jomoyeyo bino miyo wamedo niaŋ kwoŋ gimabeyo jye ma wanyalo timo ri Kristo.
57001007	Mar perin, omera ma kachunyan, okelo ran kisangala madwoŋ swa kodi miseni moasere! Kole ikelo kisangala i chuny ji pa Were jye.
57001008	Ru wach me, kada oido anyalo bedo gi miseni paka omerin i Kristo, ma orin timo gima ripere itim,
57001009	to akwayin ayino ru marok mawan kodin. An Paulo, jamikwenda pa Kristo Yesu aka onyo pama jatwech bende ri go,
57001010	akwayin ri wuodan Onesimo, ma alokere bamere i Kristo munyo anitye i twech.
57001011	Yu chien go oido ongoye gi kony rin, to pama go onyo ni gi kony rin kodi ran bende.
57001012	Onyo adwoko go rin, aka kadho kir gi chunyan.
57001013	Onwaŋo d'ayenyo kuro go bothan ka, wonyali konyan kaperin munyo anitye i twech kwoŋbedo Wach Maber;
57001014	to akimito timo ameno ma iwon ikiyeyo, ŋey gimaber mitimo wokiri wobedi gi mbaka, to wobedi gi paro perin won.
57001015	Kono miti oido ber ni Onesimo wokutho woeye bongin nyaka hongo machiek ŋey rumachien wodwoki bongin kichutho.
57001016	Kole go kobedo nyaka ŋecha, to loyo ŋecha swa: go obedo omerin ma kachunyin i Kristo. Go nitye gi kony ran swa! Aka go bino bedo gi kony rin swa loyo, paka ŋecha kodi omerin i Kristo!
57001017	Amomiyo k'iparo kwoŋan paka jatich nyawotin, joli go i dwoko pere paka d'ijolan.
57001018	K'inen go oido otyeko timo rin gimoro marach, kosa nitye gi giperin moro, onyo kwan kwoŋan.
57001019	An, Paulo, andiko gime gi chingan won: An Paulo, abino chulin. (D'akipoyin, ato, nike d'onyo iripo chulan i kwo perin bende)
57001020	Amomiyo, omera, mondo timi ran wor me, i Ruoth; sangala chunyan, paka omera i Kristo!
57001021	Aridho adyeri, munyo andiko gime, nike ibino timo gima akwayin, odoko ma kalo kir ma akwayin.
57001022	Medo kwoŋ meno, yiki reye kanindo, rupiri, ageno nike Were bino jolo kwayo mewin to dwokan ri win.
57001023	Epafura, ma nitye i twech kodan ru tich pa Kristo Yesu, dhiro rin moth,
57001024	kodi jotich jowotan Marko, Aristaruko, Dema, kodi Luka.
57001025	Weyi ŋono pa Ruoth Yesu Kristo wobedi kodi win.
58001001	I ndir mokadho, Were oluwo gi kwarere mawan di kweth i royo momore gi i dhoki jotuchi wach pere,
58001002	to i ndir machowe me, go oluwo gi wan gi i dhok Wuode m'oyero paka okayo ma le lunjo gikipiny pere jye, aka ochweyo piny gipi luwo kwoŋ Wuode no.
58001003	Go obedo lero ma nyutho dwoŋ pa Were; aka go obedo chal pa Were won gi kite, kendo go ama kuro chwech jye gi wach pere ma di men. Munyo go otyeko kelo lonyo kwoŋ recho jye, go obedo piny i polo yu chingi Jadhum Madwoŋ marachuch.
58001004	Ri ameno go olokere madwoŋ loyo jomalaika, paka nyinge ma Were omiyo go loyo apa jo.
58001005	Were otyekoye wacho ri malaika mene ni, “In Wuodan: Konon alokere Benin”? Kosa ri mene ni, “Abino bedo Bamere, aka go bino bedo Wuodan”?
58001006	Medo kwoŋ meno, munyo Were oido chiegin oro Wuode makayo i piny ka, owacho ni, “Weyi jomalaika pa Were jye jowolami go.”
58001007	Aka me a gima Were owacho kwoŋ jomalaika: “Were loko jomalaika pere koyo, aka go loko jotich pere lew mach.”
58001008	To kwoŋ Wuode, Were owacho ni, “Kom perin madhum, a Were, bino kiyindira chil gi chil, aka tiro ama ibino dhumo gine i Ker perin.
58001009	Imaro gimotire aka idak recho, amomiyo Were, ma Were perin, owirin gi mo ma kisangala to miyin dwoŋ makalo ma go omiyo jowotin.”
58001010	Go owacho kendo ni, “A Ruoth, i chakirok ichweyo piny, aka polo meno jye tich ma chingin otimo.
58001011	Gikipiny no jye jobino leny woko, to in idoŋ; jojye jobino ti pa nanga.
58001012	Iledolo jo pa kot; odoko ilewiro chal pajo pa nengin. To in idoŋ adoŋa paka initye, kendo oro perin kibino rumo.”
58001013	Were owachoye ri malaika mene ni, “Bedi yu rachuch paran chuka anoloki jokwor perin paka kasik ma ketho tyendin”?
58001014	Jomalaika meno ki chuny ma jotiyo ri Were, ma go ooro konyo joma jobino limo both?
58002001	Amomiyo, waripo chwirok matek kwoŋ adyeri ma watyeko winjo aka nyaka gimoro korweny wan.
58002002	To k'inen mikwenda ma jomalaika chango jomiyo oter paka otire, aka ŋata kotiyo gine i ndir no omiy girachula moripo gine,
58002003	onyo wanobothi nedi ka wachayo both madwoŋ me? Ruoth won gipi ama otelo luwo kwoŋ both me, aka nyaka joma jowinjo go joridho ri wan ni obedo adyeri.
58002004	Aka Were bende omedo ridho wach no gi ranyuth, gi men, gi giraura mopokere opokere, gi mich pa Chuny Maleŋ m'opoko paka won oyenyo.
58002005	Kole Were koketho jomalaika bedo jodhum i piny ma bino yuwaŋe.
58002006	Kuchiel, owach kamoro i Ndiiko Maleŋ ni, “Dhano bende aŋo, a Were, ma d'ipar kwoŋe? Dhanadhana bende aŋo, ma d'idew kwoŋe?
58002007	Iloko go nyaka ma hongo machiek bedo mapiny loyo jomalaika, to imiyo go dwoŋ gi wor,
58002008	aka iketho gimoro jye i par tyende ni wodhumi.” “Iketho gimoro jye i par tyende”, me nyutho ni go dhumo gimoro jye. To pama fuodi wakinen paka dhano dhumo gimoro jye.
58002009	To kole waneno Yesu, ma i hongo machiek oloki go mapiny loyo jomalaika, paka orwaki ri go sangarya ma dwoŋ gi wor rupiri ochandere i tho, ni ŋey kwoŋ ŋono pa Were go wonyali tho ri ji jye.
58002010	Onwaŋo otire ri Were, mochweyo aka kuro gimoro jye, miyo Yesu ma telo ji i both, chowo tich no gi chandirok, ŋey wote mathoth jowolimi dwoŋ.
58002011	Ato ŋata loko ji maleŋ kodi joma iloko jo maleŋ, jye jo ni gi Baa gin achiel. Amomiyo Yesu ongoye gi wichkwot lwoŋo jo ni wutimin go.
58002012	Go owacho ni, “Were, abino luwo kwoŋin ri wutimera. Abino pakin i chokirok pajo.”
58002013	Go odoko owacho ni, “Abino ketho geno paran i Were.” Aka owacho kendo ni, “Ee anika gi nyithindho ma Were omiyan.”
58002014	Paka nyithindho obedo ma del gi remo, Yesu bende olokere paka jo i del, aka nyaka i tho pere woreyi woko Jwogi, manitye gi men kwoŋ tho,
58002015	ŋey wogonyi ji moido jobedo ŋechin ru lworo tho.
58002016	Kole gime neno kamaler ni ki jomalaika ama go konyo, to paka Ndiiko wacho, “Go konyo nyikway Ibrayimu.”
58002017	Ri ameno, onwaŋo yenyere go wolokere paka wutimin i royo jye, ŋey go wobedi jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar mani gi wor kendo magenere i tich pere ri Were, aka nyaka wogeŋi keme pa Were ri gimarecho pa ji ŋeyi wochwak jo.
58002018	Aka go onyo pama nyalo konyo joma jolimo ratem, rupiri go won bende olimo ratem aka ochandere.
58003001	Ri ameno wutimere maleŋ, ma bende Were ama olwoŋo, kethi paro mewin kwoŋ Yesu, mobedo jamoor kendo jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, ma konyo yeyo ma watucho ni wani gine.
58003002	Kole go ogenere ri Were, moyero go timo tich me, paka Musa bende oido ogenere i tich pere i ot pa Were gipi.
58003003	Kuchiel Yesu ripo gi dwoŋ maloyo apa Musa, paka jageri ot dwoŋ loyo ot ma go ogero.
58003004	Ato ot jye dhano ama gero, to Were ama ogero kis gimoro.
58003005	Aka Musa chango obedo ŋatogenere i ot pa Were paka jatich, aka otucho gikipiny ma Were oido kidho luwo kwoŋe rumachien.
58003006	To Kristo ogenere paka Wuodi Were ma kuro ri Were ot. Aka kole waŋati wabedo ot pere ka wamedere gi miseni mawan kodi ridho geno ma wapakere gine.
58003007	Kole Chuny Maleŋ wacho ni, “Ka wiwinjo dwondi Were konon,
58003008	wikiri witimi wichtek paka chango witimo munyo ji mewin jokwedere kwoŋ Were, i hongo ma ratem i dyeri thim
58003009	kama kwarere mewin joteman iye, kada oido jotyeko neno tich paran.
58003010	Gino ama omiyo amako nge gi jono, to awacho ni, ‘Ndir jye chuny jo kelo ri jo rwenyo, aka fuodi jokuya royo paran.’
58003011	Amomiyo amako nge t'akwoŋere ni, ‘Jokonyal donjo i ywomirok paran!’ ”
58003012	Kure win, jowotan, aka moro kwoŋ win wokiri wobedi gi chunye marach ma kiyey ma eye woko kwoŋ Were makwo.
58003013	Kuchiel, wiripo kweyo chuny wadi win kis ndelo, tekin ilwoŋo ndelo no ni “konon,” ŋey moro kwoŋ win wokiri wowondi gi gimarach to lokere ŋata wiye tek.
58003014	Kole wajojye wabedo jowoti Kristo, ka wachwire matek i yeyo tundo i gike.
58003015	Me a gima ndiiko wacho: “Ka wiwinjo dwondi Were konon chuny win wokiri wobedi matek paka chango obedo munyo wikwedere kwoŋ Were.”
58003016	To kere ŋa gin ma chango jowinjo dwondi Were to jokwedere kwoŋ go? Jokobedo ji jye ma Musa owodho wok Misiri?
58003017	Kere jokune ma Were omako gi jo nge chowo oro pyero aŋwen? Go komako nge gi ji ma jotimo gimarach, omiyo jogore piny to jotho i dyeri thimi?
58003018	Aka Were okwoŋere gi jokune ni jokodonji i ywomirok pere ma kiweno joma jotimo ri go wichtek no?
58003019	Onyo waneno ni jokonyalo donjo rupiri jokoyeyo.
58004001	Onyo, Were otyeko weyo ri wan chikirok nike wanyalo donjo i ywomirok pere. Amomiyo, wagwokere win, aka moro kwoŋ win wokiri wokeŋi donjo i ywomirok no.
58004002	Kole wabende watyeko winjo Wach Maber, paka jo; to wach ma jowinjo kotimo ri jo bero moro, rupiri munyo jowinjo jokojolo gi yeyo.
58004003	Amomiyo wan ma wayeyo, wadonjo i ywomirok no paka Were owacho ni, “Amako nge t'akwoŋere ni, ‘Jokibino donjo i ywomirok paran!’ ” Meno a gima go owacho, kada tich pere oyido orumo wok chuka go chweyi piny.
58004004	Me a gima owachere kamoro i Ndiiko Maleŋ kwoŋ ndelo marabiryo: “Were oywomere i ndelo marabiryo kwoŋ tich pere jye.”
58004005	Aka kenyo odoko owach'iye ni, “Jokibino donjo i piny ma d'amiy'iye jo ywomirok!”
58004006	Joma jopen winjo wach pa Were jokonyalo nwaŋo ywomirok no; rupiri jokoyeyo amomiyo nitye joman moyey jo limo kaywomirok me.
58004007	Aka Were odoko oketho ndelo man milwoŋo ni, “konon,” ma chango oluwo kwoŋe rumachien gi i dhok Daudi, i wach motyek nyutho ni, “Ka wiwinjo dwondi Were konon, wikiri wichayi go,”
58004008	rupiri bedi Yoswa tyeki miyo ji ywomirok, di Were koluwo kendo kwoŋ ndelo man.
58004009	To paka nitye, fuodi odoŋ ri ji pa Were ywomirok ma Sabato.
58004010	Kole dhano jye ma donjo i ywomirok pa Were bende won ywomere kwoŋ tich pere paka Were chango oywomere kwoŋ tich pere.
58004011	Amomiyo, weyi watemi paka wanyalo donjo i ywomirok no. Kiripi moro kwoŋ wan chayo dwondi Were paka jotimo, to wakeŋ donjo.
58004012	Kole wach pa Were kwo aka tiyo. Bith loyo abor ma nyalewe aryo. Thumo kir kama paro kodi chuny jorom'iye, gi kama kumbo kodi more joriwer'iye. Niaŋ kwoŋ awanya kodi paro pa ji ma iyi adundo.
58004013	Ongoye gima nyalo panere ri Were. Gimoro jye i chwech othangere aka oyare i waŋe go ma wabino tito kwo mawan ru waŋe.
58004014	Weyi wachwire matek kwoŋ yeyo ma watucho ni wani gine, paka kere wanitye gi jadwoŋ mapa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, moasere gi dwoŋ mobedo Yesu Wuodi Were won, motyeko kidho i polo.
58004015	Jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, mawan me, kobedo ŋata kiniaŋi nyapo mawan. Kuchiel, wanitye gi jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar ma bende olimo ratem i royo jye paka walimo, to kotimo gimarach.
58004016	Amomiyo, weyi wabedi miseni, aka wakidhi ru nyim kom pa Were madhum, kama ŋono nity'iye. Kenyo wabino lim'iye wor to wanwaŋo ŋono ma nyalo konyo wan i hongo ma wayeny'iye.
58005001	Kis jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar jye iyero wok kwoŋ ji aka imiyo go tich ma tiyo ri Were kapa jono. Go chwayo ri Were mich kodi rachow ru gimarecho pa ji.
58005002	Paka go won bende nyap i royo momore, go nyalo tiyo gi mwolo ri jomanyap ma jonyalo rwenyo.
58005003	Aka paka go won nyap, go chowere ki nyaka ri gimarecho pa joman kende, to ri gimarecho pere bende.
58005004	Aka ongoye ŋata won yero dwoŋ ma bedo jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar; bedo ri lwoŋo pa Were won, paka chango olwoŋ Aron.
58005005	Meno apaka Kristo won bende komiyere dwoŋ ma bedo jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar. Kuchiel, Were ama owacho ri go ni, “In i Wuodan; konon alokere Benin.”
58005006	Go owacho kendo kaman ni, “Ibedo jachwayi ri Were wi alitar chil gi chil, i chal pa Melikizedek.”
58005007	I kwo pere i piny ka, Yesu odhiro kwayo kodi ywakirok pere gi pigi waŋe munyo koko malo ri Were, ma d'onyalo botho go kwoŋ tho. Aka Were owinjo go, rupiri go oido ŋatamwol ma winjo Were.
58005008	Kada go oido obedo Wuodi Were, go ofuonjere winjo Bamere i chandirok pere.
58005009	Aka munyo otyek lonyo go kichutho, go olokere jakeli kwo makirum ri ji jye ma jomako wach pere;
58005010	aka Were oketho go bedo jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar i chal pa Melikizedek.
58005011	Nitye wach kweth ma wanyalo wacho kwoŋ gime, to tek tito ri win, rupiri wibolbol i niaŋ gimifuonjo win.
58005012	Kabedo ma di wibedi jofuonji, odoko fuodi yenyere moro wofuonji win ayino adyeri pa Were michako gine! Kama di wichamiye chiemo pa jomotegino, fuodi wiyenyo chak amadha ayino!
58005013	Ŋata madho chak, meno fuodi nyathi ma kuya poko gimotire kodi gima kotire.
58005014	To chiemo manwaŋ, obedo apa jomotegino ma jotyeko ŋeyo poko gimabeyo gi gimarecho.
58006001	Amomiyo, weyi wamedere gi fuonji motegino waweyi woko fuonji machako ma mako kwoŋ Kristo, aka wakiri wagiki kendo i fuonji machako: kole wiŋeyo paka wiripo ŋuto kwoŋ tich mothootho to wimedere gi yeyo Were.
58006002	Watyeko fuonjo win kwoŋ batisimo kodi ketho chingi jo kwoŋ ji; kwoŋ chierino pa jomotho kodi thumo banja ma chil gi chil.
58006003	Weyi wakidhi yu malo. Aka meno a gima wabino timo ka Were oyeyo.
58006004	Aka tek swa dwoko jomopodho miyo jo ŋuto kendo, rupiri yado onwaŋo jonitye i lero pa Were, aka jobilo kir mich ma polo to jolimo pok pajo ma Chuny Maleŋ.
58006005	Jotyeko bilo bero ma Wach pa Were kodi men ma bino bedo i hongo ma bino yuwaŋe.
58006006	To ka jopodho, dwoko jo kendo i ŋuto bedo gimatek, rupiri joguro Wuodi Were kwoŋ musalaba kendo aka jothango go kamaler ri wichkwot i waŋ ji.
58006007	Lowo ma madho koth ma chwe noknok aka dongo gimatwi ma konyo joma jopidho ama Were miyo silwany.
58006008	To lowo ma kelo kudhin kodi doy meno bu kony: odamba ri kwoŋ, aka rumachien ibino waŋo woko.
58006009	To kada waluwo ama, merin mawan ma swa, wageno ri win gikipiny mabeyo ma both kelo.
58006010	Were kobedo ŋata chunye kotire. Wiye kibino wil kodi tich ma wityeko timo, kosa mar ma wityeko nyutho go i kony ma wimiyo i konyo ji pere aka fuodi wimedere konyo jokristo jowoti win.
58006011	Wamito ni kis dhano kwoŋ win wonyuthi kinen no kir i gike, aka nyaka gikipiny ma wigeno bino bedo adyeri.
58006012	Wakimiti nike wilokere manyap, to bedi win paka joma joyeyo ma jodiyo chuny jo nyuka jolimo gima Were otyeko chiko.
58006013	Munyo Were otimo chikirok kodi Ibrayimu, okwoŋere munyo oro nyinge won paka oido ongoye nyatoro maloyo go gi dwoŋ.
58006014	Go ochiko ni, “Abino miyin silwany ma limo nyikwayin mathoth.”
58006015	Aka munyo Ibrayimu okudere to kuro, go olimo gima Were ochiko.
58006016	Kole dhano ka kwoŋere oro nyingi nyatoro maloyo go gi dwoŋ, aka kiti kwoŋirok no chowo pyem jye i dyeri ji.
58006017	Onyo Were bende omito nyutho joma oido jokidho limo gima go ochiko, maber moloyo, nike go kibino wiro atoŋa pere, amomiyo go omedo ridho chikirok no kodi kwoŋirok.
58006018	Were ooro gikipiny aryo me (chikirok kodi kwoŋirok) ma kinyal wire, odoko ma go kinyal twodo kwoŋe, ma nyutho gino. Amomiyo wan ma watyeko limo kagoŋirok bonge wanyalo nwaŋo miseni madwoŋ ma chwirok matek kwoŋ geno moketh ruwaŋ wan.
58006019	Wanitye gi geno me paka loch ma juko yee mol, ri chuny wan, mogur piny to moko matek, aka donjo to kalo woko nanga molyer ma Ot pa Were ma polo kir denge i kisika maleŋ ma iye.
58006020	Yesu otyeko telo donj'iye ri wan kawaŋ wan, paka jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar chil gi chil i chal pa Melikizedek.
58007001	Melikizedek me oido obedo kere ma Salem kodi jachwayi ri Were Madwoŋ Maloyo. Munyo Ibrayimu oido dwoko i lweny ma go onek'iye kerin mogo kenyo Melikizedek oromo gine to miyo go silwany.
58007002	Gikenyo, Ibrayimu omiyo go achiel wiy apar ma gimoro jye moido go ni gine. (Dwoŋ nyingi Melikizedek marapena obedo, “Kere ma Tiro.” Aka go oido odoko obedo kere ma Salem, ma dwoŋ mere nyutho ni, “Kere ma Syem.”)
58007003	Kotuchi baa Melikizedek kosa yokimere, kosa moro kwoŋ kwarere pere; kotuchi nywolirok pere kosa tho pere. Go chalo Wuodi Were mobedo jachwayi ri Were chil gi chil wi alitar.
58007004	Wineno paka go onwaŋo dwoŋ? Kir Ibrayimu mobedo kwari nono jye omiyo go achiel kwoŋ apar ma gimoro jye ma go onyaga i lweny.
58007005	Kole Chik yeyo nyikway Levi ma jobedo jochwayi ri Were wi alitar choko achiel wiy apar ma gikipiny kwoŋ ji ma Israel. Meno nyutho ni jochoko kwoŋ ji pajo wegi, kada bende jobedo nyikway Ibrayimu.
58007006	Melikizedek me konywolere i nono pa Levi, to ochoko achiel wiy apar kwoŋ Ibrayimu aka omiyo go silwany paka ŋata oido ni gi chikirok pa Were.
58007007	Mongoye kiganagana, ŋata miyo silwany dwoŋ loyo ŋata limo silwany pere.
58007008	To ma mako kwoŋ jachwayi ri Were wi alitar, waneno ni Jolevi ma chango jochoko achiel wiy apar ma lim jobedo jomatho, to ma mako kwoŋ Melikizedek, ŋata kwo paka ndiiko wacho ama choko.
58007009	Wanyalo wacho ni munyo Ibrayimu ochulo achiel wiy apar, nyutho ni Levi (ma nyikwaye jochoko achiel wiy apar) bende ochulo gino luwo i chingi Ibrayimu,
58007010	rupiri Levi oido fuodi konywol paka go oido fuodi nitye kwoŋ kwarimere Ibrayimu munyo Melikizedek oromo kodi Ibrayimu.
58007011	Chungo kwoŋ tich pa Jolevi ma chwayo ri Were wi alitar ama owodh'iye Chik ri ji ma Israel. Onyo ka tich pa Jolevi oido ber, iraŋo odoko jachwayi ri Were wi alitar man oyenyere ma chale gi Melikizedek, ma kiweno kodi Aron?
58007012	Kole ka owir chik ma yero jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, meno wirok ripo bedo i Chik pa Musa bende.
58007013	Aka Ruodhiwan miluwo kwoŋe gikipiny me, oido janono mopokere; aka ongoye janono pere moro jye moido otyekoye tich paka jachwayi ri Were wi alitar.
58007014	Kole oŋeyere maber paka Ruodhiwan onywolere i nono pa Yuda; aka Musa kotucho nono me munyo luwo kwoŋ jochwayi ri Were wi alitar.
58007015	Wach no omedo nyuthirok kamaler rupiri jachwayi ri Were wi alitar man onenere, ma chalo Melikizedek.
58007016	Kokethi go bedo jachwayi ri Were wi alitar i chik ma mako kwoŋ bol ma nywolirok pa ji; go olokere jachwayi ri Were wi alitar i men pa ŋata ni gi kwo mongoye gike.
58007017	Ato ndiiko wacho ni, “Ibino bedo jachwayi ri Were chil gi chil wi alitar, i chal pa Melikizedek.”
58007018	Amomiyo, chik machon oketh gichien, rupiri oido nyap aka ongoye kony.
58007019	Kole Chik pa Musa di konyalo loko gimoro molony kichutho, to pama otyek kelo geno maber ma miyo wan tundo bongi Were.
58007020	Aka gino kotimere mongoye kwoŋirok mere bende. Joman jye olok jo jochwayi ri Were wi alitar mongoye kwoŋirok moro.
58007021	To Yesu olokere jachwayi ri Were wi alitar i royo ma kwoŋirok, munyo Were owacho ri go ni, “Ruoth okwoŋere aka kowir paro pere: ‘Ibedo jachwayi ri Were wi alitar chil gi chil.’ ”
58007022	Amomiyo, kwoŋirok no loko Yesu paka raridh ma ridho chikirok maber maloyo machon.
58007023	Nitye kendo pokirok man: joman ma jochwayo ri Were wi alitar no, oido jomore rupiri oido jotho ma jokonyalo medirok gi tich pajo.
58007024	To paka Yesu kwo chil gi chil, tich pere paka jachwayi ri Were wi alitar odoko kikodi ri ŋat man.
58007025	Amomiyo, go nyalo botho kichutho joma kidho bongi Were kodi bonge, rupiri go kwo chil gi chil ma pido gi Were ri jo ndelo jye.
58007026	Jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, ma kite no, ama nyalo konyo wan i gima wayenyo. Ato go leŋ, ongoye kodi kibenga kosa gimarach moro, olony, mopok kwoŋ jomarecho, aka otiŋ go malo kalo polo.
58007027	Go kichal jodongo pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar man; go kiyenyere chowirok wi alitar ndelo jye: ni kutho ri gimarecho pere won, aka nyaka wochowere ri gimarecho pa joman bende. Go ochowere wi alitar dichiel kende to ma kichutho, munyo go won omiyere paka rachow.
58007028	Chik pa Musa ketho dhano mobedo gimanyap bedo jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar; to wach ma kwoŋirok pa Were, mobino rumachien yu ŋey Chik, oketho Wuodi Were won m'otyek loko molony kichutho chil gi chil.
58008001	Me a gima dwoŋ kwoŋ gima wawacho: Wanitye gi jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, ma kiti dwoŋ pere omiyo go bedo yu rachuch ma kom madhum pa Were Madwoŋ Maurere i polo.
58008002	Aka go tiyo paka jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar i Kabedo Maleŋ Moasere, mobedo wema maradyeri ma Ruoth ama ogero, ma kiweno dhano.
58008003	Kis jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar jye okethi ni wochwayi mich kodi lee paka rachow ri Were: amomiyo jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar me bende oido ripo bedo kodi gi mich mamiyo.
58008004	Bedi go nitye i piny ka, di kibedi jachwayi ri Were wi alitar, rupiri nitye joman ma jochwayo mich i Chik pa Joyudaya.
58008005	Jono jochwayo i kalamo pa Joyudaya mobedo nyaka chal kodi tipo pa gima nitye i polo. Meno amomiyo ochik Musa munyo go oido chiegin gero wema pa Were ni, “Neni nike itimo gimoro jye i chal monyuthin wi got.”
58008006	To, paka nitye, omiy Kristo tich ma bedo jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar madwoŋ swa loyo apa jo, paka chikirok ma go otimo i dyer ji kodi Were bende ber loyo machon, kwoŋbedo ochungo kwoŋ chikirok ma gikipiny mabeyo loyo.
58008007	Bedi racho moro oido ongoye i chikirok marapena, di mararyo koyenyere.
58008008	To Were onwaŋo racho kwoŋe amomiyo owacho ni, “Ruoth wacho ni hongo bino, ma abino tim'iye chikirok manyien gi Joisrael kodi jonono pa Yuda.
58008009	Chikirok no kibino bedo paka m'atimo gi kwarere pajo munyo amako chingi jo t'awodho jo woko i piny Misir, rupiri jokobedo gi genirok kwoŋ chikirok m'atimo gi jo, amomiyo aeye kwoŋ jo.
58008010	Onyo me a chikirok ma abino timo gi ji ma Israel ka ndelo no okadho, abino ketho chik paran i paro pajo, odoko abino ndiko chik no i chuny jo to abedo Were pajo, aka jobino bedo ji paran.
58008011	Ongoye moro kwoŋ jo ma bino fuonjo nyawote kendo kosa wacho ri nyawote ni: ‘Ŋeyi Ruoth,’ rupiri jojye jobino ŋeyan, wok kwoŋ ŋata oasa thin tundo kwoŋ ŋata oasa dwoŋ.
58008012	Abino chwako recho pajo, aka akibino poyo gimarecho pajo kendo.”
58008013	Munyo oluwo kwoŋ chikirok manyien me, Were oloko marapena cha gima orumo tich; aka gimoro jye morumo tich aka otyeko ti, bino reyere woko.
58009001	Chikirok marapena oido nitye gi chik ma lamo Were kodi kalamo ma dhano ama ogero.
58009002	Oger wema ma Were bed'iye ama: I kisika marapena oido nitye giketho tala, meza, kodi mugat michwayo ri Were. Kenyo oido ilwoŋo ni Kabedo Maleŋ.
58009003	Yuŋey nanga mararyo oido nitye kisika milwoŋo ni Kabedo Maleŋ Maloyo.
58009004	Kenyo oido nitye alitar ma zawabu miwaŋ'iye buban, kodi sanduku ma chikirok, moum thenge jye gi zawabu. I sanduku no oido nitye atawo ma zawabu gi manu i iye kodi luth pa Aron ma boke oloth kwoŋe, kodi telin aryo mondik kwoŋe wach ma chikirok.
58009005	Wi sanduku oido nitye Chierubim aryo ma nyutho dwoŋ pa Were, ma joyaro bwombi jo kama ichwak'iye gimarecho kenyo. To me k'a hongo ma tit'iye gimoro jye.
58009006	Munyo otyek timo chan me jye, jochwayi ri Were wi alitar bin jodonjo i diro mawoko ndelo jye timo tich pajo;
58009007	to jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar kende ama oido donjo i kisika ma iye aka bin timo ameno dichiel i oro achiel. Go kidonji mongoye remo ma go kidho chwayo ri Were kwoŋ gimarecho pere won kodi gimarecho pa ji ma jotimo munyo jokuya nike oido jotimo gimarach.
58009008	Gi gikipiny me jye, Chuny Maleŋ oido nyutho ji nike royo ma donjo i Kabedo Maleŋ Maloyo oido fuodi koyaw ri ji.
58009009	Gino oido obedo chal ma nyutho ndir ma pama. Dwoŋ mere ni rachow ma mich kodi lee moido ichwayo ri Were kinyal miyo chuny ŋata lamo Were bedi molony kichutho.
58009010	Jobedo nyaka chiemo, giramadha, kodi tim momore ma lonyo del. Gino jye oido obedo nyaka chik mawoko, monwaŋo tiyo nyaka tundo ndir ma chikirok manyien oido kidho chaker'iye.
58009011	Aka Kristo obino paka jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar, ma gikipiny mabeyo ma pama nitye, amomiyo wema ma go tiy'iye ŋon mochowere aka di dwoŋ moasere (ji ama jokotimo, odoko kobedo ma chwech me).
58009012	Kristo kodonjo i Kabedo Maleŋ Maloyo gi remo dyegi kodi rochi chwayo jo wi alitar; to okwanyo remo pere won ama odonjo gine i kabedo no, aka dichiel ma kichutho, to nwaŋo ri wan gine kwo makirum.
58009013	Kole remo dyegi kodi apa thwondhe, kodi buru pa roya mowaŋ tikiro kwoŋ joma oido jokolony paka chik yenyo, olonyo jo munyo kwanyo woko chilo mawoko i chik ma nyadin.
58009014	Kosa to remo pa Kristo momiyere i leŋo chungo kwoŋ tich pa Chuny ma chil gi chil, nyalo lonyo paro ma chuny wan kalo kenyo didi, kwoŋ tim mothootho, ŋey watiyi ri Were ma kwo!
58009015	Ru wach me Kristo obedo jatimi chan ma miyo chikirok manyien wotiyi, ŋey joma Were olwoŋo jowonyali limo silwany ma Were ochiko. Kole go otyeko tho paka chul ma gonyo ji woko kwoŋ kibenga ma jotimo munyo oido jonitye i chikirok marapena.
58009016	Kama nitye'iye wach pa jatho m'ondiko, ripere bedo gima nyutho ni ŋato otyeko tho adyeri.
58009017	Ato ndiiko no ongoye kony ka fuodi won mere kotho, aka kitiy ka ŋato fuodi kotho.
58009018	Meno amomiyo chikirok marapena koridhi ma remo fuodi ongoye mooy.
58009019	Munyo Musa otyeko wacho ri ji or jye paka oketh i Chik, okwanyo remo rochi to ruwo gi pi, to kiro kwoŋ kitawo ma Chik kodi kwoŋ ji jye gi changwe m'obil, kodi lwodo ma yer rombo mobokere.
58009020	Aka go owacho ni, “Me a remo ma tweyo chikirok ma Were ooro win mako.”
58009021	I royo achiel, Musa okiro remo kwoŋ wema ma Were bed'iye kodi kwoŋ gikipiny jye moido ioro ma lamo Were.
58009022	Ato, i Chik pa Musa, chiegin kis gimoro iripo lonyo gi remo; aka gimarecho oido kichwak ka remo fuodi kooy.
58009023	Gikipiny me, ma jobedo nyaka chal ma gikipiny ma polo, onwaŋo ripere lonyo jo i kite no. To gikipiny ma polo yenyo rachow mabeyo loyo meno.
58009024	Ato Kristo kodonjo i kabedo maleŋ ma ji ama jotimo, mobedo nyaka chal pa kabedo maradyeri mere. Go odonjo i polo won kama go pama ochung'iye ri wan ruwaŋ Were.
58009025	Jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar mapa Joyudaya yado donjo i Kabedo Maleŋ Maloyo gi remo ma kobedo apere won kis oro. To Kristo kodonjo i polo miyirok kis oro be.
58009026	Kole di go ochandere dikweth wok chuka chwey piny. To, go onenere dichiel ma kichutho, i giki ndir ma rumachien, ma kwanyo woko gimarecho chungo kwoŋ rachow ma kwo pere won.
58009027	Paka oketh ri dhano jye tho dichiel, to Were thumo ri go banja,
58009028	apaka Kristo bende ochway go dichiel paka rachow ma kwanyo woko gimarecho pa ji kweth; aka go odoko bino nenirok mararyo, ki ma tiŋo gimarecho kendo, to ma botho joma jokuro go ayin.
58010001	Chik pa Joyudaya obedo nyaka chal ma riprip mapa gikipiny ma lebino, to kobedo gimaradyeri mere won, ma gikululu ma lebino. Amomiyo kiti rachow no, mimiyo ma kikee oro gi oro, kinyal loko joma chore bongi Were molony kichutho.
58010002	Bedi kiti rachow no oido nyalo lonyo joma lamo Were ma kichutho, di ji jokoweyo tero mich ma chowo recho, kareno jokiwinji banja i chuny jo ru gimarecho kendo? Kole joma onwaŋo jolamo Were di jolony dichiel kichutho, mongoye kendo winjo banja i chuny jo.
58010003	To paka nitye, kiti chowirok no poyo ji gimarecho pajo ayino kis oro,
58010004	rupiri remo thwondhe kodi dyegi kinyal kwanyo woko gimarecho.
58010005	Ru wach me, munyo Kristo obino i piny, owacho ri Were ni, “Rachow kodi mich ikiyeny, to del m'iyiko ran ayino.
58010006	Mich awaŋa ma lee kodi mich machowo gimarecho, ikisangala gine.
58010007	Gikenyo awacho ni, ‘Anika, a Were, ma timo gima iyenyo ni atimi, paka ondik kwoŋan i kitawo ma Chik.’ ”
58010008	Munyo go otyeko wacho ni, “Rachow kodi mich awaŋa ma lee kodi mich machowo gimarecho ikiyeny.” (Me mich mimiyo paka Chik yenyo.)
58010009	Gikenyo to go medo ni, “Anika, a Were, ma timo gim'iyenyo ni atim.” Amomiyo, Were otyeko kwanyo woko gichowirok machon jye to ketho manyien.
58010010	Aka Yesu Kristo otyeko timo gima Were omito ni go wotimi, amomiyo wajojye onyo olok wan molony kwoŋ gimarecho i chowirok ma go otimo ma delkwoŋe won, dichiel kende to kichutho.
58010011	Jachwayi ri Were wi alitar mapa Joyudaya jye chungo aka timo tich pere kis ndelo aka chwayo rachow ma nger achiel di kweth. To kiti rachow me kinyal kwanyo woko gimarecho.
58010012	To Kristo ochwayo rachow achiel ri gimarecho dichiel kende to bedo piny yu rachuch pa Were.
58010013	Wok i hongo no, go onyo kuro Were wokethi jokwor pere paka kasik ma ketho tyende.
58010014	Amomiyo, gi rachow ma go ochwayo dichiel no, go otyeko lonyo kichutho joma onyo pama ilonyo jo kwoŋ gimarach.
58010015	Kole Chuny Maleŋ bende ridho wach me. Marapena go wacho ni,
58010016	“Me a chikirok ma abino timo gi jo: Rumachien ma ndelo no; Ruoth wacho: abino ketho chik paran i chuny jo, aka abino ndiko i paro pajo.”
58010017	Go odoko omedo ni, “Akibino odoko poyo gimarecho pajo kodi tim pajo marecho.”
58010018	Aka kama gimarecho me otyek chwak'iye, mich ma kwanyo woko gimarecho odoko kibino yenyere.
58010019	Amomiyo, jowotan, wanitye gi syem mopoŋ donjo i Kabedo Maleŋ swa kwoŋ tho pa Yesu.
58010020	Go oyawo ri wan royo manyien, royo ma kwo i nanga mageŋo kisika, mobedo delkwoŋe won.
