58010021	Paka wanitye gi jachwayi ri Were wi alitar madwoŋ ma kuro Ot pa Were,
58010022	onyo weyi wachore chiegin gi Were, gi chuny wan jye, gi yeyo mochowere, gi chuny motyek lonyo m'odoko kiwinji banja, gi del molwok gi pi molony.
58010023	Weyi wachwire matek kwoŋ geno ma wawacho ni wani gine, rupiri ŋata omiyo chikirok ogenere.
58010024	Aka weyi wapari win kwoŋ jowoti wan, munyo wakonyere i nyutho mar gi timo bero ri jowoti wan.
58010025	Wakiri waweyi kite ma romo kanyachiel, paka joman onyo jokethere timo. Kuchiel, weyi wamiyere miseni, konda ni Ndelo pa Ruoth onyo chore chiegin.
58010026	Kole ongoye rachow man m'odoko bino kwanyo woko gimarecho ka watimo gimarecho atoŋa mato oido watyeko ŋeyo adyeri.
58010027	Kuchiel, gimodoŋ a lworo gima bino timere: thumo banja kodi mach mager mabino reyo woko joma pyemo gi Were.
58010028	Kole ŋata kiwinji Chik pa Musa ineko mongoye wor ka otyek thumo banja loyo go, chungo kwoŋ jokony aryo kosa adek ma joridho ni go otimo recho.
58010029	Onyo wiparo ni ŋata chayo Wuodi Were, to tero paka gima sisiri remo ma chikirok pa Were moloko go maleŋ, aka miyo Chuny ma kelo ŋono nge, di ripi gi girachula marach loyo didi?
58010030	Kole waŋeyo ŋata owacho ni, “Abedo jachuli kwor, abino chulo kwor,” ma bende owacho ni, “Ruoth bino thumo banja ri ji pere.”
58010031	Obedo gilworo madwoŋ swa ka nyatoro opodho i chingi Were makwo!
58010032	Poyi win paka oido winitye i ndir mokadho, munyo wijolo lero pa Were, aka wichandere i royo momore, to lweny no kolacho win.
58010033	Ndir megi oyet win ruwaŋ ji to ichando win; aka ruman wichungo kodi joma ichando jo marach ameno.
58010034	Wimako wor gi jomotwey i jera, aka munyo omay win lim mewin wichiro teko no gi kisangala, rupiri oido wiŋeyo ni winitye gi gimabeyo loyo meno, ma yindira chil gi chil.
58010035	Amomiyo wikiri wiboli woko miseni mewin, rupiri bino kelo ri win kemba madwoŋ swa.
58010036	Wiripo chiro chandirok, ŋey witimi gima Were yenyo to wilimo gima go ochiko.
58010037	Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Odoŋ nyaka hongo machiek won ŋata ripere bino wobin kendo kogal.
58010038	Ji paran ma jotire, jobino kwo i yeyo. Ka moro kwoŋ jo ogiki chien, akosangala gine.”
58010039	To wakibedo ji ma jogik chien to jorwenyo. Kuchiel wabedo joma bedo gi yeyo to jolimo both.
58011001	Onyo bedo gi yeyo meno ŋeyo adyeri nike wabino limo gikipiny ma wageno, bedo gi ridho ni wabino limo gikipiny ma wakinen.
58011002	Yeyo pajo amomiyo ji ma hongo mokadho jolimo pak bongi Were.
58011003	Yeyo ama miyo waniaŋ nike Were am'ochweyo polo gi piny munyo wodho or, momiyo gima nenere ochwey wok kwoŋ gima kinenere.
58011004	Yeyo amomiyo Abel ochwayo ri Were rachow maber loyo apa Kain. Yeyo omiyo go onwaŋo pak bongi Were paka dhano motire munyo Were ofuoyo mich pere. Aka yeyo ama miyo Abel fuodi luwo kada otyeko ri go tho.
58011005	Yeyo ama ogeŋo Enoka tho. Kuchiel, oter go malo bongi Were, aka moro konyalo nwaŋo go, rupiri Were oido otyeko kadho gine. Ndiiko wacho ni ma fuodi koter Enoka malo, go oido otyeko kisangala Were.
58011006	Ongoye ŋata nyalo kisangala Were ma bu yeyo. Kole ŋata bino bongi Were ripo bedo gi yeyo nike Were nitye aka miyo joma rango go kemba.
58011007	Yeyo ama omiyo Nowa owinjo wach pa Were kwoŋ gikipiny ma go oido fuodi koneno. Go owinjo Were, to geto yee ma go gi pecho pere joboth'iye. Ru yeyo pere go okwero recho moido timere i piny, aka olimo bongi Were tiro mawok i yeyo.
58011008	Yeyo ama omiyo Ibrayimu winjo munyo Were olwoŋo go, to kidho i piny ma Were ochiko miyo go. Oweyo piny pere munyo kiŋey ni laro yu kune.
58011009	Ru yeyo pere, go obedo i piny ma Were ochiko go igani jawiloka. Go obedo i wema paka Isaka kodi Yakobo jotimo, ma bende jolimo chikirok bongi Were.
58011010	Kole Ibrayimu oido kuro tindi ma Were ama oyiko gi gero; tindi ma tyendi geto mere yindira.
58011011	Yeyo amomiyo Ibrayimu olokere baa jo kada go oido oti aka Sara oido kinyal limo nyithindho. Go ogeno Were ni bino kuro chikirok pere.
58011012	Kada go oido chalo p'otho, wok kwoŋ ŋatachiel me nyithindho onywolere mathoth paka michalin ma polo, mathoth paka nyingi kwoyo ma dho nam.
58011013	Ji me jye chango jotho i yeyo. Jokolimo gima Were ochiko, to joneno gikipiny me gi bor to jojolo, aka joyeyo kamaler nike jo oido jobedo jowiloka ma chale pa jomobwok koth i piny.
58011014	Ji ma jowacho gikipiny me jonyutho kamaler nike jorango piny pajo wegi.
58011015	Jokoparo piny ma joweyo; bedi jotimi ameno di jolimo hongo ma gik.
58011016	Kuchiel, oido jowanya piny maber loyo, mobedo piny ma nyapolo. Amomiyo Were wiye kikwoti lwoŋirok ni Were pajo, rupiri otyeko yiko ri jo tindi.
58011017	Yeyo amomiyo Ibrayimu, munyo Were otemo go, ochwayo wuode Isaka paka rachow. Ibrayimu, ma Were oido otyeko kir timo gine chikirok, oyeyo miyo wuode paka rachow.
58011018	Were oido otyeko kir chiko go ni, “Ibino limo nyikwayin kwoŋ Isaka.”
58011019	Ibrayimu oparo nike Were nyalo chierino dhano kwoŋ jomotho. Amomiyo i kite ma luwo, chal pa Ibrayimu ojolo Isaka munyo wok bongi jomotho.
58011020	Yeyo ama omiyo Isaka omiyo Yakobo gi Esau silwany i kwo pajo ma yuwaŋe.
58011021	Yeyo ama omiyo Yakobo omiyo nyithindho pa Yozefu silwany ma fuodi go kotho; othenere kwoŋ luth pere to lamo Were.
58011022	Yeyo omiyo Yozefu munyo chiegin tho, oluwo kwoŋ eye pa Joisrael i piny Misir, to weyo wach kwoŋ gima joripo timo gi delkwoŋe.
58011023	Yeyo amomiyo jonywol pa Musa jokano go dwe adek munyo otyek nywolo go, rupiri oido joneno nike go nyathi maŋon, aka jokolworo chayo or pa kere.
58011024	Yeyo amomiyo Musa, munyo odongo, okwero nike wokiri wolwoŋi go ni wuodi pa nyapa Farawo.
58011025	Go ofuoyo chandirok gi ji pa Were loyo bedo i syem ma gimarach chowo nyaka hongo machiek.
58011026	Go oparo ni chandirok yet ri Kristo onwaŋo ber loyo ŋaŋo ma Misir; rupiri go oido oketho waŋe kwoŋ kemba ma bino.
58011027	Yeyo amomiyo Musa oweyo Misir ma kolworo nge pa kere; go ochiro rupiri oido neno Were ma kinenere.
58011028	Yeyo amomiyo go oketho chik ma kalima ma Kadho, gi wodho or ni wokiri remo kwoŋ thigin, aka nyaka malaika ma tho wokir woneki nyithindho pa Joisrael ma kayo.
58011029	Yeyo omiyo Joisrael jokalo Malawa Mobokere igani wi lowo mothwo; munyo Jomisir jotemo timo ameno, pi omwonyo jo woko.
58011030	Yeyo omiyo kor chiel ma Yeriko ogore piny munyo Joisrael jothoko chiel no chowo ndelo abiryo.
58011031	Yeyo omiyo Rahab ma oido tana delkwoŋe i timo gi wichkwot, oboth aneka gi joma jokwero winjo Were, rupiri go ojolo jopendo maber.
58011032	Onyo anomedere kendo wacho aŋo? Hongo kiromi ran ma luwo kwoŋ Gidyon, Balak, Samson, Jefutha, Daudi, Samwir, kodi jotuchi wach.
58011033	Yeyo omiyo jolwenyo gi piny pa jowiloka momore to joloyo lweny. Jotimo gimotire to jolimo gima Were ochiko jo; jochulo kir dhok simbwor,
58011034	joneko woko mach mager, to joboth aneka g'abor. Jo oido jonyap to jolokere jomen. Jolokere matek i lweny to jonyalo woko lwak jolweny pa jowiloka.
58011035	Yeyo omiyo ochierino ri mon ji pajo monwaŋo jotho. Joman ochandi jo to jokwero woko kir syem, to jotho i litho ŋey wochierino jo i kwo maber loyo.
58011036	Joman oyet jo tichwado jo, aka joman otwey jo gi lijegere tibolo jo i jera.
58011037	Ogoy jo gi telin; obar jo dyere to jopokere aryo, oneki jo kodi abor. Jothoko piny i pyen rombo gi dyegi munyo jonitye i chandi, olweny gi jo, to itimo jo marach.
58011038	Piny oido kiber ri jo odocho! Jolera i dyeri thim kodi wi gote, munyo jobedo i ŋungu kodi i buche piny.
58011039	Jome jye Were ofuoyo jo ru yeyo pajo, to kada ameno jye jokolimo gima Were ochiko,
58011040	rupiri Were oido oridho ri wan chan maber loyo. Atoŋa pere oido obedo nike jono bende woloki jo molony kichutho kiromo gi wan.
58012001	Amomiyo, paka onyo wanitye gi lwak jokony madwoŋ mothoko wan ameno, onyo weyi wakwanyi woko gimoro jye ma riwere ri wan i royo, kodi gimarecho ma mito moko kwoŋ wan matek,
58012002	wakethi win waŋ wan kwoŋ Yesu ma yeyo mawan chungo kwoŋe wok i chako tundo i gike. Go ochiro musalaba ru kisangala monwaŋo kuro go yu waŋe; koparo kwoŋ wichkwot ma tho kwoŋ musalaba oido kidho kelo ri go, kendo onyo pama obedo yu rachuch ma kom madhum pa Were.
58012003	Pari kwoŋ go, paka ochiro kiti teko no wok kwoŋ jomarecho, ŋey wikiri winyapere to chuny win ŋedhere.
58012004	Kole i lweny mewin gi gimarecho fuodi wikitundo i tho.
58012005	Chalo wiy win owil gi wach ma kelo miseni ma Were luwo gi win paka nyithindho pere ni, “Wuodan, ikiri ichayi girachula ma Were tirin gine, aka ikiri inyochere ka go ay kwoŋin.
58012006	Kole Ruoth fuonjo dhano ma go omito, aka miyo moro jye ma go tero paka wuode girachula!”
58012007	Chiri win chandirok mewin paka gima fuonjo win, rupiri chandirok mewin nyutho nike Were tero win paka nyithindho pere. Nitye nyathi ma bamere kimiy girachula ma temo tiro go?
58012008	Ka wikilimi girachula paka nyithindho man jye, meno nyutho ni wikibedo nyithindho pere maradyeri, to nyithindho ma woko ayino.
58012009	Aka kis dhano kwoŋ wan onwaŋo wani gi bachere mawan ma jomiyo wan girachula aka wamiyo jo dwoŋ. Onyo di waripi mwolirok ma rom nedi ri Baa chuny wan to walimo kwo!
58012010	Bachere wan jotemo tiro wan gi girachula, i hongo machiek paka joneno ni otire ri jo; to Were miyo wan girachula ma tiro wan ma bero mawan, ŋeyi wopoki wan ye leŋo pere.
58012011	Ka imiyo dhano girachula ma tiro go, i hongo no girachula no chali ri go gimoro ma kiber, ma kelo litho ayino, to rumachien, jomotweny jo gi girachula ma kite no jolimo kemba gi syem ma kwo motire.
58012012	Tiŋi win malo chingi win monudere no, aka weyi win chongi win wobedi mochwiny!
58012013	Hongo jye wothi win i royo mopyele maber ri tyendi win, ŋey kama oŋol wokiri womedi ukirok, to wochangi ayino.
58012014	Temi win paka winyalo bedo i syem gi ji jye, gi woth i kwo ma leŋo, rupiri ongoye ŋata bino neno Ruoth ma bu leŋo.
58012015	Gwokere win ŋey moro wokiri wokeŋi limo ŋono pa Were, kendo moro wokiri wolokere pa yath ma kech ma medere dongo to nyieko wadi gi kecho pere.
58012016	Gwokere win ŋey moro wokiri wolokere jachot kosa ŋata kigen Were paka chango Esau, motana woko silwany pere ma lunjo lim paka nyathi ma kayo nyaka ru chiemo dichiel.
58012017	Wiŋeyo paka go rumachien otemo yenyo silwany pa Bamere; to okwer miyo go, rupiri go konyalo nwaŋo royo ma wiro paro pa bamere, kada otemo ywako kir gi pigi waŋe.
58012018	Fuodi wikitundo, paka Joisrael, bongi gima winyalo geyo, paka got Sinai mani gi mach malyel; fuodi wikitundo i mudho gi kidisa pa piny gi koyo,
58012019	gi derino ma dwondi gwara, kosa kama di derino ma dwondi nyatoro, ma munyo ji jowinjo jokwayo ni jokiri jowowinji wach man kendo,
58012020	rupiri jokonyalo chiro gimowachi ni, “Ka kada ogwaŋ ogeyo got no, ripere wogoy gi tele chuka wotho.”
58012021	Gima joneno kenyo onwaŋo miyo jo lworo momiyo Musa owacho ni, “Kole akirin aka lworo omakan!”
58012022	Kuchiel, wibino wi Got Zayun kodi i tindi pa Were makwo, Yerusalem ma nyapolo, gi jomalaika mere gana gi gana.
58012023	Wibino i kweth pa jomoyeyo Kristo ma jobedo nyithindho pa Were makayo mondik nyingi jo i polo. Wibino bongi Were mobedo jathumi banja ri ji jye, kendo bongi chuny ji ma jotire moloki jo maleŋ.
58012024	Wibino bongi Yesu, mochano chikirok manyien, kodi gi bongi remo ma nyutho wach maber loyo remo pa Abel.
58012025	Amomiyo, gwokere win aka wikiri wikweri winjo ŋata luwo. K'inen joma jokwero winjo ŋat'oluwo munyo fuonjo jo kwoŋ gwokirok i piny ka jokoboth, onyo waŋati wanobothi nedi ka wawiro ŋey wan ri ŋata luwo mowok i polo ma mito ni wagwokere!
58012026	I hongo no dwonde oyengo piny, to i hongo ma pama go ochiko ni, “Odoko abino yengo ki nyaka piny kende, to polo bende.”
58012027	Wach me ni, “Odoko,” nyutho maber ni ibino yengo gi ŋilo woko gikipiny mochwey, aka nyaka gikipiny ma kiyengere ama bino doŋ.
58012028	Amomiyo, rupiri wakidho limo ker ma kinyal yengere, weyi wafuoyi win Were to walamo go i royo ma sangala go, gi bwonirok gi lworo;
58012029	kole Were mawan obedo mach ma rego woko gikipiny.
58013001	Medere win gi marok paka wutimere i Kristo.
58013002	Wiyi win kiri wowili gi jolo jowiloka i pechin mewin; kole nitye jomogo ma jotyeko timo ameno to jojolo jomalaika ma jokoŋeyo.
58013003	Poyi win joma nitye i twech igani winitye i twech gi jo. Poyi win joma chandere, igani wichandere gi jo.
58013004	Ji jye joripo miyo nywomirok dwoŋ, aka jachwo gi dhako joripo kurok i nywomirok pajo i leŋo, rupiri Were bino thumo banja ri jochot kodi jomaturo chik ma nywomirok.
58013005	Kuri win kwo mewin ma wikimunyere i maro pesa, aka gima wini gine woromi win. Kole Were owacho ni. “Akibino weyo win; akojala win.”
58013006	Weyi wabedi miseni, to wawacho ni, “Ruoth obedo jakony paran, akibino bedo malwor! Aŋo ma dhano nyalo timo ran?”
58013007	Poyi win jotel mewin machon, ma jotito ri win wach pa Were. Pari win paka kwo pajo obedo aka wimaki kiti yeyo pajo.
58013008	Yesu Kristo kiwire nyoro, konon, kodi chil gi chil.
58013009	Wikiri wiyeyi fuonji mopokere ma kotire woywayi win wok i royo motire. Ber ka chuny wan onwaŋo men wok i ŋono pa Were, ma kiweno i kuro chik ma mako kwoŋ chiemo, ma kikony kada joma kuro chik ago.
58013010	Wanitye kodi alitar ma chowirok ma joma chwayo ri Were i wema ma nyayudaya koyey chiem'iye.
58013011	Jadwoŋ pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar ma nyayudaya tero remo lee i Kabedo Maleŋ Moasere to chwayo paka rachow ri gimarecho; aka riŋo lee no iwaŋo woko ma kambi pa ji.
58013012	Amomiyo Yesu bende otho woko ma waŋkach ma tindi, ŋey wolwoki woko gimarecho pa ji gi remo pere won ma miyo ji leŋo.
58013013	Amomiyo, weyi wakidhi bonge woko ma kambi pa ji wabedi kanyachiel gine i wichkwot pere.
58013014	Ato tindi ma yindira ongoye ri wan i piny ka, to kwanyo woko warango tindi mabino ayino.
58013015	Amomiyo, weyi hongo jye wachwayi pak ri Were paka rachow mawan i Yesu Kristo, ma chali olemo ma nyak wok i dhok wan ka watucho nyinge.
58013016	Wiy win wokiri wowili gi timo bero kodi konyo jowoti win gi gima wini gine, rupiri kiti rachow no ama sangala Were.
58013017	Winji win jotel mewin, odoko bedi win ma wimwol ri jo, rupiri jo jokuro win paka joma ripo tito ri Were kite ma jotiyo gine. Ka wiwinjo jo, aka jobino timo tich pajo gi kisangala; ma kiweno gi chuny jo mochile, aka meno kinyal konyo win.
58013018	Kwayi win ri wan ma wikikeŋ. Waŋeyo ni paro ma chuny wan otire, aka wamito timo gimotire hongo jye.
58013019	Aka amedo kwayo win ni bedi win munyo wikwayo Were wonyali oran bongi win mayot.
58013020	Onyo weyi Were ma jasyem, mochierino Ruodhiwan Yesu kwoŋ jomotho, Yesu mobedo Jakwath roombo Madwoŋ ru remo pere ma ridho chikirok makirum,
58013021	womiyi win gimaber ma wiyenyo ŋey witimi gima go mito. Weyi go wotimi i wan gima sangala go i Yesu Kristo, aka dwoŋ wobedi ri go chil gi chil. Ameno.
58013022	Akwayo win, jowotan, winjo mikwenda ma amiyo gine win miseni me ma widiyo chuny win; kole balwa ma andiko ri win me obedo nyaka machiek.
58013023	Amito wiŋeyi ni omin wan Timotheyo otyek gonyo i twech. Ka go obino mapiyo, alebino gine neno win.
58013024	Mothi ri wan jotel mewin kodi ji pa Were jye. Jowoti wan ma Italya bende jodhiro ri win moth pajo.
58013025	Weyi ŋono pa Were wobedi gi wijojye.
59001001	Balwa mowok bongi Yakobo, jatich pa Were kodi apa Ruoth Yesu Kristo, Ri nonin apar g'aryo, ma jotyakere i piny gipi: Amotho win!
59001002	Jowotan, teri win paka silwany ka wiromo gi teko momore omore,
59001003	rupiri wiŋeyo ni ka yeyo mewin otem aka wok'iye men ma chiro gimoro.
59001004	Chiro ripo chowo tich pere i kwo mewin aka ŋey winyali tegino i yeyo ma wichowere, munyo wikichandi gimoro.
59001005	To ka moro kwoŋ win chando ryeko, go ripo kwayo Were, mamiyo dhano jye gimoro ma kobuyo kendo ma koŋunyaŋunya, aka bino miyin.
59001006	To ŋato ripo kwayo gi yeyo, ma koganagana, rupiri ŋata ganagana chalo pi ma tula i nam ma koyo kwadho aka wito koro.
59001007	Ŋata pameno wokiri wopari nike bino limo gimoro bongi Ruoth,
59001008	kwoŋbedo go ni gi paro aryo, aka kiridhi paro i gimoro jye ma go timo.
59001009	Omin ma jachandi wosangala gi kabedo momiy go mamalo i yeyo,
59001010	aka omin ma jaŋaŋo bende wosangala gi kabedo pere ma piny. Kole jomoŋaŋ jobino leny woko paka ŋono pa thiwi dudi.
59001011	Ato chieŋ wok gi lyetho mathoth to waŋo woko dudi; thiwe oy woko, to ŋono mere nyiekere woko. Meno bende apaka ibino reyo woko jaŋaŋo munyo go yindin gi tich pere.
59001012	Jasilwany a dhano ma chwire i yeyo i ndir ma tem, rupiri ka go onyalo loyo tem, bino limo sangarya ma kwo, kemba ma Were otyeko chiko jomomaro go.
59001013	Ka dhano olimo ratem i tem ma chalo ameno, wokiri wowachi ni, “Ratem no wok bongi Were,” rupiri recho kinyal kelo ri Were ratem, odoko Were won kikel ri nyatoro ratem.
59001014	To dhano jye nwaŋo ratem ka awanya pere marach won ywayo chunye to tero go i ratem.
59001015	Aka awanya no medere yach nyuka nywolo gimarach; aka ka gimarach ochowo tegino, to nywolo tho.
59001016	Kiri wowondi win, wutimera.
59001017	Mich maber kodi maŋon jye wok i polo; wok bongi Were Baba, jachweyi lero ma polo, aka go kiwire korin gi korin pa tipo yath.
59001018	I mito pere won, go onywolo wan manyien gi wach pere maradyeri, ŋey wabedi paka olemo pere monyak marapena kwoŋ chwech pere jye.
59001019	Maki win wach me, wutimera. Dhano jye ripo bedo mayil i winjo, ma kikwakere gi luwo, aka kimaki nge piyo.
59001020	Kole nge pa dhano kikony go limo kwo motire ma Were yenyo.
59001021	Amomiyo, boli win woko kite makoch kodi recho ma wimore gine. Aka wijoli gi mwolo wach ma go piidho i chuny win, ma nyalo botho win.
59001022	Bedi win joma ketho wach i tim, ma kiweno joma wondere gi nyaka winjo awinja wach won kende.
59001023	Kole ŋata winjo wach to kikethi i tim chalo dhano ma ŋiyere i ndewiro to nenere paka go chalo,
59001024	to ka otyeko nenere, kadho to piyo piyo wiye wil gi chal pere.
59001025	To ŋata kaŋasa chik motire ma ketho ji i syem, aka medo ketho paro pere kwoŋe, ma kichiki ithe kende to wiye wil, to go ketho wach i tim, ŋato Were bino miyo silwany i gima go timo.
59001026	Ka nyatoro paro ni go ŋatoyeyo, to kuchiel kikur lewe meno yeyo pere ongoye kony aka go won wondere.
59001027	Yeyo ma Were Bawan tero paka yeyo motire mongoye rendirok ame: kuro nyithindho kiich kodi mon ma chwogi jo otho i chandirok pajo, gi kurok kwoŋ recho ma piny.
59002001	Wutimera, i kwo mewin paka jomoyeyo Ruoth Yesu Kristo, Ruoth madwoŋ, wikiri wiyeri ji munyo wiŋisa joman ru chal pajo ma woko.
59002002	Ka jaŋaŋo moro moruko peta ma zawabu gi ruk mabeyo obino i romo mewin, to jachandi moro moruko oselo bende bino,
59002003	to wimiyo jaŋaŋo dwoŋ ka wiwacho ri go ni, “Bedi i kom moasa bero me,” to wiwacho ri jachandi ni, “Chungi kacha kosa ni bedi piny i lowo dho tyendan ka,”
59002004	meno onyo wikibenga i kelo pokirok i dyeri win kareno wilokere paka jothumi banjin ma paro pajo recho?
59002005	Winji win wutimera! Wiparo ni Were koyero jochandi ma piny ka bedo jomoŋaŋ i yeyo, gi lunjo Ker ma go ochiko jomomaro go?
59002006	To kole wichayo jochandi! Ŋata diyo win aka yware gi win tero win i kapido, ki joŋaŋo?
59002007	Ki jono ama joluwo marach kwoŋ nyingi ŋataber milwoŋo win gine no?
59002008	Ka wimako maber chik ma Ker ma nwaŋere i ndiiko ma wacho ni, “Mari nyawotin paka iwon imarere,” meno witimo gimotire.
59002009	To ka wipoko ji chungo kwoŋ chal pajo ma woko, meno witimo gimarach, aka itero win paka joturi chik chungo kwoŋ Chik ma nitye.
59002010	Kole ŋata turo nyaka kada or achiel ma Chik bedo gi banja paka ŋatoturo chik jye.
59002011	Ato ŋata owacho ni, “Ikiri itimi chot” ama bende owacho ni, “Ikiri ineki.” Kada ikitimi chot, to ka ineko dhano meno kole ityeko bedo jaturi chik.
59002012	Ri ameno luwi win, odoko bedi win gi tim, paka ji mibino thumo ri jo banja chungo kwoŋ chik ma kelo syem,
59002013	rupiri Were konyuthi wor ri ŋata konyutho wor ri wadi. To ŋata nyutho wor meno otyeko loyo banja.
59002014	Wutimera! Bero aŋo m'obedi ri dhano ka wacho ni, “Anitye gi yeyo”, to tim pere kinyuthi ameno? Yeyo pere no won kende di nyal botho go?
59002015	Paka ranen, bedi nitye omin wan kosa nyamin wan mongoye gi giraruka kodi chiemo ma romo,
59002016	bero aŋo ma nitye ka achiel kwon win owacho ri go ni, “Were womiyin silwany, kadhi i syem aka ichiemi maber,” ma komiyo go gima yenyere i kwo?
59002017	Meno bende apaka yeyo won kende, ka tim mathyelo ongoye, bedo gimotho.
59002018	To moro kwoŋ win bino wacho ni, “Kole ini gi yeyo; aka ani gi tim.” Meno adwoko ni: “Nyuthan paka inyalo bedo gi yeyo mongoye tim; to an abino nyuthin yeyo paran i tim paran.”
59002019	Wiyeyo nike Were nitye achiel? Meno ber! Kole jwogi bende joyeyo ameno aka jokirin gi lworo.
59002020	Dhano mamiŋ! Imito wonyuthin nike yeyo mongoye tim ongoye konyi?
59002021	Kere chango oketh kwari wan Ibrayimu i tiro gi Were nedi? Kole obedo i tim, munyo go ochwayo ri Were wuode Isaka wi alitar.
59002022	Kenyo inyalo neno ni, yeyo pere kodi tim pere jotiyo kanyachiel; aka yeyo pere oridhi i tim pere.
59002023	Aka ndiiko otundo i kare ma wacho ni, “Ibrayimu oyeyo Were, aka ru yeyo pere Were okwano go paka ŋatotire.” Aka Were olwoŋo go ni, mere peran Ibrayimu.
59002024	Amomiyo wineno ni dhano iketho i tiro gi Were kwoŋ gima go timo, ma kiweno kwoŋ yeyo kende.
59002025	Apaka bende obedo gi Rahab moido tana delkwoŋe i timo gi wichkwot; oketh go i tiro gi Were ru tim pere munyo go ojolo jopendo pa Joyudaya to wodho jo gi yu royo man.
59002026	Ato paka del mongoye chuny meno gimotho, apaka bende yeyo mongoye tim meno gimotho.
59003001	Jomathoth kwoŋ win kiri jowolokere jofuonji, wutimera, rupiri wiŋeyo ni wan ma wafuonjo ibino thumo ri wan banja monuŋ loyo joman.
59003002	Wajojye ndir madit wapodho. Dhano ma kipodhi i luwo pere meno dhano motire kichutho, ma nyalo dhumo kwo pere gipi.
59003003	Ka wariwo yath moro i dhoki kayina ma miyo jowowinji wan, wanyalo miyo jokidho kama wayenyo jye.
59003004	Kosa neni kwoŋ mel i wakawaka; kada dwoŋ ameno aka koyo mathoth ama tero go, to nyaka gimathin moro ama leko go, aka kidho kama jatero mito ni wokidh'iye.
59003005	Me bende apaka nitye gi lew jo: kada thin rigo ameno, to nyalo luwo wach mayumirok madongo swa. Pari paka nyaka mach mondhilo nyalo waŋo lul mombo!
59003006	Lew jo bende chalo mach. Obedo dak gimarecho ma nitye gi kabedo i delkwoŋ wan aka nyayo recho i kwo mawan gipi; go moko mach i kwo mawan gipi, aka go won bino waŋ i mach makitho.
59003007	Dhano otyeko nyalo dhumo ogwange ma nger jye, winyin, gimamol gi kore, gi rech mapi jye, to loko jo mamwol.
59003008	To ongoye moro ma nyalo dhumo lewe maber. Lew jo obedo gimarach ma kikudere, aka thoth gi kwir.
59003009	Waoro lew wan ma pako Ruoth gi Bawan odoko waoro lew wan achiel no won ma kwoŋo dhano mochwey i chal pa Were.
59003010	Wach ma pako kodi ma kwoŋo nyatoro jye wok i dhok dhano achiel no won. Wutimera, gime oido kiripi timirok ameno.
59003011	Wiparo ni waŋ pi achiel nyalo wodho pi mamit kir gi ma kech bende?
59003012	Wutimera, makuyu nyalo nyak gimanyak pa vini, kosa yath vini nyalo nyak nyandere pa makuyu? Ri ameno waŋ pi ma kech chumbi kinyal wodho pi mamit.
59003013	Ŋa kwoŋ win kenyo maryek kendo maniaŋ? Ere wonyuthi ryeko no gi kwo pere motire, gi tim pere ma nyutho bwonirok kodi ryeko.
59003014	To ka wipoŋ gi nyieko kodi mito ich, wikiri wipakere gine odoko wikiri wikwer adyeri.
59003015	“Ryeko” ma chal ameno kiwoki i polo; to obedo ma piny ka, ki machuny, to apa jwogi ayino.
59003016	Kole kama di nyieko kodi mito ich, kenyo ruwirok bende ni iye kodi nger recho jye.
59003017	To ryeko ma wok i polo olony kutho marapena; odoko kelo syem, aka nitye iye mwolo; dewo kwoŋ ji, oasere gi wor aka nywolo tim mabeyo; ongoy'iye thumo banja mokom kosa rendirok.
59003018	Aka joma kelo syem jokecho tiro mopidhi i syem.
59004001	Kere aŋo ma kelo gorok gi dhawirok i dyer win? Gikipiny no kiwoki kwoŋ awanya ma ndir jye lwenyo i delkwoŋ wini?
59004002	Wimito gimoro to wikilim. Gikenyo wichako nekirok; aka wiwanya gikipiny to wikinyal limo. Amomiyo widhaw to wigore. Wikilim gima wimito rupiri wikikway Were.
59004003	Aka ka wikwayo wikilim, rupiri wikwayo gi atoŋa marecho: wikwayo gikipiny maraora ma kisangala mewin won.
59004004	Ji ma kigenere! Wikuya ni mako mere gi piny meno bedo i kwor gi Were? Ŋata mito mako mere gi piny meno mito bedo jakwor pa Were.
59004005	Kosa wiparo ni ndiiko ongoye g'atoŋa i nyutho ni, “Chuny ma Were oketho i wan ni gi nyieko moasere?”
59004006	To Were nyutho wan ŋono mathoth loyo. Amomiyo ndiiko wacho ni, “Were chiro japakirok, to nyutho ŋatamwol ayino ŋono.”
59004007	Amomiyo, bedi win joma winjo Were. Chiri win Jwogi aka go bino eye kwoŋ win gi ŋwech.
59004008	Chore win chiegin gi Were, aka go bende bino chore chiegin gi win. Jomarecho, logi win chingi win. Lonyi win chuny win, wijokiganagana!
59004009	Bedi win gi rem, gi geregere aka wiywaki: nyiero mewin wolokere ywak, aka kisangala mewin wolokere rembo ayino!
59004010	Bwonere win ruwaŋ Were, aka go bino tiŋo win malo.
59004011	Wikiri wiluwere marach kwoŋ jowoti win, wutimera. Ŋata luwo marach kwoŋ omin, kosa thumo ri go banja, meno luwo marach kwoŋ Chik aka chayo Chik. Ka ichayo Chik, meno kere ikibedo dhano ma winjo Chik, to ijachayi Chik ayino.
59004012	Kole jakethi chik ma bende a jathumi banja nitye achiel kende. Go won ama nyalo botho kosa reyo woko. To onyo in iŋa, m'ithumo banja ri dhano nyawotin?
59004013	Ere pawinji win, win ma wiwacho ni, “Konon kosa dikin wabino kidho i tindi moro, kama wabino chow'iye oro, to watiyo to walimo pesa.”
59004014	Wikuya kada ni aŋo ma nyalo timere dikin! Kwo mewin obedi nedi? Kole wichali tor, ma nenere chowo hongo machiek to leny woko.
59004015	Kuchiel, d'onyo wiwacho ni, “Ka Ruoth oyeyo, wabino bedo makwo, to watimo gime gi mecha.”
59004016	To odoko wiyumere aka wipakere ayin; kole kiti yumirok no rach.
59004017	Amomiyo, dhano jye moŋeyo gimaber ma go ripere wotimi aka kitim meno timo gimarach.
59005001	Aka wijoŋaŋo, winji win! Bedi win gi rem aka wiywaki ru litho ma lebino ri win!
59005002	Ŋaŋo mewin otyeko top woko, aka ruk mewin masirigi otyeko chamo woko.
59005003	Zawabu mewin kodi feza otyeko mako nyal, aka nyal me bino bedo giranena manyutho recho mewin, to chamo delkwoŋ win pa mach. Wityeko dhuro ŋaŋo i ndelo machowe me!
59005004	Pawinji win! Kemba ma wikichulo jotich ma jotiyo i ndelin mewin ichade koko ka osa win. Aka ywak pa jokecho ri win otyeko tundo i ithi Were, Ruoth pa lwak jolweny!
59005005	Kwo mewin i piny ka obedo ma noro kodi ma kisangala mewin wiwegi. Wimedo chwe ri ndelo ma tho, pa dhok mikidho thumo.
59005006	Wityeko thumo banjin ni oloyo ji moido jongoye gi racho moro to wineko jo, kada oido jokipyem gi win.
59005007	Amomiyo, wutimere, diyi win chuny win, nyuka Ruoth odwoki. Neni win paka jafur diyo chunye munyo kuro ni lowo pere wonyak ri go gimawelo. Go kuro gino modiyo chunye chuka koth ma chwir kodi ma kecho tundo.
59005008	Aka wibende wiripo diyo chuny win. Chungi win matek rupiri ndelo ma dwoko pa Ruoth orikere ni chiegin.
59005009	Wikiri wigesa gi jowoti win, wutimera, aka Were kothum ri win banja. Kole jathumi banja ni dhoot, oyikere donjo!
59005010	Wutimera, poyi win jotuchi wach Were ma joluwo wach i nyingi Ruoth. Teri win jo paka ranen pa joma jochiro gi diyo chuny jo i hongo ma chandirok.
59005011	Ato wiŋeyo ni watero joma jotyeko chiro gimoro paka josilwany. Wityeko winjo paka Yobu onyalo chiro chandirok, aka wiŋeyo paka Ruoth oparo kwoŋe rumachien. Kole Ruoth oasere gi wor aka winjo malith gi teko pa dhano.
59005012	Maloyo meno, wutimera, wikiri wikwoŋere ka witimo chikirok aka witucho polo, kosa piny, kosa gimoro man jye. Wachi win nyaka ni, “Ey” ka wimito yeyo gimoro, kodi “Be” ka wimito kwero gimoro, aka ŋey wikobedi gi banja ruwaŋ Were.
59005013	Nitye moro kwoŋ win ma nitye i teko? Weyi wokwayi Were. Nitye moro ma sangala? Weyi woweri wer ma pako Were.
59005014	Nitye kwoŋ win ŋatatwo? Ripo wolwoŋi jotel ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo, ma jobino kwayo ri go to jowiro mo kwoŋe i nyingi Ruoth.
59005015	Aka kwayo mokway i yeyo, bino botho jatwo; Ruoth bino dwoko ri go men kwoŋe, aka gimarecho ma go otimo ibino chwako.
59005016	Amomiyo, tuchi win gimarecho mewin ri jowoti win, odoko kwayi win ri jowoti win, ŋey wilimi both ma del. Kwayo pa ŋatotire nitye gi men madwoŋ aka tiyo.
59005017	Eliya oido obedo dhano paka wan. Go okwayo gi ridho nike koth wongoye, aka koth bende kothon i lowo chowo oro adek g'adech.
59005018	Go odoko okwayo, to polo konjo koth to lowo nyak chiemo mani iye.
59005019	Wutimera, ka nyatoro kwoŋ win oweyo adyeri, to ŋat man dwoko go kendo,
59005020	poyi win gime: ŋat moro jye modwoki ŋatarach wok i royo pere mokom, bino botho chuny ŋatarach no kwoŋ tho, to miyo ichwako ri go gimarecho madit.
60001001	Balwa mowok bongi Petro, jamoor pa Yesu Kristo, Ri ji pa Were moyer ma jobedo paka wendo i piny aka jotyakere i adeche ma Ponto, Galasya, Kapadosya, Asya kodi Bithiniya.
60001002	Oyer win ru atoŋa ma Were Baba won oŋeyo kichutho, nike Chuny Maleŋ woloki win maleŋ, ŋey wiwinji Yesu Kristo to lonyo win gi remo pere. Weyi ŋono gi syem wobedi mewin mopoŋ kichutho.
60001003	Weyi wapaki Were Baa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo. Ru ŋono pere moasere, go omiyo wanywolere i kwo manyien munyo ochierino Yesu Kristo kwoŋ jomotho to miyo wan geno makwo i chuny wan,
60001004	to waŋiyo yu malo munyo wakiyo lunjo ŋaŋo ma kitopi, kosa nyiekere, kosa rumi, ma Were okano ri win i polo.
60001005	Ato ru yeyo mewin amomiyo men pa Were kuro win chuka tundo ndelo ma both moyik nyutho ka ndir otundo.
60001006	Sangala win gi wach me, kada onyo i hongo me wityeko nwaŋo chandirok munyo wibedo gi rem hongo machiek ru tem momore mobino ri win.
60001007	Chandirok me obino ru atoŋa ma temo yeyo mewin. Kole kada zawabu ma nyiekere jye itemo gi mach. Amomiyo yeyo mewin ma di welo loyo zawabu, bende yenyere wotem wonen ka otire, ŋey gino wokeli ri win pak kodi dwoŋ kodi wor i Ndelo milenyuth'iye Yesu Kristo kamaler.
60001008	Wimaro go kada fuodi wikineno go; wiyeyo go, kada pama wikinen go; aka wini gi kisangala ma di dwoŋ ma kiwachere,
60001009	rupiri onyo wilimo gima wok i yeyo mewin, mobedo both ma chuny win.
60001010	Both me ama jotuchi wach ma joluwo kwoŋ ŋono pa Were ma d'omiyo win, jotemo rango tyende maber.
60001011	Jotemo rango tyende munyo jomito ŋeyo ni keraŋo ma hongo no d'otund'iye, kodi paka d'obino; ato Chuny pa Kristo i jo oido chimo hongo no munyo tucho chandirok ma go d'ochiro, kodi dwoŋ ma d'owok'iye.
60001012	Were onyutho jotuchi wach me ni oido jokitiy ri jo wegi, to ri win, munyo joluwo kwoŋ adyeri ma pama wiwinjo. Jomikwenda ma Wach Maber, ma joluwo i men pa Chuny Maleŋ moor wok i polo, ama jotito ri win adyeri me. Me adyeri ma kiri jomalaika jye jomito ŋeyo dwoŋ mere.
60001013	Amomiyo yiki win paro mewin ma tich; bedi ma widhumo chuny win, aka kethi win geno mewin jye kwoŋ silwany mibino miyo win ka onyuthi Yesu Kristo kamaler.
60001014	Paka nyithindho ma winjo Were, wikiri wiyeyi awanya machon monwaŋo wini gine munyo fuodi wikuya Were wodhumi kwo mewin.
60001015	Kuchiel, bedi win maleŋ i gimoro jye ma witimo, paka Were molwoŋo win leŋ;
60001016	rupiri ndiiko wacho ni, “Wiripo bedo maleŋ, rupiri aleŋ.”
60001017	Kole wilwoŋo Were ni Baba ka wikwayo, aka go ama thumo banja ri ji jye ma rom. Amomiyo ori win kwo mewin i piny ka paka joma wendo munyo wimiyo go dwoŋ.
60001018	Ato wiŋeyo gimochul ma gonyo win woko kwoŋ kwo masisiri ma winwaŋo wok bongi kwarere mewin, aka gimonyiewo win no kobedo gimoro ma nyiekere woko paka zawabu kosa feza,
60001019	to remo pa Kristo ama ogonyo win, go mobedo paka nyathi rombo mongoye gi ŋolo moro kosa waŋpoyo.
60001020	Were oyero go ma fuodi kochwey piny, aka onyuthere i ndelo machowe me ma bero mewin.
60001021	I go wiyeyo Were, mochierino go kwoŋ jomotho to miyo go dwoŋ, momiyo yeyo kodi geno mewin nitye kwoŋ Were.
60001022	To paka onyo wilony ru winjo adyeri, aka wini gi mar mochwiny ri jowoti win ma joyeyo, ere marere win adyeri gi chuny win jye.
60001023	Kole onyo winywolere ma diryo, ki kwoŋ kodhi ma tho, to kwoŋ ma kitho, chungo kwoŋ wach pa Were makwo kendo ma yindira chil gi chil.
60001024	Rupiri ndiiko wacho ni, “Ji jye jochalo lum, aka dwoŋ pajo chalo thiwi lum; Lum tho, to thiwe oy woko,
60001025	to wach pa Ruoth doŋadoŋa chil gi chil.” Aka me a wach motiti ri win.
60002001	Amomiyo, weyi win miyo jowoti win litho, kodi twodo jye, kosa rendirok, kosa nyieko, kosa nyieko nyingi wadi win!
60002002	Bedi win paka nyithindho maŋich ma nyaka onywol jo, ma wiwinjo riiyo ma chak molony machuny, aka ka wimadho wibino dongo i both mewin.
60002003	Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Wityeko bilo bero pa Ruoth.”
60002004	Biye win bongi Ruoth, tele makwo ma ji jokwero nike bu kony, to Were oyero paka di kony ri go.
60002005	Ato wibende wibedo telin makwo, m'onyo igero gine Ot pa Were machuny, kama wibino tiy'iye paka jochwayi ri Were wi alitar ma joleŋ, kareno wichwayo rachow ma nyachuny ma Were jolo luwo kwoŋ Yesu Kristo.
60002006	Ato ndiiko wacho ni, “Neni, pama onyo aketho tele ma tyelo ot i Zayun, tele moyer ma di welo; aka nyatoro jye moyeyi go wiye kibino kwot.”
60002007	Tele me obedo mawelo madwoŋ ri win ma wiyeyo; to ri joma kiyey obedo: “Tele ma jogeto jokwero ni bu kony ama olokere tele ma mako kindi ot won gipi.”
60002008	Kendo ni, “Me a tele ma miyo ji jochier, Kidi ma miyo jopodho.” Jochier rupiri jokiyey Wach cha, paka ochan ni jowotimi.
60002009	To wibedo ji moyer, jochwayi ri Kere wi alitar, nono maleŋ, ji pa Were won, ŋey winyali pako tim pa Were ma urere, go molwoŋo win wok i mudho donjo i lero pere maŋon makiwachere.
60002010	I hongo mokadho oido wikibedo ji moyer, to pama onyo wibedo ji pa Were; i hongo mokadho oido wikijolo wor pa Were, to pama onyo wijolo wor pere.
60002011	Agoyo koko ri win jowatan, paka jowiloka ma wendo i piny me, ni ŋuti win kwoŋ awanya marecho, ma ndir jye lwenyo gi chuny win.
60002012	Kula mewin i dyer jokafiri wobedi maber ma ka jotemi kelo kwoŋ win wach ni wirecho, jobino neno tim mewin mabeyo, to jopako Were i Ndelo ma bino pere.
60002013	Ru atoŋa pa Ruoth, winji win jodhum jye ma piny; kada obedo kere madwoŋ ma dhumo joman jye,
60002014	kosa gavana, ma go oro ma miyo jotimi recho girachula, gi fuoyo joma timo gimabeyo.
60002015	Kole Were yenyo ni tim mewin mabeyo woum luwo masisiri mapa jomamiŋ.
60002016	Kwo mewin wobedi paka apa joma ni syem; to wikiri wiloki syem mewin ma umo recho moro jye; kuchiel kwo mewin wobedi paka apa jotich pa Were.
60002017	Wori win ji jye: mari win jowoti win ma joyeyo, lwori win Were, aka wiwor kere ma piny.
60002018	Ŋechin, winji win ruodhe mewin, aka nyuthi win jo wor mopoŋ, ki nyaka joma timo ri win maber aka joparo kwoŋ win kende, to kir jomager bende.
60002019	Kole nitye kony moro ka dhano ochiro litho ma chandirok rupiri dwoko paro pere kwoŋ Were.
60002020	To bero aŋo ma wilimo ka wichiro gocho ma ripere kodi win ka witimo recho? Kuchiel ka wichiro chandirok kada wityeko timo bero, meno ama Were miyo silwany.
60002021	Were olwoŋo win ri gime, rupiri Kristo bende ochandere ri win aka oweyo ri win ranen, nike winyali luwo bathe.
60002022	Ndiiko wach ni, “Go kotimo gimarach moro, aka ongoye twodo mowok i dhoke.”
60002023	Munyo oyet go, kochulo kwor; munyo ochandere, go kopiro nyatoro, to oketho geno pere i Were ma Jathumi banja i tiro.
60002024	Go won otiŋo gimarecho mawan i delkwoŋe wi musalaba, ŋey wabedi jomotho ri gimarach to wakwo ri tiro; chungo kwoŋ adholin pere, wityeko chango.
60002025	Ato oido wichalo roombo morwenyo; to onyo pama widwoko bongi Jakwath kendo Jakur ma chuny win.
60003001	I royo achiel, win mon wiripo yeyere gi chwogi win, ŋey ka mogo kwoŋ jo jokiyey wach pa Were, kiti mon pajo mabeyo wonyali ywayo jo to joyeyo.
60003002	Kole jobino neno paka kiti win olony aka di wor.
60003003	Ŋono mewin kiripi wok i gikipiny ma wiruko kosa witimo kwoŋ win paka kedo wich, kosa jaŋo kwoŋ win thiwino mawelo, kosa ruko nengin mawelo.
60003004	Kuchiel ŋono mewin ripo wok kwoŋ adyeri ma chuny win, ŋono ma kireyere ma chuny mamwol, mokudere, ma nitye gi welo madwoŋ i waŋ Were.
60003005	Kole me a royo ma mon maleŋ, ma jogeno Were i ndir machon, joloko gine kwo pajo maŋon, aka jowinjo chwogi jo,
60003006	paka Sara owinjo Ibrayimu, munyo lwoŋo go ni Ruoth! Aka wibedo nyithindho pere ka witimo gimotire ma wikibedo gi lworo moro jye.
60003007	Ameno bende, chwo bedi win i kwo maber gi mon mewin, munyo wimiyo jo dwoŋ paka chwech manyap, odoko paka joma bende jobino limo kanyachiel kodi win, mich pa Were mobedo kwo. Timi win ameno aka nyaka gimoro kogeŋ kwayo mewin.
60003008	Machowe, wijojye, riwere win i chuny win, bedi win gi wor ri jowoti win, odoko marere win paka wutimere, bedi win gi dewo kodi mwolo ri jowoti win.
60003009	Wikiri wichuli recho gi recho kosa yet gi yet, to chuli win gi silwany ayino; kole silwany a gima Were ochiko miyo win munyo olwoŋo win.
60003010	Rupiri paka ndiiko wacho, “Ŋata mito limo kwo gi neno syem, woweyi luwo marach gi lewe, aka wowey twodo.
60003011	Go ripo eye woko kwoŋ recho to timo bero; go ripo rango syem gi chunye jye.
60003012	Kole waŋ Ruoth nitye kwoŋ jomotire aka ochiko ithe ri kwayo pajo, to waŋ Ruoth gawo joma timo recho.”
60003013	To ŋa ma bino timo ri win teko ka wiyikere timo gimaber?
60003014	Aka kada wichandere ri timo gimotire, kole jye fuodi wibino limo silwany. Wikiri wilwori nyatoro, kosa wibwoki.
60003015	To i chuny win, wori win Kristo paka Ruoth. Ndir jye yikere win ma dwoko ŋata lwoŋo win tito geno ma wini gine.
60003016	To timi win ameno gi mwolo ka wimiyo jo dwoŋ. Kendo kuri win paro ma chuny win maber, aka ŋey joma joluwo marach kwoŋ kiti win maber i Kristo, wiy jo bino kwot kwoŋ gima jowacho.
60003017	Kole ber chandirok ru timo bero, ka obedo mito pa Were, loyo chandirok ru timo gimarach.
60003018	Kole Kristo otho ri gimarecho dichiel kichutho, ŋataber, ri jomarecho, ŋey go wokeli win bongi Were. Onek go i delkwoŋe, to kareno omiy go kwo i chuny,
60003019	aka i kwo machuny no, go okidho to tito wach kamaler ri chuny moketh i twech.
60003020	Me oido obedo chuny ma jokwero winjo Were munyo go otemo kuro jo munyo diyo chunye i ndir ma Nowa oido ger'iye yee. Ji manok ma jobedo i yee; ji aboro kende, ama joboth i pi,
60003021	aka pi no obedo ranyuth ma chimo batisimo ma pama botho win, ki paka gima lwoko woko chilo ma del to obedo chikirok m'itimo ri Were gi chuny maber. Gino bothin luwo kwoŋ chierino pa Kristo Yesu,
60003022	motyeko kidho i polo aka onyo nitye yu chingi Were marachuch, aka onyo dhumo jomalaika jye kodi men jye kodi adhum jye.
60004001	Amomiyo, paka Kristo ochandere i delkwoŋe, wibende wiripo miyirok miseni gi kiti paro ma go obedo gine, rupiri ŋata ochandere i delkwoŋe meno otyeko thekirok gi gimarach.
60004002	Ri ameno, wok gunyoni, mito pa Were ama dhumo kwo pere gipi i piny ka ma kiweno awanya marecho ma del.
60004003	Wityeko oro hongo moromo munyo oido witimo gima jokafiri joketho paro pajo i timo paka kidakana, awanya marecho ma waŋ i chuny jo, mero i kalima ma nyaworoworo, medho ma kitipa, gi lamo chal makichar.
60004004	Aka jokafiri no jouro nike wikiriwere gi jo i timo girawanya marecho moasere no, amomiyo joyeto win;
60004005	to jobino tito wach ri ŋata oyikere thumo banja ri jomakwo kodi jomotho.
60004006	Me amomiyo otiti Wach Maber ri joma pama jotyeko tho bende, ŋey wothumi ri jo banja i del paka ji jye, to jobedo makwo paka Were i chuny.
60004007	Giki gimoro jye orikere ochore chiegin, amomiyo bedi win milengela kendo ma widhumo kwo mewin aka winyali kwayo.
60004008	To maloyo gimoro jye, marere win gi mar madwoŋ, rupiri mar umo gimarecho madit.
60004009	Joli win jowoti win i pechin mewin mongoye kigesa.
60004010	Kis dhano ripo oro mich jye ma Were omiyo go ma konyo jowote, munyo oro mich mopokere opokere g'adyeri.
60004011	Nyatoro jye ma fuonjo wach pa Were ripo fuonjo igani obedo wach pa Were won; nyatoro jye ma timo tich wotimi gi men ma Were miyo go, aka ŋey i gimoro jye womiyi Were pak kwoŋ Yesu Kristo, ma dwoŋ gi men obedo apere, chil gi chil. Ameno.
60004012	Jowotan mamaro, wikiri widhyeri kwoŋ tem malith ma wichandere iye, igani gima ki ma kis ndelo timere ri win.
60004013	Kuchiel sangala win nike wiriwere gi Kristo i chandirok pere, ŋey rumachien kisangala wopoŋi i chuny win ka onyuthi dwoŋ pere.
60004014	Wijosilwany ka oyeti win ru oro nyingi Kristo; dwoŋ mere ni Chuny ma nigi dwoŋ aka apa Were, nitye i win.
60004015	To wongoye moro kwoŋ win ma wochandere paka janek, kosa jakwo, kosa ŋata otimo racho madwoŋ, kosa ma rire i tich pa joman.
60004016	To ka moro kwoŋ win chandere ru kwoŋbedo go Jakristo, wiye wokiri wokwoti, to wofuoyi Were ayino ni go ilwoŋo go gi nyingi Kristo.
60004017	Ato ndir otundo ma thumo banja aka lechako gi ji pa Were won. Onyo ka kidho chako gi wan, obedi nedi ri joma jokiyey Wach Maber ma wok bongi Were?
60004018	Kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Ka tek ri jomotire limo both; onyo aŋo m'obedi ri joma kilwor Were kodi jogimarecho?”
60004019	Amomiyo, jomachandere rupiri obedo mito pa Were ri jo, joripo medo miyirok ri jachwech pajo ma genere gi medo timo gimabeyo.
60005001	Onyo paka abende abedo jadwoŋ i kitipa pa jomoyeyo, kendo paka ŋata oneno chandirok mobedo ri Kristo, odoko paka ŋata bende ibino pokoye go dwoŋ milenyutho, agoyo koko ri jotel ma kitipin pa jomoyeyo ma jo ni dyeri win,
60005002	ni bedi win jokwath pa sidwol roombo ma Were omiyo win, aka wileki jo gi maro mewin, paka Were mito witimi, ma kiweno g'arom. Tiyi win, mongoye woro pesa, to ru maro tich ri jowoti win adyeri.
60005003	Wikiri widhumi joma oketh i kur mewin gi mbaka, to bedi win ranen ri sidwol.
60005004	Aka ka Jakwath Madwoŋ onenere, wibino limo sangarya ma di dwoŋ ma kibino wiro chal to rumo.
60005005	Ameno bende, wi joma fuodi soye wiripo winjo jotel mewin gi mwolo. Aka wijojye ruki win mwolo ma tiyo ri jowoti win pa nanga; kole ndiiko wacho ni, “Were lwenyo gi jopakirok, to timo ri joma wegi jobwonere ŋono.”
60005006	Amomiyo, bwonere win, i chingi Were ma di men, ŋey nyaka go bino tiŋo win malo i hongo moripo.
60005007	Kethi win rembo mewin jye kwoŋ go, rupiri go dewo kwoŋ win.
60005008	Bedi win ma wiŋeyo dhumo kwo mewin ma wineno. Kole jakwor mewin, jwogi, riwo piny pa simbwor ma hola, munyo rango nyatoro m'omwony.
60005009	Pyemi win gine, munyo wichungo matek i yeyo mewin, rupiri wiŋeyo ni jowoti win ma joyeyo i piny gipi bende onyo joluwo i kiti chandirok no.
60005010	To ka wityeko chandirok mathin, Were mani gi ŋono jye, molwoŋo win ni wopoki win ye dwoŋ ma chil gi chil i Kristo, won bino miyo win men, to miyo wichungo ma wichwiny i yeyo.
60005011	Ri go men wobedi chil gi chil. Ameno.
60005012	Andiko ri win balwa machiek me gi kony pa Silvano, ma atero paka omera mogenere. Amito medo win men gi ridho ri win nike me obedo ŋono pa Were adyeri. Chungi win matek iye.
60005013	Kitipa ma nyawoti mewin mani Babilon, ma Were bende ama oyero, dhiro ri win moth, gi Marko wuodan bende.
60005014	Mothere win akor gi mar ma nyakristo. Weyi syem wobedi gi wijojye ma wibedo apa Kristo.
61001001	Balwa mowok bongi Simon Petro, jatich kendo jamoor pa Yesu Kristo, Ri joma i tiro pa Were mawan kendo Jaboth, Yesu Kristo, omiy jo yeyo ma di welo paka mawan:
61001002	Weyi ŋono gi syem mopoŋ wobedi gi win i ŋeyo Were kodi Yesu Ruodhiwan.
61001003	Men pa Were omiyo wan gimoro jye ma wayenyo ma bedo i kwo ma lworo Were, rupiri waŋeyo ŋata olwoŋo wan gi dwoŋ kodi bero pere won.
61001004	Ameno go omiyo wan, mich m'ochiko madwoŋ swa kendo ma di welo, ŋey ka walimo mich me wabino both kwoŋ recho ma nitye i piny ka ru awanya, to wadonjo i kula ma nyawerewere.
61001005	Ri ameno, temi win paka winyalo medo bero kwoŋ yeyo mewin; kodi niaŋ kwoŋ bero;
61001006	kodi kurok kwoŋ niaŋ; kwoŋ kurok mewin medi win chiro; kwoŋ chiro medi win lworo Were;
61001007	kwoŋ lworo Were medi win iye woro jomoyeyo jowot win; aka kwoŋ woro jomoyeyo jowot win medi win iye marok.
61001008	Ka wimedo bedo gi gimabeyo me madit, bino loko win mayil to wibedo gi kony i ryeko mewin kwoŋ Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo.
61001009	To ka nyatoro ongoye gi gimabeyo me, meno kere go waŋe neno mariprip aka wiye owil ni otyek lonyo go kwoŋ recho pere.
61001010	Amomiyo, jowotan, temi win paka winyalo ridho lwoŋo kodi yer mewin; ka witimo ameno wikopodhi i yeyo mewin.
61001011	Ameno, ibino jolo win maber donjo i Ker makirum mapa Ruodhiwan kendo Jaboth mawan Yesu Kristo.
61001012	Amomiyo ndir jye abino poyo win gikipiny me, kada wityeko ŋeyo jo aka wichungo kir matek i adyeri ma wityeko jolo.
61001013	Aparo ni obedo gimotire ka achiewo paro mewin to wipoyo gikipiny me ka fuodi akwo,
61001014	rupiri aŋeyo ni achiegin lunyo woko delkwoŋan me paka Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo otyeko nyuthan kamaler.
61001015	Aka abino temo paka anyalo neno ni kada ka atyeko weyo piny me fuodi wibino poyo gikipiny me.
61001016	Wakichungo kwoŋ kigana achwoga munyo watito ri win bino pa Ruoth Yesu Kristo gi men, to waneno dwoŋ pere gi waŋ wan.
61001017	Ato oido wanitye munyo Were Bawan miyo go dwoŋ mamalo, munyo dwondi jo mowok bongi Dwoŋ ma Malo cha oluwo ri go, munyo wacho ni, “Me Wuodan mamaro aka asangala gine!”
61001018	Wawegi wawinjo dwondi ŋato munyo luwo wok i polo, kareno oido wanitye gi Yesu wi got.
61001019	Aka, wanitye gi wach pa jotuchi wach motyek ridho. Wibino timo maber ka wiketho paro mewin kwoŋe; kole obedo pa lero ma meny kamachol chuka ndelo yawere to lero pa sulwe modikini menyo chuny win.
61001020	To ma kalo me, poyi win nike ongoye ŋata won ochwogo wach motuchi i Ndiiko Maleŋ.
61001021	Ato ongoye mikwenda pa Were motuchi mowok i mito pa dhano, to ji jobedo i men pa Chuny Maleŋ munyo jotucho mikwenda mowok bongi Were.
61002001	Jotuchi wach matwodo chango jobedo i dyeri ji pa Were, paka bende jolebino i dyeri win. Jobino rwako fuonji ma kelo reyirok, aka jobino kwedere kwoŋ Ruoth jadhum monyiewo jo, to jokelo tho kwoŋ gin arwat.
61002002	Jomathoth jobino mako royo pajo ma wichkwot; aka ru tim pajo, jobino luwo marach kwoŋ Royo Maradyeri.
61002003	I woro pajo, jofuonji matwodo me jobino chiemo kwoŋ win gi kigana ma wegi jochwogo. Banja pajo otyek yiko thumo wok chon, aka reyirok pajo bende kini bor to ni chiegin.
61002004	Kesi Were koworo jomalaika ma chango jotimo gimarach to obolo jo i mach makitho kama otwey'iye jo i mudho, ka jokuro ndelo ma thumo banja.
61002005	Odoko Were koworo piny machon, to okelo mikula madwoŋ ri jomarecho, to gwoko nyaka Nowa mofuonjo tiro, kodi ji man abiryo kende.
61002006	Kole Were othumo banja ri tindi ma Sodom kodi Gomora, munyo waŋo woko jo gi mach, aka oloko jo ranen ri gima bino timere ri jomarecho jye;
61002007	kole go obotho Lot, ŋataber, ma chunye oramo swa kwoŋ kidakana pa ji moido jokidew chik.
61002008	(Ato jal maber no obedo i dyer jo, aka kis piny moyawere olimo litho i chunye munyo oneno to winjo tim pajo marecho no).
61002009	Amomiyo, kere Ruoth oŋeyo nger ma botho ji mabeyo ma jolworo Were i chandirok ma temo jo, kodi weyo jomarecho i girachula pajo chuka ndelo ma thumo banja,
61002010	kodhi joma chwire i kiti jo motop ma kidakana aka jochayo men pa Were. Jofuonji matwodo me jonitye gi miseni kodi mikenyo, aka joluwere kichar kwoŋ chwech mani hongo malo;
61002011	mato kir jomalaika ma jotek aka jomen loyo jokikeli wach marach kwoŋ chwech no i waŋ Ruoth.
61002012	To jome joluwere kichar kwoŋ gima jokuya odocho. Jochale g'ogwange madudi ma jongoye gi paro, mimako tineko jo, ilereyo jo woko paka ogwange madudi;
61002013	ilechulo jo chandirok ru chandirok ma jotyeko kelo ri joman. Kisangala pajo obedo medho odyechieŋ ma syemo delkwoŋ gin. Bedo gi wichkwot kendo gimarach ka jobedo dhower gi win, kareno josangala i royo pajo marecho!
61002014	Gi waŋ gin ma neno gimoro gi chot, jogomba kis dhako ma joneno. Awanya pajo ma timo gimarach kikwe; jodwoŋo joma nyap, aka joŋiyo timo woro. Jobedo ji motyek kwoŋo!
61002015	Joweyo royo motire to jorwenyo munyo jomako royo ma Balam wuodi pa Beyor oluwo, monwaŋo omaro pesa ma go olimo i timo recho,
61002016	to punda pere oayi kwoŋe ru gimarecho pere. Gino oluwo gi dwondi dhano to juko tim pa jatuchi wach ma janeko no.
61002017	Jome jochalo waŋ pi modwono kodi pondeponde ma koyo waro; Were oyiko ri jo kama di mudho tektek maloyo kaman jye.
61002018	Joluwo wach mamiŋo gi pakirok, aka jooro awanya ma delkwoŋ gin ma chiiko joma nyaka joeye kwoŋ joma nitye i royo ma kelo rwenyo.
61002019	Jochiko jo syem mato wegi jobedo ŋechin pa kite marecho; ato dhano bedo ŋecha pa gima dhumo go.
61002020	Kole k'inen oido jotyeko budhirok kwoŋ men ma piny ma kelo tho, to joŋeyo Ruodhiwan kendo Jaboth mawan Yesu Kristo, aka odoko jomoko kendo i men no to nyalo jo, meno kere nyutho ni jonitye marach rumachien loyo kachako.
61002021	D'ober ri jo ka jobedo ma jokuya royo ma tiro loyo ŋeyo royo no to odoko joweyo chik maleŋ momiy jo.
61002022	Gima otimere gi jo nyutho ni agecha me otire, “Gwok odoko gik naŋo ŋok pere kendo” aka “Mbiji motyek lwoko odoko gik ŋindirok i chwodho kendo.”
61003001	Jowotan mamaro, me onyo balwa mararyo ma andiko ri win. I balwin aryo me, atemo chiewo paro mewin ŋey wichaki paro mathuth.
61003002	Amito wipoyi wach ma jotuchi wach Were chango joluwo kwoŋe, kodi or mowok bongi Ruoth kendo Jaboth, ma jomoor mewin jomiyo win.
61003003	Marapena, wiripo ŋeyo nike i ndelo machowe me, jonyiero jobino fudhirok ma joluwo royo marawanya pajo marecho gi nyiero machay.
61003004	Jobino penjo win ni, “Go ochiko ni bino, kameno be? To ere go ni kune? Bachere mawan jotyeko tho, to gimoro jye fuodi romaroma paka oido nitye wok nyuka chwey piny!”
61003005	Jotimo atoŋa igani jokuya ni chango chon Were oluwo aka polo gi piny ochwey, aka piny ochwey wok i pi, aka gi pi.
61003006	Kendo mikula pi madwoŋ ama onyieki gine woko piny machon.
61003007	To gi wach no won, polo gi piny ma pama nitye okan jo ri mach; ikuro gi jo ndelo ma thumo banja ri ji ma jokilwor Were tireyo jo woko.
61003008	To jowotan, wiy win wokiri wowili gi gimoro achiel! Ri Were pokirok ongoye i dyeri ndelo achiel kodi oro gana achiel; ri go gikipiny me romaroma.
61003009	Ruoth kigal gi timo gima go otyeko chiko paka jomegi joparo. Kuchiel, go diyo chunye kodi win, rupiri go kimiti nyatoro woreyere woko, to mito dhano jye wonyali ŋuto gimarecho pere.
61003010	To Ndelo pa Ruoth bino tundo paka jakwo. I Ndelo no polo bino leny woko gi derino madwoŋ; gikipiny ma polo bino waŋ, to regere woko, aka piny gi gima ni iye jye bino lokere moyweyere pa mbolera.
61003011	Paka gikipiny me jye ibino nyieko woko, onyo wiripo bedo ji ma chali nedi? Kwo mewin ripo bedo maleŋ ma wilworo Were,
61003012	munyo wikuro Ndelo pa Were to witemo miyo wobin mayot. I ndelo no polo bino waŋ woko gi mach aka lyetho bino nyielo woko gikipiny mani iye.
61003013	To wakuro gima Were otyeko chiko; polo manyien gi piny manyien, kama tiro bino bed'iye pa pecho pere.
61003014	Amomiyo, jowotan, k'onyo wikuro Ndelo no, temi win paka winyalo bedo ma wilony kendo ma bu racho i waŋ Were to wibedo i syem gine.
61003015	Ŋeyi win ni kudirok pa Ruodhiwan, nyutho ni omiyo win hongo ma both, paka omin wan Paulo mamaro ondiko ri win gi ryeko ma Were omiyo go.
61003016	Me a gima go wacho i balwin pere jye munyo ndiko kwoŋ gino. Nitye gikipiny mogo matek niaŋ kwoŋe i balwin pere ma joma kuya kosa joma yengere i yeyo jofuonjo kichar, paka jotimo g'adeche man i Ndiiko Maleŋ. Ameno wegi jokelo kwoŋ gin teko.
61003017	To win, jowotan, paka wityeko ŋeyo gime, onyo gwokere win aka moro wokiri wonyali wondo win gi fuonji ma k'ago mapa joma kilwor chik to wipodho wok i kabedo moido wichung'iye maber.
61003018	To medere win gi dongo i ŋono kodi i ŋeyo Ruoth kendo Jaboth mawan Yesu Kristo. Dwoŋ wobedi ri go, pama kodi chil gi chil. Ameno.
62001001	Wandiko ri win kwoŋ wach ma kwo, motyeko bedo wok i chakirok, ma watyeko winjo odoko watyeko neno gi waŋ wan, watyeko kikaŋasa, aka chingi wan otyeko geyo.
62001002	Kwo no obino ma nenere; waneno amomiyo waluwo kwoŋe, aka watito ri win kwoŋ kwo makirum monwaŋo nitye gi Bawan aka onenere ri wan.
62001003	Gima watyeko neno gi winjo ama watito ri win bende, ŋey wibende wibedi kanyachiel gi wan i riwirok ma wani gine gi Bawan kodi Wuode Yesu Kristo.
62001004	Wandiko gime ŋey kisangala mawan wobedi mopoŋ.
62001005	Onyo me a mikwenda ma watyeko winjo bongi wuodi Were munyo watito ri win: Were obedo lero aka ongoye mudho i go kada mathin.
62001006	Amomiyo ka wawacho ni wanitye i riwirok gine, mato kwo mawan nitye i mudho, meno kareno watwodo aka tim mawan ongoy'iye adyeri.
62001007	To ka kwo mawan nitye i lero paka go won nitye i lero, meno wanitye i riwirok gi jowoti wan, aka remo pa Yesu, Wuodi Were, loko wan molony kwoŋ recho jye.
62001008	Ka wawacho ni wangoye gi recho, meno wawondere aka adyeri ongoye i wan.
62001009	To ka watucho recho mawan ri Were, go genere kendo otire aka bino chwako gimarecho mawan, to lonyo wan kwoŋ tim mawan marecho jye.
62001010	Ka wawacho ni fuodi wakitimo gimarach meno waloko Were jatwodo, aka wach pere ongoye i kwo mawan.
62002001	Andiko ri win gime, nyithindho paran, ŋey wikiri witimi gimarach, to ka moro otimo gimarach, wanitye gi Yesu Kristo ŋatotire, ma pido ri wan bongi Bamere.
62002002	Go won a rachow ma miyo ichwako gimarecho mawan, to ki gimarecho mawan kende, to gimarecho pa ji jye ma piny.
62002003	Me a gima miyo waridho ni waŋeyo go: ka wawinjo or pere.
62002004	Ka moro wacho ni, “Aŋeyo go,” to kiwinji or pere, meno ŋato jatwodo aka adyeri ongoye i go.
62002005	To ŋata winjo wach pere, meno a ŋata mar pere ri Were ochowere kichutho. Me apaka wanyalo ridho ni wakwo i Were:
62002006	ŋata wacho ni go kwo i Were ripo bedo gi tim paka chango apa Yesu Kristo.
62002007	Jowotan mamaro, or ma andiko ri win me kinyien; obedo or machon, ma wityeko bedo gine wok chon. Or machon me obedo mikwenda ma wityeko winjo.
62002008	To or m'andiko ri win nyien, aka adyeri mere nenere i Kristo kodi i win bende, rupiri mudho onyo eye woko aka lero maradyeri ama pama onyo meny.
62002009	Ŋata ŋoyo ni go nitye i lero, mato go odak omin, meno fuodi nitye i mudho ayino.
62002010	Ŋata omaro nyawote ama nitye i lero, aka ongoye gi gimoro ma miyo go timo gimarach.
62002011	To ŋata odak nyawote meno nitye i mudho aka woth'iye, aka kuya kama go chom'iye, rupiri mudho otyeko kelo ri go thowaŋ.
62002012	Nyithindho paran, andiko ri win, rupiri otyek chwako gimarecho mewin ru nyingi Kristo.
62002013	Andiko ri win bachere nan, rupiri wiŋeyo ŋata otyeko bedo wok i chakirok. Andiko ri win, soye ma nyaka ay, rupiri wityeko loyo jwogi, Ŋatarach. Andiko ri win nyithindho, rupiri wiŋeyo Were Bawan.
62002014	Andiko ri win, bachere ji, rupiri wiŋeyo go motyeko bedo wok i chakirok. Andiko ri win, soye ma nyaka ay, rupiri winitye gi men; wach pa Were bedo i win, aka wityeko loyo Jaracho.
62002015	Wikiri wimari piny kosa gimoro jye mapiny. Ka moro omaro piny meno mar pere ri Bawan ongoye.
62002016	Ato gimoro jye ma piny paka awanya marach ma del, kodi awanya ma waŋ jo, kodi pakirok ru kwoŋ bedo gima dhano ni gine kosa m'otimo, kobedo apa Bawan, to obedo apa piny ayino.
62002017	Piny kodi kisangala mere jye rumo; to joma timo gima Were mito jobino kwo chil gi chil.
62002018	Nyithindho paran, kole me ndir ma gike; ato wityeko winjo paka Jakwor pa Kristo bino; gunyoni jokwor pa Kristo kweth jotyeko nenere, aka meno apaka waŋeyo ni gike ni chiegin.
62002019	Adyer ji me oido jokiripi i kweth mawan, amomiyo joweyo wan; bedi joripo i kweth mawan, di jobedo gi wan, to joeye ŋey wonenere kamaler ni ongoye moro kwoŋ jo ma iyadyeri oido joripo i kweth mawan.
62002020	To Kristo otyeko wiro kwoŋ win mo ma Chuny Maleŋ amomiyo wiŋeyo adyeri.
62002021	Ri ameno andiko ri win, ki ni rupiri wikuya adyeri; to rupiri wiŋeyo, aka bende wiŋeyo ni ongoye twodo ma wok kwoŋ adyeri.
62002022	Onyo, ŋa ma jatwodo? Jatwodo meno ŋata wacho ni Yesu kobedo Kristo. Aka ŋato jakwor pa Kristo, rupiri go kwero Were Bawan gi Wuode.
62002023	Kole ŋata kwero Wuodi Were meno kwero Bamere bende; odoko ŋata jolo Wuodi Were meno jolo Bamere bende.
62002024	Amomiyo, ridhi win maber kano i chuny win mikwenda ma wiwinjo wok chon. Ka gima wiwinjo wok chon odoŋ i chuny win, meno ndir jye wibino doŋ gi wuode kodi Bamere i kwo mewin.
62002025	Aka me a gima Kristo won gipi ochiko miyo wan: manago kwo makirum.
62002026	Andiko ri win gime ma mako kwoŋ joma jotemo wondo win.
62002027	To ma mako kwoŋ win, Kristo otyeko wiro kwoŋ win mo ma Chuny Maleŋ pere. Ka tekin Chuny Maleŋ pere nitye i win, odoko wikiyeny moro wofuonji win. Kole wiir ma Chuny no won fuonjo win kwoŋ gimoro jye, aka gima go fuonjo obedo adyeri ma kiweno twodo, onyo doŋi win i Kristo.
62002028	Ey, nyithindho paran, nere win i go, ŋey wibedi gi miseni madwoŋ ka go omenyere aka wikopondi ri go ru wichkwot i Ndelo ma go ledwok'iye.
62002029	Wiŋeyo ni Kristo obedo tiro; ri ameno wiŋeyo ni moro jye ma timo gimotire meno go nyathi pa Were.
62003001	Neni win paka Bawan omaro wan moasere momiyo ilwoŋo wan ni nyithindho pa Were, aka iyadyeri, wabedo ameno. Gima omiyo piny kuya wan obedo rupiri koŋeyo Were.
62003002	Jowotan, pama onyo wabedo nyithindho pa Were, aka fuodi kiŋeyere gima wabino bedo. To waŋeyo ni ka Kristo onenere wabino bedo paka go, rupiri wabino neno go paka go nitye won.
62003003	Nyatoro jye ma nitye gi geno me i Kristo ripo lonyo kwo pere paka Kristo olony.
62003004	Moro jye ma timo gimarach meno turo chik pa Were; aka bedo i recho nyutho kwero winjo chik.
62003005	Wiŋeyo ni Kristo omenyere ŋey wokwanyi woko gimarecho mawan, aka go ongoye gi gimarach.
62003006	Amomiyo moro jye ma kwo i Kristo kimedere timo gimarach; to ŋata medere gi timo gimarach meno fuodi koneno go, aka fuodi kuya go.
62003007	Nyithidho paran, dhano moro jye wokiri wowondi win. Nyatoro jye ma timo gimolony meno ŋata otire paka Kristo otire.
62003008	Ŋata medere gi timo gimarecho meno dhano pa jwogi, rupiri jwogi ochako gi recho pere wok chon. Wuodi Were obino ru wach me: reyo woko tich ma jwogi oido otyeko timo.
62003009	Nyathi pa Were mogo jye kimedere gi timo gimarecho, rupiri kodhi pa Were ama nitye i go; aka rupiri Were obedo Bamere, go kidoki ripi medo timo gimarach.
62003010	Me apaka wanyalo poko maber i dyeri nyithindho pa Were kodi apa jwogi: nyatoro jye ma kitimi gimotire kosa ma komaro omin go, meno kobedo nyathi pa Were.
62003011	Kole me a mikwenda ma wityeko winjo wok chon: ni waripo marere.
62003012	Wikiri wibedi paka Kain: go oido obedo apa Jaracho, aka oneko omin won. Raŋo ma Kain oneko omin? Kwoŋbedo tim pere oido recho, aka gikipiny ma omin otimo oido beyo.
62003013	Amomiyo wutimera, wikiri widhyeri ka ji ma piny jodak win.
62003014	Waŋeyo nike watyeko weyo tho to wabino i kwo, rupiri wamaro wutimin wan. Ŋata kimar wadi meno fuodi nitye i tho.
62003015	Ŋata odak omin meno janek; aka wiŋeyo ni janek ongoye gi kwo makirum i go.
62003016	Me apaka waŋeyo gimobedo mar: Kristo omiyo kwo pere ri wan; aka wabende waripo miyo kwo mawan ri wutimin wan.
62003017	Ka dhano oŋaŋ to neno omin nitye i chandi, to kidew kwoŋ omin, go nyalo wacho nedi nike go nitye gi mar i chunye ri Were?
62003018	Nyithindho paran, mar mawan wokiri wobedi nyaka adhok won kende; to ripo bedo maradyeri, ma nyuthere i tim.
62003019	Amomiyo, me apaka wanoŋeyi nike wabedo joma ni g'adyeri, kendo apaka chuny wan bino bedo gi syem ruwaŋ Were:
62003020	kis ka chuny wan nyutho wan banja moro; ato waŋeyo ni Were dwoŋ loyo chuny wan, aka oŋeyo gimoro jye.
62003021	Amomiyo jowotan, ka chuny wan kinyuthi wan banja moro, meno aka wabedo gi miseni ruwaŋ Were,
62003022	aka walimo bonge gimoro jye ma wakwayo, rupiri wawinjo or pere aka watimo gima sangala go.
62003023	Me a gima go oro wan timo: nike waripo yeyo kwoŋ nyingi Wuode Yesu Kristo to wamarere paka Kristo ooro wan timo.
62003024	Nyatoro jye ma winjo or pa Were bedo i Were aka Were bedo i go. Aka me apaka waŋeyo ni Were bedo i wan: waŋeyo kwoŋ Chuny ma go omiyo wan.
62004001	Jowotan ma kachunyan, wikiri wiyeyere gi kis dhano makethere ni go nitye gi Chuny pa Were. Temi win jo ŋey winiaŋ ka adyeri jowok bongi Were, rupiri jotuchi wach matwodo mathoth jotyeko ywoyere i piny jye.
62004002	Me apaka winonyali ŋeyo ŋata nitye gi Chuny pa Were: moro jye ma wacho ni Yesu Kristo olokere dhano meno ma wok bongi Were.
62004003	To moro jye ma kwero gima kwoŋ Yesu meno chuny ma kiwoki bongi Were. Meno obedo chuny pa jakwor pa Kristo ma wiwinjo nike lebino, aka pama otyeko kir tundo i piny.
62004004	To win wibedo apa Were, nyithindho paran, aka wityeko nyalo woko jotuchi wach matwodo, rupiri Ŋata nitye i win dwoŋ loyo ŋata nitye i piny.
62004005	Jo jobedo apa piny, amomiyo joluwo paka piny yenyo aka piny chiko ithe ri jo.
62004006	To wan wabedo apa Were, aka moro jye moŋeyo Were chiko ithe ri wan. To moro jye ma kobedo apa Were kiwinji wan. Me a royo ma wanyalo poko gine Chuny maradyeri kodi chuny matwodo.
62004007	Jowotan, weyi wamarere wini, rupiri mar wok bongi Were. Moro jye mani gi mar obedo nyathi pa Were aka oŋeyo Were.
62004008	Ŋata ongoye gi mar meno kuya Were, rupiri Were obedo mar.
62004009	Me apaka Were onyutho mar pere ri wan: go ooro Wuode achiel gachiel i piny ŋey walimi kwo luwo kwoŋe.
62004010	Me a mar: ki kwoŋbedo ni onwaŋo wamaro Were, to ni go ama omaro wan to dhiro Wuode bedo rachow ma kwanyo woko gimarecho mawan.
62004011	Jowotan mamaro, k'inen me a paka Were omaro wan, meno wabende waripo marok.
62004012	Ongoye ŋata fuodi oneno Were, to ka wamarere, meno Were bedo i wan aka mar pere bino roch maber i wan.
62004013	Me apaka waridho maber ni wanitye i Were aka go bende nitye i wan; go otyeko miyo wan Chuny Maleŋ pere won.
62004014	Aka wawegi waneno aka onyo wawacho ri joman nike Bawan odhiro Wuode bedo Jaboth ri piny.
62004015	Ŋata tucho ni Yesu obedo Wuodi Were, Were bedo i go aka go bende bedo i Were.
62004016	Amomiyo wawegi waŋeyo aka wayeyo mar ma Were nitye gine ri wan. Were obedo mar, aka ŋata bedo i mar meno bedo i Were aka Were bende bedo i go.
62004017	Ameno, mar roch i dyeri wan, aka ŋey wabino bedo gi miseni madwoŋ i ndelo ma thumo banja, rupiri kwo mawan i piny ka chale kodi apa Kristo.
62004018	Lworo ongoye i mar, to mar motire kwanyo woko lworo jye, rupiri lworo wotho gi girachula, aka ŋatalwor meno fuodi mar koroch i chunye.
62004019	Wabedo gi mar rupiri Were ama otelo maro wan.
62004020	Ka nyatoro wacho ni, “Amaro Were,” mato go fuodi odak omin, meno go jatwodo, kwoŋ bedo go kinyali maro Were ma fuodi go koneno, to kwero maro omin ma go otyeko neno.
62004021	Amomiyo, me a or ma Kristo omiyo wan: ni ŋata omaro Were ripo maro omin bende.
62005001	Nyatoro jye ma yeyo ni Yesu obedo Kristo meno go obedo nyathi pa Were; aka ŋata omaro baa nyathi meno ripo maro kir nyathi bende.
62005002	Me apaka waŋeyo nike wamaro nyithindho pa were: ka wamaro Were gi winjo or pere.
62005003	Kole me a dwoŋ maro Were: winjo or pere. Aka or pere kitek ri wan timo,
62005004	rupiri nyathi pa Were jye nyalo woko men pa piny. Me apaka wanyalo loyo men pa piny: waloyo gi yeyo mawan.
62005005	Ongoye ŋata nyalo loyo men pa piny, kwanyo woko ŋata yeyo ni Yesu obedo Wuodi Were.
62005006	Yesu Kristo a ŋata obino gi pi ma batisimo kodi remo pere. Go kobino gi pi kende, to gi pi kodi remo. Aka Chuny Maleŋ won ridho adyeri me, rupiri Chuny Maleŋ obedo adyeri.
62005007	Nitye jokony adek ma ridho adyeri no:
62005008	Chuny, pi, kodi remo; aka jadek no jye joyeyere.
62005009	K'inen wayeyo wach pa ji ka joridho gine adyeri moro, meno waripo yeyo apa Were ma dwoŋ loyo; aka me a wach ma Were ridho kwoŋ Wuode.
62005010	Nyatoro jye ma yeyo Wuodi Were meno ridho adyeri no i chunye; to ŋata kiyeyi Were, meno oloko go jatwodo, rupiri go koyeyo gima Were owacho ma ridho adyeri ma mako kwoŋ Wuode.
62005011	Aka me a wach ma ridho adyeri: ni Were otyeko miyo wan kwo makirum, aka kwo me nwaŋere i Wuode.
62005012	Moro jye ma nitye gi Wuodi Were meno ni gi kwo me; aka moro jye mongoye gi Wuodi Were meno ongoye gi kwo.
62005013	Andiko ri win gime, win ma wiyeyo i nyingi Wuodi Were, winyali ŋeyo nike winitye gi kwo makirum.
62005014	Me amomiyo wanitye gi miseni ruwaŋ were: waridho nike go bino miyo wan gimoro jye ka wakwayo go paka go yenyo.
62005015	Aka ka waŋeyo ni go winjo wan ka wakwayo go gimoro, meno waŋeyo bende nike go bino miyo wan gima wakwayo jye.
62005016	Ka moro oneno omin timo gimarach ma kikel tho, go ripo kwayo, aka Were bino miyo ŋato kwo. Awacho ameno kwoŋ joma gimarecho pajo kikeli tho. To nitye gimarach ma kelo tho, aka akiwachi ni wiripo kwayo Were kwoŋ meno mere.
62005017	Tim jye ma kotire meno gimarach, to nitye gimarecho megi ma kikel tho.
62005018	Waŋeyo nike nyathi pa Were kimedere timo gimarach, rupiri Wuodi Were kuro go maber, aka Jaracho kinyali timo go marach.
62005019	Waŋeyo nike wabedo apa Were aka piny gipi nitye i dhum pa Jaracho.
62005020	Waŋeyo nike Wuodi Were otyeko bino aka omiyo wan niaŋ momiyo waŋeyo Ŋata obedo adyeri. Kwo mawan nitye i Ŋata obedo adyeri, chungo kwoŋ Wuode Yesu Kristo. Me a Were maradyeri won kendo a kwo makirum.
62005021	Nyithindho paran, eye win kwoŋ werin matwodo!
63001001	Balwa mowok bongi Jadwoŋ: Ri dhakodwoŋ moyer kodi nyithindho pere mamaro i adyeri, aka ki an kendan, to ji jye ma bende joŋeyo adyeri jomaro win,
63001002	ru adyeri ma nitye i wan aka bino bedo gi wan ndir jye:
63001003	Weyi Were Bawan kodi Yesu Kristo, Wuodi go, womiyi wan ŋono, wor kodi syem i adyeri kodi mar.
63001004	Asangala ma kichutho ru nwaŋo ni nyithindho perin megi jonitye i adyeri, paka Bawan ooro wan won.
63001005	Amomiyo, akwayin, dhakodwoŋ, ni wamarere win. Me kobedo or manyien ma nyaka andiko rin; to obedo or ma watyeko bedo gine wok chon.
63001006	Aka me a mar: ni wawinji or pere. Paka wityeko winjo wok chon, go oro win bedo gi mar.
63001007	Jotwodo megi jotyeko ywoyirok i piny gipi; ji ma jokiyey ni Yesu Kristo obino i del paka dhano. Ŋata pameno jatwodo, kendo a jakwor pa Kristo.
63001008	Amomiyo, kure win, ŋey gima wityeko tiyo ri go wokiri wobudhi win, to wilim kemba mewin mopoŋ.
63001009	Ŋata kibedi i fuonji pa Kristo, to medere i giman ayino, meno ongoye gi Were. Ŋata doŋ i fuonji, meno nitye gi Bawan kodi Wuode.
63001010	Amomiyo, ka moro bino bongi win, aka kikel fuonji me, wikiri wijoli go pecho mewin; odoko wikiri wimothi go kada ni: “Syem wobedi kodin.”
63001011	Ato ŋata jolo go gi moth meno riwere gine i tim pere marecho.
63001012	Onwaŋo anitye gi wach madit ri win, to kiber awachi ri win i papila kodi vino; kuchiel, ageno lyewo win to waluwo awaŋ g'awaŋ, aka nyaka wabino bedo gi kisangala mopoŋ.
63001013	Nyithindho pa Nyamerin moyer jodhiro rin moth pajo.
64001001	Balwa mowok bongi Jadwoŋ, Ri Gayo nyawotan ma kachunyan, mamaro i adyeri.
64001002	Mere paran, akwayo ni gimoro jye wokidhi rin maber aka ibedi m'ilama i del, paka chunyin olama.
64001003	Abedo gi kisangala madwoŋ munyo jomoyeyo mogo jotundo to jowacho paka initye gi genirok i adyeri kodi paka ndir jye ibedo i adyeri.
64001004	Ongoye gima sangala an loyo ka awinjo ni nyithindho paran joluwo adyeri.
64001005	Mere paran, igenere swa i tich mitimo ri jomoyeyo, kada nende jobedo joma ikuya jo,
64001006	aka jotyeko luwo ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo kwoŋ mar perin. Mondo konyi jo jowomedere gi woth pajo i royo ma bino kisangala Were.
64001007	Kole jochako tich ri Kristo ma jokojolo kony moro jye wok bongi jokafiri.
64001008	Amomiyo, waripo konyo jome, ŋey wariwere gi jo i tich ri adyeri.
64001009	Andiko balwa machiek ri kweth pa jokristo, to Dyoturefe, ma mito bedo marapena i gimoro jye, kiyenyi dewo kwoŋ gima awacho.
64001010	Amomiyo, ka abino, alewodho gimoro jye ma go otyeko timo kamaler: gikipiny marecho ma go luwo kwoŋ wan, kodi twodo pere. To chalo meno jye kirom go, fuodi go kijoli jomoyeyo ka jobino, aka go juko kir joman ma jomito jolo jo to ryemo woko jo i kweth pa jomoyeyo.
64001011	Mere paran, ikiri iluwi ranen marach no, to luw gimaber mere ayino. Nyatoro jye ma timo gimaber bedo apa Were. Aka ŋata timo gimarach meno fuodi koŋeyo Were.
64001012	Dhano jye luwo maber kwoŋ Demeturyo. Aka giradyeri won ama iluwo kwoŋ go. Wabende waluwo maber kwoŋ go, aka wiŋeyo nike gima wawacho obedo giradyeri.
64001013	Onwaŋo anitye gi madit awacha rin, to akotimi ameno i kalamu gi vino.
64001014	To ageno nenin mayot, aka nyaka wabino luwo.
64001015	Syem wobedi kodin. Merin perin jye jodhiro rin moth. Ibende mothi ri wan merin mawan jye.
65001001	An Yuda, jatich pa Yesu Kristo, kendo omin Yakobo, andiko balwa me ri joma Were olwoŋo ma jonitye i mar pa Were Bawan kodi kur pa Yesu Kristo.
65001002	Wor, syem, kodi mar wobedi ri win mathoth.
65001003	Jowotan mamaro, onwaŋo atemo paka anyalo ndiko ri win kwoŋ both ma wan kodi win wani gine, munyo aneno ni yenyere ndiko ri win pama ma miyo win miseni ma lweny ri yeyo ma Were otyeko miyo ji pere dichiel kichutho.
65001004	Kole jomogo motyek thumo ri jo banja wok chon, jotyeko lwi to jodonjo nyaliŋliŋ i dyeri win ma wikineno; jokuya Were aka jokomo fuonji kwoŋ ŋono pa Were ma umo recho pajo aka jokwero Yesu Kristo, ma dwoŋ loyo kendo obedo Ruoth mawan.
65001005	Kada wityeko ŋeyo gime, jye fuodi amito poyo win paka Ruoth obotho ji pa Israel i piny Misir, to rumachien reyo woko ji ma jokwero yeyo.
65001006	Poyi win ni jomalaika ma jokalo kew ma men pajo, to joweyo kabedo pajo, Were okano jo piny i mudho, to tweyo jo gi lijegere ma chil gi chil ri ndelo madwoŋ mibino thum'iye ri jo banja.
65001007	Ameno bende apaka Sodom gi Gomora, kodi tindin mothoko jo ma chango jotimo paka jomalaika jotimo, aka jotimo chot kodi kidakana, jobedo ranen ri ji paka joma chandere i mach chil gi chil.
65001008	Ameno bende, jome lek pajo wondo jo aka miyo jotimo gimarach i delkwoŋ gin won; jochayo men pa Were; odoko jochayo jomalaika ma jo ni gi dwoŋ i polo.
65001009	Kole kada malaika madwoŋ, Mikaeli, kotemo yeto jwogi gi wach marecho munyo jopyemo ni ŋa ma d'otero delkwoŋ Musa, to owacho ni, “Ruoth woayi kwoŋin.”
65001010	To jome joyeto gima jokuya dwoŋ mere; aka gima joŋeyo timo pa lee mongoye gi paro, a gikipiny ma bino reyo jo woko.
65001011	Kidamba wobedi ri jo! Joluwo royo ma Kain chango oluwo; jomunyere i fuonji mokom ru woro, paka chango Balam otimo. Jobino kisika woko ru pyem paka chango Kora gin jotimo.
65001012	Jochalo chilo ma duwo kalima mewin, jokapakapa gi medho aka jochiemo kodi win mongoye wichkwot. Jobedo jokwath ma joparo kwoŋ iyi gin wegi. Jochalo pondeponde ma koyo lera gine to kikel koth. Jochalo yen ma kinyaki olemo kada i chwir, yen motyek fudho woko gi tyendi gin aka jotho woko kichutho.
65001013	Jochalo kitula pa pi i nam, aka tim pajo ma wichkwot yenyo malo pa bwoyo. Jochalo michalin mochot, ma Were otyeko yiko ri jo kabedo ma chil gi chil i mudho.
65001014	Enoka, nyakwar Adam ma nyatirtir i luse marabiryo, chango oluwo kwoŋ jo chon ni, “Neni! Ruoth bino gi jopere maleŋ gana gi gana,
65001015	ma thumo banja ri ji jye, gi nyutho jomarecho jye ma jokilwori Were, tim pajo marecho ma kwero lworo Were, kodi wach marecho ma joma kilwor Were joluwo kwong Were!
65001016	Ji me noknok jogesa aka jopusa jowoti jo; jotiyo g'awanya pajo marecho; wegi joyumere aka jodwoŋo wadi gin, ŋey jowotimi gima wegi joyenyo.”
65001017	To poyi win, merin paran mamaro, gima jomoor pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo jowacho ri win ndir mokadho ni bino timere.
65001018	Jowacho ri win ni, “I ndelo ma rumachien, ji jobino wok ariwa ma jobino nyiero win; ji ma jotiyo g'awanya pajo marecho.”
65001019	Me a ji ma jokelo tyakirok, ma paro pajo marecho dhumo jo, ma jongoye gi Chuny Maleŋ.
65001020	To win, merin paran mamaro, medere win gi dongo i yeyo mewin moasa leŋo; aka kwayi win i men pa Chuny Maleŋ.
65001021	Bedi win i mar pa Were kareno wikuro wor pa Ruodhiwan Yesu Kristo, ma bino kelo ri win kwo makirum.
65001022	Joma fuodi joganagana, nyuthi win jo wor.
65001023	Bothi win joman munyo wifudho jo woko arwat kwoŋ mach. Nyuthi win joman bende wor kareno wikure gi lworo; aka wiripo dak kir ruk pa joma awanya pajo ma kidakana oduwo.
65001024	Ri Ŋata nyalo thyelin m'ikipodho, to kethin ma bu racho i kisangala ma di dwoŋ pere,
65001025	ri Were ma Jaboth mawan achiel kende: wor, dwoŋ, men, kodi dhum wobedi ri go, i ndir mokadho, ma pama, kodi ma chil gi chil, i Yesu Kristo. Ameno.
66001001	Me a wach momenyere ma Were omiyo Yesu Kristo, ŋey wonyuthi jotich pa Were gima ripo timirok mayot. Kristo omiyo gikipiny me oŋeyere ri jatich pere Yohana munyo ooro malaika pere bonge.
66001002	Yohana oridho wach pa Were kodi gima mako kwoŋ adyeri pa Kristo, gi gimoro jye m'oneno.
66001003	Ŋata soma wach atucha me jasilwany, aka jomachiko ithi jo ri wach me gi ketho i chuny jo jo ni gi silwany, rupiri ndir chiegin tundo ma gikipiny me bino timer'iye.
66001004	Ndiiko mowok bongi Yohana ri jomoyeyo ma kitipin abiryo ma i adech ma Asya: Ŋono gi syem wobedi ri win wok bongi Were, ma nitye pama, mobedo chon, odoko ma fuodi bino bedo, kodi ma wok bongi chuny momakere abiryo ma ruwaŋ kom pere madhum,
66001005	kodi ma wok bongi Yesu Kristo, jakony ma genere, Wuode ma Kayo motel chierino go kwoŋ jomotho, aka obedo jadhum pa kerin jye ma piny! Go omaro wan, aka gi remo pere ogonyo wan woko kwoŋ gimarecho mawan,
66001006	aka oloko wan bedo ker, kendo jomachwayo wi alitar pa Were kendo Bamere. Dwoŋ kodi men wobedi ri go chil gi chil. Ameno.
66001007	Panen, go eno bino gi pondeponde! Aka kis waŋ dhano bino neno go, kir joma jochwowo go jye. Ji jye ma piny jobino ywak kwoŋbedo go. Apaka bino bedo! Ameno.
66001008	“Aŋata marapena kendo machowe,” Ruoth Were Majameni jye wacho; go ma nitye pama, mobedo chon, kendo bino bedo.
66001009	An Yohana, omin win ma nitye gi win i Yesu i chandirok, kodi i Ker pere, kodi i chiro teko. An onwaŋo obolan i kigoda ma pi othoko ma Patmos ru fuonjo wach pa Were kodi bedo jakony ri adyeri pa Yesu.
66001010	Hongo no oido obedo ndelo pa Ruoth, aka Chuny Maleŋ onwaŋo ni kodan, to awinjo dwondi nyatoro yu ŋeyan ka koko pa gwara ni,
66001011	“Ndiki gima ineno jye i kitawo, aka idhiri ri kitipin abiryo mapa jomoyeyo ma Efeso, Simiruna, Perugamo, Thyatira, Sarudi, Filadefya kodi Lawodisya.”
66001012	Awiro waŋan chien munyo ayenyo neno ŋata oluwo kodan; to munyo awire, aneno raŋaw talin motim ma zawabu abiryo,
66001013	aka i dyeri gikipiny no, aneno ŋat mochalo Wuodi Dhano, moruko kanzu mabor to karo i kore del ma zawabu.
66001014	Wiye kodi yewiye oido tar pa yer rombo matar, waŋe oido chalo mach malyel,
66001015	tyende oido pilin pa nyweny monyiel i kendo malyeth, aka dwonde oido chalo derino ma gorok pa pi i nam.
66001016	I chinge marachuch, go oido otiŋo michalin abiryo, aka abor mabith ma nyalewe aryo owok i dhoke, aka nyime onwaŋo chalo waŋchieŋ malyel gi men mere jye.
66001017	Munyo aneno go, apodho dho tyende pa ŋatotho, to go ogeyan gi chinge marachuch to wacho ni, “Ikiri ilwori gimoro, me an, an marapena kendo machowe odoko akwo;
66001018	onwaŋo atho, to neni, onyo akwo chil gi chil. Anitye gi men kwoŋ tho kodi piny pa jomotho jye.
66001019	Amomiyo, ndiki gim'ineno, ma pama kodi ma bino timere rumachien.
66001020	Me a dwoŋ nyaliŋliŋ kwoŋ michalin abiryo mineno i chingan marachuch no, kodi raŋaw talin ma zawabu: michalin abiryo no obedo jomalaika ma kitipin abiryo mapa jomoyeyo, aka giŋawo talin abiryo meno kitipin abiryo mapa jomoyeyo no.
66002001	“Ri malaika ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Efeso ndiki ni: “Me a mikwenda mowok bongi ŋata otiŋo michalin abiryo i chinge marachuch, aka wotho i dyeri raŋaw abiryo ma talin.
66002002	Aŋeyo tim perin, paka itiyo matek aka ichiro teko mabino rin. Aŋeyo nike ikijoli ji marecho, aka ityeko kikaŋasa joma ŋoyo nike jobedo jomoor kere to be, aka inwaŋo ni jobedo jotwodo.
66002003	Aŋeyo ni ityeko chiro teko i nyingan, ma chunyin koŋedhere.
66002004	To kende me a gima anwaŋo kwoŋin ma kotire: ityeko bolo woko mar moido ndir no itelo bedo gine ran.
66002005	Poyi paka ipodho wok kama bor! Ŋuti aka idok'itimi gima chango ipen timo. Ka ikiŋuto kwoŋ gimarecho perin, alebino bongin to akwanyo woko raŋaw perin ma talin i kabedo mere.
66002006	To me a gima thyelin: wikwero gima jopa Nikola jotimo, paka abende akwero.
66002007	“Amomiyo, ŋata ni gi ithe, wowinji gima Chuny wacho ri kitipin pa jomoyeyo! Ri joma joloyo ratem abino miyo jo men ma chamo yath ma kwo ma nitye i Ndelo pa Were.
66002008	“Ri malaika ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Simiruna ndiki ni: “Me mikwenda ma wok bongi ŋat marapena kendo machowe, m'otho aka odoko onyo kwo.
66002009	Aŋeyo chandirok kodi chandi perin; aŋeyo nike ijachandi, to iyadyeri iŋaŋ! Aŋeyo recho ma joma ŋoyo nike jobedo Joyudaya mato kere jokobedo, jotimo rin; meno joma nitye i achiel gi Sitan!
66002010	Ikiri ilwori chandirok ma chiegin bino rin. Awacho rin ni, jwogi bino bolo megi kwoŋ win i jera paka ratem; chandirok mewin bino chowo ndelo apar. Bedi gi genirok tundo tho, aka abino miyin sangarya ma kwo.
66002011	“Amomiyo ŋata nigi ithe, wowinji gima Chuny wacho ri kitipin pa jomoyeyo! “Joma joloyi ratem jokolimi litho ma tho mararyo.
66002012	“Ri malaika ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Perugamo ndiki ni: “Me mikwenda ma wok bongi ŋata nitye g'abor mabith ma nyalewe aryo.
66002013	Aŋeyo ni kama ibed'iye, a kama Sitan ojeng'iye kom pere madhum. To ichwire i nyingan, aka ikiweyo medirok gi yeyo perin kwoŋan kada i ndir ma Antipa, jakony paran mogenere onek'iye i tindi mewin kenyo kama Sitan bed'iye.
66002014	To me a gikipiny manok ma anwaŋo kwoŋin ma kotire: Winitye gi jomogo i dyeri win kenyo ma joluwo fuonji pa Balam, mofuonjo Balak nger ma ywayo chuny ji ma Israel jowotimi gimarach munyo jochamo riŋo mochow gine chal pa werin makichar, gi timo chot.
66002015	Meno apaka wibende winitye gi joma joluwo fuonji pa Nikola i dyeri win.
66002016	Amomiyo ŋuti win kwoŋ gimarecho mewin! Ka kameno alebino bongi win mayot to alwenyo gi jono kodi abor ma wok i dhokan.
66002017	“Amomiyo, ŋata nitye gi ithe, wowinji gima Chuny wacho ri kitipin pa jomoyeyo! “Ŋata loyo ratem abino miyo go chiemo mopan milwoŋo ni manu. Abino bende miyo go tele matar, mondik'iye nyingi jo Manyien, ma ŋata omiy gino kende ama won ŋeyo.
66002018	“Ri malaika ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Thyatira ndiki ni: “Me mikwenda ma wok bongi Wuodi Were, ma waŋe lyel pa mach, ma tyende pilin pa nyweny ywel morudi.
66002019	Aŋeyo tim perin, mar kodi yeyo perin, tich perin gi chiro chandirok perin, odoko aŋeyo ni pama onyo imedo tich loyo kama ichak'iye.
66002020	To gima anwaŋo kwoŋin marach ame: ijolo dhako ma nyinge Jezebel, ma won lwoŋere ni jatuchi wach pa Were aka fuonjo odoko bano jotich paran i timo tim ma wichkwot gi chamo riŋo mochow gine chal pa werin makichar.
66002021	Atyeko miyo go hongo ma weyo woko gimarecho pere, to go kimiti weyo tim pere ma wichkwot.
66002022	Kuri inen! Abino pyelo go wi kitanda ma chandirok, aka abino miyo jomoido jotimo gine chot bedo i chandirok malith, kwanyo woko ka joŋuto gikipiny marecho ma jotimo kodi go.
66002023	Abino kisika nyithindho pere bende, aka kitipin pa jomoyeyo jye jobino ŋeyo nike a jamenyi chuny ji gi ŋeyo paro pa ji. Abino chulo kis dhano kwoŋ win chungo kwoŋ gima go otimo.
66002024	“To jomodoŋ kwoŋ win i Thyatira, ma jokiluwi fuonji pere no aka fuodi jokofuonjere ryeko pa Sitan ma jolwoŋo ni, ‘nyaliŋliŋ mathuth,’ onyo awacho ri win ni akokethi peko man kwoŋ win.
66002025	To maki win matek gima wini gine chuka anobin.
66002026	Ri ŋata loyo ratem, ma medere gi timo gima amito kir i gike, abino miyo go men ma dhumo piny;
66002027	go bino dhumo jo gi luth manyweny to ŋinyo jo woko pa degi malowo, paka awon atyeko nwaŋo men madhum bongi Baba.
66002028	Aka abino miyo go sulwe modikini.
66002029	Nata ni gi ithe, wowinji gima Chuny wacho ri kitipin pa jomoyeyo.
66003001	“Ri malaika ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Sarudi ndiki ni: “Me mikwenda ma wok bongi ŋata nitye gi Chuny momakere abiryo mapa Were kodi michalin abiryo. Aŋeyo tim perin; iterere pa ŋata kwo mato ityeko tho!
66003002	Amomiyo chiewi, aka imedi tich kwoŋ nyaka gima fuodi ini gine, ma fuodi kotho jye, rupiri fuodi akinen i tim perin gima otire ruwaŋ Were paran.
66003003	Amomiyo poyi gima ofuonjin aka odoko iwinjo; maki gino aka ŋuti kwoŋ gimarecho perin. To ka ikichiewi, alebino bongin pa jakwo, aka ikoŋeyi kada hongo ma alebino rin iye.
66003004	To nitye nyaka ji manok kwoŋ win i Sarudi kenyo ma fuodi jokoduwo nengin pajo gi chilo. Jobino wotho kodan i ruk matar rupiri joripo gine.
66003005	Ŋata loyo ratem bino rukere i ruk matar ameno, aka akorey woko nyinge i kitawo ma kwo aka abino tucho nyinge i waŋ Baba kodi jomalaika pere.
66003006	Amomiyo ŋata ni gi ithe, wowinji gima Chuny wacho ri kitipin pa jomoyeyo.
