66003007	“Ri malaika ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Filadefya ndiki ni: “Me mikwenda ma wok bongi Ŋataleŋ kendo ŋatobedo Maradyeri, ma tiŋo rayaw pa Daudi, ma k'oyawo gimoro nyatoro kinyali chiego, kendo gima go ochiego nyatoro kinyali yawo.
66003008	Aŋeyo tim perin. Kole atyeko yawo rin dhoot ma nyatoro kinyal chiego; aŋeyo nike initye gi men manok; to ityeko luwo fuonji paran aka ikikwedere kwoŋ nyingan. Atyeko yawo rin thigo ma moro kinyali chiego.
66003009	Ere onyo akidho kelo kitipa ma ji pa Sitan, ma jotwodo aka joŋoyo nike jobedo Joyudaya, mato jokobedo; abino kelo jo bongin to jogoyo chongi gin piny ruwaŋin to joniaŋ ni kere amarin.
66003010	Kwoŋbedo ikuro or paran ma diyo ich gi chiro chandirok; abino kurin maber i ndir ma teko obin'iye ri piny gipi ma temo ji jye.
66003011	Abino mayot; maki maber gima ini gine, aka moro wokiri womayin sangarya perin.
66003012	Abino loko ŋata oloy ratem siro ma Ot pa Were paran, aka go kodoko owok iye. Abino ndiko kwoŋe nyingi Were paran, kodi nyingi tindi pa Were paran, Yerusalem manyien, ma bino loro piny wok i polo bongi Were paran; kodi nyingan manyien won bende.
66003013	“Amomiyo ŋata ni gi ithe, wowinji gima Chuny wacho ri kitipin pa jomoyeyo.
66003014	“Ri malaika ma kitipa pa jomoyeyo ma Lawodisya ndiki ni: “Me mikwenda mowok bongi ŋata lwoŋere ni Ameno, jakony ma genere odoko maradyeri, mobedo kachakirok ma chwech pa Were:
66003015	Aŋeyo tim perin; aŋeyo nike ichali pi ma morimor. Bedi iŋich kichutho kosa ilyeth ayino kichutho dober!
66003016	To paka imorimor nyaka masisiri, aka ikiŋich odoko ikilyeth, aleŋulin woko wok i dhokan!
66003017	Ato iwacho ni, ‘Aŋaŋ kendo anitye maber,’ kendo ni, ‘Anitye gi gimoro jye mayenyo.’ To ikuya paka ichandere; kole yenyere womak kodin wor ayino, ijachandi, initye kinyoro, aka waŋin jye otho.
66003018	Amomiyo, amiyin ryeko ni nyiewi zawabu bongan, moyik gi mach, aka inoŋaŋ. Nyiewi nengin matar bende iruki aka iumi gine kinyoro perin ma kelo rin wichkwot no. Nyiewi yen ma waŋ jo bende ikethi i waŋin, aka ŋey inyali neno.
66003019	Joma amaro, apusa jo odoko atwenyo jo. Amomiyo bedi g'adyeri kendo ŋuti kwoŋ gimarecho perin.
66003020	Aka ee achungo dho thigo agudo; ka moro owinjo dwondan to yawo, abino donjo i ot pere to achiemo gine, to bende chiemo kodan.
66003021	Ŋata oloyi lweny abino miyo men ma bedo bongan i kom paran madhum, paka abende atyeko loyo lweny aka onyo abedo kabuti Baba i kom pere madhum.
66003022	“Amomiyo, ŋata ni gi ithe, wowinji gima Chuny wacho ri kitipin pa jomoyeyo!”
66004001	I hongo me alimo menyirok man, aka aneno dhoot moyaw i polo. Aka dwondi jo moluwo gi derino paka gwara, monwaŋo atyeko winjo chon ka luwo kodan, owacho ni, “Biye ka, anyuthin gima bino timere rumachien.”
66004002	Piyo piyo Chuny Maleŋ opoŋ kwoŋan, to kom pa Were madhum i polo bino ruwaŋan, kareno nitye ŋatobediye.
66004003	Ŋata obedo no oido lyel pa gee mawelo ma nyaboke pendi pa jaspa, mobokere pa kanelyan, aka lifudu ma rangi mere oruwere kweth pa emerad oido othoko kom madhum no.
66004004	I thach mothoko kom no onwaŋo nitye kombere pyero aryo g'aŋwen man, ma jodongo pyero aryo g'aŋwen i ruk matar jobed'iye, aka joruko sangarya ma zawabu i wiyi jo.
66004005	I kom madhum no oido wok pilin, kodi derino kodi mwoch pa lithkoth. Aka onwaŋo nitye talin abiryo ma lyel yu waŋ kom no, mobedo chuny momakere abiryo mapa Were.
66004006	Kendo yu waŋ kom madhum no onwaŋo nitye gima chale pa jwom ma ndewiro, maler pa gee maminyin. Thoko kom no, thenge korin gi korin, onwaŋo nitye chwech makwo ma waŋ gin nityatya kis kamoro, yu nyim jo kodi yu ŋey jo jye.
66004007	Gimakwo marapena ochale kodi simbwor; mararyo ochale kodi thwon; aka maradek wiye gi waŋe ochalo apa dhano; aka maraŋwen ochalo ango moyaro bwombe pa winyo ma ringo i hongo.
66004008	Kis achiel kwoŋ chwech makwo no oido nitye gi bwombe auchiel, aka omore gi waŋe kwoŋe gipi kir i pendi bwombe. Chwech no jowero ma jokiliŋ wor g'odyechieŋ ni: “Maleŋ, maleŋ, maleŋ, Ruoth Were Majameni jye, mobedo chon, ma pama nitye, aka lebino.”
66004009	Hongo jye ma chwech aŋwen makwo no jomiy'iye ŋatobedo wi kom madhum, ma kwo chil gi chil no dwoŋ, kodi wor, kodi fuoy,
66004010	jodongo pyero aryo g'aŋwen no jogore piny ruwaŋ ŋatobedo wi kom madhum, to jolamo ŋata kwo chil gi chil no. Jobolo sangarya pajo runyim kom madhum, aka jowacho ni:
66004011	“Ruoth mawan kendo Were! Iripere limo dwoŋ, gi wor kodi men, rupiri ichweyo gikipiny jye, aka gi mito perin ama omiyo jokwo.”
66005001	Gikenyo aneno papila momin mondik thenge aryo jye ma ŋatobedo wi kom madhum otiŋo i chinge marachuch, aka omwon gi gimwono abiryo mothore.
66005002	Aka aneno malaika ma jameni moluwo gi derino madwoŋ ni, “Ŋata ripere gi halo gimwono to yawo papila momin no?”
66005003	To ongoye moro monwaŋere i polo, i piny, kosa i pendi lowo ma d'onyalo yawo papila momin no gi neno iye.
66005004	Aywak maloŋo rupiri ongoye ŋata onwaŋere ma oripo nyalo yawo papila momin no kosa neno gima n'iye.
66005005	Gikenyo achiel kwoŋ jodongo no owacho ran ni, “Ikiri iywaki. Panen! Simbwor ma nono pa Yuda, nyakwar Daudi otyeko loyo lweny aka go nyalo halo woko gimwono abiryo mothore no jye to yawo papila momin no.”
66005006	Aka aneno Nyathi rombo moro ochungo i dyere dho kom madhum, ma chwech makwo aŋwen kodi jodongo no jothoko. Nyathi rombo no ochalo pa monek ma chowirok. Rombo no onwaŋo nitye gi tunge abiryo kodi waŋe abiryo, ma jobedo chuny momakere abiryo mapa Were modhir i piny gipi.
66005007	Nyathi rombo no okidho to kwanyo papila momin ma ŋatobedo wi kom madhum oido otiŋo i chinge marachuch no.
66005008	Munyo go okwanyo gino ameno, chwech makwo aŋwen no kodi jodongo pyero aryo g'aŋwen no jogore piny ruwaŋ Nyathi rombo no. Kis dhano oido otiŋo tongol, kodi atewe ma zawabu ma buban opoŋ'iye, mobedo kwayo pa ji pa Were.
66005009	Jowero wer manyien ni, “Iripere gi kwanyo papila momin gi halo woko gima omwon gine. Kole onekin, aka gi remo perin, inyiewo ri Were ji maleŋ, wok i nonin jye, dhudhok jye, piny jye kodi ji ma piny gipi.
66005010	Iloko jo ker pa jochwayi ri Were wi alitar; aka jobino dhumo piny.”
66005011	Odoko aneno, aka awinjo dwondi jomalaika gana gi gana! Jochungo jothoko kom madhum, kodi chwech aŋwen no, kodi jodongo no,
66005012	to jowero gi dwondi jo ma malo ni, “Nyathi rombo monek paka rachow ripere limo men madhum, ŋaŋo, ryeko kodi mwamba, Wor, dwoŋ, kodi pak!”
66005013	Aka awinjo chwech jye ma polo, ma piny, kodi ma pendi lowo, kodi chwech jye ma nam, gi chwech jye ma piny gipi munyo jowero ni, “Ri ŋata bedo wi kom madhum, kodi ri Nyathi rombo, pak kodi wor, kodi dwoŋ kodi men wobedi chil gi chil!”
66005014	Aka chwech aŋwen no jodwoko ni, “Ameno!” To jodongo no jogore piny munyo jolamo Were.
66006001	Gikenyo aneno Nyathi rombo munyo halo woko achiel kwoŋ gimwono papila abiryo t'awinjo achiel kwoŋ chwech aŋwen cha wacho i dwonde ma chalo lithkoth ma mwoch ni, “Biye!”
66006002	Aŋiyo aka ruwaŋan kenyo oido nitye kayina matar. Ŋata obedo wi kayina no otiŋo asere, aka omiy go sangarya. Go okadho paka jaloyi lweny woloyi lweny kichutho.
66006003	Gikenyo Nyathi rombo ohalo woko gimwono papila mararyo; aka awinjo chwech mararyo wacho ni, “Biye!”
66006004	Kayina man owok, mobokere; ŋatobedo wiye omiy men ma kwanyo woko syem i piny, nike ji jowonekere; ato omiy go abor mapando swa.
66006005	Gikenyo Nyathi rombo ohalo woko gimwono papila maradek; aka awinjo chwech maradek wacho ni, “Biye!” Aŋiyo, t'aneno kayina machol; ŋatobedo wiye otiŋo rapor i chinge ma kipima chiemo.
66006006	Awinjo gima ochale pa dwondi nyatoro mowok i dyeri chwech aŋwen no ka wacho ni, “Rapor ma romo kikopo mathin ma ŋano wotana welo ma siringi gana achiel, aka rapor ma romo kikopere adek ma bel wotana welo ma siringi gana achiel. Aka ikiri inyieki mo kodi vini!”
66006007	Gikenyo Nyathi rombo ohalo woko gimwono papila maraŋwen t'awinjo chwech maraŋwen wacho ni, “Biye!”
66006008	Aŋiyo, t'aneno kayina ma dibworo; ŋatobedo wiye nyinge ilwoŋo ni Tho, aka piny pa jomotho luwo go yu ŋeye dho tyende. Omiy jo men kwoŋ achiel wiy aŋwen ma piny, neko woko ji g'abor kodi kech, kodi two, kodi ogwange mager ma piny.
66006009	Gikenyo Nyathi rombo ohalo woko gimwono papila marabich; t'aneno i tyendi alitar, chuny ji monek rupiri jotito wach pa Were aka jobedo jogenirok i wodho kony i wach no.
66006010	Jokoko gi derino madwoŋ ni, “Ruoth Majameni Jye, maleŋ aka jaradyeri! Kir keraŋo aka inothumi banja ri ji ma piny t'imiyo jo girachula ru neko wan?”
66006011	Dhano jye omiy nanga matar: owachi ri jo ni jowoywomere mathin nyuka kama welo pa jotich jowoti jo kodi wutimin jo ma bende iripo nekojo paka onek jo worumi.
66006012	Aneno Nyathi rombo halo woko gimwono papila marauchiel. Yengirok pa piny obedo madwoŋ, to chieŋ lokere machol, paka bongi morwaki i chwodho, to dwe lokere mobokere tektek pa remo;
66006013	michalin jopodho piny wok i polo, paka nyandere manumu ma podho wok wiyadhe ka koyo madwoŋ oyengo.
66006014	Polo oleny woko pa papila mimino, aka gote jye kodi kigoda lowo jye mani i dyer nam okwany woko i kabedo pajo.
66006015	Gikenyo kerere ma piny, jodhum kodi jotel ma lweny, joŋaŋo kodi jomen, kodi ji man jye, ŋechin kodi joma ni syem, jopondo i ŋungin kodi i tyendi telin ma gote.
66006016	Jolwoŋo gote kodi telin ni, “Ryewere win kwoŋ wan wipan wan ri waŋ ŋatobedo wi kom madhum, kodi ri keme pa Nyathi rombo!
66006017	Kole ndelo ma keme pajo otundo, ŋata onyal chiro ŋa?”
66007001	Rumachien aneno jomalaika aŋwen jochungo i tum aŋwen ma piny, munyo jogeŋo koyo aŋwen ma piny, ŋey koyo moro wokiri wokudhi wi piny, kosa wi nam, kosa kwoŋ yath moro jye.
66007002	Aka aneno malaika man bino wok yu Wokchieŋ kodi gimwono ranyuth pa Were makwo. Go olwoŋo gi dwonde mamalo jomalaika aŋwen ma Were oido omiyo jo men ma nyieko piny kodi nam.
66007003	Malaika no owacho ni, “Wikiri winyieki piny, kosa nam, kosa yen, chuka wanokethi ranyuth kwoŋ jotich pa Were mawan ma wamwono i nyim jo.”
66007004	Aka awinjo welo pa joma okethi ranyuth kwoŋ jo, 144,000, wok i nonin jye mapa nyithindho pa Israel.
66007005	Nono pa Yuda, gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Ruben, gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Gadi,
66007006	gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Aser, gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Naftal, gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Manase gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo;
66007007	i nono pa Simeyo, gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Levi, gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Isakar,
66007008	gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Zebulun, gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Yozefu, gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo; i nono pa Benjamin, gana apar g'aryo moketh ranyuth kwoŋ jo.
66007009	Gikenyo aŋiyo, t'aneno lwak ji madwoŋ mongoye ŋata d'onyalo kwano jo! Jowok i piny jye, i nonin gi ji ma dhudhok jye, to jochungo ruwaŋ kom madhum mapa Nyathi rombo, kareno joruko nengin matar, aka jotiŋo thith i chingi jo.
66007010	Jokoko gi dwondi jo mamalo ni, “Both wok bongi Were ma bedo wi kom madhum kodi Nyathi rombo!”
66007011	Jomalaika jye oido jochungo jothoko kom madhum no kodi jodongo no kodi chwech aŋwen makwo no. Gikenyo jogore piny gi nyimi jo ruwaŋ kom madhum no to jolamo Were
66007012	ka jowacho ni, “Ameno! Pak kodi dwoŋ, kodi ryeko kodi fuoy, kodi wor, kodi men, kodi nyalo wobedi ri Were mawan chil gi chil! Ameno!”
66007013	Achiel kwoŋ jodongo no openjan ni, “Meno jokune ma jorukere i nengin matar no, kendo jowok kune?”
66007014	Adwoko ni, “Jadwoŋ, iŋat'iŋeyo.” Go owacho ran ni, “Me a ji ma jowok i chandirok madwoŋ. Jolwoko ruk pajo to joloko matar i remo pa Nyathi rombo.
66007015	Meno amomiyo jochungo ruwaŋ kom pa Were madhum aka onyo jotiyo ri go wor g'odyechieŋ i Ot pere. Ŋata bedo wi kom madhum bino kuro jo kareno bedo gi jo kenyo.
66007016	Jokowinji kech gi riyo kendo; kendo chieŋ kosa lyetho korewi jo;
66007017	ato Nyathi rombo ma nitye i dyeri kom madhum, bino bedo jakwath pajo; bino leko jo to tero jo yu waŋ pi makwo; aka Were bino yweyo woko pigi waŋ jo kichutho.”
66008001	Munyo Nyathi rombo ohalo woko gimwono papila marabiryo, liŋ obedo i polo chowo hongo ma romo adech sawa gipi.
66008002	Gikenyo aneno jomalaika abiryo ma jochungo ruwaŋ Were; omiy jo gwarin abiryo.
66008003	Malaika man monwaŋo nitye kodi giketho chukmach ma waŋo buban, motim gi zawabu, obino to chungo chiegin g'alitar. Omiy go buban madit ma womedi gi kwayo pa ji maleŋ pa Were aka wochwayi wi alitar ma zawabu ma dho kom madhum.
66008004	Yiro mowok i buban ma waŋ, kanyachiel gi kwayo pa ji maleŋ pa Were, oidho malo bongi Were wok i chingi malaika no.
66008005	Gikenyo malaika no okwanyo giketho chuk no, opoŋ'iye mach wok i alitar to wok to bolo i piny. Gino omwoch pa lithkoth gi derino, gi pilin pa koth, kodi yengirok pa piny.
66008006	Gikenyo jomalaika abiryo kodi gwarin pajo abiryo joyikere chako kudho.
66008007	Malaika marapena okudho gwara pere, to pe kodi mach moruwere gi remo wok to oy ri piny. Achiel kwoŋ adek ma piny owaŋ, to achiel kwoŋ adek ma yen waŋ woko, to lum monwaŋo nyabokependi jye waŋ woko.
66008008	Gikenyo malaika mararyo okudho gwara pere, to gimoro ma chalo got madwoŋ, ma lyel mach, bolere i nam.
66008009	Achiel kwoŋ adek ma nam olokere remo; achiel kwoŋ adek ma gikipiny makwo jye ma pi jotho woko, to achiel kwoŋ adek ma mel jye nyiekere woko.
66008010	Gikenyo malaika maradek okudho gwara pere, to michala mombo, malyel pa mach odingili gore piny wok i polo, aka opodho wi achiel kwoŋ adek ma wakawaka, kodi wi waŋ pi.
66008011	Nyingi michala no obedo Kecho. Achiel kwoŋ adek ma pi olokere ma kech, to ji mathoth jotho ru madho pi ma kech no.
66008012	Gikenyo malaika maraŋwen okudho gwara pere, to achiel kwoŋ adek ma waŋchieŋ mukere woko, kodi achiel kwoŋ adek ma dwe, kodi achiel kwoŋ adek ma michalin; ameno cholo obedo i achiel kwoŋ adek ma lyel pajo; lero oido ongoye i achiel kwoŋ adek marodyechieŋ kodi achiel kwoŋ adek ma wor bende.
66008013	Munyo fuodi aŋiyo, awinjo ango moido ringo malo swa i koyo munyo koko gi dwonde mamalo ni, “Awi kidamba! Kidamba! Kidamba kidho bedo ri ji ma piny ru derino ma gwarin ma jomalaika modoŋ adek jochiegin kudho!”
66009001	Gikenyo malaika marabich okudho gwara pere, to aneno michala moro opodho wi piny wok i polo malo; omiy michala no rayaw ma mwombe maluth ma bu gike.
66009002	Malaika no oyawo mwombe no, aka yiro owok iye, pa yiro mawok i kendo mombo. Yiro no oloko lero ma chieŋ kodi polo ma chol.
66009003	Aka bonyo oloro piny wok i yiro no, aka omiy jo men ma chale kodi apa thwolgwok ma piny.
66009004	Owachi ri jo ni jokiri jowonyieki lum, kosa yen, kosa gimotwi moro jye; to jowotimi racho kwoŋ ji ma jongoye kodi ranyuth pa Were i nyim jo kende.
66009005	Koyeyi jo neko ji me, to miyo jo achanda kende chowo hongo ma dwe abich. Litho ma ji jolimo ochale gi litho ma dhano winjo ka thwolgwok okayo go.
66009006	I hongo no ji jobino rango tho, to jokonwaŋ; jobino yenyo tho, to tho bino yombo jo.
66009007	Bonyo no oido jochalo kayina ma joyikere ri lweny; i wiy jo jobedo kodi gima ochalo sangarya ma zawabu, aka nyim jo ochale kodi nyim ji.
66009008	Yewiy jo ochale kodi yewiy mon, laki jo ochale gi laki simbwor.
66009009	Kor gin ochale pa oum kodi kwot ma nyweny, aka derino ma bwombi gin otimo ochale kodi derino pa chawula ma kayina mathoth joywayo ka joredo yu lweny.
66009010	Jobedo gi yiw gin mani gi lake ma wodho kwir, ma chale kodi apa thwolgwok, aka jobedo gi men ma kelo litho kwoŋ ji gi yiw gin chowo hongo ma dwe abich no.
66009011	Jobedo gi kere madhumo jo mobedo malaika ma kuro mwombe maluth ma bu gike. Nyinge i Dhoyudaya bedo Abadon; aka i Dhoyunani bedo Apolyon (Dwoŋ mere ni Janek).
66009012	Chandirok marapena orumo; odoŋ chandirok man aryo ma fuodi lebino.
66009013	Gikenyo Malaika marauchiel okudho gwara pere, to awinjo dwondi jo mowok i tungi alitar aŋwen ma zawabu mochungo rowaŋ Were.
66009014	Dwondi jo no owacho ri malaika marauchiel mani gi gwara no ni, “Gonyi jomalaika aŋwen motwey jo dho jwom madwoŋ milwoŋo ni Yufurate!”
66009015	Gikenyo ogony jomalaika aŋwen no, monwaŋo otyek yiko jo kichutho ri sawa, gi ndelo, gi dwe, gi oro mere, ma neko achiel kwoŋ adek ma thotho pa ji jye.
66009016	Owach ran welo pa lwak jolweny ma joŋwecho gi kayina; obedo kiti miya aryo (milyon miya aryo).
66009017	Aka i menyirok no aneno kayina kodi wegi mere ama: oido joruko kwot ma nyweny i kor gin, mobokere pa mach, molyewa kodi ma nyatongi gweno pa salufa. Wich kayina no jochalo wich simbwor, aka i dhok gin owok mach, yiro, kodi buru salufa ma moko mach i kibirit.
66009018	Thoyamo adek me: mach, yiro, kodi buru salufa ma moko mach i kibirit ma jowok i dhok kayina no oneko woko achiel kwoŋ adek ma thotho pa ji.
66009019	Ato men pa kayina no nitye i dhoki gin, kodi i yiwi gin bende. Yiwi gin ochalo thwol, mani gi wich, aka jooro gikipiny no ma kelo litho kwoŋ ji.
66009020	Ji modoŋ, ma gikipiny no koneko jo, jokoŋuto kwoŋ gikipiny ma jotimo. Jokoweyo lamo jwogi, kodi chal motim gi zawabu, feza, ywel, tele kodi yath apaya ma kinyal neno, kosa winjo, kosa woth.
66009021	Jono jokoŋuto kada kwoŋ nek, yido pajo, kidakana pajo, kosa kwalo gikipiny pa ji.
66010001	Gikenyo aneno malaika man ma jamwamba munyo loro piny wok i polo. Go oido otwodere gi pondeponde, aka lifudu othoko wiye; waŋe oido chalo waŋchieŋ aka tyende oido chalo kasikmach mokur.
66010002	Go oido nitye gi papila momin mathin moyawere i chinge. Go oketho tyende marachuch wi nam, to ketho maracham wi lowo,
66010003	aka okoko gi dwonde mamalo mowinjere paka kihola pa simbwor. Munyo go otyeko koko ameno, lithkoth abiryo jodwoko wach no gi mor.
66010004	Tekin joluwo, onwaŋo achiegin ndiko, to awinjo dwondi nyatoro moluwo i polo ni, “Liŋi kodi gima lithkoth abiryo jowacho; ikiri indiki!”
66010005	Gikenyo malaika m'aneno munyo ochungo wi nam kodi wi lowo otiŋo chinge marachuch malo,
66010006	to kwoŋere i nyingi Were, ma bedo chil gi chil, mochweyo polo kodi gikipiny jye mani iye, piny kodi gimoro jye man'iye, kodi nam gi kis gima ni iye. Malaika no owacho ni: “Galo odoko ongoye,
66010007	to i hongo ma malaika marabiryo lekudh'iye gwara pere, gikenyo Were bino chowo chan pere ma nyaliŋliŋ, paka chango onyutho jotich pere, jotuchi wach.”
66010008	Gikenyo dwondi ŋata nende awinjo ka luwo i polo oluwo kodan kendo munyo wacho ni, “Kidhi ikwanyi papila momin moyaw ma nitye i chingi malaika mochungo wi nam kodi wi lowo no.”
66010009	Gikenyo akidho bongi malaika no t'akwayo go ni womiyan papila momin mathin no. Go owacho ran ni, “Kwanyi ichami, bino daŋo iyin, to i dhokin bino bedo mamit pa mo kich.”
66010010	Akwanyo papila no t'achamo to bedo mamit i dhokan pa mo kich, to munyo achowo mwonyo, odaŋo iyan.
66010011	Gikenyo owacho ran ni, “Iripo tucho mikwenda pa Were kendo ri ji mathoth kodi nonin, ri dhudhok kodi ri kerere jye.”
66011001	Gikenyo omiyan midole ma kipima, machalo bol toŋ, to iwacho ran ni, “Ayi malo ipima Ot pa Were kodi alitar, t'ikwano joma lamo Were iye.
66011002	To weyi woko dyedipo ma Ot pa Were. Ikiri ipima rupiri meno otyek miyo Jopath, ma jobino nyono Tindi Maleŋ tyeko dwe pyero aŋwen g'aryo.
66011003	Aka abino miyo jomikwenda paran aryo, men ma tucho mikwenda paran i hongo ma ndelo gana achiel miya aryo gi pyero auchiel, kareno joruko kutyin.”
66011004	Jomikwenda aryo me, a yen vini aryo kodi talin aryo ma chungo ruwaŋ Ruoth ma piny.
66011005	Ka nyatoro otemi kwinyo jo, mach bino wok i dhoki jo to reyo woko jokwor pajo; me apaka nyatoro jye motemi kwinyo jo ibino neko.
66011006	Jonitye gi men ma chiego pondeponde to koth ngoye i hongo ma jotuch'iye mikwenda pa Were. Jonitye bende gi men kwoŋ waŋ pi, ma loko jo remo; odoko jonitye gi men ma kelo two ndir momore paka jomiti.
66011007	Ka jotyeko tucho mikwenda pajo, ogwaŋ ma lewok i mwombe bino lwenyo gi jo, to loyo jo gi men to neko jo.
66011008	Aka delkwoŋ jo bino moyere i royo ma tindi madwoŋ, kama Ruoth pajo ogur'iye kwoŋ musalaba, ma nyinge iya agecha ilwoŋo ni Sodom kosa Misir.
66011009	Ji ma nonin jye, gi dhudhok jye jobino neno delkwoŋ jono tyeko ndelo adek g'adech, aka jokoyeyi woyiki jo.
66011010	Ji ma piny jobino kisangala gi tho pa jaryo me. Jobino rweyere to jomiyere mich, rupiri jotuchi wach Were aryo no onwaŋo jokelo litho madit ri ji ma piny.
66011011	Rumachien munyo ndelo adek kodi adech no orumo, luya ma kelo kwo owok i dhoki Were to donjo kwoŋ jo, to joay malo; lworo madwoŋ omako ji jye ma chieŋino joneko jono.
66011012	Gikenyo jotuchi wach aryo no jowinjo dwondi nyatoro moluwo malo i polo ka wacho ri jo ni, “Biye win ka!” Jono joidho polo gi pondeponde ruwaŋ jokwor pajo.
66011013	I hongo no won, yengirok madwoŋ ma piny otimere; achiel kwoŋ apar ma tindi oŋinyere woko, aka ji ma romo gana abiryo jotho i yengirok ma piny no. Ji modoŋ jobwok to jopako dwoŋ pa Were ma polo.
66011014	Chandirok mararyo orumo; to neni, chandirok maradek chiegin tundo!
66011015	Gikenyo malaika marabiryo okudho gwara pere, to dwondi nyatoro ma koko malo wok i polo, ka wacho ni, “Men Madhumo piny pama obedo apa Ruoth kodi Kristo pere, aka go bino dhumo chil gi chil!”
66011016	Gikenyo jodongo pyero aryo g'aŋwen moido jobedo wi kombere pajo ruwaŋ Were no jokulo wiy jo piny to jolamo Were
66011017	munyo jowacho ni, “Ruoth Were Majameni jye, ma kwo pama aka wok chon go nitye! Wafuoyin ni ioro men perin moasere t'ichako dhum!
66011018	Keme opoŋ i chuny nonin; kole onyo ndir otundo ma nyutho keme perin, gi thumo banja ri jomotho: ndir ma miyo jotich perin, ma jotuchi wach, kemba pajo, kodi ji perin maleŋ jye, jomadongo kodi jomathindho jye ma jolworin. Ndir otundo ma reyo woko joma nyieko piny!”
66011019	Ot pa Were ma polo oido oyaw to sanduku ma chikirok nenere iye. Gikenyo pilin pa lithkoth, derino, mwoch pa koth, yengirok pa piny, kodi pe moasere otimere.
66012001	Gikenyo ranyuth madwoŋ onenere i polo: obedo dhako moro moruko waŋchieŋ, aka dwe onwaŋo nitye i tyende piny, kodi sangarya ma michalin apar garyo i wiye.
66012002	Go oido chiegin nywol, to litho kodi chandirok miyo go ywak.
66012003	Ranyuth man onenere i polo: obedo bulir mombo mobokere gi wich abiryo kodi tunge apar, kodi sangarya i wiye abiryo jye.
66012004	Go owaro woko gi yiwe achiel kwoŋ adek ma michalin ma i hongo to rwadho jo piny i lowo. Go ochungo ruwaŋ dhako moido chiegin nywol no, ni womwonyi nyathi pere tekin podho.
66012005	Gikenyo dhako no onywolo wuode, ma bino dhumo nonin jye gi luth manyweny. To, oyudhi nyathi no titero bongi Were kama di kom pere madhum.
66012006	Gikenyo dhako no oringo i thim; Were oido oyiko ri go kabedo kenyo, kama ibino kur'iye go chowo hongo ma ndelo gana achiel miya aryo gi pyero auchiel.
66012007	Gikenyo lweny oere i polo! Mikaeli kodi jomalaika pere jolwenyo gi bulir, ma bende olwenyo kodi jomalaika pere:
66012008	to oloy bulir, tiryemo go woko kodi jomalaika pere i polo.
66012009	Bulir mombo no owit woko! Go a thwol machon cha, milwoŋo ni Jwogi, kosa Sitan, mowondo piny gipi. Owit go piny wi lowo gi jomalaika pere jye.
66012010	Gikenyo awinjo dwondi nyatoro mokoko malo ipolo ka wacho ni, “Pama both gi men madhum kodi Ker pa Were mawan kodi adhum pa Kristo jye otyeko tundo! Kole jamisegey ma osa wutimin wan bongi Were, wor godyechieŋ, otyek wito piny.
66012011	To, jokengila go kodi remo pa Nyathi rombo, kodi wach ma joridho gine adyeri; aka oido joyikere kijala kwo pajo tundo tho.
66012012	Amomiyo, polo sangala win, kodi wijojye ma wini iye! To chandirok kidho bedo ri piny kodi nam! Kole Jwogi oloro ri win, aka opoŋ gi keme, rupiri go oŋeyo nike odoŋ gi nyaka hongo machiek.”
66012013	Munyo bulir oŋeyo nike otyek wito go piny wi lowo, ochako ryemo dhako monywolo nyathi ma nyichwo cha.
66012014	Dhako no omiy bwombe aryo mapa ango madongo ŋey woayi wokidhi i kabedo moyik ri go i thim kama ibino kur'iye go chowo oro adek gadech, ma thwol no kinyali mwonj'iye go.
66012015	Gikenyo thwol no oŋulo pi gi dhoke pa jwom yu ŋey dhako no, nike wonyali mol gi dhako no.
66012016	To, lowo okonyo dheno: oŋamo dhoke to mwonyo woko mikula ma jwom mowok i dhoki bulir no.
66012017	Gikenyo bulir nge omako gi dheno, to kidho chako lweny gi nyikwaye modoŋ, ji jye ma jowinjo or pa Were aka jo ni gi genirok i adyeri pa Yesu.
66012018	Aka bulir ochungo dho thengi nam.
66013001	Gikenyo aneno ogwaŋ moro munyo wok i nam. Go onwaŋo nitye gi tunge apar kodi wich abiryo, gi sangarya wi tunge apar no jye, gi nyinge ma luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Were mondik i kis wich mere.
66013002	Ogwaŋ m'aneno no ochalo kwach; tyende ochalo tyendi arara, aka dhoke ochalo dhok simbwor. Bulir omiyo ogwaŋ no men pere won, gi kom pere madhum, kodi men moasere madhum.
66013003	Achiel kwoŋ wich ogwaŋ no ochale pa ni gi adhola ma d'oneko go, to adhola no ochango. Piny gipi obedo gi dhyer to luwo ŋey ogwaŋ no.
66013004	Ji jye jolamo bulir kwoŋbedo go oido omiyo ogwaŋ no men madhum. Jolamo ogwaŋ no bende ka jowacho ni, “Ŋa ma rom g'ogwaŋ me? Ŋa ma nyalo lwenyo gine?”
66013005	Omiy ogwaŋ no dhoke ma wacho gikipiny ma kwoto gi luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Were; odoko omiy go men madhum chowo hongo ma dwe pyero aŋwen g'aryo.
66013006	Gino oŋamo dhoke to chako kwoŋo Were, gi luwo gimakotire kwoŋ Were kodi kama go bed'iye, riwo kir gi jomabedo i polo jye.
66013007	Omiy gino men ma lweny gi ji maleŋ pa Were gi nyalo jo, aka omiy go men kwoŋ nonin jye kodi ji, dhudhok jye kodi piny jye.
66013008	Ji jye majobedo i piny jobino lamo ogwaŋ no: dwoŋ mere nike dhano jye ma nyinge kondik i kitawo pa jomakwo mobedo apa Nyathi rombo monek wok i chwech pa piny.
66013009	Amomiyo ŋata ni gi ithe wowinji!
66013010	Ka nyatoro yenyere womak, ibino mako go titweyo; ka nyatoro yenyere wonek ji kodi abor, iripo neko go kodi abor. Me nyutho ni ji maleŋ pa Were joripo chiro teko kodi genirok.
66013011	Gikenyo aneno ogwaŋ man munyo wok i lowo; go oido ni gi tunge aryo paka tungi Nyathi rombo, to oluwo paka bulir.
66013012	Gino ooro men p'ogwaŋ marapena ma dhumo kawaŋe. Go oromo piny kodi joma bed'iye jowolami ogwaŋ marapena, ma adhola ma d'oneko go oido ochango cha.
66013013	Ogwaŋ mararyo me, otimo ranyuth gi giraura madongo; omiyo mach owok i polo to loro piny i waŋ ji jye.
66013014	Aka gino omiyo go owondo ji jye ma piny munyo timo giraura moyey go timo kawaŋ ogwaŋ marapena. Ogwaŋ no ooro ji jye ma piny chweyo chal ma kelo dwoŋ ri ogwaŋ moido ochwow g'abor, to odoko kwo.
66013015	Ogwaŋ mararyo me, omiy go men ma kudho kwo i chal p'ogwaŋ marapena, ŋey chal no wonyali luwo aka womiyi woneki woko ji jye ma jokwero lamo chal m'ochwey no.
66013016	Ogwaŋ no bende oromo ji jye, jomathindho kodi madongo, joŋaŋo kodi jochandi, ŋechin kodi joma ni syem, ni woketh ranyuth i chingi jo marachuch kodi i nyim jo.
66013017	Ongoye ŋata d'onyiewere kosa otana kwanyo woko ka go nitye gi ranyuth me, mobedo nyingi ogwaŋ no, kosa kwan ma nyutho nyinge.
66013018	Gime yenyo ryeko: Nyatoro jye maniaŋ nyalo menyo dwoŋ kwan p'ogwaŋ no, kwoŋbedo kwan no nyutho nyingi dhano. Kwan mere obedo: miya auchiel pyero auchiel g'auchiel (666).
66014001	Gikenyo aŋiyo, t'aneno Nyathi rombo ruwaŋan, munyo ochungo wi got Zayun. Bonge, oido nitye ji gana miya achiel pyero aŋwen g'aŋwen (144,000) ma nyinge kodi nyingi Bamere ondik i nyim jo.
66014002	Aka awinjo derino ma chalo pi ma mol piyo piyo, kendo pa lithkoth ma mor. Derino no ochalo pa wer ma jotongol jogoyo i tongol pajo.
66014003	Oido jowero wer manyien, yuwaŋ kom pa Were madhum no kodi chwech aŋwen no kodi jodongo no, aka jowero wer manyien ma ŋat man jye konyalo fuonjirok kwanyo woko ji gana miya achiel pyero aŋwen g'aŋwen (144,000) monyiew jo gi remo pa Yesu wok i piny.
66014004	Meno ji ma jokure maber ma jokotimo chot gi mon. Joluwo Nyathi rombo kama go kidh'iye jye; ogony jo wok kwoŋ ji jye modoŋ aka jobedo pa kodhi monyak marapena momiy Were kodi Nyathi rombo.
66014005	Twodo konwaŋere i dhoki jo; jongoye gi recho ma di kwan ri jo.
66014006	Gikenyo aneno malaika man munyo ringo i koyo, gi mikwenda ma chil gi chil ma Wach Maber ma wotiti ri ji ma jonitye i piny: ri piny jye, nonin, dhudhok kodi ji jye!
66014007	Go owacho gi dwonde mamalo ni, “Lwori win Were, aka paki win dwoŋ pere! Kole ndir otundo ri go ma thumo banja ri ji. Amomiyo, lami win Were mochweyo polo, piny, nam, kodi waŋ pi!”
66014008	Malaika mararyo bende oluwo marapena, ka wacho ni, “Go otyeko podho, Babilon madwoŋ otyeko podho! Go otyeko miyo nonin jye madho vini ma keme ma kidakana pere!”
66014009	Malaika maradek oluwo jaryo no ka wacho gi dwonde mamalo ni, “Nyatoro jye molami ogwaŋ no kodi chal pere, to limo ranyuth i nyime kosa i chinge,
66014010	won bende bino madho vini ma keme pa Were, ma go okonjo gi men pere motyek konjo gi men i agwata ma keme pere! Ji jye ma jotimi gime ibino chando jo gi mach ma buru salufa mobedo kidhur tongi kibirit, ruwaŋ jomalaika maleŋ kodi Nyathi rombo.
66014011	Aka yiro ma mach ma bino chando jo duny malo chil gi chil. Ongoye ywomirok, wor g'odyechieŋ, ri jomalamo ogwaŋ no kodi chal pere, kodi ri nyatoro jye molimi ranyuth ma nyinge.”
66014012	Meno amomiyo ji pa Were joripo bedo gi chiro, paka joma winjo or pa Were aka jonitye gi genirok bongi Yesu.
66014013	Gikenyo awinjo dwondi nyatoro mowok i polo munyo wacho ni, “Ndiki gime: Josilwany a joma wok pama kadho yu malo joletho i tich pa Ruoth.” “Ey,” Chuny wacho, “Jobino ywomirok kwoŋ tich pajo matek; rupiri tim pajo luwo jo.”
66014014	Gikenyo taneno ruwaŋan oido nitye pondeponde matar, aka wi pondeponde no onwaŋo nitye nyatoro mobedo piny mochale gi Wuodi Dhano, gi sangarya ma zawabu i wiye kodi pala nyangoda mabith i chinge.
66014015	Gikenyo malaika man owok i Ot pa Were to koko gi dwonde ma malo ri ŋata oido obedo wi pondeponde ni, “Ori nyangoda perin ikechi, kwoŋbedo ndir mere otyeko tundo; piny ochiek akecha!”
66014016	Gikenyo ŋatobedo wi pondeponde no owito nyangoda pere wi piny to kecho gima ni piny.
66014017	Gikenyo aneno malaika man munyo wok i Ot pa Were i polo, go bende oido ni gi nyangoda mabith.
66014018	Gikenyo malaika man ma kuro mach, owok kwoŋ alitar. Okoko gi dwonde mamalo ri malaika moido nitye gi nyangoda mabith ni, “Ori nyangoda perin ifuoni gine gimanyak i ndelo vini ma piny, rupiri vini monyak otyeko chiek!”
66014019	Gikenyo malaika no owito nyangoda pere wi piny, otoŋo vini monyak, to bolo i bur madwoŋ ma biyo vini ma keme pa Were.
66014020	Obiy vini monyak no i bur ma biyo vini ma tindi, aka remo omol wok i kabiyo vini pa mikula ma boro mere oromo mairo miya aryo, aka thutho mere obedo ma chiegin tundo i chongi kayina (futi abich).
66015001	Gikenyo aneno ranyuth man madwoŋ ma kelo dhyer i polo: jomalaika abiryo kodi thoyamo abiryo. Me ama obedo thoyamo machowe, rupiri jobedo gikipiny ma nyutho keme pa Were machowe.
66015002	Gikenyo aneno gima ochale pa nam mandewiro, moruwere gi mach: aneno bende joma joloyo ogwaŋ kodi chal pere, kodi nyinge moketh i kwan. Jono onwaŋo jochungo dho nam mandewiro munyo jotiŋo tongol ma Were omiyo jo.
66015003	Onwaŋo jowero wer pa Musa, jatich pa Were kendo apa Nyathi rombo ni, “Tich perin dongo aka obedo giraura, Ruoth Were Majameni jye! Royo perin otire aka obedo maradyeri, Kere pa nonin jye!
66015004	Ruoth, ŋata kilelworin, kosa kilemiyo nyingin dwoŋ? Kole in kendin am'ileŋ. Nonin jye jolebino ruwaŋin to jolamin. Kole tim perin motire otyeko nenere.”
66015005	Rumachien aneno munyo Ot wema ma Were bed'iye oyaw i polo.
66015006	Jomalaika abiryo ma jo ni gi thoyamo abiryo machowe jowok i Ot pa Were no; jorukere i nengin matar ma pilin, kodi del ma zawabu motwey i kor gin.
66015007	Gikenyo achiel kwoŋ chwech makwo aŋwen cha omiyo jomalaika abiryo no atewe ma zawabu abiryo mopoŋ gi keme pa Were ma kwo chil gi chil.
66015008	Ot pa Were oido opoŋ yiro mowok i dwoŋ kodi i men pere, aka moro ongoye moido nyalo donjo i Ot pa Were chuka i giki thoyamo abiryo ma jomalaika abiryo no di jokelo.
66016001	Gikenyo awinjo dwondi jo ma luwo malo munyo wacho i Ot pa Were ri jomalaika abiryo ni, “Kidhi wioli atewe abiryo ma keme pa Were piny wi lowo!”
66016002	Malaika marapena okidho to olo atawo pere wi lowo, to adholin marecho kendo malith tula kwoŋ joma oido jonitye gi ranyuth p'ogwaŋ cha, ma jolamo chal pere.
66016003	Gikenyo malaika mararyo oolo atawo pere i nam, to pi lokere mobokere pa remo dhano motho, to gimakwo i nam jye jotho.
66016004	Gikenyo malaika maradek oolo atawo pere i jwombe kodi i waŋ pi, to jolokere remo.
66016005	Awinjo malaika ma kuro pi wacho ni, “Banja me ithumo motire, a Maleŋ, ma nitye pama kendo motyeko bedo wok chon.
66016006	Rupiri jooyo remo pa ji maleŋ kodi apa jotuchi wach Were, imiyo jo madho remo; meno ripo gi jo!”
66016007	Gikenyo awinjo dwondi moro wok kwoŋ alitar munyo wacho ni, “Ruoth, Were Majameni jye! Thumo banja perin otire odoko obedo maradyeri!”
66016008	Gikenyo malaika maraŋwen oolo atawo pere kwoŋ waŋchieŋ, tiyeyo waŋchieŋ rewo piny gi lyetho mere pa mach.
66016009	Ji jowaŋ gi lyetho mager no, to jokwoŋo nyingi Were ma nitye gi men kwoŋ two ma sika ji, to jokwero ŋuto kwoŋ gimarecho pajo kosa miyo Were dwoŋ.
66016010	Gikenyo malaika marabich oolo atawo pere wi kom p'ogwaŋ madhum, to mudho umo ker pere; ji jokayo lew jo ru litho,
66016011	to jokwoŋo Were ma polo ru litho kodi adholin pajo, to jokoŋuto tim pajo marecho.
66016012	Gikenyo malaika marauchiel oolo atawo pere i jwom madwoŋ milwoŋo ni Yufurate, to jwom no dwono ma yawo royo ri kerere ma jowok yu Wokchieŋ.
66016013	Gikenyo aneno chuny mochido jadek ma jochale g'ogwal munyo jowok i dhoki bulir, i dhoki ogwaŋ, kodi i dhoki jatuchi wach matwodo cha.
66016014	Jobedo chuny ma nyajwogi ma jotimo giraura. Chuny adek me jowok kareno jokidho pa kerin i piny gipi, choko jo kanyachiel ma lweny i ndelo madwoŋ mapa Were Majameni jye.
66016015	“Neni, Alebino nyaliŋliŋ pa jakwo! Jasilwany a ŋata bedo waŋe to gwoko ruk pere, ŋey wokiri wowothi kinyoro to kelo ri go wichkwot!”
66016016	Gikenyo chuny no jokelo kerin kanyachiel kama ilwoŋo i Dhoyudaya ni Amagedon.
66016017	Gikenyo malaika marabiryo oolo atawo pere i hongo, to dwondi nyatoro maluwo malo wok i kom madhum i Ot pa Were munyo wacho ni, “Otyeko timere!”
66016018	Aka pilin, derino, mwoch pa lithkoth, kodi yengirok pa piny moasere otimere ma fuodi yado onwaŋo kotimere ye ameno wok chuka chwey dhano; me obedo yengirok pa piny marach moasere!
66016019	Tindi mombo cha okedhere didek, aka tindin ma piny jye oŋinyere woko. Were opoyo Babilon madwoŋ no, to miyo go medho i agwata mopoŋ gi vini ma keme pere jye.
66016020	Kigodin ma nam jye jokedhere woko, aka kir gote jye jokonwaŋere kendo.
66016021	Pe madongo pa telin, ma kis achiel ywayo chiegin latir miya achiel, jopodho kwoŋ ji wok malo. Ji jokwoŋo Were ru thoyamo ma pe, rupiri obedo marach tektek.
66017001	Gikenyo achiel kwoŋ jomalaika abiryo ma jo ni g'atewe abiryo obino bongan to wacho ni, “Biye, alenyuthin girachula ma jatimi gi wichkwot madwoŋ moger dho thengi jwombe madit no kidho limo.
66017002	Kerere madongo ma piny jotimo chot gi jatimi gi wichkwot madwoŋ no, aka ji ma piny jomer gi vini ma kidakana pere.”
66017003	Gikenyo to malaika no tiŋan i Chuny Maleŋ to teran yu thim, t'aneno dhako mobedo wi ogwaŋ mobokere. Kwoŋ ogwaŋ no gipi oido ondik nyinge ma luwo gima kotire kwoŋ Were.
66017004	Dheno oido oruko nengin ma rangi ariŋo kodi mobokere, aka kwoŋe oido pilin gi zawabu, gee kodi telin mawelo. I chinge, go oido otiŋo agwata ma zawabu mopoŋ gi gikipiny ma timo chot kodi makoch, gima wok i kidakana pere.
66017005	I nyime ondik nyinge ma dwoŋ mere omuŋere ni: “Babilon madwoŋ, min mon ma jotana delkwoŋ jo i timo gi wichkwot jye kodi joma duwo piny.”
66017006	Aka aneno ni dhako no oido omer gi remo pa ji maleŋ pa Were, kodi remo pa jomonek rupiri jochwire kwoŋ Yesu. Munyo aneno go, adhyer swa.
66017007	Gikenyo malaika no openjan ni, “Idhyer raŋo?” Abino tucho rin dwoŋ nyaliŋliŋ ma mako kwoŋ dhako no kodi ogwaŋ motiŋo go, ma nyawich abiryo gi tunge apar no.
66017008	Ogwaŋ m'ineno no oido chon kwo, to pama kikwo; go chiegin wok i bur mwombe ma bu gike aka bino tundo kama ilerey'iye go woko. Ji ma piny ma nyingi jo fuodi kondik i kitawo ma kwo wok i chakirok pa piny jobino dhyer ka joneno ogwaŋ no, rupiri chon oido kwo, to onyo pama kikwo, aka bino nenirok kendo.
66017009	“Gime yenyo ryeko kodi niaŋ. Wich abiryo no obedo tendere abiryo ma dheno bedo wiye, kendo jobedo kerere abiryo bende.
66017010	Kwoŋ jo, kerere abich jotyeko podho, achiel fuodi dhumo, aka man fuodi kobino; ka go obino go ripo chowo nyaka hongo machiek.
66017011	Aka ogwaŋ ma chon oido kwo, to onyo pama kikwo no, meno obedo kere maraboro ma nitye i kweth pa jabiryo marapena aka bino tundo kama ilerey'iye go woko.
66017012	“Tunge apar m'ineno no, meno kerin apar ma fuodi jokochako dhumo, to ibino miyo jo men madhum paka kerere chowo hongo ma sawa achiel, kanyachiel kodi ogwaŋ.
66017013	Japar me jye jonitye g'atoŋa marom, aka jobino miyo ogwaŋ men pajo gi nyalo madhum.
66017014	Jobino lwenyo gi Nyathi rombo, to Nyathi rombo bino loyo jo, rupiri go obedo Ruoth kodi Kere pa kerere, aka joma ni bonge jobedo jomolwoŋ kendo moyer aka jogenere.”
66017015	Malaika no bende owacho ran kendo ni, “Pi m'ineno, ma jatimi gi wichkwot obed'iye no, meno ji, kodi lwak ji, gi nonin gi dhudhok.
66017016	Ogwaŋ kodi tunge apar m'ineno no, jobino dak jatimi gi wichkwot no; jobino timo go kichar to joweyo go kinyoro; jobino chamo delkwoŋe to joreyo woko go gi mach.
66017017	Ato Were oketho i chuny jono awanya ma tiyo g'atoŋa pere, munyo jotiyo gi paro achiel to jomiyo ogwaŋ men pajo madhum, chuka wach pa Were wotimere.
66017018	“Dhako m'ineno no meno tindi mombo madhumo kerin ma piny.”
66018001	Rumachien aneno malaika man munyo loro piny wok i polo. Go oido nitye gi men madhum madwoŋ swa, aka lero pere omenyo piny gipi.
66018002	Go okoko gi dwonde mamalo ni, “Go otyeko podho. Babilon madwoŋ otyeko podho! Go onyo otyeko lokirok kabedo pa jwogi, kodi gunda ma chuny mochido joywomir'iye; winyin makoch ma nger jye ma kicham jobed'iye.
66018003	Kole go opoko ji jye vini pere ma kidakana to jomadho. Kerin ma piny jotimo gine chot, aka jomiten ma piny joŋaŋ kwoŋ kwo pere ma mito gikipiny mawelo.”
66018004	Gikenyo awinjo dwondi ŋat man i polo, mowacho ni, “Woki win kwoŋ dheno ji paran! Ŋey wikiri widonji i gimarecho pere. Ŋey wibende wikiri wilimi adech i girachula mikidho miyo go!
66018005	Ato gimarecho pere odhure pa kidho geyo polo. Aka Were opoyo recho pere.
66018006	Dwoki ri go gima rom kodi ma bende otyeko poko; chuli go diryo gima go otyeko timo jye. Poŋi agwata pere no won gi medho mager ka diryo.
66018007	Miyi go chandirok kodi rem ma rom gi dwoŋ kodi yodirok ma go oido omiyere. Ato go kwot ka wacho gi i chunye ni, ‘An abedo paka kere ma dhako; akibedo chi tho, odoko akowinji rem moro jye!’
66018008	Amomiyo thoyamo jye ma letundo ri go, jobino umo go kiromo i ndelo achiel: two, rem, kodi kech; aka ibino waŋo go gi mach, rupiri Ruoth Were ma thumo ri go banja jameni swa.”
66018009	Kerere ma piny moido joŋiyo timo gine kidakana, kodi yodirok i kwo pere mawelo, jobino winjo gi rem to joywako go kareno joneno yiro ma wok i waŋ pere.
66018010	Jobino chungo gi bor swa, kareno jolworo chandirok pere, to jowacho ni: “Awi chandi, awi chandi otundo rin, tindi madwoŋ ma Babilon ma di men! Reyirok perin obino nyaka i hongo ma sawa achiel won!”
66018011	Jomiten ma piny bende jobino rem to joywako go, rupiri ongoye ŋata onyo nyiewo gikipiny pajo kenyo kendo.
66018012	Ongoye ŋata nyiewo zawabu, feza, telin kodi gee mawelo, nengin mafuoth, kodi ma rangi ariŋo, kodi maraliri kodi mobokere; kiti mbawin mawelo maŋwe kuur, kodi gikipiny mopokere opokere motim gi laki lyech, mbawin mawelo, nyweny bangir, nyweny matheth kodi tele mafuoth ma minyin;
66018013	yath mamit, yen moregi mamoko ma ŋwe kuur i chiemo, buban, mo maŋwe kur, nger buban man; vini kodi mo, moko monuŋere kodi ŋano, dhoki kodi rombo, kayina kodi chawula, ŋechin gi jegin.
66018014	Jomiten jowacho ri go ni, “Gikipiny jye ma chunyin owanya bedo gine jotyeko leny woko; aka ŋaŋo perin jye gi noro perin joware woko kwoŋin, aka idoko ikibino nwaŋo jo kendo!”
66018015	Jomiten ma jolimo ŋaŋo wok kwoŋ go, jobino chungo gi bor rupiri jolworo chandirok pere. Jobino ywak gi rem
66018016	to jowacho ni, “Awi chandi, chandirok obedo ri tindi madwoŋ me! Go yado ruko nengin mafuoth kodi ma rangi ariŋo kodi mobokere, to jaŋ gi gikipiny ma zawabu, telin mawelo, kodi gee mawelo!
66018017	To i hongo ma sawa achiel won go onyo otyeko rwenyo woko ŋaŋo no jye!” Jotel jye ma mel kodi joma ni mel, jochiewi mel kodi joman jye ma jolimo gima kuro kwo pajo i nam, jobino chungo gi bor,
66018018	to joywak kareno joneno yiro ma wok i waŋ pere ka jowacho ni, “Tindi mene man monwaŋo nyalo rom gi tindi madwoŋ me?”
66018019	Jobino ywoyo fukefuke i wiy gin, ka joywak gi rem ni, “Awi chandi, chandirok madwoŋ otundo ri tindi mombo me! Go onwaŋo a tindi ma ji jye ma jo ni gi mel i nam jolim'iye ŋaŋo wok kwoŋ ŋaŋo pere! Aka i hongo ma sawa achiel won go onyo otyeko kir reyere woko!”
66018020	Sangala ru podho pere, a polo! Sangala win, ji maleŋ pa Were kodi jomoor kodi jotuchi wach pere! Kole Were otyeko thumo banja ri go ru gima go oido timo ri win!
66018021	Gikenyo malaika ma jameni okwanyo tele marom kodi kidi ma irego gine, to bolo i nam munyo wacho ni, “Me apaka tindi madwoŋ ma Babilon ibino rwadho piny gi derino, aka kibino nenere kendo.
66018022	Wer pa jotongol kodi jower, jokudhi madundo kodi gwarin, kowinji perin kendo! Ongoye jatich kosa jandijo moro jye modoko bino nwaŋere perin kendo. Ongoye kidi kada achiel mibino winjo ka rego moko yu perin kendo.
66018023	Aka lero ma tala k'odoko olyel perin kendo. Odoko dwondi jamweha gi mweha pere k'odoko owinjere perin kendo. Jomiten perin oido jobedo jomadongo loyo i piny gipi, aka thyeth perin ama oido iwondo gine ji jye ma piny!”
66018024	Ato kwoŋ go ama remo pa jotuchi wach Were kodi apa ji maleŋ kodi apa ji jye monek i piny onwaŋer'iye.
66019001	Rumachien awinjo gima owinjere malo pa dwondi muma ji madwoŋ ma polo munyo wacho ni, “Aleluya! Both, dwoŋ kodi men jye apa Were mawan!
66019002	Thumo banja pere otire kendo obedo maradyeri! Kole go otyeko thumo banja ri jatimi gi wichkwot madwoŋ monwaŋo topo piny gi kidakana pere. Were omiyo go girachula rupiri go oneko jotich pere”
66019003	To odoko okoko ni, “Aleluya! Yiro mawok i waŋ pere kidho malo chil gi chil.”
66019004	Gikenyo, jodongo pyero aryo g'aŋwen no kodi chwech aŋwen no, jye jogore piny to jolamo Were monwaŋo obedo wi kom pere madhum no, ka jowacho ni, “Ameno! Aleluya!”
66019005	Gikenyo dwondi nyatoro owok i kom madhum ma wacho ni, “Paki win Were mawan, win jotich pere jye, gi ji jye, jomadongo gi mathindho ma jolworo go!”
66019006	Gikenyo awinjo gima ochalo dwondi lwak madwoŋ, ma derino mere omor pa pi ma mol gi men, kendo pa mwoch pa lithkoth madwoŋ. Awinjo ka jowacho ni, “Aleluya! Kole Ruoth Were mawan Majameni jye dhumo!
66019007	Weyi wayodere wasangala; weyi wapaki dwoŋ pere moasere! Kole ndir otundo ma nywomirok maleŋ mapa Nyathi rombo, aka mweha pere otyeko yikirok.
66019008	Omiy go ruko nanga mayom matar maminyin.” (Nanga matar no meno tim motire mapa ji pa Were.)
66019009	Gikenyo malaika owacho ran ni, “Ndiki gime: Josilwany a jomolwoŋ i kalima ma nywomirok pa Nyathi rombo.” Malaika no omedo wacho ni, “Me obedo wach maradyeri mapa Were.”
66019010	Gikenyo agore piny dho tyende ni alam go, to go owacho ran ni, “Ikiri itimi ameno! A jatich nyawotin, achiel kwoŋ wutimerin ma joridho adyeri pa Yesu. Lami Were ayino! Kole adyeri pa Yesu ama gudo chuny jatuchi wach Were.”
66019011	Gikenyo aneno polo munyo yawere, to kayina matar nenere ruwaŋan. Ŋata ryemo kayina no ilwoŋo ni Mogenere kendo Jaradyeri; go thumo banja aka lwenyo i tiro.
66019012	Waŋe oido chalo mach malyel, aka oruko sangarya kweth i wiye. Go ni gi nyinge mondik kwoŋe, mongoye moro moŋeyo kwanyo woko go won kende.
66019013	Nanga ma go oruko oido orwaki i remo. Nyinge milwoŋo gine obedo, “Wach pa Were.”
66019014	Lwak jolweny ma polo oido joluwo go, munyo jonitye wi kayina matar aka joruko nengin mayom, matar, molony kichutho.
66019015	Abor mabith owok i dhoke, ma go bino toŋo woko gine nonin. Go bino dhumo jo kodi luth manyweny, aka go bino biyo vini i gibiyo vini ma keme mager mapa Were Majameni jye.
66019016	I nanga pere kodi i bat mere ondik nyinge me: “Kere pa kerere, Ruoth pa ruodhe jye.”
66019017	Gikenyo aneno malaika moro ochungo wi waŋchieŋ. Okoko i dwonde mamalo ri winyin jye monwaŋo jolekaleka wi hongo ni, “Biye win, aka chokere win kanyachiel ri kalima pa Were madwoŋ!
66019018	Biye win wichami delkwoŋ kerere, jotel ma lweny, kodi jomen, riŋo kayina kodi joryemi mere, delkwoŋ ji jye, jegin kodi joma ni syem, jomadongo kodi jomathindho!”
66019019	Gikenyo aneno ogwaŋ cha kodi kerin ma piny kodi lwak jolweny pajo munyo jochokere ni jowolwenyi kodi ŋata wotho wi kayina matar kodi lwak jolweny pere.
66019020	To imako ogwaŋ no, kanyachiel kodi jatuchi wach matwodo moido jotimo giraura ri go. (Giraura no ama go owondo gine ji monwaŋo jonitye gi ranyuth p'ogwaŋ no to jolamo chal p'ogwaŋ no.) Ogwaŋ no kodi jotuchi wach matwodo jye obol jo makwo i wakawaka ma mach kodi telin ma gamo mach mayot pa kibirit.
66019021	Onek lwak jolweny pajo modoŋ g'abor ma wok i dhoki ŋat moido ringo wi kayina cha; aka winyin jye jochamo delkwoŋ jo paka jonyalo.
66020001	Gikenyo aneno malaika moro munyo loro piny wok i polo kareno otiŋo rayaw ma bur mwombe ma bu gike kodi lijegere mombo i chinge.
66020002	Go omako bulir, thwol machon ma nyinge ilwoŋo ni jwogi kosa Sitan, to tweyo go oro gana achiel,
66020003	aka obolo go i mwombe, to chiego to mwono dhoke matek, ŋey wobedi kenyo modoko kinyali wok wondo ji ma piny chuka oro gana achiel orum. To rumachien ibino gonyo go kendo ma hongo machiek.
66020004	Rumachien aneno kombere madhum, aka jomobedo kwoŋ jo obedo joma omiy jo thumo banjin. Aka aneno bende joma ndir cha oŋadi woko ŋut jo ru ridho yeyo pajo kwoŋ Yesu kodi wach pa Were, ma jokoyeyo lamo ogwaŋ kosa chal pere, aka jokoyeyo womwon ranyuth pere i nyim jo kosa i chingi jo. Odwok ri jo kendo kwo pajo to jodhumo gi Kristo oro gana achiel.
66020005	Jomotho man jye jodoŋ chien ma jokochierino chuka oro gana achiel orumo. Me a chierino marapena.
66020006	Ji jye ma jokwanere i chierino marapena me, meno josilwany odoko joleŋ! Ato tho mararyo kibino bedo gi men kwoŋ jo, to jobino bedo jochwayi ri Were wi alitar ma jotiyo ri Were gi Kristo munyo jodhumo gine chowo oro gana achiel.
66020007	Aka ka oro gana achiel orumo, ibino gonyo Sitan wok i twech,
66020008	to idhiro go i piny bino wondo nonin jye ma jonitye i thenge aŋwen ma piny, meno Gog kodi Magog, gi choko jo ri lweny; welo pajo kareno thoth pa kwoyo ma thengi wakawaka.
66020009	Jobino wotho munyo joswana riwe ma piny to jothoko chiel pa jomaleŋ kodi tindi momar; to mach bino tukere wok i polo to podho to regarega woko jo.
66020010	Aka jwogi moido wondo jo ibino bolo i wakawaka ma mach gi telin malyel kama ogwaŋ cha kodi jotuchi wach pere matwodo jobino chandirok iye hongo jye wor godyechieŋ chil gi chil.
66020011	Odoko aneno kom moro madwoŋ matar madhum kodi ŋata obed'iye; piny gi polo joringo joeye woko ruwaŋe m'odoko jokonenere kichutho.
66020012	Aka aneno joma chango jotho, madongo kodi mathindho, munyo jochungo ruwaŋ kom no, tiyawo kitawin. To odoko iyawo kitawo man mobedo kitawo makwo. Aka joma chango jotho no othum ri jo banjin chungo kwoŋ gima kis dhano chango otimo i kwo pere, mondik i kitawin no.
66020013	Gikenyo wakawaka jye jowodho joma chango jotho i jo. Tho kodi piny pa jomotho bende jowodho joma onwaŋo ni jo, aka jojye othum ri jo banjin chungo kwoŋ gima yado jotimo i kwo pajo.
66020014	Gikenyo Tho kodi piny pa jomotho jye obol i wakawaka ma mach. Me a tho mararyo, mobedo wakawaka ma mach,
66020015	aka nyatoro jye ma konwaŋ nyinge i kitawo ma kwo, bende obol i wakawaka ma mach no.
66021001	Gikenyo aneno polo manyien kodi piny manyien. Ato polo kodi piny marapena oido joleny woko, aka nam orere woko.
66021002	Gikenyo aneno Tindi Maleŋ, Yerusalem manyien, munyo loro piny wok i polo bongi Were, moyik maŋon paka mweha morukere maŋon ka yikere romo gi ruoth pere.
66021003	Awinjo dwondi nyatoro ma luwo malo munyo wacho wi kom madhum ni, “Pama pecho pa Were nitye gi ji! Go bino bedo gi jo, aka jobino bedo ji pere. Were won bino bedo gi jo, aka bino bedo Were pajo.
66021004	Go bino yweyo pigi waŋ jo. Tho odoko kobedi, kosa rembo, kosa ywak kosa litho, rupiri gikipiny machon jotyeko leny woko.”
66021005	Gikenyo ŋata oido obedo wi kom madhum owacho ni, “Onyo pama aloko gikipiny jye manyien!” Go owacho ran kendo ni, “Ndiki gime, rupiri wach me obedo maradyeri aka genere.”
66021006	Aka owacho ran ni, “Otyeko timere! Aŋata Alufa kodi Omega, chakirok kodi gike. Ŋata riyo neko abino miyo pi amadha manono mawok i waŋ pi makwo.
66021007	Ŋata oloy lweny bino limo gime jye. Abino bedo Were pere, aka go bino bedo wuodan.
66021008	To jomalwor, joma jokoyeyo, jomarecho, jonek, jochot, jothyeth gi yido, joma lamo chal makichar, kodi jotwodo jye, kabedo pajo bino bedo wakawaka mach ma waŋ gi telin ma wodho mach kibirit, mobedo tho mararyo.”
66021009	Achiel kwoŋ jomalaika abiryo monwaŋo jonitye kodi atewe abiryo ma thoyamo opoŋ'iye obino bongan to wacho ni, “Biye anyuthin Mweha, chipa Nyathi rombo.”
66021010	Gikenyo malaika no otiŋan i chuny to teran wi got mabor tektek. Go onyuthan Yerusalem, Tindi Maleŋ, munyo loro piny wok i polo bongi Were,
66021011	ma lyel gi dwoŋ pa Were. Tindi no omeny pa gee mawelo, pa tele jaspa ma pilin, maler pa ndewiro.
66021012	Go obedo gi chiel mothoko ma kore pek aka oŋawere malo, kodi waŋkach apar g'aryo, kodi jomalaika apar g'aryo ma jokuro kis waŋkach. Kwoŋ kis waŋkach ondik nyingi nonin apar g'aryo ma Israel.
66021013	Aka obedo gi waŋkach adek i kis thenge: adek yu Wokchieŋ, adek yu Tyendi piny, adek yu Wich piny, adek yu Podhochieŋ.
66021014	Chiel ma tindi no oger wi telin apar g'aryo, mondik'iye nyingi jomoor pa Nyathi rombo apar g'aryo.
66021015	Malaika moluwo kodan oido nitye gi luth rapor ma zawabu, ma kipima tindi, kodi waŋkach mere, kodi chiel moget thoko go.
66021016	Tindi no oido nyathenge aŋwen marom; boro mere rom kodi lacho mere. Malaika opima tindi no kodi luth rapor pere no. Boro mere onwaŋo romo mairo gana achiel gi miya aŋwen; aka lacho mere, kodi ŋawirok mere, kodi boro mere jye oido jorom aroma.
66021017	Malaika no opima kor chiel, aka ŋawirok mere oido romo tyendi jo miya achiel gi pyero aŋwen g'aŋwen, chungo kwoŋ rapor ma noknok moido go oro (futi 200).
66021018	Kor chiel no otim gi tele jaspa, aka tindi won gipi otim gi zawabu, maler pa ndewiro.
66021019	Tele ma tyendi chiel ma tindi otim makichin kodi telin mawelo mopokere opokere. Tele marapena ma tyendi chiel obedo ma yaspa; mararyo safiro; maradek aget; maraŋwen emerad (ma nyabokependi),
66021020	marabich sarudonik; marauchiel karunelyan; marabiryo kurisolito; maraboro berulo; marabuŋwen topaz; marapar kurisopuraso; marapar g'achiel jasinto; aka marapar g'aryo amethisto.
66021021	Waŋkach apar g'aryo no obedo ma tele mawelo, kis thigo gi tele mopokere. Royo ma tindi obedo ma zawabu, maler pa ndewiro.
66021022	Akineno Ot pa Were i tindi, rupiri Ot mere obedo Ruoth Were Majameni jye, kodi Nyathi rombo.
66021023	Tindi no kiyeny chieŋ kosa dwe wokel'iye lero, rupiri dwoŋ pa Were ama lero, aka Nyathi rombo a tala mere.
66021024	Ji ma piny jobino woth i lero pere, aka kerin ma piny jobino kelo ŋaŋo pajo iye.
66021025	Waŋkach ma tindi kibino chiegere odyechieŋ, odoko kada cholo ma wor kobedi kenyo.
66021026	Dwoŋ kodi ŋaŋo pa nonin ibino kelo i tindi no.
66021027	To ongoye gimakoch ma bino donj'iye, kosa ŋata timo giwichkwot kosa twodo, kende ji ma nyingi jo ondik i kitawo ma kwo mapa Nyathi rombo kende ama jobino donjo i tindi no.
66022001	Malaika onyuthan bende jwom mapi ma kelo kwo, maler pa ndewiro, mamol kareno wok i kom madhum pa Were kodi apa Nyathi rombo,
66022002	aka mol i dyeri royo ma tindi. I thengi jwom korin gi korin oido nitye yath ma kwo, ma nyak gimopokere apar g'aryo i oro, dichiel kis dwe, aka boke mere obedo ma botho nonin.
66022003	Ongoye gima Were okwoŋo ma bino nwaŋere i tindi no. Kom madhum pa Were kodi apa Nyathi rombo ama bino bed'iye, aka jotich pere jobino lamo go.
66022004	Jobino neno waŋe, aka ibino ndiko nyinge i nyim jo.
66022005	Cholo ma wor odoko kibino bedo, aka jokibino yenyo lero ma tala kosa lero ma waŋchieŋ, Ruoth Were won ama bino bedo lero pajo, aka jobino dhumo chil gi chil.
66022006	Gikenyo malaika owacho ran ni, “Wach me obedo maradyeri aka genere. Aka Ruoth Were ma miyo jotuchi wach Chuny Maleŋ pere, ooro malaika pere nyutho jotich pere gima kidho timere mayot.”
66022007	Yesu owacho ni, “Winji, abino mayot! Jasilwany a ŋata mako wach pa jotuchi wach ma kitawo me!”
66022008	An Yohana, aŋata awinjo kendo aneno gikipiny me jye. Aka munyo atyeko winjo gi neno gime, agore piny dho tyendi malaika monyuthan gikipiny me ni alami go.
66022009	To go owacho ran ni, “Ikiri itimi ameno! Abedo jatich nyawotin, i dyeri wutimere kodi jotuchi wach kodi ji jye ma jomako wach ma kitawo me. Lami Were ayino!”
66022010	Gikenyo owacho ran ni, “Ikiri ipani wach motuch i kitawo me rupiri ndir orikere.
66022011	Weyi jatimi recho womedere gi timo recho, aka ŋata koch womedere gi koch pere; ŋataber womedere gi timo bero, ŋataleŋ womedere gi leŋo.”
66022012	Yesu owacho ni, “Neni, abino mayot; ani gi kemba paran, ma alemiyo kis nyatoro chungo kwoŋ gima go otimo.
66022013	Abedo Alufa kodi Omega, marapena kodi machowe, chakirok kodi gike.”
66022014	Josilwany a joma lwoko ruk pajo molony, aka ŋey jowobedi gi syem ma chamo gimanyak kwoŋ yath ma kwo, gi donjo i tindi gi i waŋkach.
66022015	To woko koro nitye gwokere kodi jothyeth, jochot kodi jonek, joma lamo chal makichar, kodi jotwodo jye, i wach kodi i kwo pajo
66022016	“An, Yesu, aoro malaika paran rin gi mikwenda me ri kitipa pa jomoyeyo. An anywola mawok i ot pa Daudi, an a sulwe modikini ma lyel moasere.”
66022017	Chuny kodi Mweha, jowacho ni, “Biye.” Aka weyi moro jye ma winjo wowachi ni, “Biye.” Aka weyi moro jye ma riyo neko wobin. Weyi nyatoro jye ma mito, womadhi pi makwo manono.
66022018	An Yohana, anyutho dhano jye ma winjo wach motuchi i kitawo me kichutho ni: ka moro omed'iye wach man, Were bino medo i girachula pere thoyamo ma sika ji mowach i kitawo me.
66022019	Aka ka moro okwany woko wach mogo jye motuch i kitawo me, Were bino kwanyo woko adech pere ma gimanyak kwoŋ yath ma kelo kwo, kodi ma tindi maleŋ, motuch i kitawo me.
66022020	Jaridhi mikwenda me wacho ni, “Adyeri, abino mayot.” Ameno. Biye, Ruoth Yesu!
66022021	Ŋono pa Ruoth Yesu wobedi kodi ji maleŋ jye.
